<pb n="r625"/>
<head>ṛjuvimalā</head>
<p><b>athātaḥ śeṣalakṣaṇam</b> । atra bhāṣyam-nānākarmalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti । tadanupapannam ।
na hi dvitīye'dhyāye nānākarmalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttaṃ api tu nānāśāstralakṣaṇamityāśaṅkyāha---<b>nānākarma-
lakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti</b> । <b>karmānubandhabhedācchastrabhedaḥ ataśśāstrabhedalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamityarthaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ-sādhyānubandhabhedābhyāṃ śāstrabheda uktaḥ । tatsidhyarthaṃ cānubandhabhūtakarmabhedaḥ pratipāditaḥ
ato nānākarmalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti śāstrabhedahetubhūtanānākarmalakṣaṇavṛttatābhidhāne phalata ida-
mevoktaṃ bhavati śāstrabhedalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti । karmaṇo niyogasyānubandhāvacchinnatvācchāstrabhedo
bhavati । ato niyogānubandhabhūtena karmabhedena śāstrabhedasiddheḥ śāstrabhedalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamityevaṃ
phalata uktaṃ bhavati । <b>nanu śāstrabhede satyaidamarthyamaṅgapradhānānāṃ na siddha‍yati</b> na hi
bhinnaśāstraprameyāṇāṃ darśapūrṇamāsajyotiṣṭāmādyapūrvāṇāṃ parasparabhaṅgāṅgitvamasti । tena hetu-
hetumadbhāvastāvannāsti, kintu vaiparītyameveti yāvat ।</p>
<p>uttaram---<b>viniyogataḥ karmabheda uktaḥ</b> । parasparaṃ padārthānāṃ viniyogataḥ kriyā-
kārakaguṇaguṇyādirūpeṇa sambandhādanubandhabhūtakarmaṇo bheda uktaḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati
---viniyoganibandhanamanubandhabhedamāśritya śāstrabheda uktaḥ । tannibandhane ca śāstrabhede satyapi
siddha‍yatyevāṅgapradhānabhāvaḥ । samprati viniyogaśabdabhaidamarthyalakṣaṇasaṃbandhaparaṃ matvā codayati
<note>(1) atra bhāṣyaṃ na mudrāpyate । punānagaramudritaśābarabhāṣyagatā puṭasaṅkhyā
bhāṣyodāharaṇasthaleṣu pradarśyate ।</note> <note>(1) puṭa. 647</note>
﻿<pb n="r626"/>
---<b>nanvidānīmeva viniyogaścintyate kathaṃ viniyogatobhedaḥ</b> yāvatā <b>bhede sati viniyogaḥ
ata eva ca bhedalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti hetvarthatayaiva bhedalakṣaṇopanyāsaḥ śeṣalakṣaṇasya</b> ।
saṃprati viniyogaśabdasya svābhimatamarthaṃ prakaṭayati---<b>satyaṃ hetvarthatayopanyāsaḥ satyañca
bhedādviniyogaḥ tathāpi śāstrabhedo'pi viniyogata eva kintvasau viniyogaḥ padanimittakaḥ</b>
na kāryanimittakaḥ । <b>kimidaṃ padanimittaka iti ? pratipattau hetuḥ padanimittakaḥ</b> vākyārtha-
pratipattau hetuḥ sambandhaḥ padanimittakaḥ । vākyārtho hi parasparānvitapadārtharūpaḥ pratīyate
parasparānvayaḥ padārthānāṃ padanimittakaḥ । anviteṣu svārtheṣu bodhyamāneṣvanvayo'rthagṛhīta iti
tadbhūtādhikaraṇe darśitaṃ spaṣṭayati---<b>padārthānāṃ saṃbandhapratipattinimittaka ityartaḥ</b> । padārthānāṃ
saṃbandha1pratipattyā gṛhyata ityarthaḥ। <b>yastvayaṃ tṛtīye cintyate sa</b> parasparasaṃbandhapratipattipūrvakaḥ
<b>kāryanimittakaḥ</b> । grahaṃ sammārṣṭīti kriyājanyaphalasaṃbandhitāmātreṇa padanimittakaḥ sambandhaḥ ।
śeṣaśeṣibhāvastu grahasammārgayoḥ kāryanimittakaḥ । kāryāntaropayogitayā hi grahāṇāṃ tān
pratyeva sammārgasya śeṣatvam । ataḥ padanimittakapadārthasaṃbandhena <b>vākyārthabhedena śāstrabhede
sati bhinnānāṃ vākyārthānāṃ parasparaṃ śeṣaśeṣicintā śeṣalakṣaṇamityucyate । nanu vrīhīn</b>
<note>(1) A. saṃbandhini pratipattyā gṛhyata ityarthaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r627"/>
<b>prokṣatīti padārthānāmapi parasparaṃ śeṣaśeṣicintā</b> yadi vākyārthānāmeva parasparaṃ śeṣaśeṣi-
bhāvaścintyate tadā śāstrabhedaḥ śeṣalakṣaṇasya heturbhavet na tvetadekāntato'sti । padārthānāmapi
parasparaṃ śeṣaśeṣibhāvacintanāt1 । <b>aśravaṇamrāparādhyate bhavataḥ । vrīhibhiryajetetyanena
sahāsya śeṣaśeṣicintā, na punarvrīhipadārthamātratayaiva</b> । vrīhirbhiyajetetyanena viniyoga-
śās‍treṇa ye vrīhayo yāge karaṇatayā pratipāditāḥ śās‍trārthībhūtāḥ taiḥ saha prokṣaṇasya śās‍trārthīṃ2-
bhūtasya śeṣaśeṣicinteti । yadi śās‍trārthānāṃ satāṃ śeṣaśeṣicintā, <b>kimiti tarhi
śeṣalakṣaṇamityucyate</b> । yadi tāvat padārthānāmeva śeṣaśeṣitā syāt tadā vrīhīn prokṣatīti
prokṣaṇaṃ prathamameva vrīhiśeṣatayaiva pratipādyata iti śeṣapratipattiparatvāccheṣalakṣaṇamevedaṃ syāt ।
śās‍trārthībhūtayostu paścāt kāryanimittakaḥ śeṣaśeṣibhāva iti dvayoḥ śās‍trapramitayoḥ śeṣaśeṣi-
bhāvaḥ kāryanimittaka iti na śeṣalakṣaṇamevedaṃ syāt api tu śeṣilakṣaṇamapīti । <b>uttaram
---viniyojyo hi śeṣaḥ, tadviṣayāṇi ca śrutyādīni, tasmāccheṣalakṣaṇamityucyate</b> ।
yo hi viniyujyate'ṅgatvena pratipādyate sa śeṣaḥ । śrutyādīnyapi tadviṣayāṇi tatpratipādakānyeva,
na śeṣitvapratipādakāni । tathā hi---vrīhīn prokṣatītyanena śās‍treṇa śās‍trāntarapratipāditān
vrīhin prati śeṣatvena prokṣaṇaṃ pratīyate na śeṣitayā । yadapi vrīhibhiryajeteti śās‍traṃ tadapi
yāgaśeṣatayaiva vrīhīn pratyāyayati na prokṣaṇādikaṃ prati śeṣitayā । ataḥ śeṣatayaiva sarvatra
codanālakṣaṇo'rthaḥ । codanālakṣaṇārthavicāraśca mīmāṃsāśāstrāntarbhūta iti । tasmāccheṣalakṣaṇa-
mityucyate । yadi tarhi śeṣatayaiva codanālakṣaṇaṃ <b>śeṣiparijñānaṃ tarhi kiṃ nimittaṃ ?
pramāṇāntaranimittakaṃ tat</b> yadā hi codanayā vrīhyādīn prati prokṣaṇādayaḥ śeṣatayā jñāpitāḥ
<note>(1) A. nirūpaṇāt (2) A. ekārthībhūtasya</note>
﻿<pb n="r628"/>
tadaivārthāt vrīhyādīnāmapi śeṣitvaṃ parijñāta bhavati । kasmāt punarna śeṣitā codanālakṣaṇetyatrāha
---<b>lakṣyate hi śeṣī śeṣapratipattau na pratipādyate</b> । yatpratipādanaparo hi śabdaḥ sa śabdārthaḥ
vrīhīn prokṣatītyādivākyāni ca vrīhiśeṣabhūtaprokṣaṇapratipādanaparāṇi prokṣaṇādīnāmeva vidhī-
yamānatvāt vrīhīṇāṃ tūddiśyamānatvāt । <b>ato yuktaṃ śeṣalakṣaṇam । yadyavaṃ</b> yadi yo
viniyujyate sa śeṣaḥ tadāpi <b>viniyojyaḥ śeṣa iti vaktavyam । kimidaṃ śeṣaḥ parārthatvā-
dityucyate</b> । pariharati---<b>uktamasmābhiḥ padanimittako'pi viniyogo vidyata iti</b> ।
yadi viniyojyaḥ śeṣa ityucyate tadā padanimittako'pi viniyogo vidyata iti tadyogenāpi
śeṣatā syāt । <b>ataḥ kārye viniyojyaḥ śeṣaḥ kathaṃ syāditi parārthatvādityuktam</b> ।
kārye viniyojyaḥ saṃbandhitvena pratipādyamāno yaḥ sa śeṣaḥ iti kathaṃ nāma jñāyetetyevamarthaṃ
śeṣaḥ parārthatvādityuktam । kathaṃ punaḥ parārthatvādityukte yasya kārye viniyogaḥ sa eva pratīyata
ityata āha---<b>yasya kārye viniyogaḥ</b> saṃbandhaḥ <b>sa tadartha eva bhavati । ataḥ</b> kārye
viniyogasvīkaraṇāya <b>parārthatvāditi lakṣitam</b> । kasmāt punaryasya kārye yasya viniyogaḥ
tasya kāryārthataiva bhavati । tatrāha---<b>na kāryaṃ parārthaṃ bhavitumarhati kāryameva hi tanna
syādyadyanyārtham</b> । asyārthaḥ-sarvo hi saṃbandho guṇapradhānabhāvamantareṇa na saṃbhavati । tatra kasya
guṇatā kasya pradhānateti cintāyāṃ yat kāryaṃ tanna tāvada‍guṇabhūtaṃ kāryatvāvagamavirodhāt । yattva-
kāryabhūtamaparaṃ tat kāryārthamiti yuktam । atastatra puruṣasya niyopaḥ/?/ kāryārthatvenāvagamyate ।
﻿<pb n="r629"/>
ato yasya niyogena saha sākṣātsaṃbandhaḥ pratīyate sa niyogārthaḥ yasya ca tena sākṣānniyoga-
saṃbandhenārthāntareṇa saṃbandhaḥ so'pi tadartha eva । tasyāpi kāryārthatvena kāryatvāt । evamapara-
syāpi tatsambandhisaṃbandhasya tādarthyamūhitavtam । ataḥ śeṣaḥ parārthatvādityasyāyamarthaḥ---kārye
yasya viniyogaḥ sa śeṣaḥ parārthalakṣaṇaḥ । tasyedaṃ lakṣaṇamucyate । na punarupayuktetarasya ।
kena punarhetunā kārye viniyojyalakṣaṇaḥ śeṣo jñāyate ? parārthatvāt kāryeṇa saha saṃbandhāvagamāt ।
atredaṃ vyutpādyam । anvitapadārthātmakatvādvākyārthasya parasparakriyākārakabhāvadimātrātmakatvā-
dvākyārthasya parasparakriyākārakabhāvādimātrātmakatvāccānvayasya padārthānāṃ śeṣatvotpattau heturnāsti ।
ato lakṣaṇārambho nirviṣaya1 iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । kāryasaṃbandhasyaivānyathā'nirvāhāt śeṣatocyate
tato lakṣaṇamārambhaṇīyamiti rāddhāntaḥ । grāhakavyutpattiḥ punaranupayoginīti nātra vyutpādyate ।
śeṣitvābhimatasya hi kāryataiva kāryapratiyoginaḥ śeṣasya śeṣatve hetuḥ na viniyojyasya grāhaka-
gṛhītatāpi । ata ādhānādīnāmapi viniyogasiddhiḥ । grāhakeṇa punaragṛhītānāṃ viniyoge
pratiprakaraṇaṃ vyavasthā na siddha‍yatīti saptamādya eva grāhako vyutpādyaḥ । tathā cāha---<q>“na ca
ṣaṭa‍keṇāpyayamartho nirūpitaḥ । sambandhamātraparyavasāyāt । ubhayathā ca sambandhopapatteḥ”</q> iti ।
yata eva ca kārye viniyogo yasya sa tadartha eva bhavati । <b>ata eva garbhadāsadṛṣṭānto
bhāṣye</b> । anyathā garbhadāsatulyatā niṣpramāṇikā syāt । <b>nanu parārthatāmātraṃ parārthaśabde-
nocyate kimidamatyantaparārtha iti</b> । atyantaśabdābhāve kathamatyantārtho labhyata ityarthaḥ ।
<b>ucyate---ata evātyantaparārthaḥ yasmāt parārthatāmātrataivocyate</b> yadi parārthaśabdena parārthā-
parārthābhidhānaṃ syāt tadā'tyantaparārthatā na labhyeta । ataḥ parārthaśabdastu parārthatāmātraṃ brūte
iti । <b>ataḥ sādhu vivṛtam</b> । eva sambandhabhāṣyaṃ vyākhyāya prasaktānuprasaktaṃ parisamāpya
<note>(1) A. niṣphalaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r630"/>
prakṛtaṃ vyācaṣṭe---<b>kaḥ śeṣaḥ kena  hetunā śeṣa iti । kimidaṃ praśnadvayaṃ ? kena hetunā śeṣa
ityetāvad‍vaktavyaṃ । siddha‍yati hi parārthatvāccheṣa</b> ityetāvatā'bhimatam । <b>ucyate---syāde-
tadevaṃ yadi siddhavadabhidhānaṃ hetoḥ syāt heturapyatra kathanīya evetyadoṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ ।
yadi śeṣatve parārthatvameva heturiti siddham syāttadā kaḥ śeṣa iti praśno'narthakaḥ syāt ।
yatastu heturapyatra kathayitavyaḥ । na ca sādhyamanabhidhāya heturabhidhātuṃ śakyata iti sādhya-
viśeṣanirdhāraṇāyārthavānayaṃ praśnaḥ । yata eva sādhyapuraḥ sarameva hetorabhidhānaṃ <b>ata eva ko
dharmaḥ kathaṃ lakṣaṇaścetyuktam</b> । nanu ca śeṣaḥ parārthatvāditi sādhyabhedo3 nirdiṣṭa eva ।
na ca śeṣaśabdasyārtho na prasiddhaḥ, । tadāha---<b>kiṃ punaḥ siddhasya kathane prayojanam ?</b>
uttaram---<b>upayuktādanyo yaḥ sa śeṣaḥ ityevamādinivṛttyartham</b> । athātaḥ śeṣalakṣaṇa-
mityetāvatyuk‍te upayuk‍tādanyo yaḥ sa śeṣa ityevamādyapi pratīyeta । na ca tādṛśasya
parārthatā hetuḥ । ato hetuviśeṣābhidhānāya sādhyaviśeṣaṃ vak‍tuṃ praśno'pyarthavān । <b>kathaṃ ca
viniyujyata iti ? ko'yaṃ praśnaḥ ? kena viniyujyata iti vaktavyam । kimidaṃ
kathaṃ ca viniyujyata iti</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 652 (2) P. 652 (3) A. sādhyaviśeṣo</note> 
﻿<pb n="r631"/>
<p><b>atrābhidhīyate---kena viniyujyata ityetāvatyucyamāne śrutyādivyāpāra eva tu
kevalaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ kathitaśca</b> bhavati । na punaḥ <b>saviniyogakānāṃ śrutyādīnām</b> ।
bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi ko doṣa ityatrāha---<b>na ca niyogaśūnyāni śrutyādīni śeṣatāmāpādayituṃ
śak‍nuvanti</b> 1kāryābhāve sak‍tṛn juhotītivat । <b>kāryanimittaṃ ca pārārthyamityuktam ।
ataḥ kathaṃ ca viniyujyata ityuktam । sahetukaviniyogasiddha‍yartham</b> । kāryarūpatvena
hi śeṣiṇaḥ śeṣasya tatra viniyogaḥ na punaḥ śrutyādimātreṇa । yata eva ca niyogavyāpāravaśena
śeṣatvamavagamyate । <b>ata eva ca śrutyādīni ca viniyoge kāraṇānītyuktam । na punaḥ
śrutyādibhiriti</b> । kāraṇamātratā śrutyādīnāṃ na sādhakatamatetyarthaḥ । śrutyādīni ca viniyoge
kāraṇānītyatrāpi kathamityanuṣaṅgādyojyam । <b>eteṣāṃ ca balavadabalavattetyatrāpi katha-
mityanuṣaṅgo vak‍tavyaḥ</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---kaḥ śeṣa iti upayuk‍tetaro vā, avayavo vā,
parārtho vā ? tatrottaraṃ parārthaḥ śeṣa iti । kena hetunā śeṣo bhavatīti parārthatvena
kāryasaṃbandhitvena śeṣo bhavatītyuktam । kathaṃ ca viniyujyate ? kena prakāreṇa śeṣabhāvo'vagamyata
ityarthaḥ । uttaram---śrutyādisacivakāryabalena । śrutyādīni ca viniyoge kāraṇānīti । katha
śrutyādīni viniyogajñānotpattau sāhāyyaṃ yāntīti । dvāraviśeṣasamarpaṇenetyuttaram । dvayamapyetat
pratyadhikaraṇaṃ vakṣyate । teṣāṃ ca kathaṃ balavadabalattetyatra śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇe uttaraṃ bhaviṣyati ।
<note>(1) G. kāryābhāvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r632"/>
kāryata eva śeṣatopapadyate । kāryeṇaiva śrutyādisacivena jñāyata iti tattvārthaḥ । <b>eba tāva-
llakṣaṇārthaḥ । naitāvatā vinā śeṣaparijñānasiddhiḥ । anyadapi sādhanasiddha‍yarthaṃ kiñcidupo-
ddhātādibhiḥ śeṣaḥ parārthatvāditi sabhāṣyaṃ sūtraṃ vyākhyātameva pūrvam</b> । ato na vyākhyāyate ।
<b>atha tatra kiṃ vṛttam ? yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate</b> ityādi bhāṣyaṃ tadanupapannam । anena
bhāṣyeṇa punaḥ paunaruktya2mivāśaṅka‍yate taccānupapannam । tatra dravyaguṇādīnāṃ śeṣatvasyā-
pratipāditatvāt । atha saṃskārasya tatra 3śeṣatā pratipāditeti evamapi teṣāmarthena paunaruktyam
tataśca tatraivedaṃ yuk‍taṃ vak‍tum । sarveṣāṃ hi śeṣatve tatrok‍te atra śeṣatvapratipādana-
pratijñākṣepo yukta ityāśaṅkyāha---<b>yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate guṇastatra pratīyate iti । uk‍taṃ
śeṣalakṣaṇaṃ manvānasyedaṃ codyam</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati-saṃskārasya śeṣatvaṃ tatrok‍tam । tenā-
viśeṣeṇa 4idamayuk‍taṃ vak‍tum athātaśśeṣalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāma iti । uttarabhāṣyam <q>“tatrā-
pūrvārthatā vyāvartitā”</q> iti tadanupapannam । saṃskārāṇāmapyapūrvārthatvāditi; ato vyācaṣṭe
<b>uttaraṃ tu niyogaviṣayatā tatrāpanītā śeṣatvaṃ tu ihaiva sarveṣāṃ pratipādyate</b> । idānīmākṣi-
pati---ko'yaṃviniyogaviṣayatvāpanhavaḥ ayuk‍ta ityarthaḥ । kutaḥ ? <b>na ca viniyoga-
śūnyāni śrutyādīni śeṣatāmāpādayituṃ śak‍nuvantītyuktam</b> । caśabdo hiśabdasyārthe
<note>(1) P. 649</note> <note>(2) R. mityāśaṅka‍yate ।</note> <note>(3) R. sya prati</note> <note>(4) idamuk‍taṃvak‍tuṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r633"/>
yasya hi niyogaḥ kāryaḥ tatra puruṣo niyujyate । ataḥ tadabhyupagamenaiva niyogaviṣayatāpvastīti
manyate । <b>tasmāccheṣatvaṃ niyogaviṣayatvāpahnavaśceti vipratiṣiddham । ataḥ śeṣatvaṃ vā
nāsti । apūrvārthatā vā nāpahotuṃ śakyate । ucyate-anabhijño bhavān viṣayaniyojyānām</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---guṇakarmaṇāṃ tāvadavaghātādīnāṃ kārakībhūtaṃ padārtha. sādhyatvenāvagamyate । tatra
yadi niyogo'pyaparo'ṅgīkriyate tadā sādhyadvayamekasmin vākye na saṃbadhyate parasparānuguṇatvāt
na ca niyojyaviśeṣaṇatā tasyāśrayituṃ yuktā । kriyāphalatayā tadviśiṣṭasya niyogasaṃbandhānupapatteḥ ।
tasmādyo viṣayo niyogasya tasyāparaṃ sādhyāntaraṃ nāstīti abhyupeyam । ato bhavān viṣayaṃ na
jānāti । yena viṣayatāṃ guṇakarmaṇāmicchati । tathā niyojyasvarūpaṃ ca na jātāti ।
yataḥ parasparānuguṇyārthaṃ kriyāphalaṃ niyojyaviśeṣaṇaṃ manyate । niyojyo hi niyogārthaṃ
kartavyatayā'vabudhyate । tasya ca tadeva sādhyabhūtaṃ viśeṣaṇatayā'nveti yanniyogādeva
sidhyati । na ca kriyāphalaṃ niyogādeva sidhyati । ataḥ kārakībhūtapadārthaviśiṣṭo
niyojyo bhavati । tena viṣayaniyojyā'nabhijñatayā guṇakarmaviṣayaniyogaṃ bhavānabhivāñchati ।
yadyapi guṇakarmasu niyogo nāsti tathāpi kimiti viṣayo na bhavatītyatrāha---<b>na brūmo guṇa-
bhūteṣu puṃso niyojyatā nāstīti । kiṃ tarhi viṣayastu na bhavatīti</b> । adhikāra-
vidhyadhīnā liṅādyanubādyasti preraṇā । guṇabhūteṣu puruṣasya viṣayastu na bhavati । yadi
preraṇāviṣayo na niyogasya viṣayaḥ, kastarhi viṣayaḥ, ityatrāha---<b>yasya punarniyoga-
siddhireva kāryaḥ sa viṣayaḥ</b> । tadidaṃ sarvaṃ teṣāmarthetyatra prakaṭataraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ । <b>ato yukta-
mukraṃ tatrāpūrvārthatā vyāvartiteti</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 660</note>
﻿<pb n="r634"/>
<head>dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣu bādariḥ</head>
<p><b><q>‘kaḥ punaratrābhiprāyo dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva pārārthyaṃ vadataḥ’</q></b> । anena pūrvapakṣa-
mākṣipati । ekadeśī samarthayate---<b>ayamabhiprāyaḥ---vibhaktibhiḥ tādarthyaṃ prātipadikārthasya
pratipādyate । tacca dravyaguṇayorupalabhyate ekahānyā krīṇātīti</b> dravyasya tādarthyam ।
ekahāyanīśabdasya yaugikatvena dravyavacanatvāt <b>aruṇayeti ca</b> guṇasya tādarthyaṃ saṃskārasya tu
tādarthyaṃ kathaṃ ? uttaram---<b>atrāpi vibhakta‍yaiva tādarthyaṃ vrīhīnavahanti vrīhīnprokṣatīti
dvitīyayā । nanu ca prātipadikārthasya prādhānyaṃ dvitīyā pratipādayati na karmaṇaḥ</b>
kriyāyā dravyaṃ prati <b>guṇabhāvam</b> । uttaram---<b>akārakajño bhavān । kārakavibhaktayo hi kathaṃ
kriyānirapekṣāḥ</b> । kriyāpekṣitvāt kārakāṇām । <b>tasmāt kriyāpekṣameva prātipadikārthasya
prādhānyaṃ guṇatvaṃ vā</b> । tena śrutyaiva dvitīyayā prādhānyaṃ vadantyā kriyāyā guṇabhāva ukta
eveti vaibhaktikameva saṃskārasyāpi śeṣatvam । yata eva vibhaktibhistādarthyaṃ pratipādyate ।
<b>ata eva vibhaktividhāne bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ kārakoddeśaḥ</b> । karmaṇi dvitīyā kartṛkaraṇayo-
stṛtīyetyādi । yadi vibhaktayastādarthyaṃ na pratipādayeyustadā naiva kārakoddeśena vidhīyeran ।
<note>(1) P. 660</note>
<pb n="r635"/>
kārakoddeśena vidhīyamānāḥ kriyāpekṣaguṇaprādhānyaṃ vadantyaḥ tādarthyaṃ pratipādayantyeva । ataḥ
kārakoddeśena vibhaktividhānādavagamyate tādarthyaṃ vibhaktibhiḥ pratipādyata iti । yadi
vibhaktibhiḥ tādarthyamavagamyate kathaṃ <b>tarhi taddhitādiṣu tādarthyamavagamyate</b> parṇamayī juhūrbhavatīti
taddhite, <q>‘śaraiḥ staritavya’</q>miti kṛtpratyaye, <q>‘yajamānasaṃmitā auduṃbarī bhavati’</q> iti samāse ।
<b>kathaṃ copapadavibhak‍tayastādarthya</b>mavabodhayeyuḥ akārakavibhaktitvāt । ato vibhaktivyati-
rekeṇāpi tādarthyadarśanāt tadvayatirik‍ta<b>manyadapi (tāda)pārārthye pramāṇam dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣu
vak‍tavyam</b> । saṃprati parasamarthanavādyāha---<b>nanu copakāradarśanameva dravyaguṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ
pārārthye heturiti vādarermatam । kimatra vibhaktyādibhiḥ kriyate</b> । tenopakārakatvāccheṣatā
dravyaguṇasaṃskārāṇām । tena vināpi vibhaktyā yasyopakārakatā tasya śeṣateti । <b>yad‍yupakāra-
darśanaṃ pārārthye hetuḥ vrīhayo'pi prokṣaṇasyopakārakāḥ syuḥ</b> utpattebrīṃhyādibhirvinā prokṣaṇa-
syānupapatterityarthaḥ । tena vrīhayo'pi prokṣaṇaśeṣabhūtā bhaveyuḥ । na caivam । tasmānnopakāra-
darśanamātraṃ śepatve heturiti । ekārthena codyavādyeva samarthanavādinaḥ āśaṅkāmāha---<b>atha
prayojanaṃ prati upakāradarśanaṃ hetuḥ</b> । tena niṣprayojanatvāt prokṣaṇasya satyapyupakārye kāryatve na
śoṣitā । prayojanavattvāt‍tu vrīhīṇāmeva śeṣitve sthite prokṣaṇasya saṃskāradvāreṇa vrīhayupakārakatayā
śeṣateti । dūṣayati---<b>prayojanavattājñānamidānīṃ kutaḥ</b> ? prayojanavattaiva vrīhīṇāṃ kuto'va-
﻿<pb n="r636"/>
gamyate । punarāśaṅkāntaramāha---<b>niyogata iti cet</b> । niyogo hi kāryasvarūpatvāt svayaṃ
prayojanabhūtaḥ yasyāpi ca tatsaṃbandhaḥ tasyāpi tadvaśenaiva prayojanavatteti niyoganirvṛttyaiva prayo-
janavattāvagamaḥ । dūṣayati---<b>evaṃ tarhi niyoganirvṛttireva pārārthye hetuḥ kimupakāradarśanaṃ
kliṣṭaṃ kariṣyati</b> । yasmin kriyamāṇe niyoganirbṛttirbhavati tat tasya kāryamiti yata eva
niyoganirvṛttyā <b>pārārthyamata eva vibhaktivyatyayo'pi prayājaśeṣeṇetyevamādiṣu siddho bhavati</b> ।
prayājaśeṣapratipattirhi vidhyapekṣitā na haviṣāmabhidhāraṇam । ataḥ prayājaśeṣapratipattiriyamiti
niyogavaśena sthite vibhaktivyatyayo bhavati prayojaśeṣaṃ haviṣṣu abhidhārayati iti । anyathā
vibhaktivyatyayo durbhaṇaḥ syāt । <b>kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca tadvaśenaivaidamarthyapratipādakāḥ</b> anyathā
teṣāṃ svabhāvata evaidamarthyabodhakatvābhāvāt । <b>evaṃ copapadavibhakterasaṃkaraḥ (saṃskāraḥ) sidhyati</b>
anyathā hi aniyamena śeṣaśeṣibhāvaḥ syāt । ekagranthetāha---<b>kimiti tarhi bādariḥ
dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva śeṣabhāvaṃ manyate yadi niyoganirvṛttiḥ pārārthye hetuḥ</b> । yadi
niyoganirvṛttyā pārārthyamavagamyate tadā yāgasyāpi niyoganirvartakatayā śeṣatā'styeva niyogaṃ
prati । tathā niyojyaviśeṣaṇaṃ svargādikamapi prati niyogasiddhidvāreṇa sādhakatvāt yāgasya
śeṣatā yuk‍taiva । tathā phalanirvṛttidvāreṇa puruṣamapi prati yāgasya śeṣatā yuk‍taiva । tathā
phalanirvṛttidvāreṇa puruṣamapi prati yāgasya śeṣatvaṃ nānupapannam । tathā phalasyāpi niyojya-
viśeṣaṇasya puruṣaṃ prati śeṣatā niyogākṣepeṇaivāvagamyata iti śeṣitvamastyeva । tathā phalabhāgita-
﻿<pb n="r637"/>
yauvaudumbarīsaṃmānādau puruṣasya śeṣateti yāgaphalapuruṣāṇāmapi śeṣatvaṃ yuktamityarthaḥ । saṃprati
samarthanavādī samarthayate---<b>na niyogaṃ phale puruṣe ca manyate । yāga eva niyogaḥ tannirvṛttyā ca
niyoganirvṛttiḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---lokavyutpattyanusāreṇa śabdādartho'vagamyate tatra loke grāmaṃ
gacchetyuk‍te grāmagamanamanutiṣṭhan puruṣo dṛśyate । kāryapratipattiścānuṣṭhānaheturiti sarvajanasya
saṃviditameva । yadviṣayameva ca kāryajñānaṃ tadviṣayameva cānuṣṭhānamiti kriyāviṣayamanuṣṭhānaṃ dṛṣṭvā
kriyākāryatvāvagatihetutvaṃ śabdasyāvagamyata iti yajetetyevamādibhiryāga eṃva kāryatayā pratyāyyate
na ca kāryamanyārthaṃ bhavatīti nāsti yāgasya śeṣabhāvaḥ । ataḥ phale niyogo nāsti yāgena
phalaṃ sādhayediti niyogo nāsti tathā puruṣepi niyogo nāsti phalena puruṣaṃ saṃbadhnīyāditi, puruṣa-
viśeṣaṇamātratayaiva svargaśabdasya śravaṇāt । na ca puruṣaviśeṣaṇasya kriyayā saha sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ
bodhahetvābhāvāt । ato yāganirvṛttimātreṇaiva kṛtaḥ śāstrārtha iti bādarirmanyate <b>dravyaguṇasaṃskāraiśca
yāgo nirvartyata iti । atasteṣāmeva pārārthyaṃ manyate bādarirācāryaḥ । nanu yāgena svargaṃ
kuryāt ātmārthamiti niyogaḥ ātmanepadaprayogāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---yajetetyātmanepadaprayogāt
kartrabhiprāye kriyāphale tasya vṛddhavyavahāre prayogāt । ātmārthaṃ yāgena svargaṃ kuryāt iti niyogaḥ
pratīyate tena phalaṃ prati yāgasya puruṣaṃ prati phalasya śeṣatā'stīti । pariharati---<b>naivaṃ
śakyate śabdāt pratipat‍tum</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---yadi svargasya kriyāphalatā syāt tadā ātma-
nepadaśravaṇāt ātmārthatā tasyāvagamyeta । na ca kriyāphalatā svargasyāvasīyate । atha[yathā]
odanaṃ pacatītyodanasya । kasmāt punaḥ kriyāphalatā nāvagamyata ityāha---<b>dvitīyā hi kārakasya
prādhānyaṃ pratipādayati yasyāḥ kriyāyāstat kārakaṃ</b> tat kriyāpekṣaṃ hi dvitīyā prādhānya
﻿<pb n="r638"/>
pratipādayati <b>na ca svargo yāgasya kārakaṃ</b> yāgotpattāvasattvenāvyāpriyamāṇatvāt । odanaṃ
pacatītyatra taṇḍulānāṃ vikāryakarmabhūtānāmasti pāke vyāpāraḥ bhāvyavasthāvācinā tvodanaśabdena
taṇḍulā eva nirdiśyante । ataḥ kārakatvaṃ tatrāviruddham । nanu yadyapyasatvenāvyāpārādyāgaṃ
prati svargasya kārakatā pramāṇāntareṇa nāvasīyate tathāpi vedādevāvasāyiṣyata ityatrāha---<b>na ca
vedāt kriyākārakarūpasaṃbandhāvagatiḥ । siddhasya hi anuṣṭhānaṃ codyate</b> । asyārthaḥ-kārye'rthe
śabdasya prāmāṇyaniyamāt na siddhaṃ kriyākārakasaṃbandhaṃ prati śabdasya prāmāṇyaṃ, kintu
pramāṇāntarasiddhameva kriyākārakasaṃbandhamāśritya vedenānuṣṭhānaṃ pratyāyyate idamanena kurviti । na
punaridamanena sidhyatīti vedādavagatiḥ । yadi vedāt kriyākārakasaṃbandho nāvagamyate <b>kathaṃ tarhi
yadāhṛvanīye juhotīti</b> alaukikasyāhavanīyasya homaṃ prati kārakatvaṃ ? pramāṇāntareṇāna-
vagamāt । uttaraṃ---<b>yuk‍taṃ pramāṇāntareṇa saṃbhavadarśanāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapyāhavanīya-
śabdavācyatā pramāṇāntareṇa nāvagamyate tathāpi tasya dravyarūpatvāt vidyamānatvācca homaṃ prati
sādhanabhāvaḥ saṃbhavatīti pramāṇāntareṇāvagamyata eva । svarge punarnaitadupapadyate asatvātsvargasya ।
yadi tathābhūtasyāpi vedaḥ kārakatāṃ brūyāt tadā pramāṇāntaravirodhena aṅgulyagrādivākyavat
vedasyāprāmāṇyaprasaṃgāt । <b>kiñca kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ cātra svargaśabdaḥ na kartṛviśeṣaṇamīpsitatamaṃ
bhavati yathā rājapuruṣeṃ paśyeti</b> । yadi tāvat dvitīyayaiva vibhaktyā svargo nirdiṣṭaḥ syāt
tadā kriyayā so'pi īp‍sita iti gamyate kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ tu svargaśabdaḥ । nanu ṣaṣṭhādye sthitaṃ
niyojyaviśeṣaṇasamarpakaḥ svargaśabdaḥ iti; kathamucyate kartṛviśeṣaṇatā svargaśabdasya । ucyate ।
asyādhikaraṇasya pūrvapakṣe kriyaiva kāryatvenāvagamyate, kriyāṃ ca kāryatayā kartaivāvabudhyate iti
﻿<pb n="r639"/>
kartureva niyojyateti । ataḥ kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ svargaḥ । na kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ kriyayepsitaṃ bhavati
yathā rājapuruṣaṃ paśyatīti karmaviśeṣaṇaṃ rājā darśaneneṣsito bhavati । nanu kāmipadasaṃbandhāt
svargasyepsitatā'vagamyata eva । satyaṃ, na yāgenepsitatā'vagamyate । dvitīyā hi kāraka-
vibhaktiḥ kriyāpekṣatvāt kārakasya samabhivyāhṛtakriyāpekṣitabhīpsitatvaṃ brūyāta, na kamiriti
niravadyam । upasaṃharati---<b>ato na svargeṃ kuryāditi niyogaviṣayatā śakyate pratipat‍tut ।
tadidaṃ paramarahasyaṃ</b> svargādeḥ sākṣāt kriyayā saha janyajanakabhāvo na ghaṭate kriyayāḥ kāraka-
samavāyiphalajanakatvaniyamāt svargādeścākārakasamavāyitvāt । yadyapi prītirūpatvāt
svargasyātmasamavāyitvaṃ tathāpi na kārakadaśāyāṃ samavaiti । na cedamāśaṅkanīyaṃ pūrvaṃ kārakatā
paścāt kriyājanyaphalabhāgiteti । yataḥ kriyāyogena kārakamucyate satyāmeva kriyāyāṃ
kriyāphalenotpannenaikārthasamavāyinā kriyā viruddha‍yeteti । ata eva kriyāphalānāmanantarabhāvi-
tā''śrīyate । kathaṃ tarhi rāddhāntepi svargādīnāmutpattiḥ ? apūrvavyavadhāneneti na doṣaḥ । na
cāyamapūrve'pi niyamo dṛṣṭaḥ apūrvatvādeva । apūrvasiddhireva kutaḥ ? kriyāta iti brūmaḥ । nanu
kārakasamavāyiphalaniyamāt kriyāyāḥ kva kārake tadapūrvaṃ samavetamutpadyate kālāntarasthāyinyātma-
nīti na kiñcit duṣyapti । na ca puruṣasaṃskārakatā darśapūrṇamāsādīnāmāpādyate saṃskāryatve
pramāṇābhāvāt । vastusvabhāvena tu āśrayamātratayā puruṣamapūrvamāśrayati ityalamatiprasaṅgena ।
atra ca naivaṃ śabdāt pratipat‍tuṃ śakyata ityanena granthena svargayāgayoḥ sādhyasādhanabhāvaśak‍tireva
nāstītyuk‍taṃ kiñcetyādinā । athavetyaṅgīkṛtyāpi sādhyasādhanabhāvaṃ dvitīyābhāvādīpsitatvāna-
vagamānna yāgasya śeṣatā'stīti darśitam । evaṃ ca bhāṣyamapi tasmiṃstu kṛte svayameva tadbhavatītya-
bhyupagamyavādena draṣṭavyam । yadi svargasya kārakatā nāsti---<b>kathaṃ tarhi svargakāmapada-
saṃbandhāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti bhāṣyam</b> । atra hi svargaṃ bhāvayediti dvitīyāprayogaḥ
kārakatvābhāve nopapadyate । uttaraṃ---<b>evametadbhāṣya</b>masmadīyavādānuguṇaṃ etadbhāṣyaṃ, na prati-
pakṣam । <b>anyathā hi</b> pratipakṣatve <b>svargamiti śravaṇāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti syāt</b> yadi
﻿<pb n="r640"/>
svargamiti śravaṇādityuk‍taṃ syāt tadā kārakatā svargasyoktā syāt na caivamuktam । kathaṃ tarhi
svargaṃ bhāvayediti ghaṭate atrāha---<b>ataḥ svayameva tad‌bhavatītyetadabhiprāyaṃ tat</b> yataḥ svarga-
śabdo hi dvitīyānto noktaḥ । ataḥ svayameva phalaṃ bhavatītyetadabhiprāyaṃ na kārakabhūtaṃ
niṣpadyata ityetadabhiprāyam । <b>nimittatvamātrakathanaṃ hi tat karmaṇaḥ</b> svargotpattau nimittamātratā
karmaṇaḥ kathyate । na punaḥ kriyākārakabhāvo vivakṣitaḥ । tena gauṇo'yaṃ dvitīyāprayoga
iti yāvat । <b>ataḥ prayojanaṃ svargo yāgasya</b> na karma <b>pākasyeva grāsaḥ pākasya grāmaḥ</b>
[saḥ]prayojanaṃ, pākāyattatvāt sūpakāryagrāma[sa]siddheḥ odanaṃ phalam । ataḥ nāsti bhāṣya-
virodhaḥ । upasaṃharati---<b>ato dravyaguṇasaṃskārāṇāmeva</b> kriyayāsaha <b>sādhyasādhanabhāvā-
vagateḥ prayojanavattayā</b> kriyānivṛttyā prayojanabhūtayā prayojanavattvāt kriyāyāḥ śeṣa(śeṣi)
bhāvaḥ । <b>na punaḥ prādhānyenāpratīyamāne phale puruṣe vā kriyāyāḥ phalasyāpi śeṣabhāvaḥ ।
tasmātsūk‍taṃ dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣu bādaririti</b> । <q>“ na cet phalayāgau guṇabhāvena codyete kasya
puruṣaḥ pradhānabhūto bhaviṣyati”</q> iti । <b>ko'yaṃ prādhānyapratiṣedhaḥ ? śeṣatā hi
puruṣasya pratiṣedhyā, <q>“na yāgaphalapuruṣeṣu śeṣatā'sti”</q> iti pratijñānāt । ucyate ।
śeṣatānivṛttyarthameva prādhānyaṃ pratiṣidhyate । kathaṃ ? sati hi prādhānye puruṣaḥ śeṣa iti</b>
<note>(1) P. 661-8</note>
﻿<pb n="r641"/>
<b>śakyate vak‍tum</b> । <b>kimiti</b> । <b>puruṣaśabdo hyayaṃ svargakāme prayuk‍taḥ yadi ca tadarthaḥ svargaḥ
syāt tadā tadviśiṣṭasya śeṣatā syāt</b> । <b>svadravyaviśiṣṭasyeva prayājādeḥ</b> । <b>atādarthye punaḥ
svargasya kevalaṃ kartṛtayaiva śeṣabhāvaḥ dravyamātratayaivetyarthaḥ na puruṣaśeṣatayā, na svargakāma-
padavācyatayetyabhiprāyaḥ</b> । atredamākūtaṃ-svargakāmaśabdena yaḥ kāmanāviṣayībhūtasvargaviśiṣṭaḥ
puruṣo'bhidhīyate sa ta tathābhūtena rūpeṇa tatraiva kartā bhavati yadeva tasya svargasya sādhanam ।
yatpunarna tasya svargasya sādhanaṃ tatrāvivakṣitakāmyārthasaṃbandhinaḥ kevalaṃ kartṛtāṃ yāti ।
ato'smin pakṣe dravyatayaiva śeṣabhāva iti । <b>tasmādanavadyam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt</b> । <b>kathaṃ phalārthatā karmaṇaḥ ?</b> uttaraṃ---<b>kāmino-
hyadhikāro yāge</b> । <b>sa ca phalasādhanatāṃ yāgasyānāpādayan na siddha‍yati iti ṣaṣṭhe
vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । ṣaṣṭhādyasiddhāntabalena hi sthitaṃ kartṛtvātirik‍taṃ niyojyatvamapi puruṣasyāstīti ।
sa hyevaṃ manyate mabhedaṃ kāryamiti । kāmī cātra niyojyatvena śrūyate । sa ca vivakṣitakāmibhāvaḥ
tenaiva kāryeṇa saṃbandhumarhati yadeva kāryaṃ tasya kāmyasādhanaṃ syāt । ataḥ kāmino(niyoge)yāge
<note>(1) 661-12</note>
﻿<pb n="r642"/>
niyuktiḥ mamedaṃ kāryamityavagatiḥ phale sādhanatāṃ yāgasya anāpādayantī na siddha‍yatīti niyojya-
viśeṣānvayabalena yāgasvargayoḥ sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ । atassiddhaṃ phale yāgasya śeṣatvaṃ ātma-
saṃbadhitvena phalasyeṣṭatvāt neṣṭaṃ parārthaṃ yataḥ । <b>yadi punaḥ yāgaḥ phale sādhanatāṃ na pratipadyate
tatra ko doṣaḥ syāt ? yathā</b> nityādhikāre vinā phalena adhikārānupapattirnāsti tathā
atrāpyastu kiṃ phalakalpanayā ? uttaraṃ---<b>na khalu kaściddoṣaḥ</b> pratīyate । <b>pratīyate tu tathā</b>
kāmino niyojyatvāt sādhyasādhanabhāvākṣepaḥ । evaṃ cātrādhikaraṇe svargayāgayoḥ sādhya-
sādhanabhāvo'stīti vyutpādyate । sthite caitasmin adhikaraṇe apūrvādhikaraṇe kriyātiriktam-
pūrvameva kāryatvenocyata iti siddha‍yati । ataḥ ṣaṣṭhādyabādaryadhikaraṇāpūrvādhikaraṇaiḥ tribhiḥ
sthitaiḥ apūrvavākyārthatā bhavatīti mantavyam ।</p>
<p><b>nanu śeṣalakṣaṇe śeṣatā'sya yuktā pratipādayitum । kimidamucyate</b> “enamevārthaṃ
ṣaṣṭhe'dhyāye <b>sūtraireva sādhayiṣyati iti 2kiṃ vā śrutyādivyatirik‍taṃ kiñcidanyat, śeṣatve
pramāṇamasti । atha śrutyādīnāmevānyatamaṃ tadihaivopanyasanīyam । kimiti sānyā-
sikaṃ kriyate । atrocyate---adhikārāpekṣiṇī hi sā śrutiḥ na śrutyapekṣo'dhikāraḥ
iti yuk‍taṃ sānyāsikam</b> । asyārthaḥ-kamiśratyā yatra yāgaḥ phale śeṣo bhavati tatra
niyoganiyojyalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandho hetuḥ anyathā anvitābhidhānānupapatteḥ । ato'dhikārā-
pekṣitvādasyāḥ śruteḥ yuk‍taṃ sānyāsikatvam । uk‍taṃ yāgasya śeṣatvam ।</p>
<note>(1) 661-13</note> <note>(2) G. kiñcana</note>
﻿<pb n="r643"/>
<p><b>phalaṃ ca puruṣārthatvāt</b> । nanu ca yadyapi svargoṃ yāgāt sidhyati tathāpi kathaṃ tasya
kāminaḥ prati śeṣatetyāha---<b>phalamapi puruṣaṃ pratyupadiśyate yaḥ svargo me bhavedityevaṃ kāmayate
tasya niyogaḥ na svargaḥ ātmānaṃ labheta iti</b> । asyārthaḥ । ātmārthameva yaḥ svargaṃ
kāmayate tasya niyogaḥ tena svārthameva puruṣo yāgena svargaṃ kuryāditi śāstrārthaḥ । tena
kāminaṃ prati phalasya śeṣatā । kutaḥ punaḥ svārthatā svargasyeti । ekadeśimatenottaramāha
---<b>ātmanepadaprayogāditi</b> । asyārthaḥ-yadā3 hi adhikāralakṣaṇasaṃbandhabalena svargaphalatā
karmaṇāmavagatā tadā ātmanepadaśravaṇāt kartṛgāmitā phalasyāvagamyata iti । paramasiddhāntī
dūṣayati---<b>nanu ca svargakāmaśabdādevedamavagamyate svargoṃ me bhavediti kimidaṃ ātmanepada-
prayogāditi । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ parasya duḥkha kāmayata ityapi kameḥ prayogāt anātma-
saṃbandhitvenāpi</b> kāmyamānasya prayogo dṛṣṭa iti । <b>tadayuk‍taṃ tatra paraśabdaprayogāt
duḥ khasya ca parasaṃbandhitvena abhīṣṭatvāt</b> । <b>yatra punaḥ paraśabdo na śrūyate nāpyaniṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ
tatra kenānyena saṃbandho'nyatra kāmayituḥ</b> sarvāhīcchā svakīyasukhaprāptiduḥ khaparihāra-
<note>(1) P. 661</note> <note>(2) P. 662</note> <note>(3) G. yathā</note>
﻿<pb n="r644"/>
viṣayaivotsargataḥ । paraśabdaprayogāt‍tu duḥ khasya ca svasaṃbandhitāyā aniṣṭatvena parasaṃbandhitayā
kāmyaviṣayā bhavati । tadabhāve kāmayitṛsaṃbandhikāmaviṣayaiveti icchāsvabhāvenaiva svārthatā
svargasya labhyate ।</p>
<p><b>atha manyase kāmyamānenaiva kāmaḥ saṃbadhyate svargo bhavatviti</b> । na puruṣaviśeṣa-
ṇatveneti2 । pariharati---na hi kāmyamātreṇaiva kāmasya saṃbandhaḥ <b>tannibandhanasukhāsmaraṇāt</b> ।
yannibandhanaṃ hi sukhaṃ smaryate tatra kāmanā bhavati । na ca sadbhāvamātreṇa sukhaṃ sukhaṃ bhavati api
tu svasaṃbandhitvena । kathaṃ punaḥ sukhahetubhāvenaiva kāmanetyāha---<b>na hi kasyacit 3sadbhāva-
mātre kasyacitkāmo bhavati</b> upekṣaṇīye heye ca kāmādarśanāt । adhunā ekadeśimataṃ
dūṣayitvā paramasiddhāntyevopasaṃharannāha---<b>tasmādātmanepadopanyāso liṅgatayā pratipattavyaḥ na
punaḥ prāpte pramāṇatayā</b> । yata eva svārthatā svargasya ata evātmanepadamapyupapadyata
iti ।</p>
<p><b>puruṣaśca karmārthatvāt । svargaścetpuruṣārthaḥ svargakāmapadavācyatayaiva yajamānasaṃmitā
audubaṃrī bhavati ityevamādiṣu kartuḥ śeṣatvaṃ, kathaṃ ? adhikṛtasya</b> niyuktasya <b>kartṛtvāt</b>
<note>(1) P. 662</note> <note>(2) G. viśeṣeṇāpīti</note> <note>(3) G. saṃbhava</note>
﻿<pb n="r645"/>
<b>kartuśca yajamānaśabdābhidheyatvāt</b> । tasmāt phalabhāgitayaiva karmaśeṣateti । <b>tasmāt
sūk‍taṃ sūtratrayaṃ jaimineḥ vṛttikāramatopanyāsaḥ</b> pūrvapakṣāparijñānārthaḥ । yadetat bhāṣyakāreṇa
vṛttikāramatamupanyastaṃ dravyaguṇasaṃskāraṇāmeva niyamena śeṣabhāvaḥ āpekṣiko yāgaphalapuruṣāṇāmiti
asau vṛttikārasya pūrvapakṣāparijñānapradarśanārthaḥ kriyāvākyārthābhiprāyeṇātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । na cātra
pūrvapakṣe yāgādīnāmāpekṣikamapi śeṣatvamasti iti । <b>kimiti kalpāntaraṃ na bhavati</b> । tatra prathama-
sūtreṇa dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣu svaśeṣāntaranirapekṣaṃ paraśeṣatvamucyate tacca bādarerapi matamiti bādareru-
dāharaṇaṃ jaiminerepyetatsammatameva3 । uttarasūtraistu yāgaphalapuruṣāṇāṃ śeṣāntarāpekṣāṇāṃ śeṣatvamucyate
ityevaṃparatayā sūtrāṇāṃ vyākhyānāntaramidamupanyasyate, tatra vṛttikāragrahaṇaṃ pūjārthamiti ।
uttaram---<b>nahyāpekṣikaṃ śeṣatvamasti</b> । yasmānnāpekṣikaṃ śeṣatvamasti tasmānnedaṃ kalpāntaraṃ
bhavatītyarthaḥ । <b>viniyojyanibandhaṃ hi tat</b> । yaddhi viniyojyaṃ taccheṣa ityetāvanmātreṇa
śeṣatvaṃ yasmāttasmānnāpekṣikaṃ śeṣatvam । viniyoga evāpekṣikaḥ tena viniyoganibandhanaṃ
śeṣatvamapyāpekṣikamiti cet; satyamāpekṣikaṃ yataḥ <b>śeṣaḥ viniyojyaṃ śeṣiṇaṃ cāpekṣate । na
punarekasya</b> śeṣaśeṣitāmāpādayati । na viniyogaḥ ekasya yāgasya svaśeṣāpekṣayā
śeṣitāmāpādayati śeṣyapekṣayā ca śeṣatāṃ, kintu śeṣyapekṣayā śeṣatāmeva kevalaṃ āpādavati ।
tasmānna svaśeṣāntarāpekṣaṃ kasyacidapi śeṣatvam । kiñca vrīhyādīnāmapi svaśeṣabhūtāvaghātādi-
sāpekṣatvamityapi śakyate vak‍tum । ato nirapekṣatvasāpekṣatvakṛto viśeṣo nāsti । tadāha
<note>(1) G. saṃbhava</note> <note>(2) R. pakṣa</note> <note>(3) G. asaṃmatameva</note>
﻿<pb n="r646"/>
---<b>vrīhyādīnāmapi svaśeṣāpekṣatayā tulyatvāt</b> । tasmāt parasya pūrvapakṣāparijñānena
<b>svakauśalapradarśanārthaṃ paramatamupanyastaṃ bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa</b> pūrvapakṣāparijñānaṃ tu parasya
spaṣṭatvānnopabṛṃhitamiti ।</p>
<p><b>teṣāmarthena saṃbandhaḥ</b> । pūrvapakṣamākṣipati---<b>uk‍taṃ niyogasavyapekṣāṇi śrutyādīni
viniyojakāni</b> ityādinā sandihyata ityayuk‍tamityevamantena । uk‍taṃ niyogasavyapekṣāṇi
śrutyādīni viniyojakānīti । śrutyādīni kāryabhūtaśeṣiṇo'napekṣamāṇāni santi niyogāpekṣāṇi
viniyojakānītyuk‍taṃ ādye । <b>śāstrāntaravihitasaṃbandhitayā ca kāryalābhaḥ</b> śāstrāntareṇa
yo vihitaḥ sa śeṣī tatsaṃbandhitayā ca kāryabhūtasya śeṣiṇo lābha <b>ityuk‍tam</b> । 2kasmātpunareva-
mityāha---<b>śāstrāntaravihitaṃ hi śeṣi bhavati na śeṣaśāstrādeva prādhānyamavagamyata iti
sak‍tuṣu pradarśitam</b> । kathaṃ tarhi <q>‘somena yajeta’</q> iti 3svaśāstrapramita eva yāgaḥ śeṣī ।
ucyate tatrāpi <q>‘jyotiṣṭomena yajeta’</q> iti śāstrāntareṇa yāvadyāgasyādhikārasaṃbandho nāvagamyate
tāvadviniyogo na sidhyatīti । <b>śās‍trāntaravihitāni ca vrīhyādīni</b> vrīhibhiryajeteti
<note>(1) P. 665</note> <note>(2) G. tasmāt</note> <note>(3) R. svavākya</note>
﻿<pb n="r647"/>
śāstrāntaravihitatvāt । <b>kathaṃ tatsaṃyuk‍teṣvavaghātādiṣu taccheṣatāṃ prati saṃśayaḥ</b> ? yadi
śāstrāntaravihitā vrīhyādayo na bhaveyuḥ tadā sak‍tunyāyena teṣāṃ śeṣitā na syāt tadā hi
kāryaśūnyaṃ hi <b>śeṣaśās‍traṃ kalpyaṃ kāryamapekṣate</b> । <b>pratyakṣaśrutakāryaṃ tu sandihyate ityayuktam</b> ।
ato nissandehatvannāsti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nacāpūrvaprayuktatayā dharmāṇāṃ tad‍rūpasya ca sarvatrābhedāt
satyapi vrīhyādīnāṃ śeṣitve pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । kāraṇāvāntaravyāpārabhutotpattiniyogabhedena anyathā'nyathā
karaṇatvādāgneyādīnāṃ pratikaraṇaṃ dharmāṇāṃ vyavasthopapatteḥ । samarthayate---<b>ucyate---niyogādanyat
viniyogagamyaṃ kāryamastīti na śakyate vak‍tum</b> । na vrīhyādisaṃskāro viniyogasya
parasparapadārthānvayasya kāryabhūto bhavitumarhati aniyogārthatvaprasaṅgāt niyogārthatvenaiva ca vyutpatteḥ ।
tasmāt vrīhinavahantītyādiṣvapi niyogaḥ kāryabhūtaḥ prayājādiṣviva । ataḥ prakaraṇaviniyo-
jyatayā sarvapradhānayāgārthateti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b><q>“nanu ca yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate”</q> ityatra
nāpūrvaṃ kāryamityuktam</b> । ataḥ kathamatrāpūrvaṃ kāryamāśaṅkyate । uttaraṃ---<b>satyamuk‍tam ।
sthite etasmin śeṣatve tat</b> etadadhikaraṇasiddhānte sthite tadityarthaḥ । <b>śeṣatvameva tvidānīṃ
niyoganiṣpattyā</b> vinā nāvagamyata ityākṣepaḥ । rāddhāntī codayati---<b>kimiti vā niyogo na
niṣpādyate vrīhīn prokṣatītyatrāpi</b> । vrīhisaṃskārotpattipraṇāḍyā niyogo niṣpadyata eveti
bhāvaḥ । pūrvapakṣī samādhatte---<b>yadyatra niyogārthaniṣpattiḥ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanena na</b>
﻿<pb n="r648"/>
<b>saṃbadhyeta</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi taṇḍulādinirvṛttidvāreṇa niyoganiṣpattyarthatvasiddhaye taṇḍulādi-
nirvṛttirapi kāryamāśrīyeta tadā darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanena na saṃbadhyeta kāryāntaradarśanāditi2
bhāvaḥ । <b>atha <q>‘phalavatsannidhau’</q> iti saṃbandhaḥ3</b> । nirākaroti---<b>sa tu niyogaikyalakṣaṇa
iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---darśapūrṇamāsādhikārasannidhau śrutāḥ prayājādiyāgāḥ tāda-
rthyena tadanvayina eva pratibhāsante kāryāntarasyādarśanāt । na ca tatra prathamameva kāryāntarabhūto
niyogaḥ pratīyata ityasakṛduk‍tam । <b>atrāpi cet sa eva saṃbandhaḥ</b> yo'sau kāryā-
ntaradarśanena niyogaikyalakṣaṇaḥ <b>na tarhi vrīhīn prokṣatītyetāvataiva niyogasiddhiḥ</b> ।
yadi sannipatyopakārakaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ syāt tadā vrīhisaṃbandhamātreṇaiva prokṣaṇasya niyogasiddhau
hetubhāvaḥ ityetāvataiva niyogasiddhiḥ syāt ityuk‍tam । ārādupakārakatve punaḥ na
vrīhisaṃbandhamātreṇaiva niyogasiddhau hetubhāvaḥ । api tu avāntarāpūrvaprasiddha‍yetyetāvati
na niyogasiddhirityuktam । yato'vāntarāpūrvasiddha‍yā <b>niyogasiddhiḥ, ataḥtuṣakaṇa-
vimoko na svargāvāptivat nāntarīyako niyogasya yathā svargāṃvāptiḥ</b> niyojya-
saṃbandhasiddhaye niyogenākṣipyamāṇā nāntarīyakī na tathā taṇḍalanirvṛttiḥ tannirapekṣasyaivā-
vadhātasyāpūrvasiddhidvāreṇādhikārānupraveśāt । ato nāsti dravyacikīrṣeti । yadi
prayājādivat <b>prakaraṇaviniyojyatayā pūrvaḥ pakṣa evaṃ tarhi ko'yamupanyāsaḥ <q>‘kiṃ sarve
ājye auṣadhe sānnāyye ca kartavyā’</q> iti । naiṣa hi padārthānāmājyādīnāṃ prādhānyamasmin
pakṣe</b> api tu yāgādīnām । tatrājyauṣadhasānnāyyarūpapadārthe'prādhānyopanyāso yukta iti ।
<note>(1) 665-1</note> <note>(2) G. kāryāntarādarśa</note> <note>(3) G. virodhaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r649"/>
<b>ucyate---naiva hi padārthānāṃ prādhānyapradarśanaparo'yaṃ granthaḥ kintu sarvayāgaśeṣatābhi-
prāyaparaḥ</b> ājyādiśabdena ājyādisādhanako yāgaḥ lakṣaṇayocyate ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe</b> sarveṣāṃ prayājādivat sākṣānniyogārthatvena śeṣatvaṃ pakṣe
<b>śeṣaśoṣitā</b> aṅgapradhānayoḥ prayājādyāgneyādyoḥ <b>nopapadyate</b> । <b>sarvaśeṣāṇāṃ svavākyo-
pāttaniyogārthaśeṣatvāt</b> । uttaram---<b>prakaraṇapramāṇanirūpaṇe asya codyasya parihāraṃ
vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । <b>iha tu kāryāntarāsaṃbhavāt pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । <b>darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanena1saṃbandhā</b>-
dityuk‍tam । yadi taṇḍulādikāryāntaramāśrīyeta tadā darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanena na saṃbadhyeta
svātantrayeṇaiva taṇḍulādeḥ kāryatvāt । prayājādikāryamavāntarāpūrvaṃ tu na svātantryeṇa
kāryatayā'vagamyate । kintu kṣaṇikānāṃ yāgānāmaṅgatvānupapatteḥ atrāvāntarāpūrvāṇyaṅgatva-
siddhaye kalpyamānāni na svātantrayeṇa pratīyante । <b>tasmāt prayājādīnāmiva</b> 2niyogo hyetallakṣaṇaḥ
sarvaiḥ <b>sarveṣāmabhisaṃbandhaḥ</b> । <b>kathaṃ tarhi vrīhin ājyamiti ca</b> dvitīyāvibhaktiḥ ।
<b>asmin pakṣe sak‍tuvadetadbhaviṣyati</b> iti । vibhak‍tivyatyayo bhavatītyarthaḥ । <b>gāṃ dadātīti-
vadvā</b> anīpsitakarmaṇi dvitīyetyarthaḥ । atra bhāṣyam---<q>“avadhātādayastu padārthāḥ śrutyā-
vidhīyante vākyenaiṣāṃ vrīhyādisaṃbandhaḥ”</q> iti tadasminneva pūrvapakṣe ghaṭate guṇakarmatvāṅgīkāreṇa
<note>(1) R. nāsaṃ</note> <note>(2) R. niyogābhedalakṣaṇaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r650"/>
tu pūrvapakṣe ghaṭate । siddhānte ca na śrutyaiva vidhānamiti darśayannāha---<b>ata idamuk‍taṃ
avaghātādayastu padārthāḥ śrutyā vidhīyanta iti</b> । <b>bhāvārthānāṃ śrutyā niyogasaṃbandha ityarthaḥ</b> ।
tenāyaṃ bhāṣyārthaḥ---vidhīyante, vidhinā saṃbadhyate iti । <q>“vākyenaiṣāṃ vrīhyādisaṃbandha”</q> iti
<b>bhāvārthānupraveśena vrīhyādīnāṃ niyogasaṃbandha ityarthaḥ</b> । etatkila bhāṣyaṃ avaghātādīnāṃ
vrīhyādisaṃbandhitā vākyeneti vadati । tadā ca vrīhyādiśeṣataivāvaghātāderiti idamāpadyata
iti matvā vyākhyātam । eṣāmavadhātādīnāṃ śeṣitayā vākyenaiva vrīhyādisaṃbandha iti
bhāṣyākṣarārthaḥ <b>na tu pradhānabhūtānāṃ</b> vrīhyādīnāṃ niyogasiddhirityarthaḥ । kutaḥ ? <b>na hi dravya-
paryanto niyogaḥ svayameva sādhyatvāt</b> । na hi dvayamekasmin vākye sādhyaṃ bhavati eka-
vākyatvāvagamavirodhāt । na ca svargavat vrīhayo'pi sādhyatvena saṃbandhamarhanti parasparānanu-
guṇatvāt । na hi te niyojyaviśeṣaṇatvenānvitāḥ । na ca dvitīyāvagatasādhyatvānugrahāya
niyojyaviśeṣaṇatā kalpayitumapi śakyā । dvitīyānirdeśādeva kriyājanyaphalabhāgitvena
aniyogaphalatvāt । yasya hi niyojyaviśeṣaṇasya sataḥ sādhyatvamiṣyate na tasya kriyā-
phalatvaṃ kriyāphalatve tatkāmasya niyogena saṃbandhānupapatteḥ । yadi hi niyogaḥ tasya nimittaṃ bhavet
tadā tatkāminaḥ tatkāmitayaiva niyogasaṃbandhaḥ syāt । anyathā avivakṣitatatkāmasaṃbandho
dravyamātratayaiva saṃbadhyeta niyogaphalatve ca kriyāphalatvānupapattiḥ । yadeva hi kriyāto vyavadhānāna-
pekṣaṃ sākṣānniṣpadyate tadeva kriyāphalaṃ kārakasamavāyiphalatvāt kriyāṇām । etenādhānasya
agnyarthanā niyogaviṣayatā ceti pratyuktam । kathaṃ tarhi āśrayiṣu dravyasaṃskāro'pi vivakṣitaḥ
pratyakṣadṛṣṭatvāt na tu kriyāphalatvāditi । <b>tasmāt sūk‍taṃ sarve sarvārthā</b> iti prayājādivat 
<note>(1) P. 665-9</note> <note>(2) R. svayamasā</note>
﻿<pb n="r651"/>
prakaraṇaniyojyatayā । <b>kimidamadṛṣṭaṃ bhavatīti</b> । idaṃ hi bhāṣyaṃ dravyaniṣṭhatvena adṛṣṭa-
upakāro bhaviṣyati iti idamāheti manyate । uttaraṃ---<b>adṛṣṭamapūrvaṃ niyoga ityekamida-
mityuk‍taṃ tena<q>‘apūrvaṃ kṛtvā’</q> ityatra</b> । ayamatra pūrvapakṣasaṃkṣepaḥ---tuṣakaṇavimuk‍teḥ adhikāra-
nirapekṣāyā api sādhyatvasaṃbhavāt tādarthye satyavaghātādīnāṃ adhikārānupraveśāsaṃbhavāt
tadanupraveśasiddha‍yarthaṃ varaṃ prayājāditulyataivāśrīyatām । prayājādyavāntarāpūrvaṃ hi adhikārāpekṣameva
kāryamiti tādarthye yukta evādhikārānupraveśa iti ।</p>
<p><b>phalaṃ tu saha ceṣṭayā śabdārtho'bhāvādviprayoge syāt</b> । <b>atrocyate---syāt sarvārthatā
yadi 1kāryārthe virodho niyogasya syāt</b> । <b>natvatra virodho vidyate</b> । <b>kathaṃ na vidyate
virodhaḥ</b> ? <b>kathaṃ vā vidyate virodhaḥ ?</b> <b>uktaṃ kāryāntaratvāt‍tuṣakaṇavipramokasyeti । na
kāryaṃ kāryāntareṇa saṃbadhyate yathā svargaḥ paśubhiḥ</b> । <b>evaṃ niyogaḥ kāryaṃ tuṣakaṇavipramo-
kaśceti vipratiṣiddham ।</b> uttaramāha---<b>anabhijño bhavān viṣayaniyojyānāmityuktam</b> ।
idamatrākūtam । dravyaṃ tāvat avadhātādiṣu dvitīyāsaṃyogena sādhyatayā pratīyate । na ca
yasya sādhyāntaramasti tasya niyogaviṣayatā, parasparānanuguṇasādhyadvayayogena ekavākyatvānupapatteḥ ।
<note>(1) G. kāryavirodho</note>
﻿<pb n="r652"/>
na ca tadeva niyojyaviśeṣaṇamityānuguṇyaṃ vācyam । akārakabhūtapadārthaviśiṣṭasya
niyojyatvāt । kā punaryuktiḥ akārakabhūtapadārthaviśiṣṭasya niyojyatve iti । ucyate ।
yatkhalu kriyāsambandhi tatkārakam । tacca dvividham kiñcitkriyāsādhyaṃ kiñcicca na, tatra
yatpūrvaṃ tatkarma dvitīyaṃ karaṇādikaṃ taccobhayamapi na niyojyaviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati । ubhayathā hi
viśeṣaṇatā svarūpasaṃbandhitayā kāmanāviṣayatayā vā, tatra na tāvat svarūpasaṃbandhitayā,
niyoganiyojyalakṣaṇasambandhātprāgasiddheḥ । na ca kāmanāviṣayatvena karaṇādi 2siddha‍yati ।
kiyājanyāpūrvasādhyatvānupapatteḥ । karaṇādīni karma ca kriyā'sādhyatayaiva na niyojya-
viśeṣaṇaṃ, niyogasādhyaṃ hi kāmyamānatayā niyojyaṃ viśinaṣṭi nānyam[ta] । tasmāt guṇakarmaṇāṃ
niyogaviṣayatvaṃ yo bravīti saḥ viṣayasvarūpaṃ niyojyasvarūpaṃ ca na jānatīti । idameva
vivarītumupakramamāṇaḥ pṛcchati---<b>kathamanabhijña iti</b> । uttaram---<b>itthamanabhijñaḥ</b> । <b>viṣayo hi nāma
2adhikārasaṃbandhī svargakāmo yajeteti</b> । yo hyadhikārasaṃbandhayomyaḥ sa viṣayaḥ । sa eva
cādhikārasaṃbandhayomyaḥ yatra niyogaḥ sādhyabhūtaḥ pratīyate । tathāpi kiṃ ? ityāha---<b>tasya ca
viṣayasya niyogasiddhireva prayojanaṃ dṛṣṭe'rthe saṃbhavatyapi yathā godohanena paśukāmasya
praṇayediti</b> । sādhyadvayasyaikatrānvayavirodhāt sādhyāntarasyānanupraveśāt । nanvatnāpi sādhyāntaraṃ
paśavaḥ ityāha---<b>nanu ca atrāpi phalasiddhiḥ</b> prayojanaṃ na niyogasiddhiḥ uttaraṃ---<b>niyoga
siddha‍yarthā phalasiddhiriti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> tenātnāpi niyogasiddhireva prayojanam । yata
eva ca niyogasidhyarthā phalasiddhiḥ, <b>ata eva ca karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) kāmādhikāra bṛ. bhā. (2) G. sādhyaṃ (3) G. adhikārapadasaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r653"/>
<p>etaduk‍taṃ bhavati-sādhyabhūto vidhyarthaḥ pratīyate sa ca viṣayasiddha‍yā siddha‍yati । sa eva
ca viṣayānuṣṭhāne pravartate yo vidhyarthaṃ svasaṃbandhitayā sādhvabhūtamavabudhyate । na cākāmasādhane
niyoge kāmī kāmitayaiva <q>‘mamedaṃ kāryaṃ’</q> iti boda‍dhṛtayā'nvayamarhati iti svasiddhihetubhūta-
viṣayasaṃpādanasamarthapuruṣalābhāya phalotpattau nimittabhāvamavalambate svayameva 2vidhyartha iti
niyogasidhyarthā phalasiddhiḥ । ato na phalaṃ nāma pṛthak prayojanāntaramiti । <b>niyojyaḥ
idānīṃ kaḥ</b> ? <b>akārakabhūtapadārthaviśiṣṭa iti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । idaṃ prāgeva varṇitam---karturanyo
niyojyo na bhavati kartā ca kārakabhūtapadārthaviśiṣṭo'pi syādityabhiprāyavān pṛcchati
---<b>kaḥ punarasau</b> ? <b>iti</b> । <b>uttaraṃ---vakṣyamāṇanyāyabalena adhikṛtaḥ karmaṇi</b> iti
īśvarabhūtaḥ karmaṇītyarthaḥ । punarapi tenaivābhiprāyeṇākṣepagarmaṃ pṛcchati---<b>kimidaṃ adhikṛta iti</b> ।
ekagranthenāha---<b>nanu ca kartaivādhikṛtaḥ nāparo'dhikṛto nāmeti</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>yathā na
karturadhikāraḥ</b> । <b>adhikṛtasya kartṛtvaṃ ityetadapi ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । <b>yadyevaṃ</b> bhavetāṃ nāme-
dṛśau viṣayaniyojyau tathāpi <b>kimāyātaṃ <q>“vrīhīn prokṣati”</q> ityatra ।</b> uttaram---<b>kāryāntare'pi
dravyagate saṃskāre sati 3niyogāvirodha itīdamāyātam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) niyogāsiddhireva</note> <note>(2) G. sidhyarthaḥ</note> <note>(3) G. niyogavirodhaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r654"/>
<p>ayamāśayaḥ । yadi yasyāpi kāryāntaramasti tasyāpi viṣayatā syāt tadā dravyagata-
kāryāvagame'pi niyogasya svavākya eva śrutatvāt paravākyagataniyogānupraveśābhāvāt
tadasaṃsparśe vrīhyādigataṃ kāryaṃ tadananuguṇamiti kāryadvayavirodhaḥ syāt । yathok‍te tu
viṣayalakṣaṇe sādhyāntaradarśanena viṣayatvābhāvāt nirviṣayatvācca liṅgādeḥ niyogajñānānupapatteḥ
svavākye niyogābhāvāt niyogasaṃbandhasidhyarthaṃ vākyāntaragataniyogānupraveśāya tatsaṃbandhāvastha-
vrīhyādisaṃskāraḥ tadapekṣita evāyaṃ pratīyata iti tatkāryānupraveśāt kāryāntaramapīdaṃ na
virodhamāvahati । yathoktaniyojyalakṣaṇābhāve tu yathoktaviṣayalakṣaṇameva na bhavati । ekasminnapi
vākye niyojyaviśeṣaṇatayā kriyāphalasyāpyanvayopapatteriti yathoktaniyojyalakṣaṇasyāpyastye-
vopayogaḥ । kutaḥ punaḥ paravākyagataniyogānupraveśa ityatrāha---<b>vrīhīna‍prīkṣatīti pradhānabhūta-
viṣayārthavrīhisaṃsparśāt niyogasya ca niyogāntarāvagatiḥ</b> kāryāṃśe <b>samidādīnāmiva</b>
prokṣaṇaṃ prati pradhānabhūta1viṣayārthā ye vrīhayaḥ tanniyogārthaṃ saṃspṛśati । ato vrīhidvāreṇa niyo-
gānupraveśasaṃbhavāt na niyogāntaraṃ <b>svavākyagatamavagamyate yathākāryāṃśe adhikārāśe
samidādīnām</b> ।</p>
<p>abhiprāyaṃ vivarītuṃ codyapūrvakamāha---<b>nanu ca kāryāntaramityuktam</b> । <b>kāryāntaratve
ca niyogāntarāvagatiḥ someṣṭīnāmiva</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>satyam 1yadi kāryāntarāvagatiḥ
syāt</b> । <b>kathaṃ na kāryāntaraṃ adhikāraniyogākṣepāt taṇḍulanippatteḥ svargasiddhivat
na kāryāntaram</b> । yathā niyogākṣitā svargasiddhiḥ na kāryāntaraṃ tathā taṇḍulaniṣpattirapi ।
<note>(1) G. vidhyarthā</note> <note>(2) G. yadi kāryāntaraṃsyāt tadā niyogāntarāvapatiḥ
syāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r655"/>
<b>tasmādadhikāraniyoga evāyaṃ</b> sādhyo vrīhisaṃskāradvāreṇa <b>vrīhīn prokṣatīti, prayājādī-
nāmiva</b> । prayājādibhiḥ <b>iyān viśeṣaḥ</b> । <b>dṛṣṭakāryadvārakastvayam</b> । <b>sākṣānniyogakārya
eva prayājādiḥ</b> । prathamaṃ niradhikāratayā sādhikāraniyogakāryatayā pratīyate prayājādiḥ ।
paścāttu svagatakāryavimarśastatretyuktam । evaṃ kāryāntarepi nāsti virodha ityuktam ।
saṃprati kāryāntaraṃ vinā'nupraveśānupapatteḥ avaśyamaṅgīkaraṇīyaṃ kāryāntaramityāha---<b>na ca
dvārameva pratiyandhakaṃ bhavitumarhati viśeṣato dṛṣṭasākṣānniyogasaṃbandhināmapi dvāraṃ</b>
karaṇopakāralakṣaṇaṃ kalpyam । idaṃ tu <b>1klṛptamiti viśeṣaḥ</b> । <b>yayā ca dvārakalpanā-
mantareṇa pradhānetikartavyatāsiddhirna bhavati tathā prakaraṇapramāṇa</b>svarūpanirūpaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ ।
anenedamuktam । prayājāditulyatvepi dvārasyāvaśyakalpyatvāt kimiti dṛṣṭadvāraṃ parityajyata
iti । <b>tadidamuktam---pramāṇābhāvānna sarvārthateti</b> । <b>na hi dṛṣṭe saṃbhavati saṃbandhahetau
kalpyaṃ hetvantaramātmānaṃ labhata ityarthaḥ</b> । <b>nanu ca biniyogataḥkāryaṃ na kāryato viniyoga
iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---viniyoga<b>pekṣayā kāryaṃ na punaḥ</b> kāryāpekṣo viniyoḥ iti viniyogānusāreṇa
vrīhimātrasaṃskāra evāyaṃ pratīyate । anyathā hi vrīhiśabdasya apūrvasādhanāṅgalakṣaṇāparatvaṃ
syāt । ataḥ kathaṃ kāryāntarānupraveśa iti ।</p>
<note>(1) G. dṛṣṭamiti</note>
﻿<pb n="r656"/>
<p>uttaram---<b>parihṛtametat-śāstrāntaradṛṣṭaviṣayatvāditi</b> । śāstrāntareṇa yo dṛṣṭaḥ
kāryasaṃbandhitayā sa viniyogasya viṣayaḥ tasminnaparaṃ viniyujyana <b>ityanena idaṃ parihṛtam</b> ।
yathā svatantradravyaṃ śeṣi na bhavati iti । yata eva śāstrāntarapratītaṃ śeṣi bhavati
<b>ata eva ca bhedābhedalakṣaṇaṃ heturiti</b> । etacca vyākhyātam । <b>tasmātsūktaṃ phalaṃ tu saha
ceṣṭayeti</b> । dṛṣṭamātreṇa kāryasya svīkāra iti sūtre pratīyate taccānupapannamiti matvā vyācaṣṭe
---<b>kāryānurodhī niyoga ityarthaḥ</b> । avāntarakāryamapi niyogo'nurudhyate apekṣata ityaryaḥ ।
<b>ato ye yatra śrūyante iti siddham</b> । ataḥ sūktaṃ phalaṃ tu tatraiva kartavyeti ।</p>
<p><b>dravyaṃ cotpattisaṃyogāt</b> । atra bhāṣyakāreṇa sandehaḥ kṛtaḥ---kiṃ yo yaḥ śakyate
ebhiḥ kartuṃ tasmai tasmai prayojanāya ita yat <b>yena saṃyuktaṃ tasmā eveti</b> । tatra kāraṇabhūtasandehamāha---
<b>idaṃ cintyate---sphyaśca</b> kapālāni <b>ceti sannidhāpanavidhayaḥ saṃyogato'viśeṣāt</b> । <b>prakara-
ṇāviśeṣācceti kiṃ sarvārthatayā'vagamyante uta sphyenoddhantītyevamādibhirupasaṃhriyanta
iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---ye'mī sannidhāpanavidhayaḥ niyogasaṃbandhamātravidhayaḥ te kimupasaṃhriyante atha
vā anupasaṃhriyamāṇāḥ svayameva sarvatra kārye viniyujyante iti । <b>kiṃ tāvad‍yuktam</b> ।
<b>nopasaṃhriyante iti । kutaḥ ?</b> । <b>aśak‍teḥ</b> upasaṃhārāśak‍teḥ । kathamaśaktiḥ ? uttaraṃ---
﻿<pb n="r657"/>
<b>sannidhāne hi sati niyogaikyāt dvāramātrānujñānācca dṛṣṭadvārakatvameva śakyate vak‍tum</b> ।
<b>kalpyapratipakṣatvāt na punaḥ dṛṣṭaviśeṣadvāramapi</b> । asyārthaḥ---sannidhāpanavidhibalena tāvat
ete sphyādayaḥ kāryaviśeṣanirapekṣā eva niyogārthā avagamyante । tatra kena dvāreṇetyapekṣāyāṃ
dṛṣṭameva dvāraṃ niyogā'numanyate nādṛṣṭam । na punaḥ dṛṣṭatve'pi dvāraviśeṣam । niyogānanumataṃ
ca na śāstrārtha iti । <b>tasmācchaktito vyavasthā</b> । atrābhidhīyate---<b>syādetadevaṃ yadi
dvāramātramevānurudhyate niyogena</b> । kasmātpunarnaivamityāha---<b>saṃbandhānusārī hi niyogaḥ</b>
yadi saṃbandhaṃ niyogo nānurudhyate niyogāsaṃbandhamapi yadi dvāraṃ syāt tadā dvāramātrameva niyoge-
nānurudhyeta saṃbandhānusārī tu niyogaḥ । <b>uk‍taṃ śāstrāntaravihiṛ/?/taviṣayatvāt (vi)niyoga-
śās‍trasyeti</b> । yo hi śāstrāntareṇa niyogena saṃbandhīkriyate tadviṣayo niyogaḥ nānyaviṣaya
iti saṃbandhānusārī niyogaḥ । nanvevamapi mābhūdasaṃbandhe viniyogaḥ saṃbandhe tu sarvatra viniyomaḥ
syāt ityatrāha---<b>ata sannidhāpanavidhayo na saṃbandhavidheḥ pratipakṣā bhavitumarhanti tanmū-
latvāt</b> । saṃbandhavidhinā hi saṃbandhe śeṣiṇaḥ āpādite paścāt sannidhāpanavidhibhiḥ
viniyogaḥ । <b>ataḥ siddhamatrāpi ye yatra śrūyanta iti</b> । yathā śeṣiṇaḥ sannidhānāpādakasya
saṃbandhavidheḥ sannidhāpanavidhiḥ na pratipakṣaḥ tathā sphyenoddhantītyasyāpi na pratipakṣo bhavitumarhati
aviśeṣāditi siddhā atrāpi vyavasthā na kevalamavaghātādīnāmiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r658"/>
<p><b>arthaikatve</b> । <b>saṃskāradravyavidhayo ye yatra śrūyante te tatraivetyuktam</b> । <b>guṇe idānīṃ
cintyate</b> । <b>kiṃ ye yatra śrūyante tatraiva uta kṛts‍ne prakaraṇe niveśa iti</b> । anenāvāntara---
saṅgatimāha । saṃskārāṇāṃ śrutyā viniyoga uktaḥ । tadanantaraṃ ca vākyena dravyāṇāṃ
viniyoga uktaḥ dravyaviniyoganirvāhyaśca guṇaviniyoga iti sa tadanantaraṃ cintyate । pūrvapakṣābhāva-
saṃśayaṃ ācikṣipsurāha---<b>nanu cānvitapadārthatvāt padānāṃ naiva kevalaṃ guṇavacanatā
saṃbhavati</b> । anvitāḥ padārthāḥ padaiḥ abhidhīyante । tena dravyānvitā eva guṇā
guṇapadairabhidhīyante tathābhūtāśca śak‍nuvantyeva kriyāsādhanatāmupagantumiti bhāvaḥ । dṛṣṭānta-
gāha---<b>yathā na kevalākṛtivacanatā ālabheta iti</b> । <b>yathā ca vāyavyaṃ ś‍vetamālabheta iti
na kevalaguṇavacanatā śakyate vak‍tuṃ</b>, anyathā tadapyatrodāharaṇaṃ syāt । pariharati---<b>satyaṃ
aparityaktadravyasyaivānvayo yatra dṛśyate amūrtasya naiṣa tadudāharaṇam</b> । <b>yatra punaḥ parityakta-
dravyābhiprāye kevalaguṇavacanasyānvayaḥ yathā paṭasya śula iti bhavati tatra saṃśayaḥ
kārakavibhak‍tau satyāmapi kiṃ kriyānvayī guṇavacanaḥ uta kevaladravyānvayyeveti</b> ।
<note>(1) P. 673</note>
﻿<pb n="r659"/>
ayamevātra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ ekavākyatayā kraya evāruṇimā viniyujyate uta vākyaṃ bhitvā prakaraṇa-
viniviṣṭeṣu dravyeṣu vidhīyata iti ।</p>
<p><b>nanu ca kevalaguṇavacanatā'sya asmin vākye naiva pratīyate</b> । <b>tatra hi paṭasya
śukla iti ṣaṣṭīnirdiṣṭatvāt dravyasya tatsaṃbandhāvagateśca śuklaśabdasya yuktaṃ kevalaguṇa-
vacanasyānvayitvam</b> । yadi hi dravyasya saṃbandhaḥ śuklaśabdasya na syāt tadā na syāt
kevalaguṇānvayitā । dravyasaṃbandhetu dravyāntarasya dravyāntarasaṃbandhābhāvāt kevalaguṇānvayitā ।
<b>iha punaḥ aruṇayā iti kārakanirdeśāt kriyāsaṃbandhāvagatiḥ na dravyasaṃbandhāvagatiriti na</b>
kevalaguṇānvayitvam । yuktyantaraṃ cāha---<b>tadavagateśca</b> kriyāsaṃbandhāvagateśca <b>guṇamātrasyāpi</b>
kriyānuṣṭhānāśak‍teḥ । <b>aparityaktadravyasyaivānvayo yuktaḥ ś‍vetamālabheta itivat</b> । pari-
harati---<b>ucyate</b> । <b>na dravyasaṃbandhāvagatireva tatra kevalaguṇavacanatve hetuḥ</b> । kastarhi ?
<b>dravyāntarānavagatirapi</b> hetuḥ । yadi hi dravyāntaramapi tatrāvagamyate tadā na syāt
kevalaguṇavacanatā paṭasya śuklo bhāga itivat । tenopātta1dravyavat dravyāntarānupādānamapi
kevalaguṇavacanatve hetuḥ । kathaṃ punaratra dravyāntarāvagatirnāsti atrāha---<b>dravyāntarāvagatau hi
paṭasya śuklo bhāgaḥ itivat guṇaguṇinoḥ saṃbandho na syāt । yadyevaṃ kimāyātaṃ aruṇayeti</b>
<note>(1) R. dravyatvavat</note>
﻿<pb n="r660"/>
<b>idamāyātam</b> । <b>atrāpi hi ekahāyanyā na dravyāntaraṃ pratīyate</b> । ekavākyatve sati
ekahāyanyavaruddhe kraye dravyāntarānupraveśābhāvāt । <b>ataḥ ekahāyanīśabdopāttatvāt dravyasya
na aruṇāśabdaḥ dravyāntaropaniviṣṭaṃ guṇamabhidhātuṃ śak‍noti</b> । <b>ekahāyanyupaniveśe ca na
krayasaṃbandha ityupariṣṭāt pradarśyate</b> । <b>ataḥ padāntaropāttadravyake vākye kevalaguṇānvayi-
taiveti sthitam</b> । <b>ata upapadyate saṃśayaḥ</b> । yasmādupapadyate saṃśayaḥ kiṃ <b>vākyaṃ bhitvā
prakaraṇe niveśaḥ guṇasya dravyayogitvāt</b> kiṃ prakaraṇaniviṣṭeṣu dravyeṣu niveśaḥ
uta karaṇavibhaktinirdeśāt krayaṇa eveti । atra bhāṣyam । <b><q>“nanu naivāyaṃ guṇavacana1”</q></b>
iti । tadākṣipati---<b>kathamiti</b> । evaṃ bhāṣyok‍tena nyāyena guṇānvayavyatirekānuvidhāna---

ityākṣepaḥ kathamupapadyate</b> । <b>ucyate</b> । <b>s‍trīliṅganirdeśāt dravyāśritatvācca</b> s‍trīliṅgasya na

tvācca liṅgasya</b> । striyāṃ yatpratipadikaṃ vartate tatra s‍trīpratyaya iti prātipadikārthagatameva

﻿<pb n="r661"/>

kevalaguṇavacanatvāt 1kathaṃ dravyasaṃbandhāśaṅketi । samādhatte---ayamabhiprāyaḥ । <b>yadā dvayoḥ

dvalīyaḥ</b> । tena nāsti dravyasaṃbandha iti । vākyālliṅgaṃ balīya ityākṣipati---<b>kimidaṃ

<p><b>atrocyate । yadi tṛtīyārthaḥ prātipadikārtha</b>syāruṇimno <b>dravyānvayavirodhī

ityādibhāṣyaṃ <q>‘nāsti vākyabhedaḥ’</q> ityantaṃ vyāvarṇitam । <b>bhavedetadevaṃ yadyekahāyanī nānyārthā

<b>saṃbandhāt krayārthatā iti</b> । pṛṣṭe tṛtīyābalenaiva uttare datte punaranyārthasyāpyanyena

pūrayituṃ sannidhānāviśeṣāt</b> । tena sākāṅkṣasyāruṇyasya āśrayākāṅkṣāṃ ekahāyanī pūrayet ।

<p><b>arthaikatve</b> । atrābhidhīyate---<b>kraya evāruṇimā niviśate । kathaṃ ? tatsaṃbandhapratīteḥ

﻿<pb n="r667"/>
<b>tasya tathāvidhasyaiva vibhaktayaḥ saṃbandhamāpādayanti । dravyaviśeṣaṇatvena ca guṇaḥ
kriyāṃ niṣpādayati aviśiṣṭasya kāraṇatvānupapatteḥ । atredamākṛtam</b> । krayasaṃbandhā-
dāruṇyasya tatraiva viniyogaḥ krayasādhanatā ca tasya saṃbhavati dravyaviśeṣaṇatvenāruṇyaviniyogāt ।
taddhi evaṃ vidhīyate yatrāruṇyaṃ samavetaṃ tena krayaḥ kartavyaḥ iti । na ca tasyopādānamāruṇyenā-
viśiṣṭasya saṃbhavati । na cānupāttena kriyā nirvartyata ityasti kriyāsādhanabhāvaḥ āruṇyasyeṃti

paṭasya śukla itivadityuka‍tam । ataḥ</b> sādhanabhāvo nāstītyuktam---<b>tatsatyamuktam । na

sarveṣāṃ sādhanānāṃ vilakṣaṇo vyāpāra iti । <b>na cānupāttadravyatayā vyāpārahāniḥ</b> vyāpāra
eva nāstīti <b>śakyate vak‍tum</b> ।</p>
<p>nanu ca dravyasādhanake karmaṇi kathaṃ guṇasya sādhanatetyāśaṅkyāha---<b>svavyāpārāpekṣāṇi

'bhidhānasya</b> । yadyapyabhidhānamarthāntaramupādatte jahāti vā tathāpi sādhanabhāvo na virudhyata
﻿<pb n="r668"/>
iti । upasaṃharati---<b>tasmādbhinnavyāpārakatvāta2 ekahāyanīdvāraka eva krayasaṃbandha upapannaḥ</b> ।
yata eva dravyadvāreṇa viniyogaḥ <b>ata eva na vikalpaḥ prayojanavada‍dravyasaṃbandhārthaṃ kriyā-
prādhānyaṃ</b> prayojanavatā dravyāntareṇa somākhyena saṃbandho yathā syādityevamarthaṃmaruṇaikahāyanya-
pekṣaṃ kriyāprādhānyamuktam । <b>tatprādhānye tu na3 pratyekaṃ vākyaparisamāptiḥ</b> । na hi
guṇaṃ prati pradhānamupadiśyate kintu pradhānameva prati guṇa iti na pratiguṇaṃ vākyabhedaḥ ।
<b>tasmādekavākyatvāt siddhaṃ dravyaguṇayoraikakarmyānniyata iti</b> ।</p>
<p><b>ekatvayuk‍tamekasya śrutisaṃyogāt</b> । nanu asaṅgataiveyaṃ cintā । nātraikatvasya
śrutinibandhano viniyoga āśaṅkyata ityāśaṅkyāha---<b>ukto dravyaguṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ
idānīṃ 4viniyojyaviṣayagatā cintā kriyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---dravyādiviniyoge cintite
tasyaiva viniyogasya viśeṣa cintayituṃ viniyojyasya yo viṣayaḥ śeṣī tadgatā cintā kriyate-kiṃ
vivakṣitasaṅkhyākaśeṣiparyanto viniyogaḥ uta neti । tenādhyāyasaṅgatiravāntarasaṅgatiścāsti ।
kutaḥ punariyaṃ cintetyatra āha---<b>evaṃ hi śrūyate <q>‘grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭi’</q> iti</b> । ekatvaśravaṇāt
<note>(1) P. 699</note> <note>(2) R. dvārakatvāt</note> <note>(3) G. omiss na</note> <note>(4) G. R.
viniyojyaviyaṣā</note>
﻿<pb n="r669"/>
saṃśayaḥ । kīdṛśaḥ saṃśaya ityatrāha---<b>atra saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ śeṣiṇo viśeṣaṇameka</b>tvādi <b>śeṣitve1
ādriyate śeṣasyeva paścādeḥ śeṣatve uta nādriyata</b> iti । <b>kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayaḥ</b> ?
praṣṭā svābhiprāyeṇa ekagranthenāha---<b>yuk‍taṃ tāvat</b> śeṣa iti cchedaḥ । kathaṃ yuk‍taṃ ? <b>upādīya-
mānatvāccheṣasya tadupayogi</b> upādānopayogi viśeṣaṇaṃ, anavacchinnasya upādānāśak‍teḥ ।
<b>śeṣiṇaḥ punaḥ kāryāntare</b> homādau <b>nirjñātayāgaśeṣabhāvasyaiva svaśeṣayogo yuktaḥ</b> । śāstrā-
ntaravihitatvāccheṣiṇa <b>iti na saṃśayaṃ paśyāmaḥ</b> । kāryāntare nirjñātopādānāśśeṣiṇaḥ nopādeyā
iti tadīyaviśeṣaṇānāmapyanapekṣitatvāt ādarāśaṅkaiva na yuk‍teti । evaṃ pūrvapakṣamākṣipya
samarthayamāna āha---<b>ucyate । śrutitaḥ sarvaṃ kalpate</b> vivakṣitatvaṃ avivakṣitatvaṃ ityādi
<b>nopādeyatvāt paśorekatvaṃ</b> vivakṣitam । <b>kiṃ tarhi ? śruteḥ । śrutiścennādriyate dvitvaṃ
bahutvaṃ vā kimityavacchedakatvena nopādīyate</b> । nāṅgīkriyate । <b>ataḥ śeṣiṇyapi yathā
brahaśrutirādriyate evamekatvaśrutirādriyatām, aviśeṣāt । tadidamuk‍taṃ ekatvayukta-
mekasya śrutisamyogāt</b> । yat‍tūk‍tamapekṣā nāstīti tadayuktam । śrutibalenaivāpekṣā
bhavatīti kalpyatāṃ rak‍tapaṭavat । yata eva śrutimātreṇa svīkāraḥ saṅkhyāyāḥ nopādeyatvamapekṣate,
<note>(1) G. ādīyate</note>
﻿<pb n="r670"/>
<b>ata eva <q>‘‘agnīnādadhīta”</q> iti śruteḥ agnīnāṃ bahutvamādhāne sidhyati । <q>“yūpaṃ
chinatti”</q> iti caikatvaṃ</b> yūpe sidhyati ।</p>
<p>sarveṣāṃ vā lakṣaṇatvādaviśiṣṭaṃ hi lakṣaṇam । atrocyate---<b>naitadevam yadekasya saṃskāra
iti । saṃskāro nāma vyāpārāntarayogyatā । yasya saṃskāro vyāpārāntarayogyatālakṣaṇaḥ
saṃbhavati sa eva saṃbandhitāṃ</b> saṃskāraṃ prati śeṣitāṃ <b>pratipadyate</b>। yasya punaḥ vyāpārāntara-
yogyatālakṣaṇasaṃskāro na bhavati vyāpārāntarābhāvāt sa saṃskārārhona bhavati । tacchabdena
pulliṅgāntena vyāpārāntarānavamarśādevaṃ vyākhyātam । etenedamuktam---grahamātrasyaiva vyāpārā-
ntarayogāt tāvanmātrasyaiva saṃskāra iti । etadeva codyapūrvakamāviṣkartumāha---<b>nanu ca
sasaṅkhyāka eva vyāpārāntarayogyaḥ saṃskāreṇāyaṃ kriyate</b> । saṅkhyāyā vyāpārāntara-
yogo nāstītyanenābhiprāyeṇa pṛcchati---<b>kuta iti</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>vyāpārāntaraṃ upādāna-
śeṣatvāt saṅkhyāyā liṅgasya ca</b> । <b>yathābhūtaścāsau</b> vivakṣitaliṅgasaṅkhyākaḥ svavyāpāre
<b>śeṣabhūtaḥ tathābhūtasyaiva saṃskāre saṃbandhaḥ kāryārthatvāt</b> saṃskārasya । <b>aindravāyavādiṣu</b>
﻿<pb n="r671"/>
<b>vākyeṣu caikasaṅkhayāyuktā eva grahāḥ śeṣatvena śrūyante । ataḥ</b> kāryayogitvādekatvasya
saṃskārārhatvāda<b>vivakṣitamekatvamityayuktam । na ca grahamātraṃ śeṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ । na
cedamāśaṅkanīyam yāvanto grahāḥ tāvanto militā eva kāryāntaraśeṣabhūtā iti yena sarveṣu
militeṣveva saṃskāraḥ syāt । kutaḥ ? <b>ekaikasya viniyogāt । nanu ca viniyuktasya
grahasyopādānaśeṣatvaṃ saṅkhyādayaḥ pratipadyante yathā śeṣabhāve prādhānyaṃ tathā śoṣibhāve'pi</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---ubhayasaṃmataṃ tābat viniyuktasya grahasyopādānaśeṣabhūtāḥ saṅkhyādaya iti yathā
śeṣatvāvasthāyāṃ upādīyamānāvasthā(yāṃ)śrayaṇena grahasya saṅkhyādīn prati prādhānyaṃ tathā
śoṣibhāvepi saṃskārayogepi prādhānyamiti syāt । upādīyamānatayaiva saṅkhyādīn prati
prādhānyaṃ syādityarthaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>bhavatu prādhānyaṃ na kaścidvirodhaḥ saṅkhyādyaparityāgena tu
yathaiva śeṣatāṃ pratipadyate tathā saṃskāryatāmiti vadāmaḥ</b> । saṃskāraṃ pratyupādīyamānatayā
bhavatu anyathā ceti na kaścidasmākaṃ virodhaḥ । rāddhāntī pariharati---<b>atrocyate । satyaṃ śeṣa-
bhūtasyaiva saṃskāraḥ tathāpi saṅkhyādayo na saṃbadhyante</b> saṃskāreṇa । <b>kutaḥ ? sarvatra hi
padārthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ pradhānasyaiva bhavati rājapuruṣamānayetivat । tatra hi rājārthaḥ</b>
﻿<pb n="r672"/>
<b>kevalamupalakṣaṇatayaiva bhāti । evamatrāṣi dravyameva pradhānaṃ yadanyattadupalakṣaṇaṃ jātyādi</b> ।
na copalakṣaṇasya kāryasaṃbandho vidheyasaṃbandhaḥ dravyopalakṣaṇatvājjātyādīnāṃ saṃskārasaṃbandho
nāstītyarthaḥ । <b>ata idamuk‍taṃ---aviśiṣṭaṃ hi lakṣaṇamiti</b> । kathamaviśiṣṭatetyatrāha
---<b>na hyekatvādīnāṃ vilakṣaṇatve grahāntaranivṛttau sāmarthyamasti</b> । kuto nāstītyāha
---<b>saṃbandhī hi saṃbandhyantaraṃ nivartayati</b> yathā āruṇyaṃ anāruṇyam । na copalakṣaṇatveṃ---
naikatvādīnāṃ saṃskāra[rya]saṃbandho'sti । ataḥ kathaṃ nivartayeyuḥ dvitīyādīn । <b>nanu cok‍taṃ na
saṃbandhimātraṃ</b> yadevopalakṣaṇatayā saṃbandhi na tadarthāntara<b>saṃbandhe hetuḥ</b> । kastarhi ?
uttaraṃ---<b>śrutyādipratipādyateti । atra caikatvaviśiṣṭaḥ śrutyā pratipādyate śeṣī । kathaṃ ca
śakyate vak‍tuṃ śrutipramāṇake vastuni ekatvasavivakṣitamiti । na coddiśyamānatvaṃ vidhīya-
mānatvaṃ vā śrutiṃ vihanti</b> । uddiśyamānatvaṃ na śrūyata iti naivamasti । vidhīmāna-
grahaṇamanāsthāparam । <b>śrutividhāte</b> hi grahaśruterapi vidhātāt grahepi saṃmārgasyāprāptiḥ
syāt । <b>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ uddiśyamānasya viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitaṃ bhavatīti । asyai-
bārthasyāsminnadhikaraṇe heturvarṇanīyaḥ na cāsāvastītyuktam । ucyate । ayamasti hetuḥ</b>
﻿<pb n="r673"/>
<b>kāryavaduddiśyamānaṃ pradhānībhavati</b> । yatkāryavaduddiśyate tatpradhānībhavati । <b>pradhānasya
ca vidheyena saṃbandhaḥ । na pradhānasya guṇānām</b> । kutaḥ ? <b>yasmāda‍guṇānāṃ pradhāno-
pādānanimittaṃ upādānaśeṣatvam</b> । anyathā upādānaśeṣatā na syāt viniyogaśaṣataiva
syāt । <b>ke punaramī guṇāḥ</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>vibhaktyabhidheyāḥ prātipadikārthasya</b> saṅkhyā-
dayaḥ । <b>kathaṃ guṇatā vibhaktyarthānāṃ ? prātipadikārthaṃ pratyavacchedakatvāt vibhaktyartho
hi prātipadikārthamavacchinatti avacchedakatayā ca upādānaśeṣatā । tasmātsiddhaṃ vibhaktya-
bhidheyasya saṅkhyādeḥ</b> prātipadikārthaṃ prati <b>guṇatvam । na ca guṇānāṃ guṇaissaha saṃbandho
vidyate</b> sarveṣāṃ pradhānasaṃbandhitvāt <b>guṇaścāyaṃ saṃskāro nāma । uktaṃ ca <q>‘guṇānāṃ ca
parārthatvāt’</q> iti</b> । tasmāt pradhānaprātipadikārtha eva saṃskāreṇa saṅkhyādibhiśca sambadhyate na
punarekatvādeḥ saṃskārasambandha iti । evaṃ tāvat vibhaktyabhidheyatāmāśritya saṅkhyāderuktam ।
<b>athāpi nāma prātipadikābhidheya evāyamartho jātyādiḥ viniyojyaśca tathāpi anuddiśya-</b>
﻿<pb n="r674"/>
<b>māno naiva</b> saṃskāraṃ prati <b>pradhānatāṃ pratipat‍tuṃ śaknoti</b> । kimityuddiśyamānataiva na
syāditi । uttaraṃ---<b>uddeśo hi nāma kāryāvacchinnasya vastuno bhavati na padārthamātrāva-

<b>dravyopalakṣaṇatayaiva uddeśyajātyāderanbayaḥ na punaḥ kārakatayā</b> karmatayā saṃskāryatayeti

tvāt <b>jātyādīnāmupalakṣaṇataiva</b> prāpnoti । <b>na caivabhiṣyate jātirevāṅgamiti mīmāṃ-
sakāḥ।</b> uttaraṃ---<b>anabhijño bhavān upāttopādeyayoḥ upāttadravyalakṣaṇaṃ hi uddiśyamāna-
padārtho bhavati</b> 1uddeśyaṃ kāryayogyupāttadravyaṃ lakṣayati2 । tena tatra dravyasaṃpratyayaḥ ।
<b>vidheyaṃ punaḥ kamupalakṣayati</b> । na hyasau kāryayogi padārthoṃpasthāpanāyocyate । kathaṃ tarhi

nopalakṣayati</b> । ataḥ uddeśe <b>uddiśyamānasyopalakṣaṇa(para)tvāt dravye sampratyayo bhavati</b> ।

﻿<pb n="r675"/>
dravyameva hi kāryāntarayogitayā pratīyate <b>na punaḥ svasaṃbandhinyabhidheye</b> saṃpratyayaḥ । yataḥ
kāryamātrāvacchinnasya uddeśaḥ <b>ataḥ kāryamātramevāpekṣyate avacchedakatayā na śrutyābhihita-
mekatvādikam</b> । kimityekatvaṃ nāpekṣyate ityāha---<b>upāttataiva tatra viśaṣāvagame hetuḥ
yatpunarupādeyaṃ tacchrutita eva viśiṣṭamavagantavyam । nānyata iti</b> । tena tatra yuktā-
'pekṣā iti viśeṣaḥ । <b>so'yamukto hetuḥ uddiśyamānasya viśeṣaṇaṃ avivakṣitaṃ</b> bhavatī-
<b>tyatrārthe</b> na punaruddeśa evāvivakṣita iti tataḥ upāttāvagateḥ । ato grahaśrutirapi na
vivakṣaṇīyeti yaduk‍taṃ tatparihṛtam । viśeṣaṇaṃ punaravivakṣitaṃ <b>upāttatvādityuktarūpo hetuḥ</b> ।
etenedamuk‍taṃ bhavati upādānaśeṣatayā saṅkhyā anvayaṃ yāti ākāṅkṣyā ca । yatpunarupāttaṃ
tatropādānābhāvāt dūrata eva taccheṣatā nāsti । ato nirviṣayatayā saṅkhyāpekṣaiva nāstīti ।
<b>kā vārtā agnīnādadhīta yūpaṃ chinatti</b> iti । atrāpyuddeśyatvādagnīnāṃ yūpasya ca aviva-
kṣitā saṅkhyā prāpnoti iti manyate । uttaram---<b>vivakṣitā saṅkhyeti</b> । kutaḥ ? atra hi
<b>idamevopādānavākyam</b> । tena anyato'nirjñātatvāt apekṣitā saṅkhyeti । <b>nanu cāgnipada-
muddeśakaṃ pradhānabhūtāścāgnayaḥ</b> na saṅkhyā, ataḥ kathaṃ vivakṣeti । uttaraṃ---<b>satyaṃ yathā
bhavānāha । kintu dvividho hyuddeśaḥ upāttasya anupāttasya ca grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭītyupāttoddeśaḥ</b>
﻿<pb n="r676"/>
aindravāyavādivākyeṣu upāttān grahānuddiśya saṃmārgo vidhīyata ityupāttoddeśaḥ । kvacidapyāha-
vanīyādīnāmanupādānāt । <b>anupāttaṃ coddiśyata iti kathamidaṃ</b> ? 1anuvādaṃ uddeśe
caikarūpaṃ manvānasyedaṃ codyam । uttaraṃ---<b>vidheyaviṣayo hyaddeśa ityucyate</b> yasmin kiñci-
dvidhīyate taduddiśyata ityarthaḥ । <b>nopāttatvaṃ anupāttatvaṃ coddeśahetuḥ । ataḥ pramāṇāntara-
siddhaviśeṣaṇamuddiśyamānamavivakṣitaviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati । yatpunaravijñātaviśeṣaṇamevoddiṣṭaṃ
bhavati taddhidheyavat śrutita eva viśiṣṭamavagantavyam । tasmāt suṣṭhu</b> prāmāṇikaṃ <b>ucyate</b>
---upāttoddeśe viṣaye grahaṃ samārṣṭītyatra <b>avivakṣitaṃ viśeṣaṇamiti2 । nanu ca grahaṃ
saṃmārṣṭīti dvitīyeyaṃ kārakavibhaktiḥ kārakaṃ ca kriyārthaṃ bhavatīti śābdāḥ</b> । atrā-
yamāśayaḥ । dvitīyeyaṃ kārakavibhaktiḥ kārakaṃ ca kriyārthaṃ bhavati । yacca yadarthaṃ tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ
tadupādeyaṃ bhavati । yaccopādeyaṃ tatrāvacchedakākāṅkṣā asti । nanu nirjñātāvacchedakaṃ
nāvacchedakāntaramapekṣate satyaṃ, yadi saṃmārgaṃ pratyupādāne'vacchedako nirjñātaḥ syāt । na
hyatrāvacchedakatā nirjñātā iti upādānaśeṣatā saṅkhyāyā iti । rāddhāntamāha---<b>nanu
cepsitatame dvitīyā na</b> cepsitatamaṃ kriyārthaṃ kintu kriyaiva tadarthā tenepsitatamasya kriyāṃ
pratyanupādānānnopādānaśeṣateti । pūrvapakṣī tvāha---<b>satyaṃ sā tu kārake</b> dvitīyāvibhaktiḥ
tena kārakatvādasti kriyāṃ pratyupādānam । sa evaikagranthenāha---<b>nanu ca vipratiṣiddhamidaṃ</b>
<note>(1) G. anupādanaṃ (2)G. aviśiṣṭaṃ hi lakṣaṇamiti</note>
﻿<pb n="r677"/>
<b>īpsitatamaṃ kārakaṃ ceti</b> । ataḥ kārakatvameva paramārthato'rthaḥ । ārthaṃ tu kārakasyāpi1
kriyāphalayogitvam । rāddhāntī pṛcchati---<b>kathaṃ vipratiṣiddham</b> ? pūrvapakṣī vikalpya
dūṣayati---<b>kimidamīpsitatamaṃ nāma ? yadi tāvat yataḥ</b> kriyāsiddhiḥ 2tatkriyarthaṃ
īpsitatamamiti । <b>evaṃ tarhi kārakamātre karmatvaprasaṅgaḥ tataśca viśeṣābhidhānamanarthakaṃ
idaṃ karma idaṃ karaṇamiti</b> sarvakārakāṇāṃ karmatvāpatteḥ । <b>atha vatkriyayā āpyate</b> yathā
adhyayanena vedaḥ, <b>utpādyate</b> yathā pākenaudanaṃ, <b>saṃskriyate</b>, yathā prokṣaṇena vrīhayaḥ,
<b>vikriyate</b> yathā vilayanenājyaṃ, na vilayanenājyamutpādyate kiṃ tarhi pārthivamājyadravyaṃ gandha-
vatvāt dhanasvabhāvamevāgnisaṃyogena dravībhavati ityaṣṭame vakṣyāmaḥ । <b>tatkarmetyucyate</b> । evaṃ
vadato'sya caturvidhaṃ karmābhipretaṃ saṃskāryavikāryayorbhinnatvāt । dūṣayati---<b>na tarhi kārakaṃ</b>
3āptyādyavasthayepsitatamaḥ san akārakamityarthaḥ । kutaḥ ? <b>kriyāparyavasānāpekṣo
hyāptyādiko guṇaḥ</b> kriyāyāṃ niṣpannāyāṃ paścāt kriyāphalaṃ niṣpādyate । hetorhi phala-
mutpadyate । hetuphalayoḥ paurvāparyaniyamaḥ । <b>paryavasite</b> hi niṣpanne <b>vyāpāre phala-
mutpadyate na phalasya sādhyaiva kriyā</b> । ato na kārakatā । rāddhāntī samādhatte---<b>atrā-
bhidhīyate---nedaṃ vipratiṣiddhaṃ āptyādiko guṇaḥ kārakasthaścākārakasthaśca । yadā kārakasthaḥ</b>
<note>(1) G. athāpi tvasyāsti</note> <note>(2) R. kiyāsiddhayarthaṃ</note> <note>(3) G. āptyādya-
vasthāyasminnaṃśe tatkārakamityarthaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r678"/>
<b>tadā kārakameva phalam</b> tadā''ptyādiko guṇo dvidhā anyathaikarūpyameva syāt । pūrvapakṣī
pṛcchati---<b>kimidaṃ kārakameva phalamiti</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>yadā hi kārakameva kayācidvi-
kārāpattyā vyāpyaṃ utpādyaṃ saṃskāryaṃ vikāryaṃ ceṣṭaṃ</b> tadā <b>tadeva phalamityucyate । tāmevā-
vasthāmaṅgīkṛtya īpsitatamavyapadeśaṃ labhate । kriyāsiddha‍yarthaṃ phalasiddha‍yarthaṃ vā</b> । yatkrārakaṃ
tat <b>kriyāsiddha‍yarthaṃ phalasiddha‍yarthaṃ ca</b> । tadeva kayācidvikārāpattyā īpsitatamavyapadeśaṃ
labhate । <b>ataḥ kārakamīpsitatamamityaviruddham</b> । kathamaviruddhaṃ ? <b>vidyate hi
kārakaṃ na phalasamavāyi yathā karaṇādi । vidyate ca phalaṃ na kārakasamavāyi yathā
svargādi</b> । tena yatkārakaṃ phalasamavāyi tatkarma yathā syādityuk‍taṃ īpsitatamaṃ kārakamiti ।
etena viśeṣābhidhānārthamanarthakamiti yaduk‍taṃ tatparihṛtam । <b>nanu svargādyapi kāraka-
samavāyyeva kartṛgāmi kriyāphalamiti</b> । śāstraphalaṃ prayoktarītyatra <b>vacanāt</b> abhi-
dhānāt । <b>uttaraṃ---na kārakatayā phalasamavāyo vidyata ityadhikāralakṣaṇavyāpāro'yaṃ
adhikāralakṣaṇe</b> uktaḥ । <b>1kathaṃ tarhi bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ sūtraṃ <q>“kartrabhiprāye kriyāphale”</q></b>
<note>(1) G. ṇa ityuktam</note>
﻿<pb n="r679"/>
<b>iti । asyāpi tatraivārtho nirūpyate</b> । prakṛtamupasaṃharannāha---<b>ato grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭīti yadyapi
saṃmārgaṃ graho niṣpādayatveva tathāpi na tasyāṃśasya vācikā dvitīyāvibhaktiḥ īpsitata-
matvamācaṣṭe phalāṃśamityarthaḥ</b> । kriyāniṣpādyamiti yāvat । anenedamuk‍taṃ yasminnaṃśe
ekatvaṃ śrutaṃ na tasyāṅgasya upādeyatā । yasya copādeyatā na tatra vibhaktiriti । <b>tasmācchrutito
viśeṣāvagama iti siddham । ataḥ upāttaviṣayaḥ saṃskāra iti sthitam । nanu ca
vyabhicāryetaddarśanaṃ</b> īpsitatame dvitīyeti । <b>anīpsitatamepi dvitīyā bhavatyeva</b> upā-
dhyāyāya gāṃ dadātīti । <b>tataḥ kiṃ</b>? <b>idaṃ tato bhavati</b> । anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ <b>kārakāṃ
śābhidhāyinī na phalāṃśābhidhāyinī । evaṃ grahamityetadapi kārakamevācaṣṭe । tataścai-
katvamavivakṣitamiti na śakyate vak‍tuṃ</b> upādeyadaśāyāmeva śrutatvāt । yadi kārakā-
bhidhāyinī dvitīyā <b>kathaṃ tarhi grahārthaḥ saṃmārgaḥ pramāṇābhāvāt</b> tādarthyamayuktamityarthaḥ ।
uttaraṃ---<b>prayojanavattvāt</b> grahāṇāṃ saṃmārgasya tādarthyaṃ, <b>yathā paśupuroḍāśo'gnīṣomadevatārthaḥ
atrābhidhīyate । īpsitatamatvaṃ tāvat dvitīyā'bhidhatte । tathā yuktaṃ cānīpsitamiti
tu kriyānirvāhyamevetyarthaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---dvitīyā tāvat phalāṃśamabhidhatte । tathā yuktaṃ
﻿<pb n="r680"/>
mityatrāpi tathāyogābhidhānāt kriyājanyaphalāṃśābhidhāyitvameva iti <b>iyān viśeṣaḥ kriyāntara-
saṃbandhitayaivaikasyopādānaṃ</b> abhidhānaṃ yathā <q>‘vrīhīn avahanti’</q> iti niyogasaṃbandhitayā
vrīhaya upādīyante tatraivepsitatamatā । <b>ekasya neti</b> yathā gāṃ dadātīti na goḥ kriyāntara-
saṃbandhitayopādānam । taccānīpsitaṃ kriyājanyaphalayogi । tathā'nīpsitatamamapīti kriyā-
janyaphalayogitve nāsti viśeṣaḥ । dvitīyāpi tāvanmātramevābhidhatte kāryataḥ tadīpsitatamatvaṃ
brīhīṇāmiti mantavyam । evamubhayatrāpi mukhyārthaiva dvitīyā bhavati tena na kārakāṃśābhidhāyinī
dvitīyetyuk‍taṃ bhavati । yadi tathā yuktabhityatrāpi na dvitīyā kārakāṃśābhidhāyinī <b>evaṃ tarhi
gāṃ dadātītyavivakṣā saṅkhyāyāḥ</b> । pūrvapakṣyevāśaṅkāmutpādya nirasyati---<b>bhavatviti cenna,
prayojanāntarakalpanāprasaṅgāt</b>। yāvaddhi prayojanāntaraṃ gaurna kalpyate tāvadavivakṣitā saṅkhyeti
na śakyate vak‍tum anirjñātasaṅkhyātvenāvacchedakākāṅkṣitvāt । rāddhāntaikadeśyāha---<b>kimiti</b>
prayojanāntaraṃ <b>neṣyate</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>pramāṇābhāvāt na</b> kāryakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇamasti ।
<b>nanu ca dvitīyaiva</b> kāryakalpanāyāṃ <b>pramāṇam---satyam</b> dvitīyā pramāṇam sā tu <b>kāryā-
kāṅkṣāyāṃ viśeṣaṃ samarpayati</b> na punardvitīyāntapadavācyasyārthasya <b>kāryamebāvagamayituṃ kṣamā</b>
saktvādivat । kasmātpunarna kṣametyāha---<b>viniyogaparyavasāyinyaḥ</b> parasparasaṃbandhamātropakṣīṇa-
śak‍tayo vibhaktayaḥ na kāryaparyavasāyinyaḥ । nanu ca kiṃ prayojanāntarakalpanayā, atraiva
vākye niyogaḥ sādhyo bhavatu ityatrāha---<b>navā'dhikāraśūnyo niyogo'stīti phalabatsannidhā-
vityatra vakṣyāmaḥ</b>। atra ca goḥ sādhyatvadarśanāt nādhikāro'pyaparaḥ sādhyaḥ śakyate'ṅgī-
﻿<pb n="r681"/>
kartum । na cādhikāraṃ vinā niyogo'sti । tasmādiyamapi kalpanaiva nāsti । yadi yatra
sādhyāntaramasti tatrādhikāro nāsti kathaṃ tarhi saṃskāravidhīnāmadhikārasaṃsparśaḥ ityāha---<b>saṃskāra-
vidhayastūk‍tāḥ <q>‘teṣāmarthena’</q> ityatra</b> । yathā satyapi teṣāṃ kāryāntare adhikārānupraveśaḥ tathā
teṣāmarthenetyatroktam । rāddhāntī pariharati---<b>uktottaramapi kimiti bhavatā paricoditam
vismaraṇāparādhāditi manyāmahe । tadidaṃ smāryate anupāttaviṣayamidaṃ prādhānyamiti
yūpavat sthitaṃ vivakṣitatvaṃ saṅkhyāyāḥ । amunā ta viśeṣeṇa</b> kāryāntarasaṃbandhāsaṃbandha-
nibandhanena īpsitatamatvānīpsitatamatvalakṣaṇena <b>sūtrāntarapraṇayanaṃ bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ <q>‘akathitaṃ’</q>
iti । atrāpi tathā yuktamityanuvartate । tasmāt dvitīyā prādhānyaṃ</b> kriyājanyaphalabhāgitāṃ
<b>na vyabhicaratīti sthitam । upātte tu viṣaye</b> pramāṇāntareṇa <b>viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti
siddham</b> । <q>“grahādiṣvekatvaṃ brūyāt na dvitīyādīn pratiṣedhet”</q> iti bhāṣyam । tadanu-
papannam । yathā paśugatamekatvaṃ vidadhat ekavacanaṃ dvitīyādīnarthān nivartayati tathehāpi
kiṃ na syādityata āha---<b>upāttaviṣayatvāt‍tu grahaśruteḥ upādeyehi ekatvādayo viśeṣaṇa-
miti । iha punaḥ upāttataiva viśeṣāvagatau heturityuk‍taṃ</b> iti । vyākhyātārtham ।
<note>(1) P. 706-3</note>
﻿<pb n="r682"/>
nanu <q>“parisañcaṣṭa”</q> iti ko'bhiprāyaḥ । tridoṣaduṣṭā parisaṅkhyeti manyate । <b>ayamabhiprāyaḥ
---ekatvamananvitaṃ syāt । na cānanvitābhidhānamastītyuktaṃ tada‍bhūtādhikaraṇe</b> । ato varaṃ
parisaṅkhyeti manyate । <b>naitadasti । satya/?/nanvitābhidhānamekatvasya prāp‍noti । na punaḥ
parisaṅkhyā saṃbhavati aprāptatvāt । grahasaṃmārgasaṃbandhasya prāptau satyāmanyanivṛttau
niyogaḥ 1prabhavati</b> na rāgaprāpte bhakṣaṇa eva <q>“pañca pañcanakhā bhakṣyā”</q> itivat । aprāpte punaḥ
<b>yathā ś‍veti śrutiḥ na kākādīn nivartayituṃ kṣamā</b> । <b>na cānanvitābhidhānaṃ, tasyāpi</b>
śuno bhakṣaṇe <b>prāp‍tyavagamāt</b> tathehāpi na dvitīyādīnāṃ parisaṅkhyeti prakṛtena saṃbandhaḥ ।
<b>nanu ca yuktaṃ śvādiṣu</b> ananvitatvāt śunaḥ,<b>ekatvaṃ 2punaḥ bahuṣūpādīyamāneṣu pakṣe'pi na</b>
prāpnoti saṅkhyāyāṃ saṅkhyāntaraṃ nivartyaiva vyavasthānāt । <b>ato'nanvitābhidhānaṃ duṣpariharam</b> ।
<b>parihṛtamidaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa---“na vibhak‍tervacanamevaikaṃ prayojanaṃ3</b> iti badatā । <b>kathaṃ
punaranenedaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavati saṅkhyāyā ananvaye'pi</b> । <b>itthaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavati</b> । <b>saṅkhyāyā ananva-
yepi karmamātrepi prayogadarśanāt yathā brāhmaṇo na hantavya iti</b> । <b>atnāpi sādhyamiti cet</b>
<note>(1) G. saṃbhavati</note> <note>(2) G. yena</note> <note>(3) P. 723</note>
﻿<pb n="r683"/>
na, asmākamatrāpi saṅkhyā(na)nvayo'bhipreta iti cet, <b>na nañarthe vadhena saṃbadhyamāne ekatva-
manvetuṃ kṣamaṃ, anyataḥ pravṛttyavagamāta</b> । asyārthaḥ---vadho hi nañarthena saṃbadhyamānaḥ pratiṣidhya-
mānaḥ anyataḥ pravṛtto'ṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ । tataścānupādeyatvānna tatropādānaśeṣatā saṅkhyāyā
ityavivakṣaiva । tasmādekatvābhidhānaṃ dharmamātre sādhu iti draṣṭavyam । atra bhāṣyam <q>“ayaṃ
cāparo doṣaḥ”</q> iti । tasya cāyamarthaḥ---ekatvagrahasaṃbandhavidhānepi sammārgaviṣaye grahasyaikatvaṃ na
niyantuṃ śakyate viṣayatvena saṃmārgasyāviśeṣāt । iti । sa cāyamanupapanna iva pratibhāti ।
yasmādekatvaśravaṇādyathā tasya karmānvayitā na saṃbhavati tathā varṇayituṃ nyāyyam । tena
grahaśabdo'nupāttoddeśyaka eva bhavatviti । sammārgaviṣaya eva grahasyaikatvaniyamaḥ sidhyatītī-
māmanupapattimapanetuṃ ṭīkākāra āha---<b>ayamaparo doṣa iti</b> pratīkena bhāṣyamanubhāṣitam ।
anupapattiṃ pariharati---<b>ekatvānvitābhidhāne āśrīyamāṇe grahatvaṃ nopāttaviṣayaṃ syāt</b>
upāttagrahopalakṣaṇārthaṃ na syāt <b>anupāttaviṣayatve ca grahasya</b> sammārgeṇa saha ananvayaḥ
<b>prāpnoti</b> । kāryāntarānupraveśinaḥ saṃskārānarhatvāt । <b>ananvīyamāne ca sammārgavidhānaṃ
nirviṣayatvāt</b> śeṣiśūnyatvādanarthakaṃ syāt । ato nānena doṣeṇāyaṃ2 anupāttoddeśaḥ
upāttoddeśa eveti sthito bhāṣyok‍to doṣa iti ।</p>
<p><q>“athaikatvasammārgasaṃbandho vidhīyeta3”</q> ityādibhāṣyaṃ tadanupapannaṃ, saṃbandhe hi vidhīyamāne
avaśyaṃ guṇapradhānabhāvo'bhyupagamanīyaḥ । tatra yasyaikatvaṃ pradhānaṃ tadekatvamuddiśya sammārgo
<note>(1) P. 715</note> <note>(2) G. dūṣaṇāyāyaṃ</note> <note>(3) P. 715</note>
﻿<pb n="r684"/>
vidhīyeta । tataśca grahaśabdo'nanvitaḥ syāt । atha grahasya caikatvasya ca uddeśyadvayasya
śravaṇāt pratyuddeśyaṃ vākyasamāpteḥ ekena grahasammārgasaṃbandhaṃ vidhāya apareṇaikatvasaṃmārgasambandho
vidhīyetetyucyeta । tanna । aprāpte grahasammārgasaṃbandhe kathamekatvasammārgasaṃbandho vidhīyeta ।
sammārgasya cāpradhānatvāt ekatvasya pradhānatvāt । na hi pradhānaṃ guṇa prati vidhīyate । atha
sammārga eva pradhānabhūtaḥ tatrāpyuddeśyabhedena vākyabhedamāśritya grahe sammārgaḥ sammārge hyekatvaṃ
vidhīyate । tadanupapannam । ekatvasyāmūrtatayā sammārgaṃ prati sādhanatvānupapatteḥ 1guṇatvā-
bhāvāditīmāṃ śaṅkāmanuvadan vyākhyānamāha---<b>athaikatvasaṃmārgasambandho vidhīyeta tatrāpi
dvayī gatiḥ syādityanena guṇaphalasaṃbandhavadvidhānaṃ na saṃbhavati</b> nāpyaruṇāvaditi darśayati
etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---yathā guṇaphalasaṃbandhe pradhānabhūto vaitānāgniḥ guṇabhūtādhānasaṃbaddho
vidhīyate tathehāpyekatvaṃ[tvavad]grahe sammārgasaṃbandho vidhīyeteti yā śaṅkā sāpi na bhavati
yathā cāmūrtasyāpyāruṇyasya krayasādhanatā tathaikatvasyāpi sammārgasādhanatayā śaṅkā yā sāpi na
saṃbhavatīti । kathamasaṃbhavaḥ? <b>ekatvaṃ tāvat nopāttasyopalakṣaṇāyālam</b> । ekatvaṃ
tāvat svavākye upāttasya saṃmārgasya upalakṣaṇāya viśeṣaṇāya alaṃ na bhavati । <b>sammārgeṇa
hi saṃbadhyamānaṃ pradhānaṃ vā bhavati guṇo vā nānyaḥ saṃbandho'sti</b> । <b>kathaṃ nāsti</b> ?
<b>prātipadikāśritaṃ hi saṅkhyābhidhānaṃ vibhaktīnāmityuktam</b> । <b>kasmānna viṣayatayā</b>
uddeśyatayā <b>vidheyatayā vā</b> sammārgasaṃbandha ekatvasya saṃbhavati ? <b>paratantratvāt</b> ।
<note>(1) guṇatvābhāvābhāvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r685"/>
prātipadikāśritatvāt saṃmārgeṇa saha saṃbandhābhāvāt । kimiti tarhi bhāṣyakāreṇa grahasya
pradhānatayā sammārgaṃ pratyanupādānāt upādānopayogitayā aruṇāvadekatvasya sammārge guṇabhāvo na
saṃbhavatītyuktam । atrāha---<b>abhyupagamyāpyaruṇāvanna sambhavatītyuktam grahasya pradhānatvāt</b> ।
<b>nanu ca pradhānepi sambhavatyeva viśeṣaṇaṃ nimittabhūtaṃ kārakatvamāśrityeti</b> । asya
ayamarthaḥ prādhānyamapi grahādeḥ kārakatvanimittakameva । kārakabhūtā eva grahāḥ pradhānabhūtā
bhavanti । tena tāmavasthāmāśrityaikatvaṃ grahādeḥ viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati aruṇāvaditi । <b>kena
coktaṃ na saṃbhavati</b> viśeṣaṇamiti । <b>iha punaḥ vidhānāsaṃbhava eva pradarśitaḥ pradhānatvāt
grahasya</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi grahaḥ sammārgaṃ prati vidhīyeta tadā asyopādeyatvāt viśeṣaṇaṃ
syāt । iha tu graho na vidhīyate pradhānatvāditi । anena <q>‘pradhānabhūta’</q>mityādigranthena
1<q>“nanu pradhānabhūta”</q>mityādibhāṣyaṃ <q>“bhidyeta vākyaṃ”</q> ityevamantaṃ vyākhyātam । <b>athocyeta
grahādi lakṣayitvā tasyaikatvasaṃbandho vidhīyate na sammārgasaṃbandha iti---ayamabhiprāyaḥ kaḥ
pakṣapātaḥ sammārgo'nvayī na punarekatvamiti</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>kriyāśūnyo'pyanvayaḥ na
saṅkhyādeḥ sambhavati asati tu vidheye</b> saṃbhavatyapi । asyārthaḥ---sammārge vidheye saṃbhavati
saṅkhyādeḥ kriyāśūnyo'nvayo na saṃbhavati । asati tu vidheye saṃbhavatyapi । <b>na ca śrutyā
grahagatasyaikatvasyānvayo'sti</b> kriyayetyuktam । uttarabhāṣyamapyevaṃ vyākhyeyam । tathā
sammārgādīnāmadhyayanaṃ pramāda ityabhyupagataṃ syāt iti yāvaddhi sammārgādīnāmadhyayanaṃ pramāda iti
<note>(1) P. 716</note>
﻿<pb n="r686"/>
