nocyate tāvadvidheye sammārgādau saṃbhavati naikatvagrahasaṃbandhavidhimātraparatā vākyasyeti ।
<q>“yadyavivakṣitamekatvaṃ3”</q> iti <b>bhāṣyeṇa lakṣaṇavirodhaṃ darśayati । bahuṣu bahuvacanamiti
śābdāḥ na vayametadvicārayāma iti pramāṇataḥ sthite lakṣye lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ kariṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ ।
na cātra lakṣaṇavirodhaḥ na vibhak‍tervacanamevaikaṃ prayojanam । etacca prāgeva vyākhyātam ।
api ca grahaḥ prātipādikārthaḥ ekatvaṃ vibhaktyarthaḥ । kimato yadyevaṃ ? etadato bhavati
prānipadikārthagataṃ hi vibhaktiḥ svārthaṃ śrutyaivābhivadati</b> । iti । anena bhāṣyeṇa
vibhaktyabhidheyasyaikatvasya <b>pāratantryaṃ</b> prātipadikārthaparatantnatvaṃ <b>4darśayati । tacca
vyākhyātam । atha yaduk‍taṃ paśupālameteti</b> yathaikatvaṃ vivakṣitaṃ tadvadihāpīti tatra kaḥ
parihāraḥ ? <b>upādeyānāṃ śrutito viśeṣaḥ</b> ityuk‍to viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<head>saṃskārādvāguṇānām ।</head>
<p><b>yadi kāryataḥ upādānaṃ upāttasya lakṣaṇaṃ śeṣitayeti tato grahaśrutirapi soma-
dhāraṇapātramātralakṣaṇaiva ekakāryatvāt</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatiṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ cāha---<b>yadi kāryataḥ
upādānaṃ</b> yasya kāryamasti tasyopādānaṃ uddeśakena śabdena <b>upāttasya ca lakṣaṇaṃ</b> upalakṣaṇaṃ
<note>(1) P. 723</note> <note>(2) P. 724</note> <note>(3) P. 723</note> <note>(4) G. adds na</note>
﻿<pb n="r687"/>
<b>śeṣitayeti</b> । <b>tato grahaśrutirapi</b> grahaprātipadikamapi somadhāraṇapāvamātralakṣaṇārthameva
grahāṇāṃ camasānāṃ copāttatvāt । somayāgaśeṣabhūtasomadhāraṇaikakāryatvāt <b>sammārgasya ca
somāvasekanirharaṇameva prayojanam</b> । tacca prayojanaṃ graheṣu[cayaseṣu] cāviśiṣṭaṃ <b>ityupapannaṃ
camasānāmapi sammārjanam</b> । <b>darśitaṃ caitadbhāṣyakāreṇa</b> <q>“yasmin gṛhyamāṇe somo vyava-
sicyeta”</q> ityanena । <b>anena sāmarthyataśca kāryasiddhau kevalasammārgavidhānalābhaḥ
prakaraṇe mantropadeśavat</b> । asyārthaḥ---avivakṣitagrahasaṃbandhaṃ sammārgamātrameva vidhīyatāṃ tathā
ca vidhilāghavaṃ bhavatīti । kathaṃ tarhi śiṣṭhadvārasaṃbandhaḥ sāmarthyāt । sammārgaḥ tāvat
somavasekanirharaṇaṃ śaknoti kartumiti liṅgena tasya tatraiva viniyogaḥ yathā prakaraṇe mantrasyopadi-
ṣṭasya liṅgena viniyogaḥ tathehāpi । <b>uk‍taṃ caitadbhāṣyakāreṇa</b>---<q>‘sammārge puruṣaprayat‍naṃ’</q> ityeva-
mādinā bhāṣyeṇa ।</p>
<head>vyavasthāvā'rthasya</head>
<p><b>atrābhidhīyate---śrutitaḥ upāttaparijñānaṃ, nopādānācchrutiḥ</b> । grahāśca camasāśca
kāryataḥ upāttāḥ ityetāvatā kāraṇena na grahaśrutiḥ sarvapātraparatayā varṇayitavyā । kāryasya hi
etāvatsāmarthyaṃ yat kāryaśūnyasya saṃskārābhāva iti । na punaḥ yāvadeva kāryavat tasya
sarvasya saṃskāraḥ । <b>nanu somāvasik‍taparimārjanaṃ</b> śuddhāvasthāprāptiḥ <b>tulyaṃ kāryamityuk‍taṃ</b>,
<note>(1) P. 723</note>
﻿<pb n="r688"/>
tena kāryayogāt sarveṣāmapi sammārgaḥ syāditi । <b>satyamuk‍taṃ na punaḥ śrutibādhe
tatsamarthamityuktamasmābhiḥ</b> । pūrvapakṣī vrūte---<b>śrute'pi hi yadeva kāryaṃ, tadeva
cet kimityaśrute'pi na bhavati</b> । asyārthaḥ---śrute grahe somāvasekanirharaṇameva
sammārgasya prayojanam । kimityaśrutepi na bhavati । tatrāpi tasya kāryasyāviśeṣāt kāryārtha-
tvāccānuṣṭhānasya । uttaraṃ---<b>na hi kāryaṃ śrūyate</b> । <b>śrūyate hi kāryamityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ
---grahaṃ sammārṣṭīti śrūyate । tatra graheṣu sammārgasya kiṃ prayojanaṃ bhavatviti cintāyāṃ somāvaseka-
nirharaṇaṃ śuddhāvasthāprāptilakṣaṇaṃ prayojanaṃ dṛṣṭamiti nānyat kalpyate । na punaḥ kāryameva
śrūyate । tena śrutibalalabdhātmakaṃ kāryaṃ na śrutimeva unmūlayitumalam । codyamāha---<b>kāryaṃ
cennādriyate kathaṃ tarhi prokṣaṇaṃ yaveṣu</b> । vrīhiṣu yaveṣu vā tulyaṃ prokṣaṇakāryam । ato
yaveṣvapi prokṣaṇaṃ yuktamiti ceta nyāyo nādriyate, kathaṃ yaveṣu prokṣaṇamiti bhrāntaścodayati ।
<b>yathā tat tathā navame vakṣyāmaḥ</b> apūrvaprayuktatvāddharmāṇāṃ vrīhiśabdaḥ tatsādhanaviśeṣa-
lakṣaṇārtha iti yaveṣvapi prokṣaṇaṃ; iha tu graheṣu camaseṣu ca abhyāsāpūrvabhedāt na tulyaḥ
sādhanabhāvaḥ ityapūrvaprayuk‍tatve'pi nāsti camaseṣu sammārgaḥ । yaduk‍taṃ sammārgamātravidhānaṃ lābho
labhyata iti tadayuk‍taṃ, viniyogaviṣayatvāt niyogasya । viniyogaḥ parasparasaṃbandhaḥ । sa
iha viṣayo niyogasya । na cāsau svaviṣayopamarde prabhavati । anyathā niyogasyaivopamardaprasaṅgāt
grahasaṃbandhānvitaśca viṣayaḥ । tadidamuk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa---2<q>“utsṛjyamāne śrutireva bādhyate
grahamiti”</q> । niyogaśrutirbādhitā syādityarthaḥ । nanu ca śrutyā sammārgasya vidhyanvayo vākyena
grahasyeti grahaṃ viprakṛṣṭaṃ parityajya sammārgamātravidhānaṃ bhavatvityāśaṅkyāha---<b>viniyoge hi sati na</b>
<note>(1) G. sādapūrva</note> <note>(2) P. 726</note>
﻿<pb n="r689"/>
<b>na kaścidvirodho niyogasya</b> ubhayamapi vidadhātyanvitapadārthatvādityarthaḥ । yo hi
viniyogasyaiva parasparasaṃbandhasya viśeṣaḥ kaścit śīghraṃ kaścit vilambeneti <b>sa ca virodhe</b> 
sati viśeṣaḥ2 । <b>iha tu virodhābhāvādatantraṃ viprakarṣa iti siddham</b> । <b>ekatvaṃ tu yathā
nānveti tathok‍taṃ grahaḥ punaruddiśyamānatayā'nvetīti</b> । <b>atrāyaṃ vicāraḥ</b> kimavāntara-
kāryavaśena grahaśrutiḥ somādhārapātramātralakṣaṇārthā bhavatu paramakāryavaśeneba vrīhiśrutiḥ
sādhanaviśeṣalakṣaṇārthā uta neti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī kāryārthatvāccheṣasya 3avāntarakārya-
saṃbandha iti manyate । rāddhāntī śrutimūlatvādavāntarakāryasya na tadupamarde sāmarthyamapi iti
śrutyanusāreṇa gahavyak‍tīnāmeva sammārga iti ।</p>
<head>ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣu ।</head>
<p>atra bhāṣye sandehaḥ kiṃ saptadaśāratritā vājapeyasya ūrdhvapātre niviśate uta tadaṅgasya
paśoḥ yūpo iti । tatra kāraṇasaṃśayamāha---<b>saptadaśāratrirvājapeyasya yūpa ityatroddeśakaṃ padaṃ
kiṃ vājapeyasya saptadaśa, uta yūpasya</b> saptadaśeti kiṃ vājapeyapadamuddeśakaṃ uta yūpapadamiti ।
<b>pūrvapakṣiṇo'bhiprāyaḥ । yadi yūpa</b> ityuddeśakaṃ <b>padaṃ tadā vājapeyasyetyananvitābhidhānam</b>
<note>(1) P. 727</note> <note>(2) G. viśeṣayituṃ</note> <note>(3) G. apavādako'rtha iti manyate</note>
﻿<pb n="r690"/>
<b>prāpnoti yūpena vājapeyasyāsaṃbandhāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi yūpasya saptadaśāratnitā vidhīyate
tadā vājapeyasya yūpena sabāsaṃbandhaḥ । na ca yūpena saha saṃbandho'vakalpate । vājapeyasya
ṣaṣṭhyantatvāt ṣaṣṭhyāśca saṃbandhavācitvāt vājapeyayūpayośca saṃbandhābhāvāt । yūpasya ca
paśuyāgamātre paryavasitasaṃbandhatvāt paramāpūrveṇa saha saṃbandhābhāvāditi । tasmāt vājapeyasyai-
voddeśyatvāt tadarthatayaiva saptadaśāratnitā vidhīyate । tatrāśrayāpekṣāyāṃ yūpaśabdo vājapeya-
saṃbandhinaṃ guṇayogādūrdhvapātraṃ pratipādayatīti । tadāha---<b>tasmādvājapeyasaṃbandhini
yūpaśabdo draṣṭavyaḥ</b> । <b>evamanvitapadārthako vākyārthaḥ samarthito bhavati</b> । <b>atrābhidhīyate
---yadi yūpaśabde śrautānvayini vājapeyaśabdo'nanvitaḥ syāt syādetadevaṃ, atra punaḥ
saptadaśāratniryūpa ityapi saṃbandhe vājapeyaśabdo'nvita eva</b> । <b>kathaṃ ? saṃbandha-
saṃbandhinyapi ṣaṣṭhyantasyānvayadarśanāt devadattasya naptā ityevamādiṣu</b> । atrāyaṃ bhāvaḥ---pūrva-
pakṣe yūpaśabdo na śrautārthaḥ asmin mate tu mukhyārthaḥ । na vājapeyasyānanvayaḥ sākṣātsaṃbandhā-
bhāve'pi ṣaṣṭhyantasyānvayadarśanāt । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---yadyapi tena saha na saṃbandho'sti tathāpi
ṣaṣṭhī na virudhyate saṃbandhināpi yasya saṃbandhaḥ tadapekṣayāpi ṣaṣṭhīprayoga iti । <b>tasmāda‍yūpa-
śabdasya lākṣaṇikatve nāsti pramāṇaṃ iti yūpenaiva saṃbandhaḥ</b> saptadaśāratnitāyāḥ ।
<b>kiṃ punaratra vājapeyasyetyanena</b> kṛtamiti pūrvapakṣī codayati । matpakṣe hi uddeśyasamarpa-
katayopapadyate iti manyate । uttaraṃ---<b>kimanenāsmākaṃ anena kṛtaṃ na kṛtamiti</b>
﻿<pb n="r691"/>
<b>anvayastāvadvidyate</b> । <b>vidyamānānvaye tu vākyārthe kiñcitkāryaṃyogi bhavati</b> । <b>kiñcit
prāptārthaṃ sat anūdyata iti doṣaḥ</b> । etaccābhyupagamyavādenoktam । paramārthatastu
pūrvapakṣepi padadvayamanarthakaṃ prakaraṇādvājapeyasaṃbandhāt yogyatvācca ūrdhvapātraprāpteḥ ।</p>
<head>kartṛguṇe tu samavāyāt ।</head>
<p>atra bhāṣye sandehaḥ---kimabhikramaṇaṃ prayājeṣveva niviśate uta kṛts‍ne prakaraṇa iti ।
tatra kāraṇasandehamāha---<b>abhikrāmaṃ juhotīti kiṃ karmaṇaḥ karmānvayo vidyate uta neti
cintyate</b> । yadya(pya)nvayo vidyate tadā prayājeṣveva niveśaḥ । atha na vidyate tadā
vākyaṃ bhitvā yogyakartari guṇavidhiriti kṛts‍ne prakaraṇe niveśaḥ । <b>kathaṃ punaranvayo bhavati</b> ?
<b>kathaṃ vā na</b> ? tatra yathānvayo na bhavati tathā darśayannāha---<b>pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ---na
karma karmasādhyaṃ bhavati</b> । tadāha <b>bhagavān kāśyapaḥ</b> <q>“karma karmasādhyaṃ na bhavati”</q> iti
(vai. sū. 1-1-11) yathā guṇasya sādhanabhāvaḥ tathā na karmaṇa iti । <b>tasmādyaḥ kaścidupāttaḥ
prakaraṇe kartā so'bhikrāmaṃ ityanvayaḥ</b> । parasparamabhikramaṇahomayoranvayābhāvāt vākyaṃ
mitvā'bhikrāmatītyanena karmavidhiḥ yogye kartaryabhikramaṇaṃ vidhīyate । <b>nanu ca prayāje'pi yaḥ
kartā tatrāpyanvayo 2bhavatyeva</b> । tena sannidhānaviśeṣāt prayājakartraiva saṃbandho bhavati ।
<note>(1) P. 729</note> <note>(2) G. vidyata eva</note>
﻿<pb n="r692"/>
<b>satyaṃ bhavati yadi juhotītyabhidhāyakaṃ syāt । anabhidhāyakatve tasmin na karturuddheśyatvaṃ
saṃbhavati nānṛtaṃ vadeditivat</b> । asyārthaḥ-yadi juhotīti vibhaktiḥ abhidhāyikā syāt tadā
gasyamānakartṛpara eva prayoga iti prayājakartureva sannihitasyoddeśyatvāt tatraiva niveśaḥ syāt ।
ahnabhidhāyikā tveṣā । siddhānte abhikramaṇākhyaguṇavidhānārthatvāt । ataḥ karturuddeśyatvaṃ
nāsti nānṛtaṃ <b>vadediti yathā</b> । <b>tasmāt saṃyogato'viśeṣāt prakaraṇāviśeṣācca</b> prakaraṇa-
sthakartrāsaṃbandhādvākyabhedaḥ prayājavākyādidaṃ bhinnaṃ vākyamityarthaḥ । yadi hi tatraivābhi-
kramaṇaṃ niviśeta <b>tadā kevalabhāvavidhānena sahaikavākyataiva syāditi । juhotiridānīṃ
kimarthaḥ ?</b> bhinnavākye abhikrāmaṃ ityetaṃ vākyaṃ juhotītyaparaṃ tadevaṃ vākyabhede sati ।
uttaraṃ---<b>yadarthaḥ tadartho bhaviṣyati</b> kiṃ naḥ etena cintanena । abhyāsanyāyena karmāntare
vā paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇanyāyena vā'nuvādaḥ ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ।</p>
<head>sākāṅkṣaṃ tvekavākyaṃ syādasamāptaṃ hi pūrveṇa ।</head>
<p><b>satyamananvayaḥ karmaṇaḥ karmaṇā</b> sākṣāta । <b>kartṛsaṃbandhāt tu aruṇāvat
saṃbhavati</b> kartṛsaṃbandhadvāreṇa karmaṇo'pi karmānvaya upapadyate yathā dravyadvāreṇāruṇyasya ।
<b>nanu ca karturupādānaṃ nāsti yathā ekahāyanyā upādānaṃ juhotītyasyānabhidhāyakatvādi</b>-
<note>(1) P. 730</note>
﻿<pb n="r693"/>
<b>tyuktam ।</b> uttaraṃ---<b>na brūmaḥ karturuddeśyatvamastīti</b> । <b>tannimittakastu karmoddeśe'pyanvayo
na virudhyata iti</b> brūmaḥ । <b>tasya</b> kartuḥ tatra prayāje saṃbhavāt । asyārthaḥ---ṇamulanta-
tvādabhikrāmamityasya juhotītyanena saṃbandhaḥ pratīyate । sa caivaṃ <b>yujyate</b> yadi kenacitprakāreṇa
saṃbandho nirvahati tatkartṛdvāreṇa ca saṃbandho nirvahati । na ca tatra kartā nāsti । yata eva
cātra kartā saṃbandhadvārabhūto nopāttaḥ ekahāyanī tūpāttā, ata <b>evāruṇādhikaraṇena vaiṣamyam</b> ।
tatrāruṇādhikaraṇe <b>dvayorapyanvayinoḥ</b> aruṇaikahāyanyau<b>rupādānaṃ iha tu saṃbhavamātreṇaiva</b>
kartṛdvārateti <b>viśeṣaḥ</b> । nanu ca bhāṣyakāraḥ pūrvapakṣe “saṃbandhamātraparijñānāt prayogavacanāt
kartavyatāsiddhiḥ iti vadan prakaraṇepi gamyamānakartṛdvāreṇa karmaṇyeva vidhānamiti darśayati[tat]
kathaṃ karturanupādānāt pūrvapakṣa ityāśaṅkyāha yaduktaṃ <b>bhāṣyakāreṇa saṃbandhamātraparijñānāt
prayogavacanāt</b> 1kartravamarśāta <b>kartavyatāsiddhiriti, tatraiva karturuddeśyatvaṃ na virudhyata
ityabhiprāyaḥ asyārthaḥ</b>---prakaraṇapaṭhitamekavedaṃ2padamiti tadyogyenārthāntareṇa ekavākyatānve-
ṣaṇe yogyaśca saṃbandhe[ndhī] karteti kartāramuddiśyābhikramaṇaṃ vidhīyate । ekavākyatve ca na
karturuddeśyatvasaṃbhavaḥ । juhotītyanenaivānvitābhidhānasiddheḥ । evaṃ vaiṣamyapradarśanārthaṃ pūrvapakṣe
kṛte yadi kasyacidāśaṅkā syāt kathaṃ rāddhānta iti taṃ pratyāha---<b>rāddhāntavādī tu saṃbhava-
mātreṇaivānvayasiddheḥ na karturuddeśyatayā prayojanamastīti manyate । atassiddhaṃ karmāpi
karmaṇaḥ uddeśyatāṃ pratipadyata iti</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) R. kartṛvaśāt</note> <note>(2) G. mekamevedaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r694"/>
<head>sandigdhe tu vyavāyāt ।</head>
<p><b>upavyayata ityatra sandihyate---kiṃ sāmidhenyanuvacanasya kartā upavyānena
saṃbadhyate uta kṛts‍ne prakaraṇe</b> niviśata <b>iti</b> saṃśayamanubhāṣate ākṣep‍tum । <b>nanu
naivātroddaśakaṃ padaṃ kiñcicchrūyate anuddiṣṭapadārthakaṃ ca yat tat prakaraṇenaiva saṃbadhyate
saṃyogato'viśeṣāt prakaraṇāviśeṣāccetyuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---asaṃyuktamupavītaṃ prakaraṇe ca
paṭhyate, upavītaṃ ca vāsovinyāsarūpaṃ vāsovinyāsena ca kartā karmaṇyanākulo bhavati iti
karturevāyaṃ dharma upadiśyate । tatra ca prakaraṇagatena kartrāsya saṃbandhaḥ kathaṃ pūrvapakṣābhāvena
saṃśayaḥ ? <b>ucyate---ādhastye'dhikaraṇe anuddiṣṭenāpi</b> sannihitena <b>kartrā anvayo
na</b> virudhyata <b>ityuktam । evamatrāpi sāmidhenīnāṃ kartṛssannidhānāt</b> uk‍tena nyāyena
<b>kriyāntarārthatayā upavyānasya loke'vagatatvāt anuddiṣṭo'pi kartā sannihitaḥ kārya-
paripūraṇāyālaṃ bhavitumarhati</b> । asyārthaḥ---upavyayata ityekamidaṃ padaṃ anvitabhidhānāya
kartāramapekṣate । vinā ca kartrā'paripūrṇamidaṃ tatra sannihitena kartrā paripūraṇasamarthena eka-
vākyatāṃ yātīti yaḥ sannihitaḥ kartā sa evānena saṃskriyate ityarthaḥ । kāryāntarākāṅkṣāpyu-
pavyānasya paripūryata iti । ānantaryamacodanetyatra tu samāptatvātpadadvayaprayogādanvitābhidhānasya
nānantaryamātreṇa saṃbandhaḥ । nanvevamabhikramaṇamapi tarhi pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣe sannihitakartṛdharma
<note>(1) P. 732</note>
﻿<pb n="r695"/>
eva syāt । na । tasyānākhyātatvāt siddhavatpratīteḥ na kartrākāṅkṣā'sti । kiṃ tarhi
prakaraṇānupraveśāya śeṣībhūtaḥ kriyāntaragataḥ <b>kartā'pekṣyate</b> tena ca śeṣiṇā'nvitābhidhānam ।
iha tu prathamaṃ kartṛtvenaivāpekṣitena sannihitenāpi paripūraṇamaviruddhamiti । <q>“nanu ca darśa-
pūrṇamāsayoreva prakaraṇamidaṃ paraprakaraṇe sāmidhenyaḥ śrūyanta”</q> iti । <b>ko'sya bhāṣyasyārthaḥ</b> ।
pṛcchataścāyamabhiprāyaḥ । yadyapi paraprakaraṇe sāmidhenyaḥ tathāpi tadīyaḥ kartā sannidhānāt
saṃbadhyata eveti yukta evopavītasya sāmidhenyanuvacana evānupraveśaḥ । uttaram---<b>varṇito'smābhiḥ
uddeśapadābhāvāt prakaraṇāviśeṣaḥ</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---uddeśapadāśravaṇāt prakaraṇagṛhītatvāt
tadanuguṇadvārabhūtakartṛsaṃbandhaḥ syāt iti sāmidhenyanuvacanānupraveśaśaṅkā na yukteti pūrvapakṣākṣepaḥ ।
samādhānabhāṣyaṃ tu <q>“satyaṃ paraprakaraṇe sāmidhenyaḥ śrūyante tathāpi tāsāmavāntara-
prakaraṇaṃ bhavati”</q> iti । <b>kimidamavāntaraprakaraṇaṃ nāma</b> ? avāntaraprakaraṇamayuk‍taṃ kutaḥ ?
<b>ekasya hi adhikāravidheḥ prakaraṇaṃ nāṅgavidhīnāmapi prakaraṇamasti</b> । asyārthaḥ
---prakaraṇaśabdena niyogasya grāhakatvamucyate tathā viniyojakatvaṃ ca prakaraṇaṃ tasyaiveti-
kartavyatākāṅkṣatvalakṣaṇam । taccedamubhayamapi adhikāravidhereva tasyaiva puruṣāṇāmanuṣṭheyatayā
<b>pratītatvāt</b> । yatkhalu anuṣṭheyaṃ tatsannidhau yat samāmnāyate tat tadarthameveti । tadetat
(idaṃ tu) grāhakatvamanuṣṭheyasyaiva anuṣṭheyasya ca itikartavyatākāṅkṣatvaṃ iti na niradhikārāṇāma-
vāntaravidhīnāmapi prakaraṇamasti । nanu niradhikārataiva kutaḥ ityatrāha---<b>pradhānavidhyabhedāt</b> ।
kathamabheda ityatrāha---<b>pradhānavidhīnāṃ cābhedaṃ caturthe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । api ca sāmidhenyanuvacanaṃ
<note>(1) 732-9</note>
﻿<pb n="r696"/>
<b>saṃskārakarma saṃskārakarmasu cāvāntaraniyoga eva na saṃbhavati</b> । prayājādiṣviva pradhānavidhereva
liṅādibhiranuvāda iti kuto'vāntaraprakaraṇāśaṅkā । tadāha---<b>saṃskāravidhīnāṃ ca teṣāmarthenetya-
trānuvādaḥ pradarśita iti । tasmādavāntaraprakaraṇaṃ grāhakaviniyojakatayā nopapadyate
ataḥ sannidhānamātramavaśiṣyate</b> । samādhātā'ha---<b>ucyate sannidhāna evāyaṃ prakaraṇaśabdaḥ
prayuk‍taḥ । kathamavagamyate</b> sannidhāna eva prayukta iti । <b><q>“yena tatsannidhāvabhidhīya-
mānaṃ”</q> iti vacanāt</b> yena tatsannidhau sāmidhenyanuvacanasannidhau abhidhīyamānamupavyānaṃ
<q>‘tasyati jñāyata’</q> iti bhāṣyakāravacanāt avagamyate । sannidhāne hi saṃbandhakāraṇe
sannidhāvabhidhīyamānamiti yujyate vak‍tum । <b>nanu ca viniyojakepi prakaraṇe sannidhāna-
śrutiśabdaprayoga upapadyata eva</b> । etena nedamekāntato bhāṣyaṃ liṅgabhūtamiti । pariharati
---<b>kena vok‍taṃ nopapadyata iti</b> । <b>kintu tanna saṃbhavatīti</b> । nanu caivaṃ sati na liṅgatā bhāṣyasya
samarthitā । ucyate । āñjasyena sannidhānā1bhiprāyeṇaitadbhāṣyamupapadyate tathāpi[yadi] viniyojakaṃ
prakaraṇaṃ saṃbandhakāraṇaṃ atra nok‍taṃ syāt tadā tatparatvenānāñjasyenāpi bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyāyeta
na tvetadastīti bhavatyeva bhāṣyaṃ liṅgam । <b>vākyabhedaśravaṇācca</b> । rāddhānte vākyabhedaḥ
śrūyate tena pūrvapakṣe ekavākyatāpradarśitā ekavākyatā ca na viniyojakatvāt । nāpi
<b>grāhakatvāt</b> । kintu sannidhānāt tasmādato'pi hetoḥ sannidhāva eva prakaraṇaśabdaḥ ।
<b>vyavadhānaṃ ca darśayati</b> । rāddhāntahetutvena । tatra viniyojakaṃ yadi prakaraṇaṃ pūrvapakṣe hetu-
<note>(1) R. dhāna evābhiprā</note>
﻿<pb n="r697"/>
tvenopanyastaṃ syāt tadā nedamupapadyate । atha tu sannidhānaṃ pūrvapakṣahetutvenopanyastaṃ syāt
tadā tasya vyavadhānaṃ pratipakṣabhūtaṃ bhavet । ato'pi prakaraṇaśabdena sannidhānamevocyate ।
tadidamāha---<b>parārthena vyavadhānamānantaryaṃ vihanti na viniyogam । anyathā hi svāhā-
kārasyāpyaviniyogaḥ syāt</b> samidādibhiḥ vyavadhānāt । <b>atha mataṃ nivitpadānā-
manyārthatvāt</b> grāhakāntarasaṃbandhāt <b>grāhakasyāpi vyavadhānamiti</b> । pariharati---<b>dvāda-
śāhīnasyetyanenāpi vyavadhānaṃ grāhakasya syāt</b> । na ca tadasti । tasmāt na
grāhako vyavadhīyate । <b>kiñca kāmyairavyavadhānaṃ nivitpadānāṃ</b> grāhakasya vyavadhānābhāvāt ।
<b>tataśca nividarthatā prāpnoti upavyānasya tena rāddhānto na labhyate</b> । ānantaryavyavadhāne
punaḥ na doṣaḥ teṣāmapi hi kāmyairvyavadhānāta । na caivaṃ sati yadi nivitpadavyavadhānaṃ
kāmyāḥ sāmidhenīkalpāḥ kurvanti tarhi sāmidhenīnāmavyavadhānaṃ prāpnoti na svayamasannihitaṃ
parasya vyavadhānamāvahati tasmādva‍yavadhāyakatvābhyupagame sannidhānaṃ sāmidhenīnāmastītyabhyupaga-
nīyam । tataśca sāmidhenyanuvacanārthatopavyānasya syāt । pariharati---<b>satyaṃ propnoti</b> । <b>yadyanu-
vacanavyavadhānamatrābhipretaṃ syāt</b> tadā tadanuguṇaṃ guṇaphalasaṃbandhena anuvacanaṃ na
vyavahitamiti bhavet tadarthamupavyānam । <b>iha tu sannihitakartṛvyavadhānamabhipretaṃ, tacca
guṇaphalasaṃbandhābhidhāne sati karmaṇo vyavadhānādupapannaṃ kartṛvyavadhānam</b> । yatra hi
yatkarma vidhīyate tatra 1tadanuṣṭheyatvenāvagamyate na ca kartrā vinā tadavagatiriti vidhāne
kartā sannihito bhavati । avidhāne punaḥ karmaṇo'nuṣṭhānabuddhivicchedāt karturvyavadhānamiti ।
<note>(1) G. kartṛtānu</note>
﻿<pb n="r698"/>
nanu caivaṃ sati pūrvapakṣa eva nāsti guṇaphalasaṃbandhe karmaṇo'vidhānāt2 kartṛsannidhānābhāvāt
ityatrāha---evaṃ <b>sthite pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ guṇaphalasaṃbandhepyanuvacanaśruteḥ kartā
sannihita eveti sāmidhenyarthamupavyānam</b> । karmaṇāpi kartā sannidhāpyata iti bhāvaḥ ।
<b>rāddhāntavādī tu nāvidhīyamānaṃ3 sannihitaṃ bhavati svasthānasthitamevānuvadanīyamanūdyate
na punaḥ sannidhāpyate । anūdyamānavaśavartitvādanubādāvanām</b> । asyārthaḥ-anuvādo hi nāma
jñānāntaropasthāpitameva vastu tadupasthāpitatvenaiva punarvadati । na punaḥ svayameva vastu
svātantrayeṇaivopasthāpayati iti yuktamanūdyamānavaśavartitvam । vidheyaṃ punaḥ vidhānānuvartyeva4
bhavati iti vidhānena sannidhāpyate । <b>ataḥ sannidhānāviśeṣāt kṛts‍ne prakaraṇe niveśa
iti siddham</b> ।</p>
<head>guṇānāṃ ca parārthatvāt ।</head>
<p>atra bhāṣye sandehaḥ । kiṃ vāraṇādīni pātrāṇi pavamāneṣṭiṣu niviśante uta darśapūrṇa-
māsādiṣu sarvayogeṣviti । <b>tadupapādayannāha---vāraṇo yajñāvacara iti yajñasaṃbandhitvena
pātraṃ</b> ādhānaprakaraṇe śrūyate । tena na tāvadādhāne saṃbadhyate । <b>ānarthakyāttadaṅga-
ṣviti sthito nyāyaḥ</b> । <b>tadidānīṃ yadi pavamānahaviṣāṃ ādhānāṅgatā tataḥ pavamāna-</b>
<note>(1) P. 736</note> <note>(2) G. yadavidhānaṃ</note> <note>(3) G. nābhidhīyamānaṃ</note> <note>(4) R. nupapattyaiva</note>
﻿<pb n="r699"/>
<b>haviṣṣveva pātravidhānaṃ</b> atha nādhānāṅgatā tadā aṅgadvāreṇāṣi ādhānānanupraveśāt vākyataḥ
utkṛṣṭasya <b>sarvayajñārthatā</b> iti । kiṃ tāvad‍yuktam ? <b>pavamānahaviṣṣu vidhānam</b> ।
<b>ādhānāṅgaṃ hi pacamānahavīṃṣi</b> svavākya evādhānasya sādhyayogitvāt pavamānahaviṣāṃ ca
aphalatvāt ādhānasannidhau na śravaṇāt <b>ādhānaprakaraṇe caitat śrūyate pātram</b> । <b>pradhāne
cāsaṃbhavan dharmaḥ aṅge bhavatītyuktam</b> । <b>nanu ca pavamānahavīṃṣyapi agnyarthānyeva <q>‘yadā-
havanīye juhvati’</q> iti vacanāt</b> । tena anaṅgatā pavamānahaviṣāmiti manyate । etacca
codyaṃ(mayathāśrutārthaṃ) yathāśrutaṃ gṛhṇataḥ । parihāraḥ---<b>anārabhya vādo'yaṃ sarvahomānāṃ
guṇatvenāhavanīyaṃ vidadhāti</b> na punaḥ pavamānahavīṣi pratyāhavanīyasya prādhānyamāheti
<b>na prādhānyaṃ</b> pavamānahaviṣāṃ <b>saṃbhavati</b> kintu ādhānāṅgataiveti । <b>tasmādānarthakyātta-
daṅgeṣviti pavamānahaviṣṣu vidhānam</b> । <b>atrābhidhīyate---naivādhānaprakaraṇe pavamānaharvīṣi
śrūyante nāpyagnyarthānyeva</b> । <b>kathaṃ</b> ? <b>yadāhavanīye juhotīti vacanāt</b> । prākṛte yāge
āhavanīyo vartate । taddharmagrāhiṇīṣvapi vikṛtibhūtāsu pavamāneṣṭiṣu codakenāhavanīyaḥ prāpyate ।
pavamāneṣṭīnāṃ ca sādhyabhūtāgnisannidhau paṭhitānāṃ avaśyaṃbhāvitādarthyānāṃ guṇabhāvena saṃbandhāsaṃbhave
sati <b>guṇabhāvamātre asaṃbhavena bādhite sākṣātsambandhasyābādhitatvāt sākṣātsaṃbandhainaiva tādarthya---
mavagamyata iti । bhavanti ca pavamāneṣṭayo'pyagnyarthāḥ nādhānārthā iti । imamabhiprāyamabudhvā</b>
﻿<pb n="r700"/>
codayati---<b>nanu guṇatayā vidadhāsyanārabhyavādo'yamityuktam</b> । abhiprāyamāviṣkaroti
---<b>na brūmo na guṇatayā vidadhātīti</b> । <b>kintu atra prakṛtitaḥ prāptipradarśanārthaṃ evaṃ bacana-
mupanyastam</b> yadāhavanīye juhotīti <b>nopadeśārthaṃ</b> sati hyasmin vacane prakṛtāvaṅgatā,
tataśca vikṛtāvatideśataḥ prāptirityetadarthaṃ vacanamupanyastam na punaranenaiva vacanena pradhānatayā
āhavanīya upadiśyata ityevamartham । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ prakṛtitaḥ prāptau prādhānyaṃ bhavati</b> ?
ekagranthenābhiprāyamāviṣkaroti---<b>nanu ca prakṛtito'pyaṅgatayaiva prāptiḥ</b> kāryanibandhanatvāt
prāpteḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>satyamevaṃ ādhānopakārakatā tu agniniṣpattyā bhavati</b> । yo hi
pavamānahaviṣyaṅgatvamādhānasyecchati icchatyevāsau pavamānahaviṣāṃ abhyutpādakatvam । tataśca
teṣvagneḥ guṇabhāvaḥ na saṃbhavati prāgeva tebhyaḥ svarūpāniṣpatteḥ । tataśca guṇabhāvamātre bādhite
sākṣātsaṃbandhāṃśasyābādhanāt yat tadutpādakatvamādhānāṅgatayā'dhyavasitaṃ tatsākṣādeveti
<b>niścīyate</b> । tadāha---<b>agniniṣpattiścetprayojanaṃ kimityādhānopakārakatayā</b> niṣpāda-
yati---<b>na punaḥ sākṣātprakṛtitaḥ saṃbandhāt</b> । <b>nanu ca guṇatayā prakṛtitaḥ prāptirityukta</b>-
mabhiprāyaṃ spaṣṭayituṃ prāguk‍tameva codyamupanyastam । <b>satyamuk‍tam</b> । <b>sā punarādhānāṅgatve-
'ṅgīkiyamāṇe na saṃbhavati aniṣpannatvādag‍neḥ</b> pavamāneṣṭibhyaḥ prāgiti śeṣaḥ ।
<b>niṣpādayatīti cet</b> yadi niṣpādayatītyaṅgīkriyate <b>siddhaṃ tarhi sākṣānniṣpādakatvaṃ uk‍tena</b>
﻿<pb n="r701"/>
nyāyena । na hi sākṣātsabandhasaṃbhave <b>parapṛṣṭhena saṃbandho</b> yuktaḥ । tasmādanaṅgatvāt
tanmukhenāpi ādhānānupraveśābhāvāt utkṛṣṭasya sataḥ <b>sarvārthatā vāraṇāderyuk‍teti</b> ।</p>
</section>
<section>
<head>mithaścānarthasaṃbandhaḥ ।</head>
<p>nanu ca punaruktamidamadhikaraṇaṃ ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣvityanenādhikaraṇenetyāśaṅkyāha
---<b>tadevedaṃ punararudāharaṇāntare cintyate kenacidviśeṣeṇa ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣviti । kaḥ
punarviśeṣaḥ । ayamasau viśeṣaḥ । tatra yūpaśabdaḥ śrūyate yaḥ</b> sākṣātsaṃbandhe nopapadyate
iha punaḥ nājyabhāgābhidhānamasti yena 1ya[ta]thā svabhāvasaṃbandhitayā vārtraghnatāṃ vṛghanvattāṃ ca
vidadhyāt ataḥ <b>pūrvapakṣavādī manyate yuktaṃ vājapeye yūpaśabdābhidhānāt vyavadhānepi
vājapeyaśabdasyānvaya iti । iha punaḥ saṃbandhisaṃbandhyanvaye</b> saṃbandhināvājyabhāgau tatsaṃbandhi
yadanuvacanaṃ tadanvaye vārtraghnatāvṛdhanvattayoḥ nasti <b>kiñcitkāraṇamiti । kathaṃ tarhi dvivacanaṃ</b>
anūcyete iti । <b>ekagranthenāha---dvayordvivacanam । nanu caikatvātpradhānasya ekaivānuvākyā</b>
syāt tataśca dvivacanānuvādo na ghaṭate । <b>kimidaṃ ekatvātpradhānasyeti</b> । ekagranthe-
<note>(1) G. ājyabhāva/?/</note>
﻿<pb n="r702"/>
nāha---<b>nanu caikatra pradhānatrayamasti</b> paurṇamāsyāmapi trīṇi pradhānāni āg‍neyagnīṣomopāṃśusaṃjña-
kāni amāvāsyāyāmapi trīṇyeva āgneyaindrāgnasānnāyyarūpāṇi । etacca prayogāvasthābhedena
āgneyasya bhedamaṅgīkṛtyoktam ।</p>
<p><b>na brūmaḥ ekameva pradhānamiti । kintu ekaikasyetikartavyatāsaṃbandha iti
vadāmaḥ । tataḥ kiṃ dvayorasaṃbandhaḥ</b> dvayormilitayoritikartavyatāsaṃbandho nāsti pratyekaṃ
karaṇatvāt karaṇādvāratvāccetikartavyatāyāḥ pratikaraṇamitikartavyatāsaṃbandha iti । ekasmin
pradhāne ekaivānuvākyeti dvivacanānupapattiḥ । evaṃ ca siddhāntāśayena codite pūrvapakṣāśaye-
nāha---<b>nanu cājyabhāgayorapi ekaikenetikartavyatāsaṃbandha</b> iti tulyā dvivacanānupapattiḥ ।
<b>satyameva tatra śrutyā tu dvayotpatteḥ dvandvābhidhānamaviruddham</b> । asyārthaḥ---ājyabhāgau yajatī-
tyekaśeṣeṇa ājyabhāgayoritaretarayuktayorutpattiḥ । tena tāmavasthāmālocya pradhānayorita-
retarayogo nāpavadituṃ śakyate dvandvaśabdena ca dvandvārthabhūtetaretarayogābhidhāyakatvādekaśeṣasyābhidhānaṃ
ekaśeṣotpatterekaśeṣābhidhānamaviruddhamityarthaḥ । <b>iha punaḥ pradhāne svata ekatvāt anuvākyāyāḥ
ekaikasyāścotpatteḥ pradhānānāṃ dvandvavirodhaḥ</b> । evamākṣipya pūrvapakṣaṃ samarthayamāna āha
<b>na virodho dvitvasya kiṃ hi vacanaṃ na kuryāt tatra hi dvitvaṃ ayathārthatvaṃ ca mantrasya
bhaviṣyati vyavadhāne pramāṇābhāvādityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---vyavadhāne pramāṇābhāvāt
sākṣādeva pradhāne vidhirayam । tatra hi vibhiktyarthabhūtadvitvaviśiṣṭamantraviśeṣavidhirastu । na
﻿<pb n="r703"/>
cānekaguṇavidhānadoṣaḥ samāsanyāyena śrutyaiva pratyayārthaviśiṣṭasya prakṛtyarthasya vidhānāditi ।
tenaikasyāmanuvākyāyāṃ prāptāyāṃ dve vidhīyete । nanu ca sārdha[svārtha]manuvākye ekasmin
pradhāne vidhīyamāne devatāmabhivadituṃ na śak‍nutaḥ । tatredamuttaraṃ---<b>ayathārthatvaṃ ca dvitvaṃ ca
mantrasya bhaviṣyati</b> aindrīvaditi pūrvapakṣaḥ । rāddhāntamāha---<b>atrocyate tadidamayuktamabhihita-
miti vadāmaḥ । kasmāt ? na tatrāpi yūpaśabdābhidhānaṃ</b> svarūpeṇaiva tadaṅgatve hetuḥ ।
kiṃ tarhi ? yupaśabdaśravaṇāt tadviśiṣṭasya saptadaśāratnitvasya <b>vidheyasyāṅgasaṃbandhayogyatā ।
saṃbhavati ca yogyatayā</b> saṃbandhitve vidheyasya <b>vājapeyasyetyasyānvaya ityuk‍taṃ tatraiva ।
evamatrāpi saṃbhavati yathāyogyamantravidhāne(nāya) yathārthatvadvitvayoḥ pramāṇamasti</b> ।
paraṃ vidheyasya yogyatānusāreṇa vyavadhānena saṃbandho na punaḥ vidheyasyānyathākaraṇamiti bhāvaḥ ।
<b>tasmādājyabhāgayoreva mantravidhānamiti siddham । yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyaṃ---nanu pradhāna-
gāmitve'pi dvayoḥ pradhānayoḥ dve anuvākye syātāṃ āgneyasya cāgnīṣomīyasya ceti
tatkathaṃ ? dvandvotpattervirodhāt</b> dvandvotpattiḥ pradhānayoritaretarayogaḥ tasyābhāvāt
dvivacanavirodhāt kathamidaṃ bhāṣyamityarthaḥ । <b>abhyupagamyāpyavirodhaṃ yuktyantareṇa</b> mantra-
liṅgānupapattilakṣaṇena parapakṣe <b>virodhamadarśanārtham</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) p. 739</note>
﻿<pb n="r704"/>
<head>ānantaryamacodanā ।</head>
<p><b>yadi vyāpārāntarayogyatā niyamahetuḥ ihāpi staraṇe dīkṣitāvedane ca parisamāptaiva
yogyatā ityatraivaidamarthyaparisamāptiriti</b> । anenāvāntaraṅgatiṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ cāha---arthastu
hastāvanejanaṃ bā/?/gyamanaṃ ca puruṣasaṃskārau saṃskāraśca kāryāntare yogyatārūpa iti kriyāntarā-
pekṣāyāṃ pūrvavadvidheyasya sannihitasaṃbandhayogyatvāt bhavatu sannihitakarmārthameva saṃskāravidhānamiti ।
<b>atrābhidhīyate---satyaṃ yadyatraiva yogyatā । kṛts‍nepi prakaraṇe sā, tathaiva yadi parameka-
vākyatāṃ niyantuṃ kṣamā sā ca nāsti dvayorākhyātayorasaṃbandhāt</b> tumun‌ṇvulau <b>kriyāyāṃ
kriyārthāyāṃ bhavataḥ tau ca na staḥ ato'saṃyuk‍tatvāt kṛts‍naprakaraṇe niveśa</b> iti
siddham ।</p>
<p><b>śeṣastu । kaḥ punaratra pūrvapakṣiṇo'bhiprāyaḥ āgneyepi saṃbhavati aindrāg‍ne'pi bhavatīti
āgneyaṃ</b> caturdhā karotīti śrūyate । tenāg‍neye bhavitavyam naindrāgne । yadi vā āgneyaḥ
kevalo na saṃbhavati tadaivaṃ kalpyeta । asti ca āgneyaḥ kevalaḥ agnirdevateti । ayamabhi-
<note>(1) P. 740</note>
﻿<pb n="705"/>
<b>prāyaḥ---uddeśe hi padārthamātrasyaivāgneḥ anapekṣitadevatābhāvasyopalakṣaṇatvaṃ sambandhimātra-
tayaiva</b> viśeṣāvagamasiddheḥ <b>na viśeṣa upalakṣaṇasyāgnerapekṣaṇīyaḥ । vidheye punaḥ viśeṣa-
niṣṭhatvātkāryasya anuṣṭhānasya yuk‍taṃ viśeṣāpekṣaṇam । tasmādāgneyasya vidhau agni-
daivatyasya vidhiḥ na punaraindrāgnavidhiḥ । upalakṣaṇe punaḥ padārthamātrasyobhayatrānugatatvāt
na virodhaḥ</b> āg‍neyaśabdasya । yata eva saṃbandhimātratayā agnerupalakṣaṇatvaṃ aindrāgne cāsti
saṃbandhitvaṃ pratyekaṃ parisamāptaṃ <b>ata eva cāvyāsajyasaṃbandhiḍitthaḍavitthadarśanam</b> ।</p>
<head>vyavasthā vā ।</head>
<p><b>atrābhidhīyate । yathā bhavānāha tathāpi tu yathābhidheyaṃ 1lakṣaṇāsambhave
nāyathārthāvagatirbhavatīti</b> । agnividhau devatābhāvena saṃbandhītyupalakṣaṇatvepi tenaiva saṃbandhe-
nopalakṣako yukta iti । na punaḥ anyathopalakṣakatvam । asaṃbhave syādapyevaṃ asti tvatra saṃbhavaḥ
<b>ato nāprasiddhalakṣaṇā bhavitumarhati । yathāprasiddhasaṃbandhābhāve tu aprasiddhasaṃbandha</b>-
<note>(1) R. lakṣaṇasaṃbhave</note>
﻿<pb n="706"/>
<b>nimittatāpi gṛhyate । tasmādāgneyasyaiva caturdhākaraṇamiti siddham । ḍitthādīnāṃ tu
pratyekameva</b> saṃbandhitvena <b>prasiddhiḥ । āgneyastu pratyuk‍taḥ</b> 1āgneyasya mastakaṃ virujya
iti yaḥ pūrvapakṣiṇoktaḥ sa rāddhāntinā nirākṛto bhāṣya eva ।</p>
<trailer>iti ṛjuvimalāpañcikāyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="r707"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<head>arthābhidhānasaṃyogāt ।</head>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāro vicāradvayaṃ kurute---kiṃ gauṇe'pi mantrāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ uta mukhya
eveti । kaḥ punarmukhyaḥ ko vā gauṇa iti । tatra dvitīyavicāramākṣipati---<b>yuk‍taṃ tāvat
kiṃ mukhya evārthe mantrāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ uta gauṇe'pīti । idantvayuktam---kaḥ punarmukhyaḥ
ko vā gauṇa iti । kathamayuktam ? yaḥ paraśabdaḥ paratra vartate sa gauṇa iti sthitam4</b> ।
ataḥ punaruk‍to'yamartha iti manyate । tathā ca tatsiddha‍yadhikaraṇe <b>darśitam । kathaṃ punaḥ para-
śabdaḥ paratravartate ? svārthābhidhāneneti । tasmādayukto'yaṃ praśnaḥ । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ lakṣaṇā-
yāmapi paraśabdaḥ paratra vartate tadva‍yāvṛttyartho'yaṃ praśnaḥ iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---yo'yaṃ gauṇa-
mukhyāpraśnaḥ sa lakṣaṇāgauṇavivekārthaḥ । tatsiddha‍yadhikaraṇok‍taṃ gauṇam । lakṣaṇayā paraśabdaḥ
<note>(1) P. 745</note> <note>(2) P. 746-1</note> <note>(3) P. Brhati Part III P. 260</note>
<note>(4) G. iti lakṣaṇāyāmapyaviśiṣṭam</note>
﻿<pb n="708"/>
paratra vartata iti sa gauṇa iti lakṣaṇāyāmapyaviśiṣṭam । iha evaṃ gauṇamukhyapraśne kṛte
gauṇasvarūpaṃ varṇyate yathā mukhyāllākṣaṇikācca bhinnimavabhāsate । tatra mukhyāt bhedaḥ tatsiddha‍yadhi-
karaṇe jñāpita iti iha lākṣaṇikāt bhedajñānaṃ praśnottarayoḥ prayojanam । <b>tannopapadyate, yadeva
hi gauṇatve lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyati---‘anādṛtyaiva māṇavakapratyayaṃ jvalanamagniśabdāt pratiyanto
dṛśyante na tvanādṛtya jvalanapratyayaṃ māṇavakaṃ pratiyanti iti lakṣaṇāyāmapyevameva । na hyanā-
dṛtyaiva gaṅgāpratyayaṃ gaṅgāsamīpaṃ pratiyanti</b> । asyārthaḥ-lakṣaṇābhedajñānārtho'pi nopapadyate,
yasmāt yadeva gauṇalakṣaṇaṃ praśnāsyottarabhāṣyaṃ vakṣyati <q>‘arthāntarānapekṣo mukhyārthaḥ, arthāntarasavya-
pekṣaśca gauṇaḥ yathā'gnipratyayāpekṣo'gniśabdo māṇavake’</q> iti tadeva lakṣaṇāyāmapi gaṅgāpratyayāpekṣa-
eva gaṅgaśabdāt gaṅgāsamīpapratyaya iti । tasmādekalakṣaṇatvāt <b>tannivṛttyarthaṃ</b> lakṣaṇānivṛttya-
rthamapi praśnottaramidaṃ <b>na śakyate vak‍tum । atha mataṃ lakṣaṇāyāmanveti lakṣaṇāpadaṃ</b> gaṅgāsaṃbaddha-
syaiva samīpasyānvayāt <b>gauṇe punaḥ na guṇipadamanveti</b> । agnirmāṇavaka iti agnisaṃbandhimāṇa-
vakāpratīte । ato lākṣaṇikagauṇayoḥ evaṃ bhedaṃ vak‍tuṃ praśnaḥ । <b>tadayuk‍taṃ pratītau tāvat
dvayamapyanveti । kārye punaḥ naikamapi</b> । gaṅgāpi pratītāvevānvayinī na kārye samīpasyaiva
kāryānvayāt tathā'gnirapi pratītāvevānvayī agnisadṛśapratīteḥ । kārye punaḥ naikamapyanvayi ।
<b>ato'nenāpi viśeṣaṇena na viśeṣaḥ । atha vākyārthanivṛttaye yat‍naḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ
<note>(1) P. 748</note>
﻿<pb n="r709"/>
---atha manyase agnirmāṇavaka ityasmāt agnisadṛśo māṇavaka iti pratītirudeti । sā ca na
padamātranibandhanā agniśabdasyāgnisadṛśe loke saṃbandhānavabodhāt । kintu padadvayaprayogāt
iyamavagatirjāyamānā vākyanimittiketi vyavasthāpyate । tena gauṇārtho vākyārthaḥ iti ye
manyante tannivṛttyarthaṃ svārthasādṛśyāt gauṇaḥ pratīyata iti idaṃ gauṇasya svarūpaṃ darśayituṃ ayaṃ
praśna iti । <b>naivārthāntare vākyaṃ vartate</b> । asyārthaḥ---vākyādeva gauṇaḥ pratīyate iti
atimandeyamāśaṅkā । tathā hi---<b>naiva vākyaṃ padārthebhyaḥ vyatirikte'rthāntare vartate । yadi</b>
tat padārthebhyo vyatirikte arthāntare vākyaṃ vartate tadā syādiyamāśaṅkā, na tvetadasti । nanu
ca svarūpamātreṇa vyavasthito'rthaḥ padārthaḥ । parasparānvitāstvarthāḥ vākyārthaḥ । evamarthāntare
vākyaṃ vartata itīmāmāśaṅkāṃ apanayannāha---<b>anvitābhidhāyīni padānyeva hi vākyam ।
anvitāśca padārthāḥ vākyārthaḥ</b> । ekaikameva padaṃ svamarthaṃ arthāntareṇa yogyena ākāṅkṣitena
sannihitena cānvitaṃ svārthaṃ bravīti । tathābhūtānyeva vākyam । anvitāśca padairevārthāḥ
ucyanta iti padārthā eva vākyārthaḥ । yathā bahuṣu padeṣu padārtheṣu vākyamekaṃ vākyārthaścaikaḥ
tathā <b>vākyārthamātṛkāyāmuktam</b> । anvitābhidhānameva kutaḥ ityāha---<b>na cānanvitā-
bhidhānamastīti pradarśitaṃ</b> tad‌bhūtādhikaraṇe; <b>vākyārthamātṛkāyāṃ ca</b> asmābhiḥ
nirloḍitameva । <b>evaṃ ca sati praśnārthaḥ vyākhyeyaḥ</b> praśnaprayojanaṃ kathanīyam । atha
kadāciducyate sopapadāt pratīyamāno gauṇaḥ, mandaprasiddho gauṇaḥ, alpaprayogaviṣayo gauṇaḥ,
iti imān siddhāntābhāsināṃ gauṇahetūn nirākartumayaṃ praśna iti tatrāha---<b>evaṃ sopapadasuṣṭhu-
prasiddhavahuśaḥ prayogāśca</b> yathāyathaṃ gauṇahetu mukhyahetu(matta)tayā <b>pratyuktā bhāṣye । ataḥ
tannirākaraṇārtho'pyayaṃ praśno nopapadyata iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---atimandatvātteṣāṃ hetūnāṃ
﻿<pb n="r710"/>
tannirākaraṇāya praśno nopapadyata iti । na hi māṇavakaśabdopapadādapi agniśabdādarthaḥ
pratīyamānastāvat gauṇatvenāvagantuṃ śakyate yāvattu svārthasādṛśyena gauṇapratyaya iti
nopavarṇyate । itarathā pratītyanyathānupapattyā bodhakatvakalpanaiva syāditi sopapadādapyavācakānna
pratītirutpadyate । evaṃ mandaprasiddha‍yapracuraprayogayorapi yojyam ।</p>
<p><b>ucyate---ayaṃ praśnasyārthaḥ vākyārthāvagamāddhi nimittatayā padārthavibhāgo'va-
gamyate</b> । vākyāditi lyablope pañcamī viśiṣṭārthapratipādakaṃ vākyamupalabhya vṛddhavyavahāre
nimittatayā vākyārthapratipattinimittatayā padārthānāṃ vibhāgo'vagamyate । viśiṣṭarūpo
vākyārtha iti viśeṣaṇabhūtaḥ padārthaḥ tatpratipattau nimittaṃ bhavati nāpratīte viśeṣaṇe viśiṣṭaḥ
śakyate pratipat‍tumiti nimittatayā padārthavibhāgo'vagamyate । tataḥ kimityatrāha---<b>sa cāyaṃ</b>
nimittatvena vibhāgo <b>māṇavake</b> māṇavakaviṣaye agnau agniviṣaye ca prayujyamānasyāgni-
śabdasya tulyaḥ । ubhayatrāpi vācakavṛttyaiva nimittateti yāvat । taddarśayati---<b>agnirmāṇa-
vaka ityuk‍te māṇavakaḥ piṅgalatā ca nimittam । agnirjvalatīti jvalano jvalanakriyā
ca । tasmānna viśeṣaṃ paśyāmaḥ asya śābdo nimittabhāvo'sya gauṇaḥ iti</b> na tu mukhyasya
ca gauṇasya ca bhedaṃ paśyāmaḥ । sarva eva mukhya iti yāvat । <b>nanu cāgnipratyayapurassarā
māṇavake pratītiḥ paiṅgalyasya</b> । asyārthaḥ---agniśabdasya tāvat nānekārthakalpanā nyāyyā ।
ekārthapratipādanaśaktyaivārthāntarapratītisiddheḥ । tathā hi---agniśabdādagniḥ pratītaḥ piṅgalatā-
mupasthāpayati । ato'gnipratītipurassaraiva māṇavake pratītiḥ । <b>pariharati---naivaṃ śakyate</b>
﻿<pb n="r711"/>
<b>vaktum । uktamidaṃ vākyānnimittabhāvāvagatiriti</b> । tena vākyārthaṃ prati yasya
nimittabhāvo'vagamyate sa padārthaḥ na cātrāgnyarthasya nimittabhāva upapadyate---<b>agnirmāṇavaka
iti kevalaṃ piṅgalataiva nimittatayā'vagamyate । yathā piṅgalo māṇavaka iti</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---na svarūpeṇa tāvadagnyarthasya nimittatā, vākyārthe asamavāyāt । na
ca lakṣaṇāyāmiva vākyārthasamavāyipiṅgalopasthāpakatayā; māṇavakavartinyāḥ piṅgalatāyāḥ
agninā saha saṃbandhābhāvāt । artho hyarthāntaraṃ pratyāsattyā upasthāpayati । gaṅgā'pi hi
tīraṃ lakṣayantī svasaṃbandhinameva lakṣayati । ato na sākṣāt nāpi paramparayā agninimittatā
agyarthasya । ataḥ piṅgalatāmeva agniśabdaḥ piṅgalaśabdavat pratipādayatīti sthitam ।
<b>tasmāt durnirūpamidaṃ gauṇo'yaṃ mukhyo'yaṃ iti manvānasya praśnaḥ</b> । guṇādāgata iti
tata āgata ityaṇ । mukhyamiti “śākhādibhyo ya iti ivārthe yaḥ । nanvevaṃ gauṇatā
nirūpyate---yadi piṅgalaśabdavadagniśabdo'pi paiṅgalyaṃ vācakavṛttyaivāha, kimiti tarhi
sopapadastatra vartate ? yāvatā nirupapado'pi tatra varteta tathā mandaprasiddhiḥ kimiti laukikānāṃ ?
tathā kimiti vā alpaprayogatā ? suṣṭha prasiddhipracuraprayogate vā syātāṃ aviśeṣādityatrāha
---<b>na hi copapadādibhirapi</b> upādhibhiḥ <b>saṃbhavatīti darśitaṃ bhāṣye</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ
---pratītirhi kāryarūpā aṃnyathānupapadyamānā kāraṇaṃ kalpayantī śabde vācakatvakalpanāyāṃ
heturbhavati । agnirmāṇavaka iti ca piṅgalatāvagatiranyathā nopapadyata ityuktam । tena vācakataiva,
anyathā sopapadādapi pratītirna syāt । avācakasya manāk‌prasiddhiralpaprayogatā ca durghaṭaiva ।
vācakatve tu prayoganiyamasyāpyanāditvāt nānupapannaṃ kiñcit ।</p>
<p>nanu yadi piṅgalaśabdavadagniśabdo'pi piṅgalaṃ māṇavakameva vakti kathaṃ tarhi agni-
sādṛśyaṃ atrāha---<b>agniriva māṇavaka ityatra yuktamagnisādṛśyaṃ ivādīnāṃ sādṛśye prayoga-</b>
﻿<pb n="r712"/>
<b>darśanāt । agnirmāṇavaka iti tu ivārthaśūnyo'rthaḥ1 vākyārthaḥ yathā piṅgalo māṇavaka
iti tulyo nimittabhāvaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---agnirivāyaṃ māṇavaka ityuk‍te sādṛśyaṃ yatpratīyate
tad‌yuk‍taṃ ivaśabdaśravaṇāt tasya ca sādṛśye prayogadarśanāt । agnirmāṇavaka iti tu
ivaśabdāprayogāt ivārthaśūnyo vākyārthaḥ yathā piṅgalo māṇavaka iti nāsti sādṛśye pratītiḥ
ivārthaśūnyatvāt vākyārthasyābhimatasya । tasmāt gauṇamukhyābhimatayoḥ tulyo nimittabhāvaḥ
vācakavṛttyaiveti । <b>ato niṣprayojanamidamadhikaraṇaṃ</b> । ke gauṇe'pi viniyogaḥ uta mukhya
eveti manyāmahe gauṇamukhyayorbhedābhāvāditi । nanu yadyapi piṅgalatā'bhidhīyate tathāpi
tadavagatyā sādṛśyamapi pratīyamānaṃ vākyārthe'nvitameva । ataḥ kathaṃ ivārthaśūnyo vākyārthaḥ ।
athāvinābhūtamapi2 sādṛśyaṃ vākyārthe nānveti <b>kathaṃ tarhi gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣaḥ kūpe gargakulamiti</b> ।
atra hi avinābhāvāt samīpadeśaḥ vākyārthe'nvīyata iti manyāmahe । <b>yuk‍taṃ tatra
prativasatītyasya sāmarthyaṃ na bhavatīti samīpānvayitā</b>3 nāvinābhāvo'vagata ityetāvatā
samīpasyānvayitā, kintu prativasatītyasya padasya sāmarthyaṃ na bhavatīti yuktam । <b>agnirmāṇa-
vaka iti tu piṅgalamāṇavakāvagatiḥ na kathaṃ cinnopapadyate</b> । ataḥ pratītamapi sādṛśyaṃ
vākyārthe nānvīyate । <b>tasmādbhavatu lakṣaṇā</b> saṃbandhabalotthāpitārthāntaratātparyāśrayaṇāt ।
<b>gauṇatve tu na kiñcitpramāṇamasti</b> । yadi piṅgalatāmevāgniśabdo <b>vakti kathaṃ tarhi
agnirmāṇavaka ityatrāgnipratyayo loke paiṅgalyādapyupapadyate</b> । agniśabdena paiṅgalyaṃ
<note>(1) G. śūnyatvāt vākyārthasya</note> <note>(2) G. avinābhūtameva</note> <note>(3) G. samīpānva-
yitvena</note>
﻿<pb n="r713"/>
vatpratipadita tatkila satiśayaṃ agnau pratītamityagnipratyayaḥ <b>pūrvādiyāparapratyayaḥ । atrābhi-
dhīyate---ivārthanibandhana evāyaṃ pratyayaḥ । asyārthaḥ</b>---ivārthaḥ sādṛśyaṃ tannibandhana evāyaṃ
pratyayaḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati । agniśabdenāgniḥ pratipādyate 1sā pratītiḥ sadṛśyamarthāntaramupa-
sthāpayati । ato'nyathāpyarthāntarapratīterupapannatvāt na śaktyantarakalpanopapadyate । tena
śabdādeva yo jvalanaḥ pratītaḥ <b>sa mukhyaḥ yastu</b> śabdapratipādyajvalanasādṛśyādavagamyate sa gauṇaḥ ।
<b>kutaḥ</b> punaravagamyate sādṛśyādayaṃ pratyaya iti ? <b>tathāvagateḥ</b> sadṛśāvagateḥ । yadi
tāvat piṅgalatāvagamyate tadā agniśabdaḥ piṅgalatāvacana iti kathyate । yatastvagnisadṛśā-
vagatiḥ ataḥ sādṛśyādevārthāntarāvagatiḥ kalpyate ।</p>
<p><b>kathaṃ punarivaśabdamantareṇevārthaḥ pratīyate ? uttaraṃ---ivaśabdo'pi tāvat
kimitīvārthaḥ kalpyate asyārthaḥ</b>---yathā ivaśabde prayuk‍te sādṛśyaṃ pratīyate tathā yatrāpi
sādṛśyaṃ pratyeṣyate ivaśabdo'pi pratipadikopāttameva sādṛśyaṃ pratipādayati na punaḥ sādṛśya-
śabdavata svatantra eva brabīti । <b>prayogadarśanāditi cet</b> । atha manyase prayogastatra
sādṛśye prātipadikasya dṛśyate ivaśabdabalāt । yatra punaḥ ivaśabdo dyotako nāsti tatra kathaṃ
sādṛśye prayogo'vagamyate । dūṣayati---<b>atrāpi tulyaṃ</b> prayogadarśanam māṇavakaviṣaye agni-
śabdaprayogāta sādṛśye prayuktiravasīyate anyathā māṇavake prayogānupapatteḥ । <b>nanu ca paiṅgalye-
'vagate jvalanasādṛśyamavagamyate aparaśabdavadityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---agniśabdaḥ piṅgalatā-
mabhivadati । tasyāṃ cāvagatāyāṃ jvalanasādṛśyāvagatiḥ । na punaḥ jvalanasādṛśyaparo'yaṃ
prayoga iti na gauṇatvam । <b>pariharati---naitadupapadyate māṇavakasadṛśo'gnirityapi pratyayaḥ</b>
<note>(1) G. sa pratītaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r714"/>
<b>syāt</b> । piṅgale māṇavake'vagate māṇavakasadṛśo'gnirityapi pratyayaḥ syāt । tathā hi
---māṇavakaḥ piṅgalo'gnisadṛśaḥ tathā'gnirapi māṇavakena sadṛśa iti māṇavakasadṛśo'gniriti
pratītiḥ syāt । niyamena tu agnisadṛśatāyāmeva pratipattiḥ tadāha---<b>iha tu punarviparītam ।
atiṣaiṅgalyājjvalanasyopamānatvamiti cet</b> । upamīyate yena tadupamānaṃ atipiṅgalatvā-
dag‍neḥ tenaivānyadupamīyate na punarasāvanyeneti cet । uttaraṃ---<b>nāsyāṃ kalpanāyāṃ pramāṇa-
masti</b> । yasyātiśayo guṇaḥ tasyaivopamānatvamiti । nanvevamapi avagatirastu māṇavaka---
sadṛśo'gniriti; bhavatu piṅgalatāvācaka evāgniśabdaḥ tatrāha---<b>yathāvagamaṃ hi nimittakalpanā
nyāyyā । tanmūlatvannimittābagateḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā'bhimataṃ hi vādinaḥ tathā
nimittakalpanā nāsti । kintu yathāvagamaṃ, avagamalakṣaṇakāryanibandhanatvāt nimittabhāvā-
vagateḥ । <b>ato yadyapi viparīto'rthaḥ saṃbhavati</b> māṇavakasadṛśo'gnirityevaṃrūpaḥ <b>tathāpi
prasiddhapratipakṣatvānnātmānaṃ labhate</b> । pratipakṣastasya agnisadṛśo māṇavaka iti prasiddhiḥ ।
ato nātmānaṃ labhate māṇavakasadṛśo'gniriti । <b>apratipakṣo1 hi saṃbhavaḥ saṃbhavaḥ</b> । na hi
saṃbhavamātreṇa pratipakṣatvaṃ, māṇavakasadṛśo'gnirityasya saṃbhavati । <b>tasmādupapannaṃ prayogapratya-
yābhyāṃ gauṇamukhyābhidhānam</b> । sthite <b>gauṇamukhyatve kiṃ mukhya evābhidheye mantrāṇāṃ
viniyogaḥ uta gauṇe'pīti yukto vicāraḥ । kiṃ tāvatprāptam ? aviśeṣādubhayābhidhānaṃ</b>
gauṇasya ca mukhyasya ca śabdātpratīyamānatayā aviśeṣādubhayoḥ mantrābhidhānaṃ yuktam ।
tadāha---<b>agnirjvalatītyapi prayogo dṛṣṭaḥ agnirmāṇavaka ityapi । tasmānna</b> vinigamanāyāṃ
<note>(1) G. kṣo'gnisaṃbhavaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r715"/>
heturasti । <b>atrābhidhīyate</b>---ayamasti vinigamanāyāṃ hetuḥ <b>mukhyābhidhānaśūnyaṃ nāsti
gauṇābhidhānamiti pradarśitam । tasmānmukhya eva śabdasya vyāpāraḥ</b> gauṇe tvarthādavagatiḥ ।
bhavatu mukhya eva śabdavyāpāraḥ tathāpi kimityatrāha---<b>abhidhānena ca mantrā upakurvanti ।
mukhye cābhidhānaṃ na gauṇe</b> । ato na mantraviniyogaḥ । <b>kutastarhi gauṇapratyayaḥ</b> ।
yadi śabdāt gauṇapratyayo na bhavati kutastarhi sa ityarthaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>sādṛśyāditi</b> ।
pratīto'g‍niḥ sadṛśamupasthāpayatītyarthaḥ । pūrvapakṣyāha---<b>satyamuktaṃ</b> sādṛśyādgauṇāvagatiriti ।
<b>tat‍tūpāyatvena na punaḥ nimittanirākaraṇatayāpi1</b> । tathāpi nimittatā na nirākṛtetyarthaḥ ।
ato nimittatvasyobhayatrāviśeṣāt gauṇepi mantrāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ । rāddhāntī tu brūte---<b>kena voktaṃ
nimittatā nirākriyata iti । mukhye</b> prathamopanipātini viniyogasaṃbhavāta <b>na gauṇepi
pāścātye viniyogaḥ kṣamaḥ</b> grāhakagrahaṇamantrāmnāmayoḥ kṛtārthatvāt <b>ityetāvaducyate yatra punaḥ
mukhye</b> viniyogo <b>na saṃbhavati tatra gauṇepi viniyogaḥ</b> । yadi tasya mukhye viniyogo na
saṃbhavati tasya gauṇe viniyogaḥ । <b>na tarhi pūṣādyanumantraṇādīnāṃ utkarṣaḥ</b> prakaraṇe pūṣṇo-
'bhāvāt । anyatra pauṣṇe karmaṇi sāmānyasaṃbandhābhāvena liṅgādviniyogānupapatteḥ । pari-
harati---<b>samākhyāyā viniyuktānāṃ</b> anumantraṇamantra ityanayā samākhyayā sāmānyānumantraṇa-
<note>(1) G. R. karaṇatayaiva</note>
﻿<pb n="r716"/>
saṃbandhasiddheḥ <b>liṅgānmukhya eva</b> prakaraṇāntaravartini <b>viniyogaḥ saṃbhavatītyutkarṣaḥ</b> । upasaṃharati
---<b>tasmāt mukhye yatra saṃpratyayaḥ</b> na tatra gauṇepi mantreṇaiva prakāśanaṃ kāryamiti <b>niyame
pramāṇamasti iti</b> । tadidaṃ sarvaṃ <b>kimarthaṃ mukhye pratyāyayatītyevamādinā pradarśitamiti</b> ।</p>
</section>
<section>
<head>vacanāttvayathārthamaindrī syāt ।</head>
<p><b><q>‘aindrayā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhate’</q> ityatra saṃśayaḥ kimaindreṇa mantreṇa gārhapatyasyābhidhānaṃ
kartavyaṃ utendrasyeti</b> । anena saṃśayabhāṣyagatamupasthānapadaṃ vyākhyātam । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti spaṣṭāyāṃ</b> dvitīyāśrutau saṃśayaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>mukhye'rthe mantro
viniyujyata iti sthitamādhastye'dhikaraṇe</b> । tena gārhapatyopasthānaṃ na saṃbhavatīti manyate ।
<b>nanu ca mukhyasyāsaṃbhavāt gauṇepi ca viniyujyata eva । etadeva na vijānīmaḥ saṃbhavo
vidyate neti । nanu <q>“gārhapatyamabhidhatta”</q> iti spaṣṭaiva śrutiḥ uttaraṃ---viniyojya-
sāmarthyānusārī viniyoga iti । anīpsitārthā dvitīyā bhavatīti matiḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yadyatra śak‍taṃ tatra tat kārakatayā viniyujyate । na gārhapatyābhidhāne samartho'yaṃ mantra iti
<note>(1) P. 752</note>
﻿<pb n="r717"/>
na gārhipatye viniyogamarhatīti anīpsitārthā dvitīyā bhaviṣyati । <b>tathā ca smaryate tathā
yuktaṃ cānīpsitamiti । ayameva cāsya viṣayo viniyojyavaśāt</b> viniyojyasya mantasya
sāmarthyavaśāt gārhapatye viniyogābhāvāt <b>kārakaparyavasāyyevaitat</b> sūtram । parihārāntara-
māha---<b>yadvā gahipatyamabhyetya abhidhatte iti dvitīyopapadyata iti । tasmādindrābhidhānam
yuktaṃ caitadevaṃ yadindrābhidhānaṃ anyathā hi alaukikī abhidhānaśaktiḥ kalpanīyā । nanu
vināpi śaktikalpanayā gauṇamabhidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati</b> । tena gārhapatye viniyogo nirvahati ।
pariharati---<b>nāsti gauṇamabhidhānaṃ siddhe hi prayoge gauṇamabhidhānam na punargauṇāt prayoga-
siddhiḥ</b> । yatra pramāṇāntareṇa paratra paraśabdaprayogasiddhiḥ tatra gauṇamabhidhānam । na punaḥ
gauṇo'stītyetāvatā prayogaḥ kalpyate । <b>na cātra gārhapatye indraśabdaprayogo'nyataḥ siddhaḥ,
kartavyatopadeśāt</b> anena mantreṇābhidhānaṃ kartavyamityevaṃparamidaṃ vākyaṃ aindrayā gārhapatya-
mupatiṣṭhata iti, na punargārhapatye indrapadaṃ prayuktamityevaṃ param । <b>ato</b> nirapekṣatvādabhi-
dhānavṛtteḥ <b>yathābhidhānaṃ viniyogaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---gārhapatyābhidhānameva kartavyaṃ mantreṇa ।
kutaḥ ? yathopadeśaṃ hi kāryaṃ, na yathā kāryamupadeśaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---upadeśanibandhanaṃ
kāryaṃ na kārye'vagate'nyataḥ upadeśavarṇanam । <b>atideśo hi saḥ yaḥ</b> kāryānurūpaḥ ।
aindrayā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti cāyaṃ upadeśaḥ । ataḥ upadeśāt mārhapatyābhidhānameva
﻿<pb n="r718"/>
kāryamiti manyate । <b>nanu ca yathākāryamupadeśo'pīti saptamādya uktam</b> ityanena
pūrvāparavirodhamāśaṅkate । pariharati---<b>viniyogārthaḥ tatra kāryaśabdenoktaḥ na punarāptyādayaḥ</b>
tena bhinnatvātkāryasya nāsti virodhaḥ । saptamādye niyogārthaṃ kāryamaṅgīkṛtya kāryānuguṇa upadeśa
uktaḥ । iha tu āptyātmakaṃ kāryamabhipretya yathopadeśaṃ kāryamuktam । <b>nanu ca viniyoga
eva sandihyate</b> । yadi hi upadeśa eva niścitaḥ syāt tadā yathopadeśaṃ kāryamiti
gārhapatyopasthānaṃ kāryaṃ niścīyeta । na copadeśo niścitaḥ । <b>kimiti na niścita iti cet ।
anīpsitepi dvitīyādarśanāt</b> । kārakamātre dvitīyā dṛśyata ityarthaḥ । pariharati---<b>kimidaṃ
anīpsitamiti । uttaraṃ---tathā yuk‍taṃ cānīpsitamiti</b> । rāddhāntī brūte---sutarāṃ
tarhi dhātvarthe prati prādhānyam । yadi hi tathāyuktasūtreṇa iyaṃ dvitīyā tadā sutarāṃ ghātvarthā-
pekṣayā sādhyatvaṃ gārhapatyasya, kriyājanyaphalabhāgitā ca prādhānyaśabdenocyate । <b>anyathā hi
tathāyogo'pi na syāt</b> । tathāyuk‍taṃ cānīpsitamityatra tathā yuktaśabdenaivamucyate
yathā īpsitaṃ kriyayā yuk‍taṃ kriyāphalabhāgitayā tathā'nīpsitamapi kriyāphalabhāgitayā kriyayā
yuk‍taṃ tatra dvitīyeti । tatra yadi gārhapatyasyopasthānalakṣaṇaphalayogitā nāṅgīkriyate tadā tathāyogo
na syāt । tataśca tenāpi sūtreṇa dvitīyā na bhavet ato dvitīyādarśanāt gārhapatyasya
kriyāphalabhāgitā'vagamyate । yadyanīpsitasya prādhānyaṃ tadā sutarāmiti yaduk‍taṃ tatredānīṃ
kastarabarthaḥ ? etāvattatra vak‍tavyam dhātvarthaṃ prati prādhānyamiti । uttaraṃ---<b>anīpsitamapi
pradhānamiti</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapyanīpsitatā tathāpīha prādhānyaṃ anyatra īpsitatve prādhānyaṃ
﻿<pb n="r719"/>
ataḥ sutarāṃ prādhānyamityucyate । <b>nanu cok‍taṃ nādṛṣṭā śabdaśaktiḥ śakyate kalpayitumiti</b> ।
anenedamāha---yadyapyupastheyatā gārhapatyasya gamyate tathāpi mantrasyāśakteḥ tathā viniyogo na
nirvahatīti vibhaktivyatyayo vā bhavet । upetyeti vā adhyāhriyatāmiti । atra rāddhāntī
---<b>kimatrādṛṣṭaṃ vacanāt dṛśyata eva</b> yadā vacanenedaṃ kāryaṃ avagataṃ tadā tadbalena yathā
nirvahati tathā kriyate । nirvahati cedaṃ gauṇatvenendraśabdasyeti nādṛṣṭakalpanā doṣaḥ
vacanādeva gauṇatvāśrayaṇena śaktidarśanādityuktavāt । pūrvapakṣyāha---<b>na vacanāt padārtha-
śaktiḥ śakyate'vagantumiti</b> । siddharūpāyāṃ śaktau kāryaikaviṣayasya śabdasya prāmāṇyaṃ
nopapadyata ityarthaḥ । yadi śabdācchaktirnāvagamyate <b>kathaṃ tarhi yāgāderniyogārthasiddhau
śaktiḥ । uttaraṃ---kāryāvagamyatvāt</b> । kāryabhūtena niyogena sahānvitābhidhānāt
sādhanatayā yāgādayo'bhidhīyante । na cāśaktānāṃ taditi teṣāṃ tatra śaktirniścīyate
<b>iha tu tadviparītam । yadyatrāpi pratipattavyamiti vacanaṃ syāt bhavetkāryadarśanam</b> ।
pratipattirhi kāryabhūtā । sā cetthaṃ kāryatvenāvagamyate । yadi indraśabdāt gārhapatyaḥ
pratyetavya iti vacanaṃ bhavet enda‍yāgārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti <b>idantvanyaparaṃ vacanaṃ endrayā gārhapatya-
mabhidhatta iti</b> mantrasya kāryamācaṣṭe na padasyetyarthaḥ । yadidamasmābhiruk‍taṃ mantraviniyoga-
paratvena padakāryapratipādakatvābhāvādvacanasya na vacanāt śaktirdṛśyata iti । <b>tadidamuk‍taṃ
saṃbandhasyāśāstrahetutvāditi</b> । nanu mābhūta śabdasya śaktiḥ <b>gauṇaṃ tarhyabhidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati</b>
pariharati---<b>nanu prayogasiddhau gauṇamabhidhānamityuktam</b> । rāddhāntamāha---<b>atrāpi kārya-</b>
<note>(1) G. sya śāstra</note>
﻿<pb n="r720"/>
<b>tayā siddha ityaviśeṣaḥ</b>1 asyārthaḥ---anena mantreṇa yeyaṃ gārhapatyopasthāpanakāryaśeṣatā
tayaivendraśabdasya gārhapatye prayogassiddhaḥ । anyathā gārhapatyaḥ kathamanena mantreṇābhidhīyata
ityarthāt gauṇīvṛttiḥ । nanu sūtre guṇādveti goṇīvṛttiruktā, kathaṃ bhāṣyakāraḥ2 indateraiśvarya-
karmaṇaḥ’ ityādinā yaugikatvamāheti tatrāha-<b>guṇa śravaṇaṃ3 pradarśanārthaṃ sūtre iti matvā yogā-
dvetyuk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa</b> ।</p>
<p><b>tathā''hvānamapīti cait</b> । nanu kathamatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yāvatā haviṣkṛdehīti trirava-
ghnannāhvatītyāhvāne mantro viniyujyata iti pratibhāti ityatrāha---<b>atrāpyavaghnannāhvayatītyā-
hvānena</b> āhūyate aneneti vyutpattyā mantreṇāvaghātaṃ <b>kuryādityarthaḥ</b> । anena mantreṇāvaghātaṃ
kurvannāhvayatītyarthaḥ । tenāvaghātasya mantrasya ca saṃbandho vidhitsitaḥ । nanu katha mantro'va-
ghātaṃ vakti ityatrāha---<b>guṇādabhidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati yogādvā</b>, haviṣkṛtpat‍nī tadguṇayogāt
avahantirapyucyate । yadvā haviḥ karotīti vyutpattyā mukhyayaiva bṛttyā yogādabhidhānam । nanu
conenāvaghāto nāhvātuṃ śakyate ataḥ kathamāhvayatirityatrāha---āhvayatītyapyanuvādaḥ yo hyehīti
brūte sa āhvayatyeva । aptyārthaḥ---cetanaviṣayepyetadevāhvāturāhvānaṃ yadehīti śabdoccāraṇaṃ,
āhūyamānastu ātmānamavabudhyatāṃ mā vā । asti cātra ehīti śabdaprayogaḥ tasmādāhvayatī-
tyanuvādaḥ । yadi mantrāvaghātasaṃbandho hi vidhīyate kathaṃ tarhi tririti śabdo'nveti ।
na hyavihitasrirabhyāso labhyate । vidhīyate cedvākyabhedaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>śākhāntare pāṭhāt</b>
<note>(1) R. &amp; G. ityadoṣaḥ</note> <note>(2) P. 755</note> <note>(3) R. grahaṇa</note>
﻿<pb n="r721"/>
prāptatvādayamayyanuvāda eva । evaṃ śākhāntare trirāvṛtto mantraḥ paṭhyate । ato'pyayamanu-
vādaḥ । <b>ucyate---trirityetāvadvidhīyate anyatsarvamanūdyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---āhvānasya
mantrasya cātra saṃbandhaḥ sa ca mantro rūpādevāhvāne prāp‍noti iti na vidheyaḥ । tathā <q>‘avaghnannā-
hvayati’</q> ityatra avaghātakālopi prāpta eva । kāryakāla eva hi sahāyānveṣaṇaṃ prāp‍noti ।
kevalamantrasya trirāvṛttiḥ aprāptā sā vidhīyate । <b>nanu trirityapi śākhāntare pāṭhāt prāptaṃ
na nityavatprāptaṃ, aniyamāt</b> । kathamaniyamḥ ? <b>kvacit dviḥ paṭyate</b> ayaṃ mantro yataḥ
tasmādaniyamaḥ । ato'vaghātādivanniyamārthaṃ vacanam । upasaṃharati---<b>ato'vaghnanniti</b>
lakṣaṇaiṣā avaghātena kālo lakṣyata ityarthaḥ । nanu cāyameva rāddhāntarapakṣe doṣaḥ yaduta
lakṣaṇā; <b>nāyaṃ doṣaḥ anyataḥ prāp‍teḥ</b> । yadā tririti vidhīyate tadā padāntaraṃ yathānvayaṃ
yāti tathā varṇayitavyam । tatrāvaghnanniti mukhyayā vṛttyā anvayāsaṃbhavāt lakṣaṇāśrayaṇamadoṣaḥ ।
<b>nanu ca pravṛttāvaghātasya naiva mantraḥ prāpnoti</b> havipkṛdāhvānakālo'pi nityavanna prāp‍noti ।
tena so'pi[tasyāpi] vidheyatayā vākyabhedāpattiriti । pariharati---<b>kālasyānyataḥ prāptatvādidama-
codyam</b> । kāryakāla eva hi sahāyānveṣaṇetyuktam । <b>tasmānna gauṇe viniyoge
pramāṇamasti</b> । tasmādayamatra vicārārthaḥ---kiṃ kālalakṣaṇābhayāt tririti pākṣiko'nuvādaḥ
uta nityavadanvitatrirabhyāsabalena kālalakṣaṇā āśrīyatāṃ iti । pūrvapakṣavādī vadati---pakṣe
paraṃ śabdārthahānāt pakṣikānuvādaḥ na punarlakṣaṇeti । rāddhāntī vadani---nityavadanvitasya
pakṣe'nvayabādhaḥ prāp‍noti । tasmādvaraṃ lakṣaṇā । tasyāṃ hi satyāṃ sarvapadānāṃ nityavadanvaya
﻿<pb n="r722"/>
iti evaṃ tāvat gauṇapakṣamāśritya rāddhāntitam । <b>yadi punarayaṃ mantro'vaghāta eva
mukhyārthaḥ syāt nāvaghāte lakṣaṇā kalpitā bhavet । śakyate ca haviṣkṛcchabdena
avaghāto vak‍tuṃ pat‍nīvat</b> । yathā pat‍nī yaugikena haviṣkṛcchabdenocyate tathā avaghāto'pi ।
ato mantro'vaghāte prāptatvāt na vidhīyate trirāvṛttireva kevalā vidhāyiṣyata iti । <b>satyaṃ
śakyate । āhvānaṃ tu ananvitārthaṃ prāp‍noti</b> । mantragatamehītipadaṃ2 āhvānātmakaṃ
ananvitārthaṃ prāp‍noti । tena liṅgāttāvat tanmātrasya prāptirnāsti । athāprāpto'vaghāta-
mantro'pi vidhīyate tatrāha---<b>tririti ca aniyataṃ tyāt । tasmādvaraṃ lakṣaṇaiva । tayā ca
liṅgamaikāntikam</b> । tathā pat‍nī haviṣkṛditi śakyā haviṣkaraṇayogena vak‍tuṃ vāk‌sādṛśyaṃ ca
haviṣkṛta ucyate । tacca s‍trītvena । tacca pat‍nyāṃ aikāntikaṃ 3puliṃṅgasyāvaghātaśabdasya
darśanāt ।</p>
<p><b>tathotthānavisarjane । nanu codāharaṇāntaramevedaṃ kimatrātidiśyate । na hi anya-
tvādṛte sādṛśyamupapadyate ।</b> anyathā tadeva hi <b>syāt idamastyanyatvaṃ pūrvasminnadhikaraṇe</b>
<note>(1) P. 758</note> <note>(2) G. hantipadaṃ</note> <note>(3) G. anaikāntikam</note>
﻿<pb n="r723"/>
<b>trirityetāvadvidhīyate anyatsarvamanūdyate । iha punaḥ kālasaṃyogo vidhātavyaḥ aprāpte ca
kālasaṃyogavidhāne lakṣaṇā na nyāyyeti pūrvapakṣavādī adhikaraṇavaiṣamyaṃ manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
-trirityetāvati vidhīyamāne sarvasyānūdyamānatvāt avaghnannityasya lakṣaṇā yuktā । iha punaḥ
kālasaṃyogona prāptaḥ sa vighātavyaḥ । na ca vidhau lakṣaṇā yuk‍teti viśeṣaḥ pūrvadhikaraṇāditi ।
<b>rāddhāntī tu praiṣārthānanvayatulyatvāt tathaivetyuktavān</b> । yathā pūrvatra praiṣārtho nānvīyate tathā-
'trāpyacetanatvāt 2utthānavisarjanayoḥ praiṣārthānanvayaḥ । nanu vidhivākye mukhyatvāśrayaṇena
mantre kimiti praiṣārtho vivakṣito na bhavati । <b>ucyate---vighivākye</b> lakṣaṇayāpi hi padā-
rthānāmaśeṣāṇāmanvayaḥ । mantre tu sarvathaiva preṣārtho'na3nvitaḥ ityavivakṣā''śrayaṇīyeti ।</p>
<p><b>sūk‍tavāke ca</b> । iha sūktavākena prastaraṃ praharatītyudāharaṇe ki [haratau4 sūktavāka-
ścodyate utātrāpi kālalakṣaṇetyudāharaṇadarśanena saśayaḥ samarthitaḥ । sūktavākeneti tṛtīyayā
mukhyasūktavākaśabdaśravaṇāt haratau sādhanatvena sūktavākaḥ codyata iti pratīyate । <b>harateśca</b>
praharaṇamātravācitvāt na sūktavākaḥ sādhanatvenaivānvayaṃ yātīti kālalakṣaṇeti ca pratibhātīti ।
kiṃ tāvad‍yuk‍taṃ ? agnīdag‍nīn viharetivat anyārthatvānmantrasya yathā praiṣārthatvānmantrasyotthāne na
viniyogaḥ tathā sūktavākasya devatāprakāśakatvāt haratau ca devatāyā ananvayāt na
viniyogo yuktaḥ । ayaṃ cāparo viśeṣaḥ yathā tatra <q>‘ag‍nīdag‍nīn vihara’</q> ityanena śakyate
utthānaṃ vak‍tuṃ ag‍nimindhe ityanayā vyutpattyā yathā'g‍nīcchabdenotthānaṃ śakyate vak‍tuṃ na tathā
<note>(1) jha. 759</note> <note>(2) G. āhān</note> <note>(3) G. vivakṣita ityarthaḥ ato vivakṣā
nāśrayaṇīyeti</note> <note>(4) G. haraṇe</note>
﻿<pb n="r724"/>
sūktavākena haratiḥ kenacitprakāreṇābhidhātuṃ śakyate । tasmāt kālavidhipratipattau ca
saṃbhavantyāṃ nārthakarma kalpitaṃ bhavati । yadi sūktavāko haratau sādhanatvena codyate tadā devatā-
prakāśakatvāt sūktavākasya devatāyāśca yoge'nanvayāt yāgarūpatā harateraṅgīkaraṇīyāḥ
tataścārthakarmatā । pratipattau ca saṃbhavantyāṃ nārthakarma kalpitaṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p><b>upadeśo vā । atrocyate---neyaṃ kālalakṣaṇā । kiṃ tarhi mantropadeśo'yam</b> ।
ayamāśayaḥ---sūktavākaśabdena mantraviśeṣaḥ śrutyā ucyate । kālastu lākṣaṇikaḥ । na ca
śrutisaṃbhave lakṣaṇā nyāyyeti mantra eva karaṇaṃ vidhīyate । <b>nanu cānyārtho manva ityuk‍taṃ, na
haraterabhidhāteti । mā bhūt haratervācakaḥ haratidevatāyā vācako bhaviṣyati</b> । yadyapi
na sākṣāddharatiṃ ayaṃ mantro'bhidhātuṃ śak‍noti tathāpi tatsādhanabhūtadevatāprakāśanadvāreṇa
bhaviṣyati haraṇe karaṇam । <b>nanu ca nirvṛttayāgadevatāvācako'yaṃ, nivṛttā ye yāgāḥ teṣāṃ</b>
yā devatāḥ tā eva mantro vakti tataścānyadīyasādhanavacanaḥ kathaṃ haratiḥ devatāvācako bhaviṣyati ।
<b>na ca haratiryajatiḥ</b> haraṇaṃ prakṣepaṇamātramucyate na yāgaḥ । na cāyāge devatā sādhanaṃ
bhavati । tasmānna sādhanadvāreṇāpi prakāśanasaṃbhavaḥ । <b>ucyate---nirvṛttayāgadevatā-
vacanatvepi</b> tatsaṃskāro yāgo <b>bhaviṣyati paśupuroḍāśavat</b> । yathā paśupuroḍāśaḥ ag‍nī-
ṣomasmaraṇārthaḥ tathā'yamapi yāgaḥ pūrvayāgasaṃpratipannadevatātvāta devatāsmaraṇārtho bhaviṣyati ।
<b>nanu cāyaṃ haratirna yajatirityuktam</b> । tenāyāgasya sato na devatāsaṃskārārthatvaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
pariharati---<b>haratiryajatiḥ mantrasaṃbandhāt</b> । tathāhi-spaṣṭena vākyena haratau mantro viniyujyata
﻿<pb n="r725"/>
ityavagamyate tena haratireva yajatirbhaviṣyati । <b>nanu caivaṃ sati saiva lakṣaṇā prāp‍noti</b>, yasyā
dṛṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣaparityāgaḥ prakṣepamātravacanena haratinā yajatirlakṣaṇayopasthāpanīya iti । pariharati
---<b>na lakṣaṇā yāge sati haratyarthasya prāptatvāt । ālametetivat</b> । asyārthaḥ-na
haratinā yajatirlakṣyate । kintu haratyartho'yaṃ yāge sati prāpta evānūdyate yathā ag‍nīṣomīyaṃ
paśumālabhetetyālabhbhaḥ । nanu ca yuktaṃ tatra dravyadevatāsaṃbandhena gāgasya kalpyamānatvāt ।
iha tu yāgopasthāpane na kiñcit pramāṇamasti । ucyate---sūktavākena prastaraṃ praharatīti
sūktavākaharaṇayoḥ saṃbandho'vagamyate । sa ca saṃbandho'tra vidhīyate । tenāyamarthaḥ saṃpadyate
tathā yateta yathā sūktavākaharaṇayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃpadyata iti । tatra sūktavākena homātmake
yāge devatāprakāśanadvāreṇa kriyamāṇe bhavati sūktavākasya haraṇasya ca kriyākārakalakṣaṇaḥ
saṃbandhaḥ । homātmakepi yāge anuṣṭhīyamāne upādhibhūtaḥ prakṣepaḥ saṃpadyate । mantreṇa ca
devatāmuddiśya homātmako yāgaḥ śakyate kartuṃ iti pāramparyeṇāsti sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ । tasmādyathā
dravyadevatāsaṃbandhavidhānenārthādyāgalābhaḥ tathehāpi mantraharaṇasaṃbandhavidhānena yāgalābhaḥ । tenaivātra
pūrvapakṣasiddhāntaviracanā---sūktavākasya haraṇe sādhakatvānupapatteḥ praharaṇena homātmako yāgo
lakṣayitavyaḥ । na cāsau yuktaḥ ākhyātārthe pradhāne lakṣaṇāprasaṅgāt । varaṃ sūktavākena
kāla eva lakṣyatāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu na haraṇena yāgo lakṣaṇīyaḥ saṃbandhavidhānādeva
homātmako yāgaḥ kalpyatāṃ; tathā sati sarvapadānyeva śrautārthāti saṃbhaviṣyantīti । atra ca
yajatyātmakatvāt haratyātmakatvaṃ yajatereva yaducyate tadupacāreṇa draṣṭavyam । prakṣepo hi haraṇaṃ; na
ca yāgaḥ prakṣepātmakaḥ । vastutastu homarūpe yoge upādhibhūto haratiḥ arthaprāpta iti । evaṃ ca
sati <q>‘idaṃ havirajuṣata avīvṛghata, ayaṃ yajamāna āyurāśāste’</q> ityupapannārthaḥ mantro bhaviṣyati ।
<b>anyathā hi vṛttamidamā(na) nirdeśyaṃ syāt</b> । pūrvapakṣe hi vṛttaṃ haviḥ sūktavākena kīrtanī-
yam । tatra sannihitābhidhāyaka idaṃśabdo nopapadyate । rāddhānte tu vartamānaṃ prastarākhyaṃ havirucyata
iti yuktaḥ idamā nirdeśaḥ । <b>āśāsta iti ca bhūtanirdeśaḥ</b> pūrvapakṣe sūktavākasya karmāntarā-
﻿<pb n="r726"/>
saṃbandhāt vṛttakarmagataivāśīrucyate । tatra vartamānanirdeśo nopapadyate । rāddhānte tu
karmāntaragatā vartamā(ne)naivāśīrucyata iti nānupapannaṃ kiñcit । upasaṃharati---<b>tasmāt suṣṭhu</b>
śobhanaṃ <b>ucyate haratiryajatiriti</b> । eṣa copacāravādo bhāṣyakārasyeti mantavyam ।
<b>yaduk‍taṃ pratipattau saṃbhavantyāṃ nārthakarma nyāyyamiti</b> । bhāṣyakāreṇa <b>sviṣṭakṛdvadavirodho
bhaviṣyatītyuktam</b> । yathā sviṣṭakṛti dravyamapi pratipādyate devatāśceṣṭāḥ smaryante tathehāpi
prastaraśca pratipādyate devatāśceṣṭāḥ smṛtā bhavanti yāgepi satīti nāsti virodhaḥ prastaramiti
dvitīyāyāḥ praharaṇasya ca prahāryapradhānatayeti ।</p>
<p><b>kṛts‍nopadeśāt । sthitaṃ tāvat vacanāddharatiryajatiḥ sūktavākamantrastheti ।
idamidānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ sakalasya sūk‍tavākasya paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāyāṃ ca prayogaḥ
uta devatāpadavibhāgeneti</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatimāha saṃśayaṃ ca pūrvapakṣābhāvenākṣeptuṃ
anubhāṣate । sthite hi vākyena praharaṇe sūk‍tavākasya viniyoge pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā nānyathā ।
ākṣepamāha---<b>nanu cinteyaṃ nopapadyate sthitamarthaikatvādekavākyatvam । na cātra pradhāna-
devatāpadānāṃ praś‍liṣṭapaṭhitānāmatra athaikatvaṃ saṃbhavati । nāpi vibhajyamānasākāṅkṣatvam</b> ।
<note>(1) P. 764</note>
﻿<pb n="r727"/>
<b>tasmādbhinnānyetāni</b> vākyāni <b>bhinnānāṃ caikavacananirdeśe sati kathaṃ kṛtsnaḥ prayoga
āśaṅkyate</b> । asyārthaḥ-praś‍liṣṭaparipaṭhitānāṃ mantrāṇāmarthaikatvāta vibhāge sākāṅkṣatvāt
ekavākyatvamuk‍tam । na cātra pradhānadevatāpadānāmarthaikatvam । na ca vibhāge sākāṅkṣatā ।
ato bhinnānyevaitāni vākyāni । bhinneṣu vākyeṣu ekavacanāntena śabdena ekasyaiva vākyasya
viniyogo na sarveṣāṃ ekavacanavirodhāt yathā paśunetyeka eva paśurgṛhyate । ataḥ sakalamantra-
prayogāśaṅkā nopapadyate । yathā āgneyyā āgnīdhramupatiṣṭhate ityatra <b>āg‍necyetyuk‍te na kṛtsnā
āgneyyaḥ prayoktavyā ityāśaṅkā bhavati । mukhye ca saṃbhavati na gauṇe viniyoga ityapi
sthitam</b> । yadi sakalasyobhayatra viniyogaḥ syāt tadā <b>ubhayadevatāvācināṃ padānāṃ</b> parasparaṃ
ubhayatra gauṇārthatā <b>syāt</b> । na ca mukhyenaiva <b>viniyogena mantre</b> kṛtārthepi gauṇe viniyoga
ityapi sthitaṃ gauṇamukhyādhikaraṇe । ato vibhajyaiva viniyogo yuktaḥ । <b>ucyate---yathāha
bhavān, kintu pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । sūk‍tavāko vartata iti vākyasamūhe ekavacana-
midam । evamatrāpi sṛk‍tavākeneti samūhagatamevedamekavacanam । ataḥ samūha evātra
karaṇam</b> । asyārthaḥ-sūk‍tavāko vartata iti sakale mantre paṭhyamāne adhyetṝṇāmadhyāpakānāṃ
śrotṛṇāṃ ca [ā]yata eva loke vyapadeśaḥ । sasa cābhinnavākyābhiprāyeṇa । anyathā bahuvacana-
prasaṅgāt । tasmādekavacanadarśanādavagacchāmaḥ samūha eva sūk‍tavākaśabda iti । evaṃ ca
sūktavākena prastaraṃ praharatītyatrāpi samūha eva viniyuk‍ta iti kṛtsna evobhayatra
prayojyaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r728"/>
<p><b>nanu ca samūhasyaikārthatā na saṃbhavati</b> na bhinnadevatāvācināṃ padānāmekārthabhāvaḥ
saṃbhavatītyarthaḥ । pariharati---<b>vacanāt kalpyate yathottame prayāje</b> । asyārthaḥ ---yathā
uttame prayāje, uttamaśabdaḥ svabhāvāt triprabhṛtīnāmantyamāha । tena svāhākāre yathā nānā-
devatāvācināmapi padānāmekārthabhāvaḥ tathehāṣi vacanāt kalpyata <b>itīmāmāśaṅkāṃ nivartayituṃ
idamadhikaraṇam । kṛtaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ । idānīṃ rāddhānto'bhidhīyate । nātra samūhaviniyoge
pramāṇamasti । kutaḥ ? sūk‍tavāko vartata ityanyathāpyekavacanopapatteḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ
-sūktamanenocyata iti sūk‍tavākaśabdena vākyamucyate vākyena hi sūktamucyate na vākyasamūhena,
tasmādvākyameva sūktavākaḥ । bhinnāni caitāni vākyāni । tasmādekavacanaśravaṇāt na
sakalasya viniyogaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi sūktavāko vartata iti sakala ekavacanamupapadyata iti ।
<b>ekābhidhānāddhi pāṭhakānāṃ sūktabāko nartata iti yujyate'bhidhānam</b> । sarvāṇyapi tāni
sūktamekaṃ vadanti । tena tadekatvāt kārakarūpatāmevāśritya bahuṣvapyekavacanaprayogo na
virudhyate yathā padaṃ vākyamiti bahuṣvapi varṇeṣu padeṣu ca ekakāryanibanghanaḥ ekavacanaprayogaḥ
<b>iha punaḥ sūktavākena prastaraṃ praharatīti na liṅgabādhenaikavākyatvaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyaṃ yathā-
liṅgaṃ viniyogopapatteḥ</b> । yena hyekamidaṃ vākyaṃ prastarapraharaṇe viniyujyata ityāśrīyate
tenāpi bhinnadevatāvācināṃ padānāṃ svasāmarthyabādhenaikārthatvaṃ kalpayitavyam । taccānupapannam ।
yathāliṅgamapi viniyogopapatteḥ । <b>tasmāt sarveṣāṃ sūktavākavacanena viśeṣāgrahaṇāt yena</b>
﻿<pb n="r729"/>
<b>kenacit sūktavākena</b> kṛte praharaṇe kṛtaṃ bhavati <b>sūktavākena prastaraṃ praharatīti</b> yathā-
coditānuṣṭhānam । nanu bhāṣyakāreṇa darśapūrṇamāsasamudāye sūktavākasamudāyaviniyogāt
vibhagaya viniyogo bhavatīti rāddhāntopakrame kimiti darśitaṃ yadi pūrvokto rāddhāntamārgaḥ ityā-
śaṅkyāha---<b>samudāyābhiprāyastu heyatayopanyastaḥ</b> । rāddhāntāmāsanirākaraṇāyedamukta-
mityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>liṅgakramasamākhyānāt । ādhastye adhikaraṇe uktaṃ---prakaraṇāt pratyekaṃ śeṣatve
prāpte liṅgādvibhāga iti idānīṃ prakaraṇāt yadbalīyaḥ tannitarāṃ kramasamākhyābhyāṃ balīyata iti
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatimāha । <b>liṅgācchebatve atantre kramasamākhye</b> ।
liṅgena mantrasya śeṣatve saṃbhavati kramaḥ samākhyā ca kāraṇameva na bhavatīti na viśeṣopasaṃhāraḥ ।
tasmādyāvadaindreāgnakarma mantrasya viniyogaḥ । <b>nanu ca liṅgaṃ naiva kevalaṃ viniyojakamiti
rāddhānte vakṣyate</b> yadi hi kevalaṃ liṅga viniyojakaṃ syāt tadā kramasamākhyānirapekṣaṃ
sarvatra viniyuñjīta । na caivamiṣyate । tatkartha sarvatra viniyojakāśaṅkā । <b>viniyoja-
katve ca balābalam</b> । asyārtha---sthite viniyojakatve kramasya samākhyāyāśca liṅgena saha
<note>(1) P. 722</note>
﻿<pb n="r730"/>
balābalacintā na cādyāpi tayoḥ viniyojakatvamuktam । tena nedamadhikaraṇamārabdhumadhunocitam ।
<b>kimarthaṃ ca prāk śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇāt balābalacintā । atrābhidhīyate---naiveyaṃ balā-
balacintā</b> । yadi balābalacintā syāt tadā syādeva pūrvoktadoṣaḥ । na tveṣā balābala-
cintā । <b>kintu sāpekṣaṃ liṅgaṃ viniyojakaṃ ityatra pratipādyate</b> । tarhi nirapekṣaṃ liṅgaṃ
viniyojakamiti pūrvapakṣeṇa bhavitavyam । na cāyaṃ pūrvapakṣo yuktaḥ । sāmarthyamātrasya
viniyojakatvānupapatteḥ । idamanena kartavyamiti na sāmarthyamātrāt jñānamutpadyate । tadida-
māha---<b>kathaṃ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>liṅgamapi śrutyādivat pramāṇāntaranirapekṣamiti
balābalasūtre</b> <q>‘śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṃ samavāye’</q> ityatrānukramāt bhrāgyataḥ
<b>pūrvapakṣo'yam</b>। tulyavadanukramaṇāt kasyacidiyamāśaṅkā śrutyādivannirapekṣaṃ liṅgamiti ।
<b>rāddhāntastu---sāmānyasaṃbandhe</b> <q>‘anena mantreṇedaṃ kartavyaṃ’</q> ityevaṃ rūpe pramāṇāntarāvasite
sati <b>śeṣiviśeṣe liṅgaṃ viniyojakamiti । yathā ca liṅgaṃ na kevalaṃ viniyojakaṃ tathā
śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇe nipuṇataramupapādayiṣyāmḥ</b> । etacca bhāṣyakārāyamāṇo <b>nibandhakāra</b>
āha-yataḥ sāpekṣaṃ liṅgaṃ viniyojakaṃ <b>ataḥ kramasahitaṃ</b> samākhyāsahitaṃ ca <b>viniyojakamiti</b> ।
nanu ca samākhyānamātrādapi prakṛtamudāharaṇaṃ siddha‍yati । tathā hi---kāmyayājyānuvākyā-
kāṇḍamiti samākhyāyāṃ satyāṃ kāmyāyāmiṣṭau yājyākārye viniyogaḥ siddhayati । <b>nanu caika</b>-
﻿<pb n="r731"/>
sminnapi karmaṇi anekayājyānuvākyāyugalasya viniyojakatvaṃ syāt । tathā dvitīye'pi
karmaṇi prathamapaṭhitasya yugalasya viniyogaḥ । naitadevam । ekena yugalena karmaṇāṃ kṛtārthatvāt
nānekayugalaviniyoge pramāṇamasti । tenaikenaivaikatra bhavitavyam । tatra vināpi liṅgaṃ
kramākhyena pramāṇena prathamapaṭhite karmaṇi prathamasyaiva viniyogo bhaviṣyati, prāthamyāta । ane-
naiva nyāyena dvitīye dvitīyasya viniyoga iti । tathā liṅgakramādapyayamartho labhyate tatra
krameṇa saṃbandhe sati liṅgena yājyākārye viniyogasiddheḥ । na ca sāmidhenīkārye viniyogaḥ
śaṅkanīyaḥ, aindrāgnatvādāsāṃ ṛcāṃ āgneyatvācca sāmidhenīnām । tasmāt kimarthaṃ liṅgakrama-
samākhyānāditi ? liṅgakramāt samākhyānāditi ca ubhayaṃ sahitamuk‍taṃ yāvatā ekamevocya-
tāmityāśaṅkyāha---<b>ubhayapramāṇasāhitye ca prayojanamuk‍taṃ bhāṣye</b> । tadyathā 2yadi
liṅgakramādityetāvaducyeta tadā pāthikṛtīye karmaṇyāg‍neyasya yugalatya sāmidhenīkārye'pi
viniyogaḥ syāt” । tathāhi tad‌yugalaṃ agnidevatāke pāthikṛtīye karmaṇi yājyākārye3paryāptaṃ
sāmidhenīkārye'pi syāt । āg‍neyyo hi sāmidhenyaḥ tasmādyājyākārya eva viniyogo
yathā syāditi vaktavyaṃ samākhyānāditi । nanvevaṃ tarhi tadevāstu kiṃ liṅgakramādityanena ?
ucyate । kāmyayājyānūvākyākāṇḍamiti yā samākhyā tayā yājyākārye viniyogo bhavet ।
ata punaḥ nirvṛtte yājyākārye liṅgakramāta sāmidhenīkārye viniyogassiddho bhavati । samākhyā tu
kāmyayāgasaṃbandhamātrahetutayā ādaraṇīyetyataḥ etadavasthitaṃ yatra liṅgakramānuguṇā samākhyā tatra
tadvaśena liṅgakramaviniyogaḥ saṃbhavati । yatra punaḥ samākhyāṃ liṅgakramaviniyogavirodhinī tatra
tadvaśena sāmānyasaṃbandhamātrapareti varṇyata iti ।</p>
<p><b>adhikāre ca</b> । atra bhāṣyam---kiṃ prakṛtābhiḥ liṅgavatībhirupasthātavyam; uta

ityevamādiṣu liṅganirdeśeṣu kiṃ yāvalliṅgaṃ grahītavyā uta prakṛtānāṃ grahaṇamiti । tatra
pūrvapakṣavādī vidheyasya prakṛtābhidhānasāmarthyaṃ na saṃbhavatīti manvāno yāvalliṅgagrahaṇa-
mityāha</b> । kā punaryuktiḥ vidheyasya prakṛtābhivānasāmarthyaṃ na saṃbhavatīti tatrāha---<b>uddeśyapadaṃ
hi prakṛtāpekṣaṃ bhavati na punarvidheyārthasamarpakamapi । kimiti ? uddeśyatvaṃ hi nāma
prayojanavadarthatā</b> । prayojanavāṃścāsau arthaśceti prayojanavadarthaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tattā prayojana-
vānarthaḥ uddeśyo bhavatītyarthaḥ । <b>na ca sāmānyaṃ prayojanavadbhavati</b> na vrīhyādisāmānyaṃ
prayojanavadbhavati <b>upāttaviṣayatvāt prayojanavattāyāḥ</b> । ya evopātto viśeṣaḥ sa eva
prayojanavattāyā viṣayaḥ । sa eva prayojanavānityarthaḥ । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi sāmānyaṃ prayojanavadeva
tasyaiva viniyogāt viniyuktasya copādānāt । tadāha---<b>nanu ca sāmānyamevopādīyate</b> ।

saṅkhyādisahitaṃ śabdādevāvagamyate anyato'navagamāditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । āg‍neyīmātra-

punarabhidhānāt tulyam</b> । atra bhāṣyamāha---virodhe sati prakaraṇaṃ liṅgena bādhyate

punaḥ parihṛta ityatrāha---<b>nātra upadiṣṭatā hetuḥ</b> । mantragrahaṇe hi yad‌yupadiṣṭatā hetuḥ syāt
tadā upadiṣṭenaiva rūpeṇa viniyogo vaktavyaḥ । sa ca viniyuktaviniyogavirodhānna nyāyyaḥ ।
yadā punaḥ upadeśānantarāpekṣeṇa liṅgenopalakṣaṇena viniyogaḥ tadā na kiñcit duṣyatīti,

uttaraṃ---<b>bhavatvabhidhānāt prakṛtabādho na doṣaḥ</b> śrutibalena prakṛtabādho bhavannapi na doṣaḥ ।

<p><b>tadākhyo vā prakaraṇopapattibhyām । atrocyate । rāddhāntī tu prakṛtepi vidheyaḥ

prakṛtepi viniyujyamāne vidheyapratyayo ghaṭate ataḥ prakṛtatyāge pramāṇābhāvāt prakṛtasyaiva grahaṇa-
miti । nanu yad‌yupadiṣṭatvenopadeśo bhavati tatra prakṛtamātragrahaṇam । upadiṣṭatvena
copadeśe duṣpariharo viniyuktaviniyogavirodhadoṣaḥ । anenābhiprāyeṇāha---<b>kathamiti</b> ।
uttaraṃ---<b>uddeśyatvaṃ hi prayojanavato bhavati</b> । yatra hyuddeśyatā tatropadiṣṭenaiva rūpeṇa
grahaṇam । iha tu vidheyatvānna kāryāntarasaṃbandha upakaroti । tasmāt kāryāntaraviniyoga-
nirapekṣeṇa rūpeṇopādānāt prakṛtānāmapi viniyoge nāsti viniyuktaviniyogavirodhaḥ । tadāha

﻿<pb n="r738"/>
---1<b>prakṛtatvaṃ punaḥ vidheyepi prakṛtapratyayaṃ naiva bādhate</b> । yathā uddeśye prakṛtapratyayaṃ naiva
bādhate tathā vidheyepi naiva bādhate kāryāntaraviniyuktatvaṃ hi bādhakaṃ na prakṛta[tva]mātraṃ,
avirodhāt । prakṛtapratyaya eva tarhi kuta ityatrāha---<b>na hi sannihite viśeṣe sāmānyaśabdaḥ
tamativartate nīlotpalamitivat gāmānayetibadvā</b> sāmānyenopādhināśabdaḥ sāmānyaśabdaḥ
viśeṣavartī sannihite viśeṣa sannihitaṃ viśeṣaṃ nātivartate sāmānyenopādhinā devatāsaṃbandhena
cāyamabhinirvṛtta āg‍neyīśabdaḥ sāmānyaśabdaḥ sannihite mantre na tamativartitumarhati ।
prakṛtamātragrahaṇe dṛṣṭāntamāha---<b>nīlotpalavaditi</b> । atra nīlaguṇasaṃbandhārhatvāt vyak‍teḥ
ākṛtivacano'pyutpalaśabdaḥ ākṛtisaṃbandhalakṣaṇasāmānyopādhipravṛtto'pi vyaktiparaḥ sannihitā-
yāmeva vyak‍tau vartate । dṛṣṭāntāntaramāha---<b>gāmānayetivadveti</b> । pūrvatra guṇayogādva‍yak‍ti-
vacanatā । iha punaḥ ānayanalakṣaṇakriyāyogāditi dṛṣṭāntadvayopādānam । upasaṃharati
---<b>tasmāt na prakṛtapratyarthī sāmānyaśabdo bhavitumarhatīti । prakṛtā evaivaṃ liṅgavyaktayaḥ

sūtraṃ paṭhitvā---<b>yaduk‍taṃ</b> yadasmābhiḥ pūrvamuktaṃ rāddhāntavādī punarityādinā tadidam । tadāha
---<b>yad‍yupadeśamātraṃ</b> vastusthityā <b>tat sarvatrāsti</b> । athopadeśāntareṇaivopadiṣṭenaiva
