﻿<pb n="r739"/>
<p><b>liṅgakramasamākhyāgyāṃ । idamidānīṃ cintyate yathā prakṛtatayā liṅgamupasaṃhṛtaṃ
kimevaṃ samākhyāpi svanimitta evopasaṃharati uta yathāliṅgaṃ viniyoga iti</b> ।
anenāvāntarasaṅgatiṃ bhāṣyakārīyasaṃśayakāraṇaṃ cāha । yathā āg‍neyyetyatra liṅgaṃ prakaraṇe-
nopasaṃhṛtaṃ prakṛtānāmeva viniyogāt tathā kiṃ bhakṣaṇānuvākasamākhyāpi svanimitte bhakṣaṇa eva
upasaṃharati uta yathāliṅgaṃ viniyoga iti । <b>kiṃ tāvad‌yuktaṃ samākhyāpi prakṛtavanniyama-
yatyeva2 viśeṣe liṅgaṃ</b> ? asyārthaḥ---samākhyayā sāmānyasaṃbandhe sati liṅgasya viniyojakatvāt
samākhyā liṅgaṃ niyamayatīti kṛts‍nasyānuvākya bhakṣaṇa eva viniyogaḥ । <b>nanu liṅgāntaravirodhaḥ
prāpnoti</b> । grahaṇāvekṣaṇaliṅgavirodhaḥ syādityarthaḥ । pariharati---na prāpnoti virodhaḥ ।
kutaḥ ? <b>viśeṣaṇatayāpi liṅgāntarasyavirodhāt</b> । yadi bhakṣaṇaviśeṣaṇatayāpi grahaṇābhidhānaṃ
tathāpi na virodha iti । yasmāt <b>svārthe</b> yadi svaniṣṭhatayā <b>parārthe</b> yadi ca
paraviśeṣaṇatayā tathā<b>pyabhidhānaṃ</b> grahaṇādīnāma<b>viśiṣṭam</b> ।</p>
<p>nanu pārārthye grahaṇādīnāṃ lakṣaṇā prāpnoti । pariharati---yadyapi lakṣaṇā <b>tathāpya-
bhidhānamaviśiṣṭaṃ</b> grahaṇaprakāśakena hi grahaṇameva prakāśyate nānyat tatra paraviśeṣaṇārthaṃ na
svaniṣṭhaṃ itīdaṃ<b>paratāviśeṣoyaṃ</b> nābhidhānaviśeṣaḥ । yathā gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityabhidhāna-
<note>(1) P. 782</note> <note>(2) niyāmaka ityevaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r740"/>
viśeṣaḥ tatheha nāstītyarthaḥ । tenābhidhānavirodhābhāvāt na liṅgavirodhaḥ । upasaṃharati
---<b>tasmānniyantumarhati samākhyā</b> ।</p>
<p><b>tasya rūpopadeśābhyāṃ</b> । atrocyate---<b>satyamavirodhilaṅgāntaraṃ, kintu anidaṃ-
paratāyāḥ pramāṇaṃ na vidyate</b> । yasya śabdasya yo'thaḥ sa tatpara iti lokaprasiddhametat
autsargikaṃ kāraṇāntareṇa anyathā bhavati । na cātra grahaṇādiprakāśakānāṃ grahaṇādiparatvā-
bhāve kiñcana pramāṇamasti । nanu pratīyamānānāmapi grahaṇādīnāmacoditatvāt prakāśyatā na
yuk‍teti na tatparatā yuktā, tatrāha---<b>bhakṣaṇavalliṅgāntaraviṣayasyāpi smaraṇārhatvāt</b> । kuta
ityāha-<b>prayogo hi smaraṇīyaḥ grahaṇādyapi ca prayoga</b> evānuṣṭhānaṃ smaraṇīyaṃ coditaṃ arthā-
kṣiptaṃ vā bhavatu । <b>tasmāt yathāliṅgaṃ vyavasthā</b> vibhajya viniyoga ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>nanu samākhyāśūnyaṃ liṅgaṃ viniyojakatāmeva na pratipadyate</b> । tena samākhyā-
nibandhanatvāt2 liṅgaviniyogasya kimiti kṛts‍nasya mantrasya samākhyābalāta na viniyogo
bhavatītyatrāha । pariharati-<b>naiva samākhyāśūnyaṃ bhakṣanimittāpi samākhyā kratusaṃbandhitā-
māpādayatyeva</b> asyārthaḥ---bhakṣaṇānuvāka iti samākhyā bhakṣaṇadvāreṇa pravartamānāpi kratusaṃba-
<note>(1) P. 784</note> <note>(2) G. samākhyādhīnatvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r741"/>
ndhitāmanuvākyasyāpādayatyeva । siddhe ca kratusaṃbandhe yathāliṅgaṃ siddho viniyogaḥ । nanu
lakṣaṇāpi laukikyeva, tena kimiti lakṣaṇayā bhakṣaṇa eva viniyogaḥ kṛts‍nasya mantrasya
samākhyābalānna bhavatītyatrāha---<b>laukikī lakṣaṇetyasyoktaḥ parihāraḥ</b> । śrutilakṣaṇāviśaye ca
śrutirnyāyyā na lakṣaṇeti ।</p>
<p><b>guṇābhidhānāt । pūrvādhikaraṇāpavādo</b>'yamityanenāvāntarasaṅgatiṃ pūrvapakṣañcāha
---pūrvādhikaraṇanyāyenaivātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । liṅgabalena tṛptiprakāśanepi mantrasya viniyogaṃ manyate ।
yathāpavādaḥ tathā''ha---<b>aprayogābhidhāno mantraḥ</b> ananuṣṭhānārthakatṛp‍tyabhidhāno mantraḥ <b>prayogā-
bhidhānena</b> bhakṣābhidhānena <b>sahaikavākyatāṃ</b> nīyate samākhyayā । sā hi kṛts‍namevānu-
vākaṃ bhakṣaṇasaṃbandhamāpādayantyapi liṅgena bādhitā । yatra punaḥ liṅgaṃ bādhitumevaṃ na śak‍noti
ananuṣṭheyasya smaraṇānarhatvāt tatra tātparyābhāvāt tasya samākhyāyā bhakṣaṇe ciniyoga iti । nanu
ca liṅgāt tadabhidhāna eva mantro'stu tadabhidhānādeva cādṛṣṭaṃ kalpyatāṃ ityatrāha---<b>liṅgaṃ hi
dṛṣṭārthatayā samākhyayopasaṃhṛtam । yatra punaḥ dṛṣṭārthatā nāsti tatrādṛṣṭakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ
nāstīti samākhyaiva viniyok‍tī</b> । adṛṣṭakalpanāto hi lakṣaṇā śreyasī । <b>lakṣaṇayā</b>
tṛp‍tyabhidhāno hi mantraḥ bhakṣaṇa eva viniyujyate । samākhyayā ca <b>svanimitta</b> eva viniyukta
iti <b>siddhaṃ bhakṣaṇenaikavākyatvādekamantratvam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 785</note>
﻿<pb n="r742"/>
<p><b>liṅgaviśeṣanirdeśāt</b> । atredṛśī sthitiḥ indrapītasyeti kimayaṃ tṛtīyāsamāsaḥ uta
bahuvrīhiḥ । indreṇa pītamiti kiṃ soma ucyate, indreṇa pītaṃ yasmin savana iti savana-
mevocyata iti mūlavicāraḥ । atra ca tṛtīyāsamāsasya uttarapadārthapradhānatvāt bahuvrīheḥ
durbalateti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । asmiṃśca pūrvapakṣe aindra eva some samantrakaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ itareṣāṃ punaḥ
upadeśatastāvat bhakṣaṇamantro nāsti atideśato'pi paramārthato nāstyeva । sarvapradānātāṃ samāna-
vidhānatvāt upadeśa eva nirākāṅkṣatvāt । tathāpi ṣoḍaśini2namanaviśeṣavidhānāta aindrasya
prakṛtitvaṃ itareṣāṃ ca vikṛtitvamityāśaṅkā3---vipariṇāme hi prāpte tadviśeṣavidhirupapadyate ।
ātideśike hi dharme vipariṇāmo naupadeśike । tasmāt prakṛtivikārabhāvaḥ । tathā <q>“aindraḥ
somo gṛhyate mīyate ca”</q> iti pratīyate grahaṇamānayoḥ aindrasya mantrasya samānatvam । yatra
mantraḥ tatraiva grahaṇamāne yatra ca grahaṇamāne tatra somaḥ tenānyāni pradānāntarāṇi anyato dravyaṃ
tatsaṃskārāṃścāpekṣanta iti vikārabhāvaḥ । upapadyate cāsau abhyāsāpūrvāṇāṃ bhedābhyupagamāditi
atideśena prāptimabhyupagamya cintā kṛtā kasyohena upalakṣaṇaṃ kasya neti । paramārthatastu
samānavidhānānyetāni sarvapradānāni । somena yajeteti yāgasya somadravyayogitvāt tasyaiva ca
yāgasyābhyasyamānatvāt । ataḥ sarvatropadeśena dravyalābhāt dravyāśritatvācca saṃskārāṇāṃ
saṃskāranirākāṅkṣatvānnāsti prakṛtivikārabhāvaḥ । namanaviśeṣavidhānaṃ ta viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ
bhaviṣyati । tasmādatideśato mantro nāstītyuktam । mūlādhikaraṇarāddhānte tu indrapītasyeti
bahuvrīhyāśrayaṇāt savanavacanatvādindrapītaśabdasya sarveṣāṃ samantrakaṃ bhakṣaṇamityuktam । iha
<b>pānopalakṣaṇaprakaraṇe</b> pānaṃ devatayopalakṣyata iti yatra prakaraṇe cintyate tasmin <b>samāna-
vidhāne</b> sarvasomayāgābhyāsānāṃ <b>sthite anuṣṭup‌chandasa iti namanadarśanāt aindraḥ somo</b>
<note>(1) P. 786</note> <note>(2) G. nāma</note> <note>(3) G. ṅkyāha</note>
﻿<pb n="r743"/>
<b>gṛhyate mīyate ca iti prakṛtivikāraśaṅkā</b> । endrapradānaṃ prakṛtibhūtaṃ śeṣāṇi vikṛti-
bhūtānītyāśaṅkā । tenātideśike <b>kṛtvācitā</b> kā devatā ūhenopalakṣyatāmityādikā ।</p>
<p><b>punarabhyunnīteṣu । atra āśrāvaṇādapanayaḥ prasthitadevatāyā iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
saśeṣe camase punassome devatāntarārtha gṛhīte yadāśravaṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tena pūrvadevatāśeṣasyāpi
devatāntarārthamupādānāt pūrvadevatāpanayanāt na sā devatā upalakṣaṇīyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
<b>agrahaṇānneti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । grahaṇena hi devatāsaṃbandho dravyasyāpādyate । taduddeśenā-
grahaṇāt taccheṣaḥ camasastho devatāntaroddeśena na gṛhyate । yacca gṛhītaṃ tāvanmātrasyaivāśrāvaṇa-
miti pūrvadevatā upalakṣaṇīyeti ।</p>
<p><b>pāt‍nīvate tu । āgrayaṇāt punaranāgrayaṇasyāpi taduddaśena grahaṇamityapanaya eva</b> ।
anena pūrvādhikaraṇavyatirekamātramidamityāha---yo'pyasāvāgrayaṇe dvidevatyasomaśeṣaḥ 4sopyanā-
grayaṇāt rasāt yakṣyamāṇadevatoddeśena gṛhītaḥ ityapanītā pūrvadevatā ityanupalakṣaṇīyā ।</p>
<p><b>tvaṣṭārantūlakṣayet । tvaṣṭari sahavacanāt pūrvapakṣaḥ</b> sajūrdevena tvaṣṭrā somaṃ piveti
sajūśśabdasya sahārthatvāt pāne sahabhāvena tvaṣṭuranupraveśāt devatātaddhitavirodhānāpādakatvāt
tvaṣṭāpi devatā । ataḥ sopyupalakṣaṇīya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>nācoditatvāditi rāddhāntaḥ</b>
<note>(1) Bhashya P. 788</note> <note>(2) P. 791</note> <note>(3) P. 793</note> <note>(4) G. so'pyāgra</note>
﻿<pb n="r744"/>
nopalakṣaṇīyaḥ acoditatvāt । coditā hi devatā bhavati । na ca mantraḥ codituṃ śak‍noti ।
stutyāpyupapatteḥ ।</p>
<p>1<b>triṃśacca । trayas‍triṃśati tu</b> trayastriṃśatamityatra <b>ag‍neḥ 2mādayitṛtvadarśanāt
punarāśaṅkā</b> । agniḥ mādayitṛmantre kīrtyate na pātā tena trayastriṃśaddevatāḥ pradhānatayā kīrtyanta
iti devatābhāvāśaṅkā । 3<b>mādayitṛtaiva tatprādhānyāt devatābhāvamāpādayatīti rāddhāntaḥ</b> ।
yadetat ag‍neḥ mādayitṛtvaṃ tadevānyathā nopapadyate yadyagniḥ pradhāno na bhavati । īśāno hi
vilambayitukāmaḥ 4hīnamāhvayati । tena 5mādayitṛtveneśānatvāt ag‍neḥ devatātvamavagamyate ।
nahyanyena prakāreṇa tasyeśānatā'sti ityagnirevānena mantreṇa devatātvena kīrtyata iti na trayastriṃ-
śato devatābhāvaḥ । ato nopalakṣaṇīyeti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>6vaṣaṭakāraśca । anuvaṣaṭakāradevatāpi taduddeśenāgrahaṇānnopalakṣyā</b> । devatā-
tvādanuvaṣaṭkāradevatāpyupalakṣaṇīyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । satyaṃ devatā, tathāpi yaduddeśena somo gṛhītaḥ
sā devatā upalakṣaṇīyetyetat । sthānapatitā'nuvaṣaṭkāradevatā nopalakṣyate ।</p>
<p><b>7chandaḥ pratiṣedhastu । sthitāduttaram-ekayāgatvāt‍tu samānavidhānaṃ syāt । tasmādaindra
eva samantrakaḥ somaḥ itītarat pradānamamantrakaṃ anāmnānāt</b> । prakṛtivikārahetubhūtaṃ
<note>(1) P. 794</note> <note>(2) āhvātṛtva</note> <note>(3) āhvātṛtaiva</note> <note>(4) arthinamā</note> <note>(5) āhvā-
tṛtvenā</note> <note>(6) P. 797</note> <note>(7) P. 798</note>
﻿<pb n="r745"/>
yaduk‍taṃ pūrvapakṣiṇā tadaparihṛtyādhikaraṇāntaramārabdham---<b>aindrāg‍ne punariti</b> । atrāyamabhiprāyaḥ
---upadeśaḥ aindravat aindrāg‍nepi nāstītyupadeśopapādanāt idameva vaktavyam । punaścopadeśābhāve
sthite atideśo'pi nāstītyevamarthaṃ prakṛtivikārabhāvāpādikā yuktiḥ nirākaraṇīyeti ।
<b>aindrāg‍ne punaḥ pānamevopalakṣaṇaṃ na devateti <q>“āg‍neyaṃ caturdhā karoti”</q> iti sthite'pi
punaḥ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । āgneye devatātaddhitaḥ ataḥ kevalāgnidevatāko gṛhyate । iha tu na
devatātvenopalakṣaṇaṃ kintu pānena । yat‍tu ubhābhyāṃ pīyate so'pi indrapīta iti śakyate
vadituṃ iti । <b>devatopalakṣaṇam pānābhāvāditi rāddhāntaḥ</b> । pāne pramāṇābhāvāt vigraha-
vattādinirākaraṇāt devatātvenaivopalakṣaṇam । na ca dvidevatā, indradevatyā ityāgneyatulyatā ।
ekasaṃbandhe'pi tulyaśruterasabhavenānekasaṃbandhyapi gṛhyata iti pratyudāharaṇamātrametat ।</p>
<p><b>chandaśca devatāvat । devatayā tulyaṃ chanda iti manvānasya</b> na pṛthagvyākhyānam ।
<b>anuṣṭup‌chandasa iti chandontaravidhānāt namatītyasya parihāraḥ</b> viśiṣṭavidhānamidamityarthaḥ ।
<b>aindraḥ somo gṛhyate mīyate ca iti samānavidhāne sthite yathāliṅgaṃ mantraḥ</b> । tatra samantrakaṃ
grahaṇaṃ mānaṃ ca । anyatra mantraśūnyam । <b>tasmādidamapyakāraṇaṃ prakṛtivikārabhāvasya</b> ।
<note>(1) Bhashya 801</note>
﻿<pb n="r746"/>
ataḥ sthitaṃ samānavidhānam । sthite samānavidhāne idānīmindrapītasyeti <b>savanasāmānādhi-
karaṇyāt sarve mantravanta iti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---indrapītaśabdo'yaṃ bahuvrīhiḥ indreṇa
pītaṃ yasmin savana iti । nanu sarvīpasarjano bahuvrīhiḥ tṛtīyāsamāsād‌durbalaḥ । ucyate ।
tṛtīyāsamāsa evātra na saṃbhavati । yo'pīndrāya dattaḥ nāsau bhakṣyate । yaśca bhakṣyate na sa
indrapīta ityasaṃbhavāt । bahuvrīhyāśrayaṇena savanasāmānādhikaraṇyāt sarve somāḥ
<b>samantrakā iti</b> ।</p>

﻿<pb n="r747"/>
<head>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<head>śruterjātādhikāraḥ syāt ।</head>
<p>atra māṣyakāreṇa sandehaḥ kṛtaḥ---kimṛg‌jātimadhikṛtya ete śabdāḥ ityādinā ।
tadva‍yācaṣṭe---<b>uccairṛcā kriyata iti kimayaṃ vedadharmaḥ uca ṛgdharma iti saṃśayaḥ</b> । ākṣipatti
---<b>ko'yaṃ vedo nāma ? nanu cargapi veda eva</b> ityekagranthaḥ । asyārthaḥ---ko'yaṃ vedo nāma
na ca vidhivākyameva kevalaṃ vedaśabdenocyate kintu ṛgapi । tataśca vedadharmatvepi ṛgdha-
rmatā na nirākriyate । tenāpratipakṣatvāt saṃśaya evānupapannaḥ । samādhatte---<b>ucyate---vidhāyakaṃ
vākyaṃ vedaśabdenocyate</b> । saṃśayavākye vedaśabdo'yaṃ vidhāyakavākyaparatvena prayuktaḥ
tenātra vidhāyakaṃ vākyaṃ vedaśabdenocyate । nanvevamapi saṃśayo'nupapanna eva । kiṃ
vidhāyakadharmaḥ utargdharma iti । ṛcāmapi kāsāṃcita vidhāyakatā'styeva yathā kapiñjalānā--
labhata iti । kiñca vidhāyakasya vākyasyānaṅgatvāt tatra dharmā vidhīyamānā vidhyasaṃsparśinaḥ
anarthakā evāpadyanta itīmāmāśaṅkāmapaninīṣurāha---<b>etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---yadṛgvedaśabdavācyaṃ
vidhāyakaṃ vākyaṃ tadvidheyadharmaḥ uta yatra pādavyavasthā tasmin mantra iti</b> । asyārthaḥ
---uccairṛcā kriyata ityasya vacanasya kimayamarthaḥ yadṛcā yadṛgvedena ṛk‌prāyaśākhādhītena vidhinā
kriyate yattenānuṣṭhetvena jñāpyate taduccaiḥ kartavyam । yat ṛgvedādhītena vidhinā'nuṣṭheyatvena
<note>(1) B. P. 803</note>
﻿<pb n="r748"/>
jñāpyate'dhikāravidhiḥ tasyoccaiṣṭvaṃ dharmaḥ sa ca sākṣādanena saṃbaddha‍umaśaktaḥ tadaṅge śabde niviśate ।
atha yadṛcā mantreṇa kriyate taduccairiti kāryāntarasmaraṇajanakatayā vyāpṛtāyā ṛcaḥ uccaiṣṭvaṃ
vidhīyata iti । <b>kiṃ tāvad‍yuk‍taṃ ? uccairṛceti vacanāt ṛgdharmo'yaṃ iti</b> । asyārthaḥ
---uccaiḥ ṛcā kriyata iti vacanāt ṛk‌śabdasya mukhyayā vṛttyā mantravacanatvānmantradharmo'yamiti ।
<b>nanu vedopakramametadvākyaṃ</b> tenopakramānuguṇatayā ṛgādiśabdenāpi vedaścocyata iti ।
pariharati---<b>ko doṣaḥ ṛkṣvapyayaṃ vedaśabdo vartata iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---vedyate aneneti
vyutpattyā vartamāno vedaśabdaḥ prayogavaśena apauruṣeyaśabdaviṣayatayā paṅkajādiśabdavanniyamyamānaḥ
ṛkṣu vidhiṣu ca mukhyaḥ tatrāvirodhādvedaśabdo'pi mantrapara eva । tenāyaṃ mantradharmaḥ ।
<b>evaṃ ca mantradharmatve sati na vikalpo vedāntarapaṭhitasya ṛg‌jātasya</b> । vidheyadharmapakṣe tu
anekadharmavidheyatayā ekatrāpi mantre anekadharmaprasaṅgāt vikalpa āpadyate ।</p>
<p><b>vedo vā prāyadarśanāt । atrocyate---vedadharmo'yam</b> । adhikāravidhidharmaḥ iti
yāvat । <b>kutaḥ ? vedaśabdopakramatvādvākyasya</b> । tenopakramavaśenopasaṃhāragataṛkśabdo
vidhilakṣaṇārthaḥ iti । <b>nanu copakramopasaṃhāravaśāt ṛkṣu vartata ityuktam । satyamuktam ।
tat‍tu nopapadyate । kathaṃ nopapadyate ? evaṃ nopapadyate । upakrame yaḥ padārthaḥ parijñāto</b>
<note>(1) P. 805</note>
﻿<pb n="r749"/>
<b>bhavati tadviśeṣapratipattireva kevalaṃ upasaṃhārādapekṣyate । na punaḥ tadvirodhyarthāntaram</b> ।
yaḥ khalu padārthaḥ prathamaśrutaḥ tamaparityajyaiva tadviśeṣa eva kevalamupasaṃhāreṇa apekṣyate na
punastadupamardyāpyarthāntaram । <b>ato'virodhidharmavidhānamevoccaiṣṭvādividhānameva kevalaṃ
vedenopakramapratītena saṃbadhyate । ṛk‌śabdastvānuguṇyādanuvādaḥ</b> । upakramagatavedaśabdānu-
guṇyāt vedānuvāda eva ṛk‌śabdo vedamanuvadati lakṣaṇayā । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ nargvedaśabdenocyate</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---upakramavaśenopasaṃhāragatark‌śabdo lakṣaṇayā varṇyata iti vadataḥ tava siddhāntavādinaḥ
ayamāśayo lakṣyate-vedaśabdo'yaṃ na ṛkṣu vartata iti । taccedamanupapannam kathaṃ vedaśabdo narkṣu
vartate yāvatā vartetaiva । tataścāvirodhāta ṛk‌para eva vedaśabdo bhaviṣyati । <b>uttaraṃ-kena vokata
nocyata iti । kintu vidheyatayā na vidhāyakavat</b> । asyārthaḥ---vedaśabdo'yaṃ yaugiko
vedayatīti tatra vidhāyakavākyasya nirapekṣaṃ vedatvaṃ vidheyasya tu mantrajātasya viniyogāpekṣamartha-
prakāśanakaraṇatvamiti sāpekṣanirapekṣatayā na tulyā vedaśabdasya pravṛttiḥ vidhividheyamantravidhyoḥ ।
ataḥ <b>upakramagatena vedaśabdena nirapekṣatayā vidhirevocyate</b> । tataścopakramagatavidhivāciveda-
śabdānuguṇyāt ṛk‌śabdo'pi vidhipara eveti adhikāravidhidharmo'yam । <b>dṛṣṭaścāyaṃ ṛk‌śabdo
vede</b> ṛgbhiḥ prātardivi deva riyate iti । tena lakṣaṇāpyeṣā nātīvāprasiddheti darśayati ।
<b>kuta etat ?</b> vede ṛgādiśabda iti <b>yajurvede tiṣṭhati madhye ahnaḥ iti sahayogāt</b>
<note>(1) G. bhedena</note>
﻿<pb n="r750"/>
vedapara evāyaṃ ṛk‌śabda ityarthaḥ । <b>dharmopadeśaśca sāmnāṃ</b> pṛthak‌tvena yassāmnaḥ uccaiṣṭ‌vo-
padeśaḥ sa <b>evamevopapadyate anyathā</b> mantradharmapakṣe hi ṛg‌vidhānāt ṛk‌śabdenoccaiṣṭ‌va-
vidhānasiddheḥ <b>pṛthagvidhānamanarthakaṃ syāt</b> । na ca prajāpaterhṛdayādiṣu anṛgāśriteṣu sāmasu
vidhānamarthavat jyotiṣṭome teṣāmabhāvāt । mantradharmapakṣe hi jyotiṣṭoma eva niveśaḥ । na
ca tatra prajāpaterhṛdayādīnāṃ saṃbhava iti ।</p>
<p><b>trayīvidyākhyā ca tadvidi1 । trayīvidyaśabdaśca tadvidi vedatrayavidi vartate ।
kiṃ tataḥ ? idaṃ tato bhavati vede ṛgādiśabdānāṃ prayogo dṛṣṭa iti</b> yo vedatrayavit saḥ
trayīvidya iti ucyate ṛgādiśabdaśca trayyāṃ prayuktaḥ ṛgyajussāmāni trīṇi trayīti । tasmā-
dṛgādiśabdo vede dṛṣṭa iti । <b>yatpunarvedāntaroktasya</b> vihitasya <b>svarāntarāpattiriti
vidhānānna doṣaḥ</b> pramāṇabalādāyāto vikalpaḥ na doṣāya bhavatītyarthaḥ । <b>prakaraṇabādhaśca
vākyādiṣyata eva</b> । tena prakaraṇālocanāsamutthāṃ jyotiṣṭomāṅgatāṃ vākyena bādhitvā sakala-
kratvaṅgateti । <b>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ vedasaṃyogepi prakaraṇaṃ nānugṛhyate ṛgdharmavidhānavat</b> । yathā
ṛgvarmavidhau prakaraṇānugrahaḥ tathā'trāpi kiṃ na syāditi । ucyate---<b>ṛcāmaṅgatvāt taddharmaḥ
prakaraṇena gṛhyata iti yuktam</b> । aṅgāśrito hi dharmo'dhikāravidhinā gṛhyata iti yuktam ।
<note>(1) Bhashya P. 808</note>
﻿<pb n="r751"/>
vedadharmatve <b>punarvidhānamupalakṣaṇam</b> । <b>na ca tadaṅgamiti yāvadvidhānaṃ dharmavidhiḥ</b> ।
vedaprameyādhikāravidhidharmapakṣe'dhikāravidhirupalakṣaṇaṃ, tatra dharkasaṃbandhāsaṃbhavāt । tadaṅgeṣu
saṃbandheṣu dharmaḥ । na cādhikāravidhiraṅgamiti yāvadadhikāravidhiṃ dharmasaṃbandhaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>guṇamukhyavyatikrame । <q>‘ya evaṃ vidvānagnimādhante’</q> iti yājurvaidiko vidhiḥ <q>‘ya
evaṃ vidvān vāravantīyaṃ gāyati’</q> ityādhānaprakaraṇe sāmavaidika iti kṛtvācintyate</b> ।
yājurvaidike pradhāne sāmavaidikamaṅgamiti kṛtvācinteyam । kimatra cintyate ? <b>yājurvaidike
bhavatūpāṃśutvaṃ sāmavaidikecoccaiṣṭvaṃ</b> bhinnādhikaraṇatve copāṃśutvoccaiṣṭbayoravirodha ipi ।
atra samādhiḥ---<b>satyamevaṃ yadyaṅgapradhānavidhī bhidyete</b> tadā vidhibhedāt tannibandhano dharmavidhiḥ
syāt <b>yathātvabhedaḥ tathā phalavatsannidhāvaphalaṃ tadaṅgamityatra vakṣyati । abhedecobhayaveda-
vidhānādbhabati saṃśayaḥ</b> । ākṣeptā''ha---tathāpi na saṃśayaḥ <b>ubhayavedavidhānāt
vikalpo bhavatu</b> । pariharati---<b>na vikalpaḥ saṃbhavati । evaṃ sati aṅgavidhiranuvādaḥ</b>
<note>(1) B. P. 809</note>
﻿<pb n="r752"/>
ityaṅgavidheḥ <b>pradhānavidhitantratāṃ darśayati</b> । asyārthaḥ---syādvikalpaḥ yadyumayadharmaprāptiḥ
syāt । vidhibhede cobhayadharmaprāptiḥ । na pradhānavidhito'ṅgavidhīnāṃ bhedo'sti ।
tena pradhānaikavidhidharmeṇaiva bhavitavyamiti na vikalpaḥ । ākṣeptā'ha---<b>tathāpi kassaṃśayaḥ</b>
niścita eva pradhānavidherdharmaḥ । samarthayitā saṃśayamāha---<b>kimasāvaṅgavidhirākṣiptasvavidheya
eva pradhānatantro bhavati uta pradhānenakībhūto vidheyaṃ vidhatta iti</b> । yadyātmīyaṃ vidheyaṃ
vidhāya paścādekatāṃ yāti tadā prathamāvasthāyāṃ 1vihitatvādvāravantīyasya sāmavaidikenaiva
svareṇa bhavitavyam । atha pradhānenaikībhūtasyaiva vidheyatvaṃ tadā yājurvaidikenopāṃśutvenaṃ
bhavitavyamiti saṃśayaḥ । tatra <b>pūrvapakṣavādī manyate svārthaṃ vidhāya prayojanavaśāt pradhāne-
naikībhavati vāravantīyaṃ gāyatītyasya svārthaḥ ।</b> <b>atassāmavaidikasvarayuk‍tasyaivāṅgabhāvaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---svavākyenaiva vākyāntaranirapekṣeṇaiva svārtho jñāpyate । tasya tu niradhikārāyā
prayuktyabhāvenāprayojakatvāt vāvayasyārthāntarānupraveśaḥ । ataḥ pradhānavidhyananupraviṣṭenaivāṅga-
vidhinā aṅgasya vihitatvāt tannibandhanasvarayuktasyaiva pradhānavidhāvaṅgateti vāravantīyasya sāma-
vaidikena svareṇa bhavitavyam । <b>atrābhidhīyate</b> । <b>satyaṃ, vihitasvārtha eva</b> nirjñāpita-
svārtha eva <b>pradhānena</b> vivinā <b>ekībhavati । na punuraṅgatāmapi vidhāya</b> । tenāṅgatvasya
aṅgavidhinā anavabodhitatvāta । tena tanna kriyate na svārthajñānamātreṇāṅgānuṣṭhānam । kiṃ
tarhi aṅgatvajñānena । ataḥ tannibandhano na bhavati svaraḥ। yadyaṅgavidhiraṅgatāṃ na jñāpayati
kastarhi jñāpayatītyatrāha---<b>pradhānavidhiraṅgatāṃ vidhatta iti saptamādye vakṣyate</b> । sa evādhi-
<note>(1) G. abhihitatvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r753"/>
kāravidhiḥ sannihitamarthaṃ svārthatayā jñāpayati । na punaravāntaravidhayaḥ svārthānāmaṅgabhāvaṃ
jñāpayantīti grāhakavyutpattyā saptamādye vakṣyati । <b>aṅgatayā ca vāravantīyasya prayogaḥ na
vāravantīyaṃ gāyatītyasya vidherviṣayatathā</b> । na svarūpajñānādanuṣṭhānaṃ karmaṇām vinopayoga-
jñānāt, duḥkhātmakatvāt karmaṇāmiti । upasaṃharati---<b>ato na svārthavidhiḥ prayogavidhiṃ
bādhitumarhati svārthasya prayogārthatvāt</b> । aṅgavidhiḥ prayogavidhinibandhanaṃ na dharmaṃ
bādhitumarhati tadarthatvāt prayogavidhyarthatvādaṅgavidheḥ । anena caitaduk‍taṃ bhavati । yadyapyaṅgavidhiḥ
svārtha pravṛttaḥ tathāpi pradhānavidhinibandhanenaiva dharmeṇa bhavitavyaṃ tasya pradhānaguṇatvāditi ।
<b>tadidaṃ</b> dvayaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇoktam ---<b>guṇasyānuṣṭhānena mukhyaḥ saguṇaḥ kathaṃ syāditi</b> guṇa-
syānuṣṭhāne pravartata ityanena granthena <b>3na guṇavidheḥ svārthe pravṛttirityuk‍taṃ</b> <q>‘guṇapravṛttyā cet’</q>
ityādinā bhāṣyeṇa । <b>prayogāṅgatvācca guṇāvidheḥ pradhānaguṇena bhavitavyamityuktam</b> ।
prayogaḥ pradhānavidhiḥ ।</p>
<p><b>bhūyastvenobhayaśruti । sthitaṃ tāvat pradhānavidhinibandhano guṇaḥ guṇavidhi-</b>

<b>nibandhanaṃ guṇaṃ bādhata iti</b> । anenāvāntarasaṃgatiruktā । adhyāyasaṅgatiśca pradhānasvara-
niyogārthācintetyarthaḥ । <b>idamapīdānīṃ cintyate yatrobhayatra pradhānasya śrutiḥ tatra kva pradhāna-
codaneti yatra vede pradhānacodanā tannibandhanena svareṇa bhavitavyam tatsidhyarthā eṣā
cintā</b> । <b>tatrāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣaṇatvāt ubhayatra</b> vede pradhānacodanetyuktvā bhūyastvenaika-
treti nirūpitam । tathā dṛṣṭāntābhidhānaṃ kṛtam । <b>bālavyajanādinā bahuṣu rājaprati---
meṣūpaviṣṭeṣu rājāvagamyata iti</b> । <b>tadidamubhayamayuk‍taṃ</b> na bhūyastvaṃ hetuḥ na vālavyajanādi-
dṛṣṭāntaḥ । hetudoṣamāha---<b>kva bhūyastvenāṅgānāṃ pradhānasya prayogābhidhātaṃ dṛṣṭam</b> । 
kvacidapi na bhūyastvaṃ prayogābhidhāne hetuḥ <b>na ca vālavyajanaṃ ś‍vetacchatraṃ ca bhūyastvādavagama-
yati । rki tarhi</b> ? <b>asādhāraṇatayā</b> rājavyatirekeṇānyatrābhāvāt vipakṣādva‍yāvṛttatayā ca
asādhāraṇābhidhānaṃ, gandhaktvāditulyatve tu anavagamakataiva syāt । <b>tasmādasaṃbandhamidaṃ
bhāṣyaṃ manyāmahe---atrābhidhīyate</b> । <b>nedamasaṃbaddha, bhūyastvena hi prayogāvagamaḥ sūcyate
sakalaprayogo'vagamyata ityarthaḥ</b> । yatrāṅgabhūyastvaṃ tatra sakalaprayogo jñāyate । alpāṅgā-
<note>(1) P. 810</note>
﻿<pb n="r755"/>
<b>bhidhāne punaḥ na sakalaprayogāvagatirbhavati sakale ca prayoge'vagamyamāne prayogābhidhānamati-
rbhavati</b> । kutaḥ <b>prameyāddhi pramāṇāvagatiriti sthitam</b> । prayogo hi prameyaḥ, prayogavidhi: 
pramāṇaṃ, sarvatra ca prameye'vagate pramāṇamavagamyate । tena sakalaprayogāvagame prameyasyā-
vagatatvāt pramāṇāvagatirbhavatīti tatraiva prayogavidhiḥ । alpāṅgāvagame tu prayogānavagamāt 
prayogavidhyanavagatiriti sthitaṃ bhūyastvena prayogavidhijñānam । yadapi vālavyajanamupanyastaṃ
dṛṣṭāntatvena tadgamakasāmānyatayā tacca astyeveti sūktam । yathā vālavyajanādinā rājāvagatiḥ
tathā bhūyastvenāpi prayogavidhyavagatiriti dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikayoḥ sāmyaṃ 2na punarubhayoreka-
prakāraṃ 3gamakatvamiti vivakṣitam ।</p>
<p><b>asaṃyuk‍taṃ prakaraṇāt</b> । <q>“kimetāvantyeva pramāṇāti”</q> iti bhāṣyam । tadā-
kṣipati---<b>kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānīti</b> ko'yaṃ <b>praśnaḥ</b> । <b>yadi tāvat sūtrārtha eva na
śakyate vyākhyātuṃ praśnena vināpi ityabhiprāyaḥ tadayuktam</b> । <b>kimatra praś‍nena</b> yāvatā
<b>yadasaṃyuk‍taṃ tat prakaraṇena viniyujyata iti</b> । śak‍yata eva sūtrārtho vyākhyātum ।
<note>(1) Bhasya P. 816</note> <note>(2) G. omits na</note> <note>(3) R. pradhānatvagamaka</note>
﻿<pb n="r756"/>
<b>nanu ca kenāsaṃyuktamiti na vidmaḥ ? evaṃ tarhi etadeva praṣṭavyam kenāsaṃyuktamiti । kaveda-
mupayucyate kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānīti । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ, kimiti śrutyā liṅgena
vākyena vā yadasaṃyuk‍taṃ tatprakaraṇena viniyujyata iti</b> । <b>kimetāvantyeva</b> catvāryeva
pramāṇāni । yadyanyadapi syāt tadā tenāpi viniyogo bhavatyeveti । yadyapyevaṃ praśno ghaṭate 
<b>tadāpi uttaraṃ tāvadasaṃbaddham anyadapyastīti</b> । kathamasaṃbaddhaṃ ? <b>yadyanyadapyasti
kimiti śrutyā liṅgena vākyena cāsaṃyuk‍taṃ</b> prakaraṇena viniyujyata <b>ityucyate</b>, catuṣṭa-
yātirekeṇāpi viniyogo vaktavya eveti । etacca praśnasyopapattimabhyupagamyocyate । paramārthatastu
praśno'pi nopapadyate eveti śrutiliṅgavākyaiḥ asaṃyuk‍taṃ prakaraṇena viniyujyata iti tenānyapramāṇā-
nirākaraṇāt praśno'pi nopapadyata iti । etacca <q>“tathāpyuttaraṃ tāvat”</q> ityatra tathāpāti
śabdaprayogādavagamyate । <b>athājñānameva naiva śrutiliṅgavākyebhyaḥ pramāṇamanyadvijñāyate</b>
iti tena pramāṇāntaramajānata eṣa praśnaḥ kimetāvannīti tathāpyevamapi vyākhyāyamāne <b>svarūpaṃ
vak‍tavyaṃ nāsaṃyuk‍taṃ prakaraṇāditi yujyate kartavyasyetikartavyatākāṅgasyeti vakṣyamāṇava-
ddhak‍tavyam</b> । yathā kartavyasyeti prakaraṇasvarūpaṃ vakṣyati tathā vaktavyaṃ na punarasaṃyuk‍taṃ
﻿<pb n="r757"/>
prakaraṇāditi vak‍tuṃ yujyate । <b>ataḥ praśnārtho'naupayika iva dṛśyate । atrābhidhīyate
-ayamabhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya । lakṣaṇādāvuk‍taṃ śeṣalakṣaṇamucyate śrutyādīni ca viniyoge
kāraṇānīti ca । tatra tāvat śrutiliṅgavākyaiḥ viniyojyaṃ śeṣatvamuktam । prakaraṇa-
viniyojyaṃ punaḥ kimatra bhaviṣyati</b> । <b>nanu ca prayājādayaḥ santyevaṃ</b> prakaraṇaviniyojyāḥ
<b>kimiti praśnaḥ ? bāḍhaṃ praśnārthaḥ</b> praśnasya prayojanaṃ <b>vidyate prayājādīnāṃ hi ekaniyogalakṣaṇa-
saṃbandhaṃ caturthe bakṣyati darśapūrṇamāsādibhiḥ kimatrānyat</b> pramāṇāntaraṃ <b>mṛgyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
---ekenaivātrādhikāraniyogena sarveṣāṃ prayājāgneyādīnāṃ saṃbandhaṃ caturthe vakṣyati tataśca <q>‘samidho
yajati’</q> ityevamādibhiḥ karaṇopakārakatayā'nvitaiḥ paramāpūrvamanvitamucyata iti śrauta evāyaṃ
viniyogaḥ kimatrānyena pramāṇena । <b>evaṃ ca tad‌bhūtādhikaraṇok‍ta eva saṃbandho'nvitā-
bhidhāyibhiḥ padaiḥ sarvatra śabdārthāvagamaheturiti vyāpakaṃ bhavati</b> । tad‍‏bhūtādhikaraṇovata
eva saṃbandho'nvitābhidhānadvārakāpūrvānvayapratipādakapadalabhyaḥ sarvatra śabdārthāvagamaheturiti
vyāpakaṃ bhavati । evaṃ ca sati <b>pramāṇāntare punaranviṣyamāṇe nānvitābhidhānanibandhanaḥ</b>
<note>(1) Bhashya 652</note>
﻿<pb n="r758"/>
saṃbandhaḥ <b>śakyate darśayitum ।</b> kutaḥ ityatrāha---<b>prakaraṇādibhirvākyārthānāṃ saṃbandhā-
vagatiḥ</b> prayājādiniyogānāṃ vākyārthānāṃ, vākyārthabhūtasyādhikāraniyogasya ca saṃbandhaḥ
prakaraṇādibhiravagamyate । <b>na ca vākyārthasya</b> ca vākyārthasya <b>saṃbandhe padābhidhānalakṣaṇaḥ
saṃbandhaḥ</b> । kasmādityāha---<b>anvitaṃ padaṃ padārthāntareṇa padārthamācaṣṭe</b> । tena padārthānā-
mevānvitābhidhānalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ <b>na punarvākyārthaṃ vākyārthāntareṇānvitamabhidhatte vākyam</b> ।
vākyasyākhaṇḍasyāvācakatvāt । bhāgaśo hi vākyādvākyārthāvagatiriti tatra tatrok‍tam ।
upasaṃharati---<b>ato darśapūrṇamāsārthatayā prayājādivākyārthānvayamaśābdaṃ manvānasya praśnaḥ ।</b>
vākyārthānvayamaśābdaṃ manyate । padārthānvayastu bhavati śābdaḥ tasmiṃstu pakṣe na śrutyādyatirikta---
pramāṇasiddhiriti manvānasyāyaṃ praśnaḥ । <b>nanu caitāvantyeva pramāṇānīti aśābdaṃ vākyārtha
saṃbandhaṃ manvānasya praś‍nena bhavitavyam</b> । <b>na punaḥ kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānīti । ucyate
---etadevok‍taṃ yadyasaṃyuktaṃ</b> śrutyādibhiḥ <b>na tarhi viniyojyamapi</b> aśābdatvādvākyārthayoḥ
saṃbandhasyeti pramāṇāntarākṣepa evāyaṃ yatastvayā siddhāntavādinā <b>1asaṃyuktamiti vadatā
etāvantyeva pramāṇāni ityuktam</b> । <b>ataḥ</b> upapanno'yaṃ <b>praśnaḥ</b> asaṃyuktagrahaṇe sati
<note>(1) G. saṃyukta</note>
﻿<pb n="r759"/>
<b>kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānīti</b> । asyārthaḥ---siddhāntavādinaivāsaṃyuk‍tagrahaṇe tu kṛte pūrvapakṣa-
vādyāha --- kiṃ tavāpyetāvantayeva pramāṇānīti sammataṃ yena śrutyādyasaṃyuk‍taṃ2 asaṃyuk‍tamiti brūṣe ।
anyathā śrutyādyasaṃyuk‍tamapi kimityasaṃyuk‍taṃ syāta ityevaṃ praśnaḥ । <b>itarastu</b> rāddhāntavādī
<b>nāvaśyaṃ padārthānvitamevedaṃ śābdam</b> । <b>aidamarthyenāpi śabdaḥ saṃbandhaṃ pratipādayatyeveti
manvāno netyuktavān</b> । asyārthaḥ---na mayā asaṃyuktaśabdaṃ prayuñjānena sarvathā'saṃprayuktatva-
muk‍tam । kintu prakaraṇasya pṛthak pramāṇatvadarśanāya śrutyādyasaṃyuk‍taṃ prakaraṇena viniyujyata
ityuktam । yastu tavābhiprāyaḥ vākyārthānāṃ parasparasaṃbandho'śābda iti so'pyayuk‍taḥ nāvaśyaṃ
padārthānvitameva śābdaṃ śabdaprameyam । kintu aidamarthyānyathānupapattyā gamyamānamapi śābdaṃ
bhavatyeva । kasmādityāha ---<b>aidamarthyenāpi śabdaḥ saṃbandhaṃ pratipādayatyeveti</b> । asyārthaḥ
--- na prathamameva padārthairitikartavyatābhāvenānvitaiḥ anvitaṃ paramāpūrvamabhidhīyate, kintu aidamarthya
mātreṇānvitaiḥ । pradhānavidhireva svārthamavāntaravākyārthairanvitaṃ abhidhatte । avāntaravidhayastu
svārthān svarūpamātreṇaiva sannidhāpayanti । ata eva ca saptamādye pradhānavidhirevāṅgatāṃ vidhatta
ityuk‍tam । tena svavākyenopāttakaraṇāvarudve paramāpūrve prakārāntareṇānvayānupapatteḥ karaṇopakāra-
katayaivānvayāt na pramāṇāntataramastīti pūrvapakṣiṇok‍te sāmānyenaidamarthyānvayāsaṃbhavāt karaṇoḥ-
pakārakatayā viśeṣānvayāsaṃbhavāt śeṣānvayābhidhānena arthabhedo vidyata iti karaṇānvayasidhyarthaṃ
prakaraṇaṃ nāma pramāṇāntaraṃ astīti manvāto rāddhāntī netyuktavāt । itarastu rāddhāntino
bhāvamanababudhyamānaḥ pṛcchati---<b>kimaparaṃ kāraṇamiti</b> <q>“praśnenaivopakrama”</q> iti bhāṣyam । 
tasyārthaḥ praś‍nenaivopakramaḥ pūrvapakṣa iti tadva‍yācaṣṭe---<b>pūrvoktasya praś‍nārthasya</b> vivaraṇametat ।
<note>(1) Bhashya P. 817</note> <note>(2) asaṃyuktamātraṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r760"/>
<b>kā nāmeyo nadīti</b> । kasyacit jñātanadyarthasyaivākṣepābhiprāyaḥ praśna upapadyata iti । sa cāyaṃ
praś‍nārthaḥ <q>‘‘kathaṃ punarasaṃyuktasyaiva viniyoga”</q> ityena manthena prakaṭīkṛtaḥ । <b>tadidamaida-
marthyalakṣaṇaṃ kathayati । iti kartavyatārthitvāt iti</b> । yadītikartavyatārthitvādityanena
śeṣatvamuk‍taṃ tadā aidamarthyalakṣaṇaṃ aidamairthyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ yasya tata tathok‍tam । <b>nanu coktaṃ
ekaniyogalakṣaṇasaṃbandho'yaṃ, kimidamitikartavyatārthitvaṃ nāma</b> । ekaniyogatvenaiva
saṃbandhasiddheritikartavyatārthitvaṃ nāma na pramāṇāntaramiti । <b>ucyate---ekaniyogalakṣaṇa-
saṃbandho nopapadyate yadītikartavyatālakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandho na syāt iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---ekaṃ 
sādhikāraniyogaṃ prati aidamarthye'vagate'pi yāvaditikartavyatālakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandho nāvagamyate tāva-
nnirviśeṣaviṣayasyaidamarthyasyānyathānupapatteḥ karaṇāvaruddhatvācca ekaniyogalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandho-
nopapadyate । kathaṃ nopapadyate itayatrāha---<b>na hyasaṃbandhavidheyasya ekavidhānatā upapadyate</b> ।
asaṃbandho vidheyo yasya vidheḥ, yadvidhirvidheyena saha sa vidhiḥ tena sahaikavidhānatāmeva na labhate
<b>vidheyanānātvāt</b> । svabhāvato nānābhūtathorvidhyoḥ vidheyona nānābhūtena nānābhūtavidheyayośca
yeyamekavidhānatā sā vidheyayoḥ parasparasaṃbandhaṃ vinā nopapadyate । tenāvāntaravidhyarthānāṃ
svavidhividheyānāṃ pradhānavidheritikartavyatārthitvalakṣaṇena prakaraṇena pradhānavidhividheyena karaṇena
saha karaṇetikartavyatālakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pradhānaniyogenaidamarthyalakṣaṇassaṃbandho'nvitābhidhānanibandhana
﻿<pb n="r761"/>
eva । tadākṣiptastu yaḥ karaṇetikartavyatālakṣaṇassaṃbandhaḥ so'pi śābda eva । atra ceyaṃ prakriyā
avāntaravidhyarthā vidheyāḥ pradhānavidhiṃ pratyupādīyamānatvāt yaddhi yatsiddha‍yarthamupādīyate
tat tadvidheyamiti tantre vyavahāraḥ pradhānavidhistu na vidheyaḥ । nanu pradhānavidhyanupraveśaḥ
kathamitikartavyatāyāḥ yāvatā2 karaṇamātraparyavasāyinyeva setyatrāha---<b>upapadyate ca karaṇasyeti
kartavyatayā saṃbandhaḥ</b> । karaṇasyetikartavyatayā niyogasya <b>saṃbandhaḥ anyatrāpi laukike
sādhye darśanāt</b> । lokikasyāpi sādhyasyetikartavyatayā saṃbandhaḥ karaṇaṃ tu dvāramātramiti
lokapratītam । <b>sādhyaścāyaṃ niyogārthaḥ</b> । upasaṃharati---<b>tasmādupapannaṃ itikartavyatā-
rthitvāditi vidheyasaṃbandhakāraṇam</b> । vidheyayoḥ saṃbandhakāraṇamiti । vyākhyāṃta cedam ।
yadi vākyārthayorapi saṃbandhaḥ śābdaḥ <b>kimiti tarhi vākyasyaivārthena autpattikaḥ saṃbandho
darśitaḥ</b> yāvatā vākyasamūhasyāpi darśayitavyaḥ । <b>ucyate---asūtrārthajño bhavān kriyārthe-
neti vadatā sarvasyaivāsya prāmāṇyaṃ darśitam</b> । yāvaddhi kriyārthatayā niyogārthatayā prati-
pādyate tasya sarvasyānvayaḥ śābda eva na pratibhāmātrakalpita iti sarvasyāsya padārthānvayalakṣaṇasya
vākyārthānvayalakṣaṇasya ca prāmāṇyaṃ darśitam । nanvevaṃ vadatā niyogārthena sahaidamarthyalakṣaṇaḥ
saṃbandha eva śābda ityuk‍taṃ na punarvidheyānāmapi parasparasaṃbandha ityatrāha---<b>aidamarthyalakṣaṇameva
saṃbandhaṃ vedavido manyanye । tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ tu padārthānāmapi anvitābhidhānaṃ dṛṣṭam</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---padārthānāmapi yaḥ parasparasaṃbandhaḥ sa aidamarthyalakṣaṇasaṃbandhasidhyartha eva । sarvasyātra
<note>(1) G. kāraṇa</note>
﻿<pb n="762"/>
niyogaidamarthyalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandhaḥ tenehāpi vākyārthānāṃ niyogaidamarthyalakṣaṇassaṃbandhaḥ ।
tatsiddha‍yarthastu vidheyasaṃbandha iti । niyogaida<b>marthyameva</b> ca śabdasya <b>pramāṇāntaratve hetuḥ</b>
tatra pramāṇāntarānavagamāt । <b>anvitārthābhidhānaṃ tu</b> loke'pi tulyam । <b>devadattaḥ
kāṣṭaiḥ sthālyāmodaṃna pacatītyevamādiṣu laukikeṣvapi</b> । adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati---<b>ataḥ
prakaraṇaviniyojyamapi śeṣatvamastīti siddham</b> । prayojanaṃ tu saptamādyapūrvapakṣanyāyena
vyākhyātamiti na vyākhyātam ।</p>
<p><b>kramaśca deśasāmānyāt । atredānīṃ kaḥ praśnārthaḥ</b> pūrvādhikaraṇe hi prakaraṇaṃ nāma
pramāṇāntaraṃ nāstītyanenābhiprāyeṇa yuktaḥ praśnaḥ । atra punaḥ kaḥ praśnārthaḥ । uttaraṃ
---<b>aidamarthyalakṣaṇameva saṃbandhaṃ vede vedavido manyanta ityuktam</b> । sa ca saṃbandhamātramevā-
pādayiṃtu samarthaḥ tāvanmātreṇaivopapatteḥ na punaḥ karaṇaviśeṣasaṃbandhamapi । api ca aidamarthya-
vyatirekeṇa deśasāmānyameva na saṃbandho'sti yo'nyathānupapadyamānaḥ viśeṣakaraṇasaṃbandhaṃ kalpa-
yatīti pramāṇāntarabhūtakramākṣeparūpaḥ2 praśnaḥ । <b>nanu caitāvantyeva pramāṇānītyākṣepeṇa
bhavitavyam । kimidaṃ <q>‘kimetāvantyeva pramāṇāni’</q> iti । atrocyate---atrāpyasaṃyukta-</b>
<note>(1) Bhashya P. 819 (2) R. kṣepaparaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r763"/>
<b>grahaṇaṃ viṣayāntarapradarśanārthatayā</b>'nuvartate । tasmin satyayaṃ praśnaḥ pūrvavadityanavadyam ।
itara āha-<b>satyamaidamarthyavyatirekeṇa saṃbandho nāsti tathāpi pramāṇāntaramastyeva aidamarthya-
viśeṣāvagatau sthānasāmānyaṃ nāma । tadidamuktaṃ kramaśca deśasāmānyāditi</b> । asyārthaḥ
---dabdhirnāmāsīdityanumantraṇamantraḥ kenacidanumantraṇīyena sahaikāvākyatāmākāṅkṣati tena
sannihietenaikavākyatāṃ yāti । yatraiva sthānena ekavākyatāpūrvakaḥ śeṣabhāvaḥ tatra sthānenaiva
viśeṣakaraṇasaṃbandhaḥ iti । <b>prayojanaṃ tu darśitameva</b> ।</p>
<p><b>ākhyā caivaṃ tadarthatvāt । atredānīṃ praśnārtho nopapadyate aidamarthye sati
sthānabat viśeṣāvagame hetutvāt samākhyāyāḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---adhvaryvādayaḥ prakaraṇe
paripaṭhitāḥ niyogenaidamarthyāpannā kathamaidamarthyaṃ bhajantāmiti ādhvaryavamityādibhiḥ 2karmaviśeṣā-
bhidhāyinīmiḥ samākhyābhiḥ viśeṣakāryasaṃbandhāvagamāt tad‌dvāreṇaiva śeṣatvamiti samākhyāyāḥ
prāmāṇyāt tadākṣepāya na praśna upapadyate । ucyate---<b>astyatra viśeṣaḥ</b> sthānasamākhyayoḥ
<b>yuktaṃ tāvat sthānasya viśeṣāvagamahetutvaṃ vaidikatvāt</b> । veda eva hi upāṃśuyājakrame
<q>‘dabdhirnāmāsi’</q> ityanumantraṇamantraḥ paṭyate । tatra sannihitenānvitābhidhānaṃ loke vyutpannamiti
<note>(1) Bh. P. 803 (2) G. dharma</note>
﻿<pb n="r764"/>
sannihitopāṃśuyājadevatayaiva asīti mantragataṃ padaṃ saṃbadhyate । tena yuk‍taṃ sthānasya viśeṣā-
vagamahetutvam । <b>samākhyā punaḥ laukikī ādhvaryavamityādikā । na ca laukika-
mabhidhānaṃ vedārthāvagamaheturbhavati । yathā pacatītyevamādiṣu</b> । asyārthaḥ---laukika-
mabhidhānaṃ vedānanupraviṣṭaṃ na padārthāvagamaheturbhavati yathā pacatītyādiḥ । anyathā pacatītyāderapi
vedārthāṅgabhūtapākavidhāyakatvaṃ syāta iti yataḥ samākhyāyāḥ vedārthāvagamahetutvaṃ nāsti ataḥ
apramāṇatvāt samākhyāyāḥ <b>idamuktaṃ kimetāvantyeva pramāṇātīti । atrocyate---samākhyā-
yā laukikatvepi vaidikasyārthasyāvagamahetutvam</b> । ādhvaryavādisamākhyā tu karmaviśeṣāṇāṃ
kartṛviśeṣāvagamahetutvaṃ pratipadyate । kutaḥ ? <b>abhidhānaṃ hi kṛttaddhitasamāsānāṃ saṃbandhini
prasiddhaṃ vaidikasyārthasya cedamabhidhānaṃ yadyapi svayaṃ</b> laukikam । asyārthaḥ---yathā pacatī-
tyādi laukikamamidhānaṃ na vaidikārthasaṃbaddhaṃ na tathā hautrādisamākhyā vaidikakarmaviṣayatvāt iyaṃ
ca samākhyā taddhitāntā taddhitāntaiścāndhiānaṃ prakṛtyarthasaṃbandhini dṛṣṭam । karmasu ca kartṛviśeṣā-
śravaṇāt kartṛviśeṣāpekṣāyāṃ samākhyayā karmasaṃbandhitvenāvagatā hotrādayaḥ eva kartāro vijñāyante ।
atassamākhyā <b>viśeṣamavagamayati</b> । samākhyāyā buddhisthatvena 1kartṛviśeṣeṇaitāni karmāṇyabhidhīyanta
ityarthaḥ । nanu ca laukikamidamabhidhānaṃ, tacca pramāṇāntarapūrvakaṃ tena pramāṇāntareṇa viśiṣṭapuruṣa-
sabanvamavagamya laukikamabhidhānaṃ prayok‍tavyam । na ca prāk samākhyāyāḥ saṃbandho'vagataḥ iti kathaṃ
samākhyayā niyamaḥ ityatrāha---<b>na cedaṃ smṛtivat pramāṇāntaramapekṣate autpattikatvācchabdārtha-</b>
<note>(1) G. kartṛviśeṣāṇyetāni</note>
﻿<pb n="r765"/>
<b>saṃbandhasya</b> । asyārthaḥ---smṛtau hi vākyaṃ puruṣapraṇītam । tacca vākyaṃ puruṣapraṇītamucyate
yatpuruṣeṇa pramāṇāntareṇārthaṃ pratītya tatpratipādanāya prayujyate । taduk‍taṃ1 <q>“kṛtiścātra
pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭārthapratipādanam । na ca varṇādikāryatā”</q> iti । tena tatra pramāṇāntarāpekṣā ।
iha tvādhvaryavamityādipadaṃ, na ca padaṃ pauruṣeyaṃ anāditvāt । ato'tra na pramāṇāntarāpekṣā ।
<b>tasmād‌yuktaṃ ākhyā caivaṃ tadarthatvāt iti</b> । kuto yuktam---<b>yato viśeṣāvagamahetuḥ</b>
sāmānyataḥ kriyākṣepeṇa kartṛmātre'vagate viśeṣāpekṣāyāṃ samākhyā yasmādviśeṣāvagamahetuḥ,
tasmādviśeṣānvitābhidhānasiddha‍yarthaṃ kartṛviśeṣamupasthāpayatīti samākhyāpi pramāṇamityarthaḥ ।
<b>prayojanamuktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthāna</b> । atra bhāṣyam---kā punarityādi । tadākṣipati
---<b>kā punaratra śrutiḥ kimidaṃ liṅgam । nanu cāyaṃ praś‍no nopapadyate । kimiti nopapadyate ?</b>
yasmāduktāni <b>viniyoge kāraṇānītyuktam</b> । atraiva bhāṣyakāreṇa । <b>na cānirjñātasyo-
ktatā saṃbhavati । tasmādvipratiṣiddhaṃ uktāni viniyoge kāraṇānīti kā punaratra śrutiḥ kiṃ
liṅgamiti ca</b> । uktānīti padaṃ nirjñātatāmāha । kā punaḥ śrutiḥ kiṃ liṅgamiti ca
anirjñātatām । na caikasyārthasya yugapat nirjñānaṃ anirjñānaṃ ca saṃbhavati ।</p>
<note>(1) Bhashya 824</note>
﻿<pb n="r766"/>
<p><b>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ viniyoga eva śrutyādibhiruktaḥ na punaḥ śrutyādīnaṃ svarūpamiti</b>
tenok‍tatā ca praśnaścopapadyate iti yadyapi viniyoga evokto na śrutyādīnāṃ svarūpaṃ, evaṃ
<b>tarhyevameva vak‍tavyaṃ uktaḥ śrutyādibhirviniyoga iti na punarevaṃ</b> vaktavyaṃ uktāmi
<b>viniyoge kāraṇātīti । kiñca viniyogoktyāpi viniyoge kāraṇānyuktānyeva bhavanti</b> ।
kutaḥ ? <b>kāryataḥ kāraṇaparijñānāt</b> viniyogaḥ kāryaṃ śrutyādīni viniyoge kāraṇānīti
kārye cāvagate <b>kāraṇamavagataṃ bhavati</b> । śrutiviniyogo yasya kāryaṃ tata śrutyākhyaṃ pramāṇamiti ।
itarapramāṇebhyaśca śābdasyāyaṃ viśeṣa ityāha<b>arthāvacchedyameva hi śābdaṃ viśeṣato bhavati
svarūpato varṇamātrāvagamāt</b> । idaṃ padaṃ vākyaṃ iti yo'yaṃ vibhāgaḥ sa kāryavibhāga-
nibandhana eva । na cārthāvagamādṛte kāryāt svarūpata eva śābdasya bhedaḥ svarūpato
varṇamātrāvagamāta । tena viniyoge'pyuk‍te kāraṇajñānasyodbhūtatvāt praśno nopapadyate ।
ākṣepāntaraṃ cāha---<b>śrutiliṅgayośca viśeṣamabhidhāya punarvākyapraś‍ne ko'bhiprāya iti na
vidmaḥ</b> । yayoreva hi pramāṇayoryasmin viṣaye balāvalasaṃpradhāraṇā tayoreva svarūpapraśnaḥ tatra
yuktaḥ, nāparasya । <b>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ</b> pṛcchataḥ <b>vākyasvarūpe pṛṣṭe---saṃhatyārthamabhidadhati
padāti vākyaṃ</b> ityuttare uk‍te śrutiliṅgayorvākyādviśeṣānupapattiḥ । ato vākyasya
vākyasya caiṣā saṃpradhāraṇeti codyaṃ kartavyamityevamarthaṃ idaṃ vākyaviṣayaṃ praś‍nottaraṃ praś‍naśca uttaraṃ ca
<note>(1) viniyogoktyāvinaiva praś‍no na ghaṭate</note>
﻿<pb n="r767"/>
praś‍nottaram । tadapi nopapadyate yasmādgārhapatyaśrabaṇaṃ śrutiḥ, indraśabdasyābhidhānasāmarthyaṃ ca
liṅgaṃ, <b>saṃhatyārthamabhidadhati padāni vākyaṃ iti spaṣṭameva trayāṇāṃ parasparamanyatvamupalabhā-
mahe</b> । nanu saṃhatyeti vadan miliṃta padajātaṃ apūrvamarthamabhidhatte itīva grantho dṛśyate । sa
cāyamanupapannaḥ । samudāyasya vācakatvaniṣedhāt । ekaikameva hi padamanvitaṃ svārthamabhidhatta
iti tatra tatroktam । ucyate---abhidadhatīti bahuvacanaprayogāt ekaikaśa eva abhidhāna-
muktam । kintu ekaikenaiva padenānvitaṃ svārthamabhidadhatā yenānvitaṃ tadupasthāpakaṃ padamape-
kṣitam । ato'rthāntaropasthāpakatayā padāntarāpekṣitayā saṃhatyetyuktam । etacca
<b>vākyārthamātṛkāyāṃ</b> tadbhūtādhikaraṇe coktamasmābhiḥ । <b>tasmādandhapadamevedaṃ bhāṣyamiti
granthajñānamānino manyante । atrābhidhīyate । satyamarthāt pramāṇāvagatiḥ tathāpi
tūpapadyata eva praś‍naḥ kā punaratra śrutiriti</b> । atrāyamāśayaḥ---viniyogābhidhānena pramāṇa-
svarūpamapyuk‍taṃ bhavati tadabhiprāyeṇaivedamuk‍taṃ uktāni viniyogekāraṇānīti । na ca svarūpa-
jñāne sati śrutiliṅgapraś‍nasyānavakāśa iti upapadyate praś‍naḥ । <b>kathamupapadyate ?</b> uttaraṃ
---<b>satyaṃ gārhapatyaśravaṇaṃ śrutiḥ satyaṃ cendrābhidhānasāmarthyaṃ liṅgaṃ tathāpi padāntaranirapekṣaṃ
naiva śakyate'vagantum । eendrayā gārhapatya upasthātavya iti</b> śrutiviniyojyatvaṃ,
<b>nāpīndraparatā mantrasya</b> laiṅgikī padāntaranirapekṣā । ataḥ <b>tulye padāntarasavyapekṣatve</b>
﻿<pb n="r768"/>
<b>kāryagamyayoḥ śrutiliṅgayorviśeṣamajānan pṛcchati---kā punaratra śrutiḥ kiṃ liṅgamiti । atha
kimiti adhyāyādau idaṃ na nirṇīta śrutyādīni ca viniyoge kāraṇānītyasmin‍neva bhāṣye
atrocyate---tatrāpyetadutsūtrameva vaktavyam</b> । yadi hi tatredaṃ sūtrok‍taṃ tadā sūtraṃ
vivṛṇvan bhāṣyakāro brūyāt tatrāpyetadutsūtramiti viśeṣābhāvādihaivoktam । <b>iyāṃstvatra
viśeṣaḥ śrutiliṅga ityasya sūtrasya vyākhyātavyatayā aupoddhātikatayā saṃbaddhamabhidhānaṃ
bhavati</b> । jñātasvarūpayorhi bhedāvagame sati balābalavivekasyāvasara iti bhavati svarūpajñānamau-
poddhātikam । <b>kathaṃ punaridānīṃ tulye padāntarasaṃbandhe gārhapatyaśabdasya śrutitocyate</b> ?
yāvatā vākyameva1 dvayamapyetaditi । <b>iyamucyate । padāntarasaṃbandho</b> mantragato viniyoga-
vākyagataśca <b>indrābhidhāne gārhapatyābhidhāne vā'viśiṣṭaḥ । gārhapatyaśravaṇameva tu gārha-
patyābhidhāne vyāpriyate</b> । tenānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ gārhapatyaśravaṇameva gārhapatyābhidhāne
vyāpriyate । <b>nanu dvitīyā vyāptiyata ityuktam</b> । indre'pi hyupastheye gārhapatyaśabdaḥ
saptamyantatayā'nvayaṃ yātyeva । na punardvitīyeti saiva gārhapatyopasthāne karaṇam । <b>satyaṃ
gārhapatyaśravaṇe sati</b> । sāpi na prātipadikārthanirapekṣā gārhapatyaviniyoge prabhavati,
<note>(1) G. vākyenanvayama</note>
﻿<pb n="r769"/>
indre'pi dvitīyārthopapatteḥ । <b>ataḥ padasyaiva darśitaṃ na prātipadikamātrasyeti</b> । dvitīyā
anuktāpyupalakṣyate । dvitīyopādānepi prātipadikamapi iti padameva gārhapatyābhidhāne
vyāpriyate । <b>evamindrābhidhāne</b> indropasthāne viniyogepi <b>mantre padāntaramudāste</b> gārhapatyā-
bhidhānepi tulyatvāt । tasmāt padāntarāṇāmudāsīnatvāt śrutiliṅgayorvākyāt bhedaḥ ।
evaṃ ca sati 1padāntarāpekṣatvena vākyatve saṃbhāvyamāne sati <b>etadvivekajñānāyaiva vākyepi
praś‍nottaramityupapannameva</b> । upasaṃharati---<b>ato'sādhāraṇapratītinimittatayā satyapi
saṃhatyārthābhidhāne śrutirliṅgamiti cocyate</b> । yato bhedaḥ śrutiliṅgayoḥ । <b>tasmādupapannaṃ
śrutiliṅgayorvirodhe kimubhayaṃ viniyojakaṃ uta śrutireveti । prakaraṇapraś‍nābhiprāyaṃ tu
svasthāne</b> prakaraṇapraś‍nasthāne vākyaprakaraṇavirodhādhikaraṇe <b>vakṣyāmaḥ</b> vyākhyāsyāma ityarthaḥ ।
<b>sthānasamākhyayośca</b> praś‍nabhiprāyaṃ <b>vakṣyāma ityanuṣaṅgaḥ । nanu cevaṃ</b> sati śrutiliṅgayo-
rbhede sati saṃpradhāraṇamevaṃ vaktavyaṃ kiṃ śrutirliṅgaṃ <b>cobhayaṃ pramāṇaṃ uta śrutirvalīyasīti</b> । iha
punarbhāṣye <b>śrutiliṅgayoḥ kiṃ balīyasī śrutiḥ āhosvilliṅgamiti na ghaṭate । kutaḥ ?
yasmādidamapi kāraṇaṃ idamapi śrutirapi kāraṇaṃ liṅgamapi</b> kāraṇaṃ iti vakṣyati iti
<note>(1) padārthāpekṣatvena</note>
﻿<pb n="r770"/>
tasmāttadanusāreṇa dvayorapi viniyojakatvaṃ uta śrutereveti saṃśayo yuktaḥ । <b>tasmādyathaiva pūrva-
mupanyastamasmābhiḥ tathaivopanyasanīyam । na tu kiṃ śrutirvalīyasī āhosvilliṅgamiti</b> ।
yadi <b>tulyabale ete kāraṇe iti ca pūrvapakṣahetudarśanāt</b> । tadanurūpeṇa hetumatā ubhaya-
viniyojakatvena bhavitavyam । ākṣipyopasaṃharati---<b>tasmādanyathaivopanyāso'nyathaivopa-
saṃhāra iti</b> । viruddhaṃ <b>phalamapi</b> pūrvapakṣasiddhāntayoḥ <b>evamevopanyastam---kimindrasya
gārhapatyasya copasthānaṃ kartavyaṃ uta gārhapatyasyaiveti । tasmādupakramopasaṃhārayoḥ sāmyaṃ
vaktavyamiti</b> । ākṣepāntaraṃ cāha---<b>yadapi caivaṃ tarhi liṅgavākye virudhyamāne iha
saṃpradhāryete na śrutiliṅge iti tadapyayuk‍tameva । sarvatra samavetaṃ vivik‍taṃ ca dṛśyata
ityuk‍tatvāt vivekasya</b> । ākṣepāntaramāha---<b>yā tvatra śrutiḥ sā liṅgena virudhyate ।
vākyaṃ punaḥ lakṣaṇayāpyupapadyata evetyuktvā athaveti punaḥ śrutyantaropanyāsaḥ kimaparito-
ghāt uta vikalpārtha iti etadapi na jñāyate</b> । pūrvaṃ gārhapatyaśravaṇaṃ śrutimuktvā athaveti
dvitīyāśrutiṃ darśayati । tatra kimaparitoṣeṇedamucyate atha vā pakṣāntaravibhaveneti na jñāyate ।
<note>(1) G. dvitīyāṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r771"/>
ucyate---<b>yastāvadayamupanyāsaḥ</b> kiṃ balīyasī śrutiḥ <b>āhosvilliṅgamiti tatrāyamabhiprāyaḥ</b>
kiṃ liṅgopamardanenaiva śrutiḥ <b>yathā pramāṇaṃ tathā</b> liṅgamapi śrutyupamardanenaiva pramāṇamiti ।
<b>yadā cobhayaṃ ubhayopamardanenaiva pramāṇaṃ tadopapadyata evāyamupanyāsaḥ kiṃ śrutirbalīyasī
āhosvilliṅgamiti</b> । kathamupapadyata ityāha---<b>etaduk‍taṃ bhavati na vidmaḥ kiṃ balīya iti</b> ।
tenāyaṃ bhāṣyārthaḥ---kiṃ liṅgāt śrutireva balīyasī āhosvicchrutistāvadbalīyasyeva । evaṃ
liṅgamapi śruterbalīya iti । <b>tasmādubhayaṃ pramāṇam । ubhayaprāmāṇye ca ubhayo-
rabhidhānam । ata eva cāniyama ityuktam । yadi tulyabale ete kāraṇe iti ca
viśeṣāgrahaṇā</b>duktamityanuṣaṅgaḥ । bhāṣyamanubhāṣyākṣipati---<b>tato vikalpa iti । ko'yaṃ
vikalpaḥ । nanu cāsmin pakṣe samuccaya eva</b> indre ca gārhapatye ca viniyogānmantrasya ।
samarthayate---<b>abhidhānavikalpamaṅgīkṛtyaitaduk‍taṃ na prayogavikalpam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadā
gārhapatyābhidhānāya prayujyate tadā mantreṇendro nābhidhīyate । yadā indropasthānāya na tadā
gārhapatyasya ityabhidhānasya vyavasthito vikalpaḥ । mantraprayogasya tu agnau indre ca samuccaya
<note>(1) Bh. P. 824</note>
﻿<pb n="r772"/>
eva śeṣibhedena pratipradhānaṃ guṇāvṛtteriti । <b><q>‘yadi tu liṅgaṃ balīya’</q> ityetadapi bhāṣyaṃ
upanyāsavat draṣṭavyam</b> । balīyastvaṃ ca śrutivat svaviṣaye nirapekṣaviniyojakatvam ।
uk‍te'pi śrutiliṅge vākyānāṃ vivekaḥ । <b>evaṃ tarhīti punaḥ</b> praś‍no na <b>kevalāt gārhapatya-
śravaṇāt tadupasthānāvagatiḥ</b> padamātrasyāvācakatvāt । <b>tāvanmātrasya śrutitvamupadarśitam</b>
taccāvācakam । yacca vācakaṃ tadvākyamiti । evaṃ codite <b>tadidānīṃ rāddhāntavādyabhiprāyaṃ
vivṛṇotīti vadan</b> pūrvoktavivaraṇametaditi darśayati---<b>satyaṃ vākyādṛte</b> nāyamavagamaḥ
gārhapatyaśravaṇāt tadupasthānāvagatiriti । etacca yā tvatra <b>śrutirityanena granthenoktam
indrābhidhānepi tulyatvāt</b> padāntarāṇām । kathaṃ tulvatvaṃ ? <b>balīyasyapi hi liṅge</b>
indrepyupastheye <b>aindrayopatiṣṭhata iti etat gārhapatyaśabdena sahaikavākyatāmabhyupetyaiva
yadi hi nopoyāt tadā liṅgena vākyaṃ</b> virudhyeta vākyaliṅgavirodha eveha bhavet na
śrutiliṅgavirodhaḥ । iha gārhapatyaśravaṇādanantaraṃ yo'rthaḥ pratīyate'gniviśeṣātmakaḥ sa liṅgena
viruddha‍yate । ataḥ <b>śrutiliṅgayorevāyaṃ virodhaḥ । 1atha vā nātraikavākyatvāditi</b>
<note>(1) G. kathaṃ vā</note>
﻿<pb n="r773"/>
<b>pakṣāntaropanyāsaḥ sakalapadapradarśanārtha iti vyākhyātam</b> । nāparitoṣeṇa nāpi pakṣāntara---
tayā śrutyantaropanyāsaḥ । kintu pūrvaṃ kevalaṃ prātipadikamuk‍taṃ, adhunā vibhaktisahitam ।
vibhaktisahitasya ca viniyojakatvamiti darśitaṃ prāk । <b>kiṃ punaratra yuktaṃ ? ubhayatra
svārthāvagamāt</b> । vivṛṇoti---<b>liṅgādapi liṅgārthaḥ</b> indropasthānātmako'vagamyate । <b>śrute-
rapi śrutyartho</b> gārhapatyopasthānātmako'vagamyate । <b>vākyasya caudāsīnyāt ubhayatrābhidhāna-
meva2</b> padamātramevobhayatra mantre viniyojake <b>ca viruddha‍yate । na cābhidhāne kaścidviśe-
ṣo'vagamyate ityatastulyabale ete kāraṇe ityuktam</b> । evaṃ cātra pūrvapakṣakaraṇe <q>‘vacanāttva
yathārthaṃ’</q> ityanena saha spaṣṭamapaunaruktyam । tatra hi pūrvapakṣe liṅgasyaiva viniyojakatvamuktvā
siddhānte śrutistāvadviniyok‍tuṃ śak‍notītyuktam । ihedānīṃ śruteḥ sthite viniyojakatve
liṅgasyāpi viniyojakatvamāśaṅkyata ityuktam । atra bhāṣyaṃ---<q>“nanu liṅgasya bhaṅgurasyeva rūpaṃ
savicikitso hi liṅgāt pratyaya”</q> iti । tadākṣipati---<b>keyaṃ vicikitsā nāma ?</b> uttaraṃ
---<b>asamyak‌pratyayaḥ</b> । kimatrāsamyaktvaṃ ? <b>uttaraṃ---nahīndrābhidhānāt indro'bhidhātavya
iti pratyayo bhavati</b> । na hi śaktimātreṇa idamanena kāryamiti kartavyatājñānaṃ bhavati ।
<b>bhavati tu gārhapatyaśravaṇāt</b> anena gārhapatya upastheya iti kartavyatājñānaṃ <b>vidhāyakavākya-
gatatvāt gārhapatyaśabdasya । nanu cāvidhāyakatvālliṅgasya prāmāṇyameva nāsti kathaṃ</b>
<note>(1) Bhashya 842</note> <note>(2) G. adds evameva</note>
﻿<pb n="r774"/>
<b>virodhaḥ</b> । nāpramāṇena pramāṇasya virodha ityarthaḥ । pariharati---<b>satyaṃ, abhidhānasāmarthyamātraṃ</b>
naiva <b>pramāṇaṃ itikartavyatāvagame sati anyato viśeṣāvagame2 pramāṇam</b> । kaiḥ kartavyatā-
vagamaḥ ? prakaraṇādibhiḥ sāmānyenātropakartavyamityavagate kiṃ kurvateti viśeṣākāṅkṣāyāṃ
yacchak‍noti kartuṃ tatkurvateti viśeṣakārye liṅgaṃ viniyojakaṃ bhavatyeva । <b>3kartavyatāvagame
cābhidhānamātramavaśiṣyata</b> ityuk‍taṃ bhāṣye । tadidaṃ liṅgakramādhikaraṇe sanyāsikīkṛtaṃ
prakaṭīkṛtam । pūrvapakṣamupasaṃharati---<b>tasmāt tulyabale ete kāraṇe iti</b> । atrāparaṃ bhāṣyaṃ
<q>“balīyānapi hetuḥ”</q> iti tadva‍yācaṣṭe---<b>na ca tāvat balīyān</b> । uk‍tena nyāyena śrutiliṅgayo-
stulyabalatvāt । <b>anvāruhyāpi na virodho'stīti manyate</b> । <q>“nanu cāyameva virodhaḥ
sakṛdupasthānaṃ coditaṃ asakṛdabhinirdhartyata iti । naivam । upastheyabhedāt pratipradhāna-
mā/?/bartante guṇā iti nyāya evaiṣaḥ na virodhaḥ”</q> iti bhāṣyamanubhāṣya ākṣipati---<b>nanu cedama-
virodhottaraṃ na ghaṭate na hyatropastheyadvayaṃ śrūyate । gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti gārhapatya evaikaḥ
upastheyaḥ śrūyate nendro'pi</b> । na liṅgāt kartavyatāvagamo'stīti । <b>tasmādanuttaramidaṃ</b>
bhāṣyam ।</p>
<note>(1) Bh, P. 844</note> <note>(2) G. vagamaḥ</note> <note>(3) G. kartavyanavagame</note>
﻿<pb n="r775"/>
<p>ucyate---<b>prakaraṇāt kartavyatāvagamāt । indrapadādapīndrābhidhānaṃ pratīyata</b>
iti prakaraṇasavyapekṣālliṅgādapi kartavyatāvagamaḥ iti <b>manvānena 1upastheyamedādityuktam ।
vākyasāmānyādvā</b> । asyārthaḥ---viniyojake'pi padamātrameva gārhapatyaṃ iti viniyojakaṃ
padāntarāṇāmudāsīnatvāt mantre'pi indrapadamaviśiṣṭamiti tadapi viniyojakaṃ saṃbhavati
<b>vākyasāmānyāt</b> sādhāraṇyāt; ubhayatrāpi tulyatvādityuk‍taṃ prāgeva । <b>evaṃ tarhi gauṇa-
mukhyatā noṣapadyata iti punarvirodhopanyāsaḥ । nanu ca pratipradhānaṃ guṇāvṛttau satyāṃ
naivāyaṃ virodho ghaṭate</b> । asyārthaḥ---pramāṇadvayenobhayatra virodhāt pratipradhānaṃ guṇānāmāvṛtteḥ
dvirayaṃ mantraḥ prayok‍tavyaḥ । tatraikasmin prayoge mukhyatā anyasmiṃśca gauṇateti na virodhaḥ ।
yadi hyekasmin prayoge gauṇamukhyārthatocyate tato virodho bhavediti । pariharati---<b>avini-
yuktamantrāpekṣo'yaṃ virodhaḥ</b> । aviniyukto yo mantraḥ tadapekṣo'yaṃ gauṇamukhyārthatāpatyā
virodhaḥ । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---svādhyāyakāle yasya mantrasyaikaḥ prayogaḥ sa gauṇamukhyārthoṃ na yukta
iti । kathaṃ tarhi na virodha ityatrāha---<b>viniyoge tu avirodhaḥ</b> । pradhānabhedena vini-
yogabhedāt । tadbhede ca pratipradhānaṃ prayogabhedādavirodha iti <b>siddho'tra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b>
rāddhāntamupakramate---<b>atrocyate śrutiliṅgayoḥ śrutirbalīyasī । kutaḥ arthaviprakarṣāt ।
kimidaṃ arthaviprakarṣāditi । arthasya viprakarṣo'rthaviprakarṣaḥ । kaḥ punararthaḥ śrutyarthaḥ</b>
<note>(1) G. indropastheya</note>
﻿<pb n="r776"/>
anenedaṃ kartavyamityevaṃrūpaḥ । <b>atra gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti sannikṛṣṭaḥ śrutyarthaḥ</b> pramā-
ṇāntarānapekṣatvācchruteḥ <b>indra upastheya iti viprakṛṣṭaḥ</b> । kathaṃ ? uttaraṃ---<q>“kadācana
starīrasi”</q> iti mantreṇendra upastheya iti na śrūyate satyapīndrābhidhānasāmarthye vacanābhāvāt ।
anupasthānīya indra ityavagamyate” iti bhāṣyamanubhāṣyākṣipati---<b>nanu ca pūrvamevoktaṃ satyāṃ</b>
kartavyatāyāṃ indro'bhidhīyate yena liṅgena sāmarthyalakṣaṇena <b>tadindrābhidhānaṃ pramāṇam ।
tataścobhayoḥ indragārhapatyayorabhidhāne syāt‍tulyataiva । ato dvayoḥ</b> śrutiliṅgayoḥ
<b>prāmāṇyamiti</b> । kimidaṃ punarākṣiptam ? liṅgaprāmāṇyaṃ <b>samāhitaṃ ca</b> samarthanamucyate
<q>“dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ syāta iti yadetat prakaraṇaṃ liṅgaṃ ca ubhayametada-
śābdam । na cātikrāntapratyakṣaviṣaya(eva) evaṃlakṣaṇake'rthe śabdamantareṇa paricchedo'va-
kalpate । ato manyāmahe viprakṛṣṭa śrutyarthālliṅgamiti”</q> <b>ucyate</b>---anena bhāṣyeṇa <b>aśābda-
metaditi 1viśeṣaṃ pradarśayituṃ</b> punarākṣip‍taṃ liṅgasya prāmāṇyaṃ samāhitaṃ ca । ucyate---
śabdaśca pūrvatra yojyaḥ । <b>nanu caivaṃ sati aśābdatve liṅgasya prāmāṇyameva hīyate</b> ।
<note>(1) G. viśeṣaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r777"/>
<b>kuto virodhaḥ ?</b> prāmāṇye hi virodho bhavati viruddhārthopasthāpakatvāt । <b>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ
asati virodhe</b> śrutyā <b>smṛtivat liṅgasya prāmāṇyaṃ</b> yathā śrutyavirodhaviṣaye smṛteḥ prāmāṇyaṃ
tathā liṅgasyāpi iti । <b>tadayuktam । kutaḥ ? smṛterhyarthamavagamya 1virodhādviparyayaḥ</b>
kalpyate auduṃbarī sarvā veṣṭayitavyeti sarvaveṣṭanaṃ smṛteravagamya śrutivirodhādarthasya viparyayaḥ
kalpyate । <b>iha punarupasthānaṃ naivāvagamyata ityuktam । kathamanavagamyamāne'rthe'numānaṃ</b>
saṃbhāvyate <b>tasmāt durgṛhītastenasaṃbhāṣitavadasaṃbandhaṃ pratibhāti</b> । durgṛhītaṃ durācaritaṃ
yena stenena tadbhāṣitavat asaṃbaddhamidaṃ bhāṣyamityarthaḥ । <b>punarapi</b> bhāṣyakāraḥ <b>prakaraṇā-
vagatakartavyatāpekṣālliṅgādevārthāvagartiṃ darśayati---śrutisaṃbhave ca avagativākyasādhāra-
ṇye sati kathamayaṃ viśeṣa iti vak‍tavyam</b> । vākyasya śrutau liṅge ca sādhāraṇyenodāsī-
natvāt dvayorapyavagatiryuk‍teti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>atrābhidhīyate---kartavyasyetikartavyatākāṅkṣasya vacanaṃ prakaraṇasiti</b> prakaraṇasya
lakṣaṇam । tena <b>caidamarthyalakṣaṇaḥ</b> karaṇaidamarthyalakṣaṇa <b>eva saṃbandhaḥ</b> prakaraṇena pratīyate,
<b>na punaranvita/?/padārthalakṣaṇaḥ</b> anvitāḥ padārthā lakṣaṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ yasya padārthānvayalakṣaṇasya sa
prakaraṇānnāvagamyata <b>ityuk‍taṃ</b> prakaraṇādhikaraṇe । <b>tataḥ kiṃ ?</b> idaṃ tataḥ । <b>anvitapadārtha-</b>
<note>(1) G. viparyayavirodhaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r778"/>
<b>lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ padārthebhya evāvasīyate । aidamarthyalakṣaṇastu kevalaṃ kāryata eva na
padārthānvaye1-2 vyāpāro'vagamyate</b> kāryasya । prakaraṇasya kāryato hi karaṇaidamarthyamevā-
vagamyate । na padārthānvayaḥ kāryamevetikartavyatākāṅkṣaṃ prakaraṇam । tena prakaraṇāta
kevalakaraṇaidamarthyāvagamāt padārthānvayo nāvagamyate । <b>evamapi ko viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti
viśeṣaḥ padārthānvitalakṣaṇaḥ</b> । kevalasaṃbandhe padārthairanvito yo vākyārthaḥ saḥ lakṣaṇaṃ yasya
padārthānvayarūpasaṃbandhasya <b>tasmin sati paścāt kāryayogaḥ</b> kāryeṇa sahetikartavyatālakṣaṇaḥ
saṃbandhaḥ <b>padārthānvayalakṣaṇastu prathamata eva</b> । kārye tu prakaraṇarūpe sati paścāt padārthānvayaḥ
sāmarthyarūpaliṅgabaleneti <b>so'yamarthaviprakarṣaḥ</b> । śrutau prathamaṃ padārthānvayaḥ liṅge tu paścāditi ।
bhavatu padārthānvayaviprakarṣo liṅgasya tathāpi kathaṃ śruterbalīyastvaṃ ityatrāha-<b>anvayapradarśanārthaṃ ca
tārtīyaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ śeṣaśeṣivido manyante</b> । tathāpi kimityatrāha---<b>sa cāyamanvayaḥ</b> śrutau
<b>prathamataramavagamyate</b> । tāvataiva grāhakasya mantrasamāmnānasya ca kṛtārthatvāt । <b>na kāryataḥ
pāścātyāyāṃ padārthānvayāvagatau pramāṇamasti । kutaḥ ? na hi anvitasyānvayo dṛśyate
yataḥ</b> । tasmād‍yuk‍taṃ liṅgācchrutibalīyasīti । atrādhikaraṇe bhāṣye <b>ānumānikābhidhānaṃ
ca padārthānvayāpekṣam</b> । padārthānvayo hi prakaraṇaliṅgābhyāṃ pāścātya iti pāścātyātma-
<note>(1) padārthānvaya</note> <note>(2) padārthebhyaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r779"/>
katvāt anumāna ivānumānika ityucyate । aśābdaṃ cocyate sākṣādanvitapadārthalakṣaṇātvā-
bhāvāt । nanu samuccayenātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ kathaṃ vikalpasya cānyāyyatvāt iti rāddhānte'bhidhī-
yate ityatrāha---<b>vikalpasya cānyāyyatvāditi mantravākyāpekṣam</b> । etadeva vivṛṇoti
---<b>nindraśabdasyābhidhānadvayaṃ nyāyyamityabhiprāyaḥ</b> । indraśabdo hi kadācidnārhapatya-
mabhidhatte kadāciccendramiti na nyāyyamiti । <b>ato</b> vikalpasyānyāyyatvāt <b>viniyuktasyaiva
mantrasya viniyogo na ghaṭata iti darśito hetuḥ</b> vikalpasyānyāyyatvalakṣaṇaḥ । <b>yaduktaṃ
avirodha iti</b> pūrvapakṣānubhāṣaṇam । so'yaṃ virodho yaduta <b>indraśabdasya mantravākyā-
pekṣayā'bhidhānadvayaṃ nopapadyata iti</b> । sakṛduccaritaṃ mantravākyam tena caika evārtho-
'bhidhātavyaḥ na punararthadvayaṃ sakṛduccaritasyānekārthatbānupapatteḥ । nanu ca viniyogadvayena
prayogadvayānna virodhaḥ ityatrāha---<b>aidamarthyasya ca anvayalabhyatvāt śrutāvuparataiva kartavyatā-
pekṣeti nākāṅkṣādvayamupapadyata iti virodhaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---śrutau padārthānvayāt prathamamavagatāt
karaṇaidamarthyasya labhyatvāt prathamamavagatena śrautena kāryaviśeṣeṇa uparataiva kāryaviśeṣāpekṣeti
nākāṅkṣādvayamupapadyata iti ubhayatrāpi viniyogāt asti mantravākyāpekṣayā virodhaḥ । yadidaṃ
śrautādviniyogāt prāk kāryāpekṣitvaṃ mantrasya grāhakagrahaṇasya <b>ca tadidamakṛtasāmarthyatvaṃ
mantravākyasya viniyogasya coktam vākyaprakaraṇaśabdābhyāṃ</b> bhāṣyagatābhyām । vākya-
śabdena mantravākyāmucyate । prakaraṇaśabdena grāhakaniyoga ityarthaḥ । kṛtaṃ sāmarthyaṃ yayo-
<note>(1) Bh. P. 846</note>
﻿<pb n="r780"/>
stau kṛtasāmarthyau mantraniyogau na kṛtasāmarthyau akṛtasāmarthyau tayorbhāvastattvam । <b>ataḥ
upapanno'rthaviprakaṣaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p>atra cedaṃ pūrvottarapakṣasāram---śrutyā tāvadaindro mantro gārhapatyopasthāne viniyujyate ।
tathā prakaraṇāpādite kāryamātre viśeṣakāryaniyāmakatayā labdhapramāṇabhāvena liṅgenāpi indropasthāne
viniyujyate । na ca virodhaḥ, viniyogadvayabalena prayogadvayādubhayatrābhidhānopapatteriti
<b>pūrvapakṣaḥ</b> । rāddhāntastu adhikāraniyogasannidhau paṭhitasya mantrasya grāhakeṇa gṛhītasya śrutyā
prathamamevāvagataśeṣabhāvasya paścādupādānenāvagatakaraṇaidamarthyasya kāryāntarākāṅkṣābhāvāt viniyo-
gānupapatteḥ na liṅgenāpi viniyogo yuktaḥ । na ca śrautaliṅgaviniyogayostulyakālatā ।
grāhakagrahaṇe sati śīghratvāt śrutiviniyogasya । prakaraṇaviniyogāpekṣitvācca liṅgaviniyoga-
syeti ।</p>
<p><b>liṅgavākyayorvirodhe kimudāharaṇam ? <q>“syonaṃ tte sadanaṃ karomi dhṛtasya
dhārayā suśevaṃ kalpayāmi । tasmin sīdāmṛte pratitiṣṭha । vrīhīṇāṃ medha sumanasmamānaḥ”</q></b>
ityanena bhāṣyamanubhāṣitamākṣep‍tum । <b>nanu cārthaviprakarṣādityukto hetuḥ sāpekṣanirapekṣatvaṃ
ca liṅgavākyayoḥ</b> । tathā---hi liṅgaṃ vākyanirapekṣaṃ sadanakaraṇe puroḍāśapratiṣṭhāpane ca
vibhajya mantraṃ viniyok‍tuṃ kṣamate । vākyaṃ tu liṅgaviniyogāpekṣaṃ viniyok‍tuṃ kṣamate viniyo-
jakena liṅgena hi ekasmin bhāge viniyuk‍te vākyenāparasyāpi bhāgasya tadanupraveśitā
kalpyate ।</p>
<note>(1) Bh. P. 847</note>
﻿<pb n="r781"/>
<p><b>ataḥ prakaṭa evārthaviprakarṣaḥ । kimityadhikaraṇāntaramārabhyate ? na kevala-
midamevādhikaraṇam । sarvādhikaraṇākṣepa evāyam</b> 1sujñāno hyarthaviprakarṣaḥ sarvatra ।
<b>kathaṃ ? liṅgaṃ tāvduktaṃ nirapekṣatvāditi vākyamapi padārthānvayāvagamyasaṃbandhaṃ aidamarthya-
lakṣaṇāt</b> prakaraṇasaṃbandhāt <b>balīya ityuktam</b> । anvitapadārthāvagamyo hi vākyārthānvayaḥ
vākyārthayoḥ prakaraṇena karaṇaidamarthyalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pratīyate, na padārthānvayalakṣaṇaḥ । tena
padārthānvayalakṣaṇasaṃbandhe prakaraṇaṃ liṅgamapekṣata iti darśitaṃ śrutiliṅgavicāre । <b>prakaraṇamapi
tadapekṣatvāt kramasya kramādvalīyaḥ</b> prakaraṇena hi sāmānyasaṃbandhe siddhe krameṇa viśeṣa-
karaṇasaṃbandhaḥ । <b>kramo'pi viśeṣakaraṇasaṃbandhakṛttayā vedāvagamyatvācca samākhyāyā
balīyāneva</b> । sannivānaṃ hi anvitābhidhānavyutpatau upādhitvena svīkṛtaṃ saṃbandhakāraṇam ।
tadā vedādeva avagamyata iti śīghraṃ saṃbandhaṃ pratipādayatīti samākhyātī balīyān ।
<b>ato nārabhbhaṇīyānyetānyadhikaraṇāni ityarthaviprakarṣajñānābhimānino manyante ।
atrocyate---yattāvaduktaṃ nirapekṣatvālliṅgaṃ balīya iti</b> । tadayuktam । kasmāt ?
<b>sakalasya hi mantrasya kartavyatāvagamānna kevalāt padāt kartavyatāvagamo bhavati</b> ।
<note>(1) G. hyanyatra</note>
﻿<pb n="r782"/>
ayamāśayaḥ---yāvanti hiṃ padāni prayujyante tāvanti saṃbhūyaikamarthaṃ pratipādayanti । śak‍nuvanti
caitānyekamarthaṃ pratipādayiṃtu iti prathamamekavākyatā avasīyate । tathābhūtasya paścālliṅgena
viniyoga iti । akṣarārthastu sakalamantravākyasya kartavyatāvagamāt anuṣṭhānāvagamakatvātṃ
na kevalāt padāt anuṣṭhānāvagamaḥ । <b>ato vākyameva prathamataraṃ padānāṃ parasparasaṃbandhā-
vagamahetuḥ</b> । ekavākyārthapratipādakatayā । saṃbandhasya ca padajātasya paścālliṅgāt
<b>kāryāvagatiḥ । tasmāt vākyameva balīya iti bhavati matiḥ । avaśyaṃ caitadevaṃ</b>
padānāṃ svata eva prathamataramekārthapratipādakatayā saṃbandha <b>ityabhyupagamanīyam । anyathā hi
2avirodhisyonādipadāntarasaṃbandho'pi na syāt</b> । ekameva sadanapadaṃ viniyujyeta ।
kutaḥ ? <b>viniyoge padāntaranirapekṣatvālliṅgasya । ato durjñāno'yaṃ vākyaliṅgayo-
rviprakaṣa iti prārabdhamidamadhikaraṇam</b> । nanu bhāṣye pūrvapakṣavādī vākyena kṛts‍nasya
mantrasya viniyoga ityāha, na punarliṅgeneti tatrāha---<b>ayameva ca pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ
padāntarasaṃbandhasavyapekṣaṃ liṅgaṃ viniyojakamiti</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadetat pūrvapakṣavādinā
vākyasya viniyojakatvamuktaṃ na talliṅganirapekṣam । kintu liṅgameva viniyojakam । tat‍tu
parasparasaṃbaddhasya padajātasyeti । <b>ubhayatra sadanakaraṇe puroḍāśapratiṣṭhāpane ca kṛts‍na---
mantrasya viniyogaḥ । yatpunaridamuktaṃ</b> bhāṣyakāreṇa <b>liṅgasya śrutyāpi bādhitatvāditi
ko'yaṃ vākyena liṅgasya bādhahetuḥ । na hi śrutyā bādhitasyānyenāpi bādhyatā yuktā</b> ।
<note>(1) Bhasya P. 849</note> <note>(2) G. svavirodhi</note>
﻿<pb n="r783"/>
<b>tasmāt bāliśalikhitamevedaṃ pratibhāti । nedaṃ vāliśalikhitam । anyo'bhiprāścoda-
kasya । yathaiva śrutyā padārthānvayasaṃbandhajñānakāraṇatvena liṅgaṃ bādhitaṃ kāryaikyaviniyojya-
tvāt evaṃ vākyenāpi</b> itikartavyatākāṅkṣakāryaikyaviniyojyatvānmantrasyetyarthaḥ iti pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---<b>yajuṣastāvadviniyogaḥ pratipadam ।</b> asyārthaḥ---praśliṣṭa-
paripaṭhitānāṃ yajuṣāmavacchedo nānyataḥ । yāvadekārthaṃ varṇajātaṃ tāvadekaṃ padam । arthāvaga-
mastu viniyogataḥ । viniyogaścānuṣṭhānaprakāśakatayā tadyenānuṣṭhānaṃ prakāśyate tasya viniyogaḥ ।
ekena ca padenānuṣṭhānaṃ prakāśyate iti tāvanmāvasya viniyogaḥ । athānvitābhidhāyitayā padānāṃ
dvitīyapadāpekṣatvaṃ tathāpi dvayorastu viniyogaḥ । kathaṃ tarhyavirodhipadāntarāṇāmanupraveśaḥ
tatrāha---<b>kāryataḥ punaḥ aikyaṃ padānāṃ yāvadekaṃ kārye tāvadaviruddhaḥ padāntarasaṃbandhaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---padāntarāṇyapi prakaraṇādhītāni kena dvāreṇānupraviśantītyapekṣāyāṃ yāvatāmanvayavatā-
mekārthānvayitvaṃ pratīyate tāvanti 1liṅgavirodhena praviśanti । liṅgāvagate <b>kāryāntare tu
pratyarthini na kāryāntarasaṃbandhitā śakyate pratipat‍tum</b> । na hi svata eva kāryalābhe
paropajīvitvaṃ yuktam । kutaḥ svataḥ kāryalābha ityatrāha---<b>pratipadaṃ</b> yajuṣāṃ <b>vidhānādeva</b> ।
kasmātpunaḥ pratipadaṃ yajuṣāṃ vidhānaṃ ityatrāha---<b>atra hi kāryato mantratvam</b> । kāryamapekṣya
mantravibhāgaḥ । <b>na mantrataḥ kāryam</b> । kāryātprāgekamantratve avagate na paścāt kāryam ।
<note>(1) G. liṅgetā vi</note>
﻿<pb n="r784"/>
kāryātprāgekamantratve pramāṇābhāvāt <b>yathā ṛkṣu sāmasu ceti</b> viparītayojanā । anyata eva
ṛcāṃ sāmnāṃ ca parimāṇajñānāt । <b>ataḥ kāryanirapekṣāṃ kevalapadārthānvayasaṃbandhitāṃ
vākyanibandhinīṃ bādhate liṅgam</b> । kāryaśūnyā yā kevalena padārthānvayena padānāṃ paraspara---
saṃbandhitā vākyanibandhinī tāṃ liṅgaṃ bāghata ityarthaḥ । <b>nanu ca śrutāvapi ainda‌‍yā</b> gārhapatya-
mupatiṣṭhata ityatrāpyevameva prāpnoti । vibhajyaivendrasya padasya indropasthāne viniyogaḥ prāpnoti ।
pariharati---<b>satyaṃ prāpnoti yadīdaṃ yajuḥ syāt tat‍tu śrutiviniyojyatvamṛkṣu darśitam ।
ṛcāṃ ca mantrataḥ kāryaṃ</b>, chandovanmantropasthāpanāvaśenāvagatānāmevarcāṃ viniyogena kārya-
mityuk‍taṃ arthaikatvādityatra । <b>yajuṣāṃ punaḥ yatrāpi iṣetveti viniyogaḥ tatrāpyupādānava-
śāt vicchedaḥ</b> । yāvadeva kāryeṇopādīyate tāvadevaikaṃ yajurityupādānādvicchedaḥ । <b>na punaḥ
kāryopādānābhyāmanyo</b> yajuṣṭve heturasti । kāryapadasya tāvat kāryata evānupraveśaḥ
tadekavākyatayā'nyeṣāṃ kāryaśūnyānāṃ upādānata iti tasmād‌yukto vākyabhedaḥ kāryabhedāt ।</p>
<p><b>yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa darśitaṃ---nanu caikavākyatvepi liṅgaṃ vyāpriyata iti
tadayuktamiva pratibhāti । kimiti</b> ? । uttaraṃ---<b>kāryato'trārthanirṇayaḥ । kutaḥ</b> ? tena
<note>(1) Bhashya P. 824</note>
﻿<pb n="r785"/>
kāryabhedāt dvāvarthau na sāmarthyamātrādarthanirṇayaḥ yena svasāmarthyavaśenaikārthatvaṃ syāt ।
<b>kāryasavyapekṣaṃ hi sāmarthyaṃ liṅgamiti nirūpitam</b> । na kāryanirapekṣam । <b>yadapi ca parihṛtaṃ
arthaviprakarṣo hyatra bādhyatve hetuḥ asti caikavākyabhūtasya liṅgasyābhidhānāt liṅgādviprakarṣa
iti । tadayuktamiva । ekavākyatāhetorliṅgasyāliṅgatvādityuktam</b> । kāryaśūnyaṃ hi
na liṅgam । aliṅgasya ca bādhacintā'nupapannā । atrocyate । <b>pratipadaṃ viniyogāt
ekavākyatayāpi ca kāryopapatteḥ yuktā liṅgatāśaṅkā</b> । ekavākyatvepi nātīva kāryaśūnyatā
kāryaviśeṣaṇatvena syonādipadānāmiva kāryalābhāditi yuktā liṅgatāśaṅkā । <b>parihāraśca</b>
yuktaḥ <b>arthaviprakarṣāt</b> yasmālliṅgādapi liṅgaṃ balīyaḥ । <b>tasmānnātra śrutirliṅgaṃ vākyamiti
tantramekā</b>ntato vivakṣitam । kintu viprakṛṣṭaṃ śrutyarthāt padārthānvayāt yattada<b>prāpakaṃ</b>
aviniyojakamiti sūtrārthaḥ । <b>ataḥ siddhaṃ kāryabhedāt vākyabhedaḥ</b> । yadi vākyabhedaḥ
<b>tarhi tasmin sīda iti sarvanāma kimālambanam ?</b> uttaraṃ---<b>pūrvaprakṛtālambanamiti brūmaḥ</b> ।
pūrvavākye yatprakṛtaṃ tadeva tacchabdenocyata ityarthaḥ । <b>nanu caivaṃ sati parārthataiva pūrvasya
prāpnoti tataśca vākyaṃ balīya ityuktaṃ bhavati</b> । pariharati---<b>nāvaśyaṃ parāmarśe tādarthyameva</b>
﻿<pb n="r786"/>
<b>bhavati । yasmādanyārthamapyanyārthenāvamṛśyata eva sarvanāmnā ityadoṣaḥ</b> । yathā svatantraḥ
kartetyetat <b>tatprayojako hetuśceti</b> tacchabdenāvamṛśyate, <b>yathā vedepi <q>‘etasyaiva revatīṣu’</q>
iti tasmādvalīyo'bhidhānaṃ liṅgamiti siddham । atha vākyaprakaraṇayoḥ kathamiti</b>
adhikaraṇasūcanam । atra bhāṣyaṃ <b>rki punaḥ prakaraṇaṃ nāmeti</b> tadākṣipati---<b>ko'yaṃ praśnaḥ</b>
nāyaṃ praś‍na upapadyata ityarthaḥ । kathaṃ ? itikartavyatārthitayā viniyogaḥ prakaraṇamityuktam ।
viniyujyate yena sa viniyogaḥ itikartavyatārthitayā yena viniyujyate tatprakaraṇamityuktam
prakaraṇāditi<b>kartavyatārthitvādityevaṃ nirjñāte prakaraṇe sati</b> [<b>na vidmaḥ kimartho'yaṃ praśna
iti</b> । samarthayate---<b>atrocyate---itikartavyatārthitvādityuk‍taṃ, na vidmaḥ kasyeyamiti-
kartavyatārthiteti । yasyeyamitikartavyatākāṅkṣā tadatrocyate kartavyasyeti niyogārtha-
syetyarthaḥ</b> । atra kartavyasya tritayākāṅkṣasya kiṃ kena kathamiti niyojyaviśeṣaṇa<b>karaṇeti
kartavyatākāṅkṣasya yeyaṃ tṛtīyākāṅkṣā</b> kathamityevaṃrūpā <b>tatprakaraṇaṃ tena viniyogaḥ</b>
prayājādīnām <b>tadviniyoge kāraṇaṃ na kartavyatāmātram</b> itikartavyatākāṅkṣārahitaṃ nāpyanyat
<b>tasmādupapannaḥ praśnārthaḥ</b> । ākāṅkṣitaviśeṣājñānena itikartavyatārthitvalakṣaṇaprakaraṇasvarūpa-
syaivājñānāt । <b>uttaraṃ</b> copapannam । etacca pūrvapakṣaupayikaṃ pṛṣṭam । viniyogākāṅkṣā-
<note>(1) Bh. P. 851</note>
﻿<pb n="r787"/>
prakaraṇamityuttare datte pūrvapakṣalābho bhaviṣyatīti । bhāṣyārthastu--- <q>“kartavyasya vidhyarthasya iti-
kartavyatākāṅkṣasya yadvacanaṃ pratipādanaṃ tatprakaraṇam”</q> । kathaṃ tatprakaraṇaṃ ityapekṣite satyāha
---<q>“prārambho hi saḥ tasya kartavyasya vacanakriyāyāḥ”</q> pratipādanakriyāyāḥ kartavyaṃ paripūrṇaṃ
pratipādayitavyaṃ, tasya ca paripūrṇatā itikartavyatābhāgena vinā na bhavatīti tadākāṅkṣasya
abhidhānaṃ bhavati prārambhaḥ । tadākāṅkṣitaiva kathamityāha---<q>“sa eṣa vidhyādirvidhyantāpekṣaḥ”</q> sa
eva kartavyatārūpo vidhyādiḥ vidhyantaṃ itikartavyatāṃ ākāṅkṣati । tena vinā pratyetumanuṣṭhātuṃ
cāśakyatvāt iti । nanu bhāṣye itikartavyatākāṅkṣaniyogapratipādanaṃ prakaraṇamuktaṃ na
punaritikartavyatākāṅkṣo niyogaḥ । ataḥ kathamitikartavyatārthitvalakṣaṇaṃ prakaraṇamucyate । kathaṃ
kāryameva itikartavyatākāṅkṣaṃ prakaraṇaṃ vakṣyatīti---ucyate । bhāṣyakāreṇa yatpratipādanaṃ
prakaraṇamuktaṃ tatpratipādyamānāvastha eva kartavyatārūpo vidhiḥ itikartavyatākāṅkṣa iti darśayitum ।
ataśca niyoga evetikartavyatākāṅkṣaḥ pratipādyamānaḥ । tasya ca yā tṛtīyākāṅkṣā prakaraṇa-
mityavirodhaḥ । <b>idānīṃ vākyaptakaraṇayorvirodhe tulyabale ete kāraṇe iti</b> yadvadati tatra
<b>ko'bhiprāyaḥ?</b> pṛcchataścāyamāśayaḥ । vākyameva balīyaḥ padārthānvayasaṃbandhakāraṇatvāditi ।
2praṣṭurabhiprāyaṃ kathayati---<b>kāryārthatvādanvayasya ubhayaṃ kāryeṇa viniyujyata iti</b> । ayamarthaḥ
---kāryārthassakalapadārthānāmanvayaḥ ato vākyenāpi yasya viniyogaḥ tasyāpi kāryeṇaiva । prakaraṇe-
nāpi yasya viniyogaḥ tasyāpi kāryeṇaiveti ubhayavirodhe biniyogastulya iti । <b>yadvā kāryādṛte
anvayasya bādhitatvāt pratyuta prakaraṇameva balīyaḥ । tatpratyayatvādvākyasya । evaṃ
manvānenoktaṃ</b> bhāṣyakāreṇa liṅgena <b>vākyasya bādhitatvāditi</b> । asyārthaḥ---iti-
kartavyatākāṅkṣā hi kāryameva prakaraṇam । tadvirodhe cānvayo bādhyata iti । yathā prayā-
<note>(1) Bh. P. 853</note> <note>(2) R. prapṛṣṭamabhi</note>
﻿<pb n="r788"/>
jaśeṣeṇetyatra sak‍tūniti ca । ataḥ pratyuta vākyāt prakaraṇameva balīyaḥ
kāryapratyayatvādvākyasya । pratīyate'neneti pratyayaḥ kāryameva vākyena pratyāyyate ।
atasyadvirodhe vākyaṃ durbalam । pradhānavirodhe guṇānāṃ durbalatvāditi । anenāśayenoktaṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇa---<q>“1liṅgena bādhitatvādvākyasya prakaraṇenāpi bādho yukta”</q>
iti । atrocyate---<b>atrāpyarthaviprakarṣādityukto hetuḥ । kathamarthaviprakarṣa uktaḥ ? kāryārtha-
tayā'nvayaḥ kalpyaḥ</b> uktametat śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇe <q>“prakaraṇenānvitābhidhānāvagatayā kāryārtha-
tayā itikartavyatātvenānvayaḥ kalpyaḥ”</q> । <b>na ca kalṛptānvayasya kāryārthatve siddhe'nvayāntaraṃ,
viniyuktaviniyogavirodhāt liṅgavacchakyate kalpayituṃ</b> k‌lṛptānvayasya viniyojyasya
vākyena punaḥ prakaraṇāt anvayāntaraṃ na śakyate kalpayituṃ viniyuktasya viniyogavirodhāt ।
yathā liṅge śrutiviruddhe । yadi yāvadvākyārthānvayānusāreṇa niyogārthatā na syāt tadā
prakaraṇenānvayāntaraṃ kalpyetāpi । iha punaḥ vākyāvagatānvayānugrahe na kāryārthatā'paiti2
iti prathamāvagatatvāt vākyagamya evānvayo balīyāt । <b>tasmādvākyaṃ balīyaḥ</b> । nanu yadyartha-
viprakarṣādeva prakaraṇabādhaḥ tadā śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇenaiva gatārthatā । tatraivārthaviprakarṣeṇāsyokta-
tvāditi tatrāha---<b>durjñānaviprakarṣajñāpanāyādhikaraṇaprapañco'yaṃ liṅgavad‌draṣṭavyaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ
---satyaṃ viprakarṣeṇa durbalatvaṃ satu viprakarṣa eva durjñāna iti tatparijñānāya adhikaraṇaprapañco'yamiti
<b>udāharaṇamuktaṃ</b> bhāṣye sūktavākanigadaḥ । <b>atha prakaraṇasya ca kramasya ca virodhe kimudā-
haraṇamiti</b> । adhikaraṇasūcanaivātrāpi । <b>pūrvapakṣavādī kramaprakaraṇayostulyabalatvaṃ manyate</b>
<note>(1) Bh. P. 853</note> <note>(2) G. kāryārthatā'nveti</note>
﻿<pb n="r789"/>
<b>kathaṃ</b> ? samarthanaikadeśyuttaramāha---<b>bhāṣyakārastāvat ajñānameva</b> tulyabalatve pramāṇaṃ
vyapadiśati <q>“na tāvadviśeṣamupalabhāmaha”</q> iti । ākṣeptā dūṣayati---<b>kimajñānāt‍tulyatvaṃ
siddha‍yati</b> । na sidhyatyeveti bhāvaḥ । <b>jñānasya hi tulyabalatvamatulyabalatvaṃ vā</b>
jñeyatayā viṣayaḥ । tathā nājñānasya । ekadeśyevāha---<b>nanu cājñānamapi pramāṇatayopanyasta-
meva abhāve</b>2 । ākṣeptaivāha---<b>vyavahāramātraṃ tadityuktaṃ</b> prathamapāde । api cābhāvasya ye
pramāṇatāmapīcchanti teṣāmapi mate <b>pramāṇāntaraprameyābhāvamātraṃ ca prameyam</b> । pramāṇāntareṇa
yatpratīyate ghaṭādi tasyābhāvamātraṃ abhāvasya prameyam । na punaranyat । ata iha
---<b>tat‍tulyabalatvamatulyabalatvaṃ ca na pramāṇāntaraprameyābhāvamātraṃ śakyate vaktuṃ</b> ato nābhāvaḥ
prameyam । saṃprati nirākṛta ekadeśyāha---<b>kathaṃ tarhiṃ etadbhāṣyaṃ <q>“na tāvadviśeṣamupalabhāmaha”</q>
iti</b> । ākṣeptā āha---<b>bhāṣyakāra evātra praṣṭavyaḥ</b> । samarthanavādyāha---<b>atrocyate
durvidagdhavacanamātramevedaṃ</b> <q>‘bhāṣyakāra evātra pṛcchyatāṃ’</q> iti । yasmādaya<b>mabhiprāyo
bhāṣyakārasya---nātrānayorviśeṣo jñāyata iti</b> । anayoḥ kramaprakaraṇayoḥ atra videvanādi-
viniyojakatve viśeṣo na jñāyata iti । yadi viśeṣo jñāyeta tadā ekameva viniyojakaṃ
<note>(1) Bh. P. 854</note> <note>(2) G. bhāṣye</note>
﻿<pb n="r790"/>
syāt na viśeṣaṃ jānīmaḥ । tasmādubhayaṃ viniyojakam । nanu ca prakaraṇamevetikartavyata-
yā'nvayaṃ sakalakaraṇasaṃbandhitayā videvanādīnāṃ bodhayatīti viśeṣaḥ gamyate ityatrāha---<b>sarvatra
prakaraṇānusyūteḥ kramo'pi kāryavānavagamyata eva</b> । sarvatra prakaraṇasya adhikāraniyo-
gasyānusyūteḥ anusyūtatvāt kramo'pi kāryavāneva krameṇāpi viniyogaḥ kāryata eva । <b>kāryataśca
bhavan sannidhiranvitamavagamayati</b> । yadi hi kāryasaṃbandho na bhavet tadā sannidhiranvayaṃ na
gamayedeva । yatastu kāryavān sannidhiḥ । ato'nvayaṃ gamayatyeva । <b>pratyuta prakaraṇamevātra
bādhyatayā'vagamyate । viśeṣopasaṃhārāt sannidheḥ</b> । prakaraṇena hi sāmānyena sakala-
karaṇasaṃbandho bodhyaḥ । tatra sannidhānalakṣaṇena krameṇa viśeṣakaraṇa evopasaṃhāraḥ kriyate ।
kasmāt punarviśeṣeṇopasaṃhāraḥ kriyate ityatrāha---<b>na hi kalṛptasya sannidheḥ kalpanā śakyate
vak‍tum</b> । asyārthaḥ---prakaraṇena pramāṇena sarvakaraṇasaṃbandhe kartavye avaśyaṃ sarvaiḥ saha sannidhiḥ
kalpyaḥ asannihitasaṃbandhānupapatteḥ । ākāṅkṣāsannidhiyogyatvānāṃ saṃbandhe hetutvāt । na ca klṛptaṃ
sannidhimanādṛtya sannidhānakalpanā yuktā anvayasyeva । yathā'nvaye k‌lṛpte na saṃbandhasya kalpanā
evamatrapīti । ataḥ krama eva balīyāniti manyate । nanu ca satyapi sannidhāne ākāṅkṣā-
viśeṣābhāvāt na saṃbandhitvena bhavitavyamiti kramasyāpi prakaraṇāpekṣāsti tathā nākāṅkṣāṣi
sannidhānamantareṇa saṃbandhaheturiti parasparāpekṣitvāt dvayoḥ tulyabalatvameva yuktam na tu kramasya
balīyastvamiti tatrāha---<b>tatpunaridamanvāruhyavacanamityuktamādye'dhikaraṇe</b> । prauḍhavāda evāyaṃ
na punaḥ paramārthataḥ । evaṃ tulyabalatvenāyaṃ pūrvapakṣaḥ ityetat śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇe darśitam ।
<b>sarvatra caivaṃ draṣṭavyam</b> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r791"/>
<p><b>atrocyate---kramāt prakaraṇaṃ balīya iti । kutaḥ ? nahyanākāṅkṣitasya kramaḥ saṃbandha-
hetuḥ</b> yasyākāṅkṣā nāsti na tena saha krameṇa saṃbandhaḥ <b>sannidhānamātraṃ hi kramaḥ । na ca
sannidhānamātrās saṃbandho'vagabhyate bhāryā rājñaḥ puruṣo devadattasyetivat</b> । yathā bhāryāpada-
saṃbandhenaiva nirākāṅkṣeṇa rājña ityanena puruṣasya saṃbandho na bhavati tathetyarthaḥ । bhaktvākaṅkṣāta
eva saṃbandhaḥ tathāpi kimityāha---<b>ākāṅkṣā ca prakaraṇavatāṃ tulyeti sarvapradhānasaṃbandho
videvanādīnām</b> । nanu ca kramavato'pi ākāṅkṣātaḥ kimiti saṃbandho na bhavatītyāha
---<b>kramāddha‍yākāṅkṣā । ākāṅkṣāto'nvayaḥ anvayāttādarthyamiti so'yamarthaviprakarṣaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---sannidhisamuccāraṇena hi svavākyopāttapadapadārthasaṃbandhanirākāṅkṣasya abhiṣecanīya-
vākyārthasyāpi vidyamānataiva videvanādipadārthāntarākāṅkṣā kalpayitavyā । kalpayitvā cānvayaḥ
kalpyaḥ । kalpite cānvaye tādarthyaṃ kalpyam । tadidaṃ kramanibandhanaṃ tādarthyaṃ vilambitam ।
prakaraṇavatāṃ tu itikartavyatākāṅkṣāṃ utthitaiva aparipūrṇatvāt । tayā ca karaṇaidamarthyaṃ
kalpyata iti śīghraṃ prakaraṇatastādarthyam ।</p>
<p><b>yaduktaṃ kramādākāṅkṣopasaṃhāra iti । tadayuktam । sarbārthatvepi kasyacit sanni-
dhānamavaśyaṃbhāvīti pāṭhārthameva tat</b> । asyārthaḥ---1yadi tadgatānāmavāntaravidhīnāmiti-
kartavyatākāṅkṣā syāt tadā yasya sannidhāvāmnānaṃ tatraivetikartavyatātvamupasaṃhriyate iha tvekasya
rājasūyādhikāravidheritikartavyatā iti nopasaṃhārassaṃbhavati । tasmādekādhikāravidhiṃsabandhibhiḥ
<note>(1) G. parihṛtānāmavā</note>
﻿<pb n="r792"/>
karaṇaiḥ itikartavyatayā videvanādayassaṃbadhyante । ekasannidhānaṃ tu avaṃśyaṃbhāvi anyathā
paṭhitumaśakteriti pāṭhārthameva sannidhānaṃ, na punaḥ saṃbandhopasaṃhārārthaṃ <b>bādhitasyahyanugraho nyāyya
ityuktam</b> ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyaṃ---<q>“prakaraṇavataḥ sannidhau āmnātena paripūrṇenāpi avakalpena ekavākyatvaṃ”</q>
iti । nanu vināpi paripūrṇeṃnetyanena sidhyatyevābhimataṃ <b>kimidaṃ paripūrṇenāpīti</b> । samādhatte-
<b>etaduktaṃ bhavati---na cetkramaḥ pramāṇaṃ ekavākyataiva nāsti iti । nanu ākāṅkṣā-
sannidhiryogyatvamiti ekavākyatve hetuḥ satyaṃ vākyārthāvagatau trayameva hetuḥ
iha punarvākyārthasya vākyārthasya ca saṃbandhaḥ । sa cetikartavyatā-
rthitayaiva saṃbadhyata ityuktam । kramaḥ punaḥ vākyārthasya ca sannidhānamityuktam ।
bhāryā rājñaḥ puruṣo devadattasyetyatra pradarśitam</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---codyanirākaraṇārthamidamuktaṃ
paripūrṇenāpīti । evaṃ hi paraḥ paricodayati kramaprakaraṇe parasparāpekṣayā tulyabale eva । na
hi prakaraṇenāpi itikartavyatātvena saṃbandhaḥ āpādyamāno vinā sannidhānenāpādyate । yasmā---
dākāṅkṣāsannidhiyogyatvānāṃ militānāmeva saṃbandhāvagatihetutvam । tena prakaraṇena kramo-
'pekṣaṇīya iti । tatredaṃ nirākaraṇam paripūrṇeneyamekavākyatā । vākyārthībhūtasya hi
sādhyātmanaḥ vidhyarthasya vākyārthabhūtenaiva aṅgavidhinā itikartavyatāṃśaniveśinā saṃbandhaḥ ।
yā ca paripūrṇenaikavākyatā sā itikartavyatārthitayā; ekasya cādhikāravidheritikartavyatārthitā
﻿<pb n="r793"/>
nāṅgavidhīnāmiti sarvakaraṇaireva saṃbandho videvanādīnāmiti । akṣarārthastu---yadi kramaḥ
pramāṇaṃ nāṅgīkriyate ekavākyataiva sarvakaraṇairapi saha videvanādīnāṃ na syāt । ākāṅkṣā
sannitiḥ yogyatvamiti trayaṃ militamekavākyatve hetuḥ । tasmāta kramo'pyādaraṇīya iti ।
parasparāpekṣāyāṃ tulyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ ākāṅkṣālakṣaṇasannidhānaṃ ca dvayamapīti krameṇāpi viniyogo
yukta iti । uttaraṃ---<b>satyaṃ vākyārthāvagatau</b> trayameva hetuḥ । <b>iha punaḥ vākyārthasya
vākyārthasya ca saṃbandhaḥ sa cetikartavyatārthitayaiva saṃbadhyate</b> na punaḥ kriyākārakādya-
pekṣitayetyuktaṃ prakaraṇādhikaraṇe । ekasya cādhikāravidheritikartavyatārthiteti tadvaśenaiva
sarvatra prakaraṇasaṃbandho nyāyyaḥ । <b>kramaḥ punaḥ</b> itikartavyatākāṅkṣāśūnyo'vāntaraprakaraṇābhāvāt
sannidhānamātraṃ kramaḥ । na ca sannidhānamātrāt saṃbandhaḥ <b>yathā bhāryā rājñaḥ puruṣo deva-
dattasyeti darśitam ।</b></p>
<p>atha kramasamākhyayorvirodhe kiṃ balīya iti cintyate---<b>kramo'hyākāṅkṣāvataḥ sannidhau
bhavati viśeṣāvagamahetuḥ । samākhyā punaḥ viśeṣanimittaiveti tulyabale ete kāraṇe iti ।
tasmādubhayaṃ viniyojakam</b> । asyārthaḥ---<q>‘śundhadhvaṃ’</q> iti mantraḥ śundhanaṃ prakāśayati । tatra
ye śudhyante te ākāṅkṣyante । tairvinā vākyasyāparipūrṇatvāt । atassannidhau sānnāyya-
pātrāṇi saṃbadhyante । tena teṣāṃ śundhanaprakāśakatvāt sānnāyyapātreṣu mantrasya viniyogaḥ ।
samākhyayā puroḍāśapātreṣu, viśeṣavartitvāt samākhyāyā ityākāṅkṣāvataḥ śundhanamantrasya
sannidhau sānnāyyapātrāṇāṃ paṭhitatvāt kramo'pi bhavati viśeṣaviniyogāvagamahetuḥ । samākhyā
punaḥ pauroḍāśikamiti viśeṣanimittaiva । <q>“adhikṛtya kṛte granthe”</q> ityasminnadhikāre
<q>“paurauḍāśapuroḍāśāt ṣṭhan”</q> iti pauroḍāśaśabdāt puroḍāśamadhikṛtya kṛte granthe ityasminnarthe
ṣṭhan vihitaḥ । paurauḍāśaśabdena puroḍāśasaṃbandhīnyucyante । tena tatpratipādakaṃ kāṇḍamiti
﻿<pb n="r794"/>
viśeṣapātrasaṃbandha eva mantrasyetyavagamyate । tasmādubhayaṃ kramasamākhyātmakaṃ viniyojakamiti ।
evaṃ prāpte <b>abhidhīyate---kramo balīyān vaidiko hyasau, samākhyā punarlokikī</b> । asyārthaṃ
tṛtvato'navabudhyamānaścodayati---<b>nanu caivaṃ vadatā samākhyā naiva pramāṇamityuktaṃ bhavati</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---tvaṃ kila siddhāntin laukikī samākhyetyevaṃ vadasi । evaṃ vadatā laukikatvena samā-
khyā vedārthanirṇayaheturna bhavatītyabhyupagatam । tathā ca sarvatraiva samākhyāyāḥ prāmāṇyoccheda iti
pariharati---<b>maivaṃ vocaḥ । arthaviprakarṣa evānena prakāreṇocyate । kathaṃ</b> punarlaukikatvenārtha-
viprakarṣaḥ ? ucyate---<b>samākhyā hi saṃbandhanimittā satī sannidhānādyavagamayati</b> । lauki-
katvena tāvat samākhyā vedārthe na sākṣātsaṃbandhaṃ vidadhāti । kintu saṃbandhanibandhanā satī
saṃbandhasidhyarthaṃ ākāṅkṣāsannidhiyogyatāṃ kalpayati । <b>kramaḥ punaḥ svayameva sannidhiḥ । na
ca pratyakṣasya sannidheḥ punaḥ sannidhānāntarakalpanā ghaṭata iti</b> । pratyakṣasya sannidheritya-
nādare ṣaṣṭhī । pratyakṣaṃ sannidhānamanādṛtya na sannidhānāntarakalpanā yuktetyarthaḥ । <b>so'yamartha-
viprakarṣaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi samākhyā ?</b> saṃbandhaṃ vinetyarthaḥ । <b>samavāyādibhirupapadyate
brāhmaṇagrāmavat</b> । tasmin kāṇḍe puroḍāśasya samavāyāt bhūyastvāt prāthamyādvā pauroḍāśi-
kavyapadeśaḥ brāhmaṇagrāmavat ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r795"/>
<p><b>atha yata tatra tatrābhidhīyate <q>‘idamanena vādhyate’</q> <q>‘idamanena bādhyata’</q> iti tatra
yadbādhyate kiṃ tat bādhakaviṣayaṃ prāptaṃ</b> uta aprāptamiti <b>kasyaṃ vyākhyānamidaṃ bhāṣyamiti</b> ।
bhāṣye ākṣipte ekadeśyāha---<b>na kasya cidapīti brūmaḥ</b> । śrutiliṅgetyasya na kaścidavayavo
vyākhyāyate'nena । ato na kasyacidapīdaṃ vyākhyānamiti । ākṣeptā āha---<b>kiṃ tarhi
anenātra kriyate</b> । nirākṛta ekadeśyāha---<b>bhāṣyakāra evātra praṣṭavyaḥ</b> yenedamuktam ।
paramasamarthanavādyāha---<b>atrābhidhīyate---śrutyādīnāṃ balābalacintāśeṣabhūtamidaṃ bhāṣyam । kathaṃ
kṛtvā ? utraraṃ---balābalacintā hi bādhyāpekṣiṇī</b> yatkilābalaṃ tadbādhyam । yacca
