balavat tadbādhakam । tena bādhyaṃ vinā balābalacintā nāsti । <b>tadidānīṃ bādhyaṃ kiṃ
bādhakaviṣayaṃ prāptaṃ sat bādhyate utāprāptameva ubhayathā cābhihito doṣaḥ</b> । yadi prāptaṃ
kathaṃ bādhyate aśakyatvāt । athāprāptaṃ kiṃ bādhyeta vādhyasyābhāvāt । nanu prāptabādho
daśame pradarśitaḥ । <b>kimiti prāptau satyāṃ virodho darśitaḥ</b> । tatkila viruddhamucyate
yatkvacinna dṛśyate । prāptatā ca bādhyatā ca dṛśyata eva । tatkathamanayorvirodhaḥ । daśame
hi prāptasya prākṛtasya padārthajātasya bāgho darśitaḥ । samādhatte---<b>kāryataḥ prāptau na doṣaḥ</b> ।
prāptasyāpi bādhe na doṣaḥ । kāryato hi prāptasya na kāryāntaraṃ kalpayitavyam । tena kalṛpta-
<note>(2) P. 858</note>
﻿<pb n="r796"/>
kāryapurassaratvāt prāpteḥ kāryalopena kṛtakṛtyatvena vā bādho yuktaḥ । anuṣṭhānabādhātmakaḥ
---iha tūpadeśaḥ cintyate tathāpi kimityāha---<b>upadeśena ca prāptidurbādhā</b> । kutaḥ ?
<b>tatraiva daśame darśayiṣyāmaḥ</b> । upadeśe hi yathopadeśaṃ kāryamityaśakyaḥ kāryato'pi bādha
iti । <b>ihaiva kasmāt tanna pradarśyate । pradarśitameva <q>“pratipradhānamāvartante guṇā”</q></b>
ityanena bhāṣyeṇa darśitamevedaṃ upadeśena prāptirdurbādheti । <b>kathaṃ pratipradhānāvṛttyabhidhānena
abādhitatā darśitā bhavati</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>dvayoḥ prāmāṇyābhyupagamanena pratipradhānābhidhānāt</b>
darśitameva । dvayoḥ śrutiliṅgayoḥ prāmāṇye'bhyupagate pratipradhānaṃ guṇā āvartanta iti
yasmādabhihitaṃ tasmādaśakyo bādha iti darśitam । evaṃ hi vadatā yathopadeśaṃ kāryamityā-
śritaṃ bhavati । tasmādupadeśena prāptaṃ upadeśāntareṇa na śakyaṃ bādhitum । <b>prāpteścā-
viśeṣānnopadeśataḥ</b> prāptasya bādhaḥ । kāryataḥ prāptasya tu atideśataḥ prāpteḥ upadeśaprāptena
bādho yuktaḥ । <b>tasmādidamayuk‍taṃ anena bādhyamiti</b> । na kevalaṃ prāpta evāyuktaṃ
aprāptepyayuktaṃ prasaktyabhāvāt । yatkhalu prasaktaṃ tadbādhamarhati nānyat ।</p>
<p><b>atredānīṃ upadeśabādhavido'bhidadhati । sāmānyataḥ prāptiṃ manvānā viśeṣamapa-
śyantaḥ smṛtipramoṣanimittaṃ prāptijñānaṃ vyapadiśanti śuktikāyāmiva rajatajñānam ।
viśeṣāvagamāt‍tu tatteṣāṃ nivartata iti bādhaśabdaprayogaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---barhidarvesadanaṃ
﻿<pb n="r797"/>
dāmītyevamādau yā liṅgasya svaviniyogaviṣaye prāptiḥ pramāṇato'vadhṛtā viniyojakāviniyojaka-
yoḥ yatsamānaṃ rūpaṃ liṅgayoḥ tatassāmānyataḥ tāmaviniyojake prāptiṃ pramāṇatāṃ manvānāḥ
smarantaḥ prāptismaraṇasya ca prāptijñānā<b>dviśeṣamapaśyantaḥ smṛtipramoṣanimittaṃ</b> prāptijñānaṃ
smarāmītyasyāṃśasya pramoṣo nimittaṃ yasya vyapadeśasyeti kriyāviśeṣaṇam । prāptiṃ jānīma
iti bhrāntā vyapadiśanti । śuk‍tikāyāmiva rajatajñānaṃ yathā rajatasādhāraṇaṃ yadrūpaṃ śuktikāyāṃ
tāvanmātreṇa tasyāṃ gṛhītāyāṃ yadrajate smaraṇajñānamupajāyate tasya smṛtirūpatāyā agrahāt
viśeṣamapaśyanto rajatajñānāt rajatasmaraṇameva rajataṃ jñānamupadiśanti rajataṃ jānīma iti ।
tathehāpi prāptismaraṇaṃ prāptijñānaṃ vyapadiśanti । <b>viśeṣadarśanāt</b> prāptismaraṇametanna
prāptijñānamiti viśeṣadarśanāt <b>tatteṣāṃ nivartyate</b> paramārthato'tra prāptirna jñāyate prāptisāmagrī-
virahāt sāmagrīvirahaścārthaviprakarṣeṇeti darśitaḥ । tasmācca prāptiriyaṃ smaryate na tu jñāyata
iti jñānataḥ prāptinibandhano'pi vyavahāro nivartyata iti bādhaśabdaprayogaḥ । paramārthatastu
svarūpajñānamevedaṃ ityetat saprapañcaṃ prathamapāda eva nirṇītam । <b>tadayamatrārthasaṃkṣepaḥ</b>
---viniyojakāviniyojakayoḥ sādhāraṇaṃ yadrūpaṃ aviniyojakasya liṅgādeḥ tadvaśena pramāṇatāṃ
viniyojakaliṅgavartinīṃ smarataḥ tasyāśca smṛteḥ viśeṣāgrahaṇena grahaṇādviśeṣamananusandadhataḥ
aviniyojakamapi liṅgādi viniyojakapramāṇamiti vyapadeśavyavahārau pravartete । tatrārtha-
viprakarṣeṇa liṅgādeḥ śrutyādivirodhe pramāṇatā nāsti asati pramāṇatve pramāṇatā na grahītuṃ śakyate
kintvanyatra dṛṣṭā smaryata iti viśeṣālocanena vyavahāravyapadeśau nivartete । evaṃ cāptāptaiva
liṅgādeḥ pramāṇatā smaryamāṇā viśeṣāgrahaṇena vyavahāraṃ gṛhyamāṇeva pravartayantī vyavahārāpahāreṇa
bādhyata iti vyapadiśyate ।</p>
<p><b>nanu cāyamaprāptabādhalakṣaṇo bādhaḥ prathamapāda evoktaḥ <q>‘yasya ca duṣṭaṃ karaṇaṃ’</q> ityatra
kimiti punarupanyastaḥ</b> । aprāptabādhasiddha‍yarthaṃ nārabdhavyamidamadhikaraṇamityarthaḥ । samādhānaṃ
.﻿<pb n="r798"/>
---<b>astyatra viśeṣaḥ tatra śuktikārthasyāgrahaṇāt । rajate ca smarāmīti pramoṣāt vyapadeśa-
siddhiḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---śuktikā rajatasādhāraṇena rūpeṇa gṛhyate । sā ca rajatāt
bhinnāpi na bhinnetyabagamyate bhedapratītihetubhūtarūpāntarāpratīteḥ । taduk‍taṃ---rūpāntara-
nibandhanā hyanyatvabuddhiḥ na vastvantaranibandhaneti । tasyāṃ ca tathābhūtāyāṃ rajate smṛti---
rārvibhavati । tadapi ca rajataṃ na śuktikāto bhinnamityanusandhīyate । ato gṛhyamāṇa-
smaryamāṇayoḥ śuktikārajatayoḥ viveko nāvasīyate । tathā yāpyasau rajatasmṛtiḥ sāpi
grahaṇādbhedena nāvasīyate । smṛtiriyamiti parikalpanāvirahāt । ataḥ grahaṇācchuktiviṣayāta
bhedenānavasīyamānā smṛtiḥ śuktikāyāṃ grahaṇanibandhanāveva vyapadeśavyavahārau pravartayati ।
ataḥ tanmātrasmaraṇādeva vyapadeśasiddhiriti ghaṭetāpi aprāptabādhaḥ । <b>iha punaḥ āgabhikatvena
dvayasyāpi tulyatāpattirbhavatyeveti punarārabdham</b> । asyārthaḥ---śrutiliṅgayordvayorapi
pramāṇatvāt tulyatāpattirbhavati । tena viniyogaḥ smaryate iti na śakyate vak‍tum yāvatā liṅge-
nāpi pramāṇena pramīyata ityetadeva kasmānna bhavatīti śaṅkā'stīti tadapanodanāyedamārabdham ।
<b>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ āgabhikatve dvayasya tulyatāpattirbhavati</b> (tulyatāpattau cābādhakena
punaḥ kāraṇena śrutyā liṅgādidvayasyāpi tulyanāpratītirbhavati) <b>tulyatāpattau ca</b> satyāṃ kena
kāraṇena <b>bādhaḥ ? atrocyate---svato viparyayābhāvāt</b> । yadi hi svata evātrā-
viniyojakametalliṅgamiti viparyayajñānamutpadyeta tadā tulyatābuddhirna bhavati । <b>na cātra śuk‍ti---
kādiṣvidha svayameva viparyayo bhavati yathā aparīkṣitakāraṇasvabhāvasyāpi</b> puruṣasya
śuktikādiṣu svayameva viparyayajñānaṃ bhavati nedaṃ rajatamityādi na tatheha । kathaṃ tarhi
﻿<pb n="r799"/>
bhavatītyāha---<b>iha punaḥ kāraṇaparīkṣādvārakaḥ viniyogaviparyaya iti prārabdhavyamidamadhi-
karaṇaṃ</b> viniyogakāraṇasvarūpaparīkṣānibandhano'tra viparyayaḥ akṛttārthayorgrāhakagrahaṇaprakaraṇa-
samāmnānayoḥ । viniyojakatvaṃ śrutyādīnāṃ, kṛtārthatvāt tayoraviniyojakatvamiti viniyojaka-
pramāṇasvarūpaparīkṣāyāṃ arthaviprakarṣeṇa liṅgādīnāṃ, sannikarṣeṇa śrutyādīnāmeva viniyojakatvamiti
sthite tāvataiva grāhakagrahaṇaprakaraṇasamāmnānayoḥ kṛtārthatvāt aviniyojakaṃ liṅgādīti viparyayaṃ
puruṣo jānātīti viniyojakasvarūpaparīkṣārthaṃ arthaviprakarṣajñāpanārthaṃ cedamadhikaraṇamārabdhavyam ।
<b>tadviśuddha‍yarthaṃ cedaṃ bhāṣyaṃ</b> yo'sau tenādhikaraṇena bādha uktaḥ tadviśudhyarthamidaṃ bhāṣyam ।
kīdṛśī punaranena bādhaśuddhiḥ <b>kṛtetyāha---so'yamaprāptabādhaḥ</b> । yathā cāprāptasya bādhaḥ
tathā darśitameva । tenāyaṃ bhāṣyārthaḥ <q>“1prāptaṃ bādhakaviṣayaṃ pūrvavijñānamiti brūmaḥ”</q> ।
bādhakasya śrutyāderyo viṣayaḥ tatpūrvavijñānaṃ liṅgādijñānaṃ prāptamiti brūmaḥ । naiva paramārthataḥ
prāptam । kintu aprāptameva paramārthataḥ prāptamiti brūmaḥ praptigrahaṇasmaraṇayoḥ vivekānavadhāraṇāt ।
kathaṃ prāptismaraṇamityāha---<q>“2sāmānyasya kāraṇasya vidyamānatvāta”</q> । pramāṇabhūtaliṅgādigatasya
sādhāraṇarūpasyāpramāṇepi satvāt । <q>“3atha kathaṃ nivartate naiva nivartate”</q> prāptismaraṇaṃ kintu
<q>“mithyājñānameva taditi pratyayāntaraṃ bhavati”</q> smaraṇameva grahaṇavyavahārapravartakaṃ mithyājñānamucyate
evaṃ ca svarūpajñānameva bādhakaṃ bhavati । tasminnavagate tannibandhanavyavahāranivṛtteḥ iti kṛtā
bādhaviśuddhiḥ ।</p>
<p><b>ahīno vā prakaraṇādgauṇaḥ । idamidānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ niyogasannidhirbalīyān</b>
<note>(1) Bh. P. 859</note> <note>(2) ibid 859</note> <note>(3) ibid 861</note>
﻿<pb n="r800"/>
<b>uta viniyoga</b>sannidhiriti । vākyaprakaraṇayorvirodhe vākyaṃ balīya iti sthite jyotiṣṭoma-
prakaraṇapaṭhitadvādaśopasattāviṣaye kiṃ vākyaprakaraṇayorvirodho'sti nāstīti cintyate । tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ-
midaṃ cintyate---kiṃ niyogasya jyautiṣṭomikasya yassannidhiḥ sa balīyān kiṃ tena sannidhānena
jyautiṣṭomikaniyogārthatā dvādaśopasattāyāḥ pratīyatām, uta viniyogataḥ sannidhiḥ viniyogataḥ
padārthasaṃbandhaḥ tena yassannidhiḥ 1ahīnaniyogasya sa balīyān tenāhīnaniyogārthatā । ahīna-
śabdena hi dvādaśāhaparimitayāgo dvādaśarātrātmaka ucyate, ahīnaśabdasya tannāmadheyatvāt ।
na punarahīnādhikāraviniyogaḥ । tena dvādaśopasattā ahīnasyeti yāgasaṃbandho'vagamyate ।
tatsaṃbandhena ca tadadhikāraniyogasannidhiravagamyate । tadvaśena tatsaṃbandha iti । etaduktaṃ
bhavati---jyotiṣṭomādhikārāpūrvasannidhānāt tatsaṃbandhapurassarā prakaraṇena kiṃ somayāgāṅgatā uta
padārthānvayavaśena ahīnāpūrvagṛhītateti । <b>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī kāryārthatvāt viniyogasya
prakṛtakāryasambhave prakṛtakāryasaṃbandho yuktaḥ iti manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---sarvo hi viniyogaḥ
padārthaḥ saṃbandho'dhikāraniyogārthaḥ । tena pradhānatvāt prakṛtaniyogasaṃbandha eva nyāyyaḥ ।
<b>kathaṃ tarhi viniyogaḥ</b> ? padārthasaṃbandhaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>kāryārthatvādviniyogasya tadanuguṇaḥ</b>
pradhānabhūtakāryasaṃbandhānuguṇaḥ <b>vyākhyāyate</b> gauṇyā vṛttyā । anena somayāga evocyate ।
<b>evaṃ tarhi vākyaṃ prakaraṇād‍durbalamityuk‍taṃ bhavati</b> । pariharati---<b>neti । kutaḥ ?
prakaraṇāviśeṣe (sannidhānāviśeṣe hi) balīyo vākyam</b> । 2ekaprakaraṇisaṃbandhe hi sthite
yadi tasminneva prakaraṇe vākyena prakaraṇena ca viniyogaḥ tadā vākyaṃ balīyaḥ yathā sūktavāke ।
<b>yatra punaḥ kāryasannidhireva nāsti kiṃ tatra vākyaṃ kariṣyati</b> । na cātrāhīnakāryasanni-
<note>(1) G. ahīnayāgasya</note> <note>(2) G. ekaprakaraṇa</note>
﻿<pb n="r801"/>
dhirasti । <b>tasmāt kāryānuguṇaiva padārthavyākhyā nyāyyā na</b> padārthānuguṇeti yuktaṃ na
hīyatta ityahīna iti ।</p>
<head>asaṃyogāt‍tu mukhyasya ।।</head>
<p><b>atra bhaṇyate---uktamasmābhiḥ padārthānvayassaṃbandhakāraṇaṃ</b> padārthayoranvayo yaḥ saḥ
aidamarthyasaṃbandhasya kāraṇamityuktamasmāgniḥ । <b>kāryato'pyanvaya eva gamyate</b> । yāvaddhi padārthā-
nvayo nāvagamyate tāvat kāryānvayasyānirvāhaḥ । tena kāryato'pyanvayo'vagamyate । <b>nacānva-
yāvagame pratītānvayatyāgo yuktaḥ</b> । <b>na hi dṛṣṭe hastini hastipadenānumānaṃ saṃbhavati</b> ।
<b>tasmādapratipakṣameva padārthavyākhyānaṃ yuktam</b> । nanu kārye pratipakṣe kathamapratipakṣatā tatrāha
---<b>padārtha eva hi padārthapratipakṣe bhavati na punaḥ kāryam</b> । <b>anyathā hi</b> yadi kāryamapi
pratipakṣaṃ syāt tadā <b>arthavādapadānāmapi kartavyatābhidhānataiva syāt</b> । sarveṣāmapyartha-
vādapadānāṃ kāryānvayitaiva syāt na pratītyanvayitāmātram । padārthānvayasaṃbandhavaśena hi teṣāṃ
stutyupayogitā । kāryasaṃbandhabalena tu sarveṣāmapyanuṣṭhānopadeśataiva syāt । kartavyatāśabdena
anuṣṭhānamucyate । <b>tasmādahīnasyeti</b> padārthānvayabalena <b>kratvantarārthataiva nyāyyā</b> ।
<note>(1) Bhashya P. 863</note>
﻿<pb n="r802"/>
<b>nanu cātra tulyameva śrautatvaṃ, ekatra somayāge na hīyata ityahīnaḥ, anyatra ahīne ahnāṃ
samūha iti</b> । ekatra naña‍samāsaḥ anyatra taddhitaḥ <q>“ahnaḥ khaḥ kratau”</q> iti khaḥ । nanu ca
svaravirodhena nañ samāso'nupapannaḥ nañ‌samāseṃ hi <q>‘tatpuruṣe tulyārthatṛtīyāsaptabhyupamānā-
vyayadvitīyā kṛtyāḥ’</q> iti pūrvapadaprakṛtisvaratvena samāsāntodāttatve bādhite ādyudātto'hīna-
śabdaḥ syāt madhyodāttaścāyamāmnāyate । taddhitapakṣe pratyayādyudāttatve madhyodāttatā
upapanneti taddhitānta evāyam । sa ca mukhyayā vṛttyā na jyotiṣṭome vartate
iti kathamubhayatra śrautatvamucyate । abhyupagamyāpyubhayatra śrautatvaṃ kṛtvācintā-
nyāyenāpi nyāyavyutpattiriti darśayitumidamuktam । tadāha-<b>kimasmākamanayā cintayā ekatra
śrauto'nyatra gauṇa iti kṛtvā cintitam</b> । <b>na cedatra śrautagauṇatvaṃ saṃbhavati tadā udā-
haraṇāntaraṃ bhaviṣyati</b> । <b>yadvā rūḍhiṃ manyate bhāṣyakāraḥ</b> । tena jyotiṣṭome yaugikatvāt
rūḍhiryogamapaharatīti nyāyāt rūḍhirevāyaṃ grahītavyaḥ । na ca somayāgeṣu mukhya iti siddha-
mekatra śrautatvamanyatra gauṇatvam । kutaḥ punaḥ bhāṣyakāro rūḍhiṃ manyate ityatrāha---<b>satreṣva-
daśanāt</b> prayogasya । nanvidamayuk‍taṃ paṅkajādiṣvapi rūḍhitvāpatteḥ te'pi hi padmavyati-
rekeṇānyatra paṅkajātepi na prayujyante । ucyate---yuk‍taṃ paṅkajādiṣu yaugikatvaṃ paṅkaśabdasya
jaśabdasya ca pṛthaka‍prayogeṇa ka‍lṛśaktitvāt । iha punarahīnaśabdasya na samūhe prayogo
dṛṣṭaḥ । tena ka‍lṛptaśaktyanusāreṇa prayogānupapatteḥ śaktiḥ kalpyate । tatra samudāyasyaiva dvāda-
śāhādiṣu yajaticoditeṣu anavasthitakartṛkeṣu prayogadarśanāt śaktiḥ kalpyate । na punarahīna-
śabdasya yaugikatvam । yadi hi satrepi prayogo dṛśyeta tadā anekaśaktikalpanābhayāt ahīna-
śabdasyaiva śaktiḥ kalpyeta । na caitadasti । tasmāt samudāyaśaktyaivāyamahīnaśabdo vartata
﻿<pb n="r803"/>
iti rūḍhirevāyam । kimarthaṃ tarhi taddhitavidhiḥ ? <b>vyutpattimātraṃ taddhitavidhiḥ śunaḥ
śepādiṣu samāsavidhiriva</b> । yathā'vibhaktāvayavatayaiva samudāyaśaktyā śunaśśepaśabde
vartamānepi samāsavidhiḥ <q>“ṣaṣṭhyā vā'lugupasaṃkhyānaṃ śunaḥ śepapucchalāṅgūleṣvaluk”</q> iti ।
vyutpatteśca prayojanaṃ svaraviśeṣavidhiḥ । <b>tasmādidamapyupapadyata evodāharaṇam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>dvibahutvayuk‍taṃ vā'codanāttasya</b> । <b>nanu ta pūrveṇaivādhikaraṇena gatamidam</b> । <b>na
hi pratītānvayatyāgaḥ kāryānurodhena yuktaḥ iti</b> । pratītadvitvabahutvānvayatyāgaḥ prakṛta-
kāryānurodhena na yuktaḥ iti । samādhatte---<b>satyaṃ kintvastyatrābhyadhikāśaṅkā</b> । prakṛtepi
dvitvabahutvasaṃbhavāt । vākyaprakaraṇayoravirodha ityabhyadhikāśaṅkā । kathaṃ punaḥ prakṛtepi
saṃbhava ityatrāha---<b>yathāśaktiprayoge nitye karmaṇi yajamānāntarapraveśamapi manyate pūrvapakṣa-
vādī pat‍nyabhiprāyaṃ vā ekaśeṣābhidhānam</b> । asyārthaḥ---nitye karmaṇyadhikṛtasya yathā-
śaktyanuṣṭhānam । tatra yadā eko yajamāno'śaktaḥ kṛts‍naprayogaṃ kartuṃ tadā yajamānāntareṇa
saha militvā kariṣyati । tatra caikakartṛtvaṃ kelamaṅgabhūtaṃ tyakṣyate । tasyāṃ cāvasthāyāṃ
jyotiṣṭomepyanekayajamānasaṃbhavaḥ । tathā pat‍nīmapi gṛhītvā ekaśeṣābhidhānam---<q>‘yajamānayoḥ’</q>
<q>‘yajamānebhyaḥ’</q> iti kalpyate । tasmādanutkarṣaḥ pratipadvidhānasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r804"/>
<p><b>na prakṛterekasaṃyogāt</b>। <b>atrocyate---yajamānāntarapraveśastāvanna ghaṭate</b> । <b>kutaḥ</b> ?
<b>yajamānasya hi yathā śak‍tuyādityucyate</b> । <b>tatra yanna saṃbhavati tasyaiva gauṇārthatā
tyāgo vā na punaryajamānāntaropādānena</b> saṃprayogaḥ । asyārthaḥ---adhikārastāvadekasyaiva
jyotiṣṭome, 1ekakartṛtvāt viṣayasya adhikārabhede pratyadhikāraṃ kartṛbhedāt kartṛbhedabhinnāḥ
pratiyajamānaṃ bhinnā eva prayogāḥ । tatra yadi militvā ‘anekayajamānā yajeran ekatvāt
prayogasya ekasyaivādhikārasiddheḥ eka eva yajamānaḥ syāt nāneke । ato yathāśaktyanuṣṭhānepi
ekasyaivādhikārapūrvakakartṛtvaṃ yajamānasyocyate na punaryajamānayormilitayoḥ ityekayajamānake
prayoge yanna saṃbhavati tasya gauṇatā tyāgo vā na punaryajamānāntarapraveśaḥ । yadi paraṃ ekenānu-
ṣṭhānāśak‍teḥ kartravasthāyāṃ puruṣāntaramanupraveśyate, na ca tasya yajamānaśabdo vācakaḥ ।
yajamānaśabdoddeśena ca pratipadviśeṣavidhānam । nanu ca yajamānoddeśena ca pratipadvidhāne
uddiśyamānaviśeṣaṇavivakṣānirākaraṇāt yajamānamātrasya ca prakṛte'pyadhikāre saṃbhavāt utkarṣo
nopapadyate । atra vadāmaḥ । dvayoḥ bahubhyaḥ iti coddeśyapadam । tacca yajamānaviṣayamiti
yajamānoddeśenetyucyate । tasmādupapannaḥ utkarṣaḥ । yadā cātra praveśyamāno yajamānaḥ tadā
<b>na yajamānāntaropādānena prayogasaṃpat</b> । kintu kartṛmātropādānena । <b>sati caivaṃ na
yajamānadvitvaṃ bahutvaṃ vā saṃbhavati</b> prakṛtau jyotiṣṭoma ityarthaḥ । <b>yadapyuk‍taṃ pat‍nyabhi-
prāyā dvayoryajamānayoḥ bahugya iti cābhidhānopapattiriti</b> । <b>tadapyayuktam</b> । <b>tasmānna
pat‍nyabhiprāyaḥ itaretarayogo ghaṭate</b> । yasmādekaśeṣe kevalāyāḥ striyastāvat grahaṇaṃ nāsti
<note>(1) G. ekatvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r805"/>
s‍trīmātrasya kvacidapi adhikārābhāvāt । ekaśeṣe avaśyaṃbhāvī dvitīyopi pumānevāvagamyate ।
ataḥ pat‍nyabhiprāyo netaretarayogaḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? puṃdvayābhiprāyaḥ । nanu ca pat‍nyabhiprāyo'pi itare-
tarayogo'styeva <q>“kṣaume vasānau”</q> iti tadvadatrāpi bhaviṣyatītyatrāha---<b>ādhāne tu lakṣaṇayā, asaṃ
bhavāt śrautasya</b> । asyārthaḥ---ādhāne lakṣaṇayā pat‍nyabhiprāya itaretarayogaḥ śrautasya
puṃdvayābhiprāyeṇa itaretarayogasyāsaṃbhavāt prakṛte ādhāne puṃdvayābhāvāt । nanvatrāpi prakṛte
karmaṇi pumanekatvābhāvāt lakṣaṇā āśrīyatāmiti tanna, vākyāt pumanekatvapratītiḥ prakaraṇānna
śakyate bādhitum । ādhāne tu vākyata evādhānaśravaṇaṃ tacca prakṛtavācīti padārthāntarasya
pratipakṣatvāt yuktā lakṣaṇā । yuktyantaraṃ cāha - <b>yathā pat‍nyā saha itaretarayogo na ghaṭate
yāge tathā ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । sahabhāvena praviśantī pat‍nī netaretarayogārhā । tenaiva ca
yajetetyekavacanāvirodha iti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । yāgagrahaṇādyāge pat‍nyā sahetaretarayogo na
saṃbhavati । abhidhānakriyāyāṃ tu saṃbhavatītyuktam । na ca bāhyakriyāpekṣe rājapurohitādi-
viṣaye itaretarayogasaṃbhave abhidhānāśrayo nyāyyaḥ । <b>satriṇāmeva hi sa itaretarayogaḥ</b> ।
na pat‍nīyajamānayoḥ । <b>tasmāt</b> dvitvabahutvābhāvāt atrāpi <b>pūrvavat</b> anvayānurodhena
prakaraṇabādhādutkarṣa iti ।</p>
<p><b>jāghanī caikadeśatvāt</b> । viniyogacintārūpatvāt adhyāyasaṅgatatvepi avāntara-
saṅgatyabhiprāyeṇa pṛcchati---<b>kena prasaṅgenedamadhikaraṇamāyātam</b> ? iti । uttaraṃ---<b>anena
prasaṅgena idamāyātamiti</b> । <b>sthitaṃ tāvat vākyaṃ prakaraṇāt balīyaḥ sannidhāne</b>
﻿<pb n="r806"/>
<b>cāsannidhāne ca kāryasya</b> । <b>atredaṃ sandihyate---kimayaṃ vākyārthaḥ uta ayaṃ iti vākyārtha eva
saṃśayaḥ</b> । <b>kiṃ jāghanyuddeśena pat‍nīsaṃyājā vidhīyante uta viparītamiti</b> । <b>pūrvapakṣī
tāvat jāghanyuddeśena pat‍nīsaṃyājavidhānaṃ manyate</b> । kutaḥ ? <b>evaṃ śrauto'rtho vihito
bhavati</b> । saṃyājayantīti śrutyāvidhānaṃ, <b>anyathā hi vākyārthavidhānaṃ syāt</b> । jāghanī-
vidhānāt । <b>nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe vākyārtha eva vihito bhavati</b> । <b>anyat karma asmin
dravye ucyate</b>---jāghanyāṃ pat‍nīsaṃyājā ucyanta ityarthaḥ । ucyate---<b>anabhijño bhavān
vacanavyaktīnām</b> । <b>na brūmo vākyārthasya vidhisaṃbandho nāstīti</b> vidheyodeśyabhāvena ।
<b>kintu na vidheyo vākyārthaḥ</b> । kintu vākyārtho na vidhīyate । idameva vivṛṇoti
---<b>etaduktaṃ bhavati---na sannikṛṣṭārthatyāgena viprakṛṣṭārthavidhānaṃ yuktamiti</b> samānapadopāttaṃ
karma parityajya na padāntaropāttaviprakṛṣṭadravyavidhānaṃ yuktamiti । <b>ayaṃ cāparo</b>'smin pakṣe
<b>lābho bhavati jāghanyā paśūpādānakalpanā</b> na kṛtā bhavati । asmin hi pakṣe yatra jāghanī
paśuyāge prāptā tatraiva tatpratipattaye pat‍nīsaṃyājavidhānamiti tatpratipattitvādaprayojakatvam ।
pat‍nīsaṃyājeṣu tu jāghanīvidhāne prakaraṇa eva niveśāt upādeyā pat‍nīsaṃyājanirvṛtyarthā jāghanī ।
tasmādatrāpyutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r807"/>
<p><b>codanāvā</b> । <b>atrābhidhīyate</b> । jāghanyevātra pat‍nīsaṃyojeṣu vidhīyate । kutaḥ ?
<b>yāgavidhāne hi pat‍nyartho'paro vidhātavyo bhavati jāghanyā</b> pat‍nīḥ saṃyojayantīti । <b>yadi</b>
paśuyāge jāghanīpratipattyartho'yaṃ yāgo vidhīyate tadā pat‍nyartho'paraḥ kartṛtvena vidheyaḥ । darśapūrṇa-
māsaprakaraṇe tu jāghanīvidhau prakṛtānāṃ pat‍nīsaṃyājānāṃ pat‍nīkartṛtvādanūdyate pat‍nīriti ।
itarasmin viśiṣṭavidhānāśrayaṇe vākyārthasya vidhānaṃ vidhigauravaṃ ceti jāghanyeva vidheyā
ityanutkarṣaḥ । codayati---<b>nanu cātrāpi pat‍nīsaṃyājāścodakena sannihita eva</b> । tena pat‍nī-
kartṛkāḥ prāptā evetyatrāpi pakṣe'nuvāda eva ghaṭiṣyate । pariharati---<b>satyaṃ</b> sannihitāḥ
<b>vidhīyamānatvena tu prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvamiti karmāntarāpattiḥ</b> । punaścodayati
---<b>nanu cāsannidhānaṃ tatra karmāntaratve hetuḥ na vidhīyamānatā</b>, sannidhānaṃ cātra, tena
karmāntaratvānupapattiḥ । yadi ca yāvatkarmasvarūpavidhānāt anyo'tra vidhiḥ na syāt
tadā abhyāsanyāyena bhaveti karmabhedaḥ । iha tu jāghanīsaṃbandhārthatvāt na karmasvarūpa-
vidhānārthatā । tadāha---<b>na cānanyārthatvamatra jāghanīsaṃbandhārthatbādvāvadhasya</b> । <b>tasmānnāyaṃ</b>
pat‍nīvidhānanibandhano <b>vākyabhedarūpaparihāra</b> upapadyate rāddhāntinaḥ । ucyate ।
<b>anabhijño devānāṃ priyaḥ śāstrabhedasya</b> । <b>vidhānasannidhirhi vihitavidhāne bhedamavaruṇaddhi</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yatra vihitaṃ vidhīyate tatra vidhānasannidhirena bhedabhavaruṇaddhi nivārayati ।
﻿<pb n="r808"/>
<b>na padārthasannidhiḥ</b> । ayamāśayaḥ---prakṛte vidhau punarvidhyantare śrutipramāṇābhāvasya pratyabhi-
jñāyamānatvāt na vidheyāntaraṃ śakyate kalpayitum । ṣadārthamātre tu sannihite pramāṇābhāvāsyā1-
pratijñāyamānatvāt vidheyāntaropasthāpakatvāt bhavatyeva śāstrāntaram । iha ca prākṛtā vidheyāḥ
yadyapi codakena sannihitāḥ tathāpi na vidheyatayā kintu padārthatayā । <b>uddeśyatve hi bhavati
padārthasannidhirapyavagamahetuḥ padārthamātrāpekṣatvāduddeśyabhāvasya</b> padārthamātramuddeśo'pekṣate na
pramāṇābhāvāt । tena padārthasvarūpamātreṇa sannihitasyoddeśyatvaṃ bhavati । navaprayājādivat
tasmāt karmāntaravidhānāt aprāptapat‍nyarthavidhāne yukto vākyārthabhedaparihāraḥ । tatra ca
etāvataiva pūrvapakṣasiddhāntayoḥ siddhatvāt kimarthaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa yatra saṃbandho vidhīyata ityādinā
saṃbandhavidhānārthaṃ prakāradvayamupanyastam । anyataratra anyatarasaṃbandhividhānaṃ saṃbandhasya ca
sākṣādvidhānamiti tadāha---<b>yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ubhayasaṃbandhavidhānaṃ</b> ubhayasyānya-
taratra vidhānaṃ saṃbandhasya ca sākṣādvidhāna<b>mupanyastaṃ tatkimarthamidam</b> । <b>ucyate---nāntarīyaka2
sākṣādvidhānavivekapradarśanārtham</b> । yatrānyatarasaṃbandhī aprāpto vidhīyate tatra nāntarīyakaṃ
saṃbandhavidhānam । yatra punassaṃbandhinau prāptau uddiśya svaśabdena saṃbandho vidhīyate tatra
svayameva saṃbandhavidhānamiti vivekaṃ darśayitumityarthaḥ । vivekapradarśanamidānīṃ kimarthaṃ ?
anyatarāprāp‍tyartham । anyatarasyāprāptiṃ darśayitum । <b>neha prakaraṇe ubhayaprāptirupapadyate tasmāda-
nyataradvidheyam</b> । <b>sā ca jāghanyeva vidheyā pat‍nīsaṃyājānāṃ prāptatvāt</b> । <b>tasmādanutkarṣaḥ</b> ।
<note>(1) G. sya pratya</note> <note>(2) R.&amp; G. nāntarīyakavidhiviveka</note>
﻿<pb n="r809"/>
<b>yatpunaridaṃ na paśuṃ prayuṅkata iti pūrvapakṣe uk‍taṃ tadapi tulyaṃ asmadīyepi pakṣe
laukikyāḥ</b> kevalaṃ jāghanyāḥ prāpteḥ saṃbhavāt 2paśuprayuk‍terasaṃbhavāt iti ।</p>
<p><b>santardanaṃ prakṛtau</b> । <b>atrāpyutkarṣāśaṅkā dīrghaśabdasyānanvayāt</b> । <b><q>‘dhṛtyai’</q>ityartha-
vādānupapatteśca</b> । yadi hi prakṛta eva somayāge niveśaḥ syāt tadā dīrghaśabdo'nanvitaḥ
syāt <q>‘dhṛtyai’</q> ityarthavādaśca nopapadyate । dāraṇāśaṅkāyāṃ hi dhāraṇamāśāsitavyaṃ bhavati । na
ca tāvatyeva some dāraṇāśaṅkā । <b>anutkarṣavādī tu latādairdhyeṇāpyanuvādaṃ manvānaḥ dīrghasya
vā somasya iti prakṛtāvevaitadvidhānamiti</b> manyate । dīrghaśabdo'yaṃ yajamānaparatayā
latāparatayā cānvīyata iti prakaraṇānugrahāya prakṛtāveva niveśaḥ । arthavādastu na prakaraṇa-
saṃbandhaṃ bādhituṃ kṣamaḥ । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu somāpekṣaivātra dīrghatā mantavyā</b> । <b>na latāpekṣeti</b>
etaccopalakṣaṇamātraṃ; yajamāno dīrgha ityetadupalakṣyate । evaṃ dīrghaśabdaḥ somasamānādhikaraṇo
bhavati, pravṛttiviśeṣakaraśca । <q>“ghṛtyai”</q> iti ca <b>nātirekādvinā arthavādopapattiriti</b> ।
somātirekeṇa vinā dāraṇāśaṅkābhāvāt nārthavāda upapadyate । tasmādadhikapradānāsu <b>saṃsthāsu</b>
niveśa <b>ityuktavān</b> । <b>nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe prakaraṇādutkarṣa</b> eva nityādhikārādutkarṣa eva
kāmyāsu saṃsthāsu niveśāt । <b>saṃsthā api hi vikārāḥ</b> iti saṃsthādhikaraṇe vakṣyate । pari-
<note>(1) P. 871</note> <note>(2) paśuprasak‍te</note>
﻿<pb n="r810"/>
harati---<b>yāgābhiprāyo'yamutkarṣaḥ</b> saṃsthāsvapyekatvādyāgasya । <b>kāryāpekṣayā</b> adhikāra-
niyogāpekṣayā tu <b>utkarṣa evetyadoṣaḥ</b> । <b>yatpunaridamuktaṃ sīsena krīṇāti itivadvikalpa iti</b>
bhāṣyamanubhāṣitam । dūṣaṇamāha---<b>nanu ca tatra samuccayo na vikalpaḥ <q>‘daśabhireva krīṇāti’</q>
iti</b> । etacca dvādaśe uktam । uttaraṃ---<b>vidhānavikalpamaṅgīkṛtyaitaddarśitam na prayoga---
vikalpam</b>। asyārthaḥ---yadi sīsena krīṇātīti krayavidhiḥ vāsasetyādayo guṇavidhayaḥ
yadi vāsasetyeva krayavidhiḥ itare guṇavidhaya iti vidhāne vikalpaḥ prayoge samuccaya eva ।
na nvekena vihite kathamanyena guṇavidhānaṃ, utpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarodhena karmāntarāpatteḥ । naitadevam ।
sannipatyopakārakāṇāṃ kāryaikyāvagame bhedābhāvāditi ।</p>
<p><b>saṃkhyāyuktaṃ kratoḥ prakaraṇāt syāt</b> । avāntarasaṅgatimāha---<b>vākyārthasamavāyā-
pekṣiṇī prakaraṇādutkarṣacintā gatā</b> । vākyārthasya yaḥ samavāyaḥ prakaraṇe samavetatā
tadapekṣiṇī prakaraṇādutkarṣacintā gatā, prakaraṇāntare vākyārthasya samavetatvāt । tatra
vākyārtha utkṛṣyata ityuktam । <b>idānīmabhidhānavipratipattirvākya eva cintyate---kimayaṃ
prathamaśabdo jyotiṣṭoma eva vartate uta jyotiṣṭomaprathamaprayoga iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---<q>‘na
prathamayajñe pravṛñjjāt’</q> iti prathamayajñe pravargyapratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate । tatra kiṃ prathamaśabdena
<note>(1) P. 876</note>
﻿<pb n="r811"/>
darśapūrṇamāsādiyajñāntarāpekṣayā jyotiṣṭoma evocyate tataśca jyotiṣṭomasya sarveṣu prayogeṣu na
pravrañjitavyam, uta jyotiṣṭomasyaiva prathamaprayogaḥ prayogāntarāpekṣayā ucyate । tena
tasminneva na pravrañjitavyam । itareṣu prayogeṣu pravargyeṇa bhavitavyamiti । pūrvapakṣamāha
<b>---<q>“eva vāva prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ”</q> iti śravaṇāt vispaṣṭaiva yajñārthavacanatā avagamyate</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---vispaṣṭaiva prathamaśabdasya jyotiṣṭomavacanatā'vagamyate yajñaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt ।
tasya ca prayojyavacanatvāt । bhavati ca jyotiṣṭomaḥ prathamo yajñaḥ <q>‘eṣa vāva prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ
yajjyotiṣṭoma”</q> iti śravaṇāt । atassarvasminnapi jyotiṣṭome na pravrañjitavyam । atra
bhāṣyaṃ <q>“evaṃ ca prakaraṇamanugrahīṣyate”</q> iti । tatra kadācit bhrāntiśīlasya pravargyavidhyabhi-
prāyo'yaṃ prakaraṇānugrha ucyate । sa ca prathamaprayogaviṣayepi pratiṣedhe ghaṭata eva । tasmāda-
sādhako'yaṃ pūrvapakṣasyeti bhrāntiḥ syāt । tāmapanetumāha---<b>pratiṣedhavidhyabhiprāyaṃ taditi</b> ।
yadi jyotiṣṭoma eva pratiṣedhaḥ syāt tadā prakaraṇamanugrahīṣyate sarvajyotiṣṭome pratiṣedha-
siddheḥ ।</p>
<p><b>naimittikaṃ vā</b> । <b>atrābhidhīyate---satyamasmāt prayogādavagamyate</b> । <q>‘eṣa vāva
prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ yajjyotiṣṭomaḥ’</q> ityasmāt prayogāt satyaṃ jyotiṣṭoma eva prathamo'vagamyate
na tadīyaprayogaḥ । kintu <b><q>“ya etenāniṣ‍ṭvā athānyena yajeta”</q> iti prayogādapi
prāthamyamavagamyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā eṣa vāveti prayogāt jyotiṣṭomasyaiva prāthamyamavagamyate
<note>(1) Bh. P. 876</note> <note>(2) ibid 877</note>
﻿<pb n="r812"/>
tathā ya etenetyetadālocanayā prayogāt prathamo na punaḥ svarūpeṇeti । kathaṃ ya etenetye-
tadālocanayā prayogāt prāthamyaṃ ? uttaraṃ---<b>kartṛsaṃbandhitayā śrūyamāṇatvāt</b> ya iti
śabdopāttakratusaṃbandhitayā śravaṇāt । tathāpi kimityāha---<b>kartṛśca prayogeṇa saṃbandho na
prayojyena</b> । prayogāṅgaṃ hi kartā na prayojyasya dravyadevatāmātrasādhyatvāt । sarvatra
karaṇādyeva kriyānupañjakaṃ antaraṅgatvāt kartā tu karaṇādi vyāparanneva 1kriyāyāṃ samavaitīti
mantavyam । tena prayogayogācca jyotiṣṭomasya prāthamyam । <b>1prayoge eva hi prathamaśabdaḥ</b>
śrautaḥ prayojye lākṣaṇikaḥ śrutilakṣaṇāviśaye ca śrutirādaraṇīyā । tena prathamaprayoga eva
pratiṣedhaḥ । <b>yuktyantaraṃ cāha---prayogapare vākye eṣa vāva prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ iti
śrutam</b> । asyārthaḥ---prayogaparametadvākyaṃ, jyotiṣṭomasya prathamaprayogaḥ kartavya iti vidhīyate
tatra ca <q>‘eṣa vāva’</q> iti śrutaṃ prayogaparameva vijñāyate । tenāyamartho bhavati---eṣa vai prathamo yajña-
prayogāṇāṃ yajjyotiṣṭomaprayogaḥ, ya etena jyotiṣṭomena prayogeṇāniṣ‍ṭvā anyena prayogeṇa
yajeta kartasyaiva āpattiḥ antaḥ jyāniṃ jīyate jyāniṃ yāti vā pramīyate mriyate vā iti ।
tena prayogasyaivedaṃ prāthamyaṃ na prayojyasya । tadāha---<b>na punaḥ prayojyaniṣṭhā । kvacidasya</b>
prathamaśabdasya <b>prayogo vidyate jyotiṣṭomasyaiva</b> । ataḥ <b>prayogavacana evāyaṃ</b> prathamaśabdaḥ ।
tenāyamartho bhavati <b>na prathamayajñaprayoge pravṛñjyāditi</b> । nanu ca yajñaśabdaḥ prayojyavacanaḥ
sa kathaṃ prayoge ghaṭiṣyate tatrāha---<b>yajñaśabdaḥ prayojyaviṣayatvāt prayogasya prayoge'pyupapadyata
eva</b> । prayojya eva prayogo bhavati । tena prayojyaśabdena vyapadeśo nānupapannaḥ । <b>tenaiṣa</b>
<note>(1) R. kriyayā</note>
﻿<pb n="r813"/>
<b>prathamaprayojyaḥ yajñānāmityarthaḥ</b> । <b>evaṃ ca prakaraṇa eva pravargyavidhirupapanno bhavati</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---kauṣītakribrāhmaṇe jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe <q>“purastādupasadāṃ pravargyeṇa pracaranti”</q> iti
pravargyavidhiḥ śrūyate । tatra yadi jyotiṣṭomaprayogamātre pratiṣedho bhavet tato vikalpa---
parihārāya prakaraṇāntaraṃ nīyate । tataḥ prakaraṇabādhaḥ । atha prakaraṇāvirodhāya tatraiva
avatiṣṭhate tato vikalpaḥ syāt । asmanmate tu naimittikatvāt pratiṣedhasya na kaścidviśeṣa
iti ।</p>
<p><b>pauṣṇaṃ peṣaṇaṃ vikṛtau</b> । <b>pauṣṇaṃ peṣaṇaṃ uttaravivakṣayetyuktam</b> । anenādhikaraṇa-
prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<p><b>tatsarvārthamaviśeṣāt</b> । <b>idamidānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ yāvatpauṣṇaṃ tatsarvaṃ prapiṣṭaṃ
kartavyaṃ uta carureveti</b> । <b>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī viśeṣāgrahaṇāt sarvārthamiti manyate</b>
carupaśupuroḍāśārthaṃ peṣaṇaṃ sarveṣāṃ pauṣṇatvāviśeṣāt । nanu ca puroḍāśe peṣaṇasya prāptatvāt
na śakyate vidhātum । uttaraṃ---<b>na, pauṣṇatayā aprāp‍teḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---satyaṃ svarūpeṇa
<note>(1) Bh. P. 880</note> <note>(2) Bh. P. 881</note>
﻿<pb n="r814"/>
peṣaṇaṃ prāptaṃ pauṣṇatayā na prāptam । 1tacca nāma na vidheyaṃ yat sarvātmanā prāptam । yat‍tu
kena ciccātmanā aprāptaṃ tadvidheyaṃ bhavatyeva tasmāt sarvārtham । <b>nanu ca</b> peṣaṇe kriyamāṇe
<b>hṛdayādyakṛtivināśaḥ paśau</b> । tataśca ākṛtināśaprasaṅgāt peṣaṇena na bhavitavyam ।
<b>uttaraṃ---bhavatu ākṛvināśaḥ peṣaṇavacanāt, kimiti vacanaṃ na kuryāt</b> । sarvaṃ kuryādi-
tyarthaḥ । atrocyate---<b>puroḍāśe tāvat</b> peṣaṇasya <b>prāptatvānna vidhiḥ</b> । <b>nanu pauṣṇatayā
'prāptirityuktam</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>kāryata eva prāptiriṣyate na saṃbandhitayā</b> । asyārthaḥ
---kāryārthaṃ padārthānāṃ prāptiriṣyate na punaḥ saṃbandhitvārtham । iha ca puroḍāśe yat
prakṛtivatpeṣaṇaṃ prāpta tenaiva kāryaṃ kṛtamiti na punaḥ peṣaṇasya kāryamasti । tataśca kāryābhāve
sati peṣaṇāntarasyānuṣṭhānābhāvāt na punarvidhānamavakalpate, anuṣṭhānaparyantatvādvidheḥ iti ।
<b>anyathā arthavādapadānāmapi kāryārthataiva syādityuktam</b> । yadi yasyāpi kāryaṃ nāsti tasyā-
pyanuṣṭheyatā, tadā arthavādapadānāmarthaḥ karaṇetikartavyatānanupraviṣṭo'pi kartavyaḥ syāt ।
<b>nanu caivaṃ sati prakaraṇādvākyaṃ dubalamityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---vākyāt puroḍāśepi
peṣaṇe prāpte yadi kāryābhāvāt puroḍāśepi peṣaṇaṃ na viniyujyate tadā prakaraṇādvākyaṃ
dubalamityuk‍taṃ bhavati । pratītānvayatyāgenāpi yadyanvayaḥ kalpyate tadā dvādaśopasattā
ahīnasyetyatrāpi kimityanvayo na kalpyata iti bhāvaḥ । <b>uttaraṃ---kārye sati anvayakalpa-
nā, ato balavattā uktā vākyasya</b> । yatra hi vākyāvagate'nvaye kāryalābhaḥ tatra vākyaṃ
<note>(1) G. tannām‍na vidheyam</note>
﻿<pb n="r815"/>
balīyaḥ । kāryaśūnye'nvaye na vākyāvagatānvayasvīkāraḥ । kiṃ tarhi anvayāntarakalpaneti ।
<b>tasmāt kāryābhāvāta puroḍāśe</b> peṣaṇasya <b>vidhānaṃ na saṃbhavati</b> । <b>paśau tarhi saṃbhavati
na hi, tatrāpi sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgāt śāstrasya</b> ākṛtibādhasāpekṣaṃ hi paśau vidhānam ।
<b>na ca nirapekṣe</b> caruviṣaye <b>saṃbhavati sāpekṣāśrayaṇaṃ yuktamiti uk‍taṃ śabdavidbhiḥ</b> ।
<b>tasmāccarāveva peṣaṇaṃ</b> kartavyamiti <b>śabdāt pratīmaḥ</b> । atra bhāṣyakāreṇa <q>“yadyapi tadā-
kṛtiḥ pratīyeta tathāpi utsādanadeśaṃ prati muhyeyuḥ”</q> ityuktam । tadanupapannam । piṣṭe hṛdayādau
punastadākṛtirna śakyate kartuṃ pāriṇāmikatvāttasyā, ityāśaṅkāmapanetumāha---<b>yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ
yadyapītatyādīnā bhāṣyeṇa tatraivamapi sāpekṣatvaṃ naiva śakyate parihartumityabhiprāyaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---satyapyākṛtisapādane pūrvārdhādikoddharaṇadeśabādhasāpekṣatvaṃ na nivartayituṃ śakyata
ityuktam । <b>anvārohamātraṃ caitat</b> । paramārthatastu ākṛtiḥ peṣaṇe kṛte naśyatyeveti
<b>pūrvamevok‍to hetirityarthaḥ</b> । <b>nanu carāvapi carutaiva hīyeta viśadasiddhaudane caruśabda-
prayogāt</b> । na ca piṣṭamaya odano bhavati । uttaraṃ---na carutā hīyeta <b>piṣṭakacarāvapi
paktisāmānyāditi</b> । paktivacanatvāccaruśabdasyetye<b>vamabhihitaḥ</b> peṣaṇepi sati
<b>caruśabdaprayogaḥ</b> । upasaṃharati---<b>tasmāccarāveva peṣaṇamiti siddham</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) Bh. P. 882</note>
﻿<pb n="r816"/>
<p><b>ekasminnekasaṃyogāt</b> । nanu caikadevatāke vihito dharmo na dvidevatāke saṃbhavati
caturdhākaraṇavat indrapītamantravacca tatrāha---<b>atra bhāṣyakāreṇa indrapītāg‍neyaśabdābhyāṃ viśeṣo
darśitaḥ pūṣā prapiṣṭabhāgo bhavatīti yathā adantako hīti hetuvacanaṃ somāpauṣṇe nema-
piṣṭaścaruḥ iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---prapiṣṭaṃ bhajatīti prapiṣṭabhāk pūṣocyate sa ca dvidevatākepi
yadi peṣaṇaṃ syāt tadā prapiṣṭabhāka‍bhavati iti । anyathā na prapiṣṭabhāgo bhavet tathā
adantako hīti hetuvacanaṃ pūṣanimittakaṃ peṣaṇaṃ darśayati somāpauṣṇo nemapiṣṭaścaruḥ ityatra nemapiṣṭatā
'nūdyate । sā ca pūṣamātranimitte peṣaṇe'vakalpate <b>somāpauṣṇacaruvidhau nemapiṣṭa ityanuvāda
eva yuktaḥ; nemapiṣṭavidhāne hi somāpauṣṇasya lakṣaṇāt taduddeśena carurityavivakṣitaṃ syāt
ityevamādyadhikāśaṅkānirākaraṇārthamidamadhikaraṇam</b> । <b>atrocyate---kathamāsāmāśaṅkānāṃ
nirākaraṇaṃ</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>kāryaprayuktatvāddharmāṇāmityukto hetuḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---kārya-
prayuktā dharmāḥ kārye asaṃbhavantaḥ tatsaṃbaddhe yāge'vakalpante । tataśca pūṣā prapiṣṭabhāga iti
vacanāt pūṣalakṣite yāge devatāvidhiravasīyate । devatātvena hi puṣā yāgaṃ lakṣayituṃ śak‍noti
saṃbandhasya lakṣakatvāt । na ca dvidevatāke pūṣṇo devatābhāvassaṃbhavati । tena tatra
dharmavidhiranyāyyaḥ । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ kāryeṇa saṃbandho devatāpadayuk‍tānāṃ bhavati</b> । uttaraṃ
<note>(1) P. 883</note>
﻿<pb n="r817"/>
---<b>niṣprayojanatvāddevatāyāḥ</b> । nanvevaṃ yāgepi saṃbandho na syādityāha---<b>kāryārthatvācca
yāgasya</b> kāryaprayuk‍taṃ pauṣṇa lakṣaṇayopapadyate devatayā yāgo lakṣyate । <b>devatā cedupalakṣaṇam na
dvidevatāke pūṣā lakṣayituṃ kṣamaḥ</b> । <b>adevatā hi sa pūṣā tatra</b> dvidevatāke karmaṇi ।
<b>adantakatvādīnāṃ tu hetuvannigadatvenārthavādatvamuktam</b> । <b>arthavādāśca guṇavādena vyākhyātāḥ
nemapiṣṭasya ca nyāyāpetatvāt</b> nyāyate'prāptatvāt <b>dvidevatāke</b> peṣaṇasya viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ
bhaviṣyati । <b>tasmādekadevatākeṣu caruṣu peṣaṇamiti siddham</b> ।</p>
<trailer>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="r818"/>
<head>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</head>
<head>tṛtoyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>nivītam</b> । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ vidhinātvekavākyatvāt stutyarthena vidhināmiti
sthite'rthavādatve punarvidhānāśaṅkā</b> । <b>ekavākyatve hi na vidhidvayamavakalpata iti na
nivītatvādividhisambhavaḥ</b> । <b>pākṣikīṃ prāptiṃ manvāno vidhiṃ manyata iti cet</b> । artha-
vādo hi <b>anuvādatayā</b> । na ca nivītādi nityaprāptam । ataḥ pakṣe'nuvādasyāpyanupapatteḥ
vidhirāśrayaṇīya iti । <b>tadapyayuktam</b> । <q>‘prāyādi’</q>tyanena parihṛtatvāt । prāyikīmapi
prāptimāśrityārthavādo bhavatītyuk‍taṃ prāyāt ityanena sūtreṇa । yathā <q>“anūtavādinīvāk iti,
prācīnāvītamiti vidhānaṃ aprāptatvāt । tatsaṃyogādidamapi vidhīyata iti cet ‘prācīnāvītaṃ
pitṛṇāṃ”</q> iti pakṣe'pi na prāptam । atastadvidheyam । taccedvidhīyate vākyaṃ bhinnaṃ tāvadāśritam
tataśca nivītamapi vidhīyata iti । <b>tadayuktam---tasyāpi vacanāntareṇa prāptatvāt upapadyata
evārthavādaḥ</b> । evamākṣip‍te samarthayate---<b>prakaraṇāṅgatayā'prāptiṃ manvānena idamadhikaraṇa---
mārabdham</b> । prakaraṇasyāṅganiyogasya aṅgatayā pakṣe'pi prāp‍tyabhāvāt prāyāt ityanena
nyāyenārthavādatvānupapatteḥ nivītaṃ vidhīyata iti manvānenedamadhikaraṇamārabdham । rāddhāntamāha
---<b>vidhānepi prakaraṇāṅgatā na saṃbhavatīti sthitamarthavādatvam</b> । yadyapi vidhīyate tathāpi
<note>(1)P. 889</note>
﻿<pb n="r819"/>
manuṣyāṇāmiti śravaṇāt svatantrādhikārāpatteḥ prakaraṇāṅgatā na saṃbhavati । kintu puruṣadharmatā
puruṣadharmaścet prāyādityupapadyata evārthavādaḥ । <b>nanu cātithyādāvaprāptirvidyata iti yuk‍taṃ</b>
vidhānaṃ manuṣyāṇāmiti śravaṇe satyapi manuṣyapradhāne ātithye karmaṇi ekāntato'prāptatvāt
kimiti vidhānaṃ na saṃbhavatīti । <b>na</b> । <b>tadanvayānavagamāt</b> । ātithyakarmānvayo nāvagamyate ।
api tu manuṣyamātrānvaya eva । sa ca prāyādibhiḥ arthavādātayopapadyata iti siddhamanuvādatvam ।
tadāha---manuṣyamātrasaṃbandhitāyāṃ tu prāyādibhirupapadyata ityarthavādataiveti siddham ।</p>
<p><b>digvibhāgaḥ</b> । <b>paruṣiditam</b> । <b>tadvadityatideśaḥ kimabhyadhikaṃ paśyataḥ</b> ?
uttaraṃ---<b>anyathā hyupavīte prāptiḥ anyathā ca dikṣu anyathā ca paruṣidinādiṣu iti viśeṣa-
pratipādanārtho'yamatideśaḥ</b> । pūrvapakṣasiddhāntau tāveva । kintvarthavādavarṇanāya prāptirva-
ktavyā । sā ca k‍vacana kathaṃ cidityadhikaraṇabhedaḥ ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 898-899</note>
﻿<pb n="r820"/>
<p><b>akarmakratusaṃyuktam</b> । <b>uktaṃ nivītādhikaraṇena kratudharmatayā nivītādi pratīyate
manuṣyādiśravaṇāditi prāyeṇa prāptatvādanuvāda iti</b> । idānīṃ nānṛta vadet <b>ityatrāpi
tadvadevānuvādaṃ manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । anenāvasarasaṅgatiṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ cāha । arthastu
nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ iti śruteḥ na kratudharmatayā nivītādi pratīyate । api tu puruṣadharmatayā
puruṣadharmaścet prāyeṇa puruṣārthatayā nivītādiprāpteḥ anuvāda iti nivītādhikaraṇe uktam ।
idānīṃ nānṛtaṃ vadeta iti pratiṣedhasyānuvādaṃ manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । codayatiḥ---<b>nanu ca tatra
manuṣyaśabdaśravaṇāt</b> puruṣamātrasaṃbandhāvagateḥ kratudharmatayā saṃbandhānavagateśca <b>yukto'nuvādaḥ
prāyikīṃ ca prāptimāśrityārthavādaḥ</b> । iha tu puruṣaśabdāśravaṇāt na puruṣārthatā'vagamyate । api
tu prakaraṇāt kratvarthataivāvagamyate । na ca kratusaṃbandhitayā prāptirasti iti nānuvādo ghaṭate । pari-
harati---<b>atrāpi pūrvaprāptapratiṣedhānuvādāt gamyata eva pumān yasyāsau pratiṣedhaḥ</b> । <b>atrāpi</b>
‘nānṛtaṃ vadet iti । yasyāsau smārtaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ sa pumān adhikāritayā'vagamyata eva । kutaḥ ?
pūrvaprāptasya pratiṣedhasyānuvādāt । tatra ca puruṣasyādhikārasmaraṇāt । nanu nāyaṃ pratiṣedhānuvādo
ghaṭate । tatra pratyavāyaparihārārthino'vikārāt । iha ca prakaraṇāṅgatayā niradhikāratvāditi tatrāha
---<b>sarvatra pratiṣedhaśās‍tre hi pratiṣidhyamānakriyākarturevādhikāraḥ</b> iti । asyārthaḥ
<note>(1) Bh. P. 900</note>
﻿<pb n="r821"/>
---na smārte pratiṣedhe pratiṣidhyamānakriyānuṣṭhānanibandhanapratyavāyaparihārārthino'dhikāraḥ
pramāṇābhāvāt । na hi niṣiddhā kriyā pratyavāyaṃ janayatīti kiñcana pramāṇamasti । nanu ca
pratiṣedhaśāstrameva pramāṇaṃ, kathaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ ? pratyavāyaṃ vinā nivṛttyanupapatteriti cenna;
1adhikārāvagamana eva nivṛtterupapannatvāt । <b>nanvadhikāro na śrayate</b>। satyamarthāt bhaviṣyati
dravyārjananiyamavat । yo hi yatra pravṛttaḥ saḥ tataḥ nivartayitavyaḥ, nānyaḥ ityarthādeva
pravṛttimānadhikārī labdha iti sādhūk‍taṃ---<b>sarvatra pratiṣedhaśāstre pratiṣidhyamānakriyākarturevā-
dhikāra iti</b> । ihāpi ca pratiṣidhyamānakriyākartuḥ anṛtavadanapratiṣedhaḥ anyasya pratiṣedhānu-
papatterityarthaḥ । <b>ataḥ pūrvaprāptasyaiva</b> pratiṣedhasyāya<b>manuvādaḥ</b> । nanu ca kratvarthatayaivānṛta-
vadanaprāptiriti pratiṣedho'pi tadartha eva yuktaḥ । na hi anyārthe pravṛtto'nyārthe niyok‍tuṃ
śakyata iti tatrāha---<b>vidyate ca prāptirarthataḥ</b> । anṛtavadanasya arthataḥ prāptirvidyata
eva । kratvarthatayāpi puruṣasya <b>prāptimātratayā ca</b> <b>puruṣasya pratiṣedhopapatteḥ na
prakaraṇārthatā</b> । yadi ca kratvarthāyāmeva prāptau pratiṣedha upapadyate na puruṣārthāyāṃ tadā
kratvarthaprāptipratiṣedhaḥ2 kratvarthaḥ syāt । na caitadasti prāptimātrādapi pratiṣedhopapatteḥ ।
<b>nanu cāyamanuvādaḥ kasya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ</b> ? ayamāśayaḥ । vidhiparatayā prāmāṇyamuktam ।
tatra vidhyuddeśasya kāryānvayitayā vidhiparatvam । arthavādapadānāṃ tu stutiparatayā pratītyanvayi-
tayā । anuvādastu na sākṣādvidhiparaḥ । teta vaktavyametat kasya vidheḥ śeṣa iti
anyathā vidhiparatvābhāvāt । uttaraṃ---<b>na kasyaciditi brūmaḥ</b> । vidhyantareṇaikavākyatvā-
bhāvāt na kasyacidapi vidherayamanuvādaḥ śeṣaḥ । yadi vidhyantaraṃ nānupraviśati nivītavat
tarhi kathamanuvādaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>prātiranuvādatve hetuḥ nārthavādatā</b> । yadi hi arthavādatā
<note>(1) G. anadhi</note> <note>(2) R. pratiṣedhāt ।</note>
﻿<pb n="r822"/>
anuvādatve hetuḥ syāt tadā vidhyantarānupraveśaṃ vinā'rthavādānupapatteḥ anuvādo vidhyantaraśeṣaḥ
syāt । kintu prāptiranuvādatve hetuḥ nārthavādatā । yadyayaṃ prāptārtha eva kimiti tarhi
nivītavadevārthavādo na bhavati । tatrāha---<b>ekavākyatvena hi arthavādo bhavati na prāpti-
mapekṣate, yathā <q>‘jārtilayavāgvā vā juhuyāt’</q> iti</b> । jartilayavāguhomo hi yadyapi na prāptaḥ
tathāpi <q>‘payasāgnihotraṃ juhoti’</q> ityanenaikavākyatvāt arthavādatvena vyākhyāyate । tena
anuvādaḥ prāptimātrāpekṣaḥ । arthavādastu ekavākyatāmātrāpekṣa iti vivekaḥ । anṛdyamāna-
vidhiparatayā vidhisaṃspṛṣṭatā'nuvādānāmiti na kiñcidapi hīnam । tasmādanuvādaḥ ।
<b>nanu cedaṃ śrutivākyaṃ tasyāḥ smṛtermūlaṃ bhaviṣyati</b> । yadi śrutivākyasya smṛtivākyasya
ca samānārthatvenānuvādo'yamucyate tarhi tasyāḥ smṛteḥ mūlamapekṣamāṇāyāḥ idameva śrutivākyaṃ
mūlaṃ bhaviṣyati iti kathamanuvādatā । uttaraṃ---<b>na bhavitumarhati atra hi śruyamāṇasyārthasya
prakaraṇārthatāvasīyate na puruṣārthatvam</b> । <b>anuvādapakṣe punaḥ puruṣārthatayaiva prāpteḥ siddhā
puruṣārthatā bhavati</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyetadvākyaṃ mūlaṃ bhavet tadā anṛtavadanapravṛttapuruṣa-
saṃbandhinyapi pratiṣedhe adhikārī kalpayitavyaḥ syāt । tataśca kalṛptādhikāreṇādhikāravidhinaiva
gṛhyeta vidhinaiva sannidhānāt । tataśca prakaraṇārthatā prakṛtādhikāraniyogārthatā asya pratiṣedhasya ।
smṛteśca puruṣārthatā bhavatīti na tasyāḥ pratiṣedhavidhirmūlatāṃ gantumarhatīti । anuvāde tu puruṣa-
saṃbandhini pratiṣedhe'vagate1 tasya klṛptādhikāratvāta adhikārāntarakalpanāvakāśo nāsti । tena
prakaraṇena na gṛhyate । adhikārakalpanāyāṃ hi prasṛtāyāṃ klṛptādhikāraḥ prakaraṇavidhirgṛhṇāti
na svabalalabdhādhikāre puruṣārthatayaiva prāpte pratiṣedhe svatantrādhikārārthatayaivetyarthaḥ । <b>nanu ca</b>
<note>(1) G. vagamyate</note>
﻿<pb n="r823"/>
<b>kratvarthatayaivāvagamyamānasya kathaṃ puruṣārthatayā'nuvādo yuktaḥ kalpayitum</b> । asyārthaḥ
---tvayā etaduk‍taṃ yadi mūlabhūtamidaṃ bhavet tataḥ kratvarthaṃ bhavatīti । evaṃ ca vadatā
kratvarthānṛtavadanapravṛttirniṣidhyata ityuktam । anyathā kathaṃ nāma vidhāyakatve kratvarthatā bhavet ।
yadā caivaṃ tadā kathaṃ kratvarthapravṛttipratiṣedho'yaṃ puruṣārthatayānuvadituṃ śakyata iti । <b>ucyate
---kraturapi hi puruṣārtha eva</b> । <b>atastatsaṃbandhitayāpi puruṣasyecchātaḥ prāp‍notyevānṛta-
vadanamityadoṣaḥ tatsaṃbandhāvagateriti</b> । asyārthaḥ---kratvarthā yā puruṣapravṛttiḥ sāpi
puruṣasaṃbandhinī bhavatyeva । tena tatpratiṣedhopi puruṣārtho yukta eva । yasmāt kraturapi
puruṣārtha eva । ataḥ kratusaṃpattyarthamapi puruṣasyaivānṛtavadanaṃ rāgataḥ prāp‍notyevetyadoṣaḥ kratu-
saṃbandhāvagateḥ । tenāyamartho bhavati darśapūrṇamāsanirvṛttyarthamanṛtaṃ na vadediti । sarvaṃ ca
puruṣārthamanṛtavadanaṃ pratiṣiddhamiti । ataścānuvādopapattiḥ । <b>upanayanottarakālabhāvitvācca
kratūnāṃ siddho'nuvādaḥ</b> । yadi kratavaḥ upanayanottarakālā na bhaveyuḥ tadā smārtānāmapi
padārthānāṃ vaidikatvāt upanayanottarakālabhāvitvācca vaidikeṣu padārtheṣu adhikārasya prāgupanayanāt
pratiṣedhābhāvāt nāyamanuvādaḥ syāt । tene kratavaḥ upanayanottarakālabhāvina iti
siddho'nuvādaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>vidhirvā saṃyogāntarāt</b> । <b>atrābhidhīyate---āyuṣmataivok‍taṃ na smṛtivākya-
syedaṃ mūlatāṃ pratipadyata iti</b> । <b>evaṃ cet tvayaivedaṃ saṃyogāntaramuktam</b> । <b>saṃyogā</b>-
<note>(1) P. 911</note>
﻿<pb n="r824"/>
<b>ntaratve ca nānuvādaḥ śakyate vak‍tum</b> । asyārthaḥ---svatastāvadidaṃ vākyaṃ prakaraṇāṅgabhūta-
pratiṣedhasamarpakam । ata eva ca smṛternamūlatāṃ gatam । evaṃ cedantaraṅgakratvarthatāṃ parityajya na
vākyāntarālocanayā anūdyatayā pratiṣedho'vatiṣṭhate । <b>nanu ca pratiṣedhe sarvatra pratiṣidhyamāna-
kriyākarturevādhikāra ityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---anadhikāraṃ hi sādhikāramanupraviśati । sādhi-
kāraścāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ pratiṣidhyamānakriyākarturevādhikārāvagamāt । <b>satyamuk‍taṃ na tu tatprakaraṇe
śakyate vak‍tuṃ</b>, niṣidhyamānakriyākartā hi nādhikāritayā śrūyate । kiṃ tarhi ? arthāt
kalpyate । na ca klṛpte'dhikāre saṃbhavati sannihite adhikārāntarakalpanāvakalpate । <b>kimiti</b>
prakaraṇopi niṣidhyamānakriyākarturevādhikāro na bhavati ? uttaraṃ---<b>padārthamātra eva pratiṣe-
dhopapatteḥ</b> । anṛtavadane <b>padārthamātra</b> eva icchādhīnapravṛttinirapekṣepi <b>pratiṣedhopapatteḥ</b> ।
etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---prakaraṇe hi prakaraṇasaṃbandhaiva pravṛttiḥ pratīyate । tataśca tanmukhenādhikārānu-
praveśe klṛpte nārthādadhikārāntarakalpanopapadyate । <b>laukikeṣu punaḥ puruṣecchāta eva pravṛtti-
rviṣayatāṃ pratiṣedhasya pratipadyata iti tatkriyākarturevādhikāro yuktaḥ</b> । <b>iha punaḥ
kratvarthatayaiva pravṛttiravagamyate padārthasyeti na tasya karturadhikāraḥ śakyate vak‍tuṃ iti</b> ।
<b>nanu ca kartaivākhyāteṣu pradhānatayā'vagamyate</b> । anenedamāha svavākya eva viṣayaniyo-
jyānvitaniyogapratipādanāt nādhikārānupraveśe yukta iti । tathā hi---nañarthaḥ vidhiviṣayaḥ,
anṛtavadanakartā cādhikārī, kartṛvācitāśaṅkā cākhyātānāṃ pāṇiniprabhṛtīnāṃ yathāśrutavacana-
bodhananibandhanā । nanvevaṃ tarhi prayājādīnāmapyaṅgatā na syāt । teṣvapi kartṛśravaṇāt
