<section>
<pb n="r825"/>
svatantrādhikāraprasak‍terityatrāha---<b>niyogābhedāt‍tu prayājādīnāmaṅgatvamavagamyate । sarveṣā-
mekaphalānubandhatvāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---prayājādiṣu kartaiva kevalaṃ śrūyate na tadviśeṣaṇam ।
prayājādaya eva yadi kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ na tarhi viṣayaḥ । atha viṣayaḥ na tarhi kartā viśeṣyate ।
tataśca kathamaviśiṣṭo'dhikārībhavet ? tasmātteṣāṃ pṛthagadhikāraniyogābhāvāt ekaniyogānupraveśāt
aṅgatvasiddhiḥ । <b>saṃskārakarmaṇāmapi kratvarthasya saṃskāryatayā'vagateḥ yuk‍taivāṅgatā</b> ।
teṣvapi viṣayaniyojyaviśeṣānvayānavagateḥ na svatantrādhikārāpattiḥ । saṃskāryadravyādidvāreṇa
kratuśeṣatvāvirodhaḥ । <b>pratiṣedhe punaḥ pratiśedhyasya akratvarthatvāt ākhyātena ca
karturabhidhānāt karturevādhikāraḥ pratīyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi kila nānūtaṃ vadedityanṛta-
vadanamātraṃ śabdādavagamyate tathāpi yadi vākye'dhikāro na śrūyate tadā prakaraṇagatamanṛtavadanaṃ
pratīyate । yadā punaḥ svavākya evādhikārī viṣayaśca labdhaḥ tadā anṛtavadanamapi svatantrameva
pratīyate । tenākhyātena karturabhidhānāt pratiṣedhasya cākratvarthatvāt karturevādhikāraḥ
adhikārāntarānupraveśe kāraṇābhāvāt । svavākye cādhikāraśravaṇāt ।</p>
<p>evaṃ tāvat vidhisyaṃ puruṣārthaśceti darśitam । saṃprati abhyupagamyāpi kratvarthānṛtavadana-
pratītiṃ anuvādo'yamiti darśayati---<b>na ca tatsaṃbandhāvagatiḥ</b> kratvarthasaṃbandhānṛtavadanāvagatiḥ
svatantrādhikārepi viruddhā । <b>kratorapi puruṣārthatvāt upanayanottarakālabhāvitvācca tadartha-
pravṛtteḥ siddho'nuvāda ityuktam</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---kratvarthānṛtavadanapratiṣedho'pi
svatantrādhikārapuruṣārthasarvānṛtavadanapratiṣedhasyaiva smārtasyānuvāda iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r826"/>
<p><b>atrocyate---syādetadevaṃ yadyākhyātānāṃ kartā'bhidheyaḥ syāt na tvākhyātānāṃ
kartrabhidhānaśaktiḥ śakyate kalpayitum । kriyābhidhānādeva sarvakārakavagateḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---tatra hi śabdasya śaktiḥ kalpyate yasya nānyato'vagatiḥ । sarvāṇi
ca kārakāṇi kriyayaivākṣipyante tairvinā kriyānupapatteḥ । <b>kathaṃ tarhi pāṇineḥ sūtraṃ
laḥ karmaṇi ca bhāve cākarmakebhya iti</b> ? । tathā kathamiyaṃ vṛttiḥ cakārāt
kartariceti । evaṃ vadatoḥ sūtravṛttikārayoḥ kārakābhidhāyino lakārā iti bhāvo
lakṣyate । pariharati---<b>saṅkhyāvidhānārthametaditi darśitam</b> । karmasaṅkhyā kartṛsaṅkhyā ca
vācyatvena vidhīyete na kartā karma cetyarthaḥ1 । karmakartṛbhyāṃ tu tatsaṅkhyā lakṣyate । kathaṃ tarhi
<q>“karmavācini sārvadhātuke yak”</q> <q>‘kartari śap’</q> iti vṛttikārāḥ paṭhanti tatrāha---<b>saṅkhyā-
viśeṣavidhānāśrayaṃ ca yak śab iti ca</b> । atrāpi karmakartṛsaṅkhyāviśeṣābhidhānamāśritya
yak śap iti cānuśāsanam । tenātrāpi na kārakābhidhānamākhyātānāmiti । yadi
kriyākṣiptakarmakartṛsaṅkhyā'bhidhīyate tadā---<b>anyakārakasaṅkhyābhidhānaṃ kimiti na bhavati ?
tulye gamyamānatve</b> । karaṇādisaṅkhyāpi kimiti nākhyātenocyata ityarthaḥ । pariharati---<b>na
lokaḥ paryanuyok‍tuṃ śakyate</b> । kasmādityāha---<b>durjayo hi mahājanaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---kiṃ
vaye kurmaḥ karmakartṛsaṅkhyāmeva loko yadi vadet na karaṇādisaṅkhyām । nanu mānāma loko
vadatu pāṇiniḥ kimiti na smarati tatrāha---laukikaprayogamūlaṃ cedaṃ śāstraṃ bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ
<note>(1) G. karmakartṛsaṅkhyā viśeṣavidhānārthaṃ vācyatvena bidhīyate kartetyarthaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r827"/>
kasmādityāha---<b>prayuk‍tasya hi niyamamācaṣṭe nāprayuk‍tasyābhidhānam । tasmādaparyanuyo-
go'yam</b> । upasaṃharati---<b>ataḥ kratvarthapadārthamātrapravṛttyāśrayamevedaṃ pratiṣedhaśāstram</b> ।
kratvarthatayā padārthamātre anṛtavadane'dhikāravidhivākyārthasaṃbandhena yā pravṛttiḥ tadāśrayamevedaṃ pratiṣedha-
śāstram । <b>nanu ca pratiṣedhyagatā pravṛttiḥ na kratvarthesyuk‍tam । acoditatvāt</b> । na
hi kratvarthatayā'nṛtavadanaṃ coditaṃ; acoditaṃ ca nāṅgamiti nānṛtavadane kratvarthā pravṛttiḥ ।
uttaraṃ---<b>naiva tādarthyena coditatvaṃ saṃbandhahetuḥ upakārakatayāpi saṃbandhitā upapadyata eva</b> ।
yadyapi tādarthyena codanā nāsti tathāpyupakārakatayā saṃbandho'nṛtavadanasya kratunā sahāstyeva ।
<b>saṃbandhini ca vidhiḥ kratvartho bhavatītyuk‍taṃ payo vrataṃ brāhmaṇasyetvevamādiṣu</b> । yadyapi
bhojanaṃ kratvarthatayā na vihitaṃ tathāpi tasya kratorupakārakatvena tadāśritaṃ payo bhavatyeva kratvarthaṃ
evaṃ upakārakānṛtavadanapratiṣedho'pi kratvartho bhaviṣyatīti । <b>nanu copakārakaviṣayatayā
pratiṣedhasya kratvarthapuruṣārthayorna kaścidviśeṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi tāvadaṅgabhūtamanṛtavadanaṃ
bhavet tadā puruṣārthena pratiṣedhena pratiṣeda‍dhumaśakyatvāt prayojanavāneva kratvarthaḥ pratiṣedho bhavet
vikalpārthaḥ । yadā arthaprāptasya pratiṣedhaḥ tadā puruṣārthena pratiṣedhena pratiṣedhasiddheḥ kiṃ
kratvarthena pratiṣedheneti । uttaraṃ---<b>yathāsti viśeṣaḥ tathok‍tam</b> । kratvarthe pratiṣedhe tadati-
krame katorvaiguṇyāt tannivṛttaye śrautaṃ prāyaścittam । puruṣārthe ca pratiṣedhe tadatikrame puruṣasya
vaiguṇyāt tadapanayāya smārtaṃ prāyaścittamiti viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r828"/>
<p><b>ahīnavatpuruṣadharmastadarthatvāt</b> । <b>kaḥ punaḥ nivīsaṃ manuṣyāṇāmityanena viśeṣaḥ
jañjabhyamānasyeti</b> ? anena pūrvapakṣamākṣipati । <q>‘jañjabhyamāno brūyānmayidakṣakratū’</q> iti
yadyapi jañjabhyamānasaṃbandhitayā mantravacanaṃ śrūyate tathāpi nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāmitivat kimiti
na prakaraṇa eva niviśate nivītamapi । nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāmiti manuṣyasaṃbandhitayā śrūyate
atha ca prakaraṇa eva niviśate tathedamapi kasmānna bhavatītyarthaḥ । <b>ayamasti viśeṣaḥ
nārthavādāt parihāraḥ saṃbhavati avākyaśeṣatvāta</b> । yathā <q>‘nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ’</q> iti
upavyayata ityasya vākyaśeṣatvādarthavādatayā prakaraṇa evānvīyate na tathā jañ‍jabhyamāno brūyā-
dityasyānvayaḥ vidhyantareṇaikavākyatvabhāvāt । nanu ca vākyaśeṣatvābhāvāt mābhūdarthavādaḥ
anuvādastu bhavatu pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣe nānṛtaṃ vadeditivat tatrāha--<b>nāpyanuvādo nānṛtaṃ vadedi-
tivat</b> jañ‍jabhyamānasaṃbandhitayā mantravacanasya anyato'prāpteḥ । <b>nāpyarthaprāptasya viṣayatva-
saṃbhavaḥ nānṛtaṃ vadet itivat</b> । yadi kratāvevārthaprāptā jañ‍jabhyamānatā mantravidherviṣayo
bhavet yathā nānṛtaṃ vadedityasyārthaprāptamanutavadanaṃ tadā kratusaṃbandhijṛmbhaṇamukhena kratusaṃbandhāvagateḥ
kratvartho mantravidhiḥ syāt । na caitadasti । kutaḥ ? <b>na hi jañjabhyamānatā kadācidapi
kratvarthatayā prāpnoti anṛtavadanavat</b> । <b>tasmāt jañjabhyamānasya mantravidhānamidaṃ na prakaraṇe
'vasthāpayituṃ śakyate</b> । svavākya evānupādeyajṛmbhaṇaviśiṣṭasyādhikāriṇo mantravacanasya
<note>(1) P. 944</note>
﻿<pb n="r829"/>
viṣayasya ca lābhe prakaraṇānupraveśe kāraṇābhāvāt । <b>nanu caivaṃ sati phalakalpanā syāt</b> ।
adhikārāntarakalpanā syādityarthaḥ । <b>bhavatu vacanāt, ko doṣaḥ</b> ? vācanike'dhikārāntare
doṣa iti । <b>ato vākyāt prakaraṇabādhaḥ siddhaḥ yathā dvādaśopasattā ahīnasya iti</b> ।
<b>atrocyate na phalakalpanāmarhatyetadvākyam</b> । idamatrākūtam । jañ‍jabhyamānasambandhitayā
mantravacanaṃ pratīyate । tatra kimidamadhikārāntaraṃ jañ‍jabhyamānaśabdaścādhikāriviśeṣasamarpako
bhavatu uta prakṛta eva kartā jañ‍jabhyamānaśabdena na nirdiśyatāṃ tasya jṛmbhaṇanimittotpannavyalau-
kapraśamanadvāreṇa mantravacanaṃ saṃskārakamiti saṃśaye klṛpte prakṛte kārye sati na kalpanopapadyata
iti nādhikārāntarakalpanā nyāyyeti jañ‍jabhyamānaḥ saṃskāryatayaivānvayaṃ yātīti । tadida-
mākūtaṃ vivarītukāmaḥ pṛcchati---<b>kutaḥ</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>vākyaṃ hi padārthasaṃbandhamātre prabhavati
na kārye</b> । <b>vākyato hi padārthānāṃ</b> saṃbandhāvagatireva, nāsti jañ‍jabhyamānasaṃyogaḥ saṃskārya-
tayāpi । kartṛbhāvenaiva kartṛbhūta evānena mantravacanena saṃskriyate । kutastarhi kāryāvagama
ityatrāha---<b>kāryaṃ hi niyogasamadhigamyameva</b> । sarvaṃ hi niyogārthaṃ tena niyogārthānumataṃ
yat tat kāryam । ata eva ca saktvādiṣu vibhaktivyatyayaḥ । bhavatvevaṃ niyogataḥ kāryam
tathāpi kimityāha---<b>prakṛtaścāyaṃ dārśapūrṇamāsiko niyogaḥ</b> । tena prakṛtena grahaṇe sati
tada‍grahaṇānuguṇaṃ kāryaṃ kalpayitavyamiti prakṛtakartṛsaṃskāraka evāyam । yadi prakṛtenāpi
niyogena na gṛhyeta tadā na padārthamātrasaṃbandhāvasāyyeva vākyaṃ bhavet kintu kāryāvasāyyeva ।
<b>sarvamevedaṃ viniyogakāraṇam</b> । nanu bhavatu prakṛto niyogaḥ tathāpi sa eva kāryamiti
nāsti pramāṇaṃ, yena tadvalena tadanuguṇaṃ kāryaṃ kalpyeta ityata āha---<b>na ca kāryāntarakalpanā</b>
﻿<pb n="r830"/>
<b>klṛp‍te sati saṃbhavati iti prakaraṇa eva niveśaḥ । nanu ca jañjabhyamānatā na kratvartha-
tayā'nṛtavadanavat saṃbhavatītyuktam</b> । tena kathaṃ kratvanupraveśaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>mābhūt
jañjabhyamānatā kratvarthā । kartustu kratvarthatā prakaraṇasaṃbandhaheturbhaviṣyati । tasmāt kratoḥ
kartuḥ dharmo'yamiti siddham । ahīne punaḥ kāryatvāt yuktaḥ utkarṣaḥ</b> । ahīne
tatsaṃbandhitvena yo'dhikāraniyogassaṃbandhī pratīyate sa kāryabhūta iti svavākye kāryāvagamādyukta
utkarṣaḥ dvādaśoṣasattāyāḥ । iha tu jañ‍jabhyamānamātrasambandhena na kāryasaṃbandho'vagamyata iti
kalpye kārye klṛptāśrayaṇaṃ nyāyyamiti viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>śaṃyau ca sarvaparidānāt</b> । <q>‘na brāhmaṇāyāvaguret’</q> iti prakaraṇa eva pratiṣedho
niviśate prakaraṇādhītatvāt, arthācca kratusaṃbandhitayā aprāpteranṛtavadanavaditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntamāha--<b>śaṃyau punaḥ śatena yātayāditi phalaśruterna prakaraṇasaṃbandhakalpanā nyāyyā
svavākyasthā hi kāryāvagatirbalīyasī</b> । yadi svavākye phalaṃ nāvagamyeta tadā prakṛtā-
vikārānupraveśenānuṣṭhānasiddheḥ kāryāntaraṃ na kalpyeta, aṅgameva syāt । iha tu svavākye
phalamavagamyate śatayātanādiparihāraḥ । svavākyasthā hi kāryāvagatiḥ śreyasī, antaraṅgatvāt
<note>(1) P. 949</note>
﻿<pb n="r831"/>
tasmāt puruṣamātradharmo'yaṃ <q>‘na brāhmaṇāyāvaguret’</q> iti । <b>nanu ca jañ‍jabhyamānepi<q>‘prāṇā-
pānāvevātmandhatte’</q> iti phalaśravaṇamastyeva</b> । paraharati-<b>na, dhatta iti vartamānopadeśāt
sādhyatayā nāvagamyate</b> phalam । atastadadhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ na bhavati vartamānatvādeva ।
yatkhalu bhāviphalaṃ tanniyogasya sādhyatvayogyatayā adhikāriviśeṣaṇībhūtaṃ phalatayā'nveti na
punaraniyogasādhyamidamiti darśitam । <b>iha punaḥ śaṃyau bhaviṣyadarthatāṃ yātayāditi liṅa-
vagamayati</b> yātayaterdhātoḥ । tena yātanā bhaviṣyatīti pratīyate । atastatparihāro'pi
bhaviṣyatīti viśeṣaḥ । liṅarthatayā liṅ‍śabdena pañcamalakāro'bhidhīyate pañcamalakārāntarastvayaṃ
yātayāditi śabdaḥ । etattvatra vaktavyaḥ---kathamatra śatayātanāyāḥ apagoraṇasya ca sādhyasādhana-
bhāvo'vagamyate । kathaṃ ca apagoraṇaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ kālāntare yātanāheturbhavīti । taducyate
śamyumadhikṛtyaitaducyate yo brāhmaṇāyāvaguret taṃ śatena yātayāditi । tatra cedamavagamyate
brāhmaṇāpagoraṇaṃ nimittaṃ śatayātanā ca naimittikī iti । na ca pratyakṣavirodhaḥ anantara-
bhāvitvenāpratīteḥ । na ca kriyāphalatayā yātanā pratīyate yenānantarabhāvinī bhavet । tatra
pratītanimittanaimittikabhāvānurodhena kiñcidavāntarakāryaṃ kalpyate yatkṛtvā avagoraṇena yātanā
niṣpādyate । <q>“na brāhmaṇāyāvaguret”</q> iti niṣedhānuguṇatayā cāyamarthaḥ pratīyata iti ।
yātanā nāvivakṣitā śakyate āśrayitum । adhikāriviśeṣaṇatā tvatra niṣidhyamānakriyā-
kartṛtāyā eva । yātanāparihārastu niṣedhavidhiviṣayībhūtanañabhihitavagoraṇanivṛttiviśeṣaṇatayā
1viṣayāṃśānupraveśāt na niyojyaviśeṣaṇam । 2aniyogaphalatvāt । avagoraṇena hi
yātanāyāṃ 3sādhyāyāṃ tannivṛttau yātanāparihāro bhavasyeva niyogānapekṣa iti viṣayaphalamevedaṃ na
<note>(1) G. viṣayāṅgānu</note> <note>(2) G. sanniyoga</note> <note>(3) G. s‍vādhyāyāntaranivṛttau</note>
﻿<pb n="r832"/>
niyogaphalamiti mantavyam । ata eva cok‍taṃ sarvatra pratiṣedhaśās‍tre nividhyamānakriyākartu-
revādhikāra iti । evaṃ ca viṣayaphalata evānuṣṭhānalabdheḥ nādhikārānupraveśa iti puruṣadharma
evāvagoraṇapratiṣedhaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>prāgaparodhānmalavadvāsasaḥ</b> । atra bhāṣyakāreṇa sandehaḥ kṛtaḥ---kiṃ malavadvāsasā
saha darśapūrṇamāsāṅgasya saṃvādasya pratiṣedhaḥ uta puruṣasya sarvatra pratiṣedhavidhiriti । sa
cāyuktaḥ apratipakṣatvādvacanavyak‍teḥ । evaṃ hi vak‍tumucitaṃ---kiṃ darśapūrṇamāsāṅgasya saṃbādasya
pratiṣedhaḥ uta saṃvādamātrasyeti । yadi vā pratiṣedhaḥ kiṃ kratvarthaḥ uta puruṣārtha iti imāṃ
bhāṣye'nupapattiṃ pariharati---<b>malavadvāsasā saha saṃvādapratiṣedhe sandehaḥ kratvarthasaṃvādaḥ</b> prati-
ṣidhyate <b>uta puruṣārtha</b> iti । bhāṣye tu puruṣārthasaṃvādapratiṣedhapakṣasya phalamidaṃ kīrtitam
puruṣasya vidhiriti । <b>kiṃ prāptaṃ ? kratau</b> saṃvādasya <q>“patni pat‍nyeṣa te lokaḥ”</q> ityevaṃvidhasya
saṃbhavāt kratvarthaḥ saṃvādaḥ pratiṣidhyate <q>‘nānṛtaṃ vadet itivat’</q> । yathā kratvarthānṛtavadanaṃ
pratiṣidhyate tathā kratvarthasaṃvādaḥ pratiṣidhyate iti prāpte । ucyate । <b>na</b> kratvarthasyāyaṃ
pratiṣedhaḥ <b>prāptatvāt</b> kratāvasaṃvādasya । tena kratvarthasaṃvādābhāvāt puruṣārthasaṃvādapratiṣedha
evāyaṃ puruṣārthaḥ । <b>kratvarthatayā hi <q>‘tāmaparudhya yajeta’</q> iti prāpta evāsaṃvādaḥ</b> । na hi
aparuddhayā saha saṃvādaḥ saṃbhavati aparodhanaṃ kratuvyāpāraudāsīnyakaraṇam । <b>tasmāt</b> puruṣārthaḥ
pratiṣidhyate pratiṣedho'pi <b>puruṣārtha eva</b> । <b>vākyaṃ ca prakaraṇāt</b> balīya ityuktameva । <b>atra</b>
<note>(1) P. 951</note>
﻿<pb n="r833"/>
cādhikaraṇe <q>‘na malavadvāsasā saha saṃvadet’</q> iti saṃvādamātrapratiṣedha evāyaṃ ityaṅgīkṛtya vicāraḥ
kṛtaḥ upagamanapratiṣedho'yamiti kṛtbācintoddhāṭanam । upagamanapratiṣedhāṅgīkaraṇe hi pūrvapakṣāśaṅkaiva
nāsti । kratāvupagamanābhāvāt । saṃvādastu kratāvastīti tatpratiṣedhāśaṅkopapadyate । aparodha-
vacanaṃ ca sākṣātkartṛtvapratiṣedhārtham । na punassā anyenāpi na saṃbhāṣaṇīyeti matvā pūrva-
pakṣitam । aparodhe tu sakalayajñasaṃbandhaniṣedhā/?/t na saṃbhāṣaṇīyeti rāddhāntaḥ । saṃprati
kṛtvācintāmuddhāṭitāṃ gṛhītvā codayati---<b>nanu ca puruṣārthatayāpi prāpta evāyamasaṃvādaḥ
<q>‘nākalyāṃ nārīmabhiramayet na rajasvalām’</q></b> iti yo'yamupamamanapratiṣedharūpo lakṣaṇayā
asaṃvādaḥ prāpta eveti kathaṃ puruṣārtho'pi niṣedha iti । uttaraṃ---<b>asyāḥ smṛteridameva mūlaṃ
bhaviṣyati</b> । tena prāgastyeva rāgata upagamanaprāptirityupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ । <b>anuvādo vā</b>
tatsmṛtiprāptārthasya । nanvanuvādaścet kratāveva kimiti na bhavati ityatrāha---<b>sarvathā tāvat
kratvarthatā nāsti</b> । puruṣasaṃbandhitayā pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyamānaḥ kathaṃ kratvartho bhavati । kratva-
ṅgatvenāvidhānādupagamanasya । anuvādaścet kimiti puruṣasaṃbandhamatikrāmet iti nāstyanuvādepi
kratvarthatā । kṛtvācintoddhāṭanāyāha---<b>nanu ca saṃvādamātrapratiṣedho'yam</b> । kathaṃ
smṛterasyāḥ mūlaṃ anuvādo vā । <b>ucyate । <q>‘nāsyā annamadyāt’</q> । abhyañjanai vai striyā
annam”</b> iti <q>“upagamanaṃ vai striyā annaṃ”</q> ityupagamanapratiṣedha evāyaṃ sayuk‍tikaṃ kṛtvā--
cintoddhāṭanaḥ upagamanapratiṣedharūpasaṃvādapratiṣedhavākyārtho vedenaiva vyākhyātaḥ ityupagamanapratiṣedha
evāyam । tasmānmūlaṃ vā smṛteḥ prāptasyānuvādaḥ[vā]iti । anuvādagrahaṇaṃ prauḍhavādaḥ ।
paramārthatastu smṛtereva mūlamiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r834"/>
<p><b>aprakaraṇe tu taddharmastato viśepāt । <q>‘hiraṇyaṃ bhāryaṃ’</q> ityanārabhyavādāt puruṣārtho'yaṃ
vidhiḥ na hyatra kratussannihito'vagamyate</b> । <b>tasmāt puruṣārtha</b> iti rāddhāntamupakramya
pūrvapakṣamāha---<b>nanu prayojanavataḥ saṃskāro na niṣprayojanasya saṃskāryatā yuktā । dvitīyā-
nirdeśācca hiraṇyasaṃskāra evāyaṃ yuktaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ kratorupakariṣyatīti</b> । asyārthaḥ
---dvitīyānirdeśāditi dvitīyārthatayā kṛtyasya karmaiva dvitīyāśabdenocyate । tena suvarṇaṃ
bhāryaṃ iti karmārthakṛtyapratyayasya nirdeśāt, hiraṇyasaṃskāra evāyaṃ dhāraṇaṃ nāma । na ca
niṣprayojanaḥ saṃskāramarhati । tasmāt saṃskṛtaṃ kratorupakariṣyatītvevamarthaṃ dhāraṇena hiraṇyaṃ
saṃskriyate iti kratvartha evāyaṃ saṃskāra iti । rāddhāntamāha---<b>atrābhidhīyate</b> । <b>syādetadevaṃ
yadi saṃskṛtasya hiraṇyasya karmārthatopapadyate । na tvatra karmārtha</b>tā hiraṇyasyāsti ।
taddarśayati---<b>na tāvat prakṛtaṃ karmāsti</b> । <b>na ceha karmacodanā dravyadevatāsaṃyogābhāvāt</b> ।
<b>tasmāt dravyasaṃskārānarthakyāt puruṣadharmo'yamiti</b> । <b>nanu cātrāpi phalaṃ kalpayitavyaṃ</b>,
adhikāriṇo'śravaṇāt adhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ kalpayitavyam । uttaraṃ---<b>niyogānāṃ kāryārthatvāt
prakṛtasya kāryasya avidyamānatvāt na doṣaḥ</b> adhikārikalpanāyām । adhikāri-
<note>(1) P. 952</note>
﻿<pb n="r835"/>
niyogārthatvāt parasparapadārthasaṃbandhasya prakṛtasya vā adhikāraniyogasyābhāvāt balādadhikārāntara-
kalpanā na doṣaḥ viśvajiddhat । <b>tasmāt hiraṇyadhāraṇaṃ karmakarturdharmaścodyate iti</b> । punaḥ
pūrvapakṣī vadati---yadi <b>kartṛsaṃskāratvena phalaṃ kalpyate kimiti dravyasaṃskāratayāpi kratūpa-
kāro na kalpyate</b> tulyatvāt kalpanāyāḥ ko viśeṣa iti bhāvaḥ । <b>ayamasti viśeṣaḥ
ekavākyāvagatena</b> hi <b>arthavādena kartṛsaṃbandhe phalakalpanopapadyate</b> । antaraṅgatvāt
<b>na punaraprakṛtena kratunā saha saṃbandhakalpanā । arthaviprakarṣāt</b> bahiraṅgabhūtatvāt kratu-
saṃbandhasya । etaccābhyuccayamātraṃ avyāpakatvāt । idānīṃ vyāpikāṃ mūlayuktimāha---<b>ayaṃ
cāparo viśeṣaḥ sarvatra draṣṭavyaḥ kartṛsaṃbandhe hyadhikārasiddhiḥ</b> । <b>adhikṛtasya ca phala-
kalpanā nyāyyā</b> । <b>na punaḥ dravyasaṃbandhe prayojanakalpaneti sak‍tuṣu darśitam</b> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---kartṛtvaṃ hi kāryabhūtamadhikārasya tena kartṛsaṃbandhe'vagate yuktā kāraṇabhūtā-
dhikārasiddhiḥ । na cāviśiṣṭo'dhikārī bhavati iti viśeṣabhūtaphalakalpanāpi 1kāryā ।
dravyasaṃbandhe tu kriyayā avagate na dravyasya prayojanakalpanā nyāyyā pramāṇābhāvāt ।
na ca dravyaṃ prati kriyāyāstādarthyāvayama eva pramāṇaṃ, niṣprayojane tādarthyānupapatteriti ।
yatastādarthyameva dravyaṃ pratyanavagatam । na ca dvitīyayā tādarthyamiti tatra tatroktam ।</p>
<note>(1) G. nyāyyā</note>
﻿<pb n="r836"/>
<p><b>śeṣo'prakaraṇe'viśeṣāt sarvakarmaṇāt</b> । <q>‘<b>yena karmaṇerset tatra</b> jayān juhuyāt’</q>
iti sthitaṃ tāvat jayāhomāḥ karmāṅgamiti ṛddhisādhanakarmasaṃyogāt phalāntarāśravaṇācca ।
idīnāṃ sandihyate---kiṃ karmamātrāṅgaṃ uta vaidikasyaiveti । karmamātraśabdenātra smārtavaidika-
karmaṇāṃ grahaṇaṃ na kṛṣyādīnām; teṣāṃ anvayavyatirekasamadhigamyāṅgatvāt vaidikāṅgānupapatteḥ ।
bhāṣye tu kṛṣyādigrahaṇaṃ āśaṅkāmātreṇa na paramārthataḥ । <b>aviśeṣāt sarvārthateti pūrvapakṣa-
vādī manyate । nanu cānāhitāgnerāhavanīyābhāvāt nāyaṃ homaḥ saṃbhavati</b> । asyārthaḥ
---jayāhomāstāvat <q>‘āhavanīye juhotī’</q>ti vacanāt āhavanīye kartavyāḥ । tatra yadi
laukikānāṃ smārtānāṃ karmaṇāmaṅgaṃ syāt tadā teṣāmanāhitāgnerapi saṃbhavāt jayāhomaḥ prāpnoti ।
na cānāhitāgnirāhavanīye hotuṃ śak‍noti । na cedaṃ vācyaṃ āhitāgnirāhavanīye hoṣyati,
anāhitāgnistu neti । nityavadviniyuktāhavanīyabādhaprasaṅgāt । na cedamapyucitam 
---anāhitāgneraṣṭakādikarmāṇi jayāhomarahitāni bhaviṣyanti āhitāgnerneti । <b>ekameva niyogaṃ</b>
prati aṅgatvānaṅgatvānupapatteḥ iti varaṃ vaidikānāmeva tretāvatāṃ karmaṇābhaṅgaṃ jayāhoma iti sthitiḥ ।
pariharati---<b>anāhavanīya evāyaṃ bhaviṣyati pradhānānurodhāt</b> । <b>na guṇānurodhena pradhāna-
syāṅgatyāgo yuktaḥ guṇa eva hi tyājyaḥ pradhānānurodhenetyaṅgavido manyante</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yena karmaṇertsediti sāmānyena śravaṇāt jayāhomaḥ sarvakarmārtha iti sthite yatra pradhāne
aṣṭakādikarmaṇi anāhitāgnitvādāhavanīyo na bhavati tatra kiṃ pradhānamastīti jayāhomaḥ
kriyatāṃ, utāhavanīyo nāstīti na kriyatāṃ iti saṃśaye pradhānasyānugrahāt homāṅgamāhavanīyaṃ
<note>(1) P. 957</note>
﻿<pb n="r837"/>
parityajya jayāhomaḥ kartavyaḥ na punaḥ aṅgasya jayāhomasyāṅgabhūtāhavanīyānurodhena
pradhānasyāṣṭakāderaṅgabhūtasya jayāhomasya tyāgo yuktaḥ । guṇa evāhavanīṃya-
styak‍tumucitaḥ <b>pradhānānurodheneti aṅgavido manyante</b> । rāddhāntamāha---(satyamāha
bhavān) <b>satyamevaitat । kintvatrāyaṃ nyāyo na saṃbhavati</b> । aṅgaguṇavirodhe ca tādarthyā-
diti । <b>kasmāt ? vaidike tāvadāhavanīyabādho nopapadyate na ca laukikasyaiva
smārtasyaivāṅgamiti śakyate vak‍tuṃ tvayaivok‍tamaviśeṣāditi</b> । ayamāśayaḥ---yatra niścita-
maṅgatvaṃ tatrāṅgaguṇavirodhanyāyaḥ । iha tu jayāhomasyāṅgatvameva niścitam । tatra yasminna-
ṅginyāśrīyamāṇe viniyojyasvarūpaṃ na bādhyate tasyaiva śeṣitvaṃ yuktam । āhavanīyayuk‍taṃ cāṅgi-
svarūpamiti tadanurodhena vaidikeṣveva viniyogaḥ tatrāhavanīyasaṃbhavāt । smārteṣvanāhitāgnerāha-
vanīyābhāvāt ityāhavanīyāṅgāvirodhena viniyoga evopasaṃhriyate । na ca yena karmaṇertsediti
virodhaḥ aviśeṣoddeśāt । <b>ato bhāvābhāvayorvirodhāt</b> āhavanīyabhāvābhāvayorvirodhāt
āhavanīyasya <b>bhāvata eva viśeṣāvadhāraṇaṃ yuktam</b> । na punarabhāvataḥ anavagamaheturasau
anavagamaṃ pratyeva heturasau <b>na punarviśeṣāvagamahetuḥ tasmādvaidika eva jayāhoma iti
sthitam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) 958</note>
﻿<pb n="r838"/>
<p><b>doṣattviṣṭirlaukike syāt</b> । <b>pauṇḍarīke śrūyate-yāvato'śvān pratigṛhṇīyāt</b> tāvato
vāruṇāñcatuṣkapālānnirvapet” iti aśvapratigrahoṣṭirasti । tatra <q>‘yāvato'śvān pratigṛhṇīyāt’</q> iti
<b>kiṃ laukike'śvapratigrahe iyamiṣṭiḥ uta vaidike iti saṃśayaḥ</b> । tatra pūrvapakṣamāha---<b>laukike
doṣadarśanāt śūdrādanyasmādvā pāpakarmaṇaḥ kṛte doṣo bhavatīti</b> । doṣavatyaśvapratigrahe iya-
miṣṭiḥ śrūyate doṣavattā ca laukikasyāśvapratigrahasyāsti yataḥ śūdrādanyasmādvā pāpakarmaṇaḥ kṛte
pratigrahe doṣo bhavati । tasmāt doṣavān laukikaḥ pratigraha iti tatraiveyamiṣṭiḥ । atra
bhāṣyaṃ <q>‘na doṣasaṃkīrtanaṃ prāyaścittaviṣayatiśeṣaṇaṃ, kintu prāyaścittastutyarthena”</q> iti । tadva‍yākhyātu-
mupakramate---<b>kimidaṃ prāyaścittaviṣayaviśeṣaṇaṃ kiṃ vā stutyartheneti</b> । <b>idamidaṃ---asya
varuṇagrahākhyasyārthasyāpanuttaye yadā prāyaścittaṃ</b> tadā prāyaścitta<b>viṣayaviśeṣaṇam</b> । yat‍tu
khalu doṣanirdhātārthaṃ tat yatraiva doṣaḥ tatraiva kartavyamityarthāt prāyaścittaviṣayabhūtapratigrahasya
varuṇagraho viśeṣaṇaṃ yatraiva ca varuṇagrahaḥ tatraiva tannivṛttaye'śvapratigraheṣṭiriti । <b>yadā tu kāryā-
ntarārthaṃ tadā stutyarthena, doṣanirdhātārthaṃ cedaṃ</b> vākyapaurvāparyālocanayā doṣanirdhātārthaṃ
prāyaścittaṃ cedaṃ pratīyate । <b>tasmāllaukike bhavitumarhati</b> । atra bhāṣyaṃ---<q>“nanu vaidikepi
pratigrahe apratigrāhyāt pratigṛhṇataḥ pāpamasti iti prāyaścittena bhavitavyam । ucyate ।
<note>(1) 958</note> <note>(2) 959</note>
﻿<pb n="r839"/>
bhavedetadevaṃ yadi pratigrahasya karturiṣṭirbhavet । sā tu khalu yathā hetukartuḥ tathottarādhikaraṇe
vakṣyāmaḥ”</q> iti । tadākṣipannāha---(atra codayati)---<b>asaṃbaddhamidaṃ bhāṣyam</b> । <b>yadi
laukike pratigrahīturiṣṭirnabhavati tataśca vaidikepi (kimiti pratigrahīturiṣṭirnabharthati</b> ।
<b>tataśca vaidikepi) aś‍vaṃ apratigrāhyāt pratigṛhṇato doṣo'stīti satyapi doṣanirṣātārthe
prāyaścitte kasmāllaukika eva pratigrahītuḥ prāyaścittāśaṅkā</b> । <b>atha upakramāvagatārthavāda-
darśanāt dāturiṣṭirityucyate laukike'pi tulyaṃ</b>, tasminnapi pakṣe upakramālocanayā dātureva
na ca tasya doṣo'sti dānasyāniṣiddhatvāt । ato doṣanirdhātārthatve nāsti laukike prasaṅgaḥ
<b>atha laukike pratigrahapakṣe'pi dāturevetyabhiprāyaḥ śūdradanyasmādveti bhāṣyamasaṃbaddhaṃ</b>
dāturhi doṣo darśayitavyaḥ na pratigrahītuḥ doṣanirdhātārthaṃ dāturiṣṭiriti vadatā dātuḥ doṣaḥ
kathanīyaḥ । na ca śūdrādanyasmādvā pratigrahe dāturdoṣo bhavati api tu pratigrahītureva । na
ca tasyeyamiṣṭiḥ upakramavirodhāt । <b>kathaṃ coparitane'dhikaraṇe pratigrahīturiyamiṣṭiriti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । <b>vedo vā prāyadarśanāt</b> । <b>ityupakrameṇopasaṃhārāvadhṛteḥ</b> । vedo vā prāyadarśa-
nādityupakramānusāreṇopasaṃhāro nyāyyaḥ ityuktam । tenehāpyupakramagatārthavādālocanayā dāturi-
ṣṭiriti pratīyate । <b>atrābhidhīyate---nedamasaṃbaddhaṃ bhāṣyaṃ; ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣiṇaḥ</b> ।
﻿<pb n="r840"/>
<b>laukike'śvapratigrahe doṣaśravaṇaṃ viṣayaviśeṣaṇatayaiva1 upapadyate</b> । laukikāśvapratigrahaviṣayā-
yāmiṣṭau āśrayamāṇāyāṃ doṣaśravaṇaṃ phalasamarpakatayā pratigrahalakṣaṇaviṣayaviśeṣaṇatayaivopapadyate ।
tasmin pakṣe doṣanirdhātārthā satīyamiṣṭiḥ saṃbhāvyadoṣasya pratigrahītureva bhavati । pratigrahītaivā-
dhikārīti yāvat । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ</b> pratigrahītaivādhikārī yāvatā upakramavaśena dātaivādhikārī yukta
iti । uttaraṃ---<b>yasmādasmin pakṣe</b> laukikapratigrahāśrayaṇapakṣe---<b>pratigrahīturiyamiṣṭiḥ yadi ca</b>
tasminnapi pakṣe <b>dātureveyamiṣṭiḥ syāt tataḥ dānasya</b> smārtasya laukikasyāṅgaṃ kalpayitavyametadiṣṭi-
<b>rūpaṃ phalāntaraṃ</b> adhikārāntaraṃ vā । <b>dānāṅgatā tāvanna saṃbhavati nimittatvenāsyopakṣayāt</b>
upakṣīṇatvāt <b>dānasya</b> śeṣitvānupapatteḥ । <b>atha viparivṛttyā punaraṅgitvaṃ dānasya kalpyate
tadā idamevāyuk‍taṃ</b> yannimittatvenopakṣīṇasya punaraṅgitvakalpanaṃ pramāṇābhāvāt । nanu
idameva pramāṇa yaddātṛgatadoṣakīrtanaṃ tatrāha---<b>guṇavādenāpyarthavādopapatteḥ</b> । evamaśvapratigraho
nidānaṃ doṣasya । yaddāturapi tāvat doṣo bhavati kimaṅga punaḥ pratigrahītuḥ iti pratigrahadoṣa-
pradarśanaparatayāpyarthavādopapatteḥ na śakyate dāturdoṣaṃ parikalpya tannirharaṇadvāreṇa dānāṅgatā
kalpayitumiti । nanu ca dānamātranimittamadhikārāntaramevedaṃ bhavitumarhatītyatrāha---<b>pāpapramo-
canasya phalatayā vā vākyenāvagateḥ</b> । tena yathā tasyānvayo bhavati tathā varṇayitavyam । tasya
ca pratigrahītari niyojye yukto'nvayaḥ na dātari tadāha---<b>na ca dātuḥ pāpaṃ śakyate kalpayituṃ</b>
<note>(1) R. tathaiva</note>
﻿<pb n="r841"/>
<b>coditatvāt loke vede ca dānasya । tasmāllaukikapakṣe pratigrahautureveyamiṣṭiḥ</b>
vaidikapakṣe tu prakaraṇa eva niveśāt prakaraṇenāṅgatvakalpanāt phalāntarakalpanābhāvāt dātureve
yamiṣṭiḥ syāt । tatra ca doṣapramocanaśravaṇamavivakṣitaṃ syāt dāturdoṣābhāvāt । ato
laukikapratigrahaviṣayaiveyamiṣṭiḥ iti । tatra hi yathok‍tena nyāyena pratigrahīturiṣṭirbhavati
pratigrahītuśca doṣa iti doṣapramocanaśravaṇaṃ vivakṣitaṃ syāt । tato'yamatra sandehārthaḥ---laukike
pratigrahe pratigrahīturiyamiṣṭirbhavatu atha vā vaidike dāturiti । tatra pāpapramocanaśravaṇāt laukike
pratigrahīturiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu yathā śrutasya tāvatpāpasya aśvapratigraho na
nidānatayā pramāṇāntareṇa prasiddhaḥ</b> na jalodarasyāśvapratigrahaḥ nidānatayā pramāṇāntareṇa
siddhaḥ । nāpi vacanāt । vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt । yadi vacanamidaṃ jñāpayet aśvaprati-
graheṇa jalodaraṃ bhavati tacceṣṭyā'panīyata iti tato'rthabhedādvākyabhedaḥ syāt । ekaṃ cedaṃ
vākyam । ato na vacanato jalodaranidānatā aśvapratigrahasya । <b>tasmāt pāpamātrabacanaṃ</b>
jalodaravacanaṃ <b>vaidikepyupapadyata eva rakṣaṇapoṣaṇādinā duḥ svadarśanāt</b> pratigrahītuḥ ।
<b>nanu vaidikapakṣe</b> dāturiṣṭa‍yā bhavitavyamiti dātureva doṣo darśanīyaḥ । kimidaṃ pratigrahītṛdoṣa-
kīrtanaṃ uttarādhikaraṇasya adyāpyasiddhatvāt । yuk‍taṃ pratigrahīturdoṣadarśanam asminnadhikaraṇe
kratvaṅgatayā dātureveṣṭāvadhikāra iti sidhyati । uttarādhikaraṇe tu kiṃ dātā yajñe uta
ṛtvigiti kartṛvicāro bhaviṣyati । tena pratigrahītari kartari ārtvijadoṣadarśanamupapannam ।
vaidikapratigrahaviṣayeṣṭipakṣe ca <b>phalaṃ ca kalpayitavyaṃ bhavati karmāṅgatayopapatteḥ</b> । prakaraṇa-
<b>viniyojyatayā karturvābhavatu pratigrahīturvā</b> yadi dātṛkartṛkeyamiṣṭiḥ । yadi ca
pratigrahītṛkartṛkā tathāpi pauṇḍarīkaprakaraṇāt tadaṅgamityarthaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r842"/>
<p><b>acoditaṃ ca karmabhedāt</b> । atra codayati---<b>yuk‍taṃ tāvat yadā kartuḥ tadā
karmāṅgaṃ</b> ekādhikārasaṃbandhāt---<b>yadā punaḥ pratigrahītuḥ tadā kathaṃ</b> ? pratigrahītuḥ adhi-
kārāntaratvenāsaṃbandhāt iti bhrāntasyedaṃ codyam । uttaraṃ---<b>upakramopasaṃhāravaśāt</b> prati-
grāhayeditivat vipariṇāmātkalpyate । asyārthaḥ---yathā rāddhānte upakramavaśāt prati-
grāhayeditivipariṇāmaḥ tathā kṛtādvipariṇāmāt pratigrahītṛkartṛkatvepi ekādhi-
kāripuruṣasaṃbandhāt aṅgatā kalpyate । tameva vipariṇāmaṃ darśayati---<b>ṛtvijo yājanīyā
upavāsavat</b>। yathā upavāsaṃ kāryante ṛtvijaḥ tathā yājanīyāḥ । varuṇoddeśena catuṣka-
pālena yājayitavyā ityarthaḥ । tena sādhūk‍taṃ dāturvā bhavatu pratigrahīturveti । <b>yatpunaruk‍taṃ
vedo vā prāyadarśanādeveti manyate</b> । nanvayaṃ doṣaḥ paramārthato nāstyevetyuk‍taṃ tatrāha---<b>arthavādī-
bhūto'pi</b> hi doṣaḥ <b>pratigrahīturevāñjasyenopapadyate</b> । rakṣaṇapoṣaṇādiduḥkhadarśanāt ।
nanvevamupakramagatadātṛkīrtanaṃ kathaṃ ghaṭiṣyata ityatrāha---<b>upakramo'pi laukikapakṣavat dāturapi
tāvaddoṣaḥ kiṃ punaḥ pratigrahīturiti vyākhyāyate</b> । etaccoktamasmābhiḥ । <b>rāddhāntavādītu</b>
<note>(1) P. 963</note>
﻿<pb n="r843"/>
<b>avaśyaṃ tāvat <q>‘nirvāpayet’</q> iti kalpanīyam । tasmādvaramupakramavaśāt <q>‘pratigrāhayet’</q>
iti yuk‍taṃ manyate</b> । vipariṇāmasyāvaśyakalpanīyatvāt varamupakramānurodhena vipariṇāmaḥ
kalpyatāmiti nyāyyam । arthavādasyāvaśyakarmavyatāparatvena bhāṣye varṇanā kṛteti na
punaruk‍taṃ <q>‘vedovā’</q> ityanenādhikaraṇena । adhikaraṇadvayaṃ tu ekīkṛtya vyācakṣāṇasyāyamāśayaḥ
---arthavādārthapratipattyā pūrvādhikaraṇe pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ samīcīnārthavādārthadarśanena nirākaraṇīyaḥ ।
avaśyaṃ kartavyatātmakapāramārthikārthavādārthavarṇanaṃ cottarādhikaraṇāyattamiti ।</p>
<p><b>pānavyāpacca tadvat । tadvadityatideśiko viśeṣaḥ</b> ? na hi viśeṣamantareṇa
tadvaditi bhavati tadeva hi syāt । <b>ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ doṣaśravaṇāt</b> <q>“indriyeṇa vā eṣa
vyṛdhyate vīryeṇa vā yaḥ somaṃ vamiti”</q> iti doṣaśravaṇāt laukike somavamane prāyaścittamiti
viśeṣaḥ । <b>nanu pūrvasminnadhikaraṇe doṣadarśanādeva laukika ityuktam</b> । ihāpi doṣa-
darśanādeva laukika ityucyamāne nāsti viśeṣaḥ । pariharati---<b>satyamanupapattiḥ tatrok‍tā
doṣasya</b> jalodaralakṣaṇasya । <b>iha tu glāniḥ vamanādupapadyata evendriyāṇāmiti adhi-
kāśaṅkā</b> । pramāṇaparigṛhītaivendriyāṇāṃ vyaddhiḥ । yata eva pramāṇaparigṛhītaiveyaṃ <b>ata eva
vamanārthaṃ taditi parihṛtaṃ</b> doṣatvam । anyathā glānireva nāstīti parihāro dātavyaḥ
<note>(1) P. 969</note>
﻿<pb n="r844"/>
syāt । kathaṃ punaḥ vamanārthatvābhidhānena doṣaparihāraḥ tatrāha---<b>glānyarthameva hi yat na
tasya glānirdoṣatvena śakyate kalpayitumiti</b> । yaddhi vamanārthaṃ tadvamansya glānyavinā-
bhāvitvāt glānyarthameva । yacca glānyarthaṃ tasya glānirna doṣa iti śakyate vaditumiti
parihṛtameva doṣatvam । yasmāddoṣatvaṃ nāsti <b>tasmāt</b> tannirharaṇārthatā tāvadasya somendrasya
karmaṇo nāstīti <b>pūrvavadevedaṃ karma phalakalpanābhayāccoditasomapānavamananimitta-
kamityarthaḥ</b> । coditaṃ yatsomapānaṃ tasya yat vamanaṃ tannimittakamidaṃ karma । tena kratu-
saṃbandhisomapānavamananimittatvāt kratvaṅgabhūtamevedaṃ karmeti sthitam ।</p>
<p><b>tatsarvatrāviśeṣāt । kiṃ yāvantaḥ somavāminaḥ tāvatāṃ vamana etatprāyaścittaṃ
uta svāmina eveti</b> bhāṣyakāreṇa sākṣādanuktamapyarthādavagamyamānaṃ saṃśayaṃ kathayati ।
<b>aviśeṣāt</b> sarveṣāṃ vamana <b>iti prāpte; ucyate---svāmina etat prāyaścittamiti</b> ।
kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ---<b>na yajamānasya ṛtvijāṃ caikā codanā saṃbhavati । ekatra yajeteti
codanā anyatra yājayediti</b> । asyārthaḥ, yadi yajamānavamane ṛtvigvamane caikā codanā
syāt tadā aviśeṣaḥ syāt । na cāsāvekā codanā saṃbhavati yasmādekatra yajamānavamanapakṣe
<note>(1) P. 971</note>
﻿<pb n="r845"/>
yajeteti codanā yassomaṃ vamiti sa somendraṃ caruṃ nirvapet iti tadā vākyārthaḥ syāt ।
anyatra tu ṛtvigvamanapakṣe yājayediti codanā । idaṃ hi pūrvoṃk‍tena kratvarthaṃ karmeti sthitam ।
tena nāyamarthaḥ yassomaṃ vamiti ṛtvika‍tamṛtvijaṃ somendraṃ caruṃ nirvāpayediti । <b>na caika-
sminvākye ubhayametatsaṃbhavati</b>। tasmānnāviśeṣāt sarveṣāṃ vamane somendraṃ karma ।
nanvevamapi ṛtvigvamana evāstu tatrāha---<b>kasmāt ? avipariṇatā eṣā codanā</b> । ṛtvigva-
manapakṣepi hi yajamānasyaivādhikārādavaśyaṃ vipariṇāmaḥ kalpyaḥ avipariṇatā ceyaṃ codanā ।
<b>sā ca svābhivamana evāvagamyate</b> yasmādyajamānavamananimittakamidaṃ karma <b>tasmāt phalavat---
sannidhāvaphalaṃ tadaṅgamiti bhavati</b> । anyathā hi ṛtvigvamane nimitte sati avipariṇa-
teyaṃ codanā ṛtvijāmevādhikāriṇāṃ svatantraṃ karma vidadhyāt । tasmādadhikāribhedādanaṅgameva
syāditi phalavatsannidhāvaphalaṃ tadaṅgamiti na sidhyati । <b>tadidaṃ</b> ṛtvigvamanapakṣe avi-
pariṇatacodanāśrayaṇe'naṅgatvamuktam <b>nānyadīyo yāgo'nyasyopakarotīti । tasmānna ṛtvi-
gvamananimittam । nahyanyasya coditamanyasyopakarotītyarthaḥ</b>। upasaṃharati---<b>ata-
ssiddhamevedaṃ svāmivamananimittamiti</b> ।</p>
<p><b>sarvapradānaṃ haviṣastadarthatvāt</b> । atra bhāṣyaṃ ki kṛts‍naṃ haviragnaye dātavyamiti
tadanupapannam । devatāṃ prati dānābhāvāt । tathā śeṣayitavyaṃ kiñcit kiñcicca dātavyamiti
<note>(1) P. 974</note>
﻿<pb n="r846"/>
tadva‍yācaṣṭe---<b>ihedānīṃ sandihyate āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla iti kiṃ kṛtsnasyaiva tyāgaḥ । uta
dvirhaviṣo'vadyati</b> caturavattaṃ juhoti iti vacanāt <b>tāvanmātrasyaiveti</b> tyāga evadāna-
śabdenocyate lakṣaṇayā । <b>nanu cātra sandeha eva nopapadyate । āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla iti
parisamāptā yāgacodanā</b> । tena sarvasyaiva tyāga iti rāddhāntavacanavyaktyabhāvāt sandeha
evānupapannaḥ । nanu ca <q>‘dvirhaviṣo'badyati’</q> <q>‘caturavattaṃ juhoti’</q> iti śravaṇāt dva‍yavadānamātrasya
tyāgaḥ pratibhāti ityatrāha---<b>dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti saṃskāracodanaiṣā haviṣaḥ <q>‘ag‍nestṛṇānya-
pacinotī’</q>tivat । nanu ca na</b> kevalamavadānaṃ śrūyate <b>juhotītyapi śrūyate</b> । tena
dva‍yavadānenaiva yāgaḥ kartavya iti pratīyate । uttaraṃ---<b>haviṣassakāśāt apanītasya
pratipattirbhaviṣyati । yathā</b> rāddhānta eva <b>yāgottarakālaṃ sviṣṭakṛdādayaḥ</b> śeṣāt śeṣa-
pratipattibhūtāḥ sviṣṭakṛdādayaḥ । <b>atrābhidhīyate---naitadevaṃ</b> bhavitumarhati kṛtsnasyaiva tyāga
iti yasmā<b>jjuhotiḥ yāgāśca svasaṃbandhidravyasādhyāḥ</b> dravyatyāgātmakau homayāgau
svadravyeṇaiva sidhyataḥ । <b>sakalasya ca parityāge homoyāgāśca sviṣṭakṛdādayo
nopapadyante</b> । asyārthaḥ kṛts‍nasya tyāgapakṣe dva‍yavadānamakṛtvaiva puroḍāśastyaktavyaḥ anyathā
kṛts‍natvasyānupapatteḥ । tataśca puroḍāśāt dva‍yavadānamātraṃ kṛtvā hotavyaṃ sviṣṭakṛdādayaśca
yāgāḥ kartavyāḥ te nopapadyante tyaktasya dravyasyāsvakīyatvāt । tasmānna kṛtsnastya-
﻿<pb n="r847"/>
k‍tavya ityasti śaṅkā । nanu ca dravyāntarāt homāḥ sviṣṭakṛdādayo bhaviṣyanti tatrāha
---<b>aṣṭākapālaviṣayā codanā</b> । tasyaiva haviṣṭa‍vāt śeṣaśabdasya prakṛtadravyaviṣayatvācca ।
<b>ata upapadyate saṃśayaḥ । asmiṃśca saṃśaye kasya pakṣasyādhyavasānaṃ yuk‍taṃ ? pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate । apratipakṣatvādāg‍neyacodanāyāḥ tatsavyapekṣatvāditarāsāṃ pūrvaiva balīyasīti ।
tadidamuktam---sarvapradānaṃ haviṣastadarthatvāditi । kathaṃ tarhi <q>‘caturavattaṃ juhoti’</q> iti</b>
homaḥ <q>‘sviṣṭakṛte samavadyati’</q> iti caturthīprayogāt sviṣṭakṛddevateti niścīyate ।
1tena dravyadevate niścīyete tena dravyadevatāsaṃbandhāt sviṣṭakṛdyāgaḥ । tau ca
homayāgau tyak‍te dravye na saṃbhavataḥ । uttara---<b>gauṇo vā yajyartho juhotyarthaśca grahītavyaḥ</b>
<b>prakṣe</b>pamātrarūpaḥ । <b>taddharmakaṃ vā dravyāntaramutpādyam</b> । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<b>dbirhaviṣo-
'vadyati havidharmakādavadyatītyarthaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>kṛtatvāt‍tu karmaṇaḥ sakṛtsyāt dravyasya guṇabhūtatvāt । atrābhidhīyate---satyamevaṃ
yathā bhavānāha---yadi <q>‘āg‍neyo'ṣṭākapāla’</q> iti tyāgaparyantaḥ taddhitaḥ syāt</b>, syāde-
<note>(1) G. omits tena.....yete</note>
﻿<pb n="r848"/>
tadevaṃ, yāvatā <b>sāsya devateti saṃbandhimātratayā'vagateḥ tadekadeśatyāgādapi saṃbandhitā
upapadyata eva । tadidamuktam akṛtsnasaṃbandhe'pi taddhitasaṃyogasyopapattiḥ</b> tato
grahīṣyata iti । nanu apradīyamānasya kathamasaṃbandhe kṛts‍nasyāgneyatā ? uttaraṃ---<b>darśitastato
grahītasya iti saṃbandhaḥ</b> dva‍yavadānasya । evaṃ ca <b>sati āg‍neyacodanāyāmupapannāyāṃ <q>“catu-
ravattaṃ juhoti”</q> <q>‘sviṣṭakṛte samavadyati’</q> iti gauṇīvṛttiḥ na śakyate kalpayitum ।
havirdharmakasya vā dravyasyotpādaḥ tathā caturavattahomenaiva kṛtaśśāstrārthaḥ <q>‘āg‍neyo'ṣṭā-
kapāla’</q> iti sviṣṭakṛdādidarśanaṃ copapannaṃ bhavati</b> । <q>‘śeṣādiḍāmavadyati’</q> <q>‘śeṣāt sviṣṭakṛte
samavadyati’</q> iti śeṣadarśanaṃ copapadyate । anyathā aśeṣe śeṣaśabdaḥ syāt । <b>yatpunaridamā-
śaṅkitaṃ dvayavadānasma saṃskāratvāt na sarvasya parityāge virodha iti । tadidamāśaṅkā-
mātrameva । haviṣo yāgārthatvādityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yatpunaridamāśaṅkitaṃ dva‍yavadānaṃ
svīkṛtāvayavadravyasaṃskāraḥ, tadeva homena pratipādyate tasmiṃśca pratipāditepi pariśiṣṭena
kṛts‍nena puroḍāśenāg‍neyaḥ kariṣyate । <b>tena na</b> kaścidvirodha iti । atrocyate---syāde-
tadevaṃ yadi tadartho yāgaḥ syāt । yadi <b>yāgena</b> haviḥ saṃbandhayitavyaṃ syāt । havistu
yāgārthaṃ tena sakṛta dva‍yavadāne kṛte kṛtatvādyāgasya dravye satyapi na punaryāgaḥ kartavya
ityuk‍taṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r849"/>
<p><b>aprayojakatvādekasmāt kriyeran śeṣasya guṇabhūtatvāt । iha śeṣakāryāṇyudāha-
raṇam । kiṃ sakṛtkṛtvoparantavma, uta yāvaccheṣamāvṛttiriti</b>। asyārthaḥ---kimeka-
syādeva śeṣāt śeṣakāryaṃ kṛtvā uparantavyaṃ uta sarvebhyaḥ śeṣebhyaḥ pratyekaṃ śeṣakāryāṇi
kāryāṇīti । <b>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī kṛtatvātkāryasya sakṛtkaraṇaṃ manyate</b> । ekasmādapi
śeṣāt śeṣakārye kṛtaśśāstrārtha iti sakṛtkaraṇaṃ manyate āgneyavat । <b>nanu ca prati-
pradhānaṃ guṇā āvartanta iti śeṣasya aprādhānyādāvṛttireva pratīyate</b> । parihartumāha
---<b>ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ । pradhānopakārāya hi śeṣasya saṃskāraḥ sakṛtkṛtena ca
kṛtaṃ kāryamiti nāvṛttiṃ manyate</b> । upakāryaikyāt sakṛdeva śeṣakāryaṃ kartavyam ।
<b>na śeṣatvāt saṃskāryatvaṃ</b>, api tu pradhānopakārāya । <b>nanu ca grahādāvapyevameva prāpnoti</b> ।
tatrāpyeka eva grahaḥ saṃmārjayitavyaḥ syāt । uttaraṃ---prāp‍notyeva (<b>vaṃ</b>) <b>yadyatra
1na samādhīyate</b> । yadyatraiva bahūnāṃ sammārgaḥ pratipādyate <b>tatra tarhi kā cintā
ekatvāvivakṣetyuktam । atrābhidhīyate---yāvaccheṣamāvṛttiḥ</b> । yadyapi pradhānopakārāya
śeṣakāryāṇi tathāpi śeṣibhedādbheda eva yuktaḥ । <b>nanu ca kṛtatvācchāstrārthasya sakṛdityuktam</b> ।
<note>(1) G. omits na</note>
﻿<pb n="r850"/>
<b>ucyate---śeṣasaṃskāradvāraṃ hi pradhānasyopakāryatvamuktam । na ca śeṣe viśeṣo'vagamyate ।
ayamayaṃ ayaṃ veti । ato'gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt pratipradhānamāvṛttiḥ</b> । dvāratvāviśeṣāt
sarveṣāmeva kāryāṇi bhavanti । <b>liṅgāni ca darśitāni bhāṣye । yatpunaraprayojakatvāccheṣāṇā-
miti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ tadevedaṃ na śeṣatvāt saṃskāryatvamiti yaduk‍tamasmābhiḥ</b> tena nāsti
bhāṣyavirodhaḥ । <b>na punarguṇabhāvaṃ śeṣasya</b> bhāṣyakāro <b>manyate</b> । na punarguṇabhāvābhiprāyeṇa
bhāṣyakāraḥ pūrvapakṣayatītyarthaḥ । kasmādityāha---<b>na hi śeṣasya prayojakatvamaprayojakatvaṃ
copapadyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi hi śeṣasya guṇabhāvaḥ syād tadā nāśadoṣāpahāraiḥ upātta-
dravyaśeṣābhāve śeṣasya dravyaṃ prati prayojakatābhāve ca aprayojakamiti । na caitada‍yuktam ।
<b>tasmātsa eva pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> yo'smābhiḥ darśitaḥ । na punaḥ śrutyupanipātamātreṇa bhāṣye
yatpratibhāti ।</p>
<p><b>ekasmāccet । pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣe'nuṣṭhānacinteyam</b> । yadi hi ekasmāditi
pūrvapakṣo bhavati tadeyaṃ cintā । tatrāpi [a]gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvādyataḥ <b>kutaściditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b>
<note>(1) P. 957</note>
﻿<pb n="r851"/>
<b>mukhya eva nimitte saṃbhavati na naimittikopaghātaḥ śakyate vak‍tumiti rāddhāntaḥ</b> ।
prathamopanipātini śeṣe nimittasya śeṣalakṣaṇasya saṃbhavānna naimittikaśeṣakāryopaghātaśśakyate
vak‍tumiti । tatra tāvata naimittikaṃ kāryaṃ, <b>jaghanyānāṃ tu</b> paścādvartināṃ śeṣāṇāṃ tu
<b>kṛtatvānnaimittikasya</b> prathamabhāvinyeva nimittopasaṃhṛtiriti <b>yuk‍taiva akriyā śeṣakāryāṇā-
miti</b> ।</p>
<p><b>bhakṣāśravaṇāt</b> । nanu kathamatra śeṣeṇa parikrayāśaṅkā viniyuktaviniyogavirodhāt
ityatrāha---<b>idaṃ brahmaṇa iti dva‍yavadānopasaṃharāt yāgasya śeṣeṇa parikrayaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣa-
vādī</b> । yāgaṃ prati dravyasya <b>yat</b> tādarthyaṃ tat dva‍yavadānamātreṇopasaṃhṛtaṃ iti <b>śeṣasya</b> anyatrā-
tādarthyāt viniyuktaviniyogavirodhābhāvāt <q>‘idaṃ brahmaṇe’</q> iti caturthāśravaṇāt <b>śeṣeṇa</b> brahmādīnāṃ
<b>parikrayaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu tasyāpyavadeyārthatayotpatteḥ yāgārtha-
taiveti nārthāntare viniyogamarhatīti</b> manyate । śeṣasyāpi dravyasya dva‍yavadānārthatayotpatteḥ
yāgārthatvam । tena nānyatra viniyogamarhatīti nānena parikrayaḥ । yadi sakala eva
yāgārthaḥ <b>kathaṃ tarhi sviṣṭakṛdādiyāgaḥ</b> yāgāntare viniyogo nopapadyate । neha[na hi]
devatāyai saṅkalpitena sveneva vyavaharanti <b>śiṣṭā</b> iti bhāvaḥ । <b>uttaraṃ---atyaktatvāccheṣasya
vacanāccopapadyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---atyaktatvena śeṣasya <b>svatva tāvannāpagataṃ kintu satyapi</b>
﻿<pb n="r852"/>
svatve śiṣṭācārānna svatvavyavahāro bhaveti । śrautavacanavirodhena śiṣṭācāre bādhite na
kācidanupapattiḥ । <b>nanu ca dānamapi vacanādbhaviṣyati</b> dānaṃ pratīyata iti । pariharati
---<b>satyaṃ yadi vacanamasti na tvatra dānaṃ śrūyate</b> । <b>nanu <q>‘idaṃ brahmaṇa’</q></b> iti tādarthyaśravaṇāt
dānaṃ pratīyate । tatrāha---<b>tādarthyaśrutistu upakārādapyupapadyata eva ityupakāro darśitaḥ</b> ।
bhakṣyamāṇaṃ hi dravyaṃ nāntarīyakīṃ prītimutpādayatyeva । tatrāpi tu <b>śeṣabhāvo viparīta eva</b> ।
dravyameva pradhānaṃ pratipādyatayā । puruṣa eva guṇabhūtaḥ pratipādakatayā ityanavadyam ।</p>
<trailer>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ tṛtīyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="r853"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>ājyācca sarvasaṃyogāt । yāvadvaviḥ kiñciccoditaṃ pradhānaṃ tadīyāt śeṣāt
samavadyatīti sthitam । upāṃśuyāje saṃśayaḥ kiṃ dhravāsthādaviśeṣāt1 aṅgapradhāna-
sādhāraṇatvādanavadeyaṃ sviṣṭakṛte, utāṅgapradhānaśeṣamapi pradhānaśeṣamityavadeyam । gṛhītā-
dvā jauhavāt camasat</b> । yathā camase tathā'vadeyaṃ uta śeṣābhāvādanavadeyamiti ।
<b>aviśeṣādavadeyamiti prāpte</b> aṅgapradhāne prati sādhāraṇatve'pi śeṣatvāviśeṣāda‍dhrauvādavadeyaṃ
camasena ca viśeṣābhāvāt jauhavādevāvadeyamiti prāpte rāddhānta ucyate---<b>na sādhāraṇe'vadeyaṃ
kevalapradhānaśeṣatvābhāvāt । śiṣṭamapi tat sādhāraṇameva</b> । bhavatu sādhāraṇaṃ tathāpi
kimityāha---<b>pradhānaśeṣācca sviṣṭakṛdavadānam</b> । ya eva hi kevalapradhānaśeṣaḥ tasmādeva
sviṣṭakṛdavadānaṃ puroḍāśādiṣu । na tvaṅgapradhānaśeṣāt । yatra hi pradhānaśeṣādavadānaṃ tatra
kevalapradhānārthatā puroḍāśādau । yatra punaḥ aṅgapradhānaśeṣāt tatrāṅgapradhānārthatā । na cedaṃ
vaiṣamyamāśrayituṃ nyāyyaṃ avaiṣamyeṇopapattau । <b>na ca tadeva kevalapradhānaśeṣa iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ</b>
<note>(1) P. 989</note> <note>(2) G. api śeṣāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r854"/>
<b>sādhāraṇatvādeva</b> । <b>yat‍tu gṛhītasyaiva pratipattiścamasavaditi, tadayuk‍taṃ</b> kutaḥ ?
uttaraṃ---caturavattaṃ <b>juhotīti śravaṇāt</b> । caturavattasya kṛts‍nasyaiva homasaṃbandhāt <b>śeṣayi-
tavye pramāṇābhāvāt</b> । <b>sviṣṭakṛdavadānavacanameva pramāṇamiti</b> cet । na hi śeṣamanta-
reṇa sviṣṭakṛdavadānamupapadyate । tena śeṣayitavye sviṣṭakṛdavadānavacanameva pramāṇamiti cet,
na pramāṇaṃ, anyataḥ <b>prayuk‍te svayamaprayuk‍te puroḍāśādiśeṣe'rthavatvāt</b> । <b>yat‍tu camasava-
dityuk‍taṃ, tanna2 anuvaṣaṭa‍kāraśruterananyaviṣayatvāt camasasya ca grahaṇamātraśruteḥ</b>
<q>‘somasyāg‍ne vīhītyanuṣaṭa‍karoti’</q> iti yeyamanuvaṣaṭa‍kāraśrutiḥ sā ananyaviṣayā, tena bhavati
śeṣayitavye pramāṇam । camasasya ca grahaṇamātraṃ śrūyate । na punarhomaḥ । tenāgrabindu-
nipātenāpi śāstrasyāvirodha iti śeṣasaṃbhavādyuk‍taṃ camase śeṣakāryam । <b>darśanaṃ pratyuktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>sākaṃ prasthāyye</b> । <b>kena viśeṣeṇāyamatideśaḥ</b> ? yāvatā atrāpi śeṣābhāva eva ।
uttaraṃ---<b>prakṛtivaditi prāp‍teḥ kāryārthatayā śeṣaṃ manyate</b> pūrvapakṣavādī । yuktamupāṃśuyāje
śeṣo nāstīti । śeṣakāryāṇāmeva tatsaṃbandhitvena prāpteḥ aniścitatvāt prakṛtitvādupāṃśuyājasya
<note>(1) P. 994</note> <note>(2) R. tatra</note>
﻿<pb n="r855"/>
vikṛtibhūtatvātsākaṃ prasthāyyasya prakṛtivaditi śeṣakāryāṇi prāpyante । teṣu prāp‍teṣu
tādarthyena dravyaṃ śeṣyate ityasti śeṣaḥ । na । <b>vacanātkāryaṃ balavaditi rāddhāntaḥ</b> ।
<q>“saha kumbhībhirabhikrāman juhoti”</q> iti vacanāt saha kumbhībhirabhikramaṇasya ca dṛṣṭārthatvāt
sarvahomaḥ pratīyate । yo'pi sviṣṭakṛdādiprāp‍tyā śeṣatvasaṃbhavaḥ, tatra vacanasya kāryato
balīyastvāt kāryaprāptasviṣṭakṛdādibādha eva nyāyya iti śeṣābhāvānna sviṣṭakṛdādīni kāryāṇi
sākaṃ prasthāyye iti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca</b> । nanu <q>‘uttare'g‍nau payograhān juhoti dakṣiṇe'gnau surāgrahān’</q> iti
gṛhītasyaiva dravyasya homaśravaṇāt śeṣābhāvānna prakṛtitaḥ sviṣṭakṛdādiśaṅkā tatrāha---<b>sautrā-
maṇyāṃ <q>‘ucchinaṣṭi na sarvahutaṃ juhoti’</q> iti punarapi śeṣaśaṅkāyāṃ sviṣṭakṛdiḍaṃ manyate</b> ।
<b>tasyānyatra viniyogāditi rāddhāntaḥ</b> । tasya śeṣasya anyatra viniyogāt saṃbandhāt
brāhmaṇena parikrītena bhakṣaṇena pratipādyatvāt na sviṣṭakṛdiḍamiti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>dravyaikatve</b> । <b>sarvapṛṣṭhe tu pratipradhānaṃ śeṣasaṃskārādavṛttiṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> ।
bahutvāt pradhānānāṃ pratipradhānaṃ ca śeṣakāryaprāpteḥ dravyasya vipulatvāt bhavitavyameva pratipradhānaṃ
<note>(1) P. 994</note> <note>(2) P. 996</note>
﻿<pb n="r856"/>
śeṣasaṃskāraiḥ । <b>agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatayā kṛtaḥ śāstrārtha iti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । ya eva hi śeṣa-
saṃskāraḥ kṛtaḥ sa eva sarveṣāṃ śeṣāṇāmiti pratibhāti agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt । ataḥ
kṛte śāstrārthe nāvṛttau pramāṇamastīti rāddhāntaḥ । <b>nanu sādhāraṇe naiva sviṣṭakṛdastītyuktam</b>
ājye । kathamatra sādhāraṇe sakṛdapi sviṣṭakṛt । pariharati---satyaṃ---<b>akṛtatvāt kāryānta-
rāṇāṃ guṇapradhānatvācceti2 viśeṣaḥ</b> । satyaṃ ājye sviṣṭakṛnnāsti । tatra hi eṣā yuktiḥ ।
upāṃśuyāje kṛtamātra eva na bhaveccheṣakāryaṃ kāryāntarāṇāmakṛtatve pratipattyanarhatvāt । kṛteṣu
kāryāntareṣu guṇaprādhānyāccheṣiṇāṃ guṇapradhānabhāvenāvasthitānāṃ yāgānāṃ sādhāraṇaṃ śeṣatvā-
diti । <q>‘na punassādhāraṇaṃ dravyaṃ’</q> ityetāvatī yuktiḥ । iha tu śeṣo'pyayaṃ pradhānānāmeva ।
ataśśeṣakāryaṃ kāryam ।</p>
<p><b>aindravāyave</b> । <b>nanu cātra pūrvapakṣa eva nāsti vacanāt</b> । dviraindravāyavasya bhakṣa-
yatīti vacanāt । <b>na hi pūrvapakṣe vacanasyānyārthatā śakyate vak‍tum</b> । <b>atrocyate
---ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ somasaṃskārārthatvādbhaśravaṇasya dviriti prayogāntarāpekṣo-
'nuvādo bhaviṣyati</b> । asyārthaḥ---bhakṣaṇena somaḥ saṃskriyate sa ca sakṛt bhakṣaṇenaiva saṃskṛta
<note>(1) P. 997</note> <note>(2) G. pradhānatvāya</note>
﻿<pb n="r857"/>
iti na dviḥ bhakṣaṇamupapadyate । tasmātprayogāntarābhiprāyeṇa dvirityanuvādaḥ । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu
vacanāt kāryakalpaneti vacanādityuktavān</b> । satyaṃ bhakṣaṇena somaḥ saṃskriyate tathāpi
vacanāt dvirvacanāt dvirbhakṣasya vihitatvāt dvirbhakṣaṇameva vacanānurūpameva kāryakalpanamiti
nyāyyam ।</p>
<p><b>some'vacanādbhakṣo na vidyate</b> । <b>some śeṣabhakṣo'sti nāstīti saṃśayaḥ</b> । <b>nanu
saṃśaya evāyamayuktaḥ somasya śeṣabhāvāt</b> । <b>yuktaṃ puroḍāśādīnāṃ dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti
vacanāt tatra yāgopasaṃhārāccheṣavattvam tasya ca bhakṣaḥ । iha tu tadabhāvāt bhakṣāśaṅkaiva
nāsti</b> । <b>kathaṃ tarhi vacanānyetāni---<q>‘dviraindravāyavasya’</q> <q>‘sarvataḥ parihāramāśvinaṃ’</q> <q>‘anu-
ṣaṭa‍karoti’</q> iti ca</b> । ākṣeptā <b>āha---atra hi bhavāneva</b> bhāṣyasamarthanāyodyataḥ
<b>praṣṭavyaḥ । atha vā bhavantvarthakarmāṇi</b> (bhakṣā)śeṣabhāvāt pratipattirnopapadyate । arthakarma tu
dravyaṃ prayok‍tuṃ samarthamiti tadevāstu । yadi kṛtsna eva gṛhītassomo <b>hūyate kathaṃ tarhi
<q>‘aindravāyavasya’</q> <q>‘āśvinaṃ’</q> iti ca</b> । dravyāntaraṃbhakṣaṇenāpi prayujyamānaṃ na aindravāyavaṃ
<note>(1) 998</note>
﻿<pb n="r858"/>
āśvinaṃ iti ca śakyate vak‍tum । uttaraṃ---<b>dharmalakṣaṇārtho bhaviṣyati</b> । aindravāyavasya
aindravāyavadharmakasyetyarthaḥ । <b>tasmādanupapannamevedaṃ kiṃ some vidyate na veti । athai-
tebhyo vacanebhyaḥ</b> śeṣāśrayebhyaḥ <b>śeṣayitavyamiti kalpyate</b> । na । <b>aprayojakatvā-
ccheṣāṇāṃ</b> na śeṣakāryāṇi dravyaṃ prayuñjate । kutaḥ ? <b>saṃskāryapradhānaṃ hi saṃskārakarma
bhavati</b> । saṃskāryaṃ dravyamucyate saṃskāryeṣu pradhāneṣu apradhānabhūtāssaṃskārāḥ । <b>na cā-
pradhānaṃ</b> pradhānaṃ <b>prayuṅk‍te</b> । tasmānna śeṣakāryairdravyaṃ prayujyate । <b>tasmādvak‍tavyo'tra nyāyaḥ</b>
śeṣasaṃbhave । ucyate---<b>nātra sarvahome pramāṇamasti</b> । yasmāt <b>aindravāyavādiṣu tādarthyena
grahaṇam</b> । <b>gṛhītasya ca ekadeśenāpi kṛte kṛtaiva aindravāyavatā</b> । <b>kimiti sarvasya śeṣaḥ</b>
ayamabhiprāyaḥ---rasībhūtassomaḥ devatoddeśena parigṛhītaḥ । tasya ca dravyasya devatoddeśaḥ evaṃ
arthavān bhavati yadi tāmeva devatāmuddiśya tyajyate । tasya ca tyajyamānasya <q>‘aṇvyā dhārayā
juhoti’</q> iti niyamāt krameṇa tyāgaḥ । tatra tu agrabindunipātena kṛte devatoddeśena grahaṇe-
'rthavati na sarvahome pramāṇamastītyagrabindumātreṇa yāgopasaṃhārādasti śeṣaḥ । <b>nanu ca sarvasya
yāgaśeṣatā śrūyate <q>‘somena yajeta’</q> iti</b> tena kṛts‍nenaiva yāgaḥ kartavya iti kṛts‍nasya homaḥ ।
pariharati---na kṛts‍nenaiva yāgaḥ । <b>tatrāpyekadeśenaiva somenetyupapannatvāt</b> । avayava-
﻿<pb n="r859"/>
dvāreṇāpi karaṇasaṃbandhopapatteḥ na kṛts‍nahome pramāṇam । <b>tathā cāsya</b> rasasya grahaṇaṃ
ṛjīṣādeśca tyāgaḥ yadyekadeśenāpi kṛte kṛtaḥ śāstrārthaḥ <b>kimiti tarhi dvirhaviṣo'vadyati
ityetasmādevopasaṃhāraḥ</b> yathā some ekadeśenāpi yāgaḥ tathā puroḍāśepi ekadeśenāpi yāga
iti vināpi dvirhaviṣo'vadyati iti vacanaṃ ekadeśenāpi yāgopasaṃhāraḥ prāpta eva । kimitye-
tasmā1dupasaṃhāropanyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ । <b>yathākathaṃcita tatrāpyupasaṃhārasiddheḥ</b> । <b>tatrāpi</b>
puroḍāśe <b>yathākathaṃcit</b> yena kenacidavayavenopasaṃhāraḥ prāpnoti । rāddhāntamāṃśaṅkayati
---<b>niyamārthaṃ taditi cet</b> । dva‍yavadānavacanaṃ niyamārthamiti cet kṛts‍napradāne'pi prāpte'va-
yavaniyamārthaṃ taditi । dūṣayati---<b>sarvapradānaṃ tarhi pūrvapakṣavādino na ghaṭate</b> dva‍yavadāna-
niyame śrute sarvapradāne śaṅkā na yuktā । <b>kiñca ekadeśenāpyupapadyata iti naitāvatā sarvaṃ
na hotavyam</b> । <b>sarvahomenāpyupapadyata eva</b> । tena somaśeṣasadbhāvo nityavannopapadyata eva ।
<b>tasmādvaktavyo viśeṣaḥ</b> puroḍāśasomayoḥ । puroḍāśe vināpi dva‍yavadānavacanaṃ kṛts‍nena
homaḥ prāp‍noti । some tu vinā vacanaṃ ekadeśenaiva homa iti । <b>ayamabhidhīyate</b>
viśeṣaḥ । some agravindunipātena <b>kṛte śāstrārthe punaḥ karaṇaṃ tāvannopapadyate ekadeśena
kṛtaḥ śāstrārtha iti pradarśitam</b> । yadi vināpi vacanena ekadeśena śāstrārthaḥ saṃpadyate
some'gravindunipātamātreṇa <b>katha tarhi sarvapradānāśaṅkā</b> ? dva‍yavadānasya vacanenaiva
<note>(1) G. ekasmāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r860"/>
<b>śrutatvāt</b> । uttaraṃ---śrute'pi vacane <b>avakhaṇḍyāvakhaṇḍya dātavyaṃ iti vacanārthāvagamāt</b> ।
avadāyāvadāya hotavyaṃ iti manyamānena sarvapradānamāśaṅkitam na sarvapradānaṃ <b>yāgārthatvāt
dravyasyetyupasaṃhāraḥ</b> । yāgārthaṃ hi dravyaṃ tena sakṛtkṛto yāgaḥ na guṇānurodhenāvartayitavyaḥ
ityupasaṃhāro dva‍yavadānena yāgasya । <b>tasmādekadeśaniyama evāyam</b> dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti ।
ekadeśena kṛts‍nena vā yāge prāpte ekadeśe niyamo'yaṃ na punaraprāptaikadeśahomavidhiḥ ।
yata evāvayavenāpi śāstrārthasaṃpattiḥ । <b>ata eva laukikāḥ pāyasādi devatoddeśena</b>
<b>kṛtvā tata uda‍dhṛtya kiñciddevetāyai datvā</b> bhavati ca devatoddeśena grahaṇe'rthavati <b>śeṣaṃ
yatheṣṭaṃ viniyuñjate</b> । anyathā kṛts‍nameva devatāyai dada‍yuḥ <b>tasmādvidyamāne śeṣe upapadyate
saṃśayaḥ kiṃ bhakṣaṇenaiva śeṣapratipattiḥ uta neti</b> । <b>tatra vacanābhāvānna bhakṣaṇeneti pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ, bhakṣaviśeṣavidhānādasti bhakṣa iti dvitīyaḥ</b> । <b>anyathā</b> hi asati bhakṣe bhakṣa-
viśeṣavidhānaṃ dviraindravāyavasyetyādi <b>nopapadyate</b> । <b>kāmaṃ mopapādi na punarvacanādṛte
śakyate bhakṣaḥ pratipat‍tum</b> । na cedaṃ nopapadyate <b>yadā bhakṣayati tadā dvirityevaṃ</b> viśeṣa-
vidhānopapatteḥ । <b>evaṃ tarhi</b> yadi nityavadbhakṣaṇaṃ na prāp‍noti tadā <b>etānyena</b> viśiṣṭasya
bhakṣaṇasya vidhāyakāni bhavantviti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r861"/>
<p><b>camaseṣu samākhyānāt । camaseṣvidānīṃ vacanābhāvānnāsti bhakṣa iti pūrva-
pakṣaḥ</b> । tat camasataivānyathā nopapadyate yadi tatra camanaṃ na syāt । tasmāt <q>‘ayamasya
camasaḥ’ </q> <q>‘ayamasya camasaḥ’</q> iti vacanāni <q>‘praituhotuścamasaḥ’</q> ityevamādīnyeva bhakṣavidhāyakāni
bhavantu <b>yathaiva viśeṣavidhānamanyathā nopapadyata iti pūrvatra vacanaṃ</b> tathehāpi camasatvānupapatteḥ
camanavidhānamiti । nanu dravyāntaravidhānenāpi camasatā upapadyate ityatrāha---<b>dravyāntara-
camanaṃ 3takṣaṇādi ca na kalpitaṃ bhavati</b> । dravyāntarameva tāvaccamanīyaṃ kalpanīyam ।
klṛptasomadravyasaṃbhave tasya cāyāgaśeṣatvāt । tacchuddhaye takṣaṇādi kalpayitavyam । some tu
tatra pānepi na somenocchiṣṭā bhavati iti vacanāt na takṣaṇakalpanā । tasmāt somacamana-
nimittaiva camasatā । sā ca vināvacanaṃ nopapadyata iti vacanānyetāni <q>“praitu hotuścamasaḥ”</q>
ityevamādīni ।</p>
<p><b>udgātṛcamasamekasya śrutisaṃyogāt</b> । atra catvāraḥ pakṣāḥ kimekasyodgāturbhakṣaḥ,
uta sarveṣāmṛtvijāṃ, atha vā subrahmaṇyavarjitānāṃ chandogānāṃ trayāṇāṃ, atha vā caturṇāmapi
chandogānāṃ udgātṛprastotṛpratihartṛsubrahmaṇyānāṃ iti । tatra taccamasatā anyathā nopapadyata iti
camanavacanānyetānīti sthitam ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 999</note> <note>(2) P. 1001</note> <note>(3) G. bhakṣaṇādi</note>
﻿<pb n="r862"/>
<p>tatra prathamapūrvapakṣavādī udgātṛpratipadikasya ṛtvigviśeṣe rūḍhatvāt prātipadikārthasya ca
pradhānatvāt tadanurodhitayā <q>‘pāśān’ </q> itivat bahutvamavivakṣitamiti manyate । dvitīyapūrvapakṣavādī
tu vacanārthasyāvivakṣātaḥ prātipadikasya lakṣaṇikatvavarṇanameva nyāyyam । ubhayorapi
vibhaktiprātipadikaborevamarthavattā bhaviṣyati । pāśe tu prātipadikasya lakṣaṇīyābhāvena
lakṣaṇayā varṇanāsaṃbhavāt agatyā vacanasyāvivakṣetyudgātṛlakṣitānāṃ sarveṣāmeva ṛtvijāṃ bhakṣa
ityāha---<b>apasubrahmaṇyavādī tu</b> gānakriyākāritayā yaugikenodgātṛśabdena trayāṇāṃ gāna-
kāriṇābhudgātṛprastortṛpratihartṝṇāṃ bhakṣa ityuktavān । rāddhāntavādī tu rūḍhiryogamapaharati iti
yaugikatve niraste ekodgātṛsamākhyātapravacanādhyetṛtvāt udgātṛśabdena chatrinyāyena sarveṣāṃ
chandogānāṃ lakṣaṇā । tataśca teṣāmeva bhakṣa ityāha---<b>prodgātṝṇāmityatra kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ na
gānaṃ lakṣayati samākhyaiva kimiti lakṣayati</b>। asyārthaḥ---kena punaḥ kāraṇena gāna-
kriyākartṝn na lakṣayati । yaugikaḥ udgātṛśabdaḥ kimiti na bhavatītyarthaḥ । <b>samākhyaiva
kimiti lakṣayati</b> kena hetunā udgātṛśabdo lakṣaṇayā vartata iti yāvat । rāddhāntaikadeśī
samarthayamāna āha---<b>ucchabdasyāvivakṣā prāpnoti gānakāriṣu lakṣyamāṇeṣu</b> । yadyudgāyatī-
tyadgātocyate tadā eka evodgānakārī na tu trayo'pi । yadi trayo'pi gānakāriṇaḥ
udgātṛśabdena gṛhyante tadā ucchabdasyāvivakṣā prāp‍noti । <b>tathā ca darśitam । anyadeva
gānamanyadevodgānamiti । samākhyāne</b> tu lakṣayati---<b>nāyaṃ doṣaḥ1</b> । tatra vyutpattimanta-
reṇa udgātṛśabdaḥ ṛtvigviśeṣavacano lakṣaṇayā anyānapi chandogānupasthāpayatīti nāsti
ucchabdasyāvivakṣādoṣaḥ pūrvapakṣī punarāha---<b>nanu codgānaṃ nāma gānameva nāsti</b> । tena
pralambata ityādivat arthāntarānupasthāpakatvāt ucchabdasya gānakāriṇa udgātṛśabdenokta
<note>(1) naiṣa doṣaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r863"/>
iti nāstyucchabdāvivakṣādoṣaḥ । arthavato hi avivakṣādoṣaḥ nānarthakasya । <b>bhaktirhi sā</b>
sāmnaḥ । sāmabhāgo bhaktiḥ । yā dvitīyābhaktiḥ yāmudgātā ṛtviga‍gāyati <b>sā codgītha-
śabdavācyā</b> rūḍha‍yaiva । <b>na punaḥ</b> tatrocchabdanvito gāyatirvartate । nanūdgīthaṃ gāyan‍nu-
dgāyatītyucyate । ataḥ ucchabdasahito gāyatistatraiva vartate ityatrāha---<b>yaḥ punaḥ udgāye-
dityevamādiṣu prayogaḥ udgīthaṃ gāyediti tatrārthaḥ ucchabdo hi tatra bhaktilakṣaṇārthaḥ । gānaṃ
tu gānameva</b> । tatrāpi gāyatirgītimātra brūte । kevalamucchabdaḥ tatrodgīthaśabdasyāvayava-
bhūtasmamudāyalakṣaṇārthaḥ evamucchabdasahitasya gāyateḥ samudāyaśak‍tirna kalpitā bhavati iti ।
yasmādgānamevodgānaṃ <b>tasmādudgāteti ṛtvigviśeṣanāmaivaitat । na punarudgānasya kartaudgātā</b>
rūḍho'yamudgātṛśabdaḥ ṛgvigviśeṣe । na punarasau yaugikaḥ; gānakāritayā sarvatra prasak‍teḥ
yadi hi udgānaṃ nāma gānaviśeṣaḥ syāt tadā tatkāritayā ṛtvigviśeṣe śabdavṛttirlabhyate na
caitadasti । tasmāda‍‌rūḍha evāyamiti । paramasiddhāntī tvāha---yata eva rūḍho'yamudgātṛśabdaḥ
<b>ata eva samākhyeva lakṣayituṃ prabhavati na gānakriyeti rāddhāntitam</b> । gānakriyāyā lakṣa-
katve yaugikatvaprasaṅgāt । na ca rūḍhau satyāṃ yaugikatvāśrayaṇaṃ yuktam । nanu rūḍhyāśrayaṇe
bahutvaṃ nopapadyate । lakṣaṇayopapadyata iti cenna । lakṣaṇaiva doṣaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---rūḍhyā
yaugikatve parihṛte vacanāt tadanuguṇā lakṣaṇā । na punaḥ vacanamupalabhya parāvṛttya yaugikatvā-
śrayaṇamiti । yata eva samākhyā lakṣayati---<b>ata eva ca apasubrahmaṇyavādino'pi
apanyāyavādina eva</b>। ekapravacananiveśena lakṣaṇāyāṃ sarvepi tatpravacanakāriṇo lakṣyante
iti na śakyate subrahmaṇyaṃ parityuk‍tum । nanu <q>‘niṣadyodgātārasstuvanti’</q> iti subrahmaṇyavarjitā
﻿<pb n="r864"/>
lakṣyante tathehāpi syāt ityatrāha---<b>na cātra stutyādiśravaṇamiva saṅkoce pramāṇamasti</b> ।
tatra hi stutisaṃbandhāt stotrakāriṇāṃ trayāṇāmeva grahaṇam । iha tu nāstīti viśeṣaḥ ।
<b>nanu ca prodgātṝṇāmiti triṣveva bahuvacanopapatteḥ</b> kapiñjalavat---<b>kimiti sasu-
brahmaṇyānāṃ bhakṣaḥ</b> kalpyate । uttaraṃ---<b>yadi bahuvacanopapattyarthaṃ satyameva</b> trayāṇāmeva
grahaṇam । <b>atrodgātṛśabdastadarthakāriṣu vartata ityuktam</b> । ato bahuvacanamatra prātipādi-
kasyārthāntaravṛttau hetuḥ na svārthanvayamātre vyāpṛtam । bahuvacanena lakṣaṇāvṛttirāśritā
lakṣaṇā caikapravacanasaṃbandhāditi sarve chandogā grāhyāḥ । tasmāt suṣ‍ṭhūcyate sasubrahmaṇyānāṃ
bhakṣa iti ।</p>
<p><b>grāvastuto bhakṣo na vidyate'nāmnānāt । uk‍taṃ vacanāt samākhyānācca bhakṣaṇam</b>।
idānīṃ <b>vacanārthavipratipattau saṃpratipattyarthametānyadhikaraṇāni ārabhyante</b> । anenāvāntara-
saṅgatimāha । nanu <q>‘sarve hāriyojanasya2 lipsante’ </q> iti vacanāt sarveṣāṃ hāriyojane bhakṣa iti
grāvastuto'pi bhakṣa ityatrāha---<b>sarveṣāṃ hāriyojanasya lipsanta iti camasināmeveti pūrvapakṣa-</b>
<note>(1) P. 1004</note> <note>(2) R. &amp; G. hāriyojanaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r865"/>
<b>vādinā śaṅkitam । vākyaśeṣāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---<q>“yathācamasamanyāṃścamasāṃścamasino
bhakṣayanti । athaitasya hāriyojanasya sarva eva lipsante”</q> iti vākyaśeṣe camasināṃ
saṅkīrtanāt sarvaśabdaḥ camasiṣveva vartata iti camasināmeva hāriyojane bhakṣaḥ । 2na camasī
grāvastuditi tasya bhakṣābhāvaḥ । <b>asandigdhatvāt prakṛtavacanatayā sarvaśabdasya nopasaṃhāro
yuktaḥ vākyaśeṣāditi rāddhāntaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---sarve hāriyojanasyeti nissandigdhasakala-
ṛtvikpratyayaḥ । prakṛtāśca ṣoḍaśartvijaḥ । prakṛtavacanaśca sarvaśabdaḥ । sa yadi cama-
siṣveva avasthāpyate tadā sarvaśabdārtho bādhyeta । tasmādvākyaśeṣādupasaṃhāro na yuktaḥ ।
yadi vākyaśeṣe camasiśabdaḥ parokṣārthavṛttiḥ syāt tadāpyupasaṃhāro'stu । na ca camasiśabdasya
parokṣārthatā camasāṃścamasino bhakṣayanti । hāriyojane tu sarve bhakṣayantīti mahābhāgatayā
hāriyoṃjana stūvate iti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>vaṣa‍ṭakārāñca bhakṣayet । atra <q>‘vaṣa‍ṭkartuḥ prathamabhakṣaḥ’</q> iti guṇaśravaṇāt na
bhakṣavidhānaṃ ityāśaṅkya viśiṣṭavidhānāditi rāddhāntitam</b> । anena yathāśrutaṃ bhāṣya-
kārīyamadhikaraṇamanubhāṣitaṃ ākṣep‍tum । ākṣepamāha---<b>nanu cātra viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ nāsti</b> ।
<b>na hi prāthamyaṃ nāma bhakṣasya kārakam, yena viśiṣṭakriyā vidhīyeta</b> । asyārthaḥ---tatra
<note>(1) P. 1006</note> <note>(2) R. nācamasī grāvastut</note>
﻿<pb n="r866"/>
hi viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ bhavati yatra hi viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati । na ca prāthamyabhakṣaṇayo-
rviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati । akārakatvāt prāthamyasya । kārakaṃ hi kārakavibhaktyā kriyāṃ
prati viśeṣaṇatayā upādīyate । tena tatra yuk‍to viśiṣṭavidhiḥ । yatra punarakārakatvāt na
kārakavibhaktyā nirdiśyate na tatra kriyāsaṃbandha iti kuto viśiṣṭavidhānam । na ca prāthamyaṃ
kārakaṃ, kramo hi saḥ । sa ca padārthāśritaḥ padārthaguṇo na kārakaṃ, padārthanivṛttāvavyā-
pārāt । tasmāt rāddhānta evānupapanna iti । samādhātā āha---yata eva viśiṣṭa-
bidhānaśaṅkā nāsti । <b>ata eva pūrvapakṣavādī na viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ saṃbhavatītyāśaṅkitavān</b> ।
ākṣeptā''ha---bhavatu pūrvapakṣaḥ, <b>kathaṃ tarhi rāddhāntaḥ</b> ? samādhātā āha---<b>prathamabhakṣa
iti padadvayasya ekārthābhidhānāt abhihitavidhānācca ekārthavirdhi manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yadi viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo na bhavet tadā na syādekārthavidhiḥ । yadā punaḥ prathamabhakṣa
iti samāsaḥ tatra ca padadvayena prāthamyaviśiṣṭaḥ eka eva bhakṣarūpo'rtho'bhidhīyate । yaccābhi-
dhīyate tadeva vidhīyate iti abhidhānādeva ekārthavidhiḥ । ākṣeptā āha---<b>tadayuktam
samāsepi hi tada‍bhūtādhikaraṇanyāyāt 1apagatirnaivāsti</b> । padadvayena ekārtho'bhidhīyata
iti vadatā tvayā pratipadamarthānabhyupagamāta sphoṭa evābhyupagataḥ । sa cāyuktaḥ । samāseṃ
hi tada‍bhūtādhikaraṇanyāyasya pratipadābhidhānasādhakasya naivāpagatirasti । tena kathamekārthā-
bhidhānam ? samādhatte---<b>satyamevaṃ, tathāpi pūrvottarapadasaṃbandhāyattā samāse ca padārthā-
ntarasaṅgatiḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---nāhaṃ sphoṭapakṣamaṅgīkṛtya ekārthābhidhānaṃ samāse bravīmi, kintu
<note>(1) G. avagati</note>
﻿<pb n="r867"/>
padadvayena viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇabhūtau arthau abhidadhatā viśiṣṭa eko'rthaḥ pratipādyate । tasya ca
padārthāntareṇa paścātsaṃbandhaḥ । vākye tu padārthāntarasaṃbandhānāṃ parasparaṃ saṃbandhaḥ । nīla-
mutpalamānaya iti dvayorānayatinā saṃbandhaḥ pūrvaṃ, paścāt guṇaguṇisaṃbandhaḥ । samāse tu
<q>‘nīlotpalamānaya’</q> iti guṇaguṇibhāvena parasparānvitayoreva ānayanasaṃbandha । tenehāpi
prathamabhakṣa iti prāthamyabhakṣayoḥ guṇaguṇibhāvena saṃbaddhayoḥ karotyupāttena vidhinā saṃbandhaḥ, na
punaḥ parasparāsaṃbandhayoḥ । tadā hi anekārthavidhānaṃ bhavati । samāse ca parasparasaṃbandhaḥ
pratīyata iti <b>yuktamuk‍taṃ samāsena ca vidadhato nānekaguṇavidhānaṃ duṣkaramiti । ataḥ
siddhamatra viśiṣṭavidhānam</b> । evaṃ ca vadato <b>bhāṣyanibandhanakārasya</b> abhihitakramo
viniyojyo vidheyaśca । yaḥ punaḥ pāñcamikaśrutyādigamyaḥ vidhivitānākhyo'bhidhānaviniyoga-
śūnyaḥ nāsau vidhīyata iti darśanaṃ lakṣyate । sarvatraiva hi śabdaśaktivaśenāyaṃ śāstrārthaṃ
varṇayati । <b>vivaraṇakārastu</b> vastusvabhāvanirūpaṇena । tena tanmate sarvatraiva kramasyā-
vidheyatvamiti tatraivoktam ।</p>
<p><b>homābhiṣavābhyāṃ ca । <q>‘abhiṣutya hutvā bhakṣayati’</q> ityapi bhakṣavidhānam</b> ।
kasmātpunaḥ bhakṣaṇaṃ vidhīyate iti darśanaṃ ? abhiṣutya hutveti kimiti homabhiṣavāveva na
vidhīyete bhakṣaṇamanūdyata evārthaprāptaṃ iti tatrāha---<b>homābhiṣavayoḥ prāptatvāt tatra</b> । nanu
ca homābhiṣavāveva bhakṣaṇāṅgatayā kimiti na vidhīyete । bhakṣaṇaṃ vā taṅgatayā kimiti na
<note>(1) P. 1008</note>
﻿<pb n="r868"/>
vidhīyate ityatrāha---<b>aṅgatayā ca vidhānānupapatteḥ</b> iti । vidhānāntarābhāvāt <b>bhakṣa eva
vidhātavyaḥ</b> iti ।</p>
<p><b>pratyakṣopadeśāt । hotṛcamasaḥ ityevamādyābhiḥ samākhyābhiḥ sakalacamasa-
saṃbandhāvagateḥ abhiṣutya hutvā ityanyatra camasebhyo bhakṣaḥ iti manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> ।
sakalasya camasya hotrādisaṃbaddhatvāt camasavyatirekeṇa homābhiṣavanimittaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ bhaviṣyatītyarthaḥ ।
evaṃ prāpte ucyate---<b>abhiṣavanimittako'pi bhakṣaḥ camaseṣu bhavatyeva । nanu hotṛcamasa
iti sakalacamasāvagatirityuk‍taṃ, satyamuk‍taṃ, na punarabhiṣavanimittatāṃ</b> bhakṣaṇasya <b>bādhi-
tumarhati</b> । abādhite ca bhakṣasya homābhiṣavanimittatve prāp‍notyeva camaseṣvapi tannimitto bhakṣaḥ
yasmāt <b>prāpakāṇyetāni vacanāni</b> na punaḥ parisaṅkhyāpakāni । kuta ityāha---<b>hotṛcamasa
ityasyāṃ saṃbandhāvagatau na saṃbandhāntaranivṛttiḥ śakyate'vagantum । prāptimātrāvagateḥ ।
prāptau hi satyāṃ kasyedamityapekṣāyāṃ anyanivṛttiḥ pratīyate</b> । sāmānyataḥ prāptau satyāṃ
kasyedamiti viśeṣāpekṣāyāṃ viśaṣanirdeśāt anyanivṛttiḥ pratīyate---<b>yathā <q>‘āg‍neya’</q> ityuk‍te</b>
<note>(1) P. 1009</note>
﻿<pb n="r869"/>
<b>naindrāgnasyāvagatiḥ । iha punaḥ prāptiphalatvādvākyasya nānyanivṛttiḥ śakyate'vagantum</b>
hotṛcamasa ityanena bhakṣaṇaṃ vidhīyate viśiṣṭakartṛkaṃ na punaḥ anyanimittakaṃ bhakṣaṇāntaraṃ nivartyate ।
<b>nanu ca prāptāvapi</b> prāpakatvepi vākyānāṃ <b>sakalāvagatervirodho vidyata eva</b> । sakala-
saṃbandhāvagamāddhi sakalaścamasibhiḥ bhakṣyata iti lakṣyate । tenānyasmin bhakṣaṇāntare sati
virodho'styeva । pariharati---<b>satyaṃ</b> virodhaḥ <b>syāt---yadi samākhyayā prāptiḥ । iha punaḥ
praitu hotuścamasa iti vacanāt</b> prāptiḥ । asyārthaḥ---satyaṃ yadi sakalacamasasaṃbandhaḥ hotuḥ
samākhyayā pratīyate । na ca samākhyātaḥ prāptiḥ । kintu <b>vacanāt</b> । nanu vacanamapi
samākhyānupapatteḥ kalpyamānaṃ yathā samākhyānameva sakalaviṣayaṃ kalpyate tatrāha---<b>kalpyaṃ tat</b>
abhiṣutyahutvā ityanena vacanāntarāvirodhena vacanaṃ kalpyate kalpyatvāt । tenaikadeśadvāreṇa
sakalasaṃbandhasamākhyopapattiḥ ।</p>
<p><b>ekapātre kramādadhvaryuḥ । sthitaṃ camasino'bhiṣotārohotāraśca bhakṣayantīti ।
atredānīṃ kaḥ prathamaṃ bhakṣayediti vicāryate</b> । anena avāntaramasaṅgatimāha । pūrvapakṣamāha
<b>adhvaryuḥ prathamaṃ bhakṣayati hastagatatvāt yasya haste sa jayatīti nyāyāt</b> । yasya hi haste
<note>(1) P. 1010</note>
﻿<pb n="r870"/>
dravyamasti sa tāvat sannihitaṃ bhakṣayati paścāditare iti । <b>nanu vaṣaṭa‍kartuḥ prathamabhakṣa iti
vacanāt kathamadhvaryorbhakṣaḥ</b> । na vacanapratipakṣo nyāyya iti bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>bhakṣamātra-
vidhānādapi vaṣaṭa‍kartureva prathamaṃ bhakṣa iti manvānasya punaridamadhikaraṇam</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yadyapi vacanaṃ bhakṣamātraṃ vidadhāti tathāpi nyāyata eva prāthamyaṃ labhyate iti manvānasya
nedamadhikaraṇamārabhyata iti । prāthamyavidhānamaṅgīkṛtyāyaṃ vicāra iti yāvat । <b>pradarśitaṃ
ca prāthamyādvaṣaṭa‍kārasyeti</b> kṛtvācintayedamadhikaraṇamārabdhamiti । darśitaṃ cedaṃ prāthamyaṃ

nyāyābhidhānaṃ akiñcitkaraṃ syāt । nanu vacanopanyāsastarhiṃ nopapadyate tatrāha---<b>vacanāccetyupa-
saṃhṛtam</b> । kṛtvācintoddhāṭanamidamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>vacanādanujñātabhakṣaṇam । kimanujñātena bhakṣayitavyaṃ utānanujñāteneti prāpti---
darśanārthamidamadhikaraṇam</b> । anujñānaprāptiṃ vācanirkī pradarśayituṃ uttaracintārthamidamadhi-

﻿<pb n="r871"/>
<b>sati kiṃ laukikena śabdenānujñāpanaṃ uta vaidikeneti cintā</b> । mantrāmnānāt <b>vaidikena</b>
mantreṇānujñāpanamiti <b>niyamaḥ</b> । <b>idamapi mantraprāptidarśanārthameva</b> । etaccādhikaraṇadvayaṃ uttara-
cintāśeṣabhūtameva । ata eva pūrvādhikaraṇaṃ likhitvā na punaḥ sūtraṃ likhitam ।</p>
<p><b>tatrārthāt prativacanam</b> । <b>idānīṃ prativacane sandehaḥ kiṃ mantreṇa prativacanaṃ uta
laukikena śabdeneti</b> । anena sandehamanubhāṣate ākṣep‍tum । pūrvapakṣābhāvenākṣepamāha
---<b>kathaṃ punaḥ upahūta iti mantrām‍nāne sati sandehaḥ</b> । prativacanasamarthasyāsya2 <b>mantrasya</b>
liṅgena viniyuktatvāt anenaiva mantreṇa prativacanaṃ yuktamityarthaḥ । samādhatte---<b>upahvayasvetyasyaiva
śeṣaṃ manvānasya</b> sandehaḥ । anujñāpanārthamantraśeṣabhūtatvāt anujñāpanārtha eveti । kutaḥ ?
na hi <b>anujñāpanāt pūrvapaṭhitaṃ prativacanasamarthamapi prativacanāyālaṃ bhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ</b> ।
yattvanujñāpanātpūrvapaṭhitaṃ tat pūrvaṃ prayoktavyam । na cānujñāpane akṛte anujñānaṃ prayujyata
ityarthāt anujñāpanārtha evāyaṃ mantraḥ iti । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu pūrvataivātra bādhyata iti
rāddhāntitavān</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathāviniyogaṃ krama iti liṅgāta viniyoge sthite pūrvataiva
mantraprayogasya bādhyate na punarliṅgaviniyoga iti ।</p>
