﻿<pb n="r872"/>
<p><b>tadekapātrāṇāṃ samavāyāt</b> । <b>sthite hyanujñāpane prativacane ca kimekapātrāṇā-
mevedamanujñāpanaṃ</b> prativacanaṃ ca <b>utāviśeṣeṇeti</b> cintā । anenāvāntarasaṅgatimāha ।
avidhānādaviśeṣaṃ <b>manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । nātra ekapātre bhinnapātre veti viśeṣaḥ śrūyate ।
tasmāt sarvatreti । <b>dṛṣṭārthatayā tu rāddhāntaḥ</b> । ekapātre'nujñāpanaṃ prativacanaṃ ca dṛṣṭārthaṃ
nānyatreti tatraiva bhavati । dṛṣṭakārye kāryāntarakalpanāyā asaṃbhavāt ।</p>
<p><b>yājyāpanayenāpanītī bhakṣaḥ</b> । <b>yājyāmātrāpanayaṃ manvānasya pūrvapakṣavādino
hotureva bhakṣa ityabhiprāyaḥ</b> । <q>‘svayaṃ vā niṣadya yajati’</q> ityanena hotussakāśādyājyāmātra-
mevāpanītaṃ na punarvaṣaṭa‍kāraḥ । tena vaṣaṭa‍karaṇanimitto bhakṣo hotureva । atra codayati
---<b>kimanavānaśrutiḥ niṣadya yajati iti vacanaṃ</b> bhavānna <b>paśyati</b> । yo hi paśyati sa
kathamevaṃ brūyāt । anavānatā yaṣṭavyaṃ ityavicchedakatā hotṛvyāpāre homayāgayorupadiśyate ।
tatra yajamānenāpi hotṛvyāpāraṃ kurvāṇenāvicchedo'ṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ । tatra yadi yajamāno
yājyāmātrameva kuryāt vaṣaṭa‍kāraṃ tu hotaiva kuryāt tadā'vānyādyajamānaḥ tadā yājyāmātreṇa
vaṣaṭa‍kārarahitena yāgānupapatteḥ kathaṃ yājyāmātraprayoge yajamāneneṣṭaṃ syāditi bhāvaḥ ।
<b>na na paśyati</b>, paśyatyeva । <b>kintu yājyāmātre</b> । <b>evaṃ dvayamapyetadupapadyata</b>
<note>(1)P. 1012</note> <note>(2) P. 1013</note>
﻿<pb n="r873"/>
<b>evetyabhiprāyaḥ</b> । yājyāprayoga evedamanavānaṃ avicchedātmakaṃ ghaṭate tathā yājyāyā api
yāganiṣpattyarthatvāt taduccāraṇepi bhavatyeva yāgaṃ prati kartṛteti anavānayāgakartṛtvarūpadvayaṃ yājyā-
prayogamātrepyupapadyata iti na vaṣaṭ‍kārāpanaye kiñcitpramāṇamasti । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<b>yājyābhi-
dhāne'pi yajeḥ kartṛtvamupapadyata evetyarthaḥ</b> । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu manyate---satyamupapannam</b> ।
<b>na punaḥ vaṣaṭa‍kārāpanaye hi kiñcitpramāṇamasti iti savaṣaṭa‍kārameva yājyāprayogamātrepyu-
papadyate iti vyāpāramaṅgīkṛtya kartṛtvaṃ yuktamiti</b> । asyārthaḥ---yatraiva hotā prāptaḥ
tatraiva yajamāno'pi niyujyate savaṣaṭa‍kāre ca hotā prāptaḥ iti, savaṣaṭ‍kāra eva yājyāvyāpāre
ca hotā prāpta iti savaṣaṭa‍kāra eva yājyāvyāpāre yajamānaviniyoga iti na vaṣaṭa‍kārāpanayane
kiñcitpramāṇamasti । tataścāpanīte vaṣaṭa‍kāre nāsti hotuḥ vaṣaṭa‍kāranimitto bhakṣaḥ iti ।
<b>yat‍tu pravaro nāpanīyata iti tadatraupadeśikatvāt yathā pravaro nāpanīyate
tathā darśitam</b> । asyārthaḥ---pravarastāvadaupadeśikaḥ sa yatraiva saguṇaḥ kartuṃ śakyate
tatraiva kartavyaḥ hotari cāsau saguṇaḥ kartuṃ śakyaḥ, na yajamāne bhraṣṭāvasaratvāt ।
vikṛtau hi bādhāt viguṇamapi kriyate na punaḥ prakṛtāviti darśitaṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<p><b>phalacamaso naimittiko bhakṣavikāraḥ</b> । <b>phalacamasaḥ ijyāvikāraḥ uta bhakṣavikāra
ityasmin saṃśaye brūmaḥ</b> । <b>naivātra saṃśayaḥ yasmāt tamasmai bhakṣaṃ prayacchet iti bhakṣasaṃba</b>-
<note>(1) P. 1016</note>
﻿<pb n="r874"/>
<b>ndhitvena vidhānāt bhakṣe somaṃ vikaroti na yāge</b> yatraiva hi śrūyate tatraiva vidhīyamānaḥ
tatsādhānabhūtameva nivartayati । kārakaṃ hi bhakṣe phalacamasaḥ śrūyate na yāge tamasmai bhakṣaṃ
kuryāditi śravaṇāt na tena yajeteti । evaṃ tāvat yāgasaṃbandhitvenāśravaṇāduktam ।
idānīṃ satyapi saṃbandhaśravaṇe aśakyatāmāha---<b>na cejyāvikāraśśakyate vak‍tum utpatti-
śiṣṭatvāt somasya</b> । somena yejetatyutpattāveva yāgaḥ somānvitaḥ pratīto nānyānvitaṃ
pratyetuṃ śakyate । <b>vidhīyamāne ca</b> dravyāntare <q>‘guṇaścāpūrvasaṃyoga’</q> ityanena nyāyena
---<b>karmāntaratvāpattiḥ</b> । <b>tataśca bhakṣavikāro'pi na syāt dūreṇejyāvikāraḥ</b> । <b>atrā-
bhidhīyate---nejyāvikāramantareṇa bhakṣaṃ vikartuṃ samarthaḥ phalacamasaḥ</b> । <b>kutaḥ</b> ? <b>ijyā-
śeṣasya hi somasya bhakṣaḥ</b> । <b>na cāśeṣabhūte bhakṣyamāṇe sa vikṛto bhavati</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yadi somenaiva yāgaḥ tadā na śakyate yāgaśeṣapratipattibhūtabhakṣavikāritāpi phalacamasasya
vak‍tum । yadi hi somenejyate sa eva bhakṣayitavyaḥ । na ca phalacamasena tasya bhakṣaṇaṃ
nivārayituṃ śakyate । nahyanyasmin pratipādite anyatpratipāditaṃ bhavati । <b>tasmāt</b>
pratipattibhūtabhakṣasaṃbandhānupapatteḥ <b>ijyāśeṣataiva phalacamasasyāpi mantavyā</b> । śrutabhakṣasaṃbandha---
siddha‍yarthaṃ aśrutamapi yāgasaṃbandhitvaṃ kalpayitavyam । <b>nanu cotpattiśiṣṭatvāt somasya yāge
vidhānaṃ na saṃbhavatītyuktam</b> । pariharati---<b>yāgānuvādena vidhāne hi apratyabhijñāna</b>-
﻿<pb n="r875"/>
<b>muktam na punaḥ kāryeṇāpi saṃgandhe</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi yajiśabdena yāgamanūdya phalacamaso
vidhīyate tadā guṇādbhinnaṃ yāgāntaraṃ syāt । yadā tu kāryeṇāyaṃ saṃbandhaḥ tadā nāsti bhedaḥ
tadyāgasaṃbandhibhakṣasaṃbandhena hi yāgānupraveśe'ṅgīkriyamāṇe na yāgāntaraśaṅkāpi bhavatīti ।
kāryataścāyaṃ saṃbandhaḥ bhakṣaṃ kuryāditi śrūyate । yathā bhakṣo bhavati tathā kartavyam । yadi
cāsau yāgaśeṣo bhavati tadā bhakṣo bhavatīti---<b>kāryata evāyaṃ saṃbandhaḥ</b> । <b>nanu ca bhāṣyakāreṇa
yāgasaṃbandhābhāvaṃ codayitvā yājayediti saṃbandha uktaḥ</b> । tena yāgānuvādena phalacamasa-
saṃbandha ukto bhāṣyakāreṇa na kāryataḥ । samādhatte---<b>yāgānvayapradarśanārthaṃ taduk‍taṃ na punaḥ
anūdya vidhānāyetyadoṣaḥ</b> । upakramo yāgaśravaṇāt yāgasaṃbandhyeva bhakṣaṇamidam । tena
tadyoge nāsti yāgasaṃbandha iti pradarśitam । na punaryāgānuvādena dravyavidhiriti ।
<b>bhakṣaṃ kuryādini copasaṃhāra imamevārthaṃ</b> bhakṣasaṃbandhadvāreṇa yāgasaṃbandhirūpaṃ <b>prakaṭīkaroti</b> ।
<b>tasmādijyāvikāraḥ phalacamasa iti siddham</b> । <b>guṇavidhānāni ca pradarśitāni</b>
darbhataruṇakādiguṇavidhayaśca pradarśitāḥ ।</p>
<p><b>anuprasarpiṣu sāmānyāt</b> । <b>daśa daśa ekaikaṃ camasamanuprasarpantī’ti vidhānāt
śata brāhmaṇāḥ somān bhakṣayantīti anuvādaṃ manvānasya nābhakṣo rājeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
<note>(1) 1021</note>
﻿<pb n="r876"/>
rājasūye rājño'dhikārāt yajamānacamase prāpte rājño eva na syāt yadi śataṃ brāhmaṇāḥ somān
bhakṣayantīti vidhiḥ syāt brāhmaṇavidhau abrāhmaṇasya rājño nivṛttirbhaveti । yadā daśa daśa ekaikaṃ
camasamanuprasarpantītyeva vidhiḥ tadā saṅkalananibandhanā ca śatasaṅkhyā'nūdyate śata brāhmaṇā iti
brāhmaṇaśabdaśca brāhmaṇeṣu bhūyastvena lakṣaṇayā vartate tadā rājño'pi yukta iti । anuvādaścāyaṃ
yuktaḥ anyathā codakaprāptabhakṣānuvādena anekaguṇavidhānādvākyabhedaḥ syāt iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
<b>rāddhāntastu satyameva yadyanuvādaḥ syāt</b> । <b>na cānuvṛtte1 rājani anuvādaśśakyate
vak‍tum ayathārthānuvādaprasaṅgāt</b> । na ceti caśabdaḥ tuśabdasyārthe । yadyanuvādaḥ
syāt tadā syādeva rājño'pi bhakṣaḥ natvayamanuvādaḥ । 2rājanyānivṛttau brāhmaṇaśabdasya
ayathārthānuvādaprasaṅgāt । vidhau tu nāyathārthatā। tasmādvidhirevāyaṃ śataṃ brāhmaṇā iti। <b>nanu cānu-
vāde ayathārthānuvādatvamadoṣaḥ bhūyastvena lakṣaṇā bhaviṣyati</b> । anuvāde yathāprāptamanūdyata iti
brāhmaṇābrāhmaṇāḥ yathā prāptāḥ tathā teṣāmanuvādo lakṣaṇayeti । uttaraṃ-<b>satyaṃ yadyekāntato'nuvādaḥ</b> ।
<b>iha tu vidheyatāpyupapadyata eveti nāyathārthatvamāśrayituṃ śakyate</b> । <b>tasmāt dvayamapyetadvidhīyate
---śataṃ brāhmaṇāḥ daśa daśa ekaikaṃ casamaṃ iti ca</b> । <b>nanu ca <q>‘samaṃ syādaśrutatvāt’</q> iti
nyāyena</b> śate vibhajyamāne ekaikatra daśadaśaprāpteḥ daśa daśa ekaikaṃ camasamanuprasarpantītyanu-
vādaḥ । kathaṃ ayaṃ vidhiruktaḥ iti codyamātraṃ na tu pūrvapakṣaḥ । yasmādanuvādatvepi
<note>(1) anivṛtte</note> <note>(2) rājanyanivṛttau</note>
﻿<pb n="r877"/>
yathārthānuvādatayā ayamevānuvādo yuktaḥ na punaḥ śataṃ brāhmaṇā iti ayathārthaprasaṅgāt । tasmāt
codyamātramevedam । pariharati---<b>na ekaikatra śataprāpteḥ pratyuddeśaṃ vākyasamāpteḥ</b> । ekai-
katra camase śataṃ syāt tanmābhūditi daśasaṅkhyā vidhīyate । adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati
---<b>tasmādabhakṣo rājā brāhmaṇavidhānāditi</b> । <b>yatpunaratra śataṃ brāhmaṇāssomān ityanekārtha-
vidhānaṃ manyate tadayuktaṃ yasmāt karmāntaravidhānenāpi prākṛtakāryārthatāṃ daśame vakṣyāmaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---bhakṣāntaramevedaṃ anekaguṇaviśiṣṭaṃ vidhīyatāṃ tathā dṛṣṭārthatayā prākṛtabhakṣaṇaṃ
nivartayiṣyatīti । etaccābhyupagamamātram karmāntaravidhānenāpītyapiśabdena prakaṭīkṛtam ।
paramārthatastu daśadaśa ekaikaṃ iti vidhiḥ tatpūrvakaṃ śataṃ brāhmaṇa iti brāhmaṇamātravidhiḥ śata-
mityetadanuvāda iti sarvaṃ samañjasam ।</p>
<trailer>iti śrīṛjuvimalāyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
pañcamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="r878"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>atha tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>sarvārthamaprakaraṇāt</b> । <b>kiṃ punaratrakāraṇaṃ pakṣadvayopanyāsasya</b> ? <b>kasya 1pakṣa-
dvayopanyāsasya</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>codakādanārabhya vidhirbalīyān sāmānyato dṛṣṭatvācceti
prathamasya tāvatpakṣasya</b> codakādanārabhyavidhirbalīyānityasya <b>idaṃ prayojanam</b> yatpūrvapakṣa-
samarthanam । kathaṃ ? tatrāha---<b>naivātra dviruktatā vidyate prakṛtivikṛtyoḥ sruksaṃbhavāt</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yadi vikṛtyarthatve anārabhyavidheḥ dviruktatālakṣaṇo doṣaḥ syāt tadā syādeva
kevalaprakṛtyarthatā । yāvatā naiva vikṛtyarthatvepi dviruktatādoṣaḥ kintu prakṛtāvupadeśāprāptāṃ
vikṛtāvapi codakaprāptāṃ srucamuddiśya parṇatā vidhīyate । tenāsāvubhayatraupadeśikīti । ato
vikṛtāvapi punaścodakato na prāp‍notyeva । codakaprāpteruttarakālabhāvitvāt । <b>etaduk‍taṃ/?/
bhavati</b> । anārabhya vidhiṃ varjayitvaiva tāvat prakṛtāvārabhya vihitāneva padārthān gṛhītvā
upakāraḥ kathyate । taduttarakālaṃ ca vikṛtiṣvatideśaḥ; evaṃ prakṛtivikṛtiṣu srucāṃ
prāptānāṃ samānavidhānena anārabhya vidhinā parṇamayītvādikaṃ vidhīyata iti । dvitīyapakṣopanyāsa-
samarthanamāha---<b>evaṃ tarhi sāmānyatodarśanena prakṛtyarthatetyaparasya pakṣasyopanyāsaḥ prāya</b>-
<note>(1) P. 1025</note> <note>(2) G. pakṣadvayasya</note>
﻿<pb n="r879"/>
<b>darśanavat</b> । yadi sruksaṃbhavāt prakṛtivikṛtyoraviśeṣaḥ evaṃ tarhi tathā prāyadarśanena nirṇayaḥ
tathā'trāpi sāmānyato dṛṣṭena saṃbhavati prakṛtyarthatāniścayaḥ । prakṛtau saṃkṣepavistāropadeśaḥ ।
ayamapi saṃkṣepavistāra eveti prakṛtyarthatā pratibhātītyayaṃ <b>tāvat anantarapakṣo</b> rāddhāntā-
bhāsarūpo <b>nirākriyate</b> । <b>1na sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ śabdārthāvagatau hetuḥ</b> । ayamāśayaḥ---vaidikaṃ
hi śeṣatvam । na ca tatra sāmānyato dṛṣṭasyānumānasyāvasaraḥ । siddhārthaviṣayatvāt
pratyakṣādīnāṃ na kāryasvarūpe śaktiḥ । prāyadarśanaṃ tu śabdārthāvagatau heturbhavatyeva śabda-
pramāṇaśeṣatvena loke dṛṣṭatvāt । tena śabda eva viśeṣaviṣaye prāyadaśanenopasyāyate । na
punaścānumānavat svatantraḥ pramāṇam । tacca prāyadarśanamapīha nāsti । vikṛtāvapi tathā
vidhopadeśadarśanāt । tadāha---<b>nāpi prāyadarśanaṃ prakṛtāviva vikṛtāvapi saṃkṣepavistāro-
padeśadarśanāt</b> । <b>idānīmaparasya pakṣasya nirasanaṃ codakāpekṣaścedanārabhya vidhiḥ prakṛtau
pūrvamupadeśo'pekṣaṇīyaḥ upadeśāpekṣatvādatideśasya</b> । asyārthaḥ---vikṛtau sruksaṃbhavārthaṃ
codakāpekṣaścet anārabhyavidhiḥ tarhi pūrvaṃ prakṛtāvupadeśo'pekṣaṇīyaḥ । kutaḥ ? upadeśāpekṣa-
tvādatideśasya । upadeśabalena hi prakṛtau k‍lṛpte upakāre tanmukhena vikṛtāvatideśaḥ padārthānāṃ
bhavati । tena upadeśasamāp‍tyarthaṃ prakṛtau tāvadanārabhyavidhiḥ niviśate ityaṅgīkaraṇīyam ।
na cānārabhyavidhinirapekṣaiva prakṛtāvupakārakalpanā, sakalāṅgasaṃpādyatvāditikartavyatāyāḥ ।
<b>upadeśena cet prakṛtāvupasaṃhṛtaḥ</b> svārthatvena <b>gṛhīto'nārabhyavidhiḥ</b> tadā vikṛtau
praveśārthaṃ srukprāptaye <b>nātideśamapekṣate</b> । vikṛtāvapi codakaprāptāṃ srucamapekṣya na parṇamayītvā-
<note>(1) G. sa</note>
﻿<pb n="r880"/>
dikaṃ vidhatta iti yāvat । kutaḥ ? <b>kāryata eva vikṛtau prāptatvāt</b> parṇatādīnām ।
na ca prāpte punarvidheravakāśo'sti । <b>ato dviruk‍terasaṃbhavāt adviruktatvāditi sthitaḥ</b>
sūtrokto hetuḥ । atra bhāṣyākāreṇa yāgenetikartavyatā saṃbadhyata ityuktam kastasyopayoga
ityatrāha---<b>yastu yāgasaṃbandhopanyāsaḥ asāvavaśyaṃbhāvī codaka iti darśayitum</b> । <b>avaśyaṃ-
bhāvitve cādviruktatvasya siddhiruktā</b> । asyārthaḥ---adviruktatvalakṣaṇahetusamarthanārthaṃ avaśyaṃ
bhāvitāṃ codakasya darśayituṃ yāgasaṃbandhaḥ itikartavyatāyā upanyastaḥ । yadi hi yāga-
nirākāṅkṣā vaikṛtā bhaveyuḥ tadā codako na bhaveti codakābhāve ca parṇatā na prāpnoti iti sā
vidhīyate । yadā tu yāgenetikartavyatā saṃbadhyate na pātraiḥ tadā yadyapi ca pātrāṇyanārabhya-
vidhinaiva nirākāṅkṣībhavanti tathāpi yāgasyākāṅkṣā'stītyavaśyaṃ codaka utpādayitavyaḥ । sa
cedutpādayitavyaḥ tarhi parṇatāpi prāptā । na ca prāptāpi sā bādhituṃ śakyate iti sthitaḥ
dviruk‍terasaṃbhavaḥ siddhāntahetuḥ ।</p>
<p><b>prakaraṇāviśeṣāttu vikṛtau virodhi syāt</b> । pūrvapakṣamāha---<b>nanu cānārabhyādhītaṃ
sāptadaśyaṃ yacca prakaraṇādhītaṃ pāñcadaśyaṃ ubhayamapi</b> śrutyaiva <b>sāmidhenīsaṃbandhitayā</b>
<note>(1) 1029</note> <note>(2) P. 1029</note>
﻿<pb n="r881"/>
<b>codyate viniyujyate</b> । <b>ko'yaṃ prakaraṇopanyāsaḥ</b> ? ekagranthenāha--<b>naivātra
prakaraṇaṃ viniyojakaṃ yena prakaraṇavidhirbalīyān</b> । asyārthaḥ---saptadaśa sāmidhenī-
ranubrūyāditi yadanārabhyādhītaṃ sāptadaśyaṃ ca <q>‘pañcadaśasāmidhenīranubrūyāt’</q> iti
prakaraṇādhītaṃ pāñcadaśyaṃ ubhayamapi śrutyaiva sāmidhenīsaṃbandhitayā codyate, viniyujyate na
prakaraṇeneti । yadi prakaraṇena viniyogaḥ syāt tadā yatprakaraṇādhītaṃ tadeva viniyujyate
nānyat । na cātra prakaraṇaṃ viniyojakam । ata ubhayorapi viniyoga iti । āśaṅkayati
---<b>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ prakaraṇasavyapekṣā eva śrutyādayaḥ viniyojakā iti</b> saptamādye sthā-
syati । tena yasyaiva prakaraṇapāṭhaḥ tasyaiva śrutyādiviniyogo nānyasyeti । dūṣayati---
<b>satyaṃ grāhakalakṣaṇaprakaraṇasavyapekṣāḥ na tu viniyojakamapekṣante</b> । <b>grāhakasya savya-
pekṣā ca anārabhyavidherapi tulyaiva</b> । pāñcadaśyamapi sāmidhenīsaṃbandhamukhenaiva gṛhyate
sāmidhenīsaṃbandhaśca anārabhyadhītasyāpi tulya iti dvayoḥ grāhakagrahaṇāviśeṣāt । <b>ato'trāpi
dviruk‍terasaṃbhavāt prakṛtādeva sāptadaśyamiti yuktam</b> । rāddhāntamāha---<b>astyatra viśeṣa
prakṛtatve hi pāñcadaśyasya grāhakapratyabhijñānaṃ saṃbhavati avyavāyāt, anārabhyavidhe
kāryato grāhakāvamarśaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yatkila sādhikāragrāhakāvasthāniyogasannidhau śrūyate
tattadarthamiti śrutyaivāvagamyate । yat‍tu punaḥ dūre śrūyate tasya tadīyapadārthasaṃbandhakartavyatā
﻿<pb n="r882"/>
nyathānupapattyā tada‍grāhakasaṃbandhaḥ । tena yadeva śīghraṃ gṛhītaṃ tadeva śīghraṃ viniyujyate
viniyogasāmagrīśaughrayāt । yatpunarvilanbitaṃ tatpratipakṣākrāntatvāt śeṣiṇo na tatra niviśata
ityanyatra viniyujyate । tadāha---<b>evaṃ ca sati na klṛp‍te</b> pāñcadaśye pratipakṣe <b>saṃbhavati</b>
sāptadaśya<b>kalpanā saṃbhavati iti na prakṛtau niveśaḥ</b> । <b>pratipattyanurodhinī hi kalpanā na
pratipannopamardinī</b> । tasmādvikṛtau sāptadaśyamiti yuktam । ihādhikaraṇe etadva‍yutpādyate
kiṃ padārthasaṃbandhamukhena prakṛtamaṅgaṃ gṛhyate uta sannidhānamātreṇeti । tatra padārthasaṃbandhamukhena grahaṇaṃ
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । anyathā dvādaśopasattāyā api jyotiṣṭomagrāhyatvopapatteḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu
sannidhānamātreṇa grahaṇamāha । dvādaśopasattāyāstu balīyasā viniyogasannidhānena niyogasannidherbā-
dhitatvāt na jyotiṣṭomena grahaṇam । na ca sannidhānamātreṇa grahaṇe'tiprasaṅgaḥ sannidhānasyaiva
sarvathā bhāvāditi ।</p>
<p><b>naimittikaṃ tu prakṛtau</b> । <b>kathaṃ punaratra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā</b> ? । ayamāśayaḥ---yathā
prakṛtau camasaḥ śrūyate tathā vikṛtāvapyatidiśyate tenobhayatra kratvarthāvirodhāt kena viśeṣeṇa
vikṛtau niveśa āśaṅkyate ? uttaraṃ---<b>itthamāśaṅkā</b> । <b>kratvarthe bādhyamāne upadeśaḥ
pīḍito bhavati</b> । <b>na copadeśādṛte sāda‍guṇyāvagatirbhavati</b> । yathopadeśaṃ kāryaṃ prakṛtau
<note>(1) P. 1032</note>
﻿<pb n="r883"/>
tena yadi camaso bādhyeta prakṛtau kratorvaiguṇyaṃ syāt <b>vikṛtau punaḥ kāryata eva sāda‍guṇyāvagati-
rbhavati ityekakāryatvāt puruṣārthenāṣi kratoḥ sāda‍guṇyaṃ śakyate vak‍tum kāryaviśeṣāt</b>
kāryato hi vikṛtau padārthāḥ prāpyante । tatra puruṣārthenāpyekārthakāriṇā kāryaṃ yadi
nirvartitaṃ bhavati tadā nāstyeva vaiguṇyāvagatiḥ padārthapradhānabhāvatvāt । tasmāt puruṣārthānāṃ
<b>paraṃ vikṛtau niveśaḥ</b> । <b>satyamevaṃ yadi prakṛtāvapi kāryaviśeṣo na syāt</b> । <b>iha tu dṛṣṭārthatvā-
dupadeśasya</b> camasādīnāṃ <b>tulyaḥ kāryaviśeṣaḥ</b> । tena puruṣārthena kṛte kārye camaso bādhyate
bādhite cānanuṣṭhīyamāne kratorvaiguṇyaṃ nāsti । nanu kena viśeṣeṇa godohanena camaso bādhyate ।
kāmyatvāditi cet kā tarhi vārtā phalacamase tasmādvak‍tavyaṃ phalacamase । <b>taducyate</b> ।
phalacamase <b>viśeṣāvagamācca sāmānyato balīyastvaṃ viśeṣopadeśasya</b> padādivadeva,
viśeṣabhūtapaśukāmarājanyādiviṣayasya viśeṣopadeśasya sāmānyabhūtadarśapūrṇamāsajyotiṣṭomādhikṛta-
mātraviṣayāt sāmānyata upadeśāt āhavanīyopadeśādivat valīyastvamiti <b>prakṛtāveva niveśo</b>
naimittikānāmiti ।</p>
<p><b>iṣṭa‍yarthamagnyādheyaṃ prakaraṇāt</b> । atra bhāṣyakāraḥ iṣṭa‍yarthamādhānaṃ prakaraṇāditi
pūrvapakṣayati । tadākṣipati---<b>kathaṃ punaratreṣṭeḥ prakaraṇaṃ</b> ? <b>iṣṭerapi hi naivādhikāraśrutirasti</b> ।
<note>(1) 1037</note>
﻿<pb n="r884"/>
<b>ādhānasyaiva hi sādhikārasya vidheḥ prakaraṇam</b> । taduk‍taṃ---<q>“ākāṅkṣādvayasya tatprasṛteḥ”</q>
iti । na ca pavamāneṣṭeradhikāraśrutiriti । <b>tasmānneṣṭeḥ prakaraṇamiti śakyate vak‍tum</b> ।
evamākṣip‍te sati ekadeśī samādhātāraṃ pṛcchati---<b>kathaṃ tarhi pūrvapakṣaḥ</b> ? iti । samādhātā
ekadeśinameva parihāsena pṛcchati---<b>bhavato vā ko'bhiprāyaḥ</b> iti । ekadeśyāha
---<b>na kiñcit pratibhāti</b> । paramasamādhātā āha---<b>atrābhidhīyate dvayamapyetaduhāraṇam</b> ।
<b>kimādhānaṃ pradhānaṃ uteṣṭiriti</b> । asyārthaḥ dvayamapyekattāvat agnyarthaṃ na bhavati । tathā
hi---viniyuktā agnayaḥ dvayasya śeṣiṇaḥ aviniyuktā vā ? viniyuktāgnyarthatve parṇatādi-
vatkatvaṅgatvaprasaṅgaḥ । aviniyuktāstu kāryaśūnyāḥ sak‍tuvanna śeṣitāmarhanti iti sthite
adhikāraḥ kalpayitavyaḥ । tatra kiṃ pavamāneṣṭiṣvadhikāraḥ kalpyatāṃ tā eva pradhānaṃ bhavantu,
yadi vā ādhāne adhikārakalpanā tadeva pradhānamiti dvayamapyetadādhānapavamāneṣṭirūpamudāharaṇa-
miti । tatra <b>dvayoḥ prādhānyamayuktamiti manvānasya iṣṭeścāṅgabāhulyāt prādhānyāropeṇa
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । bhūyastvenobhayaśrutirityanena nyāyena aṅgabāhulyāt prādhānyaṃ kalpayitvā tadaṅga-
mādhānamiti yuktam । paramārthatastu agnyarthatā dvayornāstīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>rāddhāntastu
dvayorapyadhikārābhāvāt</b> । <b>agnyarthatayā ca viniyogopapatteḥ dvayoragnyarthatvam</b> ।
yadyapi bhūto viniyogo nāsti tathāpi bhāvināpi 1viniyogena ag‍nīnāṃ śeṣitvopapatteḥ agnyartha-
mevedaṃ dvayamiti । <b>tathā ca liṅgadarśanam</b> iti ।</p>
<note>(1) G. niyogena</note>
﻿<pb n="r885"/>
<p><b>tatprakṛtyarthaṃ yathānye</b> । sthite hyagnyarthatve <b>kimidānīṃ prakṛtyarthamādhānaṃ uta sarvārtha-
miti</b> । anena bhāṣyakārīyasaṃśayo'nubhāṣitaḥ । atra kāraṇabhūtaṃ saṃśayamāha---<b>etaduktaṃ
bhavati---kiṃ kratvarthānāmādhānaṃ uta āhitānāmagnīnāṃ kratvarthateti</b> । yadi kratvarthānā-
magnīnāṃ ādhānaṃ tadā parṇātādivat kratoraṅgam । tataśca tadvadeva prakṛtyarthatā'sya syāt ।
atha tu āhitānāmagnīnāṃ kratvarthatā tadi svatantrāgnīsaṃbandhāt na kratoraṅgam । tenāhavanī-
yādimātrasaṃbandhāt āhavanīyādīnāṃ ca sarvakratvarthatvāt taddvāreṇa sarvārthamādhānamityucyate
paramārthatastu na kasyacidaṅgamiti । imamarthaṃ praśnapūrvakaṃ prakaṭīkaroti---<b>kaścātra viśeṣaḥ</b> ?
<b>ayamasti viśeṣaḥ</b> । <b>yadi kratvarthānāmādhānaṃ tadā parṇamayītvavat prakṛtigāmitvamādhānavidheḥ</b> ।
<b>atha tvāhitānāṃ kratvarthatā tadā homādimātraśeṣatayā agnīnāṃ sarvārthamādhānamityucyate</b>
pūrvapakṣamāha---<b>kiṃ punaratra yuktam</b> ? evaṃ manyate---<b>parṇatādivat kratusaṃbandhānāmevāgnīnāṃ
ādhānamiti</b> । rāddhāntamāha---<b>āhitāgneradhikārāt āhitānāṃ kratvarthateti yuktam</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yathā'dhikṛtenaivāvaghātādi kriyate tathā ādhānam । kintu āhitogneḥ sataḥ
karmavidhiṣvadhikāraḥ niyatopāyatvādag‍nīnāṃ prayogakāle ca kartumaśakyatvāt । ataḥ puruṣeṇa
lohasuvarṇādivat prayogāt bahiragrayaḥ upārjyante । upārjitāgneśca karmaṇi samarthatvādadhikāraḥ ।
tataśca prāgadhikārābhāvāt grāhakagrahaṇāsiddheḥ agnīnāṃ viniyogābhāvāt na tanmukhena paṇītāvat
﻿<pb n="r886"/>
kratvaṅgabhāvaḥ । yathā vā āṅitāgneradhikāraḥ tathā ṣaṣṭhe yathāviniyogamadhikāra iti
varṇayanto vakṣyāmaḥ । yadā <b>ādhānamanaṅgaṃ tadā vasantādikālavidhiścopapannataro bhavati</b> ।
itarathā aṅgatve sati <q>‘aṅgānāṃ mukhyakālatvāt’</q> iti mukhyakālatve prāpte jyotiṣṭhome vasanta-
vidheranuvādaḥ । pradhānakāla eva prāpteḥ darśapūrṇamāsādiṣu kālāntareṣvanuṣṭhīyamāneṣu aprāptā-
dhānakālavidhiḥ । basante <b>anuṣṭhīyamāneṣu</b> prāptādhānakālavidhyanuvādaḥ । na caika eva vidhiḥ
kadācidanuvādaḥ kadācidvidhiriti yuk‍tam । vaiṣamyaprasaṅgāt । āsminmate tūpapannataro
bhavati । sarvatra svakālavidhānāt tadaṅgakādhānavidhāyakatvāditi ।</p>
<p><b>tāsāmagniḥ</b> । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ pavamāneṣṭiṣu pavamāneṣṭisaṃskṛtā agnayaḥ āśaṅkyante</b> ।
<b>yā ag‍nyarthā iṣṭayaḥ tā api pavamāneṣṭaya eva</b> । <b>tasmādanāśaṅkanīyamevedamāśaṅkitam</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yadeva yasya kārthaṃ tadeva tasya kāraṇaṃ na bhavati pavamāneṣṭavaścahavanīyādīnāṃ
kāraṇam । kathaṃ tā evāhanīyādīnāṃ sādhyā bhaveyuḥ । asaṃbhāvanīyatvādasyārthasya neyamāśaṅkopa-
padyate---<b>atrocyate idamevātra cintyate kimayamatideśaḥ prakṛtau yāvadupakārakaṃ tāvadatidi-
śati uta yathākāryamatideśa iti</b> । na pavamāneṣṭiṣu pavamāneṣṭiprāptiratra cintyate । kintu
<note>(1) P. 1040</note>
﻿<pb n="r887"/>
idavātra cintyane yo'yamatideśaḥ sarvatra sa kiṃ yāvadupakārakaṃ prakṛtāvaṅgamanaṅgaṃ vā tatra
tāvadatiśati । tenānaṅgabhūtānāmapi pavamāneṣṭīnāmatideśaḥ syāt । atha yathākāryaṃ yāvadeva
upakāraṃ janayati tāvadevātidiśyate aṅgaṃ tu upakāraṃ janayati na punaḥ anaṅgamapi । tenāṅga-
mātramatidiśyata iti yāvat । tataśca pavamāneṣṭīnāṃ vikṛtiṣu anatideśaḥ tāsāmanaṅgatvāt ।
<b>tatra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ yāvadupakāramatideśa iti</b> । upakārasaṃbandhaṃ hi padārthajātamati-
diśyate । anaṅgabhūtasyāpi copakārakasya upakāra(ka)saṃbandho'stīti tasyāpyatideśo yukta
iti । <b>rāddhāntī punarāha---yathākāryamatideśa iti</b> । yāvadupakārajanakamaṅgabhūtaṃ tāvadati-
diśyate । yena hi vinā upakāro na śakyate pratipat‍tuṃ tadevopakarapratīpattau kāryapratipattau
jātipratipattau vyaktivat nāntarīyakatayā pratīyamānaṃ vikṛtiṣvatidiśyate । yaccopakārajanakaṃ
tena vinā upakāro na śakyate nirūpayitum । yat‍tu upakārakapadārthajanakaṃ tadupakārānanu-
praviṣṭima[na]ṅgabhūtam । tena vināpi janakapadārthavargāvacchinnaḥ śakyata evopakāraḥ pratipat‍tu-
miti na tadvadatidiśyate । <b>upadeśe tu viparītam</b> । upadeśe hi yāvadupakārakamapyupadeśo
bhavati yathā pavamāneṣṭīnāṃ kratūpakāritā । anaṅgabhūtā api pavamāneṣṭayaḥ upadiśyanta eva ।
tasmādidamatideśākhyaṃ padārthaprāptipramāṇaṃ <b>upadeśavanna draṣṭavyam</b> । nanu mā nāma upakāraka-
mātramatidiśmatām । tathāpi1 tasyāṅgabhūtapadārthajanakatayā ākṣepo'styeva । kimanati-
deśārthavyutpādanena । ucyate yadyatideśaḥsyāt atidiṣṭameva padārthajātamaṅgamiṣyate tataśca
vikṛtiṣu pavamāneṣṭīnāmaṅgabhūtatvāt svāṅgasaṃskṛteṣvevāgniṣu vikṛtayo bhaveyuḥ । vikṛtyāhisā
hyagnayaḥ vikṛtyapavarge apavṛjyerat । tasmāt 2saprayojanamanatideśavyutpādanam । <b>upadeśa-
viśeṣapradarśanārthaṃ caitat upadeśalakṣaṇe cintitam</b> । yo hi manyate yathā'tideśe
<note>(1) G. tavāpi</note> <note>(2) G. saprayojanamāhātideśa</note>
﻿<pb n="r888"/>
yāvatkāryatideśaḥ tathopadeśenāpi yāvatkāryeṇāpi bhavitavyam । tataścādhānapavamāneṣṭa‍yu-
padeśo nopapadyate । atha yāvadupakārakamupadeśaḥ atideśo'pi tathā syāditīmāmā-
śaṅkāmapanetumupadeśādviśeṣa uktaḥ । upadeśe yāvadupakārakamapyupadiśyate atideśe
tu yāvatkāryameveti darśayitumupadeśalakṣaṇe cintitam । <b>anyathā yadyati</b>---
deśopadeśavivekāspadamadhikaraṇaṃ na syāt kintu pavamāneṣṭiprāp‍tyaprāptivicārārthaṃ
syāt । tadā <b>anvārambhaṇīyādhikaraṇenaiva gatārthaṃ syāt</b> । tatra hi ākṣepataḥ
prāptiścintitā । iha tu sā na cintyate । kintu atideśa eveti viśeṣaḥ । <b>agnyarthatayā ca
pavamāneṣṭīnāṃ</b> upadeśānyatve yat‍naḥ । <b>pavamāneṣṭīnāmagnyutpādakatvācca</b> pavamāneṣṭiṣu
pavamāneṣṭisaṃskṛto'gniḥ na prāp‍notīti pavamāneṣṭiviṣaye'nena abhyuccayena <b>upadeśānyatve</b>
yāvadupakāraprāpakatve yat‍naḥ kṛto bhāṣyakāreṇa । tadarthameva pavamāneṣṭa‍yudāharaṇam ।</p>
<p><b>tulyaḥ sarveṣām</b> । <b>kathaṃ punaridamadhikaraṇaṃ prārabdham</b> । samādhātā āha
---<b>yathaiva bhāṣyakāreṇa</b> । ākṣeptā āha---<b>na tathā śakyate'vagantum</b> । pṛcchati---<b>tasmā-
diti</b> । ākṣeptā''ha---<b>tasmāt yadi tāvadidaṃ jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇaṃ tadā</b> paśuyāgānāṃ
<note>(1) P. 1042</note>
﻿<pb n="r889"/>
prakaraṇābhāvāt śrutyādibhireva <b>paśuyāgasaṃbandhāt viśasanādīnām</b> । <b>kimidaṃ prakaraṇāviśeṣā-
diti sarvārthatocyate</b> । prakaraṇāviśeṣāditi dvivā saṃbhavati prakaraṇasyāviśeṣāditi vā, prakaraṇe
aviśeṣāditi vā । tatra tāvat ṣaṣṭhīsamāso nopapadyate paśūnāṃ prakaraṇābhāvāt ।
<b>atha prakaraṇe</b> jyautiṣṭomike nāstyatra <b>viśeṣa sarvapaśūnāmityaviśeṣatocyate</b> । dūṣayati
---<b>kathaṃ tarhi sūtraṃ <q>‘asti tu prakaraṇe viśeṣa’</q></b> iti । na jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe kaścidasti viśeṣaḥ
sarvapaśūnām । atha paśūnāmevāvāntaraprakaraṇaṃ asti jyautiṣṭomikaṃ mahāprakaraṇaṃ tadantargatānāṃ
dīkṣaṇīyādīnāmavāntaraprakaraṇamiti ghaṭata evedaṃ asti tu prakaraṇe viśeṣa iti, <b>tatrāha
---na cāvāntaraprakaraṇaṃ nāma kiñcidasti jyautiṣṭomikamahāprakaraṇe</b> ekasyaiva vidheḥ sādhi-
kārasya karaṇetikartavyatākāṅkṣā, na punaḥ niradhikārāṇāmavāntaravidhīnāmapi । svayamiti-
kartavyatābhūtatvāt sādhyasyetikartavyatākāṅkṣā, na punaḥ sādhanasya । <b>itikartavyatākāṅkṣā ca
prakaraṇam</b> । tenaikasminnevādhikāravidhau nāsti prakaraṇadvayasaṃbhavaḥ । <b>prakaraṇāntare cābhyupa-
gamyamāne</b> itthaṃbhāvapūrakatvaṃ itikartavyatāṃśapūrakatvaṃ <b>agnīṣomīyāderna syāt</b> । kasmādi-
tyāha---<b>kimityeva hi tadā jyotiṣṭomasaṃbandho'bhyupagataḥ syāt</b> । <b>evaṃ ca dīkṣaṇīyādeḥ
itikartavyatābhāva eva hīyeta</b> । kāraṇataiva syāt । asyārthaḥ---yo hi vādī avāntara-
prakaraṇamicchati tena dīkṣaṇīyādiniyogānāṃ sādhyatvasiddhaye sādhikāratvamicchatā prakṛta eva
jyotiṣṭomāpūrvapravṛttaḥ puruṣo'dhikārī vaktavyaḥ । tathā ca sati adhikāriviśeṇabhūtameva
﻿<pb n="r890"/>
jyotiṣṭomāpūrvaṃ svargavat, sādhyabhāvena ca apūrvamadhikāriviśeṣaṇam । yacca sādhyaṃ sat
adhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ tatparyantaṃ viṣayībhūtasya bhāvārthasya 1karaṇatvam । yadeva hi niyoge karaṇaṃ
tadeva phalepi karaṇaṃ nānyat । sādhyaṃ hi vivṛddhaṃ bhavati । iha na punaḥ sādhyāntaraṃ phalaṃ
na punaḥ sādhyāntarakalpanā । <b>tataśca dīkṣaṇīyādikarmaṇaḥ</b> svaniyoge (karaṇe eva)
karaṇabhūtasyādhikāraviśeṣaṇībhūtaṃ apūrvamapi prati karataiveti <b>itikartavyatābhāvo hīyate</b> ।
nacotpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarodhadoṣaḥ kāryataḥ karaṇatvopapatteḥ phalacamasavat । adhikāraviśeṣaṇī-
bhūtaṃ hi prati etatkaraṇatvaṃ na punaḥ sādhyatvena nirdeśyakaraṇalasamarpaṇam । athocyeta evaṃ sati
itikartavyatākāṅkṣāyāḥ2 pradhānavidheranivṛttiriti; satyaṃ, tathāpi na pramāṇamantareṇetikartavyatātvaṃ
śakyamadhyavasātum । adhikāravidheritikartavyatākāṅkṣaiva pramāṇamiti cet, na, avagate hi
pradhānavidhisaṃbandhe kathaṃbhāvākāṅkṣā karaṇopakāradvārarūpaṃ parikalpayantī prakaraṇaśabdābhidheyā
pramāṇaṃ bhavati । na cāsmin pakṣe prāgadhikāravidhisaṃbandho'bhyupagataḥ । prāgavagame adhikāra-
vidhisaṃbandhasyābhyupagamyamāne adhikārakalpanāvakāśa eva nāsti । tatsaṃbandhe'vagate prakaraṇena
viniyoge sati pradhānavidhiprayojyatayānuṣṭhānasiddheḥ । anuṣṭhānalābhārthaṃ hi niyogo niyojyā-
nvito'bhidhīyate iti loke dṛṣṭaṃ na punaḥ adṛṣṭena rūpeṇa niyojyānvitābhidhānasya upakāraḥ ।
ata evādhyayanavidhāvapi na niyojyakalpanā, adhyāpanavidhiprayuk‍tyaivānuṣṭhānasiddheḥ । tena
prāganavagatādhikāravidhisaṃbandhānāṃ dīkṣaṇīyādīnāṃ sannidhānamātre paramāpūrvapravṛtto'dhikārī
kalpyate । tatra ca svarasena yo'rthaḥ pratīyate sa grāhyaḥ । svarasena ca karaṇa-
tāmevāvagacchāmaḥ iti netikartavyatātvasiddhiḥ । api ca yadyaṅgavidhiṣu adhikārā-
kāṅkṣā tadā svavākyaśrutānyeva kimiti varmādīni rātrisatravadadhikāriviśeṣaṇatayā nāvatiṣṭhante ?
kimiti sākṣācchruṃta svarga kāmapadamevādhikārisamarpakatayā nānuṣajyate ? । tathā payovratādiṣu
kimiti prāṅa‍mukhaniyamavat bhojanapravṛtto'dhikārī na syāt । kiñcānuṣṭhānasiddhaye'dhikāra-
kalpanā । tatra varaṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajetetyanena vacanena saptamādyapūrvapakṣavata
adhikāravantaṃ yajimuddiśya <q>‘samidho yajati’</q> ityevamādiḥ itikartavyatayā samidādividhirā-
<note>(1) G. karaṇatvāya</note> <note>(2) G. kṣayoḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r891"/>
śrīyatām yada‍ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajeta samidho yajatītītthaṃ iti । tataśca
uddiśyamānaviśeṣaṇasyāvivakṣitatvāt adhikāravat yāgamātrasaṃbandha eva samidādīnāṃ syāt
ityupadeśata eva aindrāgnādiṣvitikartavyatālābhaḥ syāt । kiñca yadyapi paramāpūrvapravṛtta
evādhikārī yadyapi ca dīkṣaṇīyāderitikartavyatātvenānvayaḥ tathāpi sarvairitikartavyateti na
siddha‍yati । api tu pratyekameva apūrvasyādhikāriviśeṣaṇatvenānvitatvāt pratyekamiti-
kartavyatātvaṃ syāt svargavata । <b>tathā</b> hi---svargo'gnihotradarśapūrṇamāsādiṣu pratyekamevādhi-
kāriviśeṣaṇatvenānvitaḥ । pratyekaṃ nirapekṣaireva saṃbadhyate । tathā'trāpi syāt । adhikāri-
viśeṣaṇatayāpi sādhyabhūtasyopāyopeyabhāvamantareṇānvayo na paryavasyati ityupāyopeyatvaṃ kalpyam ।
dvividhastūpāyaḥ kareṇetikartavyatālakṣaṇaḥ । tatra karaṇatvenānvaye'sati itikartavyatātvenānvaya
ekaikavākyocca dīkṣaṇīyādayo nirapekṣā evāvagamyante iti nirapekṣamevetikartavyatātvaṃ syāt ।
yasya tu mate svavākyamātravartinā paramāpūrveṇa sannidhānamātreṇaiva dīkṣaṇīyādisaṃbandhaḥ tasya
khalakalpe'dhikāravidhau ekasminnaṅgānāṃ kapotavat nipatitatvāt tadanurūpamekameva karaṇopakāra-
lakṣaṇadvāraṃ kalpyeteti yuktamuk‍taṃ <b>savairevetikartavyateti</b> । na ca sannidhānamātreṇaiva
saṃbandho loke na dṛṣṭaḥ । dṛṣṭakāryādiṣviva adṛṣṭepi sannidhānamātreṇaiva saṃbandhopadeśādanuṣṭhāna-
darśanāt । na ca sannivānamātreṇa saṃbandhe'tiprasaṅgaḥ । sannidhānasya sarvatrābhāvāt ।
yadi <b>sannidhānamakiñcitkaraṃ kimiti paramāpūrvapravṛtta eva sannihitepvaṅgeṣu adhikārī bhavati</b> ।
yadi tu sarvatra padārthānvayamukhenaiva adhikārisaṃbandhaḥ na punassannidhānanātreṇa, tarhi sāmidhenī-
dvāreṇa saṃbaddhayoḥ prakaraṇāprakaraṇādhītayoḥ pāñcadaśyasāptadaśyayoḥ tulyatā syāt iti kṛtamiti-
vācālatayā । prakṛtamanusarāmaḥ । dūṣaṇāntaraṃ cāha---<b>darśapūrṇamāsayośca prayājāderiti---
kartavyatāprasaṅgaḥ prakaraṇaviniyojyatayā</b> । asyārthaḥ---prayājādaye'pi daśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
prakaraṇaviniyojyāḥ । tataśca teṣāmapi paramāpūrvapravṛtta evādhikārī । tena sādhikāratvāt
tatrāpi itikartavyatā prasajyeta । yadi hi śrutyādiviniyojyā eva prayājādayo bhaveyuḥ
﻿<pb n="r892"/>
tadā'dhikārikalpanānavakāśa eva parṇatādivat । asaṃyuktānāṃ tu anuṣṭhānamalabhamānānāṃ
adhikārikalpanā paramiti matvok‍taṃ <b>prakaraṇaviniyojyatayeti</b> । nanu bhavatu prayājādebhiti-
kartavyatā laukikītyata āha---<b>tataśca <q>‘avyaktāsu tu somasya’</q> iti saumikītikartavyatā
prāp‍noti dīkṣaṇīyāderiva daśipūrṇamāsikīṃ</b> । asyārthaḥ---satyāmitikartavyatākāṅkṣāyāṃ
avyak‍tatvena codanāliṅgena prayājādiṣu saumikī itikartavyatā'tideśena prāpnoti । na
ceṣyate । athocyeta kathaṃ pradhānasyetikartavyatā'ṅgeṣu ityatrāha---<b>dīkṣaṇīyāderiva dārśa-
pūrṇamāsikī</b> । na pradhānaguṇabhāvaḥ sādhyatve viśeṣabhāvahati । tathā ca pradhānayorapi
darśapūrṇamāsayoraṅgeṣu dīkṣaṇoyādiṣvitikartavyatā dṛśyate iti । atra kaścitpaṇḍitaṃmanya
āha---yadi prayājādiṣu saumikavidhyantābhyupagamaḥ tarhi 1vinā somopakārakalpanayā darśapū-
māsayorupakārakalpanā nāsti । darśapūrṇamāsayorupakārakalpanayā binā somepyupakārakalpanā
nāsti iti parasparopakārakalpanayā āpatitā itaretarāśrayateti । <b>tadapi</b>svapramāṇānabhi-
jñasya mūrdh‍nā'bhidhātena girividāraṇāsaṃśasanam । tathāhi---svāṅgairevopakāraḥ kalpyate na
punaraṅgāṅgairapi । prayājādyaṅgāni pradhānavidheraṅgāni na bhavanti avāntarāpūrvapratiṣṭhitatvāditi
navame uktam । tataśca vināpi prayājāderātideśikīmitikartavyatāṃ darśapūrṇamāsayorupakāra-
kalpanā । tathā somepi vinaiva dīkṣaṇīyāvidhyantaṃ ātideśikamiti ghaṭata eva paraspara-
maṅgeṣvatideśaḥ । yāvadaṅgamatidiśyata ityuktam । tena yāvadeva saumikamaṅgaṃ tāvat
prayājādiṣvatidiśyate na punardīkṣaṇīyādṛṅgāni । tathā dīkṣaṇīyadiṣvapi yāvadaiṣṭikamaṅgaṃ
tāvata evātideśo na punaḥ prayājādyaṅgasyāpi । yadi paraṃ samāpte'tideśe aṅgānāmākṣepataḥ
prāptiḥ saiva itaretarāśrayatayā ātmāśrayatayā vā svayaṃ bādhyata iti sūkṣmadṛśāmeṣa viṣayaḥ ।
pṛcchati <b>kimiti vā na bhavati</b> iti । evaṃ manyate adhikṛtādhikāreṇa prayājādīnā-
mapi sādhikāratvāt sādhyabhūtānāṃ bhavatu saumikī itikartavyatā, pramāṇata eva bhāvitvāt
<note>(1) G. vidhinā</note>
﻿<pb n="r893"/>
iti । uttaramāha---<b>uktamavāntaraprakaraṇābhāvāditi</b> । yadyavāntaraprakaraṇaṃ syāt tadā bhavedapyati-
deśaḥ na tvasāvasti । kuto nāstītyāha---<b>na hi ekasmin prayogavacane nānā kimityā-
kāṅkṣā saṃbhavati</b> । ekasmin prayogavacane na ubhayarūpā kimityākāṅkṣā
saṃbhavati । ekenaivādhikāravidhinā prayogasyānuṣṭhānalakṣaṇasyok‍tatvāt । anuṣṭhānalābhāya hi
avikāriviśeṣaṇākāṅkṣā । labdhe punaḥ anyato'nuṣṭhāne kimadhikāriviśeṣaṇā-
kāṅkṣyā । atha manyase nānyenānuṣṭhānamākṣiptamiti tatrāha---<b>ekaścāyaṃ prayogavacanaḥ
setikartavyatākasya prayogasyaikaśabdyāditi vakṣyati</b> । eka evādhikāravidhiḥ sarvaṃ
niradhikāraṃ sannihitaṃ svārthatvena gṛhītvā viniyujya prayogamākṣipatīti darśitaṃ <b>aikaśabdāditi</b>
tasmānnāsti nānāvidhādhikāriviśeṣaṇākāṅkṣeti । niradhikāratayā prayājādīnāṃ sādhyatvāna-
vagamāt netikartavyatākāṅkṣā'stīti nāsti saumikadharmātideśaḥ । <b>kathaṃ tarhi dīkṣaṇīyāderiti</b>-
kartavyatākāṅkṣā vinā cākāṅkṣāṃ nāsyātideśikā dharmāḥ । abhyupagataṃ cedaṃ tvayā dṛṣṭāntamabhi-
dadhatā <b>dīkṣaṇīyāderiva dārśapaurṇamāsikītikartavyateti</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>mābhūvannātideśikadharmāḥ</b> ।
<b>na punaḥ kimityākāṅkṣādvayamekasmin prakaraṇe saṃbhavati</b> । asyārthaḥ---nābhyupagamena
vastu vyavasthāpyate । yadyabhyupagamo nyāye'smin sthite na ghaṭate mā ghaṭiṣṭa । etaccānvāruhya-
vacanam । paramārthatastu bhavatyeva dīkṣaṇīyādiṣu dharmaprāptiḥ । yasmādaṅgabhūteṣvapi tāvat
apūrvāṇi teṣvaṅgīkaraṇīyāni । anyathā kṣāṇikānāmaṅgatvānupapatteḥ ityuk‍tamekādaśe
<b>bhāṣyakāreṇa</b> । tāni cāpūrvāṇi prākṛtopakārāpekṣīṇīti prayājādidarśanena kalpyate । taduktaṃ
---vikṛtitve punaḥ liṅgameveti sthitiḥ । etacca kṛtsnavidhānādhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="r894"/>
<b>evaṃ sthite</b> avāntaraprakaraṇābhāve <b>yadidamucyate prakaraṇātsavanīyasyeti sthānāccāgnīṣo-
mīyasyeti tatsarvamidaṃ andhapadam</b> । asamīkṣya pravṛttatvāt । <b>tasmāt mahatā prayat‍nena
bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyeyam</b> ityākṣepaḥ । samādhānaṃ tu---<b>atrābhidhīyate । prakaraṇaṃ tābadidaṃ jyoti-
ṣṭomasya । aupavasathye'hani dharmāścodyante । na ca paśavastasminnahani sarve sannihitāḥ ।
sannihitavacanaṃ coddeśakaṃ padam । ataḥ kasyāyamuddeśaka iti cintyate viśasanādi-
vidhiṣu</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---nātra paśūnāṃ prakaraṇamaṅgīkṛtya cintyate । kintu jyotiṣṭo-
masyaiva prakaraṇam । viśasanādayaśca śrutyaiva paśusaṃbandhitayā viniyujyante । tatra paśuśabdaḥ
uddeśakaḥ uddeśakaśca śabdaḥ sannihitavacanaḥ । tatra dharmavidhiṣu kaḥ paśuṣu sannihitaḥ
yo'yamuddeśakaiḥ śabdairupādīyate iti cintyate । <b>tatra prakaraṇāviśeṣāt sarve paśavo
jyotiṣṭomārthatayā prakṛtā iti sarvārthatāṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> ।</p>
<p><b>apareṇa tu pūrvapakṣiṇā ahassāmānyasannidhānāt</b> ekasminnaupavasthye'hani
savanīyasya dharmāṇāṃ ca vidhānāc savanīyasya <b>sannidhiviśeṣo vidyata iti asti tu prakaraṇa-
viśeṣa ityuktam</b> । nanu cāvāntaraprakaraṇāṅgīkāra evātra dṛśyate yata evamāha---savanīya-
﻿<pb n="r895"/>
prakaraṇe paśudharmāssamāmnātā iti tatrāha---<b>prakṛtalakṣaṇaṃ sannidhānalakṣaṇaṃ prakaraṇamatrābhipretam</b> ।
na punaritikartavyatākāṅkṣālakṣaṇam । tena nāsti virodhaḥ । yata eva sannidhānalakṣaṇaṃ tatra
prakaraṇamabhipretaṃ <b>ata eva sthānādagnīṣomīyasyeti</b> yuktam । anyathā itikartavyatā-
lakṣaṇāt prakaraṇāt sthānasya durbalatvāt sthānasya viniyojakatvameva na syāt । sannidhāna-
pakṣe tu yuktamubhayostulyabalatvam । vidhānena hi savanīyāstatra sannihitāḥ । sthānena hi
agnīṣomīyaḥ iti yuktamubhayaśeṣatvam । <b>aprakṛtasiddh‍yarthaṃ ca sautye'hani vidhānaṃ</b>
savanīyasyetyevamādi yaduktaṃ tadupapannārthaṃ bhavati । anyathā aharantare satyapi vidhāne na jyoti-
ṣṭomavat prakaraṇābhāvaśśakyate vak‍tum । kathaṃ punaḥ <b>sannidhānaviśeṣeṇāgnīṣomīyārthatve
siddhe jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe cām‍nānasya arthavattve tasminneva prakaraṇe paśudvayasyātideśaḥ</b>
kṛtaḥ ? <b>na hyekaḥ prayogavacanaḥ upadeśena atideśena ca tāneva dharmān gṛhṇāti</b> । prayoga-
vacana evāṅgānāmitikartavyatāṃ gṛhṇāti iti bhrāntasyedaṃ codyam । uttaramāha---<b>asya codyasya
parihāramatideśe</b> vakṣyāmaḥ <b>“kṛts‍navidhānādapūrvaḥ soma’ ityatra</b> । <q>“prāptyupādānayorbhedāna-
bhijñasyaiṣā vidhiparicodanā”</q> ityanena aṅgavidhiryaḥ sa eva 1svāṅgānāṃ prāpako liṅgadarśanotthāpita-
prākṛtopakārākāṅkṣaḥ । prayojakatā tu pradhānavidheriti tatraiva vakṣyati । <b>asmin punaradhi-
karaṇe upadeśaviśeṣo darśitaḥ । upadeśaviśeṣatvācchaiṣalakṣaṇasya</b> । tenopadeśastāvadevaṃ
rūpaḥ । yadi paśudvaye atideśo ghaṭate ghaṭatām । atha na ghaṭate mā ghaṭiṣṭeti bhāvaḥ ।
<note>(1) G. savanāṅgānāṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r896"/>
<b>kaḥ punaraupavasathye'hani savanīyeṣu vidhīyamāneṣu sādhyeṣu āśvinakāle vākyabhedaḥ</b>
pūrvapakṣavādinā paricoditaḥ, pūrvapakṣavādī hi aupavasathye'hani savanīyānāṃ vidhānaṃ sādhayituṃ
āśvinakāle savanīyavidhāne vākyabhedamāha ko'sau1 vākyabheda ityarthaḥ । <b>kathaṃ vā
sautye'hani</b> savanīyeṣu <b>vidhīyamāneṣu</b> sādhyeṣu satsuṃ <q>‘āśvitaṃ grahaṃ gṛhītvā trivṛtā’</q>
ityasya vākyabhedaḥ pūrvapakṣiṇaṃ prati <b>rāddhāntinā paricoditaḥ । kiñcobhayatra vākyabheda eva
coditaḥ</b> । tataśca tulyatvāt kathaṃ siddhāntasiddhiriti manyate । uttaramāha---<b>anekaguṇa-
vidhānameva pūrvapakṣī vākyabhedaṃ manyate</b> । parivyāṇakālalakṣaṇastāvadeko guṇaḥ aparaśco-
pākaraṇa kālalakṣaṇaḥ iti guṇadvayavidhānaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । <b>rāddhāntavādyapi vapāpracāra-
mātrotkarṣaṃ manvānaḥ punarālambhavidhāne ca vākyabhedameva coditavān</b> dvayārthatāmuktavān ।
asyārthaḥ---rāddhāntavādī tu aupavasathye'hani samāmnātasyālambhasya punassautyehani vidhāne,
tathā āśvinakāle vidhāne ca vākyabhedamuktavān । na ca vapāpracāreṇa sautyāhassaṃbandhinā2
arthāt sautyamevāhaḥ prāpitaṃ tasya paścālambhasyāśvinakālatāmātraṃ vidhīyata iti śakyate
vak‍tum । vapāpracārasya guṇabhūtatvāt paśuyāgaguṇabhūto hi vapāpracāraḥ sa paśuyāga-
guṇabhūtamālambha na śaknotyutkraṣ‍ṭum । tena vapāpracāra eva sautye'hani ।
paśvālambhastvaupavasathya eva ।</p>
<note>(1) G. tenāsau</note> <note>(2) G. saṃbandhinī</note>
﻿<pb n="r897"/>
<p>nanu arthādutkarṣaḥ paśvālambhasya; na hi pūrvedyurālambhe paśorvapoddharaṇadeśaṃ yajamāno muṣṭinā
1pidhāyāsituṃ śak‍noti । avaśyaṃ hi tena hastenāhārādi kartavyam । tathā vihāro'pi
kartavya iti । na ca viharamāṇaḥ āsta ityucyate । upaveśane āste iti bhavati ।
ucyate । yadyavaśyaṃ muṣṭinā pidhāyāsituṃ tadā muṣṭiśabdena tṛṇamuṣṭiḥ syādityāśrīyatām ।
āstestu audāsīnyamarthaḥ parigṛhyatām । api codāsīnepi āsteḥ prayogaḥ kṣetrāṇi
parigṛhyāste iti । tasmādālambhotkarṣe āśvinakāle vidhāne ca vākyabhedaḥ prāp‍noti ।
<b>kiṃ punaranayorvākyabhedayordūṣaṇam</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>rāddhāntavāda‍yuktameva dūṣaṇam । apari-
hāryaṃ hi tatra vākyāntaratvam</b> । prāptakriyānuvādenānekaguṇavidhānāt । <b>pūrvapakṣavāda‍yu-
ktasya tu vākyabhedasya viśiṣṭavidhānādapi parihārasiddhiḥ</b> । anekaguṇaviśiṣṭameka-
meva vidhīyata iti । atra bhāṣyam---<b><q>“saṃskāro'yaṃ paśuprayogaprayuk‍to na jyotiṣṭoma-
prayukta”</q> iti</b> । tadākṣipati---<b>kimidaṃ jyotiṣṭomaprayuktaṃ iti</b> ? ekagranthenāha---<b>nanu
ca sarvamevedaṃ jyotiṣṭomaprayuk‍taṃ tatprakaraṇāmnānāt</b> । eka eva hi sādhikārobidhiḥ
prakaraṇām‍nātaṃ sakalaṃ prayuṅk‍te svāṅgaṃ aṅgāṅgamapi । samādhitte---<b>ucyate---viniyogābhi-
prāyo'yaṃ granthaḥ na punaḥ prayojyābhiprāyaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---dīkṣaṇīyāvāṅ‌niyamavat3 avāntarā-
pūrvasaṃbandhe paśau śrutyā dharmāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ । tena paśuyāgaprayukto na jyotiṣṭomaprayukta
ityucyate । na punaḥ jyotiṣṭomādhikāravidhinā na prayujyate । api tu tenaivānuṣṭhāpyata iti ।</p>
<note>(1) 1051</note> <note>(2) R. vidhāya</note> <note>(3) G. yāvanniyama eva</note>
﻿<pb n="r898"/>
<p><b>etadeva spaṣṭayati---na prakaraṇaviniyojyatayā prayuktiḥ, kiṃ tarhi śrutyaiva viniyogaḥ</b>
yasya hi prakaraṇena viniyogaḥ tasya sarvasya prakaraṇavat adhikāravidhigarbha eva viniyogaḥ ।
ayaṃ tu saṃskāraśrutiviniyojyaḥ । paśusaṃbandhaścāsya śrutyā avabhāti । paśuścāvāntara(vi)
niyogasaṃbandha iti tadgarbha eva viniyogo yuktaḥ । atra bhāṣyaṃ---<q>“prakaraṇavantaśca paśava”</q>
ityādi tadanupapannaṃ teṣāṃ prakaraṇābhāvādityātrāha---<b>prakaraṇavantaśceti । śak‍noti hi
tatsthānepi prayogavacanaḥ prayok‍tumiti darśayati</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadidaṃ prakaraṇavantaśce-
tyuk‍taṃ idamāśaṅkitottaram । kimāśaṅkitam ? yadyavāntaraniyogagarbhe dharmaviniyogaḥ tadā
paramāpūrvasaṃbandhābhāvāt prayuktirna labhyata iti tatredamuttaraṃ---prakaraṇavato jyotiṣṭomasya prakaraṇe
samāmnānāt tadvantaḥ । tena tān paśūnaṅgabhūtān prayuñjānaḥ tānapi viśasanādidharmān
prayuṅk‍tete, 2tairvinā svāṅganirvṛttyabhāvāditi na virodhaḥ । yata eva tānapi dharmān adhikāra-
vidhireva prayok‍tuṃ śaknoti <b>ata eva prakaraṇasthāne api prakṛtābhiprāyeṇaivetyuktam</b> ।
adhikāravidherhi prayojakatve tasyaivaikasya prakaraṇaṃ sthānaṃ ca tena sannidhānamātrābhiprāyeṇaiva
prakaraṇasthāne api draṣṭavye । na punaritikartavyatākāṅkṣālakṣaṇaṃ prakaraṇaṃ paśūnām । na
punaḥ sthānaṃ ākāṅkṣāsannidhānamiti । <b>darśanacchidrāpidhāne</b> bhāṣya eva <b>prayuk‍te</b> ।</p>
<p>dohayoḥ <b>kālabhedāt । pūrva /?/gdatrāpi sannidhānaviśeṣamaṅgīkṛtya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yathā pūrvādhikaraṇe sannidhānādagnīṣomīyārthāḥ paśudharmāḥ tathā'trāpi sannidhyāmnānāt3
<note>(1) P. 1052</note> <note>(2) G. tairvidhānāt</note> <note>(3) G. sannidhānāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r899"/>
dohadharmāḥ sāyaṃdohārthā eveti pūrvapakṣaḥ । <b>rāddhāntastu naiva dadhipayasoḥ kālabhedena
vidhānamasti</b> kintu ekakālenaiva vidhānam । tena vidhānatastāvanna dadhnaḥ sannidhānam ।
<b>yadi paraṃ krame sthāne kālabhedaḥ</b> । sāyaṃkālo hi dadhnaḥ <b>sthānaṃ sa ca prakaraṇe pratyarthini na
viniyojaka ityuk‍taṃ</b> kramaprakaraṇavirodhādhikaraṇe । dohābhinirvartyadravyasaṃbandhā hi
dohadharmāḥ adhikāravidhinā parigṛhītāḥ । adhikāravidhisaṃbandhaśca dvayorapi dadhipayasoḥ
ityaviśeṣāt dvayorapi dharmāḥ prāp‍nuvanti । sthānena tu dadhimātrasaṃbandhitā । durbalaṃ ca
sthānaṃ prakaraṇādityubhayārthā dohadharmāḥ । paśudharmāḥ punaḥ avāntarāpūrvasaṃbaddhapaśusaṃbandhānna
paramāpūrvaparigṛhītā iti sthānataḥ sannihitapaśusaṃbandhina eva yuktāḥ iti viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>tadvatsavanāntare । atrāpi pūrvavadeva sannidhānaviśeṣāśaṅkā pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ</b> ।
yathā pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣe kramataḥ sannidhānaviśeṣāśaṅkyā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ tathehāpi prātassavanaviśeṣe
sannihitā dharmā iti prātassavanakālānāmeva grahāṇāṃ syuḥ na savanāntaravartināmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu---<b>na dharmāṇāṃ savanaviśeṣe vidhānamiti sarvārthatā</b> । asyārthaḥ---sutyā-
kāle dharmāṇāṃ vidhānaṃ na savanaviśeṣe । sutyāhaḥ pracāra eva savanatrayavibhāgenopadiśyate ।
na punaḥ prātarādikālaviśeṣamāśritya dharmaviṣaya iti nāsti vidhānataḥ sannidhānaviśeṣa iti
sarvagrahārthā eva grahadharmā iti ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1053</note>
﻿<pb n="r900"/>
<p><b>raśanā ca liṅgadarśanāt । raśanāvāstu agnīṣomīyaprakaraṇa eva vidhānamiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā grahadharmā viśeṣagrahasannidhānena śrutāḥ na tathā raśanā paśu-
viśeṣasannidhānena śrutā । api tu agnīṣomīyasannidhāna eva śrutā । tenāgnīṣomīyārtheti ।
anena viśeṣeṇa pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>rāddhāntastu satyaṃ tatprakrame vidhānaṃ yūpastveka iti sarvārthatā
raśanāyāstaddharmāṇāṃ ca</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi agnīṣomīyapaśusannidhānaṃ raśanāyāḥ tathāpi
sarvapaśūnāṃ yūpasya tantratvāt ekayūpasaṃbandhena sarvapaśuṣveva raśanāyāḥ śeṣatvaṃ tanmukhena
taddharmāṇāṃ ca । tathā ca liṅgamuktam ।</p>
<p><b>ārācchiṣṭamasaṃyuktam । aṃśvadābhyayostu prakaraṇe avidhānāt uddeśakasya ca
sannihitavacanatvāt na tad‍ddharma iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । ya eva prakaraṇapaṭhitāḥ dharmavidhiṣu
sannihitā grahāḥ tāneva grahaśabda uddiśati । tena teṣāmeva grahadharmāḥ nāṃśvadābhyayo-
ranārabhyādhītayoḥ । <b>rāddhāntastu na sannihitamātravacanamuddeśakaṃ prayojanavatsannihitavacanaṃ
hi tat</b> । asyārthaḥ---na sannihitamātraṃ saprayojanaṃ niṣprayojanaṃ ca uddeśakena śabdenocyate
<note>(1) P. 1054</note> <note>(2) 1054</note> <note>(3) prakrama eva</note>
﻿<pb n="r901"/>
kintu prayojanavat yasya dharmavidhiḥ saṃbhavati sa eva dharmavidhānārthamuddiśyate । niṣprayojane
ca na dharmavidhisaṃbhavaḥ prayojanavati coddiśyamāne grahe eṣo'rthaḥ saṃpadyate yatsaubhikaṃ grahajātamupāttaṃ
tatsarvaṃ sammārjayitavyamiti । <b>abhinnaṃ cātra prayojanaṃ prakṛtānāmaprakṛtānāṃ ca grahāṇām</b> । 
tasmāt <b>prayojanāvacchinnagrahajātīye grahaśabdo vartamānaḥ na prakṛtatvena keṣāṃcid‍grahāṇāṃ
saṅkocamarhati</b> na viśiṣṭeṣu graheṣu vyavasthātumarhatītyarthaḥ । nanu ca yathā payasā maitrāvaruṇe
śrīṇātīti śrayaṇaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya na sarvagrahāṇāṃ tathehāpi kimiti na syāt ityāha---<b>maitrā-
varuṇe tu nirdeśāt</b> tasyaiva śrayaṇaṃ tatraivāvatiṣṭhata iti । <b>iha tu viparīto nirdeśaḥ</b> graha-
śabdasya grahajātīyopasthāpakatvāditi darśitaṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<p><b>agnyarthamaprakaraṇe । kaḥ punaranayoradhikaraṇayorviśeṣaḥ</b> ? [yathā anārabhyādhī-
tayorgrahadharmāḥ tathā anārabhyādhītānāmiṣṭakānāṃ dharmairbhavitavyamityarthaḥ । ekadeśī viśeṣamāha
---<b>ayamasti viśeṣaḥ । tatra</b> pūrvādhikaraṇe <b>ekasomadravyasaṃbandhitvāt yuk‍to viśeṣaḥ</b>
sarveṣāṃ grahāṇām । iha <b>punaḥ ekaikeṣṭakāvyāpārasaṃbandhitayāpi dharmavidhayo'rthavanto
bhavanti</b> । tataśceṣṭakāvyāpārabhedāt prayojanabhedāt na bhavitavyaṃ dharmairiti śaṅkāṃ ākṣeptā
﻿<pb n="r902"/>
dūṣayati---<b>tatrāpyekaikagrahavyāpārabhedo vidyate eva</b> । tathāpi sarveṣāṃ grahāṇāṃ grahadharmā
bhavanti tathaivehāpi syādeva sarveṣāmeveṣṭakānāṃ dharmasaṃbandhaḥ iti । paramasamarthanavādī tvāha
---<b>evaṃ tarhi citibhedādabhyadhikāśaṅkā</b> । asyārthaḥ.- sthūlarūpāyāściterbhedāt tatsaṃ-
nnidhāne ca dharmāḥ samāmnātāḥ । tataśca taccitiśeṣabhūtāsviṣṭakāsu syurityadhikāśaṅkā । 
<b>rāddhāntastu yadyapi citibhedaḥ tathāpi citau dharmāṇāmapratiṣṭhitatvāt</b> । apūrvasaṃbandhānāṃ
dharmairbhavitavyaṃ abhinnaṃ ca sarvacitiṣu apūrvamiti ।</p>
<p><b>naimittikamatulyatvāt</b> । evaṃ tāvat anaimittikānāṃ samānavidhānamuktam ।
<b>idamidānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ naimittikānāṃ godohanaphalacamasādīnāṃ dharmavidhayaḥ । samānāśca</b>-
masādibhiḥ camasādīnāmivopadeśata eva sarvatra dharmā iti yāvat uta camasādyarthā <b>dharmavidhayaḥ</b>
godohanaphalaṃ camasādiṣu kāryata tatkāryakāritayā dharmā bhavantīti । <b>tatra tulyabalatvāt
prakaraṇasya samānā dharmavidhaya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । 1ekasmin prakaraṇe sarveṣāṃ paṭhitatvāt
avikāravidhisaṃbandhadvārayogyatvācca sarveṣāmevopadeśāddharmairmavitavyam । <b>na ca nityatayā</b>
camasādīnāṃ viśeṣaḥ । teṣāmapi godohanādipakṣe vyudasyamānatvāt iti pūrvaḥ pakṣa
ityarthaḥ । rāddhāntastu---<b>satyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ tulyaṃ dharmavantastu nityāḥ</b> camasādayaḥ nitya-
<note>(1) R. etatprakaraṇe</note>
﻿<pb n="r903"/>
viniyuktatvāt । <b>naimittikāśca</b> godohanādayo nimitte sati sannidhānāt । <b>tad‍dvāraṃ</b>
dharmadvāraṃ <b>ca prakaraṇasya dharmagrāhakatvamiti sthitam</b> । asyārthaḥ---ete dharmā nityavadadhi-
kāravidhinā gṛhītāḥ tatra yadeva tadanuguṇaṃ tadeva dvāraṃ yuktam । nityaṃ ca nityagrahaṇānuguṇaṃ
dvāraṃ na tvanityam । tena naimittikeṣu nāsti dharmaviniyogaḥ grāhakeṇa svataḥ tasyānupāttatvāt
<b>naimittikaṃ ca nityakāryāpannaṃ bhavati ataḥ kāryataḥ siddheḥ na punarupadeśamarhati iti</b> ।
<b>dviruktatādoṣaścoktaḥ</b> । api ca kāryata eva naimittikeṣu dharmalābhānnopadeśo ghaṭate ।
anyato'pāpte vidhiriti vijñeyaḥ1 । yadi punaḥ tatrāṣi vidheyaḥ tatrāha---<b>dviruk‍tatādoṣa-
ścoktaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>pratinidhiśca tadvat</b> । <b>athedānī pratinidhau kā vārtā</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatiṃ
saṃśayaṃ cāha । <b>atrāpi hi kāryataḥ prāptiriti</b> mukhyakāryāpatteḥ mukhyadharmāḥ pratinidhā-
viti <b>pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । kutaḥ ? <b>kāryeṇākṣiptatvāt pratinidheḥ</b> । kāryeṇa hi
yathāśaktisaṃpādyena pratinidhirākṣipyate । tenānityatvātpratinidheḥ phalacamasavaditi bhāvaḥ ।
<b>atrābhidhīyate---satyaṃ kāryeṇākṣiptaḥ pratinidhiḥ upadeśasaṃpadā tulyaḥ nānyasādhyatayā</b> ।
vrīhyādyapacāre nīvārāḥ pratinidhīyante । na te svātantryeṇaiva vrīhyupadeśasaṃpattyarthameva ।
<note>(1) G. vibhāgaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r904"/>
tena vrīhaya 1evaite kiñcidvikṛtāḥ gṛhyanta iti <b>aupadeśika eva dharmasaṃbandho na kāryasādhana-
tayā dravyāntaraṃ nīvārāḥ</b> । yadi kāryasādhanatayā dravyāntaraṃ nīvārāḥ syuḥ tadā
na syādaupadeśiko dharmasaṃbandhaḥ । iha punaḥ na kāryasādhanatayā dravyāntaratvaṃ, kintu
svarūpeṇaiveti ।</p>
<p><b>niyamārthā guṇaśrūtiḥ । yatra punaḥ śrūyate pratinidhiḥ</b> yathā <b>‘yadi somaṃ na
vindet pūtīkānabhiṣuṇuyāt’</b> iti <b>tatra śrutāśaṅkatayā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । yadi pratinidhirevāyaṃ
tadā kāryata eva prāptatvāt kiṃ vidhinā । tasmāt rasāntaramevedaṃ sādhanatvena vidhīyata
iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>śrutopapattyartho'yaṃ niyama iti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । śrato yaḥ somaḥ
tadupapattyartha evāyaṃ niyamaḥ । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---pratinidhirniyamyata iti nāsti vidhyānartha-
kyamiti tenātrāpyupadeśata eva dharmā iti ।</p>
<p><b>saṃsthāstu samānavidhānāḥ । nanu cedaṃ phalacamasena gatamevādhikaraṇam</b> । tatra
hi etaduktam---<b>na naimittikasya dharmā bhavantyupadeśena iti</b> । naimittikāśca saṃsthāḥ ataḥ
tāsāmapi upadeśato na dharmairbhavitavyamiti । uk‍tameva samādhatte---<b>ucyate astvatrādhikā-</b>
<note>(1) R. ete</note>
﻿<pb n="r905"/>
<b>śaṅkā । kā punanasau ? iyamasau</b> । iha somena yajeteti śrūyate somasaṃskārāśca śrūyante 
abhiṣavaṇābhiplavanotpavanādayaḥ । tadālocanayā rasabhāvamupagataḥ somaḥ yāgasādhanamiti
<b>pratīyate</b> । tasya ca indravāyvādidevatoddeśena grahaṇamāmnāyate । devatoddeśena grahaṇamevaṃ
dṛṣṭārthaṃ bhavati yadi tāmeva devatāmuddiśya tyajyate । tataśca yā eva grahaṇe devatāḥ śrūyante
tā eva yāge devatā bhavanti । tāni ca grahaṇāni grāhyasya dravyasya vipulatvāt niyata-
parimāṇatvācca upakalpyamānānāṃ rasāṃśānāṃ samuccīyante । teṣāṃ ca prayuktānāṃ grahaṇānāṃ
1anāvṛtau yāgasyopasaṃhartumaśakyatvāt yāgasyāvṛttiravasīyate । tathā'parāṇyapi grahaṇāni
ukthyādisaṃjñakāni kāmayogena codyante <q>‘prajākāma ukthyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt’</q> iti । yatra stotra-
codanā <q>‘vīryakāmaḥ ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta’</q> iti tatrāpi grahaṇacodanā'styeva । stotrasya grahaṇa-
nimittatvāt <q>‘grahaṃ vā gṛhītvā camasaṃ vonnīya stotramupākaroti’</q> iti । tānyapi cokthyādi
grahaṇāni prakṛtasomayāgasaṃbandharasībhūtasomadravyaviṣayāṇyeva । tena tatrāpi sa eva yāgaḥ
prajākāmādibhirukthyādisaṃjñakaiḥ grahaṇaiḥ somarasamupakalpyānuṣṭheya iti pratīyate । tatra
ekatvādyāgasya yāgadharmairdīkṣaṇīyādibhirbhavitavyameva iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । tataśca teṣu
sarveṣu dharmeṣu bhavatsu aindravāyavādigrahairapi bhavitavyam । teṣāṃ ca klṛptakramatvāta 2antata eva
kāmyairgrahairbhavitavyaṃ iti saṃsthāvyapadeśo'pyupapatraḥ । yāni punaratra grahaṇāni ukthyādīti tāni
nimittasaṃyogena codyamānāni grahaṇadharmaśūnyāni bhavantu । godohanavat na teṣāmiha
dīkṣaṇīyādidharmasaṃbandhāśaṅkā yāgadharmatvāt । na hi yāgadharmaiḥ yāgadharmaḥ saṃbadhyate samatvā-
diti । sarvamidaṃ darvamidaṃ darśayitumupakramate---<b>ukthyādayo hi grahaṇaviśeṣāḥ</b> somarasāvakalpana-
viśeṣāḥ <b>te ca gṛhyamāṇasya saṃskārāḥ svayamitikartavyatābhūtāḥ</b> । <b>na cetikartavyatā
itikartavyatayā saṃbadhyate</b> । kiṃ tarhi ? <b>yāgena</b> । idamatrābhipretam---yadi grahaṇānāmeva
<note>(1) R. anāvṛtte</note> <note>(2) R. atantrata eva</note>
﻿<pb n="r906"/>
dīkṣaṇīyādayo dharmāḥ śaṅkyeran tadā naimittikānāṃ na bhaveyuḥ । <b>na ca grahaṇānāṃ dharmasaṃbandhaḥ</b> ।
kintu yāgasya । <b>sarvagrahaṇasaṃskāryadravyakaścāyaṃ yāgaḥ somena yajeteti</b> । ya
eva yāgaḥ sarvagrahaṇasaṃskāryadravyakaḥ sa evāyamukthyādipvapi sarvairgahaiḥ yaḥ saṃskāryaḥ somarasaḥ
sa eva dravyaṃ yasyeti vigrahaḥ । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---devatāviśeṣoddeśena ca yāni grahaṇāni kriyante
tairyo rasabhāgaḥ upakalpyate tenāyaṃ somayāgaḥ kriyate । ukthyādiṣvapi tāvata yāgaśeṣasoma-
grahaṇameva । tena tatrāpi sa eva yāgaḥ kartavya iti । <b>nāsya yāgasya ukthyādiṣu
anyā utpattirvidyate</b> । api tu somena yajetetyevotpatiḥ । <b>sa cedyāgaḥ grahaṇāntareṣūkthyā-
diṣu itikartavyatāpi saiva yaiva</b> aindravāyavādigrahaṇaiḥ yāge kriyamāṇe iti yāvat1 ।
yadi yāvad‍grahaṇaviśeṣo'gniṣṭomāntaḥ yāgasya dharmaprāptau nimittaṃ syāt tadā grahaṇāntareṣu
ukthyādiṣu na syāditikartavyatā । na caitadasti । tadāha---<b>na ca grahaṇaviśeṣo yāga-
syetikartavyatāprāptau nimittaṃ, kiṃ tarhi prayogacodanaiva</b> anuṣṭheyatvena codanaiva dharmaprāptau
nimittam । <b>na ca grahaṇāntareṣu prayogāntaracodanā yāgasya</b> । ukthyādiṣvapi grahaṇā-
ntareṣu na yāgasya prayogāntaracodanā । kiṃ tarhi ? ya eva somena yajeteti prayoyaścoditaḥ
sa evokathyādiṣvapi । aindravāyavādiṣviva <b>guṇānāmeva hi grahaṇaviśeṣāṇāṃ tatrokthyādiṣu
phalāya codanā na yāgasya</b> । <b>yathā godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayediti na darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ</b>
<note>(1) R. iti yāvat --- iti nāsti</note>
﻿<pb n="r907"/>
<b>prayogaścodyate । tasmādbhavantu grahaṇāti grahaṇadharmopadeśaśūnyāni phalacamasavat । na
punaryāgo'pi yāgadharmairasaṃbaddha iti śakyate vak‍tum । sarvasaṃskāreṣu ekaprayogasya
ekasyānuṣṭhānasya coditatvāt prayogagrāhyatvāditikartavyatāyā ityuk‍taṃ prāk</b> । yata
eva samānavidhānāḥ <b>sarvasaṃsthāḥ ata evāgniṣṭomagrahaṇam</b> । <q>‘yadyagniṣṭomaṃ juhoti’</q> iti ।
dyagniṣṭomāntasyaivaupadeśikā dharmāḥ ttadā antareṇāpyagniṣṭomagrahaṇaṃ agniṣṭomasyaiva syāt । 
tatrāgniṣṭomagrahaṇamanarthakaṃ syāt । samānavidhāne tu viśeṣasaṃskārasaṃbandhārthaṃ agniṣṭomagrahaṇaṃ
<b>samuccayaśca pradarśitaḥ</b> । paśūnāṃ samānavidhānena hi āg‍neyasya sarvasaṃsthāsu aupadeśikatvāt
vaiśeṣikaiḥ ukthyādisaṃsthāsaṃbandhibhiḥ paśubhiḥ samuccayo ghaṭate । tena tasmin sati 
dvitīyatṛtīyadarśanamupapadyate itarathā ātideśikasyāgneyasya ukthyādisaṃsthābhāgbhiḥ
aupadeśikairvādhe sati samuccayo na syāditi । atra codayati---<b>paśūnāmadṛṣṭārthatayā
samuccaya eva nyāyyaḥ</b> । tathā ca vakṣyati prājāpatyeṣu cāmnānāt iti । <b>atrocyate
---savanīyasamākhyayā sarvapaśūnāṃ tulyakāryāvagamāt</b> yukta eva bādhaḥ । tasmādupapannaṃ
liṅgadarśanam । <b>atrābhidhīyate---satyamevaṃ syāt yadi, saṃsthāntareṣūkthyādiṣu prayoga-
codanayaiva</b> yāgakartavyatā <b>labhyate yathā godohanena darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ</b>। iha tu agniṣṭoma-
﻿<pb n="r908"/>
<b>saṃskāraparyantaiva yāgasya prayogacodanā</b> । iha tu anaimittikāḥ kratvarthāḥ ye
agniṣṭomāntā grahaṇākhyāḥ saṃskārāḥ tatparyantaiva yāgasya somena yajetetyanenānuṣṭhāna-
codanā । <b>ata ūrdhvaṃ kāmasaṃyogena codyante grahā ukthyādayaḥ ta eva yāgacoda-
nāmākṣipanti</b> । yathā ainadravāyavādayo nityā <b>grahāḥ āvṛttim । evaṃ cet na
yāgacodanayā dharmāḥ śakyante grahītuṃ ukthyādiṣu । ataḥ phalacamasavat
nityānityasaṃyogavirodho yuktaḥ</b> । ukthyādiṣu yāgasyānuṣṭhānacodanā naimittikī kāmyairgrahai-
rākṣipyamāṇatvāt । <b>nityāśca yāgasaṃbandhino dharmāḥ te nityānuṣṭhānena gṛhītā bhavitumarhanti</b>
anityānuṣṭhānagṛhītatve tu nityānityasaṃyogavirodhaḥ syāt iti siddhamatrāpi phalacamasavat
nokthyādiṣu grahaṇākṣiptasya ekasyāpi yāgasya dharmā iti । <b>kāryataśca dharmaprāptiḥ । ataḥ
samuccayagrahaṇaṃ vacanāt bhaviṣyati</b> । asyokthyādigrahaṇākṣiptayāgaviṣayasyādhikāravidherupa-
kārāpekṣāyāṃ sannihitanityasaṃsthādhikāraniyogopakāragrahaṇāt kāryato dharmāṇāṃ prāptiḥ । tataścau-
padeśikena bādhe prāptaṃ vacanāt samuccayo bhaviṣyati । <b>agniṣṭomaśabdaścānuvādo</b> bhaviṣyati । 
<q>“yadyagniṣṭomo juhoti”</q> iti vacanena । na anuvādo doṣaḥ anuvādakānyapi hi vacanāni
dṛśyante yathā <q>“dvayoḥ praṇayanti”</q> iti । <b>tathā homādīnāmabhāvadarśanamupapannaṃ bhaviṣyati</b> ।
<q>“yadyukthyaḥ paridhimanakti na juhoti”</q> iti pracaraṇīhomaśeṣasya pratipattiriyam । tatra
samānavidhānapakṣe yadyagniṣṭomo juhotīti agniṣṭomahomaḥ prāpnoti iti । tathā ukthye paridhya-
﻿<pb n="r909"/>
ñjanasya । tanna <q>‘na juhoti’</q> iti homābhāvānuvādo na ghaṭate anuvādasarūpaṃ cedam । vartamānā-
padeśāt । prakṛtivikārabhāve caupadeśikena paridhyañjanena tulyakāryeṇa bādhitatvāt homā-
bhāvānuvādo yujyate । upadeśataḥ prāptau yathopadeśaṃ kāryamiti ubhayorupadeśabalena samuccayaḥ
kalpyaḥ । kāryatastu prāptau klṛpta eva kārye vidhānamiti yuk‍taiva prākṛtapratipattibhūtahoma-
nivṛttiḥ iti ।</p>
<trailer>iti ṛjuvimalāpañvikāyāṃ
tṛtīyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="r910"/>

<section>
<head>atha ṛjuvimalāyāṃ
tutīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>prakaraṇāviśeṣādasaṃyuk‍tam</b> । <b>barhirdharmāśca kimaṅkapradhānārthā uta pradhānārthā eveti
sandehe prakaraṇāt pradhānārthā ityuk‍tvā upakārakatvenāṅgapradhānārthatāmāha</b> । anena yathā-
śrutamadhikaraṇamanubhāṣitamākṣep‍tum । ākṣipati---tadayuktam । <b>śrutyādibhirhi tādarthyamavagamyate
nopakāreṇa</b> । yatpradhānārthatvaṃ pratibhāti na tadupakāreṇa śakyane'nyathākartum । upakāralakṣaṇasya
viniyogapramāṇasyābhāvāditi । samādhatte---<b>ucyate । śrutyādaya evopanyastā</b> aṅgapradhānārthatva-
siddhaye । <b>barhiṣi havīṃṣyāsādayatīti</b> haviśśabdena sarvahaviṣāmevābhidhānāt aṅgapradhānārthatā
barhiṣaḥ śrutyaiveti । yadi śrutyā śeṣatvaṃ <b>upakāragrahaṇaṃ tarhi kimartham ? uttaraṃ---kadā-
cit tadabhāvāt śruteḥ saṅkocaḥ syāt</b> । <b>asti cāsāvekarūpa upakāra iti tadabhidhānam</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yadidamupakārābhidhānaṃ tadāśaṅkānivṛttyartham । śeṣatvaṃ sarvatropakāravyatirekeṇa
nāsti । tena aṅagapradhānahavirarthaḥ upakāro'vepaṇīyaḥ । tatra yadekatra dṛṣṭa upakāraḥ anyatrā-
dṛṣṭarūpaḥ syāta tadā dṛṣṭenaivopakāreṇa yatra śeṣatvaṃ tatraiva śeṣatā syāt seyamāśaṅkā mābhūditi sarvatra
<note>(1) P. 1073</note>
﻿<pb n="r911"/>
dṛṣṭa ekarūpa upakāra iti darśayitumupakārābhidhānam । yadyaṅgapradhānārthatā <b>evaṃ tarhi vākyenaiva
śebasya varhirdharmāṇāmanvayaḥ</b> । vākyena cedanvayaḥ barhirmātre piṣḍapitṛyajñavartinyapi 
<b>kimiti na bhavati</b> । prakaraṇena hyanvaye yasyaiva prakaraṇaṃ tasyaiva dharmāḥ syuriti। codyaṃ
pariharati - grāhakatve sati śeṣatvamuktam । <q>“prakaraṇaviśeṣādvikṛtau virodhi syāt ”</q> ityatra
grahakeṇa gṛhītaṃ viniyujyata ityuk‍taṃ saptamādye । <b>grāhakaścātra dārśapūrṇamāsikaprayoga-
vidhiḥ tatsannidhānāddharmāṇāmiti</b> nānyadīyadharmāṇāṃ prāptiriti । <b>liṅgadarśanamuktama</b> ।</p>
<p><b>phalasaṃyogāt‍tu</b> । atna bhāṣyakāraḥ keśaśmaśruvapanādīnāṃ kimaṅgapradhānārthatā uta
pradhānārthataiveti vicārayati । tatna kāraṇabhutaṃ sandehaṃ vak‍tumudāharaṇaśuddhimāha - <b>iha purūṣa-
saṃskārā udāharaṇamiti</b> । yadyapyatna dvitīyānirdeśo nāsti tathāpi lokata eva vapanādīnāṃ
purūṣasaṃskāratvena darśanāt purūṣasaṃskārā evaite । saṃprati kāraṇasandehamāha---<b>te kiṃ kartṛbhutasya
utādhikṛtasyeti</b> । dve hi purūṣasyāvasthe karmaṇi । ekā tāvadadhikṛtāvasthā aiścaryalakṣaṇā,
aparā kartravasthā । tadyadi kartravasthasya purūṣasya saṃskāraḥ tadā karturaṅgapradhānārthatvāt tatsaṃskāro-
pyaṅgapradhānārthaḥ ityagrīṣomīyapaśuvikāre paśubandhepi vapanādayaścodakātsyuḥ । athāddikṛtāva---
sthasya saṃskāraḥ tadā pradhāna eva purūṣasyādhikārāt tadarthā vapanādayaḥ syuḥ iti । <b>katṛbhūtasya
evaṃ karmāṅgatopapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ kartā hi karmaṇo'ṅgam । yadi 
<note>(1) P. 1077</note>
﻿<pb n="r912"/>
tasyaiva te saṃskārā bhaveyuḥ tadā karmāṅgatā dharmāṇāmapi syāta । adhikṛtāvasthastu pradhānabhutaḥ
tasya saṃskārā na karmaṇo'ṅgam । anaṅgāvasthāsaṃbandhitvāt akarmāṅgabhūtasya ca niyoga---
saṃbandhitaiva hīyate । tasmāt kartṛbhūtasyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntamāha---<b>kimityaṃ-
śopanipātinī itikartavyateti saptamādye vakṣyāmaḥ । ākāṅkṣādvayasya tatprasūteḥ</b>
asyārthaḥ---yā kācidirk‍tavyatā sā sādhyāṃśopanipātinī । na śādhanāṃśe । kutaḥ ?
kena kathamityākāṅkṣādvayasya 2tatkartṛtvāt । sādhyameva setikartavyatākaṃ karaṇamākāṅkṣati ।
na punaḥ karaṇamitikartavyatāmākṣipati iti saptamādye darśitam । evaṃ sthite kiṃ kartṛbhāve
yogyatāmāpādayati utādhikṛtabhāve ayaṃ saṃskāra iti cintyate । tatra <b>yadarthaḥ kartṛbhāvaḥ
saṃskāro'pi tadartha eva yuktaḥ</b> । adhikṛtabhāvārthaṃ hi kartṛtvam । aiśvaryalakṣaṇasyādhi-
kārasya saṃpatyarthaṃ puruṣaḥ kartṛtāmavalambata iti । pradhānabhūtādhikṛtāvasthasyaiva puruṣasya saṃskāro
yuktaḥ <b>adhikāraniṣpattyarthatvācchāstrasya । tasmādadhikṛtasya saṃskāra iti yuktam</b> । 
phalabhūtādhikāranirvṛttau ca sāhāyyaṃ vāñchantau'dhikṛtasaṃskārā api bhavantītikartavyatābhūtā
yāgasyetyuk‍taṃ bhāṣye ।</p> 
<p><b>cikīṃrṣayā ca saṃyogāt । barhirdharmādhikaraṇena kimatrānyatvaṃ yenedamadhikaraṇa-
mārabhyate</b> । yathā tatra barhirāderaṅgapradhānārthatā tathā'trapi vederaṅgapradhānārthataiva yuktā ।
<note>(1) P. 1078</note> <note>(2) R. tatkṛtatvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r913"/>
kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamārabhyate । uttaraṃ---<b>pradhānacikīrṣāṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
-pūrvapakṣavādī pradhānasyaiva cikīrṣāṃ manyate । tathāpi kimityāha---<b>yadarthā cikīrṣā tadarthānye-
vāṅgānītyabhiprāyaḥ</b> । yadeva hi cikīrṣitaṃ tadarthānyevāṅgānīti yuktam । etenaiva nyāyena
saṃrvatraivam---yadapi sāmānyatopadiṣṭaṃ---barhiṣi havīṃṣyāsādayatīti tadapyatrodāharaṇamityava-
seyam । ata eva tadarthānyaṅgānīti bahuvacanam ।</p> 
<p><b>tathā'bhidhānena । abhimarśane tu sākṣāt pradhānaśabdasaṃyogāt pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
caturhotrā paurṇamāsīmiti paurṇamāsīśabdasya pradhānavacanatvāt pradhānahaviṣāmeva abhimarśanaṃ,
pradhānasaṃbandhīnyeva havīṃṣi abhimarśanaṃ prati pradhānaśabdenopasthāpyante na punaraṅgahavīṃpyapi । eva-
mudāharaṇadvaye nyāyena vacanena ca pūrvapakṣaṃ kṛtvā saṃprati rāddhāntamāha---<b>satyaṃ pradhānaṃ cikīrṣyate 
tat‍tu sāṅgamadhikāranirvṛttāviti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । ko brūte pradhānaṃ na cikīrṣyata iti ।
kintu tadeva cikīrṣyata iti na śakyate vak‍tum । adhikāranirvṛttyarthaṃ tasya cikīrṣā ।
sāṅgaṃ ca pradhānamadhikāraṃ nirvartayati । nāṅgarahitam । tena sāṅgaṃ cikīrṣyata iti । 
<b>evamabhimarśanamapyadhikārasādhanasyaiva</b> । tatrāpi hi dvitīyādarśanena īpsitatamatvāvagateḥ ।
īpsitatamatā ca sādhanasyaiva, na kevalaṃ karaṇamātrasya । sādhanaṃ ca setikartavyatākaṃ karaṇa-
<b>mityubhayoḥ</b> vedyabhimarśanayoḥ <b>aṅgapradhānārthatā</b> । tulyāsiddhāntatayā ca dvau pūrvapakṣau kṛtvā
siddhāntitam ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1079</note>
﻿<pb n="r914"/>
<p><b>dīkṣādakṣiṇaṃ tu vacanātpradhānasya । dīkṣādakṣiṇamapi sāṅgādadhikāranirvṛtte.
sāṅgasyetyāśaṅkya vacanātpradhānasyeti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । kutaḥ ? anena pūrvapakṣarāddhāntau
dvāvapyuk‍tau । kartṛsaṃskāratāṃ ca dīkṣāyā abhyupagamyeyaṃ cintā । tatra sāṅgasyādhikāra-
nirvartakatvāt sāṅgamevānuṣṭheyam । tadaṅgabhūtaḥ kartā । kartṛsaṃskāro'pi tadaṅgabhūta eveti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । vacanaṃ tu sāṅgapradhānābhiprāyeṇa varṇanīyam । na vacanasyānyārthatve pramāṇa-
mastīti rāddhāntitam । saṃprati codayati---<b>yuk‍taṃ tāvat dīkṣā pradhānasya । yadā punardakṣiṇā
pradhānasya tadā kathamaparikrītairaṅgāni kriyante</b> ? tāni cārtvijyādīni । <b>kena vok‍taṃ 
aparikrītairaṅgāni kriyanta iti</b> । 3<b>prākṛtamānatikāraṇaṃ bhaviṣyatyeva</b> । dīkṣaṇīyā-
diṣvaiṣṭikeṣu codakaprāptā dakṣiṇā bhaviṣyati । yadi tatra prākṛtī dakṣiṇā <b>na tarhi prasaṅgo</b>
dakṣiṇāyāḥ । <b>yathā prasaṅgaḥ tathā prasaṅgalakṣaṇa eva vakṣyāmaḥ । darśanamuktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>tathā yūpasya vediḥ । ardhamantarvedīti śrūyate kiṃ vediḥ yūpāḍgaṃ uta neti saṃśaye</b>
<note>(1) P. 1081</note> <note>(2) P. 1082</note> <note>(3) prākṛtamāha kiṃkāraṇaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r915"/>
<b>śruteraṅgamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । ardhamantarvedīti vacanāt vediraṅagaṃ yūpasyeti pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu---<b>bahirvedipadaikavākyatvāt na śrutyarthavidhānaṃ saṃbhavatīti deśalakṣaṇā ।
ubhayavidhāne vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt</b> । asyārthaḥ--- <q>“vajro vai yūpaḥ, yadantarvedi minuyāt nirdaheta
yadvahirvedi anavaruddhaḥ syāt ardhamantarvedyardhaṃ bahirvedi minoti । avaruddhaḥ syāt na nirdahati”</q>
iti upakramopasaṃhārayoḥ ekavākyatvāt ekamidaṃ vākyāmiti niścīyate । yadyantarvedīti
śrutyarthaḥ parigṛhyate tadā bahirvedipadaikavākyatā nopapadyate ityekavākyatāsiddha‍yarthaṃ deśalakṣaṇaiva
nyāyyeti ।</p> 
<p><b>śāmidhenīstadanvāhuriti । kaḥ punaḥ pūrveṇāsya viśeṣaḥ</b> । yathā pūrvatra deśa-
lakṣaṇā, tathā'trāpi havirdhānena deśo lakṣyatāmiti । uttaraṃ---<b>ayamasti viśeṣaḥ padāntarā-
saṃbaddhaṃ hyatra havirdhānaṃ śrūyate । nāntarvedivat bahirvedipadasaṃbaddham । tasmādaṅgāṅgibhāva
eva nyāyya iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । śruteḥ</b> । tatra hi śrutyarthaparityāge bahirvedipadaika-
vākyatā kāraṇam । iha tu tadabhāvāt śrauta evārtho grāhyaḥ । tena havirdhānāṅgatā
sāmidhenīnām, sāmidhenyaṅgatā vā havirdhānasya yuktā । na viniyuktaviniyogavirodho nāma
kaścidvirodho'sti । tathā hi---ekaiva dadhijātiḥ kratau puruṣe ca viniyujyate । yaddhi na
<note>(1) P. 1084</note>
﻿<pb n="r916"/>
yathā dṛśyate tadviruddhamityucyate tadāha---<b>vijñānaviparītaṃ hi viruddhamabhidhīyate</b> । itamevā-
viruddhaṃ yadyathā jñāyate tathā iti । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu ubhayoḥ anyārthatvāt deśalakṣaṇasaṃbandha
eva nyāyya iti manyate</b> । ayamāśayaḥ---yadyapi vastuvirodho nāsti tathāpi yadanyasaṃbandhitayā
pratipat‍tumeva na śakyate, yathā na devadattīyaṃ yajñadattīyamiti pratipattiḥ । iha havirdhānamiti
havissaṃbabandhaḥ pratīyate tathā samidhenīriti samindhanasaṃbandhaḥ pratīyate tena śrautārthānvayānupapatteḥ
deśalakṣaṇayā saṃbandho'vasīyate । <b>tathā <q>‘havirdhānaṃ’</q> <q>‘sāmidhenyaḥ’</q> iti samākhyā na
pīḍitā bhavati । anyathā hi</b> śrutyarthaparigrhe, <b>havirdhānaṃ sāmidhenīnāṃ sāmidhenyo vā
havirdhānasyeti devadattasyedaṃ yajñadattasyeti yathedamasaṃbaddhaṃ tathedamapi syāt tasmādatrāpi
pūrvavat deśalakṣaṇaiveti yuktam । āg‍neyyadhikaraṇavacca sāmānyaviśeṣasaṃbandhe vākyabhedaḥ
syāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā āg‍neyyadhikaraṇe aprakṛtānāṃ grahaṇe tāsāṃ sāmānyasaṃbandhe
viśeṣasaṃbandhe ca vākyabhedaḥ, tathehāpi syāt atrāpi sāmānyena tāvaddhavirdhānasaṃbandhaḥ punaśca
yasmin sunvanti havirdhāne tatsaṃbandha iti vākyabhedaḥ syāt ।</p>
<p><b>śāstraphalaṃ prayoktari । kathaṃ punaratra parikrayādiṣu śrūvamāṇeṣu saṃśayaḥ ?</b>
asyārthaḥ---yadā varaṇaṃ parikrayaśca śrūyate tadā tayoḥ dṛṣṭārthatvenānatikāraṇatvāt parikrītai-
<note>(1) P. 1086</note>
﻿<pb n="r917"/>
ranyaireva padārthāḥ kartavyāḥ । tathā <b>‘maitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyati cānucāha’</b> iti sākṣādanya eva
śrūyate । tathā ādhvaryavaṃ ityādyāḥ samākhyāḥ santi iti kathamatra saṃśayaḥ ? pūrvapakṣā-
bhāvāditi । samarthayate---<b>ayamabhiprāyaḥ-kartṛgāmikriyāphalaṃ atra śrūyate</b> । adhikāra---
vidhisāmarthyāt kartṛtvamatrādhikāriṇaḥ śrūyate । tatra yadi paraḥ padārthān kuryāt kartṛtvameva
vihanyeta । <b>atastadvirodhāt</b> adhikārasāmarthyāvagatakartṛtvāvirodhāt parikrayaṃ manyate
gauṇaṃ tena nāyaṃ parikrayaḥ parikrayavadbhaviṣyati parikrayo'dṛṣṭārtho vā bhaviṣyati । tadāha
---<b>adṛṣṭārthaṃ vā manyate</b> pūrvapakṣavādī । maitrāvaruṇādiśabdaśca kathañcita yajamānaparatayā
varṇanīyaḥ । <b>kathaṃ tarhi ādhvaryavamitvādyāḥ samākhyāḥ?</b> karmaṇāmadhvaryusaṃbandhābhāvāt ।
<b>granthasaṃyogādupapannā bhaviṣyanti</b> । granthā evādhvaryavaḥ tadvihitaṃ ca karma ādhvaryavaṃ
bhaviṣyati । <b>tasmāt svayaṃ kartṛtaiva nyāyyeti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । aniyamavādī tu
dravyotsargamātraṃ svayameva kartavyaṃ svatvatyāgalakṣaṇatvāttasya, śeṣaṃ tvanyaḥ svayaṃ vā kuryāditi ।
aniyamaṃ yo vadati , sa manyate <b>parikrītairapi kriyamāṇaṃ tenaiva kṛtaṃ bhavati</b> । kṛtaḥ ?
<b>sa hi teṣāṃ prayok‍tā prayok‍tuśca kartṛtvasmaraṇaṃ</b> tatprayojako hetuśceti cakārāt kartṛtva-
smaraṇāt । adhikāraśca niyoganibandhanāṃ siddhimākṣipati । <b>na punarāhatyaiva kartṛtvam</b>
tena na kaścittasya virodhaḥ । utsargastu svadravyatyāgalakṣaṇatvāt svayameva kartavyo yajamānena
<b>evaṃ kartṛtve upapanne na parikrayasya gauṇatā adṛṣṭārthātā vā śakyate kalpayitum । samā-</b>
﻿<pb n="r918"/>
<b>khyāśca</b> ādhvaryavamityevamādyāḥ karmaṇāṃ <b>mukhyā bhaviṣyanti na granthadvārikāḥ</b> । nanu
grantha evādhvarya<b>vādayaḥ</b> samākhyāḥ <b>na karmaṇi ityatrāha---na hyadhyetāraḥ adhvaryuśabdābhidheyāḥ
adhyayanakāle</b> । yadyadhyetṝṇāmadhvaryuśabdenābhidhānaṃ syāt tadā tadyogāt granthe samākhyā
syāt । na caitadasti । karmakāla eva tadva‍yapadeśa iti karmakarāṇāmevādhvaryvādiśabdā vācakāḥ
tadyogāt karmaṇyeva mukhyā saṃjñeti । <b>kathaṃ punaraniyanaṃ manyate ?</b> parikrayaṇādīnāṃ
nityavacchravaṇāt । yuk‍taṃ cotsargadvāreṇāpi kartṛtvopapatteḥ nityamanyaireva śeṣaḥ kartavya iti ।
<b>ayamabhiprāyaḥ---yadā svayamanutsāhī tadā parikrayaḥ yadā'sau parikrayaḥ tadā anyaireveti
manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ--- dṛṣṭārthaparyālocanayā aśaktipakṣa eva puruṣāntarāpekṣāyāṃ parikrayādaya
iti । śak‍tena tu svayaṃ kartavyamiti । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu manyate nityavadāmnānāt parikrayasya
yadā svayaṃ na śak‍nuyāt tadā parikrayeṇeti na śakyate kalpayitum</b> । tena nityaṃ
parikrītaireva śeṣakāryaṃ kartavyam । <b>nanu sāmarthyāt bhaviṣyati</b> । yadā na śak‍nu-
yādityetat sāmarthyāt bhaviṣyati lokavat । pariharati---<b>na hi śrutau pratyarthinyāṃ sāmarthye
prabhavati</b> । śrutiścātra nityameva parikrayaṃ bravīti । yadetyaśravaṇādityuktam । <b>loke tu
dṛṣṭārthatvādyadhathārthamiti yuktam</b> । niyogastvatrādṛṣṭarūpaḥ parikrītapuruṣasādhya eveti nityaṃ
parikraya upādātavyaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r919"/>
<p><b>tatrārthāt kartṛparimāṇam । evaṃ sthite utsargādanyatra parikritakartṛtve pareṣāṃ
saṅkhyā'niyamaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । kāryārthaṃ hi puruṣā upādīyante । tatra yadā
yāvadbhiḥ kāryaṃ tāvanta upādeyāḥ । nanu stokeṣūpādīyamāneṣu kathaṃ samākhyā ghaṭiṣyate ?
kathaṃ ca varaṇabheda upapadyate ? vṛtatvāditi । tatrāha---<b>ekasminnapi samākhyāvaraṇayośca
upapatteḥ</b> । ekatraiva samākhyānāmupapattiḥ vṛkṣatarunyāyena । tathā ekasyaiva tatatkarmārthatayā
varaṇabheda upapadyate । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu utpattau tāvat samākhyāto bhedaṃ manvānaḥ</b> । śrutau
tāvadādhvaryavādisamākhyā pratīyate । tatra tadbhedāt sajñināmapi bheda evāvabhāti ।
<b>ma punareka eka saṃjñau codanāvagamyatvāt saṃjñānām</b> । etā hi saṃjñāḥ codanāta evāva-
gamyante na lokataḥ । yadi lokato'vagamyeta tadā tadanurūpo'bhedo bhedo vā bhavet ।
codanāvagamye yathācodanaṃ saṃjñābhedāt saṃjñibheda iti <b>yāvaccodanaṃ</b> puruṣāḥ yāvatyaḥ
utpatticodanāḥ tāvantaḥ puruṣā ityuktavān । <b>evaṃ darśapūrṇamāsādiṣvapītyuktam</b> । atrādhi-
karaṇe pūrvapakṣasiddhāntaracane īdṛśī---ekatrāpi saṃjñānānātvadarśanāt na bhedaḥ saṃjñināmiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu puruṣāṇāmetāḥ saṃjñāścodanāvagamyāḥ । tatra ca śabdabhedāt
adhikārthatvameva nyāyyam । na punarekasyaiva śabdārthasya anekaśabdatvādupapattiḥ2 । yatra
punaḥ pramāṇāntareṇa darśanaṃ tatra kiṃ kriyatāmiti ।</p> 
<note>(1) P. 1089</note> <note>(2) śabdatvāpattiḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r920"/>
<p><b>camasādhvaryavaśca tairvyapadeśāt । camasādhvaryavaśca kiṃ ṛtvik‌saṅkhyāsaṅkhyethāḥ
uta saṅkhyāntaraparicchedyāḥ</b> ityākṣeytuṃ saṃśayo'nubhāṣitaḥ । ākṣepamāh---nanu <b>ca
hotṛkāṇāṃ camasādhvaryava iti vyapadeśāt anyaireva</b> camasādhvaryubhirbhavitavyam । tataśca
pūrvapakṣābhāvāt saṃśaya eva nāstītyarthaḥ । <b>parasparavyapadeśādapyetadupapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
anyonyamṛtvijāṃ ṛtvigantarāpekṣayā sa vyapadeśa iti na ṛtvik‌saṅkhyātiriktāścamasādhvaryavaḥ ।
<b>na ṣaṣṭa‍yantānāṃ parasparasaṃbandho vidyata iti saddhāntavādī vyatirik‍taṃ manyate</b> । asvārthaḥ
---sarva eva ṛtvijaḥ ṣaṣṭha‍yantena nirdiśyante <q>‘hotrakāṇāṃ’</q> <q>‘madhyataḥ kāriṇāṃ’</q> ityevamādiṣu
vākyeṣu । na ca ṣaṣṭha‍yante parasparaṃ sabandhāvagatiḥ yathā devadattasya bhrātā yajñadattasya bhrāteti
tābhyāmanyaḥ pratīyate na punaḥ parasparaṃ tayoḥ saṃbandha iti ṛtvigdhyatirik‍tāścamasādhvaryavaḥ ।
<b>utpattau ca saṃjñābhedāt</b> yad‌yutpattau saṃjñābhedo na syāt tadā laukikīyaṃ samākhyeti
yathālokaṃ varteta । tataśca bhedo na syāt । uttpattau saṃjñābhedāt yukto'rthabhedaḥ । tasmādanye
camasādhvaryavaḥ iti ।</p> 
<p><b>utpattau bahuśruteḥ । idamidānīṃ sandihyate---kimaniyatā uta bahava iti</b> ।
<note>(1) P. 1089</note> <note>(2) P. 1092</note>
﻿<pb n="r921"/>
<b>prātipadikārthasiddheraniyatāḥ</b> । ekasminnapi prātipadikārthasiddheraniyatāḥ । nanu kathaṃ
bahuvacanaṃ camasādhvaryūn vṛṇīta iti tatrāha---<b>aniyame'pi pakṣe bahuvacanopapatteḥ</b> ।
rāddhāntamāha---<b>na, nityavadbahuvacanasya śrūyamāṇatvāt</b> pākṣikatvānupapatteḥ । nanu ca
camasādhvaryūṇāmūddeśyatvāt grahavadavivakṣitā saṅkhyetyatrāha---<b>utpattau ca bahuvacanasya
vivakṣitatvāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi camasādhvaryavaḥ iha vākye uddeśyāḥ tathāpi teṣāṃ
saṅkhyā'navagatā ityasti saṅkhyāpekṣā kiyanta utpādyanta iti । tenāpekṣitatvāt vivakṣitā
saṃkhyeti । grahe tu vijñātatvāt saṅkhyāyāḥ apekṣaiva nāstīti yuktā tatrāvivakṣā ।
tadāha---<b>asiddhārthalakṣaṇaṃ prātipadikaṃ na vacanamapekṣate notpādyavacanam । tasmādvahavaḥ</b> ।
idamevātra vyutpādyate utpādyagatā saṅkhyā uddeśyatvepi vivakṣiteti ।</p>
<p><b>daśatvaṃ liṅgadarśanāt । sthite bahutve kimaniyamaḥ, uta niyataiva kācit
bahuvacanābhidheyā saṅkhyā, uta tritvasaṅkhyaiveti</b> saṃśayaḥ । anena avāntarasaṅgatimāha
---<b>kapiñjalavat tritvasaṅkhyaiveti</b> aniyama iti vā prāpte <b>daśapeye</b> vikṛtibhūte siddhavat
daśa camasādhvaryudarśanāt daśaiveti niyamaḥ । <b>svāmidaśatvācca । atra ca aniyamapakṣa</b>
<note>(1) P. 1092</note>
﻿<pb n="r922"/>
upakramamātram । kapiñ‍jalānyāyena traya eveti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ daśapeye daśadarśanādiha
daśa bhaveyurityatrāha---<b>anyatrāpi niyatā saṅkhyā upadeśaṃ niyantumarhati avirodhāt</b> ।
yadyatra trayo bhaveyuḥ tadā siddhavaddarśanaṃ nopapadyate daśapakṣe tu bahuvacanasya na kaścidvirodhaḥ daśā-
nāmapi bahutvāt । <b>tathā cok‍taṃ kāraṇadatikrama iti</b> । nanu tenaiva tarhi gatārtha-
midam । na । anyavartitvāt daśasaṅkhyāyāḥ pūrvapakṣiṇo'dhikāśaṅkā ।</p>
<p><b>śamitā ca śabdabhedāt</b> । yathā saṃjñābhedāt camasādhvaryavaḥ ṛtvigbhyo bhidyante
evaṃ <b>śamitāpi śabdabhedādbhidyate</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatiruktā । yuktimāha---<b>saṃjñā-
bhedaścopapanno bhavati</b> । anyathā ekasyaivārthasyānekaśabdatvamanyāyyamāśritaṃ syāt iti ।
rāddhāntamāha---<b>nātra bhedaḥ utpattinibandhano hi bheda uktaḥ । na cāsyotpattirasti</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---na śabdabhedamātrādbheda uktaḥ । api tu utpatticodanābhedāt । utpatticoda-
nāyāṃ hi alaukikī saṃjñā bhavati । anyathā tu alaukikārthāntarābhāvāt prakṛtānāmanya-
tarasminnayaṃ śabdo vartata iti niścīyate । yadyasyotpattirnāsti <b>kathaṃ tarhi saṃjñānyatvaṃ</b>
<note>(1) P. 1092</note>
﻿<pb n="r923"/>
nārthāntaraṃ vinā saṃjñānyatvamupapadyata iti autsargiko nyāyaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>naiveyaṃ saṃjñā, kiṃ
tarhi ? yaugikābhidhānameva</b> śamayatīti śamitā । tena yaḥ śamayati paśuṃ sa prakṛtā-
nāmanyatamo bhaviṣyati । <b>evaṃ cādhvaryavamiti samākhyā upapannā bhaviṣyati</b> । śāmitra-
mapyādhvaryavamiti samākhyāyate । yadi cādhvaryureva śamitā evamupapadyate samākhyeti ।</p>
<p><b>upagāśca liṅgadarśanāt । kena viśeṣeṇāyamadhikaraṇātideśaḥ</b> ? yāvatā upagā-
śabdo'pi yaugikaḥ । na2 cāsyotpattirasti । <b>ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ upagā iti gānakāriṇāṃ
saṃbandhāt camasādhvaryava iva hotrakāṇāmiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
---gātṝṇāmupagāḥ saṃbandhino bhavanti । na ca ṛtvigantarasaṃbandhitā ṛtvijaḥ । tena
yathā camasādhvaryavo hotrakāṇāṃ saṃbandhino'nye ca ṛtvigbhyaḥ tathā upagā iti pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate । <b>utpatteraśravaṇādityatidiṣṭo rāddhāntaḥ</b> । utpatteraśravaṇādarthāntarābhāvāt
teṣvevābamupagāśabdo yaugikaḥ । yaśca gātṛsaṃbandhaḥ sa gānopacayakāritvanibandhano na svāmi-
karmakaratvanibandhanaḥ । <b>liṅgamuktam</b> ।</p>
