﻿<pb n="r924"/>
<p><b>vikrayī tvanyaḥ। somavikrayī punaḥ</b> kimṛtvigeva utānya iti <b>teṣāmṛtvijā-
mevānyatama iti</b> pūrvapakṣavādī <b>manyate</b> । codyamāha---<b>nanu cācodito vikrayaḥ codi-
tasya ca ṛtvijaḥ kartṛtvenopādīyante</b> । asyārthaḥ---<b>yaccoditaṃ tatkratoraṅgam । yaccāṅgaṃ
tadyajamānena kartavyam</b> । tadeva kartuṃ puruṣā upādīyanta iti kathaṃ <b>vikrayaḥ</b> ārtvijaḥ ।
pariharati---<b>krayopādānaśeṣaṃ</b> vikrayaṃ <b>manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । krayastāvaccoditaḥ
na cāsau vikrayaṃ vinā sidhyati । na kaścitsomavikraye svataḥ pravṛttaḥ somavikrayasya pratiṣiddha-
tvāt । kratvarthatve tu vikrayasya nāsti pratiṣedhaḥ iti krayopādānaśeṣatayā vikrayo'pyaṅgam ।
ataḥ ṛtvijaiva kartavyaṃ itarāṅgavaditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu lobhādeva</b> vikretu-
<b>rākṣepasiddheḥ dravyārjanavanna śeṣaṃ manyate</b> । yadyapyasti pratiṣedhaḥ tathāpi kecillobhāt ati-
krāntaniṣedhāḥ svata eva somavikraye'pi pravṛttāḥ । tānāśritya prayogavidhiḥ na somavikraya-
mākṣipati yathā dravyārjanam । api ca śūdrādīnāṃ sarvavikrayābhyanujñānāt niṣedhātikramo'pi
nāsti <b>ityanārtvijameva । ato'nyaḥ</b> somavikrayīti siddham ।</p>
<p><b>karmakāryāt sarveṣām । nanu cātra rāddhānto na ghaṭate । kathaṃ na ghaṭate</b> ? ākṣeptā
<note>(1) P. 1094</note>
﻿<pb n="r925"/>
āha---<b>utpattāvapi parisaṅkhyaiva prāpnoti</b> yadyutpattireva ṛtvika‍śabdasya pravṛttau nimitte
tathāpi <b>parisaṅkhyaiva prāpnoti</b> saptadaśartvija iti । kutaḥ ? <b>camasādhvaryūṇāmapyutpatti-
śravaṇāt</b> । utpattinimittatve teṣāmapi ṛtvika‍śabdapravṛttau saptadaśeti saṅkhyānupapattau
parisaṅkhyaivāśrayaṇīyā । <b>atha parisaṅkhyaiveṣṭā</b>'bhidhānasya <b>ṛtuyajananimittanirasanamanarthakaṃ
syāt</b> । ṛtuyajananimittatvepi ṛtvigabhidhānasya parisaṅkhyaiveyaṃ bhaviṣyati saptadaśaṛtvija
iti rāddhāntaṃ saṃbandhayati---<b>atrocyate । utpattau</b> nimittabhūtāyāmaṅgīkriyamāṇāyāṃ
<b>naivaṃ parisaṅkhyā prāp‍noti ekaikatrodgātrādiśabdatulyatvāt ṛtvika‍śabdasya nātrāpahnavanīyaṃ
kiñcidasti</b> । asyārthaḥ---tatra parisaṅkhyā bhavati yatrāpahnavanīyaṃ kiñcidasti, utpattau śabda-
nimittāyāṃ aṅgīkriyamāṇāyāṃ yathodgātrādiśabdaḥ ekaikavālaukikārthaḥ tathā'yamapi ṛtvik-
śabdaḥ ṣoḍaśasu codanaikasamadhigamyavācakabhāvaḥ । tena yatraiva vedena prayuktaḥ teṣāmeva
vācaka iti niścīyate nānyeṣāmiti nāsti parisaṅkhyeyam । <b>ṛtuyajananimitte punaḥ</b>
ṛtvika‍śabde'rthāpahnavaḥ । sarveṣāmṛtau yajanāt । bhavatu ko doṣa ityatrāha---<b>na cāsau śakyate</b>
vacanaśatenāpi । 1vacanapravṛtteḥ sati nimitte durvāratvāt । yata evotpattinimittā ata
eva laukikīyaṃ saṃjñā । <b>ata evoparitanamadhikaraṇamupapannaṃ bhavati</b> । vaidikaprayogeṇa
ṛtvika‍śabdārthaniścaye yatraiva prayujyate tatraiva vācaka iti niścīyate । tena ṣoḍaśānāmeva
ṛtvika‍tvaṃ sidhyati । anyathā ṛtuyajananimittatve sarveṣāmṛtvika‍śabdābhidheyatā syāt ।
<b>evaṃ ca vadatā</b> pūrvādhikaraṇasya viśeṣaparyantatāvyavasthāpanamātramidamityuk‍taṃ bhavati ।</p>
<note>(1) G. śabdavṛtteḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r926"/>
<p><b>niyamastu dakṣiṇābhiḥ । ke ta iti saṃśayaḥ । <q>‘ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti’</q> iti
prakramya</b> dakṣiṇāviśeṣavidhipare vākye saṃpradānatvena <b>kīrtayati yān te ta iti rāddhāntaḥ ।
tathā ye yajamānāsta ṛtvija iti ca darśitam</b> । yajamānānāmevārtvijye vidhānāt
ṛtvikkarmakaratayā yajamāneṣveva codakaprāptadīkṣākartṛviśeṣavidhipare vākye yān śabdān
prayuṅk‍te tacchabdavācyā ṛtvija iti siddhamadhvaryvādīnāmevartviktvam ।</p>
<p><b>svāmisaptadaśāḥ । <q>‘saptadaśa ṛtvijaḥ’</q> iti śrūyate । tatra kiṃ yajamānena saha
saptadaśa uta yajamānavyatiriktā anye saptadaśeti</b> saṃśayaḥ evaṃ ca bruvatā gṛhapatiśabdo
yajamānaparo bhāṣye iti vyākhyātam । <b>kiṃ prāptam</b> ? yajamānādanye <b>saptadaśa yasmāt</b>
<b>karma</b>karasaṅkhyaiṣā । na svāmī karmekaraḥ <q>‘karmaṇi bhṛtau’</q> iti bhṛtipūrvaṃ karma kurvāṇe karmakara-
śabdo vyutpāditaḥ na svāmī bhṛtyakarma kurute3 । nanu mā nāma bhṛtyakarma karotu । kurute
tāvadasau tena kimiti tameva gṛhītvā saptadaśeti vyapadeśo na bhavati ityatrāha---<b>ekadharma-
yuktānāṃ cāvāntarasaṅkyopapadyate । ityanya eveti yuktam</b> । yadi hyekadharmayogo nāśrīyate
<note>(1) P. 1094</note> <note>(2) P. 1099</note> <note>(3) R. bhṛtyāḥ karma kurvate ।</note>
﻿<pb n="r927"/>
tadā sarveṣāṃ padārthānāṃ ekasaṅkhyaiva syāt avāntarasaṅkhyayā vyavahāro na syāt । asti
cāsau । tatra hi ekadharmayoga eva nimittam nartvijāṃ yajamānasya ca ekadharmayoga iti na
tadabhiprāyeṇa saṅkhyopapadyata ityanya eva saptadaśo yajamānāditi । <b>atrocyate । svāmi-
saptadaśāḥ saptadaśaḥ svāmī yeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ । nanu ca karmakarasāmānyaprayuktaiṣā avāntara-
saṃṅkhyā</b> । pariharati---<b>kena vok‍taṃ na</b> karmakarasāmānyaprayuk‍teti । <b>kathaṃ tarhi svāmi-
saptadaśāḥ saptadaśaḥ</b> । uttaram---<b>na svāmi/?/yā yajamānaḥ saptadaśaḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? kartṛ-
tayaiva</b> । etadeva spaṣṭayati---<b>yajamānāpekṣaiṣā saṅkhyā nādhikāritayā । nanu ca <q>‘sadasyaṃ
vṛṇīta’</q> iti varaṇotpattimaṅgīkṛtya eṣā saṅkhyā । na ca yajamāna utpadyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yajamānotpādyatālakṣaṇaikadharmayogādeṣā saṅkhyā bhavati । asti ca yajamānenotpādyo'nyo'pi
saptadaśaḥ sadasyo nāma । tathā hi tasya varaṇaṃ samāmananti <q>“sadasyaṃ vṛṇīte”</q> iti ।
atrāpi ca ṛtvika‍śabdo lākṣaṇika eva । satyapi sadasye puruṣāntare tatra ṛtvika‍śabdā-
prayogāt । ata eva bhāṣyakārīyaṃ sandehaṃ parityajya nibandhanakāreṇānyathā sandeho
darśitaḥ । bhāṣye ca sadasyagrahaṇamupalakṣaṇam । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---yajamānādanyaṃ yaṃ kañcidabhi-
pretya iyaṃ saṅkhyā uta yajamānamabhipretyeti । codyaṃ pariharati---<b>ucyate । ṣoḍaśānāmeva
varaṇenotpattiḥ । nanu ca sadasyaṃ vṛṇīte’ iti sadasyaḥ saptadaśo bhaviṣyati yadi brahmaṇye-
cāyaṃ sadasyaśabdo vartate</b> । asyārthaḥ---dakṣiṇayā puruṣāṇāmupādānamiti vakṣyāmaḥ । varaṇaṃ
﻿<pb n="r928"/>
tadanugrāhakam । tena yadyapi sadasyasya varaṇaṃ śrūyate tathāpi dakṣiṇāśravaṇāt na sadasyo
nāmānyaḥ kaścit saṃbhavati । dakṣiṇā ca brahmaṇaḥ śrūyate । varaṇaṃ ca tasya brahmaśabdena
noktam । hotrādīnāṃ tu varaṇaṃ hotrādiśabdenaiva । tena brahmaṇa evedaṃ varaṇam । śaknoti
ca tatra yogikayā vṛttyā sadasyaśabdo vartitum । sa hi sadasi bhavaḥ । <b>tasmāt svābhi-
saptadaśāḥ</b> parigṛhyante । <b>atha kasmādekaścamasādhvaryurna parigṛhyate</b> notpādyapuruṣābhi-
prāyā saptadaśasaṅkhyeti । pariharati---<b>na te yajamānena varitavyā ityuktam</b> tenotpattiḥ
teṣāmekarūpā na bhavatītyarthaḥ । tasmāt <b>karmakaraiḥ</b> ṛtvigbhiḥ <b>sāmānyāt</b> samatvāt
yajamānasya nityakarmakaratvāt <b>yajamāna eva</b> saptadaśo na camasādhvaryuḥ aśakti-
viṣayatvāditi ।</p>
<p><b>te sarvārthāḥ prayuk‍tatvāt । idamidānīṃ sandihyate---kiṃ sarvārthā ṛtvijaḥ
yāvatyuruṣakāryaṃ yajamānasya tāvataiḥ kriyate,uta yāvadvacanamiti</b> । kratuprakaraṇaṃ eva
yāvatpuruṣakāryaṃ tāvattaiḥ sarvaiḥ kartavyaṃ aniyamena, uta yadeva yasya vacanena samākhyayā vā
prāptaṃ tadeveti । <b>agnayaśca svakālatvāditi kibhidaṃ</b> ? ekagranthenāha---<b>nanu cādhānasya
sarvārthatāṃ vadatā agnīnāṃ sarvārthatvamuktam । kimidaṃ punassarvārthatocyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
<note>(1) P. 1102</note>
﻿<pb n="r929"/>
yadi sādhyatayā sarvārthatā'gnīnāmucyate, tadayuktam, sādhitatvāt । atha nirākāryatayocyate,
tanna, sthitasya nyāyasyoddhārābhāvāt । vadati ca svakālatvādagnayaḥ sarvārthā iti । <q>‘samadhigata-
metadi’</q>ti sthitamevārthaṃ darśayati । tasmādayuktamityākṣepaḥ । samādhatte---<b>saiveyaṃ sarvārthatā atra puna-
ssādhyate svakālatvāditi</b> । asyārthaḥ---etaduk‍taṃ bhavati bhinnena sūtreṇādhikaraṇāntarametat
sarvārthatāmākṣipya samarthayitumiti । tatrāyamākṣepaḥ pūrvamuktaḥ āhitāgneradhikāraśravaṇāt
āhitānāṃ kratvarthatā । tena(na) viniyuktānāmagnīnāṃ utpattiḥ ityādhānaṃ sarvārthamuktam ।
tatredamucyate---nanvetadevāyuk‍taṃ āhitāgneradhikāra iti yathā'dhikṛtaḥ puroḍāśādikamutpādayati
tathaivāgnīn ityetadeva yuktamiti । tatredaṃ samādhānam svakālatvādādhānasyāntataḥ kartumaśak‍teḥ
āhitāgneradhikāra iti । atra codayati---<b>nanu ca svakālatvāt yāvadagnikāryaṃ tatsarvaṃ
agnibhirityucyate yathā yāvatpuruṣakāryaṃ tatsarvamṛtvigbhiriti</b> । asyārthaḥ---eka-
sūtropāttatvādagnīnāṃ ṛtvijāṃ ca īdṛśī sarvārthatocyate । ṛtvijāṃ ca yāvatpuruṣakāri-
tayā sarvārthatvamucyate । tenāgnīnāmapi svakālatvāt sakalāgnikāryakāritaivocyata iti ।
ekadeśī pṛcchati---<b>tataḥ kiṃ</b> ? ākṣeptā āha---<b>tadetannopapadyate 1samadhigatametat
ag‍nayaśca svakālatvāditi</b> । kutaḥ ? <b>na hi svakālatvādyāvadagnikāryaṃ tadarthatā
sidhyati</b> tatra svakālatvasyāhetutvāt । <b>kiṃ tarhi</b> ? <b>svakālatvena sarvakarmārthatā
sidhyatītyukto</b> nyāyaḥ । <b>na hi pratikarma utpattirbhavatītyarthaḥ</b> । svakālenādhānenāgnayo
lohasuvarṇavat ārjyante, na punaḥ pratikarmeti darśitam । samādhatte---yadi svakālatvena
<note>(1)G. samarthita</note>
﻿<pb n="r930"/>
sarvakarmārthatā sidhyati---<b>evaṃ tarhi tvayaivok‍taṃ</b> asmadabhipretam । kutaḥ---<b>yasmāt
yasyaiva hetuḥ sa eva pratijñātārthaḥ</b> । tena sarvakarmārthatā pratijñāyate tadanurūpatvāt
hetoḥ । <b>tasmāt sūtradvayametat</b> । yataḥ sūtradvayam ata eva <b>ādhastyasūtrasya
parihāro'mamucyate idaṃ tu</b> idānīṃ sarvārthatvaṃ <b>sthitameva</b> । idānīṃ parihāramāha---<b>na hyatra
vacanāni nityānuvādatayā kalpyante</b> । yadi hi vacanāni nityānuvādatayā kalpyeran
tadā sarvapuruṣakāryārthatā ṛtvijāṃ syāt । na tvedasti pakṣe puruṣāntarāṇāmapi tatra
prāptatvāt । <b>tasmāt yāvadvacanameva kāryamṛtvijāmiti</b> ।</p>
<p><b>tasyopadeśasamākhyānena nirdeśaḥ । idamidānīṃ cintyate---yadyena samākhyāyate
tat tenaiva puruṣeṇa kartavyam uta kiñcidanyenāpi iti</b> bhāṣyoktaḥ sandeho darśitaḥ ।
<b>eṣa tāvadutsargaḥ yadyena samākhyāyate tattena kartavyamiti । ucyate---tatra vacanāt</b>
<note>(1) P. 1106</note>
﻿<pb n="r931"/>
<b>viśeṣasamākhyānāccāpavādaḥ</b> । <b>kathaṃ tarhi sāmānyasamākhyā</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>brāhmaṇagrāma-
vadityadoṣaḥ</b> । anyathāpyupapannatvāt sāmānyasamākhyā durbalā । anyathā'nupapadyamānatayā ca
viśeṣasamākhyā balīyasī । vacanāt‍tu śīghraviniyogāvagamāt vacanaṃ balīya iti nirṇayaḥ ।
darśanamuktam ।</p>
<p><b>praiṣānuvacanaṃ metrāvaruṇasya</b> । <b><q>‘maitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyati cānucāhe’</q>ti kiṃ praiṣamātra</b>
anuvacanasaṃyuktamasaṃyuk‍taṃ ca sarvaṃ tathā anuvacanamātraṃ tu yatpraiṣeṇa saṃyuktamasaṃyuktaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ
maitrāvaruṇena kartavyaṃ uta saṃyuktameveti sandihya rāddhāntamāha---<b>saṃyuktasya vidyamānatvāt nā-
saṃyuk‍taṃ parigṛhyata iti</b> । pūrvapakṣo'tra spaṣṭatvānnoktaḥ pratyuddeśaṃ vākyasamāpteḥ praiṣamātre
maitrāvaruṇasya viniyogaḥ tathā'nuvacanamātra iti । rāddhāntagranthasya tvayamarthaḥ sahacaritā-
sahacaritayoḥ sahacarite pratyaya iti sarvajanaviditametat । asti ca praiṣavacanasahitamanu-
vacanam, anuvacanasahitaśca praiṣaḥ iti tena preṣyatītyayaṃ śabdo'nuvacanasahita eva praiṣe
vartate । tathā cānucāheti śabdaḥ praiṣasahacaritamevānuvacanamāha । asti ca tat tathāvidhaṃ
dvayamapīti । <b>caśabdaścaivaṃ samarthito bhavati samuccitāvasthādyotakaḥ</b> samuccitayoreva maitrā-
varuṇaviniyogadarśanāt । <b>darśanamuktam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1106</note>
﻿<pb n="r932"/>
<p><b>camasāṃścamasādhvaryavaḥ</b> । <b>kiṃ camasaiścamasādhvaryavo juhvati utādhvaryureveti saṃśaye
samākhyā anyathā nopapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । yadi camasādhvaryavaḥ camasaina juhvati kathaṃ te
camasādhvaryava iti samākhyāṃ labheran । camase adhvaryavo bhavantīti camasādhvaryavaḥ ।
adhvaryoścānyatra homakāritā'vagatā । tatsamānatā teṣāṃ puruṣāṇāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>rāddhāntastu
adhvaryuśabdasyotpattinimittatvāt</b> anekārthābhidhānaṃ na nyāyyamiti <b>adhvaryuriva camaseṣu
bhavantīti camasādhvaryavaḥ tasmādadhvaryurjuhotīti</b> । asyārthaḥ---adhvaryuśabdastāvat
anekārtho na bhavati । kintu viśiṣṭasya ṛtvijo vācakaḥ puruṣāntare gauṇaḥ । tatra yadi
camase adhvaryoḥ homo na syāt kathaṃ tarhi camase adhvaryuvadbhāvaḥ ? tasmādavaśyāṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ
camaseṃ adhvaryorhomaḥ । tena sa eva juhoti । <b>kathaṃ tarhi adhvaryuvadbhāvaḥ</b> ? vinā
karmaṇā tatsādṛśyamanupapannamiti । <b>uttaraṃ---anyatra vyāpṛte tasmin</b> mukhye adhvaryorgauṇasya
<b>tatkāryakaraṇadarśanāt</b> । <b>darśanamuktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>vedopadeśāt</b> । <b>śyenavājapeyāvudāharaṇam</b> । <b>kiṃ śyena udgātrā samākhyātaḥ</b>
udgātrā sāṅgaḥ <b>kartavyaḥ samākhyānāt, adhvaryuṇā ca vājapeyaḥ uta ṣoḍaśabhirapīti saṃśaye</b>
<note>(1) P. 1108</note> <note>(2) P. 1109</note>
﻿<pb n="r933"/>
<b>viśeṣasamākhyānāt udgātrā adhvaryuṇā ceti prāpte upakāradarśanāt ṣoḍaśabhirapīti
vadāmaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---prakṛtau padārthā yena kṛtāḥ vikṛtāvapi tenaiva kartavyā ? teṣāṃ padārthānāṃ
tatra prāpteḥ । nanu ca vaikṛtī viśeṣasamākhyā kartrantaraṃ kalpayatītyatrāha---<b>klṛptakalpyayoḥ
klṛpto balīyān ityukto hetuḥ</b> । tata etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---prakṛtau klṛptaḥ puruṣāntara-
saṃbandhaḥ vikṛtau kalpyaḥ । na ca klṛpte pratipakṣe kalpanā ātmānaṃ labhate iti tatra
tatroktam ।</p>
<trailer>iti ṛjuvimalāpañcikāyāṃ tṛtīyasya
saptamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>

<section>
<head>atha ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</head>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya aṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>svāmikarma parikrayaḥ</b> । <b>samākhyayā ādhvaryavamiti prāpte adhikāraśrutiviro-
dhāt yājamānamiti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---ādhvaryavamiti samākhyāte kāṇḍe pari-
krayatya paṭhitatvāt adhvaryukartṛkameva prāptam । na cedamāśaṅkanīyam kimiti parakīyakarmakaraṇāya
paraḥ puruṣāntarāṇi parikrīṇīte iti, yataḥ samadhikadhana2lobhādayamartho loke dṛśyata iti । evaṃ
prāpte brūmaḥ---adhikāraśruteryajamānasya sarvatra kartṛtāmāpādayantyāḥ pradhānabhūtāyā virodhāt
samākhyābādhena yājamāna eva parikrayaḥ । adhvaryuparikrītapuruṣāntarakṛtāḥ padārthāḥ na
yajamānena kṛtāḥ nāpi kāritāḥ । nanu laukikīmadhvaryuprayuktimāśritya yajamānakāritā
bhaviṣyati । netyucyate । yāvadeva śrūyate tāvadevāśritya śāstrārthavarṇanā yuktā । na ca parikrayā-
ntaramadhvaryoḥ śrūyate । yāvatī cādhvaryoḥ dakṣiṇā''mnāyate na tāvatyā yajamānasya puruṣāntarapari-
krayārthaṃ adhvaryuṃ prati prayojakatā saṃbhavati । tasmādādhvaryavatve parikrayasya adhikāraśrutivirodhaḥ ।
<b>vacanādṛtvijāmapi parikrayaḥ syāt</b> । tatra ca parikrayāntarakalpanā'nupapanneti ।</p>
<p><b>saṃskārāstu puruṣasāmarthye</b> । <b>vapanādīnāṃ samākhyayā nādhikāro virudhyata iti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । anena pūrvādhikaraṇādviśeṣamāha । yathā pūrvatrārtvijatve adhikāraśrutivirodhaḥ
<note>(1) P. 1112</note> <note>(2) R. lā</note>
﻿<pb n="r935"/>
tathā'tra nāsti kītaiḥ ṛtvigbhiḥ kriyamāṇā vapanādayo yajamānenaiva kṛtāḥ yataḥ । tena vapanādayaḥ
samākhyayā''dhvaryavāḥ । evaṃ ca sthite'sminnadhikaraṇe yajamānasaṃskāratve phalasaṃyogādityatra
(3-7-2) adhikṛtāvasthāsaṃskāratvamuktam । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu puruṣasaṃskāraṃ manvāno na
saṃskartuṃ puruṣāḥ parikrīyante kiṃ tarhi kārayitum</b> । <b>ataḥ sāmarthyāt samākhyābādhaṃ
manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyayaṃ puruṣasaṃskāro na bhavet tadā bhavedeva nirvāpādivat ādhvaryavaḥ ।
(iti puruṣasaṃskāraḥ) puruṣasaṃskārāścaite lokavat । tatra cādhvaryusaṃskāratve adhikāraśrutervirodhaḥ
yajamānasya teṣu kartṛtvānupapatteḥ । parikrayadvāreṇa hi teṣu yajamānasya kartṛtā । na ca
saṃskārārthaḥ parikrayaḥ । kāryāntaraśeṣabhūtasya hi dravyasyopādānaṃ na punaḥ śeṣibhūtasya ।
parikrayaśca puruṣopādān । tenāsau karma kartu na saṃskartumiti parikrayasya tādarthyābhāvāt
na parikrayadūreṇa yajamānasya ṛtvika‍saṃskāratvena vapanādiṣu kartṛtvopapattiriti adhikāraśruti-
virodhāt samākhyābādhaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>yatra punaḥ śrutyaiva ṛtvika‍saṃskāraścodyate na tatrādhikāraśrutisāmarthyāt
ṛtvijo nivṛttiḥ yathā upavāsaṃ vakṣyati</b> kathaṃ punaḥ teṣu yajamānasya kartṛtvaṃ ? ucyate
saṃskārasaṃskṛtaṛtvika‍kartṛkapadārthatvena parikrayaḥ saṃskārārthaḥ tatra kathyate । iha sandigdhaṃ
ṛtvika‍saṃskāratvamiti viśeṣaḥ । <b>athobhayānugrahāya</b> samākhyādhikāraśrutisāmarthyānu-
grahāya <b>samānavidhānaṃ1</b> ṛtvigyajamānasādhāraṇaḥ <b>kasmānna bhavatīti cet</b> ? uttaraṃ
---<b>ṛtvikṣu kriyamāṇo yajamānena kṛtaḥ kārito vā</b> yasmānna bhavati tasmānna sādhāraṇaḥ
<note>(1) G. omits vidhānaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r936"/>
<b>kimiti na kṛto na kārito vā</b> ? । uttaraṃ---<b>sādhāraṇyādeva</b> ṛtvigyajamāna-
sādhāraṇyādeva । <b>nanu ceḍākhyabhakṣaṇavat svayaṃ ca karoti kārayati ca</b> । yatheḍābhakṣaṇaṃ
svayaṃ yajamānaḥ karoti ṛtvijaśca kārayati tathā vapanādīnvapi । paraharati---na, tatra
<b>kartṛtvenāviśeṣāt</b> । <b>iha tu prādhānyāviśeṣādanupapattiḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---bhakṣaṇaṃ dravya-
saṃskāratvāt tatra yajamānasya ṛtvijāṃ ca kartṛtvena saṃbandhaḥ । tena parikrayasya tadarthatvāt
kāritatvamupapannam । iha tu prādhānye aviśeṣa āśaṅkyata iti kāritatvānupapattiḥ ।
<b>tasmādyājamāna iti siddham</b> । iḍābhakṣaṇe parihārāntamāha---<b>vacanādvā yajamānapañcamā</b>
iḍāṃ bhakṣayantīti vacanādvā sādhāraṇassaṃskāro bhaviṣyati । iti ।</p>
<p><b>tapaśca phalasiddhitvāllokavat</b> । <b>kimatrātidiśyate</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>rāddhāntaḥ</b>
atidiśyate । <b>kā punaratra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā</b> ? <b>iyamasti kleśarūpatvāt tapasaḥ</b> । kleśa-
rūpaṃ tapa iti lokasiddham । tathāpi kiṃ ? <b>parikrayaśca kleśāpanuttaye dṛṣṭārtho bhaviṣyati</b>
kleśāpanuttyarthatve hi parikrayo dṛṣṭārthoṃbhavati । tena parikrayasya tapo'rthatvāt bhavati
<note>(1) P. 1115</note> <note>(2) sāmānyabhidhānādeva---mū</note>
﻿<pb n="r937"/>
parikrayadvāreṇa yajamānasya kartṛtvamiti nādhikāraśrutervirodha iti । rāddhāntamāha---<b>na saṃskāra-
sāmānyāditi rāddhāntaḥ</b> । yadyapi kleśarūpaṃ tapaḥ tathāpi puruṣasaṃskāra evāyam । na ca
saṃskartuṃ parikrayaḥ iti saṃskāraiḥ vapanādibhiḥ samānatvāt tadapi yājamānameva । <b>upavāsaśca
vacanādityapyuktam</b> । <q>‘ṛtvija upavasati’</q> iti sākṣācchravaṇāditi ।</p>
<p><b>guṇatvācca vedena</b> । <b>hiraṇyamālyādiṣu tu guṇatvādeva padārthasya na samākhyayā
kartṛtvaṃ niyamyata iti sarvartvijāṃ pratipradhānāvṛttyā guṇo bhavitumarhati</b> । vājapeye hyeta-
taduktam । ye sākṣādupadiṣṭāḥ padārthāḥ te adhvaryuṇaiva kartavyā iti sākṣādupadiṣṭāśca
hiraṇyasragādayaḥ tena te adhvaryuṇaiva kartavyā iti pūrvapakṣamāśaṅkya rāddhānto'yamucyate guṇa-
bhūteneyaṃ puruṣeṇa karmaṇāṃ samākhyā ādhvaryavamiti na pradhānabhūtena, tena pradhānabhāve niyamaṃ na
karoti । guṇatvena puruṣaṃ prati hiraṇyasragādīnāmupadeśa iti pratipradhānaṃ guṇā āvartanta
iti nyāyāt sarvartvijāmeva hiraṇyasragādayaḥ pradhānabhāvapūrvakaṃ ca kartṛtvamiti na samākhyā
niyantumarhati pradhānabhāvabādhaprasaṅgāditi । <b>yatra punaḥ kartṛtayaiva puruṣasaṃbandhaḥ yathā 2ukthyā-
diṣu tatroktaḥ samākhyāniyamaḥ</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1116</note> <note>(2) G. upagavādiṣu</note>
﻿<pb n="r938"/>
<p><b>tathā kāmo'rthasaṃyogāt</b> । <b>kāmasaṃyoga idānīṃ śrūyamāṇaḥ kimārtvijo bhavatu
guṇaphalasaṃbaddheṣu uta yājamāna iti sandehaḥ</b> । <b>kiṃ yuktam</b> ? <b>ārtvijaḥ । kutaḥ</b> ? <b>ṛtvika‍-
padārthāśritatvāt guṇaphalasaṃbandhasya kāmasaṃyogo'pyṛtvijāmeva</b> । asyārthaḥ---sado-
mānaṃ tāvadārtvijameva । tasya tatra kartṛtvāt । tatra <q>‘yadi kāmayeta varṣukaḥ parjanya iti
nīcaiḥ sado minuyāt’</q> ityuk‍te ya eva mātā tasyaiva kāma iti pratīyate । ato guṇa-
kāmeṣviṛtvijāmevādhikāra iti । <b>atrocyate---yajamāna evādhikriyate sāṅge karmaṇyadhi-
kṛtatvāt</b> । yāvatkiñcitprādhānyamatra tattāvadutsargataḥ pradhānatvena sāṅge karmaṇi adhikṛtasya
yajamānasyaiva । tena guṇaphalamapi yajamānasya । <b>nanu cāsāvārtvijapadārthaḥ</b> । āśraya-
bhūto mānādiḥ na tasya yajamānena saṃbandhaḥ । kathaṃ tadāśrito yajamānavasyetyarthaḥ । pariharati
---<b>netibrūmaḥ</b> । <b>tatkartṛko hi saḥ na punaḥ tasya saḥ</b> । tasya ṛtvijaḥ sa nopakārakaḥ
kiṃ tu yajamānasyaiva । tena tatra guṇabhāvena saṃbaddhasya ṛtvijaḥ na prādhānyam । kiṃtu
pradhānabhāvena saṃbaddhasya yajamānasyaiva prādhānyamiti । tadāha---<b>yasya karma tadāśritamapi
tasyaiveti yajamāna evādhikriyate</b> । <b>evaṃ cātmanepadamupapannaṃ bhavati</b> । jyotiṣṭomena
<note>(1) P. 1117</note>
﻿<pb n="r939"/>
yajeta’ iti । itarathā yajamānartvika‍phalakaraṇatve yajamānābhiprāyeṇātmanepadamupapannaṃ bhavati
ṛtvigabhiprāyeṇa tadanupapannam, 2yadyapi hyetat guṇaphalaṃ tadapi pradhānādeva । ata evā-
purvarnirvṛtteriti sūktam । <b>yatra tu vacanādārtvijo'dhikāraḥ tatrānyadīyapadārthāśrite'pi
guṇe vyāpṛtasya phalaṃ bhavatīti kalpyate</b> । na hi vacanasyātibhāro'stīti ।</p>
<p><b>mantrāścākarmakaraṇāstadvat</b> । <b>idānīmāśīrmantrā udāharaṇam</b> । <b>kiṃ yājamānāḥ</b>
yajamānena kartavyāḥ । tataśca <q>“āyurdā ag‍nesyāyurbhedehi”</q> iti yajamānena phalamāśāsyate
<b>utārtvijāḥ</b> । ṛtvika‍prayojyāḥ ṛtvijāmeva phalamāśīriti । <b>ārtvijāḥ samākhyayeti
prāpta ucyate</b> । <b>liṅgadyājamānā iti</b> । phalāśāsakatvādeṣām । yajamānaphalaṃ cāśā-
sitavyam । <b>liṅgaṃ hi samākhyāto balīya ityuktam</b> । <b>proṣita3samidādhānadarśanaṃ ca
liṅgam</b> । na proṣitaḥ ṛtvigbhavati । yajamānastu proṣito bhavati iti darśitaṃ bhāṣye ।
<b>nanu ca mama yajamānasyetyevamādi liṅgamupapannam</b> । asyārthaḥ-yajamānaśabda evādhyāhariṣyate
ṛtvik prayok‍tā'stu । tenāyamartho bhavati---madīyasya yajamānasya āyurdehīti । tena
<note>(1) P. 1118</note> <note>(2) G. yadapi</note> <note>(3) G. proṣitasaṃvidhāna</note>
﻿<pb n="r940"/>
liṅgasamākhyayordvayorapyupapattiḥ । pariharati---<b>ayameva doṣaḥ yadutādhyāhāro nāma</b> । <b>tasmādvak‍tu
reva mametyupapannaṃ bhavati</b> yajamānaprayojyapakṣe ।</p>
<p><b>dva‍yām‍nāteṣūbhau</b> । <b>kecinmantrāḥ yājamānakāṇḍe ādhvaryave ca samām‍nāyante</b> ।
<b>tatra saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ dvābhyāṃ kartavyāḥ utādhvaryuṇaiveti</b> । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ dvayām‍nānāt</b> dvayoḥ
kāṇḍayorāmnānāt <b>dvābhyāṃ ca</b> adhvaryuyajamānābhyāṃ <b>samākhyātā ekena vaktavyā</b> iti
pratibhāti pūrvapakṣiṇaḥ । samādhatte---<b>ekakāryatvānmantrāṇā</b>mekārthaprakāśanakāryakāritvāt
<b>ekaprayojyatāṃ</b> ekādhvaryuprayojyatāṃ <b>pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । adhvaryoreva karmakaratvāt
tenaiva smaraṇārthaṃ prayoktavyā mantrā iti । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu ekasyādhvaryoranuṣṭhānasmaraṇāt
anyasya ca yajamānasya pratyavekṣaṇāt ām‍nānadvayasyāpyarthavattvāt dvābhyāmapi prayokta-
vyā iti manyate samākhyādvaye cānugṛhītaṃ bhaviṣyati</b> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r941"/>
<p><b>jñāte ca vacanaṃ na hyavidvān vihito'sti ।</b> <q>“klṛptīryajamānaṃ vācayati”</q> iti
śrūyate । ki vidvāneva vācayitavvaḥ utāvidvānapi” iti saṃśayaḥ bhāṣyokto'nubhāṣitaḥ
ākṣep‍tum । ākṣipati---<b>kathaṃ punaḥ viduṣo'dhikāre aviduṣyāśaṅkā</b> । yadi hi
aviduṣo'dhikāraḥ syāt tadā tasya vācanaṃ syāt । na ca tasyādhikāro'sti । samādhatte
---<b>vācayatītyetasmādeva । na hi viduṣi vācayatīti dṛṣṭārthatā saṃbhavati iti</b> viduṣyādhi-
kāriṇi svayameva bruvati vācayatītyadṛṣṭārthaṃ bhavati । aviduṣi dṛṣṭārtham । tasmādaviduṣo'dhi-
kāraḥ । nanu yadyaviduṣi dṛṣṭārthatā <b>evaṃ tarhi aviduṣa eva vācanaṃ syāt</b> । samādhātā
<b>āha---bhavatu ko doṣaḥ</b> । ākṣeptā āha---<b>viduṣo'dhikārahāniḥ prāpnoti</b> । tatpakṣe
vācanāṅgābhāvāt sakalāṅgopasaṃhārī prayogavidhiḥ yasminneva tathābhūtaḥ saṃbhavati tasyaivādhikāraḥ ।
samādhātā āha---<b>nādhikāraṃ nivārayāmaḥ aviduṣo'pyadhikāro'sti idaṃphalamidapradhi-
karaṇaṃ pūrvapakṣadaśāyām</b> । asyārthaḥ-dvayorapyadhikāraḥ avidvatpakṣe ca dṛṣṭārthatayā vācana---
maṅgam । rāddhāntamāha---<b>nādhikāramaviduṣo'pyākṣep‍tuṃ</b> arthādupasthāpayituṃ samarthamidaṃ
<b>vacanam</b> । kutaḥ? <b>brūvantameva hi vācayatīti śabdo bravīti iti nābruvataḥ pravṛtti-
māha</b> । ya eva prakṛtyarthe pravṛttaḥ tatprayojakatva eva ṇijutpadyate nānyatra । viduṣaśca
<note>(1) P. 1121</note>
﻿<pb n="r942"/>
<b>prakṛtyarthe pravṛttiḥ nāviduṣaḥ ।</b> dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ uk‍tasyoccāraṇenāpi bhavati । tena vidva-
dviṣayatvādasyāpi vācanasya nāviduṣo'dhikāraḥ । <b>ato yathādhikāraṃ vācanamiti siddham</b> ।
yasyaiva viduṣo'dhikāraḥ <b>tasyaiva vācanamiti yāvat</b> ।</p>
<p><b>yājamāne samākhyānāt । iha dvandvānyudāharaṇam । kiṃ yajamānena kartavyāni,
utādhvaryuṇeti saṃśayaḥ</b> । kathaṃ saṃśayaḥ ? <b>ekātrādhvaryave padārthānāmām‍nānāt anyatra</b>
yājamāne <b>samabhyāśīkaraṇāt</b> । padārthānuṣṭhānena ca samabhyāśīkaraṇasaṃpattiḥ । tena yatra
padārthāḥ tena samabhyāśīkaraṇamapi kriyatām, uta yatra samabhyāśīkaraṇaṃ tena padārthā api
kriyantāṃ iti । <b>tatra viśeṣasamākhyāyā yājamānāni ।</b> sāmānyenādhvaryave prāpte viśeṣeṇa
yājamānasamākhyayā adhvaryusamākhyābādhena yājamānāni dvandvāni । nanu bhavatu samabhyāśīkaraṇaṃ
yājamānam । padārthastu kathamityatrāha---<b>padārthapūrvakatvāt samabhyāśasya</b> । anuṣṭheya-
padārthasamabhyāśaḥ padārthānuṣṭhānenaiva saṃpadyata iti padārthā api yājamānā eva । <b>atrocyate
---padārthāstāvadādhvaryavā eva</b> samāmnātāḥ anupajātavirodhittvādadhvaryuṇaiva kartavyāḥ ।
<note>(1) 1122</note>
﻿<pb n="r943"/>
pūrvabhāvino hi padārthāḥ । teṣāṃ tāvadadhvaryukartṛtaiva । <b>akriyamāṇe padārthe na yajamānena
samabhyāśaḥ śakyate kartumiti so'pyādhvaryava eva । viśeṣasamākhyāpravṛttistu darśitā</b> ।
yajamānena idaṃ cedaṃ ca kurvityabhidhānāt keṣuciccānumantraṇaprayogāditi ।</p>
<p><b>vipratiṣedhe karaṇaḥ । ṛtvigantarakāryopadeśe kimātmīyaṃ karma karotu virodhe
utātidiṣṭimiti saṃśaye atidiṣṭaṃ pratyakṣavidhānāditi siddham</b> । spaṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣo
na likhitaḥ । pratyakṣavihitenaikakāryakāriṇā ātideśikasya bādhaḥ । na cātraikaṃ
kāryamastīti nāsti bādhaḥ । yadi paraṃ virodhādanuṣṭhānāśaktiḥ tatraikamanuṣṭhāsyatīti । rāddhāntastu
ekakāryatvābhāvepi tāvadasti virodhaḥ । tatra pratyakṣavihitasyānanyagatitvāt balīyastvaṃ,
itarasya prakṛtāvarthavatteti ।</p>
<p><b>praiṣeṣu parādhikārāt । praiṣapraiṣārthau kimekena kartavyau uta dvābhyāmiti saṃśaye</b>
<note>(1) 1123</note> <note>(2) 1127</note>
﻿<pb n="r944"/>
kathaṃ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ aśakyatvāt ityatrāha---<b>prāptakālabhrāntyā ekeneti</b> pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
agnīdagnīna vihara iti prāptakāle loṭbhaviṣyati । tenānuṣṭhātā evaṃ brūte-agnīt agni-
viharaṇasya prāptaḥ kālaḥ । tena nāstyaśakyateti samākhyānāt dvayamapyādhvaryavameveti pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ । <b>yuṣmadarthāparigrahe kāraṇābhāvāt</b> praiṣa evāyaṃ loḍiti <b>rāddhāntaḥ</b> । madhyama-
puruṣāvivakṣāprasaṅgāt na prāptakāle loṭ । kintu praiṣa eveti aśakyatvāt dvābhyāṃ kartavyau
praiṣapraiṣārthau iti ।</p>
<p><b>adhvaryustu darśanāt । idānīṃ sthite kartṛdvaye2 kimadhvaryuḥ praiṣārthaṃ</b> praiṣarūpamarthaṃ
<b>karotu</b> utānya iti saṃśaye <q>“yadanvañcaṃ spha‍yaṃ dhārayet vajro vai spha‍yaḥ vajreṇaivādhvaryuḥ
kṣiṇvīta”</q> ityarthavādāt anyaḥ praiṣaṃ karotīti । anyatra spha‍yadarśanāt । yasya ca haste
spha‍yaḥ sa preṣakaḥ tena agnīt preṣakaḥ preṣyaścādhvaryuḥ । samākhyāpyarthavādapadānuguṇyena
bādhyate । evaṃ prāpte <b>mantraliṅgādadhvaryuḥ</b> praiṣaṃ karotīti । <q>‘agnīdagnīn vihara’</q> iti
mantre agnīvaḥ praiṣārthāvagateḥ arthavādācca mantrasya balīyastvādanuṣṭhānabodhakatvāt <b>samākhyānārtha-
saṃbhavācca adhvaryureva</b> praiṣakaḥ । <b>arthavādastu guṇavādena</b> gauṇyā vṛttyā <b>parihṛto</b>
bhāṣye ‘adhvaryuśabdenāgnīdeba gauṇyā vṛttyocyata iti ।</p>
<note>(1) 1129</note> <note>(2) G. kartṛbhede</note>
﻿<pb n="r945"/>
<p><b>ṛtvik phalaṃ karaṇeṣvarthavattvāt । kaḥ punarasyāśīrmantrairviśeṣaḥ</b> ? āśīrmantrā
yājamānā eveti nirṇītam । tatheme mantrā yājamānā eva kimiti na saṃbhavantīti viṣaya-
śuddhireva nāsti । ādhvaryavatve hi cinteyamupapadyate ki yajamānaphalaprakāśaḥ utartvik‌phala-
prakāśa iti na yājamānatve । uttaraṃ---<b>samākhyātaḥ sthite adhvaryukartṛtve agnyanvādhānasya
śrutyā mantravidhānam । na ca guṇānurodhena pradhānabādhaḥ śakyate kartum । tasmādādhvaryabo
mantraḥ</b> । agnyanvādhānaṃ tāvat ādhvaryavameva । tadaṅgabhūto mantro'pi tasyaiva । na
punarmantraliṅgālocanayā mantre yajamāne prayoktari siddhe'gnyanvādhānamapi yājamānameva ।
pradhāne'gnyanvādhāne kartṛbādhaprasaṅgāt । tena mantragatakartṛbādhādādhvaryavo mantra iti
<b>sthite kasyāśīriti cintyate । liṅgādadhvaryoḥ । vaktā hi uttamapuruṣeṇa saṃbadhyate
sarvatra</b> hi vaktrabhiprāyeṇa uttamapuruṣo bhavati karomīti । yathā asmacchabdottamapuruṣau
ca samānaviṣayau । tenāsmacchabdo'yaṃ <q>‘mamāgnevarcaḥ’</q> iti । tatra kartṛbhūtādhvaryu-
viṣaya eveti । ākṣipātaṃ---<b>nanu karmasaṃbaddhaphalasaṅkīrtanāt karmārthatā
mantrāṇām</b> । na ca yaśaḥ karmaphalaṃ codanāvagatamiti kathaṃ tatprakāśakatayā karmārthatā ।
uttaraṃ---<b>karmaprayuktayaśaḥ prakāśayataḥ upapannaiva karmārthatā iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । rāddhā-
ntavādītu yaścārthādartho na sa codanārtha iti manbānaḥ karmasaṃbaddhameva phalaṃ prakāśayan mantraḥ</b>
<note>(1) P. 1130</note>
﻿<pb n="r946"/>
<b>karmārtho bhavati iti manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---na yaśaḥ karmaphalatayā codanāto'vagamyate; kintu
arthāt । yaścārthādarthaḥ na sa codanārtha coditaṃ ca phalaṃ mantreṇa prakāśayitavyam ।
nānuṣaṅgikamapi । ato yajamānasaṃbaddhameva phalaṃ varcaḥ śabdena prakāśyate । <b>mama yajamāna-
syeti mantrārthaḥ</b> । asmacchabdena bhaktyā yajamāna evocyata iti ।</p>
<p><b>karmārthaṃ tu phalaṃ teṣāṃ svāminaṃ pratyarthavattvāt । yatra punaḥ dṛṣṭārthameba</b> phalaṃ asantāpa-
lakṣaṇaṃ <b>tat kiṃ ṛtvijāmeva utātrāpi karmaphalameveti</b> । kiṃ ṛtvik‌saṃbandhyasantāpa
āśāsyate <q>‘mā mā santāptaṃ’</q> iti uta yajamānaphalameva karmajanyaṃ saṅkīrtyata iti sandehe
<b>uk‍tena nyāyena karmaphalameveti vadāma iti</b> pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>atrocyate---yaścārthādartho
na sa codanārtha iti anupakārakaṃ phalamaṅgīkṛtya karmānupakārakaphalābhiprāyeṇaitaduktam ।
yatpunaḥ karmaṇa upakaroti</b> yathā'santāpaḥ । asantaptaḥ adhvaryuḥ karma kartuṃ śak‍noti ।
tena yatkarmopakārakaṃ <b>tadupādānaśeṣatayā bhavatyeva karmārthamiti</b> tatprakāśakānāmapi
mantrāṇāṃ na karmārthatā'pahīyate ityārtvija evāsantāpaḥ kīrtyate iti ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1132 </note>
﻿<pb n="r947"/>
<p><b>vyapadeśācca । yatra ca vyapadiśyata</b> evartvijaḥ phalaṃ taddarśitaṃ <q>“tannau saha"</q>
iti । etaccāpavādamātram । tannau saheti dvivacanasyāvivakṣākāraṇābhāvāt ṛtvijo'pi
bhavatyeva phalam ।</p>
<p><b>dravyasaṃskāraḥ prakaraṇāviśeṣāt । vedirvedidharmāścetyuktamuttaravivakṣayeti</b> ।
vedirvedidharmāścāṅgapradhānārthā ityuktameva । tadeva tu uttaracintārthaṃ smaryate ।</p>
<p><b>nirdeśāt‍tu । sthitamaṅgapradhānārthaṃ barhiriti prakṛtau । vikṛtāvidānīṃ cintyate
-kimatrāpi aṅgapradhānārthe barhiṣi dharmā bhavanti</b> yāvantyaṅgāni prākṛtāni aprākṛtāni ca
kiṃ tadarthe barhirdharmā bhavanti । <b>uta prākṛtakāryaprayukta eveti</b> prakṛtau yatkāryāpanne
barhirdharmā dṛṣṭāḥ vikṛtāvapi tatkāryāpanne eveti । tatrāṅgapradhānasaṃbandhitāsāmānyena
<b>prakṛtivadvikṛtāvapīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---prakṛtau aṅgapradhānārthā dharmāḥ
﻿<pb n="r948"/>
vikṛtāvapi tadarthā eva । anyathā prakṛtivadvikṛtirna syāt । prakṛtau ca sarvāṅgapradhānārthā
dharmāḥ vikṛtāvapi sarvāṅgapradhānārthā iti । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu manyate kāryamukhena dharmāṇāṃ
vikṛtau nirūpaṇam । na yathāprakṛtisaṃbandhitayā</b> । asyārthaḥ---vikṛtāvupakāralakṣaṇa-
kāryākāṅkṣāyāṃ prākṛta upakāraḥ prāp‍tyate । sa ca padārthairvinā pratyetubhaśakyaḥ iti padārthai-
ravacchinnaḥ pratīyate । tatkāryamukhena vikṛtau padārthānāṃ nirūpaṇam । na punaryathāprakṛtau
sabanvaḥ tathā vikṛtāvapi saṃbandhayitavyā iti । <b>sambandhasāmānyena hi sarvetropadeśaḥ
syāt</b> । kāryamukhena hi padārthaprāptiratideśaḥ svatantrapadārthaprāptirupadeśa iti viśeṣaḥ ।
yadi vikṛtāvapi kāryanirapekṣa eva padārthasaṃbandhaḥ tadā upadeśa eva syāt । <b>tataścohadarśanaṃ
nopapadyate</b> । upadeśe hi yathopadeśamevāvikāreṇānuṣṭhānaṃ syāt । <b>tasmāt siddhaṃ</b>
kāryāntarāpanne aprākṛte <b>yūpāṅgabarhiṣi barhirdharmā na kartavyāḥ</b> aprākṛtatvāt । <b>añjanā-
jye ca nājyadharmāḥ</b> iti ।</p>
<p><b>virodhe ca śrutiviśeṣāt । anekatra śeṣabhāvo na nyāyya iti paribhojanīyādanyat
kartavyam</b> । atra spaṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣo na likhitaḥ । tathā hi---apracchinnāgrau darmau
<note>(1) P. 1134</note>
﻿<pb n="r949"/>
prādeśamātrau pavitre karoti iti svarūpamātreṇa viniyogāt viniyuktavirodho nāstīti
prakṛtayoreva staraṇāntargatayoḥ darmayorupādānamiti । rāddhāntagranthārthastu-anyatra śeṣabhūtasya
vyāpṛtasyaiva sato'nyatra kārakatvābhāvāt paribhojanīyādbarhiṣo darbhāvupādāya pavitre
kartavyau ।</p>
<p><b>apanayastvekadeśasya। pūrvādhikaraṇanyāyenānekatra</b> yāge aindravāyavapātranidhāne
<b>ca śeṣabhāvo na nyāyya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । dva‍yavadānopasaṃhārāt pratipatteśca rāddhāntaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---na tāvadanekatra kārakabhāvavirodhaḥ dva‍yavadānamātreṇa yāgopasaṃhārāt pariśiṣṭasyā-
nyatrāvyāpṛtatvāt vyāpārāntaropapatteḥ na ca viniyuktaviniyogavirodhaḥ pratipattitvāditi ।</p>
<p><b>vikṛtau sarvārthaḥ śeṣaḥ । idānīṃ vikṛtāvupāṃśutvādayo dharmāścintyante---kimatrāpi
prakṛtivat aṅgapradhānārthatā dharmāṇāṃ neti saṃśayaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ-yajñātharvaṇādiṣu vikṛtiṣu
kevala pradhānopadeśavatīṣu cintyate-kimupāṃśutvādayo dharmāḥ aupadeśikāḥ tatrāpyaṅgapradhānārthā
iti uta kevalapradhānārthā iti । <b>prakṛtivadaṅgapradhānārthatā dharmāṇāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
upāṃśutvaṃ kartṛdvāreṇāṅgam । upāṃśubhāvena hi akhinnaḥ kartā karma kartuṃ śak‍noti । aṅga-
<note>(1) P. 1135</note> <note>(2) 1135</note>
﻿<pb n="r950"/>
pradhānārthaśca kartā । tena yathā sākṣādupadiṣṭāyāṃ prakṛtau aṅgapradhānārthatā evaṃvidhasya
2karmaṇaḥ tathā vikṛtāvapīti <b>naupadeśikātideśikaiḥ upadeśaḥ saṃbadhyata iti rāddhāntaḥ</b> ।
atulyatvādaupadaśikena pradhānena ātideśikaiścāṅgaiḥ upāṃśutvopadeśo na saṃbadhyata ityarthaḥ ।
<b>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ na saṃbadhyata iti । uttaraṃ---upadeśāpekṣatvādatideśasya</b> pradhānopadeśama-
pekṣya aṅgārthamatideśaḥ utpadyate । tena pūrvopanipātipradhāna evopāṃśutvasya saṃbandhaḥ na
pāścātyeṣu ātideśikeṣvaṅgeṣu । <b>sāpekṣanirapekṣayoḥ nirapekṣaṃ balīya iti nyāyavido
manyante</b> ।</p>
<p><b>sannidhānaviśeṣāt । śyene tu aupadeśikasaṃbandhābhāvāt ātideśikaireva
saṃbandha iti viśeṣaḥ</b> । atra pūrvādhikaraṇaviśeṣeṇa pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । tena pradhāne śyena eva
<q>‘dṛtinavanītamājyaṃ bhavati’</q> iti navanītaṃ vidhīyate । ājyagrahaṇaṃ tu anuvādamātraṃ, navanīta-
syājyatvāt । rāddhāntastu-ājyaśabdasya kāryānvayitve saṃbhavati nānuvādamātreṇānvayo nyāyyaḥ
ityājyoddeśena navanītavidhirbhavati । na ca pradhāne śyene ājyamasti ityātideśikāṅgaviṣaya
evāyamupadeśaḥ ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1136</note> <note>(2) G. dharmasya</note>
﻿<pb n="r951"/>
<p><b>tatkāle vā । liṅgadarśanabhrāntyā sutyākālānāmevātra vidhānamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---sādyaskre <q>‘saha paśūnālabhata’</q> iti sahatvaṃ śrutam । tat sutyākāla eveti
tato'vagacchāmaḥ । yatsāmānyavihitaṃ tat sutyākāla eva bhavatīti । anayā bhrāntyā
sutyākālānāmevāṅgānāṃ dṛtinavanītavidhiriti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । pradhānāsattistu mūlayuktiḥ pūrva-
pakṣe । <b>aviśeṣāt sarveṣāmiti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । pratyāsannānāmapratyāsannānāṃ ca pradhāna-
saṃbandhāviśeṣāt navanītavidhiriti rāddhāntaḥ nyāyālliṅgopapattiruk‍tā । sutyākāla eva yaḥ
paśūnāṃ sahālambhaḥ so'gnīṣomīyānubandhyayoravaiṣamyāditi bhāṣye uktam ।</p>
<p><b>māṃsantu savanīyānām । <q>‘tarasāḥ savanīyāḥ puroḍāśā bhavanti’</q> iti śrūyate ।
tatra savanīyapuroḍāśayorvivakṣāyāṃ vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt kasyāyathārthatvaṃ</b> yuktamiti
<b>carcāyāṃ dṛṣṭavyabhicārāt puroḍāśasyāyathārthatvamiti rāddhāntitam</b> । asyārthaḥ---tarasāḥ
savanīyāḥ puroḍāśā ityatra savanīyoddeśena vā tarasā vidhīyante, puroḍāśoddeśena vā । tatroddiśya-
mānānāṃ savanīyānāṃ na puroḍāśo viśeṣaṇatvena vivakṣituṃ nyāyyaḥ vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt । nāpi
<note>(1) P. 1121</note>
﻿<pb n="r952"/>
puroḍāśasyoddiśyamānasya savanīyo viśeṣaṇam, vākyabhedaprasaṅgādeva । ataḥ ekasya nityānu-
vādatvena varṇanam । na ca sarve savanīyāḥ puroḍāśā eveti puroḍāśāpuroḍāśeṣu daṇḍinyāyena
lakṣaṇayā puroḍāśaśabdo varṇanīyaḥ । tathā puroḍāśasya sarvasva sabanīyatvābhāvāt savanīyā-
savanīyeṣu savanīyaśabdaḥ । tatra kasya lakṣaṇayā varṇanaṃ kriyatāmiti cintāyāṃ savanīyaśabdasya
prathamopanipātino yathārthatvaṃ yuktam । puroḍāśabdasya jaghanyatvāt dṛṣṭavyabhicārācca । dṛṣṭo
hi prakṛtau puroḍāśāpuroḍāśeṣu puroḍāśaśabdaḥ tadvadihāpi, prakṛtivadatidiṣṭatvāditi puroḍāśa-
śabda eva lakṣaṇayā varṇanīya iti nyāyyam । atra bhāṣye <q>“tarasāḥ puroḍāśāḥ savanīyā
bhavanti”</q> ityudāhṛtam । tatra puroḍāśaśabdasyaiva prāgbhāvitvāt yathārthatvaṃ nyāyyamiti
rāddhānto na śakyate vak‍tumiti matvā <b>nibandhanakāreṇa</b> <q>‘tarasāḥ savanīyāḥ puroḍāśā
bhavanti iti’</q> iti viparyasyodāhṛtamiti ।</p>
<trailer>iti mahāmahopādhyāyaśālikanāthamiśrakṛtāyāṃ
ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
aṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="r953"/></section>
<section>
<head>atha ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>athātaḥ</b> । atrādhikaraṇe upādānalakṣaṇo vidhivyāpāraḥ pramāṇāntarabhūtaḥ kvacidaida-
marthye kvacidanuṣṭhāne kvacidadhikāre kvacidutpattau vidyata iti pratipādyate । tadyathā prokṣaṇādīnā-
manvitābhidhānataḥ pratipannaniyogaidamarthyānāṃ śrutyādisiddhanaiyogikavrīhyādidvāraidamarthyānāṃ paścādau
pādānikaṃ tadubhayapratītinirvāhakaṃ dvāraidamarthyasādhyaṃ karaṇaidamarthyam । tathā nimittaparyante-
'dhikāre sāṅgeṣu pradhāneṣu prayoga upādānata eva । tathā viśvajidādiṣu adhikārakalpanā
aupādānikī । sauryaṃ caruṃ nirvapet brahmavarcasakāma ityādiṣu kevalādhikāracodanāsu utpatti-
niyogākṣepa upādānādeva । na khalu utpattiniyogaṃ vinā tatrāṅgopaskṛtātpradhānāt adhikāra-
niyogasiddharupapadyate । karmasvarūpāṇāṃ kṣaṇikatvena upakāryopakārakatvābhāvāditi darśita-
mekādaśe bhāṣyakāreṇa । sa cāyamupādānalakṣaṇo vidhivyāpāraḥ śrutyādipramāṇaṣaṭ‌kātirekī
tārtīyaviniyogāpekṣa iti tatra tatra vakṣyāma iti lakṣaṇayorapi hetuhetumadbhāvaḥ । <b>kratvartheti
ṭīkāyā ayamarthaḥ</b>---kratvarthapuruṣārthacintā kimiti pṛthak pratijñāyate athātaśśeṣalakṣaṇamityane-
naiva pratijñātatvāt । na ca vācyaṃ śeṣatvaṃ tatra pratijñātaṃ na punaraidamarthyamiti । yasmāta
<b>aidamarthyalakṣaṇameva śeṣatvaṃ śeṣaḥ parārthatvādityuktam</b> । pṛthagadhyāyārthābhāvāt adhyāyā-
<note>(1) P. Bhasya 1193</note>
﻿<pb n="r954"/>
ntaramayuktamityapi dūṣaṇaṃ hṛdi vartate । <b>atha matamityādi</b>---tatrāyamabhiprāyaḥ vainiyogikaṃ
śeṣatvaṃ vicāritam । idānīṃ punaḥ aupādānikaṃ pṛthak pratijñāyate । tathāhi---puruṣārthatā
yāgasya svargasādhanabhāvaḥ svargasya cādhikāripuruṣopabhogyatā 1na śrutyādibhiravagamyate । tathā
cok‍taṃ---<b>tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇeti</b> । tatrāha---<b>kratvarthagrahaṇaṃ tarhi pratyuktam</b> । yasmāt
kratvarthatā sarvaiva śrutyādigamyeti <b>na ceyamapi puruṣārthatālakṣaṇeti śakyate vak‍tum ।
yasmānna śabdādṛte yāgaḥ svargārtha iti jñānamupapadyate । na ca tatsādhyaḥ svargaḥ puruṣārthaḥ</b>
adhikāryarthaḥ iti jñānamutpadyate śabdatadbhāvabhāvitvāt śabdāt puruṣārthajñānaṃ śrutyādikṛtameveti
bhāvaḥ । <b>yadapi ceti</b> śrutyādisaṅkīrtanaṃ yattadapyanarthakamityarthaḥ । <b>yadapi ca kratvartha-
puruṣārthayoḥ iti</b> । bhāṣyakāro hi prayojakāprayojakādīnyatrāntarbhāvayati । tasyedaṃ
prayojanam---kathaṃ nāmottaro vicāraḥ pratijñātārthaviṣayaḥ syāditi । sa punarayamantarbhāvo
nopapadyate । <b>antarbhāvo hi bhavan svarūpato</b> vā syāt śeṣatvaidamarthyayoriva <b>kāryato
vā</b> ? sarveṣāmekaṃ kāryaṃ yathā viśeṣaliṅgādīnāṃ vaikṛtacodanāparipūraṇaṃ kāryamiti tatkāraṇa-
tvena pratijñāyate । sarveṣāmuttaraṣaṭ‌kārthānāmantarbhāvo bhavati । sa lakṣaṇato vā, sarveṣāmeka-
<note>(1) G. omits na</note>
﻿<pb n="r955"/>
meva lakṣaṇaṃ yadi syāt yathā codanābhedādīnāṃ tal‍lakṣaṇatayā pratijñāte sarve vedārthā antarbhave-
yuḥ । <b>trayamapi cātra nāsti yasmāt svarūpaṃ tāvat pṛthagabhidhānādeva bhinnam</b> ।
yadyeṣāmekameva svarūpaṃ syāt tadā tatra tatrādhikaraṇe bhedenaiṣāmabhidhānaṃ pratipādanaṃ na syāt ।
<b>lakṣaṇamapi</b> yena nyāyenaiṣāṃ svarūpaṃ lakṣyate tadapi <b>svarūpabhedādeva bhinnam</b> । na hyekena
lakṣaṇena svarūpabhedo bhavati pramāṇāyattatvāt prameyasiddheḥ, tadbhedādeva bhedo yataḥ prameyasyeti ।
kāryamapi yatprayojakaphalavidhipradhānāni puruṣārthe'ntarbhāvayatā puruṣopakāraḥ । tathā aprayo-
jakārthavādapradhānāni kratvarthe'ntarbhāvayatā kratūpakāro bhāṣyakāreṇa darśitaḥ । <b>tadayuktam</b> ।
nyāyavirodhāt <b>pradeśāntaraviruddhaṃ ca</b> arthavādādhikaraṇoktavirodhāditi । <b>arthavādaḥ
stutyarthaḥ</b> ukto hi yasmāt । <b>prādhānyamapi ca upakāryopakāranibandhanam</b> । yadupa-
kāryamupakārakasya tat tatpradhānam । na punaḥ puruṣārthatayā prādhānyam । kintūpakāryatayā ।
<b>prayojakamaṣi prayojyaṃ prati prādhānyamātmanaḥ pratipādayati</b> । na punarātmanaḥ parārthatām ।
prāvānyena hi prayojakatvaṃ, na punaḥ puruṣopakārakatvena1 । tasmāta kāryato'pi nāntarbhāvaḥ ।
<b>tadidaṃ rātriprayāṇakamivādeśakaṃ bhāṣyam</b> rātrau bhavaṃ rātriprayāṇakaṃ, avidyamānamārgakathaka-
puruṣakaṃ <b>vyāmohamupajanayati rātribhavatvena svapratyayavirahāt ādeśikapuruṣābhāvācca</b> ।
parapratyayābhāvāt deśīti mārgādeśika ucyate । ‘hetave puruṣārthānāṃ jyāyasāṃ deśine pathaḥ ।
<note>(1) G. katvaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r956"/>
iti । yathā ca ‘aviśrāmyaṃ anālambyaṃ apātheyamadeśikam । iti । atrocyate---<b>dvayamapye-
tad‌yuk‍taṃ</b> bhedena prayojakādīnā<b>mupanyāsaḥ antarbhāvakathanaṃ</b> ca tena tatra tāvanna kiñci-
dvācyam । <b>yatpunastādarthyaṃ śeṣatve hetuḥ</b> tena śeṣatvapratijñānāt tādarthyapratijñānāt
kratvarthapuruṣārthapratijñāpi kṛtaiveti । tatrāpi <b>satsu śrutyādiṣu tadityuk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa</b>
śrutyādisaṅkīrtanena । tena kevalaniyogavyāpāranibandhanapratijñeyamityuk‍taṃ bhavati । <b>nanu
caivaṃ sati kratvarthatā pratyuk‍tetyapyuktam</b> । tasyāḥ śrutyādinibandhanatvāt । <b>bhavedetadevaṃ
yadi vainiyogikamucyate kratvarthaṃ; iha tu upādānanibandhanaṃ</b> sarvaṃ kratvarthapuruṣārthaprayojakā-
prayojakaphalavidhyarthavādāṅgapradhānātmakaṃ pratijñāyate aupādānikamapi kratvarthamastīti bhāvaḥ ।
puruṣārthatā tu yadyapi śābdī tathāpi vainiyogikī na bhavati iti lipsādhikaraṇe vakṣyati ।
<b>kiṃ punaratropādānaṃ nāma</b> iti pūrvapakṣaṃ karoti । tatrāyaṃ bhāvaḥ---na śrutyādyatirekyupādāna-
lakṣaṇaṃ vidhivyāpārātmakaṃ pramāṇaṃ loke vyutpannamiti । rāddhāntaṃ karoti---<b>niyogākṣepa
upādānam</b> । satyaṃ na loke vyutpannaṃ tathāpi śabdena pratipādito'rtho yenārthāntareṇa vinā na
nirvahati tadākṣipatīti sāmānyatastāvalloke prasiddhirasti dvārakarmībhāvādau । vede ca
niyogaśśabdena pratipādito'rthāntaraṃ svanirvāhāya ākṣipatīti nānupapattiḥ । kiṃ punaru-
pādānasya prameyamiti tatrāha---<b>tatkṛtaṃ ca prokṣaṇādeḥ kratvarthatvam</b> karaṇārthatvamiti
prāgevāktam । <b>viniyogāt punaḥ vrīhyarthataiva</b> । naiyogikavrīhyādyaidamarthye viniyogasya
sāmarthyāt na karaṇaidamarthye । nanu yadi vidhyākṣiptamidaṃ cintyate atideśo'pi cintyaḥ
﻿<pb n="r957"/>
syāt । na । ekopadeśaparisamāpyamiha cintyate । atideśaśca upadeśāntarārthaparyālocanayā
parisamāpyate । tasmādiha na cintyate । <b>bhedārthapratijñānaṃ tarhi kimiti</b> । bhedena
arthasya pratipādyasya prayojakāprayojakāṅgapradhānādeśca pratijñā kimiti । <b>kimiti vā</b> kena
prakāre<b>ṇāntarbhāvaḥ । avagatihetubhedāt bhedena</b> upanyāsaḥ । avagatihetṛnāṃ nyāyānāṃ
bhedāt bhedena pratipādyatvāt kratvarthatādīnāṃ bhedena upanyāsaḥ । <b>upakārasāmānyādantarbhāvaḥ</b>
aprayojakāṅgārthavādāḥ kratūpakārā iti kratvarthe'ntarbhūtāḥ । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---kratvarthagrahaṇena
kratūpakārakasyāpi grahaṇam । arthavādasyāpi pramāṇakoṭiparyavasāyinaḥ pramāṇasyānuṣṭhānopakārakatvāt
kratūpakārakatāprayojakapradhānaphalavidhayaśca puruṣopakārasāmānyāt puruṣārthāntarbhāvina iti
siddham । <b><q>“prayojakaḥ kaścit puruṣārtha”</q> iti kaścid‪grahaṇaṃ prayojakasyāpyapuruṣārthatā-
jñāpanārtham</b> yatheti kathanopakrama eva <b>vak‍tuṃ kasyeti</b> praśnaḥ । <b>ācāryakaraṇavidheḥ
svādhyāyādhyayana</b>prayojakasyetyuttaramuktam । asyārthaḥ---ācāryakaraṇavidheḥ svādhyāyādhya-
yanaprayojakasyāpi svatantrakartṛrūpapuruṣaśabdavācyamāṇavakārthatvābhāvāt apuruṣārthatvam2 ।
yadīyaṃ hi karma yo vidhiḥ prayuṅ‌k‍te sa tatpuruṣārtha eva । yathā darśapūrṇamāsādayaḥ । ācārya-
karaṇavidhistu māṇavakīyamadhyayanaṃ prayuṅ‌k‍te । natu māṇavakārtha iti siddham ।</p>
<p><b>yasmin prītiḥ puruṣasya</b> । <q>“tasya lipsārthenaiva bhavati na śās‍treṇa”</q> iti
<b>viruddhamuktam</b> । anena hi kila bhāṣyeṇa yāgasya svargasādhanatātmikā puruṣārthatā svargasya ca
<note>(1) P. 1193</note> <note>(2) R. rthatvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r958"/>
adhikāribhogyatātmikā śās‍treṇa na gamyata ityuktam । tacca viruddham । yasmāt dvayamapye-
tat na śāstrādṛte'vagamyate । <b>saṃbandhaśāstramaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktamiti</b> । viniyogaśāstramabhi-
pretya idamuk‍taṃ nādhikāraśāstram । adhikāraśāstrādevopādānavaśena dvayamapīdaṃ gamyate yataḥ ।
ata evok‍taṃ arthenaiva bhavatīti । <b>arthaśca niyogasiddhiḥ</b> tasyā eva vākyārthatvāt
<b>taccopādānamityuktam</b> । atra cādhikaraṇe kratvarthapuruṣārthayoḥ pratipādayitavyayoḥ lakṣaṇa-
mucyate । tathāhi---na puruṣārthatvaṃ tāvat prītyutpādakatvam । nityeṣu niyamaniyogeṣu
cāvyāpteḥ । na ca sādhikāritvam, adhyayanādiṣvasaṃbhavāt । nāpi aupādānikaidamarthya-
bhāktvam, aupādānikakratvaṅgeṣu saṅkhyādiṣu atiprasaṅgāt । 1tasmiṃścāvivicyamāne puruṣārthatve
kratvarthatāpi tadbhadena durlabheti vivekāya lakṣaṇārambhaḥ । tatra puruṣārthalakṣaṇamaupādānikameva ।
yasyaidamarthyaṃ sa puruṣārtha iti yathā yāgaḥ svargaśceti । <b>nanu ca kratvarthatāpyupādānenaivoktā</b>
saṅkhyādīnāmityanenātiprasaṅgadoṣamāśaṅkate । <b>viniyoge satītyuktamiti</b> parihāraḥ ।
asyarthaḥ---viniyoge sati saṅkhyādīnāmaupādānikī śeṣatā । tathā hi---vastusvabhāvataḥ
tātsthyena liṅgaviniyoge sati saṅkhyādīnāmaupādānikaśeṣatvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ । tena viniyogena
vinā aupādānikaṃ yasya śeṣatvaṃ sa puruṣārthaḥ iti nāstyatiprasaṅgaḥ । <b>arthādeva hi puruṣārtha
iti viśeṣaḥ । kimidamavibhāgāditi</b> । bhāṣyakāro hi prītyā'vibhāgamāha । tadayuktam
nimittaparyanteṣu adhikāreṣvasaṃbhavāt । anayā śaṅkayā brūte kimidamiti । tatrottaraṃ
---<b>puruṣasya kratusambandhāvibhāgāditi</b> । anena cedamuk‍taṃ yasmāt kratuṣu puruṣo'nuṣṭhātā'sti
<note>(1) G. tasmiṃścāpivivicya</note>
﻿<pb n="r959"/>
tasmāt sādhyabhūto vidhiḥ śak‍notyākṣep‍tuṃ yāgasyaidamarthyamiti । <b>etacca ṣaṣṭhe nipuṇataramupapāda-
yiṣyāmaḥ</b> । nanvevaṃ puruṣārthatvamātramuk‍taṃ bhavati tatrāha---<b>pariśeṣādviniyoge sati iti
kratvarthatok‍tā bhavati</b> । tasmādubhayamapyatra likṣatam ।</p>
<p><b>evaṃ vā । nanu guṇaphalacodanā etā ityuktam । ko'yaṃ punarvicāraḥ ?</b> dvitīye
tṛtīye ca guṇasya godehanādeḥ phalāya codanā etā ityuktam । tataśca phalaṃ prati śeṣatā
kevalopādānagamyeti puruṣārthatve sthite punarvicāro'narthakaḥ । <b>ucyate । pradarśitamasmābhiḥ
viniyogatastaduktamiti</b> । viniyogaparyālocanayā kratvarthatvaṃ na saṃbhavatīti hetoḥ
tatpuruṣārthatvamuktam । <b>iha punaḥ upādānato dṛṣṭaprayojanasiddhisaṃbhave nādṛṣṭārthatvaṃ saṃbhavatīti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । godohanādeḥ praṇayanādinirvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭaṃ prayojanam paśvādisiddhiradṛṣṭam । tatra
kiṃ niyogaḥ dṛṣṭena dvāreṇopādatte uta adṛṣṭena dvāreṇopādatta iti cintāyāṃ dṛṣṭasya śīghra-
bhāvitvāt tenaiva dvāreṇopādatte । tataścopādānārthatvādviniyogasya viniyogo'pi tathaiva ।
paśukāmapadaṃ ca adhikṛtamātropalakṣaṇam । vākyena ca godohanena praṇayet iti praṇayane
godohanasya viniyogāt kratvarthatvamiti । <b>na, yathāviniyogaṃ kāryāvagamāt । viniyuktasyaiva
hi kāryakalpanā nāviniyuktasyeti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathāviniyogaṃ viniyo-
﻿<pb n="r960"/>
gānusāreṇa; kāryāvagateḥ dvārakāryāvagamāt rāddhānta iti saṃbandhaḥ । kasmādevamityāha
---viniyuktasyaiva hi kāryakalpanā nāviniyuktasyeti kratvarthasyāpi kratuviniyogasiddhiḥ ।
kāryabhūtā kalpanīyā । tatkalpanāyāṃ ca viniyogaśśaraṇam । vaniyogabalena ca dvārakārya-
parigrahaḥ । na cātra kratvarthatayāpi viniyogo'sti । <b>tasmāt</b> dṛṣṭamapyetatkāryaṃ na1 viniyomā-
pekṣamiti । <b>ato viniyogato'pi</b> viniyogaparyālocanayā <b>niyogataśca</b> upādānaparyā-
locanayā <b>puruṣārthataiva guṇaphalacodanāsviti sthitam । bādarigrahaṇaṃ punaḥ upakāra-
pradarśanārthaṃ na punaḥ parārthatvāditi śeṣahetunivṛttyartham</b> । nanu ca bhāṣyakāraḥ upakārataḥ
śeṣatāmāha, na punarupādānataḥ yato bādarimatamupanyasyati sma । taccānupapannam ।

yitum</b> । tataścopādānataḥ karaṇaśeṣateti । na punaḥ parārthatvāditi śeṣatve yo hetuḥ
tannivṛttyartham । kasmāt ? <b>viniyoge hi</b> yasmāt saḥ parārthatvāditi heturuktaḥ ।

ityevamarthaṃ, tena bādarimatopanyāsāt upakārata eva śeṣatok‍teti pratibhāti । <b>ata evāsau
nirākṛta</b> iti parihāraḥ । yata evopakārataśśeṣatā bādariṇoktā ata eva bādarirnirā-
kṛtaḥ । tena punarāśaṅkā nopapadyate । kimiti tarhyupanyāsaḥ ? <b>atrāha---iha punaḥ kāryata eva</b>
upakārata <b>evopādānamiti</b> na punarupanyasto bādariḥ upakāro'tra dṛṣṭo'sti । tathā ca

pralāpa ityatrāha---<b>ārjanaṃ svatvaṃ nāpādayatīti vipratiṣiddham</b> । atrāyaṃ bhāvaḥ---na yatheṣṭa-

marhati tattasya sva”</q>miti । tena yatheṣṭaviniyogārhatayā svatvaṃ, tadarhatā ca tatra tasya yatra

anena dhanakāmanā nādhikāriviśeṣaṇam । kintu dhanārjanapravṛttiḥ yadā yadā dhanārjanāya

rāganibandhanā tatra pravṛttiriti tadatikrame vihitatikramo na syāt । jīvanaśabdena ca dhanamabhida-
dhato'yamabhiprāyaḥ saṃbhavati tatra jijīviṣoḥ pravṛttyavyabhicāraḥ vyabhicarati tu kratusaṃbandha-

<b>na cārjanasya viśeṣopādānatve pramāṇamasti</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadā dravyamukhenārjanaṃ kratvarthaṃ

<p><b>tadutsarge karmaṇi । yasmin pratiḥ purupasya tasya lipsā arthalakṣaṇetyuktam । iha

<b>ato'dhikāriśūnyatāvidheḥ na cānadhikāraṃ puruṣārthaṃ bhavati iti kratvarthasyekṣaṇasyāyaṃ

pratiṣedhyamukhena kratāvantarbhavet । ucyate---anīkṣaṇaniyamasaṃkalpo'pi yadi svatantra eva

dāharaṇaṃ bhavantu । bhavatu na kaściddoṣaḥ । <b>atrābhidhīyate---prītyutsargepyetaduk‍taṃ
bhavati adhikārāśravaṇe'ṣyadhikāro yuktaḥ kalpayitum । na punaḥ kratusaṃbandhakalpanā ।
kaḥ punaranayorviśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśeṣaḥ---yathaiva adhikāre śrūyamāṇe gamyamānatatkartṛtaiva
nyāyyā</b> । yasyādhikāraḥ śrūyate tasyādhikārānyathānupapattyā tatkartṛtā kalpyate । kāryatayā
hi niyogaṃ yaḥ pratipadyate so'dhikārī । viṣayasādhyaśca niyogaḥ । sa yadi viṣayaṃ na
﻿<pb n="r967"/>
saṃpādayet tasya niyogaḥ kārya eṃva na syāt iti viṣayasaṃpādakatayā kartṛtvāvagamāt ।
tacca kartṛtvaṃ sākṣādvā puruṣāntaraprayuktyā vā yadyapyubhayathā upapadyate tathāpi sākṣāt saṃbhave
paramparānupapatteḥ tatkartṛtaiva nyāyyā । na punaḥ puruṣāntarakartṛtākalpanā, vinā vacanā-
dārtvijeṣveva । <b>evaṃ kriyākṣepeṇa gamyamānakartravagamāt adhikārakalpanaiva nyāyyā</b> ।
adhikāraṃ vinā kartṛtvānupapatteḥ । na cānyatrādhikāreṇānyatrāpi tadaṅgatayā'dhikāranupraveśena
kartṛtvasiddhiḥ । atraivādhikāre sākṣātsaṃbhavati paramparānupapatteriti । evaṃ ca nyāyataḥ
sthite'dhikāriṇi prayuktikalpanāpi na doṣaḥ । <b>kathaṃ tarhi kartradhikaraṇamiti</b> <q>‘nānṛtaṃ
vadet’</q> ityatrāpi tarhi gamyamānakartṛtvasiddha‍yarthaṃ sākṣādadhikārakalpanāt kimarthaṃ karturvācyatva-
nirākaraṇaṃ ? nirākṛtepi vācyatve, gamyamānepi kartari tasya kartuḥ svatantrādhikārāpatteḥ ।
