svatantrādhikārakalpanaiva netyanavadyam । evaṃ tāvat samāhitamidamadhikaraṇam । idānīṃ suhṛdbhāve-
nādhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ nirūpayati---<b>kiṃbhūtaḥ punaratrādhikriyate <q>“etāvatā hainasā viyukto
bhavati”</q> iti śravaṇāt jīvata eva vā'dhikāraḥ</b> । asmin‍nudāharaṇe etāvatā hainasā pāpena
viyuk‍to bhavatītyarthavādaḥ । tatra yadi jīvanavānadhikārī bhavati tadā nityatvāt atrākaraṇe
vihitātikramadoṣa evainoyogo bhavatīti sālambano'rthavādaḥ । viśvajidādivat‍tu svarge'dhikāri-
<note>(1) G. rikalpa</note> <note>(2) G. prakṛtāyāṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r968"/>
viśeṣaṇe kalpyamāne kāmyasyākaraṇe'pi na doṣaḥ । tatrārthavādasyātiparokṣā vṛttiḥ syāt
<b>ato nityo'yaṃ jīvanānupālanīyo niyamaḥ svadharmatayā</b> ।</p>
<p><b>nanu ca prasajyapratiṣedho nyāyyaḥ</b> asyārthaḥ---nanu prasajyapratiṣedho'yam । tatra
niṣidhyamānakriyākataiṃvādhikārī । kimiti jīvanavānucyate । satyaṃ svavākyamātrālocanayā
evaṃ, kintu <b>tasya vratamityanvayāvagateḥ lakṣaṇaiva nyāyvā</b> । anīkṣaṇasaṅkalpo vratarūpo lakṣyate
tena 1nāyaṃ prasajyapratiṣedhaḥ । nanvevaṃ ādhānavat kimita saṅkalpo'pi dravyārthoṃ na syāt ।
tatrāha---<b>ādhānavadapyatra dravyārthatā naiva saṃbhavati</b> sākṣācchrutyabhāvāt । <b>aviniyukta-
dravyasaṃyogāt dṛṣṭasya ca saṃskārasyābhāvāt naiva</b> dravyārthatā । yadi punaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
saṃskāraḥ syāt । <b>kiṃ dṛṣṭārthatā śakyate vak‍tum</b> । asyārthaḥ---sarvaṃ śabdāvagamyaṃ
codanāsviti sthitam । yadyapi saṃskāro dṛṣṭaḥ tathāpi tadarthatā na yuk‍teti । <b>bāḍhaṃ śakyate
darpaṇapramārjanavat loka evopayogadarśanāt</b> । atrābhiprāyaḥ---kalpanīye prayojane pratyakṣamapi
prayojanaṃ nirākāṅkṣīkaraṇayogyaṃ na tyak‍tuṃ śakyata iti । <b>tasmāt puruṣārtho niyamassaṃkalpa</b>-
rūpo'yamiti yuktam । <b>dṛṣṭārthāsaṃbhavena ca karkarīkarṇādayo'pi2 puruṣārthā ityuktam</b> । 
gokarṇalakṣaṇānyapi 3kakarīkarṇyāḥ kartavyāḥ ityevamādīni kratusaṃbandhini dravye dṛṣṭasaṃskārā-
bhāvena purupārthānyeva gomāneva cādhikārīti sthitam ।</p>
<note>(1) G. nāprasajya</note> <note>(2) G. kartarikaraṇādayo'pi</note> <note>(3) G. kartarīkarṇyaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r969"/>
<p><b>dravyāṇi tu</b> । nanu tṛtīye uddhananādiṣveva spha‍yādīnāṃ viniyoga uk‍taḥ ।
tatkathamihānyatrāpyāśaṅkyate tatrāha---<b>uk‍tamityādi</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---spha‍yaścetyādibhiḥ
sahoddhananādivākyānāṃ viniyogavicāraḥ kṛtaḥ । tatroddhananādivākyāni viniyojakanīti
sthitam । idamidānīṃ cintyate---etāni vai daśa yajñāyudhānīti kimidaṃ śāstrāntaraṃ spha‍ye-
noddhantītyevamādibhyaḥ uta teṣāmevānuvādaḥ iti cintāntaraṃ darśayati । nanu dvitīyādhyāya-
cinteyaṃ śāstrabhedābhedaviṣayā । kimiti caturthe cintyate । ucyate । pṛthak‌prayuktyarthaṃ
dvitīyārthavamarśaḥ kriyate । yadi śāstrāntaramidaṃ syāt tadā asya sākṣādyajñasādhanatvena
pṛthagidaṃ prayoktavyaṃ syāt abhedapakṣe tu śāstrābhedāt bhedena prayuktirnāsti । kīdṛśo
dvitīyārthāvamarśaḥ ityatrāha---kiṃ bhedalakṣaṇayuk‍tamidaṃ vākyaṃ guṇāntaravidhānapakṣe sādhyabhedāt,
guṇavatkarmāntaravidhānetu anubandhabhedāt, utānuvādakatayā sādhyānubdhabhedābhāvāt abheda-
lakṣaṇayuktamiti । <b>pūrvapakṣavādī spha‍yenoddhantītyevamādibhirvākyaiḥ sākṣādyajñasaṃbandhānava-
gamāt yajñāyudhānīti vidhyantaraṃ manyate</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---yajñāyudhānīti ṣaṣṭhīsamā-
so'yam । ṣaṣṭhī ca yadyapi saṃbandhamātre bhavati tathāpi sākṣātsaṃbandhe saṃbhavati na paramparā
āśrayituṃ nyāyyeti sākṣādyajñasaṃbandha evāvagamyate । na cāsau prāptaḥ yenāsāvanuvādaḥ
syāt । <q>‘ato vacanāni tvapūrvatvāt’</q> ityayamapi vidhiḥ । 1sa ca āgneyādiṣveva dravyaṃ
vidhatte । guṇāntarāvaruddhatvādvā teṣāṃ guṇāntarayuk‍taṃ karmāntaramiti । <b>nanu vājapeyasya
yūpa itivat praṇāḍyāpi saṃbandha upapadyate । yuk‍taṃ yūpābhāvātkratostatra</b> । na ca
<note>(1) G. na ca</note>
﻿<pb n="r970"/>
vidhāsyata iti vācyam । saptad‌śārat‍nitāvidhānaparatvāddvākyasya । anuvāde yathā prāptiḥ
praṇāḍyāpyāśrīyate । <b>iha punaḥ</b> vidhānepi saṃbhavati <b>kiṃ nopapadyata</b> ityabhiprāyaḥ ।
<b>atrābhidhīyate---yajñāyudhānīti tāvallakṣaṇā । lakṣaṇā cetsākṣāt vyavadhāne ca na
kaścidviśeṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yajñāyudhaśabdena tāvat na sākṣāta tatsādhanamucyate, kintu
tatsaṃbandhī lakṣyate । saṃbandhilakṣaṇā cet na sākṣādva‍yavadhāne ca kaścidviśeṣaḥ । saṃbandhitvā-
viśeṣāt । tena yajñāyudhaśabdena sākṣātsaṃbandho bodhyate iti aprāptārthatā na śakyate
vak‍tum । nanvevaṃ prāptārthatāpi naikāntataḥ śakyā vak‍tum । satyam---kintu vidhiśūnya-
midaṃ vākyaṃ kalpyavidhikam । kalpanā cānupapattau satyāṃ, nacānupapattiḥ uddhananadvāraka1vyavahita-
saṃbandhāśrayaṇenopapatteḥ । tasmādanuvādo'yaṃ na vidhiḥ । atraiva yuktyantaramāha---<b>pramāṇānta-
rānusāriṇī ca lakṣaṇā । na ca vidyamāne pramāṇe pramāṇāntarakalpanā śakyā । spha‍ye-
noddhantītyubhayasiddhatvāt</b> । loke ca lakṣaṇā prasiddhā gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityādau । tatra
yadgaṅgākūlaṃ lakṣayati, tat1 pramāṇāntareṇa kūle ghoṣadarśanāt । tadevamihāpi pramāṇāntara-
prasiddhatvāt uddhananādidvārikaiva saṃbandhitā āśrayituṃ yuk‍tā । tasmādanuvādo'yam ।
<b>evaṃ ca vikalpaḥ parihṛto bhavati</b> । yadyāgneyādiṣu dravyavidhiḥ tadā puroḍāśādibhiḥ saha
yo vikalpaḥ sa parihṛto bhavati । <b>liṅgaṃ copapannaṃ bhavati</b> । yadi karmāntaravidhānaṃ tadā
devatābhāvena avyak‍tatvāt saumikavidhyantaprāp‍tyā āhṛtisaṅkhyādarśanaṃ nopapadyate । tathā
somasthānāpattyā abhiṣutānāṃ spha‍yādīnāṃ paridhānīye karmaṇi na syāddarśanam ।</p>
<note>(1) G. dvārakasya</note>
﻿<pb n="r971"/>
<p><b>tatra caikatvamayajñāṅgam</b> । nanu caikatvādi vibhaktyāpi kāryānvayitvenābhihitam ।
tataśca kāryāṅgatvāt tadanupādāne kāryameva na saṃvarteta ityatrāha---<b>ekatvaṃ viniyogābhāvānna
yajñaṅgamiti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapyekatvaṃ grāhakagṛhītaṃ tathāpi
viniyogābhāvāt dvārasabandhābhāvāt tadabhāve ca sāmānyasaṃbandhānirvāhāt na yajñāṅgamiti ।
<b>kathaṃ punaḥ ekatvaṃ na viniyujyate ? vibhak‍tayo hi prātipadikārthasya svārthasaṃbandhama-
bhidadhati</b> । svārthasya karaṇatvādeḥ prātipadikārthasaṃbandhitvāt । na punaḥ svārthabhūtai-
katvādisaṃbandhitā vibhaktayo'bhidadhati । <b>tasmādekatvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ ca prātipadikārthasyaiva ।
naikatvasya karaṇabhāvaḥ</b> karaṇatve cāsati kriyāsaṃbandhābhāvādayajñāṅgamiti । <b>karaṇasaṃbandhe</b>
hi karaṇatayā kriyāsaṃbandhe <b>prātipadikārthasaṃbandho na syāt । yathā aruṇayeti</b> kriyā-
saṃbandhe dravyaguṇasaṃbandho na bhavati । <b>tasmāt pratīyamānamapyetat na kriyayā saṃbadhyate</b>
yathā pūrvo dhāvatītyaparapratyayaḥ । pratīyamānamapītyapiśabdena evamāha---kriyāsaṃbandhābhāvena
1kāryānvayitayā anabhidheyameva । yadyapyabhidhīyate tathāpyanaṅgamiti । <b>liṅgadarśanāni
caivamupapannāni bhavantīti । evaṃ prāpte ucyate---na viniyogādeva kriyāṅgatā kiṃ tarhi</b>
<note>(1) G. iti yat</note> <note>(2) R. bhāvenākārya</note>
﻿<pb n="r972"/>
<b>upādānādapi śeṣatā bhavati । yathaiva karaṇībhūtasyaivopādānaṃ evamekatvayuktasyāpi</b> ।
yathaiva hi akārakabhūtasyānupādānaṃ evamasaṅkhyākasyāpi । <b>na hyakārakasyopādānaṃ asaṅkhyā-
yuk‍tasyāpi saṃbhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ</b> । paśustāvat viniyukta upādātavyaśca । sa ca
saṅkhyayā vinā na śakyate upādātum; śrutaṃ ca tatsthamekatvam । tadapi ca kāryānvayitvena
śrutam । tadanupraveśāyāvaśyamāśrayamapekṣate । ataḥ 2tadvadevāvacchedakatayā svīkriyate ।
svīkṛtaṃ ca viniyuktasthaṃ tātsthyenāṅgatāṃ yāti । saṅkhyā hi svasāmarthyenaiva svasaṅkhyeyaśeṣa-
bhūtā । sā hi prāk prātipadikārthamātre sthitā samprati upādānadaśāyāṃ viniyuktasthā
jātā । śeṣabhāvastu tasyāḥ vastusvabhāvalakṣaṇālliṅgāt ityanavadyam । <b>tathā ca laukikāḥ
gāmānayetyādiṣu tathaiva pratipadyante</b> । nanu bhāṣyakāraḥ vākyabalena kriyāśeṣatāmāha
nopādānata iti tatrāha---<b>tadidamuk‍taṃ</b> yadasmābhiruk‍taṃ tadetat bhāṣyakāreṇāpyuk‍taṃ <q>“na śruti-
rbrūte vākyārtho nāstīti”</q> anena granthena । kathamuktamityatrāha---<b>na viniyogo brūte upādānaṃ
nāstītyarthaḥ । nanu cānya evārthaḥ pratīyate na śrūtyā vākyasya virodho'stīti । yataḥ
3śrutyarthāparityāgena vākyāt kratvarthatāvagamyate । virodhe na daurbalyamuk‍tam</b> ।
<note>(1) P. 1205</note> <note>(2) G. tadaivāva</note> <note>(3) G. śrutyaparityāgena</note>
﻿<pb n="r973"/>
atrottaraṃ---<b>uk‍tamasmābhirviniyogo na saṃbhavatīti</b> । vākyenāpi viniyogo nāsti kriyā-
saṃbandhāvagamābhāvāditi । tasmādyathāśrutaṃ na vyākhyeyamidaṃ bhāṣyam iti । <b>kathaṃ tarhi vākya-
śabdaḥ ? samabhivyāhāraparyāyo'yaṃ na viniyojakaparyāyaḥ</b> । ekasmin vākye kriyā
caikatvaṃ ca samabhivyāhṛtam । tadbalena copādānaśeṣateti। tasmādeva kriyāṅgatocyata
ityarthaḥ । tasmāt siddhamupādānaśeṣatvaṃ saṅkhyāyā liṅgasya ca । nanu <q>‘vasantā
prātarāgneyīṃ kṛṣṇagrīvīmālabheta’</q> ityatra liṅgaṃ prakṛtibhāgābhihitaṃ vibhaktyā viniyujyate prātipadi-
kābhidheyamiveti kathamupādānaśeṣatā ? ucyate---prātipadikena yo'rthaḥ pradhānabhūtaḥ pratipādyate
tatraiva s‍trīpratyayābhidheyamapi liṅgaṃ vibhaktyarthaśca kārakatvaṃ saṅkhyā cāvagamyate । na punaḥ
s‍trītvayuk‍te pradhānāśrayamātrāpekṣatvādguṇanām । prātipadikabhāgena prathamoccaritena liṅga-
śūnyasya prātipadikārthamātrasya avagatatvāt tanmātreṇa vibhaktyarthaḥ saṃbadhyata iti tulyaṃ
saṅkhyayā । <b>evaṃ darśanānyupapannāni । pūrvapakṣadarśanaṃ cānuvādaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>evaṃ vā । liṅgādhikaraṇam punarevaṃ veti vadataḥ ko'bhiprāyaḥ ?</b> asyārthaḥ
---pūrvādhikaraṇe hi liṅgamapyupādānaśeṣamityuk‍tam । kimaparamiha punaścintyata iti ।
<b>aparicchedakatvaṃ liṅgasya pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । paricchedikā hi saṅkhyā dravyasya parimāṇa-
mācaṣṭe</b> । asyārthaḥ---saṅkhyāntareṣūpādīyamāneṣu kārakaparimāṇānyatvenānuṣṭhāne(nai)'nekatvā-
﻿<pb n="r974"/>
vagamāt yuktā saṅkhyāviśeṣāpekṣāyāṃ 2tasyā upādānaśeṣatā । liṅge tu dravyāntaropādānā-
bhāvenānuṣṭhānaviśeṣānāpādakatvāt viśeṣāpekṣā nopapadyata । ato nopādānaśeṣateti । śravaṇā-
viśeṣālliṅgamapyupādīyata iti rāddhāntaḥ । yathā saṅkhyā śrutā tathā liṅgamapi । <b>nanu
cāparimāṇāpādakatvāt liṅgaṃ nopādātavyamityuktamiti</b> pūrvoktasmāraṇam। parihartuṃ
<b>nātra parimāṇamupādāne upayujyate viśeṣaniṣṭhatvādupādānasya yathā'nuṣṭhānaviśeṣākāṅkṣā
tathā kārakaviśeṣākāṅkṣāpi</b> । tena kārakaviśeṣāpādakaṃ liṅgamapyupādeyam । <b>atassaṅkhyā-
vadupādānamiti siddham</b> । śeṣaṃ pūrvavat ।</p>
<p><b>āśrayiṣvaviśeṣeṇa । ihāśrayiṇaḥ padārthā udāharaṇam</b> । sandehaṃ kartuṃ udāharaṇa-
mupanyastam । nanu bhāṣyamayuk‍taṃ <q>“kiṃ yajimātraṃ saṃskāraḥ devatāyāḥ, uta yajinā'dṛṣṭaṃ
devatāyāṃ kriyata”</q> <b>iti yasmāt saṃskāramātramadṛṣṭamakurvat anarthakam</b> । avaghātādiṣvapi
niyamādṛṣṭaṃ yāvannābhyupagamyate tāvadānarthakyameva niyamasya । tasmāt saṃskārapakṣe'(sya)pya-
<note>(1) P. 1207</note> <note>(2) tasyopā</note>
﻿<pb n="r975"/>
dṛṣṭamastītyatrāha---<b>dvividhamākhyātamuk‍tam । paraprāptaniyogānuvādakaṃ avahantītyāg‍neyā-
dicodanāvagataniyogānuvādakaṃ svaniyogasaṃbandhitayā cādhikārasādhanaṃ</b> samidho yajatī-
tyādibhinnotpattiniyogābhyupagamāt । ihedānīṃ sandihyate---<b>kiṃ paraprāptaniyogānuvādātmakami-
damākhyātaṃ uta svaniyogasaṃbandhitayā'dhi1kārasādhanamiti</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---saṃskāra-
mātrapakṣe niyogāntaraṃ nāstīti devatāyāmadṛṣṭaṃ kriyata iti । atrādṛṣṭamapūrvamabhimatam ।
tenāyaṃ bhāṣyārthaḥ---devatāyāṃ saṃskriyamāṇāyāṃ yajinā paramapūrva kriyata iti । tenāpūrvāntara-
sadasadbhāvasaṃśayo'yamiti yāvat । <b>kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ aṃśena</b> homaparyantatayā dravyaprakṣepāṃśena
dravyavirecanasya, tathā'ṅgabhūtamantrāṃśena devatāsmaraṇasya <b>ca dṛṣṭasya saṃbhavāt aṃśena</b> yāgāṃśenā-
<b>dṛṣṭasya</b> ca saṃbhavāt tenāṃśena dṛṣṭāntarasyāsaṃbhavāt <b>pūrvapakṣavādī manyate dṛṣṭe</b> dravyadevatā-
gatopakāre saṃti <b>adṛṣṭakalpanā</b> apūrvāntarakalpanā <b>na nyāyyā</b> । 2taddvāreṇādhi-
kārāṅgabhāvopātteḥ । <b>nanu yajyartho'tra na niṣpadyate</b> tena aṃśena dṛṣṭopakārābhāvāt
adhikārānanupraveśāt tatprayuktyabhāvāt yajyartho na niṣpadyeta <b>anuṣṭhānād dṛṣṭopapattyartho
bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ</b> । yathā'vaghātādiṣu mantrādikam । <b>atrābhidhīyate---dṛṣṭo-
papattyarthataiva na ghaṭate kasmāt ? niyogasiddheravivakṣitatvāt</b> । utpattiniyogasiddhera-
<note>(1) G. vikāra</note> <note>(2) G. vyākhyātadvāreṇa</note>
﻿<pb n="r976"/>
vivakṣitatvāt । tathāpi kimityāha---<b>niyogāddhi1niyogārthe pravṛttiḥ</b> । atrābhiprāyaḥ
niyoge'vivakṣite na śuddhaṃ yajimātraṃ kṣaṇikaṃ adhikāraniyogārthaṃ bhavati asati ca tadarthatve
na tatra pravṛttiḥ yasmāt niyogādyā pravṛttiḥ sā niyogārthe na punaraniyogārthe । nanu yāgāṅgasya
dravyadevatādvāreṇāṅgatā'stītyuktam । <b>ucyate</b>---na tāvat sākṣāt dravyadevatārthatā yāgasya ।
kintu aṅgabhūtamantrāt । sā cāṅgamukhena tatra cetaretarāśrayatā; nirūḍhe niyogārthatve'ṅgasaṃbandhaḥ
aṅgasaṃbandhe na dravyadevatārthatayā niyogārthatā । yasmānna svarūpamātre aniyogake dharmasaṃbandho
ghaṭata iti । <b>atha tadarthaṃ 2adhikārārthaṃ utpattiniyogo vivakṣyate siddhamapūrvārthatvam ।
3paścādadhikāraniyogārthatve yāgasya nirūḍhe'ṅgasaṃbandhe sati tad‌dvāreṇa dravyadevatāgata-
dṛṣṭasaṃskāraniṣpattyarthamityanumanyata eva</b> । tasmāt tṛtīyaprakāro'yaṃ niyogānuvādakaḥ
svaniyogasaṃbandhibhyāmiti paramatenopasaṃhṛtam ।</p>
<p>svamatamāha---<b>na ca tṛtīyaprakāro'yaṃ niyoganiṣpattestulyatvādeva svaniyoga-
saṃbandhasya vidyamānatvāt । samidādivat</b> । nanvevaṃ sati dravyābhāvepi sviṣṭakṛto na
lopaḥ tatrāhaṃ---<b>prayojanaṃ tu dṛṣṭamadṛṣṭaṃ vā bhavatu prayojanavaśācca anuṣṭhānamanuṣṭhānaṃ vā
bhavatu asyārthaḥ</b>---yadyapi niyogasiddhiḥ tathāpi dṛṣṭatvāt dravyādisaṃskāra eva
prayojakaḥ । niyogārthastvaprayojaka eva । tena dravyābhāve sviṣṭakṛto lopaḥ tasmāt
siddhā svaniyogārthatā ।</p>
<note>(1) vini</note> <note>(2) G. utpatti niyogārthaṃ</note> <note>(3) paścādyadyadhikāra</note>
﻿<pb n="r977"/>
<p><b>arthe samavaiṣamyamato dravyakarmaṇām । atikrāntastṛtīyaviṣayaḥ iti । ko'yaṃ
tṛtīyaviṣayaḥ ?</b> yadi tṛtīyaviṣayo'yaṃ kimiti caturthe cintyate ityanenābhiprāyeṇāya praśnaḥ ।
atrottaraṃ---<b>pārārthyapratipattiḥ । sā'tikrāntā</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ-<b>yadyapyeṣā pārārthyapratipattiḥ
sā'tikrāntā</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---yadyapyeṣā pārārthyapratipattiḥ tathāpi śrutyādibhirna bhavati
niyogavyāpāranibandhanaiveti iha cintyate । <b>idānīṃ punaḥ sthite pārārthye kevalamupādānameva
cintyate</b> । prayuktiḥ upādānam । taccintyate । <b>kena prayojanenāmikṣādīnāmupādānaṃ
kena neti । nanu ca prāgapyasmāt prayojanakṛtaiva upādānacintā</b> । saṅkhyādīnāmapi
yadupādānaṃ tadapi upādānakṛtameva <b>kena viśeṣeṇedamucyate idamidānīmiti । satyam । kintu
pārārthyamapi tannimittakameva na niyoganimittakam । ata idamuktaṃ tṛtīyaviṣaya iti ।
tṛtīyasyāyaṃ viṣayaḥ na punastārtīyaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ śakyate'vagantum । ato vidhinimittaka---
mevāsya pārārthyamiti caturthe cintitam । etacca vyākhyātaṃ <q>“na śrutyādibhiḥ sarvasya
<note>(1) P. 1208</note>
﻿<pb n="r978"/>
pārārthyaṃ śakyate pratipādayituṃ”</q> iti । etadevātra kathyate । tathā ca yāgaphalayoḥ
adhikārāt pārārthyaṃ vakṣyati</b> ṣaṣṭhādye । niyoganiyojyalakṣaṇasaṃbandhāvagamabalena yāgasya
svargaṃ prati phalasya puruṣaṃ prati śeṣatvaṃ vakṣyati । yata eva śrutyādibhiryā1gaphalayoḥ pārārthyaṃ
2nāvagamyate <b>ata eva bādarereṣā bhrāntiḥ dravyaguṇasaṃkāreṣveva śeṣatvamiti । śrutyādīnāṃ
tatra dravyādau saṃbhavāt upādānādhikārayoḥ sāmarthyamapaśyato'vadhāraṇāt</b> । etacca bruvatā
bādaryadhikaraṇaṃ caturthādhyāye saṅgatamapi 3vyavadhānanirākaraṇāya tṛtīya eva kṛtamityuktam ।
yata eva śrutyādinibandhanamidaṃ na bhavati śeṣatvaṃ <b>ata evedaṃ lakṣaṇāntaramityucyate
śeṣāvagamatulyatvepi</b> ।</p>
<p>ekaniṣpatteḥ । ataḥ <b>prabhṛtīdānīṃ kevalopādānavyāpāra eva</b> kevalā prayuktireva
cintyate । <b>śeṣatā tu viniyogata eva nopādānataḥ । pūrvapakṣavādī tu kevalopakāradarśanā-
devopādānamāha, na śeṣatā'pekṣaṇīyeti manyate । yathaivopādānaśeṣeṣu paś‍vekatvādiṣu</b> ।
<note>(1) G. śrutyādibhiḥ sarvasya pārārthyaṃ śakyate</note> <note>(2) G. cāvagamyate</note> <note>(3) G.
avadhāraṇa</note>
﻿<pb n="r979"/>
asyārthaḥ---dadhyānayanamāmikṣāyā vājinasya copakārakam । yadi paramāmikṣāṃ prati śeṣaḥ
upakāranibandhanā ca prayuktiḥ na śeṣatvanibandhanā, ekatvādīnāṃ prāgaśeṣabhūtānāmapyupādānenaiva
1śeṣatā yataḥ, tasmādumayaṃ prayojakamiti । <b>atrābhidhīyate---nātra prayojakatvaṃ vājinasya ।
kutaḥ ? śeṣabhūtasya hi prayojanākāṅkṣā । sā ca yasya śeṣabhūtā tenaiva prayojanena nivṛtteti
na prayojanāntaraṃ prayojakatvena</b> kalpayituṃ śakyate । asyārthaḥ---śeṣabhūtaṃ dadhyānayanaṃ
kena prayojanena prayujyatāmiti prayojakaviśeṣākāṅkṣā । tatra yasyaiva payasaḥ śeṣabhūtaṃ tadeva
prayojakaṃ yuktam । śabdataḥ tatsaṃbandhitvenāvagamāt । āmikṣā ca payaḥ tasyāmeva tadrasa-
pratyabhijñānāt । etacca <b>vivaraṇapañcikāyāṃ</b> vakṣyāmaḥ । tena saiva prayojikā na
vājinamiti siddham । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ aśeṣabhūtasyopādānaśeṣatvamekatvādeḥ । aśeṣabhūtasya
prayojanākāṅkṣaiva nāstīti</b> । kathamaśeṣabhūtasyaikatvādeḥ upādānaśeṣatvaṃ <b>aśeṣatve upādāna-
syaivānupapatteḥ । atrocyate---śeṣasyāvagamāt</b> śeṣabhūtaṃ hi yat paśvādi tadekatva---
śūnyaṃ nāvagatamiti na tadrahitamupādīyata iti । <b>anyathā'navagamāt avagama---
pūrvakatvāccopādānasya । kiñci śeṣabhūtasya prayojyatvānyathānupapatteḥ</b> śeṣabhūtasya hi
paśoḥ prayojyatvamanyathā nopapadyate । kasmāt ? <b>na hi anavacchinnamupādātuṃ śakyata
ityuktam</b> । na hi saṅkhyānavacchinnamupādātuṃ śakyata iti śeṣopādānārthamaśeṣasyāpyupādānaṃ
<note>(1) G. śeṣakāryataḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r980"/>
<b>yatpunaḥ na śeṣabhūtaṃ na ca śeṣasthamavagamyate</b> tena vināpi śeṣatvāvagamāt <b>na śeṣopādāne-
nāpyapekṣyate</b> tena vināpi śeṣopādānasiddheḥ <b>na tat prayojyaṃ bhavitumarhati yathā dadhyānayanaṃ
na vājinasya śeṣabhūtaṃ tathā pradarśitaṃ bhāṣye । tathā ca liṅgaṃ pradarśitam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>padakarmāprayojakam । kaḥ punarādhastyenādhikaraṇenāsya viseṣaḥ</b> । athaiva hi
āmikṣāśeṣabhūtaṃ dadhyānayanaṃ tayaiva prayujyate na vājinena, tathā krayaśeṣabhūtā ekahāyanī tadā-
nayanamapi tanmukhena krayaśeṣameveti krayeṇaiva prayoktavyaṃ na padapāṃsubhiḥ । <b>ayamasti viśeṣaḥ
---tatra hi dadhyānayanamāmikṣānirvṛttisamakālameva vājinaṃ niṣpādayati । ato yuk‍taṃ
vājinaniṣpatteḥ na kāraṇāntarāpekṣā</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi dadhyānayanamābhikṣāśeṣabhūtaṃ
tathāpi yadi vājinamapi tathā bhedena niṣpadyate tadā kāraṇāpekṣāyāṃ prakṛtaṃ dadhyānayanaṃ tatrāpi
kāraṇatvena viniyujyeta । taccāmikṣaikaniṣpattikamiti na yuktastatra kāraṇāntarāpekṣayā prakṛtasya
dadhno viniyogaḥ । <b>iha punaḥ saptamaṃ padamityuk‍te bhavatyākāṅkṣā kasyeti prakṛtatvādeka-
hāyanyā iti gamyate</b> । bhinnaniṣpattikatvādatra kāraṇāntarāpekṣāyāṃ ekahāyanīmātraṃ padā-
﻿<pb n="r981"/>
pekṣitaṃ saṃbadhyate <b>ityubhayārthāṃ</b> krayapadapāṃsvarthāṃ <b>ekahāyanīṃ manyate । evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate ।
satyaṃ yadi kasyetyapekṣopapadyate</b> । tadā tasyāmākāṅkṣāyāṃ svarūpamātreṇaivaikahāyanī saṃbadhyeta
na krayaśeṣabhāveneti bhavedubhayārthā ekahāyanī । kasyeti punarihākāṅkṣaiva nāsti yasmāt
<b>anirjñātasaṃbandhyantare saṃbandhinyupadiśyamāne bhavatyākāṅkṣāpūrvikā prajñā</b> । yatra
saṃbandhyantaraṃ pūrvaṃ pratītaṃ nāsti tatra ākāṅkṣapurassarā sambandhini buddhiḥ āvirbhavati ।
<b>yatra punaḥ saṃbandhyantarapūrvaka evopadeśaḥ tatra</b> yathāvagamaṃ saṃbandhāvagamāt <b>yathā nirjñāta-
saṃbandhipurassaramevopadeśaḥ iti samarthitamaśvapratigrahe । ataḥ krayārthaiva ekahāyanī
saptamapadasaṃbandhinīti na prayujyate</b> krayārthāyā eva tasyāḥ prakṛtatvāt tathābhūtāyāḥ saṃbandhi-
tvenāvagatatvāt । <b>atra bhāṣyaṃ <q>‘prasaṅgamupajīvatā’</q> iti</b> prasaṅgaśabdaśravaṇāt bhrāmya-
taścodyam । <b>nanu cedaṃ prayojakāprayojakalakṣaṇam; kaḥ prasaṅgasyāvasaraḥ । vidyamāne hi
prayojakatve prasaṅga uktaḥ</b> <q>“evameva prasaṅgaḥ syāt vidyamāne svake vidhau”</q> iti ।
<b>iha prayok‍tṛtaiva nāstīti । ucyate---śāstraprasaṅgamaṅgīkṛtyaitraduktam na prayogaprasaṅgamitya-
doṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---aruṇayaikahāyanyā piṅgākṣyā somaṃ krīṇātīti śās‍treṇa ekahāyanyu-
pāttā । saiva śāstrāntarepi saṃbadhyate saptamaṃ padaṃ gṛhṇātīti na punaranuṣṭhānaprasaṅgo'yaṃ bhāṣya-
kāreṇokta ityadoṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r982"/>
<p><b>arthābhidhānakarma ca bhaviṣyatā । ‘puroḍāśakapālena tuṣānupavapatīṃti nātra
śāstraprasaṅgaḥ saṃbhavatīti prayok‍tṛtvaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate tuṣopavāpasyāpi । na ca
nāntarīyakaḥ śakya upavāpo vak‍tum bājinavat । tasmādubhayaṃ prayojakamiti</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---<q>‘puroḍāśakapālena tuṣānupavapati’</q> ityatra puroḍāśakapālasya sākṣādevopādānaṃ na
punaḥ prakṛtatvena grahaṇaṃ yathaikahāyanyāḥ । tena svavākye śrutaṃ puroḍāśakapālamupavāpepi
vākyena viniyujyate । nanu puroḍāśakapālamiti puroḍāśasaṃbandhikapālaṃ śrapaṇaśeṣamucyate ।
na cānyaśeṣasyānyaśeṣatvaṃ saṃbhavati । anyatra vyāpṛtasyevānyatra vyāpāraḥ । tatkathamupavāpepi
vākyena viniyogaḥ । ucyate---ekavākyatā hi guṇapradhānabhāvena vinā na nirvahati ।
tatra ca tuṣopavāpasyāgnyabhijvalanārthasya na kapālaṃ prati tāvat guṇatayā saṃbandhaḥ । kintu
kapālasyaiva taṃ prati । na ca viniyuktaviniyogavirodhaḥ adhiṣṭhānalakṣaṇayā viniyogopapatteḥ ।
viniyuktaviniyogavirodho hi 2pratipattivirodhaḥ । sa ca yadi viniyuk‍tenaiva rūpeṇa viniyo-
go'bhyupagamyate tadā syāt । yadā punaḥ viniyogopalakṣitaṃ dravyameva viniyujyate
tadā nāsti virodhaḥ । na ca nāntarīyakastuṣopavāpaḥ yena kāraṇāntarāpekṣābhāvāt
viniyogo na syāt । tasmāt viniyogāviśeṣāt ubhayaṃ prayojakamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
<b>atrābhidhīyate । satyaṃ viniyoge nāsti śāstraprasaṅgaḥ । nāpi nāntarīyaka-</b>
<note>(1) P. 1212</note> <note>(2) G. pratīti virodhaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r983"/>
<b>bhāvaḥ । kintu upāttasyāyaṃ viniyogo nopādānakalpanā kramate</b> । asyārthaḥ---puroḍāśa-
kapālamiti puroḍāśasaṃbandhitvena kapālaṃ lakṣyamāṇaṃ tadeva lakṣyate yasyaiva puroḍāśasaṃbandhā-
dhiṣṭhānatā, yathā gaṅgyā kūlaṃ lakṣyamāṇamapi svasaṃbandhitayaiva lakṣyate । tacca kapālaṃ
śrapaṇārthamupāttaṃ ityupāttaviṣayo'yaṃ viniyogaḥ । ata āha---<b>nopādānakalpanā kramata iti ।
tadidamuk‍taṃ bhaviṣyatāsaṃyogo'yaṃ na bhūtavartamānābhyāmiti</b> । bhaviṣyatā saṃyoge hi
upāttaviṣayataiva । nopādānāvakāśo'sti <b>yadi punaḥ bhūtavartamānābhyāṃ saṃbandhaḥ kimupādānaṃ
syāt</b> iti praśnamātram । <b><q>“ucyata”</q></b> ityuttaram । <b>na bhūtasya</b> saṃbandhī <b>yaḥ
tasya bhaviṣyadarthatayā anupāttasyaiva pālanaṃ bhaviṣyati pālanabhūtamevopādānaṃ yataḥ ।
vartamānasyāpi yaḥ saṃbandhī</b> tasyāpyanyatra vyāpṛtatayā<b>pyanyatra viniyogo na saṃbhavatī</b>-
tyarthādanyadupādeyam । <b>bhaviṣyadarthatve punaḥ anyārthamevopāttasya</b> svīkṛtasya dhāritavyasya
<b>viniyogaḥ saṃbhavatīti siddhamaprayojakatvam</b> । nanvevaṃ sati yatra puroḍāśaśrapaṇaṃ nāsti
vikṛtau tatra kathamupavāpaḥ puroḍāśakapālaṃ vinā kārya iti tatrāha---<b>tuṣopavāpastu kartavyo na
kartavya iti nāsyādhikaraṇasyāyaṃ viṣayaḥ</b> । sarvathā'dhikaraṇasiddhāntasiddheḥ agnihotra-
havaṇīnyāyena kartavya eveti gamyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r984"/>
<p><b>paśāvanālaṃbhāt । asminnadhikaraṇe hṛdayādyavadānavacanaṃ saṃpravyādhavacanaṃ ca
tulyaṃ prakṛtapaśuviṣayatayā <q>‘agnīṣomīyaṃ paśumālabheta’</q> iti dvayoḥ</b> prakṛtagrahaṇamiti
<b>pūrvapakṣavādī dvayorapi prayojakatāṃ manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---agnīṣomīyaṃ paśumālabheteti yadyapi
paśorevāgnīṣomīyatā āpātamātreṇa pratibhāti tathāpi viśasanaśravaṇāt paśornaṣṭatvāt paśu-
saṃbandhināṃ dravyāṇāmagnīṣomīyatā । śukṛllohite ca paśusaṃbandhinī eva । tena tayorapi
devatāsaṃbandhaḥ । yāgārthadravyaprakṛtidravyatayā ca paśoragnīṣomīyatā । na caivaṃ vācyaṃ
hṛdayādyartha eva paśuriti । yasmādubhayatrāpi prakṛtitayā paśorgrahaṇam । hṛdayādivākye ca
na sākṣācchravaṇamasti । devatāsaṃbandhācca yāgaśeṣabhūtayoreva lohitaśakṛtoḥ nirasanasaṃpravyādhau
śeṣapratiṣattibhūtau bhaviṣyataḥ । kathaṃ tarhi tayoḥ prayojakatāśaṅkā । ucyate---<b>na nirasana</b>-
sapravyādhayoḥ prayojakatvamucyate । kintu lohitaśakṛtoreva । te ca yāgārthatayā yāgārtha-
prakṛtidravyasya paśoḥ prayojake yuk‍te evetyadoṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>atrābhidhīyate---hṛdayasyāgre'vadyatīti yāgopasaṃhṛtiriyam</b> । atrābhiprāyaḥ
--- satyaṃ na paśoḥ sākṣādyāgārthatā । kintu svasaṃbandhidravyopakārakatayā paśusaṃbandhināmeva
dravyāṇāṃ sākṣādyāgārthatā । sā tu hṛdayādiṣveva upasaṃhṛtā । <b>aṅgaistṛtīyasavana iti
śravaṇāt</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । aṅgairiti śravaṇāt aṅgānāṃ tāvaccheṣatā'stīti
niścīyate । tatrāpi hṛdayādīnāṃ prākṛtakāryāvadānasaṃskāradarśanāt yāgakāryopayogitayā
﻿<pb n="r985"/>
ca tadupapatteḥ । teṣāmeva yāgārthatā nāpareṣāṃ, paśusaṃbandhināṃ lohitaśakṛtādīnāmanaṅgatvāda-
hṛdayāditvācca । <b>śakṛtsaṃpravyādhastu tāvanmātraparyavasāyitvāt</b> nirasanasaṃpravyādhayoḥ
styānarūpatvena kāryāntarānanupraveśāt । yāgārthaprakṛtapaśusaṃbandhisaṃpātāyātapratipattyarha-
<b>dravyāśrayatvāt</b> pratipattiḥ । nanu saiva dravyaṃ prayokṣyata ityāśaṅkya 1prasiddhaṃ pratipatteḥ
dravyaprayojakatvāsaṃbhavaṃ darśitavān । <b>pratipattiśca na prayojikā <q>‘na pratipādyaṃ pratipattyartha-
mupādīyate’</q> iti nyāyāt । ato na prayojakaṃ paśoḥ śakṛtādītyadhikaraṇārthoṃpasaṃhāraḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>ekadeśadravyaṃ cotpattau । nanu cātra pūrvapakṣa eva nopapadyate upāttadravya-
viṣayatvāt</b> <q>‘uttarārdhāt sviṣṭakṛte samavadyati’</q> iti (puroḍāśa) śruteḥ upāttapuroḍāśaviṣaya
evottarārdhaḥ pratīyate । sa ca kṛtakāryadravyaviśeṣa iti dravyapratipattiriyam । na ca
pratipattiḥ prayojikā । kathaṃ punaḥ upāttadravyaviṣayā ityāśaṅkyāha---<b>ikṣukhaṇḍavaccheṣāvagateḥ</b> ।
yathā <q>‘ikṣukhaṇḍamasmai prayaccha’</q> iti sannihitasyaivekṣoḥ khaṇḍaḥ pratīyate, nāsannihitasya
tathehāpīti sannihitapuroḍāśahutaśeṣāvagateḥ upāttadravyaviṣayatā । <b>satyamevam । kintu
atra puroḍāśasyānyārthatvāt</b> । āg‍neyayāgārthatvāt <b>nānyatra kāryāntare</b> sviṣṭakṛdyāge
<b>viniyoga upapadyate</b> । yāgārthena kāryāntarakaraṇe śiṣṭācāravirodhāt । prakṛtatvena
<note>(1) G. pratiṣiddham</note>
﻿<pb n="r986"/>
grahaṇe'pi puroḍāśakapālanyāyena adhiṣṭhānamātratayāpi viniyogānupapatteḥ । <b>ato dravyāntara-
mupādeyamiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । rāddhāntavādī tu na dva‍yavadānamātropasaṃhāraḥ dva‍yavadāna-
mātreṇaivāgneyayāganirvṛttimupasaṃhāramanyatra viniyogopapattyarthamupanyastavān</b> iti । atra
ko'bhiprāyaḥ । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---satyaṃ dva‍yavadānamātreṇaiva yāgo nirvartitaḥ na punaḥ puroḍāśasya
tādarthyaṃ nirvartitam । yasmāt dva‍yavadānārthamapi yāgārthameva । tasmādidamuttaraṃ dattavān ।
satyam । śiṣṭācāravirodhaḥ syāt <b>yadyanyasmai dīyate dīyamānaṃ hi tadā saṃpradānārthamiti
tannopapadyate । tasmānna yāgakāryadanyatra viniyogassaṃbhavati । yāgakāryatayā punaḥ
nānyārthatā śakyate vak‍tum</b> । āgneyādiyāgaḥ kāryo yasya tasya bhāvastattā tayā nānyārthatā
śakyate vak‍tum yāgārthā ca pratipattiḥ । tadīyadravyapratipādanadvāreṇa devadattaśiraso'vatāri-
tāyāḥ sraja iva śucideśanidhānaṃ devadattārtham । <b>ato nāgneyādicodanāyā virodhaḥ
1ato'pratipakṣekṣukhaṇḍanyāyenānupādānaṃ siddham । śeṣadarśanāt</b> śeṣātsviṣṭakṛte sama-
vadyatīti । <b>tathā samavadānaśrutirityuk‍taṃ bhāṣye</b> ।</p>
<p><b>abhidhāraṇe । kiṃ punaḥ puroḍāśakapālenātra viśiṣyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---bhavatva-
<note>(1) G. tasmāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r987"/>
bhidhāraṇaṃ pradhānabhūtānāṃ haviṣāmarthakarma । tathāpi prayājārthamupāttasya śeṣasya śravaṇāt
dravyāntaraṃ nopādeyam । yathā puroḍāśakapāleneti śruteḥ kapālāntaramupādīyate artha-
karmatve'pi । tasmāt prayojane viśeṣābhāvāt nārabdhavyamidamadhikaraṇamiti । pariharati
---<b>dravyopādānaṃ tāvat tadvannāstīti sthitameva dhāraṇasya tūpādānaṃ haviṣaḥ prādhānyānnā-
nyārthatayā1 virudhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---tatra bhaviṣyadarthatvāt kapālānā-
mupādānaṃ dhāraṇaṃ ca na prayuñjītaivopavāpaḥ; prayājaśeṣasya tu bhūtaprayojanasaṃbandhitvāt yadyapi
kapāladravyaṃ nopādeyaṃ tathāpi prayājaiḥ pariniṣpannaiḥ dhāraṇasyāprayuktatvāt anyārthadravyasyāpi
arthakarmapakṣe haviṣāṃ prādhānyāt dhāraṇaprayuktiḥ na virudhyate । prādhānye hi haviṣo yadeva
haviḥ nābhidhāryate tasyaiva saṃskāraparilopaḥ syāditi yuktameva dhāraṇam । tatsidhyarthaṃ ca
pātrāntaramupādeyamiti ।</p>
<p><b>kathaṃ punarhaviṣaḥ prādhānyaṃ dvitīyāśravaṇādabhidhāraṇasya tadarthatvāt prayājaśeṣasya
ca puroḍāśakapālavat tadarthatvāt</b> । na ca viniyuktaviniyogavirodhaḥ । 2prayājopala-
kṣitadravyasyādhiṣṭhānarūpasya puroḍāśakapālavat viniyogopapatteḥ <b>siddhāntastu na prādhānyaṃ
haviṣāṃ dṛṣṭārthatayā ājyasyaiveti yuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi havīṃṣyabhidhārayatīti
śrūyate tathāpi haviṣāṃ prādhānyaṃ na yuktam tadarthatve'bhidhāraṇasyādṛṣṭārthatvaprasaṅgāt । prayāja-
śeṣasyaiva tu prādhānyaṃ dṛṣṭārthatvāt pātre3virik‍te dṛṣṭaṃ prayojanaṃ ājyabhāgārthenāsaṃsparśaḥ ।
<note>(1) G. nānyārthayāḥ</note> <note>(2) G. prayojakopala</note> <note>(3) G. pātrepi rik‍te</note>
﻿<pb n="r988"/>
<b>tasmāt pratipattireveyaṃ prayājaśeṣasyeti । kathaṃ tarhi havīṃṣyabhidhārayatīti bahuvacanam</b> ।
<b>ekena haviṣā'bhidhāraṇanirvṛtteḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi dṛṣṭārthatayā ājyasyaiveyamabhidhāraṇena
pratipattiḥ tarhi tasyā ekenāpi haviṣā siddhatvāt bahuvacanaṃ kathamupapadyate ।
ekatrābhidhāryamāṇaṃ sarvamevābhidhṛtaṃ syāt । na hi tadā dravyasya
dhāraṇaṃ prayoktavyam । abhidhṛtaṃ ca na havirantare'bhidhārayituṃ śakyate iti ।
atrottaraṃ---<b>agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt bahuvacanamaviruddham</b> । satyamekenāpi haviṣā
pratipattiḥ siddha‍yati । tat‍tu na jñāyate <q>‘kiṃ tat’</q> iti । santi cātra bahūni havīṃṣi ।
tasmādabhidhāraṇe bahuvacanamaviruddham । paryāyeṇa yatra tatra pratipattiḥ kariṣyate <b>ato dravyo-
pādānavat dhāraṇopādānamapi na yuktam sannihita eva habiṣi pratipattisiddheriti</b>
siddhāntopasaṃhāraḥ ।</p>
<p><b>nanu ca dvitīyātṛtīyayoranyarthatā grahītuṃ na śakyā, yathārthatayāpi vacanā-
virodhāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---na dṛṣṭārthatvamātrabalena vibhaktidbayasyāyathārthatvaṃ kalpayituṃ śavayaṃ1
yasmādviniyogānusāri prayojanam । tatra yadi dṛṣṭaṃ na saṃbhavati mā sambhavatu adṛṣṭameva
prayojanaṃ viniyogabalādāśrayituṃ nyāyyam । <b>satyaṃ yadyavirodho vacanasya syāt । iha tu</b>
<note>(1) R. tasmāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r989"/>
<b>prayājaśeṣaśabdena virudhyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---nahyanyārthatvenānyaśeṣatopapadyate viniyuktaviniyoga-
virodhāt । atha mābhūdviniyuktaviniyogavirodha ityadhiṣṭhānamātraṃ lakṣyate tathāpi upalakṣaṇamātraṃ
prayājāḥ2 syuḥ puroḍāśakapālavat । yathā puroḍāśakapāle upalakṣaṇamātraṃ puroḍāśaḥ tathā
atrāpi prayājāḥ syuḥ । na caitadyuk‍tam, anupalakṣaṇārthatve saṃbhavati upalakṣaṇamātratvānupapatteḥ
puroḍāśakapāle tu gatyantarābhāvādyuktam । iha tu saṃbhavati gatiḥ mukhyaprātipadikānvayāhānāt
tadāha---<b>pratipattau punaḥ nāyaṃ virodha iti prātipadikārthānurodhinī guṇabhūtārthavādinī
vibhaktiriti</b> yuk‍tamanyārthatvam, dvitīyārthe vyatyayena tṛtīyeti yāvat । sthite cātra
prātipadikānurodhena vibhaktyarthadarśa/?/ne pāśādhikaraṇe ubhayārthānugrahāya utkarṣa āśaṅkitaḥ prāti-
padikārthaliṅgabalīyastvena nirākṛta iti । tṛtīyārthānavagamāt havīṃṣītyapi nāñjaso'rthaḥ
saṃbhavatīti । <b>atrāpyanyārthataiva nyāyyā dvayoḥ karmaṇorekasmin vākye saṃbandhāt ।
saṃbandhānuguṇaḥ saptamyartho draṣṭavyaḥ । darśamuk‍tam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>samānayanaṃ tu mukhyaṃ syāt</b> । atra bhāṣyakāraḥ <q>‘kiṃ samānayanāmālyasya dharmāṇāṃ
caprayojakaṃ’</q> iti vicārayati । tatra kāraṇasandehaṃ ṭīkākāro darśayati---<b><q>‘atihāyeḍo
barhiḥ prati samānayate’</q> ityatra sandehaḥ । kimuparitanaprayājadvayārthamevedaṃ samānayanaṃ</b>
<note>(1) P. 1216</note> <note>(2) prayājasya</note>
﻿<pb n="r990"/>
<b>tataścaupabhṛtasya ājyasya prayājānūyājārthasya taddharmāṇāṃ ca prayojakaṃ utamiśrī-
karaṇārthamevedaṃ jauhavasaṃskārārtham । tataśca paraprayuk‍tadravyasādhyatvādaprayojakamānyasya
dharmāṇāṃ ceti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī samānayanamātraśravaṇānmiśrīkaraṇamātraṃ manyate ।
aṣṭāvupabhṛti gṛhṇātīti ca sarvaprayājārthatāṃ manyate । kutaḥ ? viśeṣāśravaṇāt tasmāda-
dṛṣṭārthamevedaṃ samānayanamiti</b> । asyārthaḥ---uparitanaprayājadvayaṃ yaṣṭumityevaṃ tāvanna śrūyate
tatra na śakyate tadarthataiveti vak‍tum । yadi caupabhṛtasya grahaṇasyoparitanaprayājadvayārthatā
avagatā syāt tadā tasmin yakṣyamāṇe idamapi samānayanaṃ tadarthamiti gṛhyatāpi । na caivaṃ
śrūyate । kintu sarvaprayājārthatā । sā ca yadyadṛṣṭārthaṃ samānayanaṃ tadā saṃbhavati miśrīkaraṇena
hi jauhavadravyaṃ saṃskriyate । tacca sarveṣāṃ kṛtānāṃ kariṣyamāṇayośca iti tatsaṃskārārthatvādyuk‍tā
sarvārthatā । itarathā tu dvayārthatā syāt na ca sā yuktā । tasmādadṛṣṭārthaṃ samānayanam ।
<b>evaṃ prāpte abhidhīyate । prayājadvayasādhanārthamevedaṃ samānayanam । kutaḥ ? evaṃ
dṛṣṭārthatā samānayanasya bhavati upabhṛti ca prayājārthasya grahaṇasya</b> । asyāthaḥ---yadyapi
samānayanamātraṃ śrutaṃ, tathāpi prayojanākāṅkṣāyāṃ cikīrṣitaprayājadvayanirvṛttireva prayojanaṃ yuktam
dṛṣṭārthatvāt, na punaḥ adṛṣṭasaṃskāraḥ pramāṇābhāvāt । dṛṣṭenaiva nirākāṅkṣatvāt । tathopabhṛti
﻿<pb n="r991"/>
ca yad‍grahaṇaṃ tadeva dṛṣṭārthaṃ bhaviṣyati anyathā 1adṛṣṭasaṃskāradvāreṇa praṇājārthatve 2adṛṣṭārthaṃ syāt
<b>nanu cāviśeṣeṇa tadaupabhṛtaṃ sarvārthaṃ śrūyate śrutānusāreṇa cādṛṣṭārthatāpi nyāyyā</b> ।
atrottaraṃ---<b>nāviśeṣaśrutiḥ sāmarthyena viśeṣe'vasthāpyamānā śabdārthatāṃ jahāti</b> । yadi
viśeṣe'vasthāpyamānā uparitanaprayājadvaye sāmānyā prayāja(dvaya)śrutiḥ śabdārthatāṃ jahyāt tadā
adṛṣṭamapi kalpyeta । na caivaṃ, uparitanamapi prayājadvayaṃ prayājaśabdavācyameva । <b>tasmāt
śabdasya apratirodhitvāt dṛṣṭe saṃbhavatyadṛṣṭakalpanā na nyāyyeti rāddhāntaḥ । darśanā---
muktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>tatrotpattiravibhaktā syāt</b> । nanu ca jauhavasya kevalaprayājārthatvaśravaṇe ubhayārthatā
na yuk‍tetyāha---<b>kaḥ punaratra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥubhayamubhayārthamiti vadata iti ।
ayamabhiprāyaḥ---aviśeṣeṇa śravaṇāt caturjuhvāṃ gṛhṇāti iti । viśeṣataśca kāryasiddheḥ
prayājagrahaṇamanūyājavannityānuvādaṃ manyate jauhave</b> । yathopabhṛti anūyājagrahaṇaṃ nityānu-
<note>(1) G. dṛṣṭa</note> <note>(2) G. dṛṣṭārthaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r992"/>
vādaḥ tathā jauhave prayājagrahaṇamapi syāt । atha kevalaprayājaśravaṇāt prayājārthatā 1tarhi
aupabhṛtasya kevalānūyājaśravaṇāt anūyājārthataiva syāditi pratibandhena pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
<b>atrocyate---yadyupādānata eva prāptiḥ syāt, syādetadevaṃ upādānamātrādubhayārthatā
pratīteḥ</b> । yāvatā viniyogānusāryupādānamityuktam viniyogaśca prayājaviniyogamātrārtha eva
jauhavaḥ । idānīṃ pūrvoṃktapratibandhāśayamāviṣkaroti---<b>evaṃ tarhi anūyājārthamevaupabhṛtaṃ bhavatu
kevalānūyājārthaśravaṇāt । ucyate---prāptārthatvādasya viniyojakasya kevalānūyāja---
saṃbandhino'nuvādaṃ: manyate । kutaḥ prāptiḥ ?</b> uttaraṃ---<b>prayājānūyājebhyastadgṛhṇātītyu-
bhayārthatvāt । nanu samānayanādhikaraṇe sthite kathamidānīmāśaṅkyate । tatra hi
uparitanaprayājārthamaupabhṛtaṃ samānīyata iti vadatā ubhayārthatvamuktam । kathaṃ kevalānū-
yājārthatā śaṅkyate । ucyate---sthita etasmiṃstadbhavati । anyathā'dṛṣṭārthameva samāna-
yanaṃ saṃskāramātraṃ syāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---asminnadhikaraṇe ubhayārthatve sthite tatra siddhānta-
lābhaḥ anyathā kevalānūyājārthatve aupabhṛtasya samānīyamānasya prayājārthatvānavagamāt jauhavameva
sarvaprayājārthaṃ syāt । tataścārthādadṛṣṭārthaṃ samānayanaṃ saṃskāramātraṃ syāta । yata evaita(ka)-
<note>(1) G. nahi</note>
﻿<pb n="r993"/>
sminnadhikaraṇe sthite tadadhikaraṇasiddhāntalābhaḥ, ata evaivaṃ ca samānayanaṃ dṛṣṭārthaṃ bhavatītī-
hopanyāsaḥ ।</p>
<p>tadaṣṭasaṅkhyaṃ <b>śravaṇāt</b> । atra bhāṣye kimaupabhṛtamaṣṭasaṅkhyena grahaṇena saṃskiyate uta
catussaṃkhyā guṇabhūtā dvayorgrahaṇayoriti saṃśayo'sti । tatra phalasaṃśayaṃ ṭīkākāraḥ karoti
---<b>aṣṭāvupabhṛti gṛhṇātīti śrūyate । atra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ dve ete caturgṛhīte utāṣṭagṛhīta-
mekamevedamiti । nanu samānayanādhikaraṇe idamuk‍taṃ dvau prayājau yaṣ‍ṭumekamidaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ 
samānīyata iti । kayā yuktyā ? evaṃ ca dṛṣṭārthatā bhaviṣyatītyanayā yuktyetyarthaḥ
tadevedamākṣipyate aṣṭasaṃkhyāśravaṇāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi dve caturgṛhīte prayājānūyājārthe
upabhṛti syātāṃ tadā yadevātra prayājārthaṃ tasyaiva tatsamānayanaṃ ca yadi bhavati tadā dṛṣṭārthatā
bhavati iti samānayanādhikaraṇasiddhānto bhavati । yadā punaḥ aṣṭagṛhītamekamidaṃ tadā
yatsamānīyate tanmātrasya prayājārthatā'navagatā । yāvataścāṣṭagṛhītasyāvagatā na tāvatsamānī-
yata iti noparitanaprayājārthamidaṃ samānayanaṃ syāt । nanvevamadṛṣṭārthaṃ samānayanaṃ syādityatrāha
---<b>dṛṣṭārthatā ca samānayanasyopapadyata eva । ādhāre prācīne prayājatraye ca vyāpṛtasya
jauhavasyājyasya svakāryaṃ pratyaśak‍tasyānugrahāya samānīyata iti । ato'tra</b>
<note>(1) Bh. P.1222</note>
﻿<pb n="r994"/>
<b>pūrvapakṣavādī śrutatvādaṣṭasaṅkhyākameva grahaṇamiti manyate । rāddhāntastu bhinnaviṣayatvāt
catussaṅkhyāṣṭasaṅkhyayoḥ nānyatarasyāprāptiḥ śakyate varṇayitum</b> । asyārthaḥ---caturavattaṃ
juhotīti home catussaṅkhyā śrūyate । <q>‘aṣṭāvupabhṛti gṛhṇāti’</q> iti ca aṣṭasaṅkhyā grahaṇe ।
tena bhinnaviṣayatvāt virodhābhāvāt ubhayamapi viniyujyate । na ca homārthatvād‍grahaṇasya
tulyārthatāṃ prāpya virodho vak‍tuṃ śakyate, yasmāt grahaṇe'ṣṭasaṅkhyā śrutā home catussaṅkhyā-
niṣpādakatayā śakyate vak‍tumiti avirodhāt nānyataratyāprāptiḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ aṣṭa-
saṅkhyā catussaṅkhyāṃ niṣpādayati । uttaraṃ---<b>home yasmāt dve ete caturgṛhīte saṃyoginī
prayājānūyājebhya ityubhayārthatvena viniyogāt । ubhayośca dvābhyāṃ caturgṛhītābhyāṃ
prayojanamaṣṭagrahaṇena saṃpādyate । aṣṭāvupabhṛti guhṇātīti । dve ete caturgṛhīte iti
darśanaṃ ca pūrvavat samarthitaṃ bhavati</b> । yaddarśanaṃ caturgṛhītabahutvasya yat tatsamarthitaṃ bhavati
prayojanaṃ ca pūrvoṃk‍taṃ samānayanasya1 samarthitaṃ bhavati tataścāñjasameba dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ bhavet ।

﻿<pb n="r995"/>
anyathā kathañcit alpadravyānugrāhakatvena syāt anūyājābhāve cānūyājārthaikacaturgṛhītābhāve
caturgṛhītadvayārthāyā aṣṭasaṅkhyāyā anupayogācca । <b>caturgṛhītānyājyāni bhavantīti hetuva-
nnigadaśca samarthito bhavati</b> ।</p>

<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>svarustvanekaniṣpattiḥ</b> । nanvatra eka eva viṣayaḥ saṃśayo vicāraḥ nirṇayaḥ prayojanaṃ
cādhikaraṇadvaye'pi dṛśyata iti kathamadhikaraṇabhedaḥ tatrāha---<b>ekamatrādhikaraṇaṃ vākyāntarābhi-
prāyeṇa varṇitam । dvitīyastvekavākyamaṅgīkṛtya । yuktayastvekavākyavicāre vākyāntarā-
pekṣiṇyāṃ ca mīmāṃsāyāṃ tulyā iti pradarśitam</b> । asyārthaḥ---prathame'dhikaraṇe <q>‘yūpasya
svaruṃ karoti’</q> iti <q>‘svaruṇā paśumanakti’</q> iti ca vākyadvayamudāhṛtya cintitam । kiṃ kiṃ-
pūrvakamiti । kiṃ yūpasya svaruṃ karotītyetatpūrvakamiṃda svaruṇā paśumanak‍tīti, atha vā
viparītamiti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī yūpasya svaruṃ karotītyetatpūrvakaṃ svaruṇā paśumanak‍tītyāha
---<b>yuktiśca śrutyā vidhānam</b> yadi svarukartavyatā vidhīyate śrutyā vidhānaṃ bhavati itarathā
vākyena vidhānaṃ syāt । yadā hi svaruṇā paśumanaktīti viniyogaḥ pūrvabhāvī syāta tadā
añjanakāryakāritayaiva svaruśabdo vartate tadā ca yūpasya svaruṃ karotītyasya vacanasyāyamarthaḥ
saṃpadyate---yo'sāvañjanakāryakāritayā prāptaḥ svaruḥ sa yūpasya grahītavya iti । evaṃ ca
yūpasaṃbandhavidhiparatvādvākyasya vākyena vidhānaṃ syāt । śrutiśca vākyādbalīyasī tataśca
svarukartavyataiva vidhīyate । yūpasyeti yūpakāṣṭhasya khadirāderityarthaḥ । tathā ca jo/?/ṣaṇādi-
kamapi svarūtpādakatayā saṃbadhyate । nanvetadayuktam yasmāt <q>‘yūpaṃ joṣayati’</q> <q>‘yūpaṃ chinatti’</q>
﻿<pb n="r997"/>
<q>‘yūpaṃ takṣati’</q> iti yūpasaṃbandha eva joṣaṇāderavagamyate na svarusaṃbandhaḥ । ucyate---yūpaṃ
joṣayatītyāderayamarthaḥ khadirādi joṣayati yūpaṃ kartuṃ iti, na punaḥ prāk‌siddhaṃ yūpaṃ joṣayatīti ।
tatra ca nāparaṃ yūpaṃ kartumiti viśeṣaṇaṃ vivakṣituṃ nyāyyam vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt । kintu kāryārtha-
tvātsaṃskārasya1 kāryadvayasya yūpasvarvātmakasyaikakaisya prakṛtitvāt tadarthameva joṣaṇādikaṃ
khadirāderavagamyate । ataśca yūpaśabdaḥ prakṛtakāryapradarśanārtha eva syāt । tenāyamarthaḥ saṃpadyate
---joṣaṇādibhiḥ khadirādayo yūpībhavanti svarurbhavanti ceti । atra ca pakṣe viśiṣṭotpatti-
nibandhanaḥ svaruśabdaḥ । tena svaruḥ pṛthagutpattiṃ prayojayatīti manyate । jātyantarāśaṅkā-
vacanamapyevamevopapadyate । tataśca yūpaśabdaḥ prakṛtakāryapradarśanārtha eva syāt nānyatheti ।
siddhāntī tu svaruṇā paśumanaktītyetatpūrvakamidaṃ yūpasya svaruṃ karotīti manyate, yasmāt yūpasya
svaruṃ karoti iti yūpasaṃbandhaḥ svaruḥ śrūyate । na ca yūpena saha prakṛtivikārabhāvo ghaṭate
yūpanāśaprasaṅgāt । na ca yūpakārakāṇi khadirādīni yūpaśabdena lakṣayitvā 2svaruprakṛtitā
yūpasyeti bhaviṣyatīti śakyate vak‍tum । lakṣaṇāprasaṅgāt । tasmād‍yūpaśabdasya śrautānvaya-
paryālocanayā svaruṇā paśumanaktīti viniyogapūrvakamidaṃ yūpasya svaruṃ karotīti । tatra ca pakṣe
añjanakāritayaiva svarutvasiddheḥ svarustāvanna kartavyaḥ kintu kimīyena añjanaṃ kartavyamityapekṣāyāṃ
yūpasyeti vidhīyate3 sa kathaṃ yūpasya bhavati yūpamanuniṣpadyata iti । tataśca svarukartavyatāyā-
macoditāyāṃ khadirādisaṃbandhaṃ ca4 joṣaṇadikaṃ yūpasyaiva śeṣa iti yūpa eva prayojakaḥ svarustvaprayo-
jakaḥ । śakalaśruteśca svarurekadeśabhūtaḥ vidyamāne cāvayavini nāvayavinaṃ prayuṅk‍te । asmiṃśca pakṣe
karotiḥ upādāne vartate upādāne ca karoteḥ mukhyārthataiva yathā kāṣṭhān kurviti । tadevamidamiha
vicāryate---kiṃ śrutyarthavidhānabalena lakṣaṇā'stu uta lakṣaṇāparihārāya vākyārthavidhānamiti ।
tatra pūrvapakṣavādī śrutividhānameva balīyaḥ pratyakṣatvāt vākyasya vyavahitānvaye parokṣaṃ kalpanīya-
mityāha । rāddhāntī tu syādetadevaṃ yadi vyavahitānvayaḥ syāt । kintu bhāvārtha eva
vidhiḥ prāptāprāptavivekena guṇavidhirityucyate । tena vākyārthavidhānepi vyavahitānvayo
nāstīti lakṣaṇā na nyāyyeti manyate । jātyantarāśaṅkā tu prāgetasmāt anuniṣpannagrahaṇa-

vidhīyate tayā</note> <note>(4) G. na joṣaṇādikāryotpattiḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r998"/>
vidhistutaye । pratiyūpaṃ svarudarśanaṃ ca liṅgamuktam । dvitīye tvadhikaraṇe svaruṇā paśuma-
naktītyetadeva vākyamudāhṛtya cintitam । yo'yaṃ svaruḥ añjane viniyujyate sa kiṃ
utpādyaḥ utopādeya iti । tatra tathaiva śrutividhānabalāt utpādya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । tathaiva
yūpasaṃbandhasyotpādakatayā'nupapatteḥ yūpakāṣṭhalakṣaṇāyāṃ ca lakṣaṇaiva doṣaḥ । tasmādyūpānuniṣpanna-
evopādeya iti rāddhāntaḥ । abhyuccayayuktayaśca pūrvottarapakṣayostā eva । ādāne ca
karoterapi pravṛttiriti tathaiva rāddhānta iti yuktam । yuktayastulyā ubhayorapyadhikaraṇayoḥ ।
viṣayabhedāt saṃśayaprakārabhedāccādhikaraṇabhedaḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati---yadi vākyadvayāṅgīkāreṇa
paurvāparyavimarśaḥ kriyate tathāpi svaruraprayojakaḥ । atha ekavākyāśrayaṇenopādānavimarśaḥ
tathāpi svaroraprayojakataiveti ।</p>
<p><b>śākhāyāṃ tatpradhānatvāt । kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamasmin prayojakāprayojaka-

<p><b>utpattyasaṃyogāt । apaḥ praṇayatīti kāryadvayāsaṃbandhamapāṃ praṇayanamutpannam ।

praṇayanotpantau saṃyavanaṃ ninayanaṃ ca kāryaṃ na śrutaṃ paścāt‍tu dvayaṃ śrūyata iti dvayorapi prayojakatāṃ
manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । <b>nanu ca <q>‘apo ninayati’</q> iti dvitīyā śrūyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
---dvitīyāśravaṇādapāṃ prādhānyam । ninayanaṃ ca tatpratipattyarthameva । saṃyavane tṛtīyāśravaṇāt
guṇabhāva eveti tadeva prayojakamityabhiprāyaḥ । atrottaraṃ---<b>anīpsitatvāt kārakamātre
bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ</b> iti । tathā yuktaṃ cānīṣsitamityanīpsitakarmaṇi dvitīyetyarthaḥ ।
kathaṃ punaranīpsitatvamucyate sarbā evātra pratipattayaḥ udāharaṇam । tatredaṃ cintyate kimupa-
yuktasyāpi dravyasya cikīrṣitatvaṃ saṃbhavati neti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī manyate dravyaṃ hi kriyāyā
upakaroti iti cikīrṣitaṃ bhavati । yatpunaḥ kṛtaprayojanaṃ tasya kimarthā cikīrṣā ।
tasmādarthakarmaivedaṃ ninayanam । tatra cāpāṃ karaṇabhūtānāmapi kriyājanyaphalabhāgitā astīti
anīpsitakarmatayā tathāyuktamiti dvitīyeti । <b>atrocyate---nānīpsitatve heturasti
kṛtaprayojanamapi hi tat pratipādyatayā iṣyata eva</b> । atrābhiprāyaḥ---yadyapi pratipattiṣu
kṛtaprayojanaṃ dravyaṃ tathāpi cikīrṣā ghaṭata eva---kimidaṃ saṃprati kriyatāṃ ? upekṣyatāṃ, yadi vā
taddeśāntare tyajyatām ? iti । etat‍tu loke'pi pratītameva । tathā lokavadvedepi vyavahāraḥ
tatra yadyasya śrūyate tat 2tatsāpekṣaṃ svīkriyate । śrūyate cātrāpāṃ tāvadantarvedideśaninayanam ।
<note>(1) P. 1235</note> <note>(2) G. tasyāpekṣitaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1006"/>
na ca tadanupayogitayā2 na nirvahati, kṛtakṛtyasaṃskārasyāpi loke dṛṣṭatvāt । yathā devadatta-
śiraso'vatāritāyāḥ srajaḥ śucideśanidhānam । tatra ca devadattasaṃskārameva laukikā
manyante । tathehāpi śeṣiṇaḥ saṃskāro bhaviṣyatīti kalpyate । nanu cānīpsite'pi
kriyājanyaphalasaṃbandhāvyabhicārāt tāvanmātrameva dvitīyārtho nyāyyaḥ nepsitatvaṃ, vyabhicārāt ।
tataśca mukhyārthatve kuta etadavagamyate anīpsite karmaṇi neyaṃ dvitīyeti tatrāha---<b>na cepsite
saṃbhavati anīpsitāśrayaṇamupapadyate, tatpurassarāvagateḥ</b> । yadyapyubhayatra dvitīyā mukhyārthā
tathāpi sarvatra kriyāyāḥ prayojanākāṅkṣitvāt tādarthyaṃ tāvat kvacidvaktavyam । tatra yadeva
tajjanyaṃ dṛśyate tadeva prathamopanipātīti prayojanamavabhāti । yacca prayojanaṃ tadeva tayā
kriyayepsitamiti īpsitatvameva pūrvāvagamyamānamapekṣitatāṃ yātīti tattyāgena nāparaṃ parikalpyate
tasmāt tatpurassaraṃ prathamaṃ yasyāḥ 3tādṛśyā avagateḥ hetorityarthaḥ । <b>tasmāt saṃyavane
kṛtārthānāmapāṃ pratipattireva ninayanamiti siddhamaprayok‍tṛtvam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>prāsanavanmaitrāvaruṇasya । <q>‘maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṃ prayacchati’</q> iti pratipattirapāmi-
veti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । yajamānadhāraṇe kṛtārthatvāt daṇḍasya maitrāvaruṇadhāraṇaṃ pratipattireva daṇḍasya
dvitīyānirdeśāt । <b>nanu ca karmaṇā yamabhipraiti sa saṃpradānamiti siddho guṇabhāvaḥ</b> ।
<note>(1) P. 1236</note> <note>(2) R. na vā instead of tayā</note> <note>(3) G. tasyāḥ
tādarthyāvagateḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1007"/>
<b>sasaṃpradānake karmaṇi । asyārthaḥ</b>---karmaṇeti karaṇabhāvasmaraṇāt yatra saṃpradānamasti tatra
karmaṇo guṇabhāvaḥ । tena na prādhānyaṃ daṇḍasyeti neyaṃ pratipattiḥ । atrottaraṃ---<b>saṃpradānaga-
prītyutpādakatayaiva karmaṇo guṇabhāvaḥ । na punaḥ karmāntarasādhyatayā, karmabhāvānupapatteḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---na dānaṃ pratīdaṃ karaṇaṃ kintu saṃpradānaprītyutpattau । yadi hi dāne'pi
karaṇatā syāt tadā karmabhāvo na bhavet । tasmāt dānaṃ prati karmatvāt tatprati prādhānyāt
dānaṃ pratipattireva yuk‍teti karmāntaraṃ dīkṣitadhāraṇāt dānaṃ tatsādhyaṃ yasya tat tathok‍taṃ tasya
bhāvastattā 1tayā punarna guṇabhāvaḥ । sthite pūrvapakṣe codayati---<b>kathaṃ tarhi <q>‘daṇḍī praiṣānanvāha’</q>
ityevamādidarśanam ?</b> atrāyamabhiprāyaḥ---yadīdaṃ maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍadānaṃ syāt tadā
tādarthyameva dānasya syāt । tacca tādarthyamevaṃ bhavati yadi dīyamāno daṇḍaḥ kāryaṃ kurvāṇasya
sāhāyye vartate tena 2yāvatpradhānaṃ dhāraṇamupapadyeta । daṇḍārthe tu dāne maitrāvaruṇagamanamātreṇaiva
kṛtaḥ śāstrārthaḥ iti daṇḍo na dhāryeta tadā tatpraiṣeṣu daṇḍadarśanaṃ nopapadyata iti । uttaraṃ
---<b>yadṛcchayā prāptasyāyamanuvādaḥ</b> । yadṛcchayā prayojanāntaranirapekṣaṃ kriyāmātraṃ loke bahula-
mupalabhyate 3tathā dhṛtasya daṇḍasyedaṃ darśanaṃ bhaviṣyati । nyāyataḥ pratipattau sthitāyāmityarthaḥ ।
atrābhidhīyate---<b>maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṃ iti vyapadeśāt daṇḍī praiṣānanvāheti ca darśanāt
arthakarmaivedaṃ na pratipattiḥ</b> । atrābhiprāyaḥ---dvitīyātastāvat śabdārthatayā tādarthyameva na
pratīyate । kintu kriyājanyaphalabhāgitā । sāpi maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍadāne na viruddhā ।
<note>(1) R. tatpratyayaḥ tena na guṇabhāvaḥ</note> <note>(2) G. yāvatprāsanaṃ</note> <note>(3) G. tadvadetasyedaṃ
daṇḍasya</note>
﻿<pb n="r1008"/>
prathamāvagatatvena tādarthyasvīkāra ityuktam । sa cāpratipakṣe śabde । atra tu maitrāvaruṇa-
ṇāya daṇḍa iti vyapadeśo virudhyate । yasmādatra vyapadeśe maitrāvaruṇaprādhānyaṃ pratīyate ।
itthaṃ ca tatprādhānyaṃ bhavati yadi tadarthaṃ dānaṃ, tathā ca pūrvoktanītyā daṇḍī praiṣāniti ca darśanāt
arthakarmatā'vasīyate । tasmādanīpsitadvitīyeyamiti yuktam । <b>nanu ca yadṛcchayā prāpta-
syāyamanuvāda ityuk‍tam । ayameva doṣaḥ pākṣikatvaprasaṅgāt</b> nityavacchravaṇavirodhaḥ
syāt । <b>kathaṃ tarhi dvitīyā ? tathā yuk‍taṃ cānīpsitamityuktam । tadayuk‍tamiva prati-
bhāti । 1anupādeyaṃ hi tatrodāhṛtam</b> ahiṃ laṅghayati kaṇṭakān mṛdnāti iti । upādeyaśca
daṇḍo dātuṃ yajamānenaiva dhāryamāṇatvāt । pratipattāvevānupādeyatvāt2 dvitīyopapattiriti bhāvaḥ ।
<b>tathā ca sak‍tuṣu vibhaktivyatyaya uktaḥ upādeyatvāt anīpsitatvaṃ na bhavati</b> । upādeyaṃ
hi kriyāsidhyarthamīpsitameveti । ucyate---3<b>suṣṭhūk‍taṃ sak‍tuṣu,</b> homārthaṃ hi tatropādānam
<b>iha tu na prayacchatyarthamupādānam । upāttameva hi prayacchati । atastathāyuktamevedaṃ karma
nepsitaṃ nāpi vibhaktyantarayogyam</b> । yajamānadhāraṇārthameva hi daṇḍa upāttaḥ pratīyata
ityanupādeyatā । etacca parihāravibhabamātreṇoktam । paramārthatastu yatra sūtre anīpsita-
śabdena kriyānirvartyamabhipretaṃ na punastatkriyārthatvena hyanupāttamanīpsitaṃ, na cātra kriyāyā
<note>(1) G. anuvādoyaṃ</note> <note>(2) yāvadupādeyatvāt</note> <note>(3) R. yuktaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1009"/>
daṇḍa īpsitaḥ prayacchaterarthakarmatvāt । ata eva gāṃ dadātīti 2gordānārthatvenopādāne'pi
dvitīyopapattiḥ । atrāpi yadyapi ca daṇḍasyopāddānaṃ na prayujyate dhāraṇaṃ tvavaśyaṃ prayoktavyaṃ
ityupādeyatvamaparihāryam sak‍tuṣu tu tathā yuktatā nāstīti vyatyaya uktaḥ । yasmāt na
tasmin bhasmībhāvo homāt kintu upādhibhūtāseṃcanāditi dvitīye darśitam । <b>kiṃ punardhāraṇa
meva prayujyate utotpattirapīti cintāntarametat</b> । asti tāvat prayok‍tṛtvamiti
rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>utpattau yena saṃyuktam । adhikaraṇāntaramuktamiti</b> । asyārthaḥ---idamadhikaraṇaṃ
bhāṣya evoktam । tatra ca siddhānte kṛtārthatvābhidhānāt pūrvapakṣe akṛtārthatā'bhimateti gagyate ।
pūrvapakṣavādī evaṃ manyate sakalaprayogānta eva kṛtārthatā viṣāṇāyāḥ । prayogamadhye punaḥ
kaṇḍūyanasya saṃbhavāt akṛtārthatayā na pratipattarhā । tena cātvālaprāsanaṃ na pratipattiḥ
kintvarthakarmaivedam । ucyate---nītāsu dakṣiṇāsu cātvāle kṛṣṇāviṣāṇāṃ prāsyatīti śrutam ।
tena prāgeva kaṇḍūyanaṃ kṛṣṇaviṣāṇayā kāryāmiti rāddhāntaḥ । nanu 3aviśeṣaśrutaṃ kathaṃ
viśeṣe'vatiṣṭhate । pratipattividhānāditi cet na, itaretarāśrayāpatteḥ । maivam ।
dvitīyāśravaṇena pratipatteranyatassiddheḥ ।</p>
<p><b>saumike ca kṛtārthatvāt</b> । pūrvapakṣamākṣipati---<b>kaḥ punaratra prayājaśeṣeṇa viśeṣaḥ ?</b>
yathā prayājaśeṣeṇetyasatyāmapi dvitīyāyāṃ prayājaśeṣasya pratipattiḥ । evamatrāpi yatkiñcitsoma-
liptaṃ tenāvabhṛthaṃ yantīti pratipattireva yuktā । samādhānamāha---<b>nanu ca prayājaśeṣeṇeti</b>
<note>(1) P. 1238</note> <note>(2) G. godānamātrabodhane'pi</note> <note>(3) G. ananvayaśeṣaḥ śrutaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1010"/>
<b>prayājārthatā'vagamyate</b> । somalipteneti karmārthatā । <b>kimiti na viśeṣaḥ</b> । prayājaśeṣo
nāma prayāje vyāpṛtasyājyasya śeṣaḥ । na cātadarthaṃ tatra vyāpṛtamiti tādarthyaṃ tatrāvagamyate ।
somaliptānāṃ tu somalepanamātraṃ na tādarthyamākṣipatīti punarākṣepamupodbalayati । <b>ucyate---soma-
liptenetyapi somayāgārthatayaiva somasaṃbandhaḥ</b> । yasya hi somayāgārthatā sa niyamena
tatra vyāpriyamāṇaḥ somalipto bhavati nānyat tena prayājaśeṣatulyateti । <b>evaṃ tarhi avabhṛtha-
śruteḥ karmāntarayogaṃ somaliptasya manvānaḥ śeṣatāṃ manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---avabhṛthaśabda-
stāvat prakṛtatvādavabhṛthasya nānyatra vartate । tasya ca pradhānakarmatvāt abhidhāraṇavat
somaliptārthatā na saṃbhavati । na ca guṇapradhānabhāvamantareṇa saṃbandhaḥ । tasmāt puroḍāśa-
kapālavat adhiṣṭhānalakṣaṇayā somaliptasyaivāvabhṛthaśeṣabhāvena viniyogaḥ । evaṃ ca tṛtīyā
yathārthaiveti । evaṃ caiṣa(evaṃ) vākyārtho bhavati---avabhṛthaṃ kartuṃ yadapo'bhyavayanti tat
somalipteneti । <b>atrocyate---karmāntarayoge'pi nānyaśeṣo'nyaśeṣatayā pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate
anyatra vyāpṛta ivānyatra । tasmātkarmaśabdo lakṣaṇayaiva pratipattavyaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---śrauta-
somaliptārthagrahaṇe tāvat anyaśeṣaḥ somayāgaśeṣaḥ anyaśeṣatayā avabhṛthaśeṣatayā pratipat‍tuṃ na
śakyate(yathā) anyatra vyāpriyamāṇamivānyatra tena ca lakṣaṇayā saṃbandhaḥ । tatrāpi cintā
---kiṃ somaliptaśabdaḥ adhiṣṭhānalakṣaṇayā varṇyatāṃ, utāvabhṛthaśabdo deśalakṣaṇayeti । śrutyartha-
﻿<pb n="r1011"/>
vidhānānugrahāya avabhṛthaśabda eva deśalakṣaṇāparaḥ iti nyāyyam । <b>yantīti ca prakṛtyartho-
'ntarṇīṃtaṇijartho vihito bhavati । anyathā'nuvādamātraṃ dhātvarthasya syāt</b> ।
vākyena ca somaliptavidhānaṃ bhavati । <b>tadidamuk‍taṃ</b> bhāṣye---<b>śrutiśca vākyādbalīyasīti</b> ।
tenāyamarthaḥ---somaliptamavabhṛthadeśaṃ nayantīti ।</p>
<p><b>kartṛdeśakālānāmacodanam । nanu cānuvādapakṣe'pratipādakatvāt vākya-
syānarthakyameva prāp‍noti</b> । atretthaṃ kecit pūrvapakṣayanti---śaktasya kāryakaraṇāt aśaktasya
cākaraṇāt śaktireva kāraṇaṃ na dravyaṃ vyabhicārāt । sā ca śaktiḥ kāryagamyā samādiṣvapya-
viśiṣṭaiva । saiva ca kriyāyāṃ kārakatvena codayitavyā । sā ca nityaprāptaivetyanuvādāḥ
kārakaviniyogā iti । tadabhiprāyeṇa pūrvapakṣākṣepaparo'yaṃ granthaḥ । yadā hi śaktiḥ kārakaṃ
tadā samādīnāṃ kriyānvayo nāsti । ananvitasya ca na pratipādakatvaṃ ityapratiṣādakatā ।
apratipādakatvāccānarthakyameva syāt anuvādapakṣe । <b>atrottaraṃ---na brūmo viniyoge
ānarthakyamiti । viniyoge itthamevānvito vākyārthaḥ pratīyate । prayok‍tṛtvaṃ tu na
saṃbhavati । kathaṃ na saṃbhavati ? nityaprāptatvāt kārakagrāmasya dravyasya hi atra niyamaḥ</b>
﻿<pb n="r1012"/>
<b>pratīyate । na kārakāṇām na cākārakasya1 prayok‍tṛtvaṃ saṃbhavati । tasmāt viniyoga
evāyaṃ viṣayaviśeṣo'vagamyate na prayok‍tṛvyāpāra iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । atrāyamabhiprāyaḥ
---dravyameva tāvat śaktimatkārakaṃ tadbhāve kāryadarśanāt tadabhāve cādarśanāt । etāvacca kāraka-
lakṣaṇam । yadi(paraṃ) dravyamātrameva kārakaṃ kimiti tarhi mantrauṣadhādipratibandhe'pi na karotīti
vyabhicāre parihāro vaktavyaḥ । tatrāpekṣaṇīyaṃ kiñcidrūpamastīti yasmānmantrauṣadhādyapaharaṇīyamatīndriyaṃ
kimapi rūpamastīti śaktiḥ parikalpate । na ca sā kārakam । kārakānugrāhikā hi
sā । na punaḥ svayameva kārakam । tataśca śaktimad‌dravyameva kārakamiti dravyasyaiva
kārakatvāt samādīnāṃ kriyārūpatvasaṃbhavāt anvitābhidhānopapattiriti viniyogenā-
syānarthakyam । kintu prayok‍tṛvyāpāre upādānaparyālocanayā anuvādakatvamucyate । yasmā-
dviniyuktasyāpi yadupādānaṃ tatkārakatayaiva । kārakatā ca sarveṣāmaviśiṣṭā । yadi paraṃ dravya-
mātratayā tadbhedaḥ । na ca dravyamupādīyate । tadrūpasya kriyāsaṃbandhābhāvaditi kārakatvena
niyamābhāvādana2rthakamanuvāda eveti । tasmādviniyogāvasthāyāmevāyaṃ niyogaviṣayasya yāgādeḥ
viśeṣo'vagamyate nopādānadaśāyāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>atrocyate---yadi dravyādanyat
kārakatayā'vagamyate tato yathā bhavānāha । iha tu dravyameva kārakatayā'vagamyate
tasyābhidhānādvibhaktyutpatteḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---samādaya eva tāvat kriyāyāḥ kārakatayā-
'vagamyante । te ca bhinnā eva kārakabhūtāḥ tāneva vidhirapyupādatta iti bhinnaviṣayaḥ
<note>(1) G. kārakasya prayojyatvaṃ</note> <note>(2) G. dānarthakyam</note>
﻿<pb n="r1013"/>
<b>prayok‍tṛvyāpāraḥ</b> samādiviśeṣavyatirekeṇānyasyāviniyogāt । <b>etadeva vivarītuṃ</b> codayati
---<b>nanu ca kārakaṃ hi kriyāprayuktyaiva prayujyate । na ca kārakaśūnyaṃ karmāsti iti</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---kārakaprayuk‍tistāvat pṛthak nāsti । <b>kintu kārakaśūnyā kriyā nāstīti</b>
kriyāprayuktyaiva kārakaṃ prayujyate । tasya ca kārakarūpasyāviśeṣādaniyataviṣayamevopādānam ।
satyam na kārakaśūnyaṃ karma । na punaḥ sāmānyaṃ kiñcidasti kārakaṃ nāma । yadeva hi
vibhaktyā dravyaṃ guṇo vā samarpyate tadeva kārakam । <b>tasmāt viniyogavaśāt
prayok‍tṛtve'pi</b> bhinnaṃ kārakamiti <b>prayuk‍terniyamasaṃbhavaḥ</b> । nanu bhavatu viniyoge niyamaḥ
upādāne tu kathamityāha---<b>uktaṃ tu viniyogānuvartī niyogaḥ sati saṃbhava iti</b> । yadeva hi
viniyogato niyogasādhanatayā'vagataṃ tadeva niyogasiddha‍yarthamupādeyam । anyopādāne
sādhanābhāvānniyogāsiddhiprasaṅgāt । evaṃ ca niyamārtho 2vidhirucyate na punaranyatheti ।</p>
<p><b>tathā dravyeṣu</b> । nanu vibhaktibhiḥ guṇajātyorapi kārakatvena viniyogāt kartrādivadeva
virdhiyuk‍to nānuvādaḥ tatrāha---<b>yuktaṃ tāvat dravyasyopādānaṃ vibhaktibhiḥ tasya kārakatayā-</b>
<note>(1) P. 1240</note> <note>(2) G. na vidhirucyate</note>
﻿<pb n="r1014"/>
<b>'vagateḥ । guṇastu tadviśeṣaṇamātrameva ś‍vetādiṣu । yatra punaḥ aruṇayeti vibhaktyaiva
kārakatvenāvagatiḥ tatra pūrvādhikaraṇenaivāvagatam । ato dravyopādānārthatvāt guṇa-
jātyoravivakṣaiveti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---kārakavibhaktyanupātte tadviśeṣaṇamātra-
tayaiva <q>‘śuklānāṃ vrīhīṇāṃ caruṃ’</q> iti śrute guṇajātī ihodāharaṇam । tatra sākṣāttayoḥ
kriyāṅgatvenāśravaṇāt vibhaktyarthavacca dravyaviniyoge (a)bhinnaprātipādikabodhyatvenāpi viniyojya-
tvābhāvāt anuvādo'yam niyogasaṃsparśābhāvena ca niyamānupapattiḥ । ato dravyopādā-
nārthamevedaṃ na guṇajātyupādānārthamiti । <b>atrocyate---satyaṃ dravyopādānārthamidam ।
etadeva hi dravyaṃ tadrahitaṃ na śakyate tadviśiṣṭamupādātumiti guṇajātyorapi dravyava-
dupādānasiddhiḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---bhinnapadavācyatayā tāvat dravyaṃ tābhyāṃ viśeṣyate । tacca viśiṣṭaṃ
2tatkriyāṅgamiti tathāvidhadravyasādhyo niyogaḥ tadanyaguṇopādāne tathāvidhadravyābhāvādaṅga-
vikalatayā na niyogassidhyatīti tayorapyupādānaṃ niyamena kāryamiti niyamārtho vidhiḥ ।</p>
<p><b>saṃskāre ca tatpradhānatvāt । saṃskāre punaḥ ko viśeṣaḥ ? ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ atra ।
adhikāraśūnyo hi saṃskāravidhirbhavati saṃskāryārthatvātsaṃskārasya । nātrādhikṛtārthaṃ</b>
<note>(1) P. 1241</note> <note>(2) G. tadyāgāṅga</note>
﻿<pb n="r1015"/>
<b>karmāvagamyate । tasmādavivakṣaiveti pūrvābhyāṃ viśeṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yaḥ khalu adhikāra-
niyogaviṣayaḥ so'dhikāraniyogasaṃsparśādadhikāravidhinā upādīyate । tatra na tāvat
saṃskārakriyā sākṣādvidherviṣayaḥ, saṃskāryārthatvāt saṃskārasya । yasya hi niyogasiddhireva
kāryaṃ sa viṣaya iti viṣayajñāḥ । tasmādadhikāraviṣayatvābhāvānnātra adhikṛtapuruṣārthatā
saṃskārāṇām । tasmānniyogāsaṃsparśādatrāpi niyamānupapatteranuvāda iti । <b>atrocyate
---satyamadhikāro nāvagamyate । adhikṛtadravyārthatā tu pratīyate । tataḥ kim ? idraṃ
tato bhavati । saṃskāraviśiṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ adhikāraviṣayaviśeṣaṇatayā'vagamyate । tataśca
guṇavat tadapyadhikāravidhinopādīyata iti tadvadityucyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---evaṃvidhadravya-
sādhyayāgasādhanatvānniyogasya nānyadapi dravyamupādeyam । tena vinā tathāvidhadravyābhāvena
yāgābhāvānna niyogasiddhiriti darśitam । yadidamadhikāraviṣayānupraveśāt puthagviṣayatvābhāvenā-
bhinnaniyogatvādanuvādakatvaṃ vrīhīnavahantītyādividhīnāṃ <b>tat pradarśitaṃ evaṃ satyaṅgavidhiranuvāda
iti</b> ।</p>
<p><b>yajaticodanā dravyadevatākriyam</b> । nanu asaṅgatamidaṃ padārthasvarūpamātrakathana-
masmin śās‍tre, kimutādhyāye ityāśaṅkya saṅgatimāha---<b>ke punaste'dhikāraviṣayā2</b> yadanu-
praveśena kārakaṃ tadviśeṣaṇaṃ, tatsaṃskārā adhikāravidhyanupraveśinaḥ । ke punaste'dhikāravidhi-
<note>(1) P. 1241</note> <note>(2) G. viṣayaniyogāḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1016"/>
viṣayāḥ ? iti pūrvok‍tena prasaṅgatiriti yāvat । <b>uttaraṃ---yāgādānahomāḥ svargakāmo
yajeta, āyuṣkāmaḥ suvarṇaṃ dadyāt saubhāgyakāmo juhuyāt ityevamādayaḥ । etaccopa-
lakṣaṇamātram । anye'pi ye kāmaśrutisaṃyuktāḥ upavāsavratādayaḥ tapaśca । kaḥ punaḥ
svatvatyāgātmakatve sati yāgadānahomānāṃ parasparaṃ viśeṣaḥ ityāśaṅkānivṛttyarthaṃ svarūpavarṇana-
mityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yāgo'pi dravyatyāgātmakaḥ homadāne api । ko viśeṣaḥ
eteṣāmityāśaṅkā bhavati । tāṃ nivartayituṃ sūtrakāreṇa <b>svarūpaṃ varṇyate</b> । <b>tena sūtratrayeṇa
taduktamiti । devatoddeśena dravyatyāgo yāgaḥ । sa evāsecanādhiko homaḥ</b> । parasvatvā-
pādanātmakastyāga eva dānamiti । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । śabdārthatāyāṃ 1viśeṣo'sti ।
upādhiviśeṣavaśena śabdapravṛtteḥ । tyāgātmakatve tu na kaścidviśeṣa iti । kathaṃ punarevaṃ-
vidhe'rthe yāgaśabdasya vyutpattiḥ ? vācyabhūtaṃ pratītya saṃbandhinamarthaṃ(ca) avadhārya tatra
śabdasya śaktyadhyavasānam । na cāyamarthaḥ pramāṇāntarasamadhigamanīyaḥ । devatābhāvasya
pramāṇāntareṇāvagantumaśakyatvāt tathedamapi vācyam ।</p>
<p>kā punariyaṃ devatā nāma ? tathoddeśo'pi kimātmakaḥ tathātyāgo'pi kiṃrūpa iti ।
atrocyate---āgneyādicodanāvasitadevatābhāvān agnyādīnuddiśya yadā puroḍāśādikaṃ
kaścittyajati tadā bālān <b>vṛddhāstatraivamāhuḥ</b>---agnyādīnayaṃ yajata iti । yadā sa
eva svadravyatyāgamātraṃ karoti tadā yajati śabdaṃ na prayuñjate । tenānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ
devatoddeśena dravyatyāgo yāga iti yajyarthe vyutpattiḥ bālānāmanayaiva diśā ।
<note>(1) G. tāyāmaviśeṣo nāsti</note>
﻿<pb n="r1017"/>
te'pi vṛddhāḥ bāladaśāyāṃ vyutpadyanta ityanāditayā vṛddhavyavahārasya na kiñcid‌duṣyati । nanu
kathaṃ devatārthe vyutpattiḥ ? ucyate । āgneyādihaviṣi sūk‍te ca codite yadi kaścidagni-
muddiśya tyajati agniguṇavacanaṃ stotraṃ śas‍traṃ vā prayuṅa‍k‌te tatraivaṃ laukikāḥ prāhuḥ---agniratra
devateti । tatra bālāḥ paribhāvayanti yamuddiśya havistyajyate yaḥ stṛyate, praśasyate vā
sā devateti । atrāpi vṛddhavyavahāraparamparānāditvāśrayaṇena na kaściddoṣaḥ । tathaiva
vyutpannāḥ sāsya devatā ityadhikāravihitapratyayāntaśabdaśravaṇena vede'pi devatābhāvaṃ pratipadyante
yā ca tatra devatātvena codyate tatraiva tāṃ devatāmāhuḥ nānyāmuddiśyānyasmin haviṣi tyajya-
māne'pi iti laukikavyavahārānusāreṇa coditatvamapi devatāyā evetyadhyavasyanti । na caivaṃ
vācyaṃ vedādeva devatārthaṃ pratipadya vyavaharamāṇeṣu vyutpattiriti vṛddhavyavahārapūrvako devatārthapratyayo
na syāditi । yataḥ pūrveṣāmapi vyutpattau vṛddhavyavahāra eva hetuḥ । tatpurassarā tu vedārtha1-
pratītiḥ । tatpūrvakaśca vyavahāra iti tatpūrvikā aparasya aparasyāpi vyutpattiriti । uddeśaśca
saṃpradānakārakasyaiva svaśabdenābhidhānam yathā <q>‘agnaya’</q> iti । tyāgo'pi svāminaḥ audā-
sīnyasaṅkalpaḥ laukikatvācca svatvasya । yatraivaṃ svāminaḥ saṅkalpo bhavati <q>‘mamaitanna’</q> iti
tatraiva tasya svamidamasya svāmitvaṃ na bhavatīti laukikavyavahārāt saṅkalpamātrādeva svatvanivṛtti-
rityanavadyam । tadevaṃ yāge vyutpattisaṃbhavāt homaśabde'pi vyutpatterupapattiḥ । yato yajati-
codanācodita eva yatra viśeṣadeśādhāradravyaprakṣepoṣādhiko homaḥ śabdaprayogādavagantuṃ śakyate
eva prakṣepopahito homa iti ।</p>
<p>nanu kimarthamuktaṃ parasvatvāpādanātmakaṃ iti dānaviśeṣaṇam । ucyate---na
tyāgamātraṃ dānaṃ api tu saṃpradānakārakībhūtapuruṣasvīkāro'pi । sa caivaṃvidho na
kevalatyak‍tṛpuruṣamātreṇa saṃpādyaḥ । api tu svīkartrāpi । na hi svīkāriṇaṃ vinā
svīkaraṇaṃ bhavati । tena tyāgaḥ parasvīkaraṇarūpanirvṛttaye svīkartāramapekṣate । anyathā
hi tyāgamātrameva syāt । na caivaṃ prāk‌svāminā tyak‍te yadi samakālamagrataḥ2 tyak‍tureva
kaścitsvīkaroti3 tadā tadīyameva tatsyāt । maivamāśaṅkitavyam । avocāmaivedaṃ laukikaṃ
<note>(1) G. devatārtha</note> <note>(2) R. kālamagrataḥ</note> <note>(3) R. svīkāro'sti</note>
﻿<pb n="r1018"/>
svatvamiti । tatra yatsvatvāpattiparatayā svāmī tyajati tasya svīkaraṇe tadīyameva syāt
nānyasyeti laukikavyavahāraḥ । nanu yatsvatvāpattiparatayā svāmī tyajati sa yadi na svīkaroti
tadā'pi tyak‍turdānāt phalaṃ syāt tyāgamātrasya tadva‍yāpāratvāta tasya ca tena kṛtatvāt iti ।
keyaṃ mandatā bhavataḥ ? uktamasmābhirna tyāgamātraṃ dānamiti । kintu svīkaraṇarūpamapi ।
yathācoditānuṣṭhāne ca phalaṃ coditārthasya । coditārthaśca yamuddiśya tyāgaḥ tatsvīkaraṇamapīti
pratipattavyam । coditaṃ yathā bhāvi tathā yatitavyam । tatra kaścit prasijighṛkṣuḥ tyāgamātre-
ṇaiva svīkaroti । kaścit prārthanādibhiḥ iti saṃpradānasvīkaraṇarūpāpattaye samāśrayaṇīyaḥ ।
svīkartā ca tadānīṃ ṛtvik‌sthānīya iti kṛtamatibahunā ।</p>
<p><b>vidheḥ karmāpavargitvāt</b> । atra bhāṣyaṃ viniyogameva cintayatītyasaṅgatimāśaṅkate
---<b>kaḥ punarupādānalakṣaṇe'sya saṃbandhaḥ ? eṣa saṃbandhaḥ kimupāttasyātithyārthaṃ dhāraṇa-
mātraṃ dvābhyāṃ</b> upasadagnīṣomābhyāṃ <b>prayujyate, uta niriṣṭakasya punarupādānam, uta
pṛthagevopādānaṃ dharmamātrātideśakamide vacanam, utta sādhāraṇameva upādānamiti</b> ।
idameva cintayitukāmaḥ bhāṣyakāraḥ kāraṇasandehaṃ kṛtavānityabhiprāyaḥ । atra pūrvapakṣotthāna-
bījaṃ yāvanti padāni śrūyante tāvatāmeva tāvadanvayo vācyaḥ nāśrutapadāpekṣayāpi । tatra
yadātithyāyāmityatra yacchabdaḥ śrūyate । sa ca pūrvavṛttasaṃbandhyantarasavyapekṣaḥ । ātithyā
cātra samabhivyāhriyate । tenātithyāpekṣa evāsau varṇanīyaḥ । tenaiṣa saṃbandho bhavati yadā-
tithyāsaṃbandhibarhiriti । tatra yadyātithyopāttatayaiva tatsaṃbandhitvaṃ tadā prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ । atha
vyāpṛtatayā tadā dvitīyaḥ । atra rāddhāntamāha---<b>anyaśeṣasya</b> tāvanmukhyasya <b>anyatra</b>
﻿<pb n="r1019"/>
<b>viniyogo nāsti । pratipattivirodhāt yathā'nyatra vyāpṛtasyānyatra vyāpāraḥ vastuvirodhāt
ityuk‍taṃ</b> somaliptādhikaraṇe । <b>viniyogānusārī copādānamitīdamapyuktam</b> ।
āmikṣādhikaraṇe । <b>tasmādvi</b>viniyuktatvāt ātithyāyāmiti <b>ātithyopāttasya agnīṣo-
mopasadbhayāṃ dhāraṇamātraṃ prayujyata iti na ghaṭate । niriṣṭakopadeśaśca śiṣṭācāra-
virodhānna bhavati na hi</b> niriṣṭakena śiṣṭā yāgamācaranti । <b>lakṣaṇāśrayaṇācca</b> prayogānte
ātithyāsaṃbandhasyābhāvāt sambandhe tenāsaṃbandhirūpatā <b>lakṣaṇīyeti lakṣaṇaiveyamiti
nopapadyate । evaṃ dharmātideśo'pi lakṣaṇābhayādeva</b> barhirdharmā lakṣaṇīyā iti <b>tyajyate ।
tasmāt sādhāraṇāvagatireva śrutyopapannā bhavati</b> । tasmāt <b>sādhāraṇamevopādānamiti
siddham</b> । lavanasaṃbandhāpekṣaśca yacchabdo draṣṭavyaḥ । lavanapūrvakatvādbarhiṣaḥ । yadidaṃ
barhirlūyate tadātithyāyāḥ, tadupasadāṃ tadagnīṣomīyasyetyavirodhādvarṇanīyam ।</p>

ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ

dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>

<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>dravyasaṃskārakarmasu</b> । nanu ca bhāṣyakāraḥ phalavidhyarthavādacintāṃ karoti sā
cāsaṅgatā punaruktā ca, arthavādādhikaraṇena stutyarthatāyā uktatvāditi śaṅkāyāṃ nirākaraṇamāha
---uktamadhyāyādau <b>sarvatra niyogavyāpāraścintyata iti । ihedānīṃ phalasaṃbandhitayā
puruṣasya vidhivyāpārassaṃbhavati neti cintyate</b> । vidhivyāpāranibandhanaṃ phalavidhitva(pakṣa)
māśaṅkyānuvādakatvamucyata iti nāsaṅgatiḥ । punaruktatāpi nāsti । sthite <b>puruṣaphala-
saṃbandhāsaṃbhave</b>'sminnadhikaraṇe <b>kathaṃ prāmāṇyasaṃbhava iti pramāṇalakṣaṇe'</b>rthavādādhikaraṇe
<b>cintitam</b> । tenaitatpūrvako'sau vicāra iti yāvat । tathā <b>yo'pi tatra</b> pramāṇalakṣaṇe
audumbarādhikaraṇe <b>pūrvapakṣaḥ asāvapi kriyākārakasaṃbandho'vagamyamānaḥ</b> phalasiddhikriyāyā
audumbarayūpakārakatvasya ca sādhyasādhanalakṣaṇassaṃbandho'vagamyamānaḥ <b>kathaṃ kriyāntaraviṣayaṃ niyogaṃ
pratipādayati</b> । udumbareṇa yūpaḥ kartavya iti yūpakārakaviṣayaṃ niyogaṃ <b>kathaṃ pratipādayati</b>
svayaṃ vihitatvābhāvāt vidheyatvābhyupagame ca 2vidheyāntarānupraveśāt । na hi vidheyadvayasyaika-
<note>(1) P. 1244</note> <note>(2) G. vidhānā</note>
﻿<pb n="r1021"/>
vākyatvaṃ saṃbhavati । ekavākyatā cāvagamyate । na cāvagamyamānā tyak‍tuṃ yuktā । tasmāt
pramāṇāntaramapekṣaṇīyam । nacaitadasti ityaprāmāṇyaṃ syāditi । <b>asyārthasya nirākaraṇā-
yoktam</b> । tena phalāṅgīkaraṇenānyaccintitamiti na punaruktatā । pūrvapakṣaśca 1siddhāntopo-
ddhātatayā cintyata iti matvā nirākāryanirākaraṇāya pūrvapakṣa ityuk‍tam । <b>iha tu svaviṣayo
niyogo na saṃvatīti cintā । kathaṃ ? yasyetyevamādīnāmadhikāriviśeṣaṇatayā'saṃbhavāt2</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---ihāpāpaślokaśravaṇādīnāṃ parṇamayajuhvādīnāṃ ca sādhyasādhanasaṃbandha evanāstīti
pratipādyate yasmāt <q>‘yasya parṇamayī juhūrbhavati na sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śṛṇoti’</q> iti apāpaślokaśravaṇa-
madhikāriviśeṣaṇatayā na śrūyate । tenātra phalāpahnava evādhikaraṇārthaḥ । tenaudumbarādhi-
karaṇenāpi na punaruktatā । <b>kathamasaṃbhavaḥ ?</b> ayamāśayo'tra pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ pṛcchataḥ
---evaṃ vidhādvākyālloke sādhyasādhanabhāvo'vagamyate । tadvadvedepyavagatiḥ 3avagamyate cet
4svavākyakārya eva phalavattvāt svātantryameva syāt । na ca sādhyasādhanabhāvo'dhikāri-
viśeṣaṇatvamantareṇa saṃbhavatītyaupādāniko'dhikāriviśeṣaṇabhāvaḥ pratīyate । uttaraṃ-<b>tatsaṃbandhasya
niyogasyānupapatteḥ</b> iti । tenaivāśayena pṛcchati---<b>kimiti</b> । uttaraṃ---<b>siddhavadupa-
deśāditi । yathā devadattaḥ odanaṃ pacatīti puruṣopalakṣaṇaṃ pratīyate</b> odanapākaḥ ।
<b>na punaḥ puruṣeṇodanaḥ paktavya iti</b> sādhyabhūtaḥ odanapāko na pratīyata ityarthaḥ ।
tathehāpyapāpaślokaśravaṇamapi vartamānāpadeśāt । upasaṃhāravyājena pūrvapakṣaṃ nirākaroti-
<b>tasmānnāyaṃ śabdārtho yasya parṇamayī juhūrbhavati na sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śṛṇotīti । pratyayāntarā</b>-
<note>(1) G. siddhāntotpannaḥ kena</note> <note>(2) G. viśeṣaṇatayoḥ saṃ</note> <note>(3) G. avagate ca</note> 
<note>(4) R. svavākya eva</note>
﻿<pb n="r1022"/>
<b>gamyatvādasyārthasya</b> । anena lokavaiṣamyamāha । loke'pi yadevaṃvidhāt vākyāt sādhyasādhana-
bhāvādhyavasānaṃ tat <b>tathāvidhasya vākyasya pramāṇāntareṇa</b> tatparatvasya <b>niścitatvāt</b> । <b>na ca</b>
vedavākyetātparyamanyato'vagantuṃ śakyate tadāha---<b>na ca tatpratyayāntaraṃ</b> tātparyāvadhāraṇakāraṇa-
masti iti prathama evādhyāye arthavādādhikaraṇe yo'rtha uktaḥ stutirūpaḥ sa eva nyāyya iti
sthitaṃ <b>evaṃ bhūtānāmā</b>pātamātreṇa laukikavākyasāmānyato darśanena phalamiva samarpayatāṃ ālocya-
māne nimittaśūnyānā<b>marthavādatvamiti</b> ।</p>
<p><b>naimittike vikāratvāt</b> । atra bhāṣye ‘godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayedityevamādīnāṃ
vākyānāṃ kratvarthapuruṣārthātmakārthadvayapratipādakatayā pūrvapakṣitam । tadākṣipati---<b>kathaṃ punaratra
dva‍yarthaṃ vākyamupanyasyata iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---nedamekaṃ vākyamanekārthaṃ yuk‍taṃ yasmāta padānāṃ
saṃbhūyakāritā vṛddhavyavahārāvagatā । tripadaṃ cedaṃ vākyam । tatra na paśukāmapadaparityāgena
arthaśśakyate pratyetum । tatsvīkāre ca puruṣārthatvameva na kratvarthatvamiti । athocyeta
agṛhyamāṇāviśeṣatayā'rthadvayamiti । tanna । paśukāmapadaprayogeṇa viśeṣagrahaṇāt । yatrāpi

dhikaraṇaṃ pratibhāti</b> । atrocyate---<b>evamevaitat ekārthatvameva anvitābhidhāne</b> । vini-
yogāvasthāyāṃ 2puruṣārthatvameva, na kratvarthatvamityarthaḥ । <b>prayojanadvayaṃ tvatra saṃbhavatīti

<b>sahāvagamāt</b> । yasmāt <b>kriyāsaṃbandhatyāgena dravyādeḥpuruṣārthatā</b> na2 praṇayanakāraṇī-

nusārī । śabdācca puruṣārthatayaivānvayo'vagamyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---tadeva vidhirupādāpayati

upāyaḥ । <b>nanu kriyayāpyanvayo'vagamyata3 eva । satyaṃ gamyate puruṣārthaupayikatayā,</b>
na svārthaupayikatayā । atrāya bhāvaḥ---godohanapraṇayanasaṃbandho lokata evāvagataḥ paśukāmaṃ prati
vidhīyate । na punassa eva śabdena jñāpyate yena viniyogaparyanto'sau saṃbandho bhavet । tena

pādeyam । <b>tasmāttadeva niyamenopapādakaṃ2 yadarthamanvayāvagamaḥ</b> । puruṣārtha evopapādaka3
ityarthaḥ । nanu bhāṣyakāreṇok‍taṃ śabdenaiva saṃbandhadvayaṃ 4pratipādyata iti atrāha---<b>yatpunaruk‍taṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇa viśeṣānavagamāt dviṣṭhaṃ vākyaṃ alambusānāṃ yāteti tat prakaraṇādyasambhave
anirṇayāyaiva । na punaḥ śabdāt dvayamavagantuṃ śakyate । iha tu viśeṣāvagamānnānirṇaya
ityarthaḥ</b> । satyaṃ pūrvapakṣadaśāyāmidamuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa tanna siddhāntadaśāyāṃ bhavet tatra
viśeṣānavagamādubhayārthatāvagatiḥ’ ityanena bhāṣyeṇa prakaraṇādibhirviśeṣānavagamāt tatra,
loke bhavedanirṇayaḥ5 ata ubhayārthāvagatiriti varṇitam । etaduktaṃ bhavati---prakaraṇādyasaṃbhave
bhavatu loke'nirṇaya iti na punaḥ śabdāt dvayamavagantuṃ śakyamityevaṃparaṃ tat । iha tu
kāmipadaśravaṇāt nirṇaya ityarthastasya bhāṣyasya । nanvidamadhikaraṇaṃ kratvarthaṃ kiñcinnāstīti
kṛtvācintayā prārabdha; tatra sāmānyavihitopanyāso nopapadyate tatrāha---<b><q>‘nanu na kiñcidvihita-
mastīti’</q> paricodya sāmānyato vidhānopanyāsaḥ sāmasādhyastutyapekṣayā nābhivartapara-
tayetyadoṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---nedaṃ sāmānyavidhānamupanyastaṃ kintu stutisvabhāvena
sāmasādhyatvena kiñcidabhivartādikaṃ sāma bhaviṣyatītyevaṃparaṃ tat na punarabhivartasvarūpameva
vivakṣitam ।</p>

puruṣārthatvaśaṅkā; tadāha---<b>kaḥ punaḥ pūrvapakṣiṇa āśaṅkāhetuḥ iti । ayamastyāśaṅkāhetuḥ

<p><b>dravyāṇāṃ tu kriyārthānām</b> । kathamatra prakaraṇādhītasyāpi vratasya puruṣārthatāṃ
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ityāśaṅkyāha---<b>iha tu prāṇadhāraṇārthatvādvratasya puruṣārthatāṃ manyate

tatpravṛttasya kṣīrādiniyamaḥ pratibhāti । prakaraṇaparyālocanayā ca kratvaṅgatā tasya । tatra

'dhikārasya sthāpitatvāt tatrāha---<b>ihādhikāraśūnyā vidhaya udāharaṇam</b> । ayamāśayaḥ

yāvaddhi kaścit mamedaṃ kāryamiti na pratipadyate tāvat nānutiṣṭhet । anuṣṭhānābhāve ca

﻿<pb n="r1031"/>
<b>dviśeṣākṣepaḥ</b> । kiñca aparipūrṇe vākye loke'dhyāhāro dṛṣṭaḥ aparipūrṇaṃ ca taducyate

muccāryate tadā <b>raktaḥ paṭo bhavatītyapi bhavati</b> na punaḥ dvipadaṃ na vākyam । <b>tasmāt
padāntaraśravaṇanibandhana eva vākyeṣu</b> padadvayamātreṇopapanneṣu <b>arthāntarāvagamaḥ</b> tena
yatrādhikāripadaṃ śrūyate bhavatu tatrādhikāryavagamaḥ । na punastadabhāve aparipūrṇateti tadāha

nopapatteḥ paripūrṇatā'sti <b>kathaṃ tarhi <q>‘vasantāya kapiñjalānālabhate’</q> grīṣmāya kalaviṅkān</b>
ityatrālamatyanuṣaṅgaḥ grīṣmāya kalaviṅkānityatra padadvayenānvitābhidhānopapatteḥ । vibhaktyarthasya

satyadhyāhāraḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>yuk‍taṃ kārakāṇāṃ kriyāpekṣatvāt</b> kārakapadānāṃ kriyāpade-
'śrūyamāṇe'paripūrṇatvāt bhavatyadhyāhāraḥ । <b>na punarniyogo'dhikāramapekṣata ityuk‍tam</b> ।
tena vināpi viṣayeṇa sahānvitābhidhānopapatteriti । <b>tasmādyāvadvacanaṃ vacanaṃ</b> na puna-
radhyāhārāpekṣamiti । <b>atrābhidhīyate---kārakamiva kriyāpekṣaṃ niyogamapyadhikārāpekṣaṃ
vadāmaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā kārakasya kriyayā sahānvitābhidhānaṃ tathā niyogasyāpi na
kevalaṃ viṣayeṇa sahānvitābhidhānam । api tu niyojyapadenāpi । ubhayānubandhavyatirekeṇa
anvita evābhidhātuṃ na śakyate । yathā kriyā ekenāpi kārakeṇānvitā'bhidhīyate dvābhyāṃ
bahubhirapi tatheha nāsti । sarvathā anubandhadvayānvito'bhidheyaḥ nānyatheti adhikāryanubandhā-
śravaṇe aparipūrṇatvādadhyāhāro yuktaḥ । ubhayānvita evābhidheya iti kutaḥ ? <b>loke tathā
darśanāt । abhyāja gāṃ śuklāṃ’</b> ityetāvanmātramanapekṣya niyojyaviśeṣaṃ <b>vaktāro na bhavanti
yasmāta devadattaṃ yajñadattaṃ bā'dhikṛtya liṅādayaḥ prayujyante । nanu devadattādayaḥ kartṛ-
viśeṣaṇaṃ</b> tena vināpi niyojyena loke prayogo'stīti1 codyārthaḥ । <b>yathā kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ
na bhavati tathā ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । yasya hi viṣayānupraveśaḥ śabdavirodhānna saṃbhavati so'dhi-
kāriviśeṣaṇaṃ yathā svargakāma iti yāvajjīvamiti ca । atrāpi saṃbodhanavibhaktiyogaśca
kartṛtve nopapadyata iti devadattādayo niyojyaviśeṣaṇameva । nanvārthama(na)dhikāriviśeṣaṇatva-
<note>(1) R. nāstīti</note>
﻿<pb n="r1033"/>
māśritya saṃbodhanavibhaktiḥ । bhavatu ca kartṛviśeṣaṇatvameva śābdaṃ tatrāha---<b>adhikārāddhi kartṛtvaṃ
sthāsyati1 na kartṛtvādadhikāraḥ</b> । nārthamadhikāritvaṃ saṃbhavati ārthaṃ tu kartṛtvaṃ saṃbhavati ।
<b>tasmāt śrutyekadeśaḥ sa ucyate । yatpunaratra bhaṣkāreṇok‍taṃ evaṃ laukiko'dhyāhārā
prāpnotīti । parihṛtaṃ ca vaidikamevādhyāhariṣyāma iti tathā vyavadhānaṃ cāśaṅkya <q>‘api
paśyasi’</q> iti dṛṣṭāntābhidhānaṃ tatsarvamasamañjasamiva pratibhāti yanniyogādavagamyate</b>
adhyāhṛtenāpyadhikāriviśeṣaṇena tāvat yatphalamavagamyate <b>kathaṃ tadavaidikam</b> । sākṣācchruta
ivādhikārapade । tatra hi niyogata eva phalam । <b>vyavadhāne ca kathamanuṣaṅgaḥ । yadapyuktaṃ
<q>‘api paśyasi dhāvantaṃ’</q> ityasaṃvandhipadavyavāyānnaivāyaṃ vyavāyaḥ</b> na hi dūre jātamityā-
dīni padāni dṛśinā saṃbadhyante । tena ca na dṛśiṃ vyavadadhati <b>saṃbandhayogyena</b> hi sajātīyena
<b>padena saṃbaddhaṃ vyavahitamucyate</b> । atrocyate---phalamadhyāhriyata ityuk‍te kasyacidiyamāśaṅkā
syāt phalatayaivādhyāhāra ukta iti tadabhiprāyeṇa codyamevaṃ laukiko'dhyāhāra iti ।
parihārastu niyojyaviśeṣaṇādhyāhāreṇa niyogāt phalamiti । tadetadāha---<b>atrocyate---vaidika-
mevādhyāhariṣyāma iti । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । na kārakatayā'dhyāhriyate</b> na kriyāyāḥ
<note>(1) G. sthāpyate</note>
﻿<pb n="r1034"/>
karmakārakatayā <b>kiṃ tarhi adhikārimukhenaiva</b> adhikāriviśeṣaṇalābhāyaiveti । <b>kārakatayā
hi phalasaṃbandho laukiko bhavati pramāṇāntarāpekṣatvāt</b> । kriyākārakabhāvo hi sarvatra
pramāṇāntaravedya eva । <b>dṛṣṭānto'yi yathā na padabyavadhānamātrāt vyavahitaṃ bhavati kintu
yogyapadasaṃbaddhaṃ vākyāntaravyavahitaṃ bhavati</b> tathā'trāpi yogyapadasaṃbandhābhāvāt vyavadhānā-
bhāvaḥ । <b>tasmānnādhikārādhyāhāre vyavadhānam</b> । api paśyasi iti ca sūktam ।
<b>ato'śrūyamāṇādhikārāṇyapi sādhikārāṇīti siddham</b> ।</p>
<p><b>tatsarvārthamanādeśāt sa svargaḥ syāt</b> । atra sūtradvayamekīkṛtya paṭhataḥ ṭīkākāra-
syāyaṃ bhāvaḥ---svargakāmādhikāra2nirṇayaparyantamekamidamadhikaraṇaṃ nānyathā'yameva siddhānto'vatiṣṭhate
kalpite'pi niyojye punaragṛhyamāṇaviśeṣaṇatayā sarvārthināmadhikāraḥ syāt । na ca
paramārthatassarveṣāmadhikāraḥ śakyate'vagantum ekenaiva kṛtārthatvāt । punastatrāpyagṛhyamāṇa-
viśeṣatvāt viśeṣakalpanānupapatteḥ pūrvādhikaraṇabhaṅgo'pi syāt 3yāvanna viśeṣakalpanā syāt
tāvadasyaivāsiddheriti । <b>sthitaṃ niyogo nādhikāraśūnya iti</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatimāha ।
sthitamiti cānenātra pūrvapakṣe pūrvādhikaraṇasiddhāntaḥ sthito'pi na nirvahatītyāha । <b>kenādhi</b>-
<note>(1) P. 1255</note> <note>(2) G. ri</note> <note>(3) G. nanu vikalpaḥ syāt na, anvayasyaivāsiddheḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1035"/>
<b>kāreṇeti na jñāyate । ato'gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatayā sarvārthibhiḥ saṃbandha iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yadyapyantaraṅgatayā avaśyaṃbhāvitayā ca jīvanamevādhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ yuktaṃ tathāpi
prayuktigauravaprasaṅgāt puruṣāṇāṃ ca kāmapravaṇapravṛttitvāt arthitaivādhikāriviśeṣaṇam । tatra ca
viśeṣo na gṛhyata iti sarvārthināmadhikāra iti । <b>atrocyate---bahubhissaṃbandhe niyatamekena
saṃbandhaḥ । ekena cedupapanno niyogaḥ nādhikārāntarasabandhe pramāṇamasti</b> । 1tadeka
evātrādhikārīti yuktam । <b>nanu cāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt nāsau nirūpayituṃ śakyata
ityuktam । satyamuktaṃ yadi na gṛhyate viśeṣaḥ । iha tu sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt
svargakāmasyaivādhikāro'vagamyate sāmānyakalpanāyāṃ hi viśeṣāvagame hetvabhāvāt</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---kāmino hyadhikāre kalpyamāne duḥkhanivṛttikāmitā tāvannādhikāri-
viśeṣaṇaṃ āśrayaṇīyam । sukhakāmanāyāṃ puruṣāṇāmatyantonmukhatvāt । 2sukhīti tāvata
svayaṃ sukhamanubhūyate3 । duḥ khaṃ ca tadvirodhādeva nānubhūyate । duḥ khanivṛttimātre ca
suṣuptidaśāyāṃ sukhānubhavo nāvaśyaṃ bhavati । tatra sukhe kāmyamānatayā'dhikāriviśeṣaṇe
sthite tadviśeṣagrahaṇakāraṇābhāvāt anavacchinnaṃ sukhamātramevāvaśiṣyate । atassāmānya-
kalpanāyāṃ satyāṃ viśeṣāvagame hetvabhāvāt sukhasāmānyamātraṃ svarga evādhikāriviśeṣaṇamiti ।
nanu sūtrakārassarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāditi yuktimāha---<b>tadidamuktaṃ---sa svargaḥ syāt sarvān</b>
<note>(1) G. tasmādeka</note> <note>(2) G. sukhe hi</note> <note>(3) adds duḥ khanivṛttimātraṃ
suṣup‍tyādidaśāyāṃ sukhānubhāvo nāvaśyaṃ bhavati ।</note>
﻿<pb n="r1036"/>
<b>pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt iti । anena yadevāsmābhiruk‍taṃ sarvān sukhaviśeṣāt prati</b> sukhasāmānya-
syāviśiṣṭatvaṃ tadeva sūtrakāreṇāpyuktamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>kratau phalārthavādam । sthitamaśrūyamāṇādhikāreṣu sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt
svargo'dhikāraheturiti</b> । anenāvāsaṅgatiṃ <b>pūrvapakṣabījaṃ cāha</b> । atra bhāṣyakāraḥ phala-
vidhyarthavādacintāṃ karoti । sā cāyuktā । parṇamayyadhikaraṇe hi sarveṣāmevaṃjātīya-
kānāmarthavādatvamuktam phalapratipādakatvābhāvāditi । anayā śaṅkayā ṭīkākāro bhāṣyakārīya-
saṃśayābhiprāyaṃ darśayannāha---<b>yatra punarviśeṣaphalabhidhāyino'rthavādāḥ śrūyante tatra saṃśayaḥ
kiṃ tatrāpi svarga evādhikārahetuḥ athavā'rthavādābhihitaṃ vastu</b> iti । asyārthaḥ
---sthitamevārthavādatvaṃ tathāpyevaṃ cintyate adhikāraśūnyavidhau kalpyamāne cādhikāriṇi
kimarthavādābhihitaphalakāmo'tra adhikārī kalpyatāṃ uta svargakāma evātrāpi bhavatu yatrāpi

gamyate tadeva yuktamiti manyate । arthavādastvarthavāda eva</b> asyārthaḥ---sthitaṃ arthavādā-
stāvanna phalapratipādakā iti, yadi paraṃ niyogasāmarthyamātreṇa kalpanā sā viśvajidādiṣvivāviśiṣṭa
﻿<pb n="r1037"/>
iti svargakāmina evātrādhikāro yuktaḥ । <b>atrābhidhīyate---arthavādābhihitameva phalaṃ

<p><b>kāmye karmaṇi । nanu</b> cedamadhikaraṇaṃ pūrvādhikaraṇena dūrotsāritam । yatrārthavāda-

tasmādupādhikārā anvācīyeran । ko doṣaḥ ? । rāddhāntamāha---<b>na khalu kaścit brahma-

<p><b>sārvakāmyamaṅgakāmaiḥ pradharaṇāt । <q>‘sarvebhyaḥ kāmebhyo darśapūrṇabhāsau’</q> iti
