﻿<pb n="r1041"/>
<p><b>tatra sarve'viśeṣāt</b> । yadā pūrvādhikaraṇe sthitaṃ vidhiriti tadā cinteyamupapadyate
ityavāntarasaṅgatiṃ vadan saṃśayamāha---idamidānīṃ cintyate---<b>kiṃ sakṛt</b> prayoge sarveṣāṃ putra-
paśvādīnāṃ prāptiḥ <b>uta yāvatkāmaṃ prayoga iti</b> । yāvantaḥ kāmyamānāḥ tāvantaḥ prayogā
iti । sarveṣāṃ kāmyamānānāṃ phalānāṃ nimittatayā darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ śrutatvāt <b>prayoge viśeṣā-
vadhāraṇaṃ na śakyate vak‍tum</b> । asmātprayogādanena bhavitavyaṃ asmātprayogādanena iti
abhinnatvāddarśapūrṇamāsayoḥ । tau ca sarveṣāṃ ca nimittabhūtau kṛtau cet kimiti tadīyaṃ
sarvameva naimittikaṃ namavati । atha na bhavati kadācidapi tarhi tannimittaṃ na syāt ।
nimittābhāve ca naimittikamāpi kadācinna syāt । punaḥ punaḥ karaṇe vihitau tāveva iti tena
sakṛtkaraṇe sarvaphalāvāptiṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । <b>nanu ca sarvakāmo naiva kaścidastyadhi-
kārī anadhikārācca phalātpatterasaṃbhava</b> iti pūrvapakṣamākṣipati । asyārthaḥ---kāmyamāna-
phalamūtasarvaviṣayakāmanāyuktaḥ kaścitpuruṣaḥ nāsti kāmanānāṃ yugapadanutpādanāt1 । tādṛśaśce-
dadhikārī nāsti phalamapi yugapanna saṃbhavati anadhikṛtānāṃ jyotiṣṭomādiṣviva śṛdrādīnāṃ
phalābhāva iti । samādadhāti---<b>ucyate---yadi kāmanā'ṅgaṃ syāt anutpannā satī nāṅgatayo-
papadyata iti bhavati kāmanānāmanutpādaḥ sakṛtprayoge sarvaphalānutpattau hetuḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ
---kāmanānāṃ tāvat 2niyogotpattau viniyogābhāvāt nāṅgatā । kintu adhikārotpattau tāveva
<note>(1) G. anuvādāt</note> <note>(2) G. viniyogotpattau</note>
﻿<pb n="r1042"/>
kāraṇam । tatra kāmanānāṃ yadyapi yaugapadyaṃ nāsti tathāpyavaiguṇyāt sarvaphalāvāptiḥ ।
śūdrādīnāṃ tu vaiguṇyādeva sarvaphalānutpādaḥ । <b>iha punaḥ sarvaiḥ kāmairyuk‍tasya kāmino-
'dhikāraḥ iti na prayogakāle kāmanotpāda upayujyate । tasmānna nimitte sati naimittikasya
vyāghāto bhavitumarhati । atrocyate---yāvatkāmaṃ prayogaḥ iti । evamadhikāra-
siddhirupapannā1bhavati । na hyakāminaḥ phalādhikāro'stīti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> । atrāya-
mabhiprāyaḥ kāmino hyadhikāraśravaṇāt phalānutpāde ca tasyādhikārānupapatteḥ phalasādhakatvaṃ niyoga-
siddhipurassaraṃ yāgādeḥ kalpyate । tatra yadā yaiva kāmanotpannā tadā saivādhikāriviśeṣaṇam ।
yadā ca yatkāmyate tadā tatsidhyaiva kāmino'dhikārasiddhirupapannā bhavatīti na phalāntarotpāde
pramāṇamasti । nanūtpādakāviśeṣa eva pramāṇaṃ syāt syādetadevaṃ yadi 2niyogo'rthalakṣaṇaṃ na
syāt; kṣaṇamaṅgini yāge niyogādeva kālāntare phalamityasakṛduktam । pratikāmaṃ cādhikāra-
niyogā bhidyante sādhyabhedena śāstrabhedāt śāstrabhedena ca śāstrārthabhedāt । tena yadā
yaiva kāmanā tadā tatsaṃbandha eva niyogo niṣpadyate nānya iti sarvaphalānutpādaḥ ।
nanu niyogā api sādhanābhedāt kimiti na niṣpadyante । naivam । niyoga-
siddhāvadhikāriṇo'pi sādhanatvāt । tasya ca pratikāmaṃ bhinnatvāt sādhanābhedānupapatti-
riti । imamevābhiprāyaṃ codyapūrvakaṃ prakaṭayati---<b>nanu ca prayogakāle kāmanotpādo'naṅgatvā-
nnopayujyata ityuk‍tam</b> । tenānutpannāyāmapi kāmanāyāṃ avaiguṇyāt phalotpādena bhavitavya-

﻿<pb n="r1043"/>
mityarthaḥ । <b>kena vok‍taṃ prayogakāle utpādo heturiti ? adhikārāvagatāveva sarva-
kāmitā yugapanna saṃbhavatītyuktamasmābhiḥ</b> । yugapat kāmanānāma<b>saṃbhave ca yugapat
sarvaniyogānupapattiḥ</b> । sarvānniyogān yugapat kāryatayā puruṣo nāvabudhyata ityarthaḥ ।
upasaṃharati---<b>tasmāt pratikāmamadhikāraḥ</b> । adhikāraparyantā ca phalasiddhiriti pratikāmaṃ
phalārthināṃ prayogabhedaḥ । atra bhāṣyakāreṇa <q>“yadyapi yugapatkāmā bhavanti tathāpi teṣāṃ
sāhityamavivarkṣitaṃ uddeśyatvāt”</q> ityuktam । tatreyamāśaṅkā bhavati yadyapyuddeśyatā tathāpyu-
pāttoddeśyatvāt kimiti viśeṣaṇavivakṣā na saṃbhavati iti । tatra ṭīkākāro bhāṣyārthaṃ tāvadāha
---1<b>yathoddiṣṭakāmābhiprāyaṃ vidhānaṃ iti bhāṣyakāreṇoktam</b> । ye pratikratvantaraṃ kāmā
uddiṣṭāḥ ekaikena ta eveha nirapekṣā uddeśyā iti । nanu kasmāt yathoddiṣṭā eva sarvaśabde
nocyante ityatrāha---<b>anirdiṣṭānāmavagamābhāva ityabhiprāyaḥ</b> । yato'nirdiṣṭānāmanavagatiḥ
<b>tena nirdiṣṭāpekṣī sarvaśabdaḥ <q>“sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ”</q> itivat</b> । yato nirapekṣāḥ kāmā adhikāra-
hetavaḥ ataḥ <b>pratikāmaṃ</b> adhikārabhedāt yāvadadhikāraṃ <b>prayoyogabheda</b> iti । yata eva
paryāyeṇa phalotpādaḥ <b>ata eva viruddhānāmapi</b> sarvasvāraphalamaraṇa, prājāpatyaphalāyuḥ prabhṛtī-
nāmapi viruddhānāṃ <b>cādhikārassiddho bhavati । sakṛtprayoge hi maraṇāyuṣoranupapattiḥ ।
tasmādyogasiddhirveti sūktam</b> ।</p>

﻿<pb n="r1044"/>
<p><b>evaṃ vā</b> । nanu ca lakṣaṇasaṅgatirevātra nāsti । kimitīha loke kāmā utāmuṣmi-
nnityāśaṅkāmapanayannāha---<b>asminnadhikaraṇe niyogasya phalaṃ prati kiṃ śarīragrahaṇapūrvakaḥ
prayojakabhāvaḥ uta yāvacchrūtaṃ prayok‍tṛtvamiti1</b> । adhyāhṛtyaupaskāraḥ । asyārthaḥ
---ya eke iha loke gegārhaphalāścitrādividhayaḥ kiṃ te śarīraṃ bhogāyatanaṃ vinā phalaṃ
bhojayitumaśak‍nuvantaḥ śarīramākṣipyaiva phalamākṣipanti, yadi vā śarīrākṣepaṃ vinā putrādyākṣepa
eveti cintyate । yadi śarīrākṣeṣaniyamaḥ tadā amuṣminneva loke kāmāḥ; atha na
tadā'niyamaḥ iha vā'muṣmin veti । <b>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī śarīragrahaṇasya kāraṇāntarā-
darśanāt paśvādīnāṃ ca kāraṇāntareṇopapatteḥ śarīragrahaṇapūrvakaḥ phalākṣepa iti manyate</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---śarīraṃ tāvadbhautikaṃ bhūtasaṃyogajanyaṃ bhūtānāṃ ca sarva eva saṃyogo na śarīrārambhakaḥ
kintu kaścideva, tatra bhavitavyaṃ kena citkāraṇaviśeṣeṇānugrāhakeṇa । tatrānyasya tāvatkāraṇatvaṃ
na dṛṣṭam । karmavidhīnāṃ tu phalaprasavānyathānupapatteryuk‍taṃ tatra kāraṇatvam । tena śarīrāraṃbha-
pūrvakaṃ phalaṃ vaidikāni karmāṇi dadatīti phalamāmuṣmikam । nanu aihikānāṃ paśvādīnāṃ kiṃ
nimittamityatrāha---<b>paśvādīnāṃ kāraṇaṃ pratigrahādi pratyakṣaṃ bhaviṣyatīti । rāddhāntavādī tu
yāvacchrutaṃ prayok‍tṛtvaṃ manyate</b> । ityadhyāhāreṇopaskāraḥ । kasmāt ? <b>kevalaśravaṇāva-
gamyatvāt prayok‍tṛbhāvasya</b> । śabdaikasamadhigamya eva niyogasya prayojakabhāvaḥ । sa cā-
<note>(1) G. adds cintyate uttaraṃ saṃskāro'syārthaḥ ।</note>
﻿<pb n="r1045"/>
viśeṣeṇa gamyate । <b>na hi gamyate viśeṣaḥ ihaiva phalamamutraiva veti</b> । kasmāt ?
<b>kāmaśrutisāmānyāt</b> । kāmasya cobhayatrāpi saṃbhavāt । yat‍tu śarīrārambhasya kāraṇāntaraṃ
na dṛśyate iti । satyaṃ idamami na dṛśyate । phaladānaṃ tu kāraṇāntaropāttepi śarīre

hi nānantaryamupalabhyata ityuktam</b> । atrocyate । <b>ayamabhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya---sā-
mānyāvagamāt <q>‘iha’</q> <q>‘amuṣmin’</q> iti ca viśeṣānavagamāt śabdato na pramāṇāntarābhāva
ānantaryaṃ vihantīti</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapyānantaryaṃ na dṛśyate tathāpi ekāntataḥ
ānantaryaṃ na syāditi na śakyate vak‍tuṃ pramāṇāntarādarśanepi śabdādaniyamāvagateḥ
kadācidanantaramapi kadācidanantaramapi phalaṃ syāditi । <b>liṅgaṃ pūrvapakṣavādyuktamuktam</b> ।
itthaṃ vyākhyātamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>samavāye codanā</b> । nanu kathamatra pūrvapakṣaḥ yāvatā k‍tvāpratyayāt aṅgaprayojana-
saṃbandha evāyamiti tatrāha---<b>vājapeyeneṣṭā bṛhaspatisavena yajeta iti lakṣaṇe k‍tvāpratya</b>-
<note>(1) P. 1262</note> <note>(2) R. karmaṇi</note> <note>(3) G. bhavaṣyatīti</note>﻿<q>yotpattau kālaśravaṇāt kālārthassaṃyoga iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---aṅgāṅgibhāvastāvat
ktvāpratyayotpattau hetubhūto lakṣaṇe na śrūyate । pūrvakālatā tu tāvata śrūyata eva tadvaśenā-
nantarakālabhāvitāpyavagamyate । atasta1dvidhānārthaṃ nūtana evāyaṃ viniyogo'stviti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
<q>samānakartṛkayordhātvarthayoranvayāvagaterdhātusaṃbandha evāyam । sa cāṅgāṅgibhāvā-
dṛte na saṃbhavatīti aṅgāṅgitaiveti rāddhāntaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---satyaṃ lakṣaṇe śrūyate pūrva-
kālatā tathāpi sā na dhātvarthagatā <q>‘saṃmīlya hasati’</q> ityādau vyabhicārāt । kintu pratīti-
gatā । upādhimātram । samānakartṛtā tu dhātvarthagataiva । samānakartṛtayā ca dvayordhātvarthayo-
ranvayapratīteḥ dhātusaṃbandha evāyaṃ <b>ktvā</b>pratyaya iti dhātusaṃbandhādhikāre vihitatvāt ।
sa ca dhātvarthasaṃbandho dvayordhātvarthayoḥ anyathānupapatteḥ aṅgāṅgibhāvādṛte na saṃbhavatīti
aṅgāṅgitaiveti ।</p>
<p><b>ubhayārthamiti cet । <q>‘paurṇamāsīṃ saṃsthāpya’</q> iti parisamāptivacanatvāt
saṃsthāśabdasya nāṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ paurṇamāsyāḥ saṃbhavati iti prakaraṇāt darśapūrṇamāsāṅgataiva
vaimṛdhasyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---saṃsthāśabdaḥ parisamāptivacanaḥ parisamāptiśca niśśe-
ṣānuṣṭhānam; tatra yadi saṃsthitā paurṇamāsī na tarhi tadaṅgamasti । atha tadaṅgamaparaṃ vaimṛdhākhya-
miti na tarhi saṃsthāśabda upapadyate । tasmānnāto vākyāttāvat aṅgāṅgibhāvo'vagamyate ।
<note>(1) P. 1262</note> <note>(2) G. tadvidhipara evāyaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="1047"/>
tenāsaṃyuktatvāt prakaraṇādevobhayāṅgatā yuk‍teti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । atrocyate---<b>yadi samāpti-
vacanatvāt saṃsthāśabdastha nāṅgitvaṃ paurṇamāsyāḥ prakaraṇādapi nāṅgitvaṃ saṃbhavati</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yadi niśśeṣapaurṇamāsīsamāptivacanādasaṃbandho vaimṛdhasya tarhi prakaraṇādapyaṅgatā na
syāt tasminnaṅge'vaśiṣṭe niśśeṣasamāp‍tyanupapatteḥ । <b>atha saṃsthāpyeti pūrvavihitāṅgakalāpa-
parisamāp‍tyabhiprāyo'yaṃ saṃsthāśabdaḥ</b> । atha prākaraṇikāṅgasaṃbandhasiddha‍yarthaṃ saṃsthāśabdaḥ
āpekṣiko'vakalpate <b>evaṃ tarhi vākyāt paurṇamāsyaṅgataiva vaimṛdhasya</b> । na caivaṃ vācyaṃ,
mābhūt prakaraṇāt vākyācca paurṇamāsyaṅgaṃ vaimṛdhaḥ samāptivacanasyāpekṣikatve pramāṇābhāvāt paraṃ
amāvāsyāṅgameva prakaraṇādastviti । tathā hi sati yaḥ paurṇamāsīsaṃbandho'vagamyate sa
ekāntena tyakta eva syāt samāpterāpekṣikatvenāpyaṅgatopapattau1 । <b>na ca niyogaikye kaści-
dviśeṣaḥ । asyāpyadhikārasaṃbandhāt</b> darśapūrṇamāsaniyogaikyaṃ ca yadvaimṛdhasyāvagamyate tasya
kevalapairṇamāsyarthatvepi na virodhaḥ paurṇamāsīdvāreṇāpi tadanupraveśāt । <b>atassiddhaṃ paurṇamā-
syaṅgaṃ vaimṛdha iti</b> ।</p>
<p><b>anutpattau tu kālaḥ</b> । <q>‘agnimārutādūrdhvamanūyājaiścaranti’</q> iti kathamatrāṅgapradhāna-
saṃbandhaḥ ūrdhvaṃśabdasya kālavacanatvāt kālārtha evāyaṃ saṃbandha iti । <b>ucyate</b> । yeṣāmevaika-
prayogatā prāptā teṣāmeva yugapadanuṣṭhānāsaṃbhavāt paurvāparyāpekṣāyāṃ kālārtha upadeśa iti yukta-
<note>(1) tvenāp‍tyayoga</note>
﻿<pb n="1048"/>
matrāpyaṅgāṅgitvam । prahṛtya <b>paridhīn</b> ityatra ktvāpratyayādaṅgapradhānaśaṅkā । nanu prakṛtatvādeṣāṃ
nirjñātaparāṅgabhāvānāṃ kathamiyamāśaṅketi । ucyate---aṅgatvāvagamādeva taddharmakāṇi karmānta-
rāṇi bhaviṣyanti anyathā'ṅgatvānupapatteriti । atrottaraṃ---<b>nirjñātaparāṅgabhāvayoreva saṃbandhe

ca na vidhīyate । tenāṅgapradhānasaṃbandho'tra na vidheyaḥ । pāriśeṣyāt kālavidhiparamevedaṃ
vacanam । <b>tasmāt kālārtho niyogaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>utpattikālaviśaye । <q>‘darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvā somena yajeta’</q> ityatrākarma-
vidhānāt kālārtho niyoga ityuktam</b> । anena bhāṣyārthamanubhāṣya ākṣepamāha---<b>tatpunarida-
mayuktam</b> । kasmāt ? <b><q>‘vājapeyeneṣṭvā bṛhaspatisavena yajeta’</q> ityanenāviśeṣāt</b>
bṛhaspatisavaśabdādapi mukhyabṛhaspatisavāvagatireva । <b>tenātrāpi kālārthena niyogena
bhavitavyam</b> । athāsannidhānādiha bṛhaspatisavapratyabhijñā nāstīti karmāntaravidhānaṃ tatrāha
---<b>ubhayatra vā karmārthatvaṃ</b> karmavidhānārthatvaṃ <b>niyogasya</b> । atrāpi karmaṇoḥ prakṛtatvāt ।
﻿<pb n="1049"/>
<b>vak‍tavyo vā viśeṣaḥ । atra kaiścit anārabhya vidhānaṃ viśeṣa uktaḥ</b> <q>“darśapūrṇamā-
sābhyāmiṣṭvā somena yajeta”</q> iti nedaṃ kasyacitprakaraṇe vākyam । kaḥ <b>punaratnānārabhyavādena
viśeṣo'vagamyate । ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ । karmadvayavidhānaṃ tāvanna saṃbhavati aneneṣṭvā anena
yajetetyevamādiṣu</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityādiṣu nāmnā tāvatkarma dūrasthamapi
pratyabhijñāyate । tathā somena yajetetyapi dravyeṇa karma pratyabhijñāpyata eva । <b>tenaikamapi
karma vidhātuṃ na śakyate । anārabhyavidhāne ca naikamapi karma prakṛtamasti</b> । vājapeya-
prakaraṇe tu bṛhaspatisaveneti prakṛtavājapeyādhikārasannidhānāt yajistāvat aṅgavidhipara
evābagamyate । nāma ca tatparatayā na pratyabhijñāmāpādayituṃ śaknoti । yatra hi vidheyatayā
dhātvarthaḥ pratibhāti tatra vidheyasya bhinnatvāt tasmin prayuk‍taṃ nāmadheyaṃ na pratyabhijñāmāpādayati ।
vidhito dhātvarthasya prakaraṇāntaraṃ pratibhāti । adhikārāntaraṃ prati karmaṇo vidhīyamānatvāt ।
tathā yatrāpi guṇadvayaśravaṇaṃ tatrāpi karmavidhiḥ kārakaniyamārthamuktam । <b>tasmānnāmataḥ
prasiddhakarmopādānaṃ kālaniyogārtham---uk‍taṃ ca nāmadheyamapi guṇaphalopabandhenārthavaditi ।
vājapeye punaḥ prakṛtatvāt karmāntaravidhānaṃ śrutyopapadyate । nāma ca taddharmātideśakaṃ bhavi-
ṣyati । prakaraṇāntare prayojananyatvamiti nyāyāt । anārabhyavāde punaḥ prakaraṇāntarā-
bhāvāt ubhayorapi karmāntaratvamayuktam</b> yatrāpi dūrasthaṃ karma phale vidhīyate tatrāpi phalasyā-
﻿<pb n="1050"/>
vidheyatvāt karmaiva vidheyam । anārabhyavāde yadadhikāraṃ prati karmavidhirnāsti tatkālaniyamārtha-
muktamapi <b>karmāntaratvamayuk‍tam</b> । tadetatsarvaṃ kṛtavyākhyānam ।</p>
<p>evaṃ tāvat anārabhyavādamātraṃ yatra śākhāyāṃ tatra kālārtho niyoga1 uktaḥ ।
<b>yeṣāṃ punaḥ darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇa eva paṭhyate tatra kā kathā</b> । atrāyamabhiprāyaḥ---tatra na
dravyasaṃyogāt pratyabhijñātuṃ śakyate prakṛtārthatvena karmaṇo vidheyatvāt । tena tatra aṅgaprayojana
saṃbandha eva yuktaḥ tatrāha---<b>bhavatu tatrāṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ, kā no bādhā ? anāra</b>bhyavādamātraṣareṇai-
vādhikaraṇena siddhāntopapatteḥ । <b>atha vā parihṛtametadaṅgāṅgitvaṃ śākhāntarādhikaraṇe sarva-
śākhāpratyayamekaṃ karmeti vadatā</b> । kathaṃ parihṛtaṃ ? yāvatā yasya yo'rthaḥ pratibhāti tasya
tenaivārthena bhavitavyamiti bhāvaḥ, tadevedaṃ śāstramiti vākyasya pratyabhijñāyamānatvāt ekaṃ
śāstraṃ yuk‍taṃ na śāstrāntaramiti । atra pṛcchati ।---<b>bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi na vidmo'nārabhya-
vādasya yo'rthaḥ</b> kālārthoṃ niyoga iti <b>tena śās‍traṃ pratyabhijñāyatāṃ</b>, sa eva śāstrāntare
prakaraṇāntarādhītepi bhavatu, <b>uta prakaraṇepi yo'rtho</b>'ṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ teva śās‍traṃ pratyabhijñāyatāṃ sa
evānārabhyavāde'pi śākhāntarīye bhavatu । uttaraṃ---<b>avirodhādanārabhyavādena pratyabhijñānaṃ
bhedavido manyante</b> । anārabhvādhītasya yo'rthaḥ sa evārabhyādhītasyāpi avirodhāt । anāra-
bhyabādārthe sarvatrāśrīyamāṇe nāmnā dravyeṇa ca yatpratyabhijñānaṃ na tasya virodhaḥ prakaraṇādhītārthe tu
pratyabhijñānaṃ virudhyata iti । <b>tasmātsūk‍taṃ kālārthassaṃyoga iti । darśanamuk‍tam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) R. saṃyogaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="1051"/>
<p><b>phalasaṃyogastvacodite । atra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ yasya niyogaḥ</b> pituḥ tasya śāstrāt
<b>phalaṃ utānyasya niyogaḥ anyasya phalamiti</b> । kathaṃ saṃśayaḥ ? arthavāde phalapadena
brahmavarcasādinā anyasya putrasyānvayāt jātasya phalasaṃbandhāvagamāt । adhikāripadena ca
<q>‘putre jāte’</q> <b>ityane</b>nānyasya pituranvayāt । nanvevamapi pitā niyojyo bhavatu; bhavatu ca
putra/?/sya phalamiti ko virodhaḥ tatrāha---<b>adhikārī ca niyujyate । yadarthaṃ karma so'dhikārī</b> ।
yaścādhikārī <b>sa eva niyujyate</b> । parārthe hi karmaṇi na parasya niyogo ghaṭate । tatra
yadīdaṃ putraniḥ śreyasāya karma syāt tadā nātra pituradhikāraḥ <b>syāt</b> । atadarthatvātkarmaṇaḥ ।
<b>anadhikāre ca pituḥ 1nāsya niyojyatā syāt । tasmāt</b> pitari niyojye <b>bhavatyeva
saṃśayaḥ । kiṃ yuktaṃ ? niyojyasya pituḥ phalamiti kutaḥ ? adhikārasidhyartho hi</b>
yasmāt phalayogo <b>na saṃbandhamātrāvagamyaḥ</b> puruṣasya yadaiśvaryaṃ adhikāriśabdavācyaṃ tatpuruṣasya
karmaṇi yathā syāt ityevamarthaṃ phalayogo'ṅgīkriyate na punaḥ phalasaṃbandho'vagamyata ityetāvanmātreṇa ।
<b>tasmāt pituridaṃ phalam । putraphalānvayasya stutyā vā'nvayo bhavatu</b> । putrasyāpi tāvadidaṃ
phalamiti <b>lakṣaṇayā vā'dhikṛtaviśeṣaṇam</b> । putrapadena pitureva lakṣaṇayā pitureva phalaṃ
viśeṣaṇamastu । sarvathā pitṛniḥ śreyasāyedaṃ karmeti । <b>tathā ca kratusaṃbandhini nimitte</b>
<note>(1) G. nānyasya</note>
﻿<pb n="1052"/>
<b>yasmānniyojyasyaiva</b> phalaṃ dṛśyate tena kratunā saṃbadhyate । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---asaṃbandhinyapi
nimitte yanniyojyasyaiva phalaṃ śrūyate yadi yatsaṃbandhinimittaṃ/?/ yathā putrasaṃbandhijanma tasyaiva
phalaṃ syāt tadā kratusaṃbandhameva phalamuk‍taṃ syāt na ca tathoktamiti । <b>atrocyate---yasya
phalānvayaḥ putrasya tasyaiva phalaṃ nimittatayāpyadhikārasiddheḥ itarasya putrajanmanā
nimittenāpi</b> nimittādhikāraniyoganirvṛttyāpi <b>puruṣārthatā</b> karmaṇo'<b>stītyadhikārassiddha‍ya</b>-
tyaiśvaryalakṣaṇaḥ । tasmāt putragatā phalaśrutiryathārthaivāstu । yadi nimittatayāpyadhikārassidhyati
<b>kathaṃ tarhi phalapadaṃ ?</b> ekagranthenāha-<b>na karmaviśeṣaṇaṃ phalaṃ</b> na kārakāṃśopanipāti ।
<b>nāpyadhikārāṃśopanipāti</b> । nimittabalenādhikāralābhāt । <b>ucyate</b> । bhaviṣyatyadhi-
kāropanipāti । <b>kathamevaṃvidhasya</b> putragataphalakāmasya <b>putrajanmavato'dhikāritvena
śravaṇāt</b> । ayamāśayaḥ---nimittasyāpi tāvat sākṣādadhikāriviśeṣaṇatā na śrūyate ।
kintu anuṣṭhānaṃ pratyeva nimittatā । adhikāraikanibandhanatvāccānuṣṭhānasyādhikārahetutā
kalpyetyadhikāriviśeṣaṇatā kalpyā । tathā'rthavādagatasyāpi phalasya kalpyamānatayā tulyatvāt
sammili/?/madhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ upasaṃhāravyājena prakārāntareṇaiśvaryamāha <b>tasmādyasya niyogaḥ tasya
phalamiti</b> । yadetadadhikārasāmarthyena kalpyate aviruddhametat putraprītyā<b>pyadhikārasiddheḥ</b> ।
putragāmiphalotpādanimittaprītyupabhogena pituraiśvaryasiddheḥ । <b>yaduk‍taṃ kratusaṃbandhe</b> nimitte
naimittikā<b>nniyojyasyaiva phalamiti</b> pūrvoktamanubhāṣitam । pariharati---<b>yuk‍tamadhikārānu</b>-
﻿<pb n="1053"/>
<b>praveśānnimittasyeti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ</b> nimittaṃ hi balādadhikāriviśeṣaṇam । tena
nimittasaṃyogena yaducyate tatpuruṣasyaiva bhavatīti phalaṃ puruṣasyaiveti yuktam ।</p>
<p><b>evaṃ vā । <q>‘putrejāte’</q> iti śrūyate । tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ jananānantarameva naimittikaṃ
bhavatu, utāṅgopasaṃhāramapekṣate prakṛtivadabhiprāptamiti</b> । tatrākṣepamāha---<b>yadyevaṃ</b> saṃśayaḥ
<b>kriyate---kimiti tarhi kumārasya prāṇadhāraṇasāmarthyamutkarṣahetutvenopanyasyate</b> । eka-
mevedamadhikaraṇamastu । <b>sāṅgasya</b> śaucakālāṅgayuktasya vaiśvānarayāmasya <b>naimittikatvāt</b>
na nimittānantaraṃ putrajanmānantaraṃ prayogaḥ saṃbhavati । nityavatkālānupasaṃhārāpekṣe ca
śaucānupasaṃhārāditi <b>svakāla eva</b> paurṇamāsyādike । upalakṣaṇaṃ caitat śucinā <b>kartavyo'yaṃ</b>
prayogaḥ । etacca naimittikasya prādhānyānnimittabādhamaṅgīkṛtyoktam । <b>na cānantarye'sati
paramārthato nimittavyāghāto'sti bhūtapratyayayogāt</b> jāta iti nimittasya <b>na ca pratīkṣaṇe
kālaśaucayorbhūtatvamapaiti</b> । tasmāt prathamādhikaraṇaṃ[pṛthagadhikaraṇaṃ]niṣprayojanamiva pratibhāti ।
﻿<pb n="1054"/>
na ca tāvanmātreṇa kālaśaucāpekṣāpi sidhyati । putre jāte kṛte ca jātakarmaṇi prayogasyā-
śaṅkyamānatvāt । tatra sthitvāpi yadeva kāraṇaṃ vaktavyaṃ sāṅganaimittikānugrahātmakaṃ
paraṃ tadeva prathamamupanyasyatāmiti bhāvaḥ । <b>atrābhidhīyate---nimittānantaraṃ naimit‍ti---
kamityautsargiko nyāyaḥ na ca kāraṇādṛte kālotkarṣo'vagamyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---nimittaṃ
taducyate yasmin sati bhavati naimittikaṃ taccennimittamāgataṃ naimittikamapi tena tadanantarameva
yuk‍taṃ vilambakāraṇābhāvāt । <b>nanu ca kāraṇamuk‍taṃ sāṅgasya naimit‍tikatvam</b> । parihartu-
mupakramate---<b>etadeva na vidmaḥ kiṃ nimittakāle niyogāvagamāt viniyogāvagamyamaṅgaṃ
tyajyatāṃ uta niyogakālasyotkarṣa iti</b> । niyogasya pradhānatvāt <b>niyogārthatvācca
viniyogasyāṅgatyāge viniyogavido manyante । yathā rajasvalādisparśanena pūrvāhṇādi---
kālaḥ s‍nānāṅgatvena vihita upekṣyate</b> । jīvanādikaṃ tu na nimittasaptamīnirdiṣṭam । iha
tu svabhāvālocanayā jananānantaryaṃ niyogasya pratibhāti । nimittasya hīdameva nimittatvaṃ
yattasmin sati niyogaḥ । nimittaṃ cedbhūtaṃ niyatamanuṣṭhānaṃ prāpnoti niyogārthatvādanuṣṭhānasya ।
ata evaiṣā prayuktirna śakyate 1naimittikānugraheṇa bādhitum । <b>ata etadbādhanārthaṃ pūrvamadhi-
karaṇam</b> । kathaṃ bādhyet ? etadāha---<b>yadi hi niyogakāla evānuṣṭhānaṃ kriyate
yadartho niyogaḥ</b> kumāragataphalārthaḥ <b>tadeva hīyate</b> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---kāmyeṣu karmasu phalaṃ
<note>(1) naimit‍tikagraheṇa</note>
﻿<pb n="1055"/>
prayojakamanuṣṭhānasya na niyogaḥ tena phalābhāve prayojakābhāvādananuṣṭhānamiti । kathaṃ punaḥ
phalābhāvaḥ ? kumārasya prāṇaviyogaprasaṅgāt । jātakarmaṇi kṛte stanapraṇidhānam । jñātakarma
ca pitrā kartavyam । sa cediṣṭau vyāpriyate kathaṃ jātakarma kriyeta । akṛte ca
jātakarmaṇi stanadānaṃ nāsti । apītastanaḥ kathamiva dhārayetprāṇān । <b>tasmāñjātakarmānantaraṃ
phalābhāvādiṣṭorniyogakālavagatirevotkraṣṭavyā</b> । kathaṃ tarhi uttarādhikaraṇe rāddhāntaḥ ?
tatrāha---<b>utkṛṣṭā cet svakāle nāṅgatyāge pramāṇamasti iti dvitīyamadhikaraṇaṃ likhitam</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---nimittasvabhāvalabhyānantaraniyogabalena tāvadanantarānuṣṭhānaṃ nāstīti siddhe sāṅga-
mevānuṣṭheyaṃ kāle śucitā ceti ।</p>
<p><b>pradhānenābhisayogāt । vājapeyeneṣṭvā bṛhaspatisavena yajetetyatra saṃśayaḥ---kimeko
niyoga uta niyogadvayamiti</b> । anena bhāṣyakārīyaṃ saṃśayaṃ vyācaṣṭe । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati
---kimeka evāyaṃ niyoga uta bhinna iti । ekatve ekaprayogatā bhinnatve bhida iti । tatra
pūrvapakṣamāha---<b>nanu ca niyogadvitve</b> bhinnaniyogābhisaṃbandhāt <b>aṅgāṅgitvaṃ na syāt</b> । eka-
prayogānupraveśanibandhano hyaṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ । <b>asti cāṅgāṅgitvaṃ tasmānna prayogabhedaḥ</b> ।
rāddhāntamāha---<b>bāḍhamapapadyate । viniyogāddhi aṅgāṅgitā</b> । asti cātra viniyogaḥ
﻿<pb n="1056"/>
<b>prayogānyatvena niyogānyatvaṃ,</b> tena dvayamapi bhavatu aṅgāṅgitvaṃ prayogabhedaśca । nanu ca
prayogānyatve niyogānyatvā<b>cchās‍trabhedaḥ prāpnoti</b> । abhinne śāstre śāstrārthabhūtaniyogabhedānu-
papattiḥ । <b>bhavatu prayogāpekṣayā na kaściddoṣaḥ । viniyogāpekṣayā tu ekamevedaṃ śāstram
kathaṃ punarekatve śās‍trasya prayogabhedaḥ</b> । ekaśāstratvamekaśāstrārthatve tathā ca prayogabhedo na
syāt । uttaraṃ---<b>kena bāryate vidhānabhedavat anubandhanimittakam</b> । vidhānabhedavat
prayogavidhibhedāt kālarūpānubandhabheda nimittakaḥ । <b>yadyathā'nubadhvate tattathā tantraṃ prayogaṃ
bhinat‍ti</b> । yat kālādi yathā'nubadhyate anubandhībhavati tattathā tantraṃ prayogaṃ bhinatti ।
<b>iha ca prayogānubandhabhede prayogabhedaḥ । tasmānna śāstrāntarāpat‍tiḥ kevalaṃ prayogabhedaḥ ।
yathā ca prayogabhedaḥ tathā darśitam</b> । iṣṭevati bājapeyābhinirvartitiḥ pṛthagbhūto bṛhaspatisavaḥ
pratibhāti । tena bhinnānuṣṭhānānubandhatvādanuṣṭhānabhedaḥ । aṅgaṃ ca prakṛtakāmādhikāragṛhīta-
tvāditi yuktam । tathā <q>‘agniṃ citvā’</q> ityagnisaṃskārabhūtacayanābhinirvṛttitaḥ pṛthagbhūtā
sautrāmaṇī prayogāvagamādaiṣṭikakāla eva prayoga iti darśitaṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<trailer>iti śrīśālikanāthamiśraviracitāyāṃ ṛjuvimalāyāṃ
pañjikāyāṃ caturthādhyāyasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="1057"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>prakaraṇaśabdasāmānyāt</b> । atra bhāṣyakāro rājasūyaśabdasya sakalaprakṛtotpattivacana-
tayā anijyānāmapi prādhānyamāha । tadākṣipati---<b>nanu ca nāmadheyavicāre yajisāmā---
nādhikaraṇyānnāma bhavatītyuktam । kathaṃ punarayajyarthasyāpyetadabhidhānaṃ śaṅkyate । ataḥ
pūrvapakṣa evāyaṃ nopapadyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---rājasūyena svārājyakāmo yajeta’ iti yāgastāva-
dvidhīyate । tatra rājasūyaśabdo'pi yadyarthāntaravacanaḥ syāt tadā vākyabhedo bhavet । tena 
yāgānāmevedaṃ vacanamiti niścīyate । evaṃ ca yāgānāmetannāmeti yāgānāmeva prādhānyam ।
kathamayāgānāmapi prādhānyāśaṅkā । <b>ucyate</b> । satyamevam---<b>iha tu niyogaikyāt yuga---
padabhidhānaṃ dhātvarthasya; niyogaikyaṃ ca prakaraṇāyattamiti sarvaprakṛtābhidhāyī dhāturiti
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---yajinā sarve'pi yāgā yadvaktavyāstantreṇa tatrāpyadhi-
kāraniyogaikyameva kāraṇam । adhikāraniyogo hi prakṛtatvāt sarvameva svīkaroti । svīkṛtāśca
yajinā adhikāraniyogasya viṣayatayā samarpaṇīyā iti sarveṣāmeva tantrābhidhānaṃ(niyogaikyaṃ)
prakṛtatvanibandhanam । tacca prakṛtatvaṃ yajīnāmayajīnāṃ cāviśiṣṭamiti prakṛtānubandhasamarpaṇe nirjñāta-
<note>(1) P. 1269</note>
﻿<pb n="1058"/>
tātparyo yajiḥ ayajiṣvapi daṇḍinyāyena vartate । na ca vācyaṃ---iti kartavyatayā cāyajināṃ
niyogaikyam iti । yasmāt sākṣātsaṃbandhe sambhavati paramparāśrayaṇamayuktameva । sākṣācca
sarveṣāṃ niyogārthatve'vagate tatsamarpaṇatayā nirjñātatātparyo yajiḥ lakṣaṇayā ayajiṣvapi
vartamāno nānupapannaḥ । evaṃ ca yajiśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt rājasūyaśabdo'pi sarveṣāṃ vācaka
iti kāryabhūtaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇoktam । nāmadheyavicāraśca dhātvabhihito'rtho nāmnā'bhidhīyate
ityetāvati paryavasitaḥ । tasmādupapadyate pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā । <b>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyaṃ
prakaraṇānniyogaikyaṃ na punaḥ śrutānubandhaparityāge kāraṇamasti</b> । asyārthaḥ---<q>‘rājasūyena
svārājyakāmo yajeta’</q> iti yāgaviṣayastāvanniyogaḥ prathamaṃ pratīyate । paścāttu tathābhūtena
niyogena sannihitāssarve padārthā gṛhyante । tataśca kathaṃ kasyānvayaḥ ityapekṣāyāṃ yāgānāṃ
karaṇatayā saṃbandhaḥ yāgānāṃ viṣayatvāt viṣayībhūtasya ca karaṇatvāt । tena yāgānāmeva
karaṇatvam । ayāgānāṃ cetikartavyatātvamiti । <b>kathaṃ ?</b> itikartavyatātva ayāgānāṃ
niyogakyāvirodhābhiprāyeṇa pṛcchati । atrottaramāha---<b>itikartavyatāpi hi naiva niyogaikyaṃ
niruṇaddhi । tathā bhūtopadeśāditi vakṣyāmaḥ । ato yāgavyatiriktamaṅgamiti siddham</b> ।
etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---utpattiśiṣṭyāgaviruddhe niyoge karaṇatayā niveśāsabhavāditikartavya-
tathaivānvayaḥ, anyatrāpi sādhye darśanāditi ।</p>
<p><b>madhyasthaṃ yasya tanmadhye । nanu cātrāpi kramāt prakaraṇaṃ balīya ityetadevodā-
hṛtam</b> । asyārthaḥ---kramātprakaraṇaṃ balīya ityatrāpyadhikaraṇe tṛtīye etadevodāhṛtam ।
<note>(1) P. 1271</note>
﻿<pb n="1059"/>
yadīhodāhṛta bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityāha---<b>sthitaṃ ca sarvārthatvaṃ</b>, ataḥ punaruktamiti ।
pariharati---<b>satyaṃ viniyogāt sthitaṃ idānīṃ pṛthak‌prayojyatvāt abhiṣecanīyaniyogasya
tasya ca sannidhānāt tenaivaikyaṃ yuk‍tamiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---pṛthak
prayok‍tṛtvenābhiṣecanīyasya tāvat prayuktibhedo'ṅgīkāryaḥ tadīyaprayuktimadhyapatitāśca videvanādayaḥ
atassannidhānāt sa evāsya prayojako yuktaḥ । tataśca prayuktiparyantatvādviniyogasya viniyogo'pi
tatraiveti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । <b>na ca prakaraṇaviniyogavirodhaḥ</b> । abhiṣecanīyāṅgatvepi
<b>pratyekasaṃbandhahetutvāt prakaraṇasya;</b> pratikaraṇaṃ itikartavyatayā saṃbandhāpādakatvādasyāpi
kāraṇatvāt । <b>atassannidhiviśeṣātikramo nopapadyate । atrocyate---sthitamaikaśabdyama-
dhikāravidheḥ</b> । ekādhikāraniyogasya sādhyatvenvayāttatsādhanatvenāṅgapradhānopadeśāt । ekaṃ
śāstramaṅgapradhānātmakam । <b>tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tato bhavati yasyaiva prayogānubandhabhedaḥ
tasyaiva pṛthak prayogo'vasīyate svenetikartavyatākalāpena । yasya punaraṅgasyādhikāravidhi-
reva prayogaṃ jñāpayati na tasyāvāntaraprayogānupraveśaḥ śakyate'/?/gantum । tasmāt
kramāttaddeśasyaivānuṣṭhānamadhikāravidhisamadhigamyameva</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathāviniyoga tāvat
prayuktiḥ viniyoge ca sarvārthatvameva । ato'dhikāravidhirevāsya prayojakaḥ na punaravāntara-
﻿<pb n="1060"/>
niyogaḥ, tadarthatvena viniyogābhāvāt tatsannidhānāstu tatraivānuṣṭheyamadhikāravidhinaiva prayujyata
iti viniyogāt prayuk‍teśca sarvārthatvameva । <b>prakaraṇāvirodhastvayaivok‍taḥ</b> । asminnaiva pakṣe
prakaraṇāvirodho yathā bhavati tathā tvayaivoktaḥ pratyekasaṃbandhahetuḥ prakaraṇamiti vadatā । tacca
prakaraṇaṃ pratyekasaṃbandhe eva na virudhyate । niyataikasaṃbandhe tu prakaraṇaṃ sarvasaṃbandhāpādakaṃ
virudhyata eva । tasmāt prakaraṇāvirodhāt sarvārthamiti ।</p>
<p><b>prakaraṇāvibhāge । ākṣipati-kaḥ khalu āgnimārutādūrdhvamanūyājaiścarantīsyanenāsya
viśeṣaḥ</b> । purastādupasadābhityanena purastāditi kālasya śravaṇāt kālārtha eva saṃyogo yukta iti
yāvat । <b>na khalu kaścidi</b>tyādi subodham । <b>ayaṃ tarhi viśeṣaḥ । prakaraṇāt sarvasya prādhānyaṃ
itikartavyatāvyaṃ vā rājasūye । asaṃyuk‍taṃ ca prakaraṇādityuk‍tam</b> । yatsarvasya prādhānyaṃ
itikartavyatātvaṃ vā sarvān prati rājasūye uktaṃ tat prakaraṇāt । adhikāravidhyaṅgatayā 1ca
prakṛtagrahaṇātmakaṃ prakaraṇamihābhipretam । rājasūye cānabhivyaktarūpatvāt viṣayībhūtasya yāgasya
rūpavadyāgāpekṣā bhavati । tathetikartavyatāpekṣāpi । tatra yajatayo viṣayānupraveśinaḥ pradhānāḥ
ayajatayaścetikartavyatā । asaṃyuktaṃ ca prakaraṇādviniyujyata ityuk‍taṃ tṛtīye । saṃyuk‍tāśca
<note>(1) P. 1272</note> <note>(2) R. vidhyākāṅkṣāyāṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="1061"/>
saumyādayaḥ upasadbhirvākyena । evaṃ hi pūrvapakṣī manyate---upasadāṃ saumyeneti saṃbandhaḥ
na cānyathā saumyādayaḥ upasadbhissaṃbandhinaḥ ityaṅgāṅgitā । 1śeṣaṣaṣṭhyeveyaṃ yuktā nopapadaṣaṣṭhī ।
prādhānye copasadāṃ ṣaṣṭhī । tena sāpekṣatvāt upasadāṃ saumyeneti saṃbandhaḥ purastāditi tu
saṃbandhāpekṣaḥ । paścāt prakṛtatvāt upasadapekṣameva bhaviṣyatīti । <b>tasmāt vākyādupasa-
daṅgateti pūrvapakṣiṇo'bhiprāyaḥ । api ca sannidhānaviśeṣeṇopasadaṅgataiva yuk‍tā, adhi-
kāraniyogāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---upasadāṃ purastādityapi saṃbandhe upasatsannidhānaviśeṣāt
saumyādīnāmadhikāraniyogādapi buddhāvanusandhānāt tadaṅgataiva yuk‍teti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
<b>atrābhidhīyate---na tāvadupasadāṃ prakaraṇamasti</b> । na ca buddhisannidhimātraṃ prakaraṇam ।
kutaḥ । <b>adhikāranibandhanatvāt prakaraṇasya</b> । asyārthaḥ-sādhikāro hi niyogo'nvitā-
bhidhānanirvāhakaḥ kāryarūpaḥ pratīyate na niradhikāraḥ tena sarvaṃ tadarthameveti paścāt tadadhi-
kārānupraveśāt 2tadadhikārānupraveśāya nādhikārāntaramapekṣate tenaivānvitābhidhānasiddheḥ niradhi-
kārāṇāṃ kāryāvagame'pi3 4viniyojakaśaktirnāstīti na prakaraṇaṃ teṣāmasti । <b>nanu ca
vākyādupasadaṅgatvamityuktam, nobhayapadasaṃbandhābhāvāt vākyaṃ saṃbhavati</b> । asyārthaḥ
---na saṃbhavati vākyārthaḥ upasacchabdasya saumyapurastātpadābhyāṃ saha sakṛduccāraṇe saha saṃbandhā-
bhāvāt । <b>tasmādeka</b>padasaṃbandhe sthite <b>purastādupasadāmityeva saṃbandhaḥ । atha kasmādupasadāṃ
saumyenetyeṣa saṃbandhaḥ na bhavati ? purastādityananvayaḥ prāpnoti</b> । asyārthaḥ---purastā-

﻿<pb n="1062"/>
cchabdo'yaṃ nityasāpekṣavacanatvāt upasadbhirasaṃbadhyamāno nārthamavabodhayati । tena purastādityanena
saha tāvadananvaye abodhakameva vākyamāpadyeta । na ca vācyaṃ paścāt prakṛtatvādupasadā saṃbadhyata
iti, yasmādavaśyāpekṣaṇīyasaṃbandha eva tāvan‍nyāyyaḥ । itarathā hyapratipādakameva syāt ।

<p><b>phalavadvoktahetutvāt</b> । nanu ca kathaṃ samapradhānabhāva āśaṅkyate yāvatā sāṅgrahaṇyā
evādhikārayogāt prādhānyam । anadhikārāṇāṃ vāmanahomānāmaṅgataiveti tatrāha---<b>sāṅgrahaṇyāṃ
tu phalavatsannidhau aphalaṃ tadaṅgamiti siddhepyanuṣaṅganivṛttyarthamidamadhikaraṇam । darśitaṃ ca</b> ।
satyaṃ niradhikāraṃ sādhikārasyāṅgaṃ; āmanahomāstu sādhikārā eva, adhikārapadasya teṣvapyanuṣaṅga-
saṃbhavāt । na ca paridhimantrā vyavadhāyakāḥ asamānajātīyatvāt । samānajātīyakaṃ hi
vyavadhāyakaṃ bhavati yathā---<q>‘saṃte vāyurvātena gacchatāṃ ityatra gacchatāmiti śabdo'vyāhṛtena
saṃyajatrairaṅgāni’</q> ityatra gacchantāmiti kriyāpadāntareṇa <q>‘saṃ yajñapatirāśiṣā’</q> ityatra vyavadhīyate ।
na cādhikāraparasya mantrapadāni samānajātīyānītīmāśaṅkāmapanetumidamadhikaraṇam । siddhānta-
yuktiśca paridhintrairvyavahitatvāt nānuṣaṅga iti । vyavadadhati ca paridhimantrāḥ adhikāra-
saṃbandhāyogyatvāt । adhikārabuddhivicchedakatvameva vyavadhāyakatvam । tadyathā samānajātīyasya
<note>(1) P. 1272</note> <note>(2) G. ihāpi</note>
﻿<pb n="1063"/>
tathā vijātīyasyāpi tatsavandhāyogyasya । asaṃbandhi hi vyavadadhāti tatrāpi tadbuddha‍yanutpā-
danāt iti ।</p>
<p><b>dadhigraho naimittikaṃ</b> । nanu nimittāsaṃyogena codyamānamidaṃ kathaṃ naimittikamityāśaṅka-
yāha---<b>anityadoṣanirharaṇārthasaṅkīrtanāt naimittikaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi
nimittaṃ na śrūyate tathāpi dadhigrahasya dvārāpekṣāyāṃ devatāntarāyavaiguṇyasamādhānamevārthavādasaṅkī-
titamapi kāryaṃ yuktam । tataśca phalato naimittikatvaṃ <b>khādiravadubhayārthatāmācāryadeśīyaḥ</b> ।
siddhāntaikadeśī tu doṣanirharaṇārthametadadṛṣṭena dvāreṇa kratūpakārārthaṃ dadhigrahaṇaṃ khādirayūpavanmanyate
kā yuktirityāha---<b>nityatve sati jyeṣṭhaśabdopapattiriti manyate</b> । praśasyatvājjyeṣṭhatā
bhavati । praśasyatā 2cobhayarūpayogitayā'bhyadhikārthatvāditarebhyaḥ । <b>rāddhāntastu nimitta-
saṃyogābhāvānna doṣanirharaṇārthatayā naimittikatvaṃ śakyate kalpayitum । kimiti na
śakyaṃte ?</b> ekagranthenāha---<b>naimittikadoṣanirharaṇānyathānupapattyā tasyāpi naimittikatvaṃ
bhavitumarhati</b> । na hi nityasyānityadoṣanirghātārthatā na saṃbhavati iti । tasmādasāvapyanitya
iti । <b>satyaṃ yadyanyathā nopapadyate । arthavādatayā tūpapadyata eveti na kalpanāmarhati</b> ।
<note>(1) 1273</note> <note>(2) R. ubhayopayo</note>
﻿<pb n="1064"/>
asyārthaḥ---svarūpeṇa tāvat na nimittaśravaṇābhāvānnaimittikamatra pratibhāti । na cānityakārya-
balenāpyanityatā kalpanāmarhati । nityānityasaṃyogāvirodhenānityakāryakalpanānupapatteḥ ।
na hi nityaṃ kartavyamanityaṃ doṣaṃ nirhartumiti yujyate tathāpi tāvat tadeva kāryamiti kalpyeta
yadi doṣanirharaṇaśravaṇamanyathā nopapadyeta । tacca stutyarthatvenārthavādatvenāpyupapadyate iti na
prayojanakalpanāmarhati । <b>sārūpyād‍yuk‍taṃ</b> bhāṣye ।</p>
<p><b>vaiśvānaraśca nityaḥ syāt । anityadoṣanirharaṇārthatayāpyupapadyata iti yadyatyeta</b>
vaiśvānare'pi nityatā <b>bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhimānaḥ</b> । ukhāyāmasambharaṇanimittadoṣa-
nirharaṇamarthavādatayāpyupapatasyate pūrvavaditi pūrvapakṣavādino'bhimānamātramiti abhimānaśabdena
mandatāmāha pūrvapakṣasya । <b>rāddhāntastu na brūmo doṣanirharaṇānnaimittikatvaṃ nimittasaṃyoga</b>
evātra śrūyate । <q>“yo vai saṃvatsaramukhyamabhṛtvā'gniṃ cinute savaiśvānaraṃ nirvapet”</q> iti
abhṛtokhyapuruṣādhikāraśravaṇāt naimittikatvamevātra sākṣācachrutam । ato nityānityasaṃyoga-
virodhābhāvāt na doṣanirharaṇārthavādatvena varṇayituṃ nyāyyam । <b>na ca nimittaśrutirartha-
vādatayā śakyate vyākhyātum । śrutyarthe saṃbhavati nārthāntarakalpanopapadyate</b> yataḥ ।
dadhigrahe tu puruṣasaṃyogo nāstīti । nityatva<b>darśanamuktam</b> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1065"/>
<p><b>ṣaṭ‌citiḥ pūrvavattvāt</b> । <q>“saṃvatsara evainaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai nudate yo'gniṃ citvā na
pratitiṣṭhati । atha ṣaṣṭhīṃ citiṃ cinute”</q> ityakṛtapratiṣṭhapuruṣasaṃyogānnaimittikataiveti kathaṃ
nityatā śaṅkyate ityatrāha---<b>ṣaṣṭhīṃ citimiti pūraṇārthapratyavāvagamānnimittaśrutirarthavādatayaiva
varṇayituṃ nyāyyeti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ</b> । ṣaṣṭhīśabdaḥ pūraṇārthapratyayāntaḥ । tena ṣaṭ
saṅkhyā yayā pūryate cityā sā citiḥ ṣaṣṭhī । na ca pañcasu nityāsu iyaṃ naimittikī citiḥ ṣaṭ‍saṅkhyāṃ
pūrayati । ekāvacchedānupraveśāt dvitvādisaṅkhyotpattiḥ । tasmādiyamapi nityā । nityānāṃ
ca nimittaśrutirāñjasyenānuṣapannā kathañcit arthavādatvena varṇayitavyeti । nanu ca
nimittaśrutibalāt ṣaṣṭhīśabda eva kimityanyathā vyākhyātavyaḥ ityanenābhiprāyeṇa pṛcchati
---<b>kuta iti ? vidheyānurodhādadhikārakalpanā nyāyyeti manyate</b> । yathāviniyogaṃ niyoga
iti tiryagadhikaraṇe siddhatvāt । <b>rāddhāntastu satyamevaṃ yadi virodhaḥ syāt na tvatra virodhaḥ</b>
kasmāt ? <b>upadeśavivakṣayāpi</b> pūraṇarūpa<b>pratyayārthopapatteḥ</b> 2ekāpadeśakriyānupraveśāta
ṣaṭ‍saṅkhyāsaṃbhavāt <b>nāvaśyamanuṣṭhānāpekṣayaiva bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ pūraṇasūtraṃ śakyate varṇa-
yitum</b> । yadi hyanuṣṭhānāpekṣayā saṅkhyāniveśābhiprāyeṇa sūtraṃ bhagavatā pāṇininā praṇītamiti
niścayaḥ syāt tadā upadeśāpekṣayā ṣaṣṭhīśabdo na ghaṭeta na tvenadasti । tasmādvidheyasyā-

﻿<pb n="1066"/>
virodhaḥ । vidheyāvirodhe ca na nimittaśrutistyak‍tuṃ pāryate । tasmānnaimittikatva-

2pitṛyajñaḥ svakālatvāt । nanu <q>“amāvāsyāyāmaparahṇe piṇḍapitṛyajñena caranti”</q>

<b>viśeṣāt piṇḍapitṛvajñasya । nāmāvāsyāyāṃ śrautaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñe ca lakṣaṇeti viśeṣo'va-
gamyate । ubhayatra kālayogasya saṃbhavāt</b> । asyārthaḥ-yadi darśopadeśapūrvakaḥ piṇḍapitṛ-

sāreṇa lakṣaṇayā varṇyeta । yadā punaḥ parasparanirapekṣamidamupadeśadvayaṃ tadā ubhayatrāpi pūrvāvagata-
saṃbandhābhāvānna lakṣaṇā varṇayituṃ nyāyyā । na ca kālopadeśaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñe na saṃbhavati ।
itaretarāśrayatāṣatteḥ । amāvāsyākarmāṅgatve pradhānakālatvādaṅgānāṃ amāvāsyākālaḥ prāpnotīti
nopadeśaḥ syāt । kālānupadeśake cāmāvāsyāśabde śeṣisamarpake sati amāvāsyāṅgateti ।
<b>tasmāt pūrvāparaśrutistatkālalakṣaṇetyavirodhaḥ</b> । anena copasaṃhāravyājena paricodanāntaraṃ
nirākaroti । evaṃ hi codyate---arthavādena hi(na)paurvāparyaṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñasya darśasya ca
śrūyate । taccaikaprayogānupraveśanibandhanam । ekaprayogapraveśitvaṃ cāṅgāṅgibhāve sati । tasmāda-
ṅgataivāvabhātīti paricodanā sā evaṃ parihriyate---yadā'ṅgatvakhyāpakaṃ pramāṇaṃ nāsti tadā yā
pūrvāparaśrutiḥ sā svatantrayoreva karmaṇoḥ kālalakṣaṇāmāvāsyāyāṃ2 darśasya piṇḍapitṛyajñaḥ3
pratipadi iṣṭiriti । tasmādarthavādenāpyavirodhaḥ । <b>prayojanamuktam</b> । paurṇamāsyupakramatvā-
ddarśapūrṇamāsayoḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ kṛtādhānasya amāvāsyāyāmāgatāyāmapi darśo na kāryaḥ । tatra
siddhānte piṇḍapitṛyajño bhavati itarathā pradhānābhāve na kriyeta । kuṇḍapāyināmayane cānaṅga-
tvānnātidiśyate piṇḍapitṛyajñaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>paśvaṅgaṃ raśanā</b> । nanu <q>‘trivṛtā yūpaṃ parivīya’</q> iti parivyāṇaṃ tāvat dvitīyāśrutyā
yūpāṅgam । trivṛteti ca vākyena raśanāpi parivyāṇāṅgam । tataśca parivyāṇamukhena

﻿<pb n="1068"/>
raśanāpi yūpasyāṅgamaruṇādaya iva somasyeti kathaṃ paśvaṅgatāśaṅkā ? ityatrāha---<b>atrāpi
ktvāpratyayasya kriyāntarāpekṣitvāt ekaniyogatāṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ
---<q>‘paśumupākaroti’</q> iti tāvadupākaraṇasya paśvaṅgatvaṃ pratīyate । tathā parivyāṇamapi
ktvāpratyayenopākaraṇasamānakartṛkam । samānakartṛkatā caikaprayoganibandhanā । ekaprayogatā
cāṅgāṅgibhāvenetyupākaraṇāṅgameva parivyāṇam । <b>nanu yadyapi ktvāpratyayādaṅgāṅgitā</b> bhavati ।
tathāpi viparītaṃ kasmānna bhavatītyatrāha---<b>tatra ca paśvarthataiva prāpnoti yūpasyāpi tadarthatvāt</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---nopākaraṇaṃ parivyāṇārthaṃ tathā hi sati yūpārthataiva sarvasya syāt । sā cāyuktā
yūṣasyāpi paśvaṅgatvāt । tasmāt paśvaṅgameva raśaneti । <b>siddhāntavādī tu samānakartṛkatā-
mātraṃ ktvāpratyayādavasīyate na niyogaikyamiti yūpasya dvitīyātaḥ prādhānyaṃ yuktamiti
siddhāntitavān</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā dvitīyātaḥ <b>prādhānyāvagamaḥ</b> na tathā ktvāpratyayāt,
kintu vimarśāntarāpekṣa iti 1dvitīyāvaśena yūpārthaparivyāṇānupraveśinī raśanāpi yūpārthā ।
<b>nanu caikaniyogādṛte samānakartṛkataiva na saṃbhavati</b> । dvitīyātvanīpsitārthāpi saṃbhavati ।
<b>satyaṃ na saṃbhavati kintu adhikāraikyāt siddhaṃ samāna kartṛkatvam</b> nanu tarhi kiṃ ktvā-
pratyayena, evamucyatāṃ---<q>‘trivṛtā yūpaṃ parivyayati’</q> iti । <b>ucyate</b>---kālārthā ktvāśrutiḥ ।
<note>(1) G. dvitīyārthāpannā</note>
﻿<pb n="1069"/>
atrāha---<b>nanu kālalakṣaṇā atra naiva saṃbhavati । uccāraṇakālavibhāgo hi ktvāpratya-
yotpattau heturityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---nānuṣṭhānakālapūrvatā ktvāpratyayotpattau hetuḥ । kintu
uccāraṇapūrvakālatā । ataḥ kathamanuṣṭhāne pūrvakālatopadeśaḥ syāditi । <b>satyamuktam sa
evoccāraṇakālo'nuṣṭhāne'pi lakṣaṇayocyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---ktvāpratyayasyānanyaparatvāt
uccāraṇagato'pi kālo lakṣaṇatayā'nuṣṭhāne vidhīyate । <b>sarvatra kālavidhāviyameva pratipattiḥ
loke vede ca</b> । tatrāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ <b>samānakartṛkatāpi naiva tatrādriyate kālaniṣṭhatvā-
nniyogasya</b> । yata eva kālavidhipare vākye samānakartṛkatā'vagamyamānāpi na vivakṣitā
ekatvavat । <b>ata eva ca <q>‘darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvā somena yajeta’</q> iti samānakartṛ-
katācodyaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavati । prayojanamuktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>svaruścāpyekadeśatvāt</b> । <q>‘yūṣasya svaruṃ karoti’</q> iti śrūyate । kathaṃ yūpārthatā
svarorāśaṅkyate । na hi ṣaṣṭhī tādarthyamāha, tatrāha---<b><q>‘yūpasya svaruṃ’</q> iti svarumān yūpa iti
matvarthaḥ pratīyate gomānitivat tādarthyaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । dṛṣṭo hi tādarthye sati</b>
<note>(1) P. 1271</note>
﻿<pb n="1070"/>
<b>matvarthaḥ । evamatrāpītyabhiprāyaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---<q>‘yūpasya svaruṃ karoti’</q> iti svarostāvat
kalpayitavyaṃ tādarthyam । <q>‘yūpasya svaruṃ’</q> ityatra svarumān yūpa iti matvarthaḥ pratīyate ।
matvarthaśca prāyeṇa tādarthye sati dṛṣṭa iti tatraiva tādarthyakalpanā yuktā । tenotpattivākye
prayojanāvagamāt yūpārtha eva svaruḥ । svaruṇā yūpamanak‍tīti ca tasyaivāñjanena pratipattiḥ ।
<b>rāddhāntavādī tu yavamatītyevamādiṣu anaikānyāt paśumanak‍tīti ca dvitīyānirdeśāt
dṛṣṭārthatvācca paśvarthataiveti</b> manyate iti vyavahitena <b>saṃbandhaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---na tāvanma-
tuvarthasya niyamaḥ yavamatītyevamādiṣu vyabhicārāt । paśumiti ca dvitīyayā añjanasyāpi
kāryāntaraśravaṇāt । añjanā(tā)rthatve ca svaroḥ kriyānirvṛttyā dṛṣṭārthatvāccāñ‍janārtha eva svaruḥ
<b>ṣaṣṭhī tu utpa1ttisaṃyogepyupapannaivetyadoṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---pratīyamāno'pi tāvanmatvarthaḥ śeṣa-
tāvyabhicārī prāyikādapi kathā nānupapannā । añjane vākyena viniyogāt । nacāñjanameva
pratipattiḥ paśuṃ ityañjanasyāpi dvitīyayā kāryāntaraśravaṇāt । añjanārthatve ca svaroḥ kriyā-
nirvṛttiśca dṛṣṭo'rthaḥ । na/?/ ca ṣaṣṭhī matvarthamapyekāntato'vagamayati utpattisaṃyogenāpi yūpārthānu---
niṣpannatayā ca ghaṭamānatvāt । <b>prayojanamuk‍tam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>darśapūrṇamāsayorijyāḥ prādhānyaviśeṣāt</b> । paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇe <q>‘ya evaṃ vidvān
paurṇamāsīṃ yajate’</q> <q>‘ya evaṃ vidvānamāvāsyāṃ yajate’</q> iti samudāyānuvādāviti sthitam ।
tathā'nuvādapakṣepi kālasaṃbandhitayā śravaṇādutpattikālayogināmevānuvādaḥ na sarveṣāṃ rūpavatā-

﻿<pb n="1071"/>
miti sthitam । idānīmadhikāravākyagataṃ yajiśabdaṃ prati cintā kiṃ sarve yāgā adhikāra
prati vidhīyante utānūditā eveti । nanu ca yathākālamevādhikārasaṃbandho nyāyaḥ । upapadānu-
rodhāt 1teṣāmevādhikārasaṃbandho nyāyyaḥ kālasaṃbandhasya vidyamānatvāt samudāyānuvādavākyavat ।
tasmāt kathamatra pūrvapakṣe sarvayāgānāṃ samapradhānatāśaṅkā ityatrāha---<b>sthitaṃ rājasūyādhikaraṇe
'nijyā vyudasyante yajiśabdasaṃyogenādhikāraśravaṇāt yatraiva ca dhāturvartate tatraivopapadaṃ
nāmatayā vartata iti nāmadheyavicāre sthitam । ataḥ pūrvapakṣavādī yāgamātravacano'yaṃ
yajiḥ । yatra yajiḥ tatravopapadaṃ vartata iti manvāno dvivacanāntasarūpamevedamabhidhānaṃ
manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---yajirayaṃ yāgamātravacanaḥ na kālayogiyāgasamudāyavacanaḥ kāla-
saṃbaddhāśca yāgā bahavaḥ teṣu dvivacanāntamupapadaṃ nāñjasyena vartitumarhati । anāñjase ca
dvivacane kālayogiṣveva darśapūrṇamāsapadaṃ nākhyātādbhedena vartate । kintu sanni-

bahuvacanārthe । ekayajyabhidhānatayā vā tadanūditasamudāyābhiprāyamekabacanārthe
draṣṭavyamiti । <b>yatpunaḥ <q>‘prayāje prayāje kṛṣṇalaṃ juhoti’</q> iti vikṛtiṣu darśanaṃ tatkatha---</b>

﻿<pb n="1072"/>
<b>masmin pakṣe bhaviṣyati ?</b> yadi sarve yāgāḥ pradhānabhūtāḥ tadā prayājānāṃ pradhānatvāt

<b>yatpunaḥ <q>‘ya evaṃ vidvānamāvāsyāṃ yajate’</q> <q>‘ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajate’</q>

ca bahava iti dvivacanaṃ na ghaṭate dvivacanānupapattau satyāṃ na bhedena nāma vartate । na cobhayapadānu-
rodhī kaścidyāgo'sti iti nopapadānusārī yajiḥ । kiṃ tarhi yajyanusāryupapadamiti ।

tenāmāvāsyākālānuvādo nāvagamyate । tenānyatvamadhikāraviṣayasyāvagamyate । tena <b>rāyajasūya-

<b>tathāpi samudāyadvayasya prakṛtatvāt dvivacanasya cārthāntarānupapatteḥ । saṃbhavati ca

kintupapadārthavirodhābhidhāne nāsti pramāṇamityuktamasmābhiḥ</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---na
prakṛtaṃ parityajyate yajeteti yajiḥ prakṛta eva vartate । kintupapadānuguṇyāt kālayogiṣu

āpannasamudāyabhāveṣu vartata iti । <b>yacca darśaśabdaśravaṇānna prakṛtapratyabhijñā'stīti

<p><b>jyotiṣṭome tulyāni</b> । nanu jyotīṃṣi stomā asyeti bahuvrīhiṇā somayāga
eva pradhāno'vagamyate । athocyeta satyaṃ stomavattā somayāgānāṃ kintu jyotiṣṭomatā nāstīti
bahuvrīhyartha evātra nopapadyate iti ananvitasvārthatvāt yajimātrasyāpi kārakasaṃbandha1 iti ।
tanna vākyaśeṣe trivṛdādistotrāṇāṃ jyotiṣṭvakīrtanāt । arthavādakīrtitenāpi vyapadeśo
dṛśyate2 eva <q>‘āgneyo vai brāhmaṇaḥ’</q> itivat । tasmāta kathamatra pūrvapakṣa ityatrāha---<b>iha tu
dvivacanādyabhāvāt na yāgamātrapratipattiḥ śakyate vārayitum</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā
darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti dvivacanānurodhānna sarvayogeṣu vṛttiḥ tatheha nāsti kiñcit । tasmānna
yāgamātre vṛttiḥ śakyate vārayitum । nanu jyotiṣṭomaprātipadikādeva vārayituṃ śakyate
tatrāha---<b>jyotiṣṭomaśabdasya ca nāmadheyatvāt pravṛttau nimittamabhidheyaṃ nānvayītyuk‍taṃ
nāmadheyavicāre</b>। asyārthaḥ---<b>na jyotiṣṭe maśabdo yajeḥ viśeṣakaḥ kiṃ tarhi,</b> nāmamātram ।
<b>na</b> hi vidhīyamānasya viśeṣaṇaṃ <b>vivakṣituṃ nyāyyam</b> । na ca aruṇaikahāyanīnyāyaḥ saṃbhavati ।
jyotiṣṭomaśabdasyārthāntarābhāvāt <b>bhāvārthamātrasya ca niyogena</b> sākṣātsaṃbandhāt । tasmāda-
viśiṣṭaṃ yajimātramatra pradhānaṃ <b>ayajirevātrāpyaṅgaṃ, rājasūyavat nāmāpi tadvat</b> । atrocyate

﻿<pb n="1076"/>
---yadi nāmatvādananvayitvamuktamasmābhiḥ syādetadevaṃ, yadi yadyannāma tattat kāryānvayi bhavatī-

udbhidādayaḥ kārye'nvayavantaḥ । tena kārye'nanvayinaḥ uktāḥ, na satyanvaye nāmatvādananva-

yuktamiti bhāvaḥ । <b>kiṃ naśchinnam</b> tathāpi rāddhāntassiddha eva । etaccābhyupagamyavāda-
mātram । <b>kintu viśeṣaṇapadamapyetannāmaiva, arthāntarānupapatteḥ । yajyarthasya viśeṣa-
mātrāvagamahetutvāt । ato'nvitamapi viśeṣaṇamātraniṣṭhamiti nāmaiva arthāntarānupādā-
nāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---nedaṃ nīlādivadviśeṣaṇaṃ, kintu etannāmānuguṇyena yajireva
viśiṣṭe yāge vartate । yadi hi yāgamātre varteta tadā nām‍no ['rthānvayaśca yāge syāt ।
tasya ca somayāgavacanatvāt । tenaitadanuroddhaṃ viśiṣṭe yāge yajireva vartate]
'tiparokṣā vṛttirāśrayaṇīyā tenaitadvirodhādviśiṣṭe yāge vartate yajireva । jyotiṣṭo-
mapadamapi tatraiva nāmatayā vartate arthāntarānupasthāpakatvāt । nanvevaṃ vaiśvadevena
yajetetyatrāpi kimiti vaiśvadevapadānurodhāt yajiḥ vaiśvadevyāmikṣāsādhyeyāga eva na vartate ।
tataśca vaiśvadevapadamapi tasyaiva nāmāstu na sarveṣām ।</p>

<p>atrocyate---1dvividhaṃ hi nāma, kiñcit pravṛttaṃ, kiñcicca pravartyaṃ, yatra vākyāntarālo-
canayā yāge pravṛttiravadhāritā, tatpravṛttaṃ nāma । yathā darśapūrṇamāsau iti । kālavacanayo-
rapyanayoḥ anutpādāt āgneyādivacanatā । tathā jyotiṣṭomaśabdo'pi pravṛttanāma ।
arthavādālocanayā yāge pravṛttyavagateḥ । pravṛttena ca nāmnā vākyāntareṇa yajirviśeṣe'vasthāpyate
tannirapekṣanāmatvāvagateḥ । rājasūyaśabdastu yadyapi rājā somaḥ sūyate'sminniti vyutpattyā
somābhiṣavasaṃbandhāt somayāge pravṛttanāma tathāpi na yajiṃ viśeṣe'vasthāpayitumalam, svārājya-
phalatvātkarmaṇaḥ । rājā sūyate asmāditi vyutpattyantasaṃbhavāt । yasya nānyato yāge pravṛtti-
ravagatā, kintu svavākyagatayajisāmānādhikaraṇyenaiva kalpyā tat pravartyaṃ nāma । yathā
vaiśvadevaśabdaḥ । sa hi sūktahaviṣoriti niyamāt sūktahaviṣoreva vartate na yāge । tena
vaiśvadevena yajeteti yajisāmānādhikaraṇyāt asya nāmatā kalpyā । tataśca pūrvaprakṛtayāgavartinaṃ
yajiṃ na viśeṣe'vasthāpayitumalamiti siddham । anuvādavākyagataśca yajireva yathotpattikāla-
yogiṣveva tava vartate teṣāmevāmāvāsyāpaurṇamāsīśabdau nāmanī tathā paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇe
uktamiti । iti nāmacatuṣṭayavivekaḥ ।</p>

viśvadevaśabdena yāge vaiśvadevaśabdo vartate viś‍veṣāṃ devānāmiti । na ca
saṃbandhaḥ viś‍vairdevaiḥ vihitairvā syāt vidhīyamānairvā । tatra vidhīyamānatā
tāvat na saṃbhavati āmikṣāyā vihitatvāt । anyatra cāśakyatvāt ।
avidhīyamānatayā tu sarveṣāmapi vyapadeśo ghaṭate daṇḍivat yathaikapuruṣavarti-
nāpi daṇḍena sarva eva daṇḍhino'bhidhīyante । tena vyapadeśamātrasidhyarthe
vyapadeśānna vidhirāśrayaṇīyaḥ । vyapadeśaścedupapanno yajiṃ saṅkoca-
yitumarhati ।</note>
﻿<pb n="1078"/>
<note>nanvevamatrāpi jyotiṣṭomaśabdo'pi somayāgasāhacaryāt yāgāntare varteta ।
ucyate---adhikāravākye sāṅgo yāgo vidhīyate । nānūdyate । tena jyoti-
ṣṭomaśabdavācyayāgaviṣayo niyogaḥ pratīyate । na ca svārthatayā sarvān
yāgān gṛhṇāti । gṛhītānāṃ ca kathaṃ syādanvaya iti cintāyāṃ na sarve yāgāḥ
karaṇatayā'nvayaṃ yānti nāmno'tiparokṣapravṛttyāpatteḥ । tena somayāgā
eva sarve karaṇatayā'nvayaṃ yānti । tadā na ca nām‍no'tiparokṣavṛttiprasaṅgaḥ ।
tena somayāgasyeva prādhānyaṃ vaiśvadevenetītyanuvādaḥ । sa ca prakṛtāpekṣī ।
prakṛtāpekṣitve ca sarveṣāmanuvādaḥ । nanvevaṃ ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajate
ityanuvādaḥ syāt nākālasaṃbandhanibandhanenānuvādaḥ tathā tatraivok‍tam ।
ataḥ kālayogināmevānuvādaḥ rājasūyaśabde tu sarvayāgānāṃ karaṇābhāvena
nām‍no na kācitkṣatiḥ । yasmādrājāsūyate yasmin karmaṇīti phala-
nibandhanameva nāmeti ।</note>
<trailer>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ caturthasya 
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="1079"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>atha ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>śrutilakṣaṇamānupūrvyaṃ</b> । atra bhāṣyakāreṇa prayojakāprayojakalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamityuktam ।
tadākṣipati---<b>nanu kratvarthapuruṣārthacintāpi tatra vṛttā । kimidaṃ prayojakāprayojakalakṣaṇaṃ
vṛttamiti</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi tāvat saṃkṣepeṇādhyāyārthaḥ kīrtyate tadevaṃ kīrtanīyam ।
aupadānikaṃ vastuvṛttamiti । atha vistareṇa tataḥ kratvarthapuruṣārthāṅgapradhānaphalavidhyarthavādā
api kīrtanīyāḥ । kimiti prayojakāprayojakameva kīrtyate । teṣāmapi caturthe cinti-
tatvāditi । <b>ucyate---kramacintāyāmasyaivopayogāt</b> । prayojakāprayojakalakṣaṇameva
kramacintāyāmupayogi yasmāt tasmāttadeva kīrtyate nāparam anupayogitvāt । <b>vakṣyamāṇaupa-
yikaṃ hi vṛttaṃ kīrtyate</b> । yasya hi vakṣyamāṇamarthaṃ pratyupāyabhāvaḥ tadevātra kīrtyate । <b>na
vṛttatayā</b> vṛttamityetāvatā na vṛttaṃ saṅkīrtanīyam । kathamupāyatvaṃ kramacintāyāṃ prayojakā-
prayojakalakṣaṇasyetyāha---<b>ekaprayogaprayuktānāṃ hi kramo bhavati nāprayuktānāmiti prayojakā-
prayojakasaṅkīrtanam</b> । ekena prayogeṇa prayogavidhinā prayojyānāṃ svasidhyarthamākṣiptānuṣṭhānā-
nāṃ padārthānāṃ anuṣṭhānavitānarūpaḥ kramo bhavati । nāprayuktānām । tena prayojakatve jñāte
<note>(1) P. 1284</note>
﻿<pb n="1080"/>
kramajñānamutpadyate anuṣṭhānavaitatyena ca prayogaparyantaprayojakatvaṃ nirvahatīti parasparāpekṣitayā'sti
saṃbandha iti yuk‍taṃ prayojakāprayojakasaṅkīrtanam । <b>yadi prayuktānāṃ kramaścintyate avidheya-
starhi kramaḥ</b> । yadi prayuktānāṃ satāmuttarakālaṃ kramaścintyate avidheyastarhi kramaḥ । tataśca
pratītimātreṇa kramasvīkāre pratītānāṃ tadāśaṅkā na yuk‍teti bhāvaḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ prayuktyuttara-
kālabhāvitvenāvidheyatvamityatrāha---<b>vihitaṃ hi prayujyate nāprayuktasya vidhānamiti</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---tat vidheyamityucyate yadvidhinā svasiddha‍yarthamupādīyate । tathā coktaṃ śyenagranthe
---<q>“yattu siddha‍yarthamupādīyate tadvidheyamiti tantre vyavahāraḥ”</q> iti । tena vidheyatvaṃ prayuktatvena
vyāptam । taddarśayati---yadvihitaṃ tatprayujyate । yatpunarna prayujyate tadvidheyamapi na bhavati iti
vyāpakabhūtaprayuktinivṛttau vyāpyabhūtasya vidheyatvasya nivṛttiriti । pariharati
---<b>kena voktaṃ kramo vidhīyata iti</b> । nanu yadyavidheyaḥ kimiti tarhi cintyate vidheyatve
hi kramasya siddhānte kiṃ kramo vidhīyate na veti cintā yuk‍tetyāśaṅkya cintāviṣayaṃ svarūpaṃ
cāha---<b>na vihitavitānamevātra cintyate । kiṃ yathā pratipannavihitavitānamanuṣṭheyaṃ
utāniyameneti</b> । vihitā ye padārthāsteṣāṃ prayogāvasthāyāṃ yo'yaṃ vitānaḥ sa evātra cintyate ।
yo'yaṃ śrutyādibhiḥ pratipanno vihitavitānaḥ kiṃ tamananikramyānuṣṭheyaṃ anuṣṭhānaṃ kartavya utāniya-
meneti । pratipannaścāsau vihitavitānaśceti karmadhārayaṃ kṛtvā paścādyathāśabdena sahāvyayī-
bhāvaḥ । <b>evaṃ ca vadatā</b> asminnadhikaraṇe sarva eva śrutyādyavagamyaḥ kramaḥ kimādaraṇīyaḥ
uta neti cintyata iti pradarśitam । pradarśanamātratayā tu śrutikrama udāhṛtaḥ । <b>kathaṃ punari-
tyatrāyamāśayaḥ</b>---pratītamātreṇa kramādare pratītānādarāśaṅkā'nupapannā । 1vidheyatayā svīkāre tu
<note>(1) G. vidheyayoḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="1081"/>
pratītasyāpyavidheyatā yuk‍teti । pariharati---<b>viniyogaśūnyatvāt vihitavitānāvagamasya</b> ।
yathāpratipatti anuṣṭhānamāśaṅkyate iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ । asyārthaḥ---vitānābhidhāyakaḥ
śabdaḥ kaścinnāsti । yaśca nābhidhīyate nāsau viniyujyate tārtīyaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ । nāpi
caikatvādivat viniyogenāpyupādānaśeṣī kriyate । tena tārtīyacāturthikaviniyogarahitatvāt
vitānapratyayasyādaraṇīyatā nāsti । avidheyatve'pi kramasyeyameva yuktiḥ abhidhānaśūnya
tayā1 viniyogābhāvenānaṅgatvāt । vidhinā ca svasiddha‍yarthatvenāprayuk‍teriti । <b>nāntarīyako
hi vidheyāvagatau vitānapratyayaḥ</b> bahuṣu padārtheṣu ekena kartrā prayujyamāneṣu nāntarīyako'yaṃ
vitāna(vat prayogaḥ prayoga) pratyayo nābhidhānika ityarthaḥ । upasaṃharati---<b>yaścārthādartho na sa
codanārtha iti manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī aniyamaṃ manyate</b> । tena pratītamātreṇāpi kramasvīkāre
anādarāśaṅkā upapadyata eveti samarthitam । <b>nanu ca <q>‘adhvaryurgṛhapatiṃ dīkṣayitvā’</q> ityatra
kramavidhānamevopanyastaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa</b> । dīkṣāṇāṃ prāptatvāt ityanena granthena <b>vidheyāntarā-
bhāvāt</b> kramavidhānārthaiva śrutiriti <b>vadatā</b> । tenāvidheyatvābhidhānaṃ bhāṣyaviruddhamiti
vadati । idānīṃ pariharati---<b>yadyevaṃ yadi</b> vidheyāntarābhāvena kramavidhānamayuktaṃ tarhi yasmāda-
<b>styevātra vidheyāntaraṃ anenāmī dīkṣitavyā iti kartṛviśeṣavidhānām</b> । adhvaryvādi-
dīkṣāsu pratiprasthātrādikartṛviśeṣavidhānamapyatra pratīyate । nanu <q>‘adhvaryurgṛhapatiṃ’</q> ityatra tarhi
<note>(1) G. tayāpi</note>
﻿<pb n="1082"/>
vidheyāntaraṃ nāsti adhvaryoścodakata eva prāptatvāt, atrāha---<b>adhvaryuvidhāvapi niyamaḥ</b> ye
yajamānāsta ṛtvija ityanena vākyena yajamānā evārtvijeṣu viniyuktāḥ । tenādhvaryustāva-
nnivartitaḥ । kintu kenacidyajamānena kecidyajamānā dīkṣayitavyāḥ । tatra ṛtvikkarma-
karatayā te yajamānā eva tena tenartvigviśeṣavācinā adhvaryvādiśabdenocyante । tatra
yenaiva kiñcidādhvaryavaṃ kṛtavatā adhvaryuvyapadeśo labdhaḥ tenaivāparamapyādhvaryavaṃ kartavyamiti nāsti
niyāmakaṃ pramāṇaṃ ata āha---<b>adhvaryuvidhāvapi niyama iti</b> । tena pratiprasthātrādi-
vidhirapi niyamārtha eveti mantavyam । <b>kiṃ heyamevedaṃ bhāṣyaṃ ?</b> yadi dīkṣāṇāṃ prāptatvena
kramavidhānārthaiva śrutirityāha---<b>tadbhāṣyaṃ kiṃ heyameva</b> । neti vadāmaḥ । <b>yadidaṃ ktveti
paurvāparyamabhidhāne gamyate kartṛvidhau tadanuṣṭhānaupayikatayaiva kartṛvidhāvupayujyate na
saṃbandhividhāviti tanniṣṭhā śrutirityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---na ktvāpratyayastāvat anuṣṭhānagataṃ
paurvāparyamāha । kintu samānakartṛkatāmeva । prayogagatāṃ tu pūrvakālatāṃ upādhitvena
svīkaroti । tena ktvāntaṃ pūrvaṃ prayoktavyaṃ; yacca pūrvaṃ prayujyate tadarthaḥ pūrvamavagamyate ।
yacca pūrvamavagamyate tatpūrvamanuṣṭhīyate aparaṃ ca paścāt । tena prayogavitativiśeṣo'vagamyate
teva ktvāśrutibalena vitānāvagateḥ śrauto'yaṃ kramaḥ । atha kasmāt pāṭhakrameṇāyaṃ kramaniyamo
na bhavatīti cenna । dīkṣāṇāṃ codakataḥ prāptatvāt vākyasya ca kartṛviśeṣavidhānārthatvāt
yadi dīkṣaiva yāvadvidhīyate tadotpattivākyekrameṇānuṣṭhānamapi bhavet । yenaiva krameṇotpatti-
vākyānyuccāryante tenaiva tadarthāvagatiḥ avagatikrameṇa cānuṣṭhāne kramo'pi bhavati, avagati-
nibandhanatvādanuṣṭhānakramasya । codakaprāptā tu dīkṣā na vākyenāvagamyate iti na tatra
pāṭhakrameṇa kramāvagatiḥ kiṃ tarhi ktvāśrutita eveti । akṣarayojanātu---yadidaṃ ktveti
śruterupādhibhūtaṃ paurvāparyamabhidhāne śabdaprayoge'vagamyate kartṛvidhau tat kartṛvidhāvanuṣṭhānaupayika-
﻿<pb n="1083"/>
tayaivopayujyate vitativiśeṣāvagamaṃ vinānuṣṭhānābhāvāt । anuṣṭhānaupayikakramāvagamahetutvādanu-
ṣṭhānaupayikaṃ paurvāparyam । kartṛvidhānapakṣe tu dīkṣāṇāmavidheyatvānna pāṭhataḥ kramaḥ api tu
śruteḥ । saṃbandhividhau tu kramasaṃbandhidīkṣāvidhau tu pāṭhata evānuṣṭhāne'pi kramāvagateḥ nānu-
ṣṭhānaupayikatayopayujyate । kintu śabdasādhutāmātreṇeti hetostanniṣṭhā kramaniṣṭhāśrutirityuk‍taṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇa । tena bhāṣyākṣarāṇyevaṃ yojyāni । dīkṣāṇāṃ prāptatvādiha vākye tāsāma-
vidheyatvāt pāṭhataḥ kramānavagateḥ ktvāśrutireva kramavidhānārthā kramāvagatyartheti yāvat ।
vidhānavācoyuktistu gauṇī vidheyavatkrame'pi tātparyaśruteḥ iti darśayitum । tena śrutilakṣaṇamānu-
pūvyamiti sūtraṃ adhvaryurbrahmāṇaṃ ityatra śrauta eva kramo na pāṭhakrama iti darśayituṃ sūtrakāreṇa
praṇītamiti darśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa । tenāye vicāraḥ---kiṃ ‘adhvaryurityādivākye śrutikramo'yaṃ
uta pāṭhakrama iti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī avadānavākyavat pāṭhakramo'yamityāha । rāddhāntavādī
tu codakata eva dīkṣāṇāṃ prāptatvāt utpattau nāsti dīkṣāṇāṃ pāṭhakrama iti nāyaṃ pāṭhakramaḥ ।
kintu śrutikrama evāyamiti । cintāprayojanaṃ tu yatra codakataḥ prāpteṣu anyapare vākye
śrutirnāsti tatra pāṭhata eva kramo nādaraṇīyaḥ iti । evaṃ ca varṇakadvayamatra । prathamavarṇake
sarvakramādarānādaravicāraḥ । dvitīye tu kimayaṃ śrautakramaḥ uta pāṭhakrama iti vicāraḥ । ayaṃ
ca tṛtīyaḥ punaruktiparihāraḥ । dvitīyetu punaruktyāśaṅkāparihāre kramādarānādaravicāreṇa
ekameva varṇakamiti mantavyam । prathamastu parihāraḥ paramatenoktaḥ । ata evāparitoṣeṇa
parihārāntaramuktam । tṛtīyaparihārastu viṣayavyāp‍tyartha iti । kasmāt punaḥ kramasya
vidheyatvameva paramārthato nāṅgīkriyate yena vidheya iva tanniṣṭhatāmātreṇa gauṇo vidheyavyapadeśo
varṇyata ityatrāha---<b>aprayuk‍tasyāvidheyatvameva heturuk‍taḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi hyaprayuktasyāpi
vidheyatvaṃ syāt tadā kramo'pi paramārthata eva vidheyaḥ syāt na tvidamastīti । yadi
śrutyavagatapaurvāparyabalāyātaḥ kramaḥ śrauto bhavati <b>evaṃ tarhi hṛdayasyāgre'vadyatyatha jihvāyā atha
vakṣasa ityetadapyudāharaṇamatra syāt</b> । atrāpyagrāthaśabdābhyāṃ paurvāparyabalena kramāvagateḥ ।
﻿<pb n="1084"/>
<b>neti brūmaḥ</b> । naitadudāharaṇamiti brūmaḥ <b>pāṭhādavagatasyāyamathaśabdo'nuvādaḥ</b> । idaṃ vākya-
mavadānavidhāyakaṃ tenotpattivākyena kramāvadhāraṇaṃ pāṭhata eva । <b>kartṛviśeṣavidhau punartānyataḥ
kramo'vagantuṃ śakyate'nyadataḥ ktvāpratyayāt । kartṛvidhirayaṃ na dīkṣāvidhiḥ । tena</b>
dīkṣāṇāṃ nāyamutpattiścodanālakṣaṇa iti nānyataḥ pāṭhādayaṃ kramo'vagantuṃ śakyate । ataḥ ktvā-
pratyayādvinā'nyaḥ śabdo'pi [vitā]nārthe vartata iti sūk‍taṃ prayojakāprayojakalakṣaṇasaṅkīrtanam ।
saṃprati pūrvapakṣamāha---<b>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ nāntarīyako'yaṃ niyama ādriyate । na hyacodanā-
lakṣaṇasya codanālakṣaṇaniyoganirvṛttāvaṅgatopapadyate</b> । yatkhalu acodanālakṣaṇaṃ na tasya
codanālakṣaṇaniyoganirvṛttāvaṅgatopapadyate । taduk‍taṃ---‘na cāvihitamaṅgaṃ bhavati” iti ।
yaccāṅgaṃ na tanniyamenādaraṇīyam । siddhāntamāha-<b>satyaṃ nopapadyate</b> । satyamaṅgatā nopapadyate
yata evāṅgaṃ kramo na bhavati ata eva ca nānuṣṭhīyate । nāpyupādīyate padārthāstvanuṣṭhīyante
na kramaḥ, kintu anuṣṭhīyamāneṣu bahuṣu padārtheṣu ekakartṛkeṣvarthāt kramo vitatirūpa āpatati ।
yadyanaṅgaṃ kramaḥ kimiti tarhi tanniyamādaraṇaṃ tatrāha---<b>kintu arthaprāptaṃ kramāntaraṃ niruṇaddhi ।
tasyānavagamādityucyate śrutyādibhiḥ</b> । krame hyavagate kramāntarāvagatireva nodeti । yathā-
vagati cānuṣṭhānaṃ buddhipūrvakāriṇāmiti kramaniyamānādaraḥ । <b>ato'napekṣatvamivāvidhīya-
mānamapyupakārāyaiva bhavatīti na doṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā'napekṣatvaṃ na vidhīyate
1tathānuṣṭhānopakāri bhavati tathā yadyapi kramo na vidhīyate tathāpyanuṣṭhānopayogi bhavati kramarahita-
<note>(1) G. athavā'nuṣṭhānopakārā bhavanti</note>
﻿<pb n="1085"/>
syānuṣṭhānāsaṃbhavāditi na doṣaḥ । <b>punaruktyādyāśaṅkā tūktā</b> । prathamaṃ punaruk‍tatāśaṅkā ।
punaścāptasmaraṇe prayojane darśite vṛttikāreṇa tatkāryamityāśaṅkā darśitā bhāṣye uktā ।</p>
<p><b>arthācca । evaṃ tāvadananyaparā(rthā)kṣaratayā niyamitaḥ kramaḥ idānīṃ kāryānu-
rodhena kramo'pi niyamyate tatparatvāt padārthānuṣṭhānasya</b> । pūrvaṃ tāvat ktvākṣarāṇāmananya-
paratayā kramaniyamamātraparatvāt kramaniyamo2varṇitaḥ । adhunā yadyapi kramaparāṇyakṣarāṇi na
santi tathāpi kāryānurodhena kramo niyamyate । yena kālayogena kāryaṃ saṃpadyate tena tāvat
paurvāparyamāśrayaṇīyam । tadvaśena yā vitatiḥ saivādaraṇīyā kāryaparatvātpadārthānuṣṭhānasya, kāryaṃ
nirvartsyatīti padārthā anuṣṭhīyante । tena tadanurodhenaiva 3kālaviśeṣaparigrahaḥ tannāntarīyakaśca
kramo'pyāśrayaṇīyaḥ । atra pūrvapakṣāśaṅketyantamuktvā anananyaparākṣatarayā śrutyā kramāvagamaḥ,
arthe tu na kiñcit avagatau pramāṇamasti prayojanamātratvāt prayojanasya । rāddhāntastu
prayojanamapi bhavati anuṣṭhānakālabhedāvagamadvāreṇa kramāvagatau kāraṇamiti---<b>tatra ca pradarśitānyu-
dāharaṇāni । kiṃ pāṭhakramasyāyaṃ bādhaḥ</b> । <q>‘agnihotraṃ juhoti’</q> <q>‘yavāgūṃ pacati’</q> iti
pāṭhādanyādṛśaḥ kramaḥ । arthāccānyādṛśaḥ । tatra pāṭhakramaṃ bādhitvā'rthakramaḥ svīkriyata
iti bruvan bhāṣyakāro bādhamiva darśayati । taccāyuktam । kramakopādhikaraṇena punaruktatvā-
dityāśayaḥ । <b>neti brūmaḥ idamapi kramaniyamahetukāraṇaṃ na kasyacidvirodhitayā pradarśyate</b> ।
<note>(1) P. 1290</note> <note>(2) G. niyamo'vatīrṇaḥ</note> <note>(3) kārya</note>
﻿<pb n="1086"/>
idamapyarthākhyaṃ kramaniyamasya yo hetuḥ kālaviśeṣaḥ tasya kāraṇaṃ pradarśyate । na kasya
cidvirodhitayā । <b>balābalacantāyāṃ tu virodhe balīyastvaṃ ca</b> pradarśyate kramakopīdhi-
karaṇe । <b>iha punaḥ</b> arthākhyapramāṇa<b>svarūpapratipattyarthamevedaṃ vacanamupanyastam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>aniyamo'nyatra । yatra kramaniyamapramāṇamuk‍taṃ</b> śrutyarthātmakaṃ <b>vakṣyamāṇaṃ ca
pāṭhādikaṃ nāsti tatrāniyama eva</b> । anuṣṭhānasvabhāvena kramamātrāvagateḥ । kimudāharaṇaṃ
tatrāha---<b>yathā śākhāntarīyāṅgavidhānaṃ śākhāntara upasaṃhriyamāṇaṃ,</b> tatra hi pāṭhato'pi
kramaniyamo nāstīti pratyudāharaṇamātramidam ।</p>
<p><b>krameṇa vā niyamyeta । yatra punastātparyamakṣarāṇāṃ nāsti, yathā ‘adhvaryuḥ, ityādau;
na ca kāryato virodhaḥ yathā</b> yavāgūpāke yathāpāṭhamanuṣṭhīyamāne । <b>tatra kā kathā</b>
kramaniyamasya । yathā <q>‘samidho yajati, tanūnapātaṃ yajati’</q> iti । uttaraṃ---<b>tatrāpi</b>
<note>(1) P. 1290</note> <note>(2) P. 1291</note>
﻿<pb n="1087"/>
<b>pāṭhānniyamaḥ</b> yatkramaḥ pāṭhaḥ prayogo'pi tatkramaka eva bhavati । <b>nanu ca pāṭhakramāvagati-
rnimūlā । na tasyāḥ kiñcinnimittamasti । 1padānāṃ 2vākyārthāvagatihetutvāt</b>
yadi pratyastamitapadāvibhāgadvākyādeva vākyārthaḥ pratīyate tadā vācakapadābhāve'pi vākyādeveya-
marthāvagatiḥ ityavadhāryeta । na caitadasti । <b>nirmūlā cāvagatirna pramāṇam । pūrvo dhāvatītyatra
(parānvayaikye)parānvayāvagatiriva</b>pūrvasaṃbandhamūlā cāparāvagatiḥ syāt, nānvitāvagatiḥ ।
<b>tasmādyatheṣṭamatra kramaparigrahaṃ nyāyyaṃ manyate । maivaṃ vocaḥ । vākyakrama iva vākyārtha-
kramo'pi śabdanibandhana eva</b> । yādṛśo vākyakramaḥ tādṛśo vākyārthakramaḥ so'pi śabda-
nibandhana eva । yathā <b>na śabdādṛte śabdakramo'vagamyate</b> na śrutyā vinā śrutikramo'vagamyata
ityarthaḥ । <b>arthādṛte nārthakramaḥ । yasmiṃśca satyeva yadavagamyate avyabhicārāt tasya
tannimittamiti vadāmaḥ</b> । nanu ca padānāṃ vākyārthapratipattinimittatvāt pādabhāve
kramāvagatiriyamudīyamānāpi pratibhā, na pramāṇaṃ bhavitumarhati । ucyate---yathā'tra śabdasya
nimittatā tathocyate । yattāvat prathamaṃ paṭhyate tattāvat prathamamavagamyate tathā
prayogakāle prathamaṃ smaryate yathāsmaraṇamanuṣṭhanamiti tasyānuṣṭhānamapi prathamamavagamyate ।
tadanantarāvagatasya (smṛtasya) tadanantaramevānuṣṭhānam । evaṃ ca prayogavitatiravagamyata
iti । yata eva pāṭhakrameṇānuṣṭhānakramo'vagamyate । <b>ata eva ca niyatakramamadhyayanaṃ</b>
<note>(1) R. padārthānāṃ</note> <note>(2) G. vākyāvagati</note>
﻿<pb n="1088"/>
<b>dṛṣṭārthameva bhavati । anyatra kāryaviśeṣāt</b> yatra kāryaviśeṣo'vagamyate yathā yāvagūpāke
tatra hi niyatakramamadhyayanaṃ dṛṣṭārthaṃ na bhavati । yathaiva pāṭhādapi kramāvagatirbhavati
<b>ata eva ca lokikāḥ pāṭhakrameṇa dhūpādiṣu krame'vagate vyutkramābhidhāne pratiṣedhaṃ
kurvate । adṛṣṭārtheṣvapi taddarśitam</b> । dṛṣṭārtheṣu hi prayojanavaśenāpi kramo'vagamyate । adṛ-
ṣṭārtheṣvapi tu yo'yaṃ laukikānāṃ kramādaraḥ saḥ pāṭhakrameṇānuṣṭhānakramo'vagamyata ityetannibandhanaḥ ।
etaddarśitaṃ bhāṣye । upasaṃharati-<b>tasmādatrāpi na kramāntarakalpanā yukteti yuk‍tam</b> । yata eva
avagati nimittamātrasaṃbhavenāvagatimātreṇa kramasvīkāraḥ <b>ata eva <q>‘adhvayurgṛhapatiṃ dīkṣayitvā’</q>
ityevamādiṣu tātparyamātrāt kramasiddhiḥ</b> । ktvākṣaratāptaryamātreṇa kramasiddhiḥ । mātra-
grahaṇena ktvāpratyayenāvidhānamanabhidhānaṃ cāsya kramasya darśitam । anabhidheye ca tātparyamaviruddhaṃ
lakṣaṇāyāmiva । kasmātpunavidheyatvābhāvepi tātparyamātreṇa kramasiddhiḥ tatrāha---<b>nimittamātraṃ hi</b>
atra parigṛhyate na punarvidhayaparābhidhānameva pratipattau hetuḥ । avagatimātreṇa svīkāro yasya
tasyāvagatihetumātraṃ parigṛhyate na punarvidheya eva yo'vagatihetuḥ avagatimātreṇa kramasvīkāra
ityuktamupasaṃharati---<b>tasmāt sanimittā pratipattiḥ1 pramāṇamityuk‍taṃ pramāṇaparīkṣāyām ।
ato yāvatī sanimittā pratītiḥ sā sarvaiva kramāvadhāraṇe anyatra vā vedārthānuṣṭhāno---
pakāriṇī pramāṇamiti mantavyam । darśanamuktam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) G. pratītiḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="1089"/>
<p><b>pravṛttyā tulyakālānām । kimaparaṃ kramaniyame kāraṇamiti</b> । praśnenaivopakramaḥ ।
uttaraṃ---<b>pravṛttiriti brūmaḥ pravṛttyāpi hi kramabuddhirupajāyate</b> । pravṛttiranuṣṭhānaṃ tenāpyapara-
smin padārthe'nuṣṭheyarūpakramabuddhirupajāyate । yatkramakaṃ pūrvapadārthānuṣṭhānaṃ tatkramakamevottarapadārthānu-
ṣṭhānamapi pratīyata iti । <b>kathaṃ punarvaidikatvaṃ pravṛttikramasya</b> । nāyaṃ vedādavagamyat iti
bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>tadarthāśrayāt</b> । tadarthaṃ vedārthamāśrayati yato vedādanuṣṭhānam prathama-
padārthasaṃbandhyavagamyate । tataśca dvitīyādipadārthakrama iti pāramparyeṇāsti vaidikatvam ।
<b>tasmātpravṛttirapi niyamahetubhūtā । yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ <q>‘evaṃ pradhānapratyāsatti-
rbhavati’</q> iti tathā sauryādibhiśca sāmyamāśaṅkya punaḥ vaiṣamyābhidhānaṃ kastasyopayogaḥ?</b>
ekagranthenāha---<b>nātīva kramāvadhāraṇa upayujyata iti</b> । yadā hi pūrvapravṛttikrameṇottara-
padārthakramo'vagamyate tadā pradhānapratyāsattyupanyāso na yuktaḥ । tathā yadaparamuk‍taṃ <q>“yathā
sauryādiṣu kṛts‍naṃ guṇakāṇḍaṃ pradhānapratyāsattaye pratipradhānamapavṛjyate tathā prājāpatyeṣvapi syāt”</q>
iti sāmyamupanyasya punarvaiṣamyamuk‍taṃ “ekapayogacodanācoditatvāt prājāpatyānāmaṅgapradhānayaugapadye
prāpte 2puruṣāśaktyā yuktaḥ kramānupraveśaḥ । sauryādīnāṃ tu ekaprayogacodanānupraveśābhāvāt
sahacodanā nāstīti ekaikasya kṛts‍naṃ guṇakāṇḍaṃ apavṛjyeta3 iti vaiṣamyamuktaṃ tadapi nopayogi ।
<b>astyatropayogaḥ, pravṛttirnāma kramanirapekṣa kvacidanuṣṭhānaṃ, nirapekṣaṃ cedamanuṣṭhānaṃ pravṛttaṃ na</b>
<note>(1) P. 1293</note> <note>(2) G. puruṣe aśaktyā</note> <note>(3) G. upayujyate</note>
﻿<pb n="1090"/>
<b>punarapekṣāyāṃ prayojanamastīti manvānasyedamuttaraṃ---pradhānapratyāsattiḥ sahacodanā'vagatā
vaiṣamyāt pīḍitā syāt । sāmye punaḥ yathābhyanujñātaiva bhavatīti</b> । asyārthaḥ-prathama-
pravṛttivaśena dvitīyādipadārthānuṣṭhānakramāvagamo niyamyata iti etāvati pradarśite iyamāśaṅkā-
'vatarati---pravṛttyavasthāyāṃ hi yathā prathamapadārthānuṣṭhānaṃ kramaniyamanirapekṣamavagamyate tathā
dvitīyādipadārthānuṣṭhānamapi । yathāvagati cānuṣṭhānaṃ sarveṣāmapi kramaniyamanirapekṣaṃ yuktam ।
punardvitīyādipadārthānuṣṭhā[ne]kramaniyamāpekṣāyāṃ tu prayojanaṃ nāsti aniyatakramatayā prathama-
pravṛttiryā tathaivānuṣṭhānukramasiddhiriti na śakyate prathamapadārthapravṛttikrameṇottarapadārthakramāvagamaḥ
kartumitīmāmāśaṅkāmapaninīṣuḥ bhāṣyakāra uttaraṃ likhitavān prayogacodanayā sahāṅgaiḥ pradhānānāṃ
yaugapadyenānuṣṭhānasya coditatvāt puruṣaśaktyā yāvadva‍yavadhānamanupraviśati tāvadeva vidhiranu-
manyate nānyat । tatra yadi prathamapadārthapravṛttikrameṇottareṣāmapi padārthānāmanuṣṭhānaṃ bhavati
tadā sarveṣāmapi sadṛśameva vyavadhānam । itarathā kasyacidatisannidhānaṃ kasyacidativyavadhānamiti
vaiṣamye sati prayogacodanāvagate sannidhānavyavadhāne ubhe api bādhite syātām । anavagata-
sannidhānāśrayaṇepi hi yathāvagatasannidhānabādho bhavatyeveti prayogacodanānupālanāya punaḥ
kramaniyamāpekṣāstīti । prāvṛttikeca krame svīkriyamāṇe tadanupālanamiti <b>tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ</b>
prayogacodanāvagatapradhānapratyāsattisiddha‍yarthaṃ prāvṛttikakrama<b>niyamo'bhyupagantavyaḥ</b> । nanvevaṃ
sati prayogacodanāvagatapradhānapratyāsattinibandhano'yaṃ kramaniyama iti na prāvṛttiko vyapadeṣṭuṃ
yuktaḥ, tatrāha---<b>sa ca niyamaḥ prathamapravṛttipūrvaka iti tayaiva vyākhyāte । sauryādidarśana-
midānīṃ kimarthaṃ ?</b> ekaprayogānupraveśābhāve na yuktaṃ kṛts‍naṃ guṇakāṇḍāpavarjanaṃ sauryādiṣu ।
﻿<pb n="1091"/>
prājāpatyeṣu tu ekaprayogacodanācoditatvāt yuktamekaikapadārthāpavarjanamiti spaṣṭatva dvaiṣa/?/sya
sauryādidarśanaṃ pūrvapakṣok‍taṃ kimarthamiti । asyāpyasti prayojanaṃ idamapyāśaṅkānirākaraṇāyaivopa-
nyastamiti kā punarāśaṅkā ? tāmāha---<b>yadi kramāvagatimātratayaiva krama ādriyate
sauryādiṣu kaḥ pradveṣaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---sauryādiṣvapi bahuṣu pradhāneṣu ekaikasya padārthasya
sakalapradhānasaṃbandhitayā yugapadanuṣṭhānāśak‍teravaśyaṃbhāvini krame dvitīyādiṣvapi padārtheṣu
tathaiva kramo'vagamyate । avagatimātreṇa kramasyādara iti tasyāpi prāvṛttikaḥ kramaḥ prāpnotīti ।
atha pradhānasya sāṅgasya vihitatvāt tatra sauryādiṣu kṛtsnameva guṇakāṇḍamapavṛjyeta naikaikaḥ
padārtha itīhāpi tathā syāt । athātra ekaikasyāpavarjanaṃ tatrāpi tathā syāditi sauryādisāmyā-
śaṅkā । saṃpratyāśaṅkānirākaraṇāyāha---<b>na khalukaścit pradveṣaḥ । anuṣṭhānānaupayikatayā
tatra pratītamapi tyajyate</b> । sauryādīnāṃ bhinnaprayogacodanācoditānāṃ sahānuṣṭhānābhāvāt
yadyapi 1prāvṛttikaḥ kramo'vagamyate tathāpi anuṣṭhānopāyabhūto'sau na bhavatīti tyajyate । prājā-
patyeṣu tu pradhānapratyāsattyanuguṇo'nuṣṭhānaupayika iti svīkriyate । avagatasyāpi parityāge
dṛṣṭāntamāha---<b>varṇasvarūpamiva padeṣu</b> । yathā varṇasvarūpaṃ ekaikavarṇasvarūpaṃ pratītamapi
2vācakāvasthāyāmekaikasya varṇasvarūpasyānupāyabhūtatvāt tyajyate । <b>ekatvamiva graheṣu</b> । yathā
grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭītyanupāyabhūtamekatvam । sādhanaparicchedadvāreṇa hi sakhyā upāyatāṃ yāti ।
na ca paricchinne sādhane grahākhyasādhyasādhane punastadapekṣā'stīti । <b>ubhayatvamiva haviṣṣu</b> ।
yathā <q>‘yasyobhayaṃ havirārtimārcchati’</q> iti ubhayatvamanupāyabhūtaṃ tyajyate <b>naitāvatā'</b>nupāyabhūtasya
tyāgo dṛṣṭa ityetāvatā <b>aupayikasyāpi</b> upāyabhūtasyāpi <b>tyāga upapadyate</b> । upasaṃharati
<note>(1) pravṛttitaḥ</note> <note>(2) vācakāvācaka</note>
﻿<pb n="1092"/>
---<b>ato'pekṣitaṃ pratipannamādriyate’ । pratipannamapyanapekṣitamupekṣaṇīyameva । nanu caivaṃ
sati pratipattiranarthikā</b> prayojanaśūnyā prāpnoti iti । codyamātraṃ pariharati-<b>kena vok‍taṃ
pratipatterarthavattvaṃ</b> prayājanavattvam । <b>arthavatpratipattireva arthavattve hetuḥ na prati-
pattimātraṃ,</b> tacchūnyā prayojanaśūnyā pratipattiḥ । <b>pratipattimātraparyantaiveti sūktam</b> ।
atrādhikaraṇe saṃkṣepārtho'yam---aniyatakrameṇa prathamapadārthe'nuṣṭhite dvitīyapadārthe punaḥ pradhāna-
pratyāsattyanugrahāya kramāpekṣā bhavati । tatra yenaiva krameṇa prathamapadārtho'nuṣṭhitaḥ sa eva kramaḥ
parigṛhyate । tasminneva gṛhyamāṇe yathāvagatapradhānapratyāsattyanugrahāditi ।</p>
<p><b>sthānāccotpattisaṃyogāt । atra bhāṣyakāreṇa triṇavādiṣvadarśanāt samāmnāyakramasya-
vidyamānasyāviṣayatāṃ manvānairidamudāhṛtam ityaviṣayatāṃ matvaitadudāhṛtam-saha paśūnālabhata
iti</b> । atretraṃ yojanā-atra kila bhāṣyakāreṇa prathamamudāhṛtaṃ triṇavenaujaskāmaṃ yājayediti ।
stomavivṛddhau ānīyamānā ṛcaḥ kimaniyatena krameṇa prayoktavyā uta yathāsamāmnāyakramamiti
saṃśayaṃ kṛtvā triṇavādiśabdeṣu vidhāyakeṣu pāṭhakramābhāvādaniyama iti pūrvapakṣaṃ kṛtvā sthāna
krameṇaiva prayoktavyā iti rāddhāntayitvedamuktam---<q>‘atra mantrasamāmnāyapāṭhakrameṇāyaṃ kramaniyama
iti’</q> na pāṭhakramādbheda ityanena ca doṣeṇa sthānakramasyāyamaviṣaya iti matvā <q>‘saha paśūnālabhata’</q>
<note>(1) P. 1295</note>
﻿<pb n="1093"/>
ityudāharaṇāntaraṃ dattam । atra bhāṣyakāreṇedamudāhṛtaṃ sahapaśūnālabhata iti saṃbandhaḥ । kiṃ
kṛtvetyatrāha---<b>triṇavenojaskāmamiti sthānakramasyāviṣayaṃ matvā</b> । kimityaviṣayatāṃ manyata
ityatrāha---<b>triṇavādiṣvadarśanāt</b> samāmnāyakramasya bhrāntaiḥ pairarvidyamānasya pāṭhakramasya
mantragatasyāviṣayatāṃ manyānairidamudāhatamiti triṇavādicodanāsu pāṭhakramasyādarśanāt
nāyaṃ pāṭhakramasya viṣaya iti manvānairidamudāhṛtam । paramārthatastu pāṭhakramasyāyaṃ
viṣaya iti vidhipāṭhakramo vā bhavatu mantrapāṭhakramo vā; sarvathā pāṭhakrama evāyamiti
hetoḥ nāyaṃ sthānakramasya viṣaya iti matvā bhāṣyakāreṇānyadudāhṛtamiti । atra
codāharaṇe <b>adhikaraṇāntarasiddhamarthamupādāya saha paśūnālabhata ityanena savanīyasthāne
sahatvaṃ</b> coditamiti <b>sthite kaḥ kramaniyama iti cintyate---kimatrāpi pravṛttireva nimittaṃ</b>
somavikārāṇāṃ somapūrvakatvāt some yā pravṛttiḥ1 pūrvamagnīṣomīyaḥ tadanantaraṃ savanīyaḥ
tadanantaramanūbandhya iti saiva kimatrāpi kramaniyamanimittaṃ <b>uta nimittāntaramapi sthānākhya-
mastīti</b> vicāraḥ । <b>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī avaśyaṃbhāvini krame yadi pravṛttirneṣyate</b>
prayogāntaravartitvāt <b>pūrvāvagatapāṭhādeva niyama iti manyate । siddhāntavādī tu
sahavacanena sthānasyābādhitatvāt savanīyasyaiva pūrvamanuṣṭhānaṃ nyāyyamityuk‍tavān</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---saha paśūnālabhata ityanena vacanena savanīyasthāne sarveṣāmālambhasya coditatvāt
savanīyasthānamabādhitam । āśvinagrahaṇottarakālatā tatra । yadyagnīṣomīyastasmin kāle'nu-
ṣṭhīyate tadā śrutakālabādhaḥ syāt । tasmāt savanīya eva pūrvamālabdhavyaḥ ।</p>
<note>(1) G. somayāgapravṛttiḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="1094"/>
<p><b>yadyevamagnīṣomīyānubandhayoḥ kā vārtā ? kathaṃ pūrvāparakālatā</b> । vakṣyamāṇena
dṛṣṭāśayena pṛcchati । rāddhāntī tu pūrvapakṣiṇa āśayamajānanniva brūte---<b>kimanayā'nupanya---
stayā cintayā ? yadvā sthānavatkālabādhopyayukta iti agnīṣomīya eva pūrvaṃ</b> prakṛtāva-
nūbandhyāpekṣayā pūrvakālatā'gnīṣomīyasyāvagatā । atastadanugrahāyāgnīṣomīya eva pūrvaṃ
prayoktavyaḥ । <b>yadyevaṃ savanīyādapi tarhi pūrvaṃ bhavitumarhati</b> । savanīyādapi hi prakṛtau pūrva-
kālatā agnīṣomīyasyāvagateti । <b>na । vihitatvāt savanīyakālasya</b> । āśvinaṃ
grahaṃ gṛhītveti savanīyakālo vihitaḥ <b>pracayāvagamyatvādagnīṣomīyakālasya</b> bahuṣu paśuṣu
vihiteṣu bhinnakāleṣu pūrvāparakālatā'vagamyate । tataḥ kimityāha---<b>vidhānārthatvāt
pracayasya vihitaṃ balīyaḥ</b> । vidhānasya hi pracaya ārthaḥ na punaḥ pracaya eva vidhīyate ।
ato vihitaṃ balīyaḥ । yadi pāṭhakramabādhena sthānakrameṇānuṣṭhānaṃ kalpyate <b>evaṃ tarhi
balābalacintyeyaṃ</b> na pramāṇāntaropanyāsaḥ <b>naivaṃ, sthite pramāṇatve balavadabalatvamiti
yuktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>mukhyakrameṇa cāṅgānām</b> । ihādhikaraṇe mukhyakrameṇāṅgānāṃ kramaḥ pratipādyate ।
tatra yāstāvadvikṛtayaḥ krameṇa paṭhyante tāsāṃ pradhānacodanāparigṛhītatvāt ātideśikānā-
<note>(1) P. 1297</note>
﻿<pb n="1095"/>
maṅgānāṃ pradhānacodanāpāṭhakrameṇaivāṅgānāṃ krama iti na tāstāvadihodāharaṇam । yānyapi
tāsvevaupadeśikānyaṅgāni teṣāmapi vā pāṭhakrameṇaiva kramaḥ । etenaiva nyāyena na prakṛtayo'pya-
trodāharaṇāni । kintu yā eva vikṛtayo yugapaccoditāḥ tāsāṃ pradhānapāṭhakramābhāvāt na
pāṭhakrameṇāṅgānāṃ kramaniyamassiddha‍yatīti tā evodāharaṇam । tadāha---<b>yatra yaugapadyena codanā
sārasvatau bhavata iti tatra kiṃ pramāṇāntaramasti kramaniyamasyāṅgānāṃ uta yatheṣṭā
pravṛttiriti । tantreṇoccāraṇācchāstrasya na kramaḥ pratīyata ityabhiprāyaḥ</b> pūrvapakṣiṇaḥ ।
pradhānacodanā pāṭhakramābhāvāt tad‍gṛhītānāmaṅgānāmapi na kramaḥ pratīyata iti । <b>evaṃ prāpte-
'bhidhīyate mukhye kramadarśanādaṅge'pi kramaḥ</b> pratīyata iti <b>yuktam</b> yājyayoḥ kramavattvāt
pradhānayoḥ kramaḥ pratīyate yatkramake ca pradhāne tadaṅgānyapi tatkramakānyeva yuktāni । kimevaṃ
bhaviṣyati ? <b>evaṃ ca yābadanujñātaṃ vyavadhānaṃ bhaviṣyati । aniyame hi anujñātātikramaḥ</b>
syāt । tasmānniyamo yuktaḥ । yājyānibandhanamukhyakramābhidhānamatra sauhṛdamātram । aniyama-
pakṣe'pi mukhyakramānuṣṭhānena bhāvyam ।</p>
<p><b>prakṛtau tu svaśabdatvāt । idānīṃ pāṭhamukhyayorvirodhe cintyate । tatra mukhyā-</b>
<note>(1) P. 1297</note>
﻿<pb n="r1096"/>
<b>rthatvādaṅgānāṃ mukhyakrama eva balīyāniti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । pradhānaṃ hi mukhyaṃ pradhānānuguṇā
cāṅgākalpanā । tena pradhānānusāreṇa yaḥ krama āpatati sa eva balīyāniti । <b>evaṃ ca prayoga-
codanānugrahaḥ pratyāsatteḥ</b> prayogacodanā hi yugapadanuṣṭhānaṃ bodhayati । tatra puruṣāśakti-
mātreṇa yāvadva‍yavadhānamupanipatati tāvadevānumanyate । nānyat । anujñātavyavadhānamātra-
svīkāre'sāvanugṛhītā bhavati । mukhyakramāṅgīkāre ca yāvadanujñātavyavadhānam । itarathā
parakīyāṅgavyavadhānamāpadyeta । <b>atrābhidhīyate---na pratītasya bādho yuktaḥ । pāṭhācca
nirapekṣāt kramo'vagato'ṅgānāṃ nānyāpekṣayā bādhituṃ yuktaḥ</b> । antaraṅgabhūto hi
pāṭhakramaḥ nirapekṣāvagamāta । bahiraṅgabhūtaśca mukhyakramāpekṣayā upajāyamānatvāt । <b>nanu
pratyāsatteḥ prādhānyācca</b> mukhyakramasya <b>balavattā uk‍teti</b> pūrvapakṣasmāraṇam । <b>satyamuktā ।
ayuktā tu sā</b> kathamiti । <b>yathāpratītaṃ hi prayogavacano gṛhṇāti । na prayoga-
vacanādavagatiraṅgānām</b> । tatra cāṅgāni svapāṭhāt klṛptakramāṇyeva prayogavacanena gṛhyante ।
kathametadityāha---<b>aṅgaṃ sat prayogavacanena gṛhyata ityuktam</b> । <q>‘prāpitānabhisamīkṣya
prayogavacana upasaṃharati’</q> ityanena granthena । <b>tasmādyathāvagamaṃ pratyāsattiḥ । na pratyāsatterevā-
vagamo'ṅgānām । ataḥ pāṭho balīyāniti yuktam । uk‍taṃ ca svaśabdatvāditi</b> ।
kimuk‍taṃ bhavati ? svaśabdatvenāntaraṅgatā pāṭhasyoktā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r1097"/>
<p><b>mantratastu virodhe syāt । mantrabrāhmaṇapāṭhakramavirodhe kiṃ balīya iti</b> sandehe
yadi mantro balīyān tadā mantrakrameṇānuṣṭhānam । atha brāhmaṇaṃ balīyaḥ tadā brāhmaṇakrameṇānu-
ṣṭhānam । tatrāniyama eva ubhayorapi pāṭhasvarūpatvāditi prāpte ucyate---<b>mantrakramo
balīyān kutaḥ ? pāṭhasyānanyaparatvāt prayojyatvānmantrāṇām</b> । asyārthaḥ-prayok‍tumeva
mantrāḥ paṭhyante । tena teṣāṃ yaḥ pāṭhaḥ sa prayogāyaivāvagamyate । ato yatkramakā eva
mantrāḥ āmnāyante tatkramakā eva te prayoktavyāḥ mantraiśca smṛtaṃ karma kartavyam iti karmāṇyapi
tatkramakāṇyeva prayok‍tavyānīti । <b>nanu brāhmaṇepyananyapara eva</b> anuṣṭhānakramapara eva
<b>pāṭhakramaḥ । yatpunaḥ karmotpattiḥ prayojanamityuk‍taṃ, vākyasya tatprayojanaṃ na pāṭhakramasya ।
ucyate---utpattyarthaḥ sa pāṭhakramaḥ na prayogārtha ityuk‍taṃ bhavati</b> aprayojyatvāt brāhmaṇa-
vākyānām । <b>mantre punaḥ prayogārthaḥ kramo'pīti balavattvam</b> । etaduvataṃ bhavati-mantreṣu
yaḥ pāṭhakramaḥ sa prayojyamantragataḥ sākṣātpratīyate । brāhmaṇapāṭhakramastu na sākṣātprayojyagataḥ
kintu vidhikramadarśanāt vidheye'pi kramaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ sa klṛptamantrakramavirodhe nātmānaṃ
labhata iti ।</p>

﻿<pb n="r1098"/>
<p><b>tadvacanādvikṛtau । kiṃ mukhyakramādvikṛtau kramaḥ uta pāṭhakramāt prakṛtau yathā
nirjñāto'ṅgakramo vikṛtāvapi tathaiva prayok‍tavya iti vicāraḥ । kiṃ yuktaṃ ? prayogārthatvāt</b>
kramasya 2avitatasya prayogānupapatteḥ <b>vikṛtau ca prayogāvagamāt yathāvikṛti prayoga
iti</b> pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । yadyapi prakṛtau prayogāntare kramāntaramavagataṃ tathāpīha vikṛtijñāpye
prayogāntare yathāvikṛti mukhyakrameṇaivānuṣṭhānaṃ yuktamiti । anenaiva ca viśeṣeṇa prakṛtau
svaśabdatvādityato'dhikaraṇāntarārambhaḥ । <b>rāddhāntastu na nirjñātakramaṃ prayogaṃ prayogavacano</b>
vaikṛto <b>bādhitumarhati</b> । yadyapi prayogāntaraṃ tathāpi prayojyānāmabhedāt kramāpekṣāyāṃ ya eva
teṣāṃ prayogāntare kramo nirjñātaḥ sa eva tāvadbuddhistho bhavatīti na kramāntarakalpanāvakāśo'sti
<b>nirjñātasya hi kramasya prayogo'ṅgānāmiva</b> । yathā'ṅgāni prakṛtau nirjñātānyeva vikṛtau
prayujyante tathā kramo'pi । <b>anirjñāte hi vastuni</b> svarūpāvadhāraṇāya sarvatra hetvantara-
<b>kalpanā bhavati na nirjñāte</b> । tadāha vārtikakāraḥ(ślo) yāvadajñātasandigdhaṃ jñeyaṃ tāvatpra-
mitsyate । pramite tu pramātṝṇāṃ pramautsukyaṃ vihanyate ।। <b>iti । tasmādyathā prakṛtau tathā
vikṛtāvapyaṅgānāṃ prayoga iti</b> ।</p>
