﻿<pb n="r1099"/>
<p><b>vikṛtiḥ । sadyaskāladvayahakālacintā । keyaṃ kramacintāyāṃ ?</b> ityanena
saṅgatirnāstītyākṣipati । <b>kramasiddhayartheti brūmaḥ sadyaskālatāyāmanyathā kramo bhavati ।
dvayahakālatāyāṃ cānyathā । tasmādyukto vicāraḥ । tatra prakṛtivaditi dvayahakālatāṃ
manyate</b> pūrvapakṣavādī । <b>aharantarepi savanaśruteraviśeṣāt</b> । tatra hi auṣa/?/deśikenā-
tideśikaṃ bādhyate yatra dvayorasaṃbhavaḥ । iha tu dvayamapi saṃbhavatīti prākṛtī dva‍yahakālatā
svīkriyate । vaikṛtī ca prāhṇādikālatā aharantaravartinyapi prāhṇādau prāhṇādiśabdasyā-
viśeṣāditi । <b>rāddhāntī tu kālāntaraśravaṇānna prākṛtaṃ kālamapekṣata iti sadyaskālatāṃ
manyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---sarvatra vaikṛta upadeśaḥ kāryaviṣayaḥ upadeśakalpyaṃ ca kāryam । tatra
prakṛtau dvayahopadeśena kālakāryaṃ yatprāptaṃ tatraiva vikṛtāvapi kālāntaramupadiśyate na punaraha-
ravayavakārye । prakṛtāvaharavayavakāryasyāklṛptatvāt । tataśca vaikṛtenaiva kālena prākṛtakārya-
siddherna punaḥ prākṛtakālāpekṣā'stīti sadyaskālataiva yak‍teti । nanu tathāpi kathamekāhasaṃbandho
labhyata ityāha---<b>savanāni caikāhassaṃbandhānyeva śrutyā'vagamyamānāni na kāraṇādṛte
aharantarāpekṣāṇi yuktāni kalpayitum</b> । asyārthaḥ---aharavayavabhūtāni prāhṇādīni ।
tāni avayavībhūtamaharākṣipya paryavasyanti । tatra caikāhākṣepeṇaivopapattau nāharantarākṣepaḥ
﻿<pb n="r1100"/>
kramata iti nyāyabalena prāhṇādīni śrutāni samānāharvartīnyeva pratīyanta iti । <b>darśana-
muktam</b> ।</p>
<p><b>aṅgānāṃ mukhyakālatvāt । aśrūyamāṇāmutkarṣavākye'pakarṣavākye ca kimi-
tyutkarṣāpakarṣau</b> । anena pūrvapakṣamāha । sarvaṃ śabdāvagamyaṃ codanāsviti kimityaśrūyamāṇā-
nāmutkarṣāpakarṣau bhavata ityarthaḥ । <b>satyaṃ śrutasya padārthasyotkarṣo'pakarṣo vā śrūyate na
punaruparitanamādhastyaṃ vā akṛtveti । na cedidamavagamyate kramāvagatamanuṣṭhānaṃ kena vāryate ?</b>
asyārthaḥ । yad‌yuparitanamanuṣṭhānaṃ parityajya kevala evotkarṣaṇīya iti śrutaṃ syāt tadā
kevalasyotkaṣaḥ syāt । yadā punarutkarṣamātraṃ śrūyate tadā prāgavagatakramabalena uparitanānya-
pyutkarṣaṇīyāni । tāni hi utkṛṣyamāṇānyabhimataṃ padārthaṃ kṛtvā kartavyānīti prakṛtāvavagatam ।
ataḥ kramānugrahāya teṣamuparitanānāmapyutkarṣeṇa bhavitavyam । tathā'pakarṣe'pi ādhastyamakṛtvai-
vāpakṛṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ kartavya ityevaṃ yadyaśroṣyata tadā kevala evāpakṛṣyatām । na caivam ।
ato'vagatakramānugrahāyādhastyamapi kartavyam । tatkṛtvā tatrāsau prakṛtau kṛta iti ।
<b>ataḥ kimatrotkarṣavākye aśratatvaṃ kariṣyati notkarṣamapakarṣaṃ</b> ca vārayituṃ kṣama ityarthaḥ ।
<b>anyata</b> eva kramādevotkarṣasiddheḥ । yadi śravaṇādevotkarṣa ityucyate tadā'śrutatvaṃ bhave-
dvighātakaṃ <b>tasmād‌yuktamuk‍taṃ---tadādi vā'bhisaṃbandhāt tadantamapakarṣaḥ syāditi</b> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="r1101"/>
<p><b>pravṛttyā kṛtakālānām । kimalaṅkaraṇādayo dharmāḥ praiṣottarakālaṃ kartavyāḥ uta
pāṭhādevāvagatāḥ saumikā iti</b> । asyārthaḥ---nirvāpātparāñco ye padārthāḥ pauroḍāśikāḥ
alaṅkaraṇācca prāñcaḥ alaṅkaraṇatya ādayaḥ alaṅkaraṇātprāgbhāvinaḥ te kiṃ <q>‘savanīvānnirvapasva’</q>
iti nirvāpapraiṣottarakālaṃ kartavyāḥ nirvāpapraiṣānantarakālaṃ hi nirvāpastāvatkartavyaḥ । tasmiṃstu
kṛte prakṛtau tadanantarabhāvino ye dṛṣṭāḥ prokṣaṇaprabhṛtayo'laṅkaraṇātprāgbhāvinaḥ te'pi kiṃ kartavyāḥ
alaṅkaraṇaṃ tu <b>vacanenaiva</b> bahiṣpavamānottarakāle śrutamiti tatraiva kartavyam, uta pāṭhādevāvagatā-
ssaumikāḥ padārthāḥ pracaraṇīhomādayaḥ kartavyāḥ । saumikāśca padārthāḥ pāṭhataḥ klṛptakramāḥ
tatra vacanabalānmadhye padārthāntaramanupraviśati । tatra yāvadvacanaṃ vācanikamiti <b>nirbāpamātrameva
madhye kartavyam</b> । tataḥ paraṃ ca pracaraṇīhomādaya iti ubhayathāpi pāṭhakrama eva । <b>ato-
'niyama iti prāpte । ucyate</b> । alaṅkaraṇasya prāgbhāvinaḥ kartavyā iti । kutaḥ ? <b>anirjñāta-
kartavyatā hi pāṭhānniyamyate</b> । yadanuṣṭhānamanirjñātaṃ tatpāṭhena niyamyate । <b>na punarnirjñāta-
kartavyatāṃ niruṇaddhi pāṭhaḥ</b> । nirjñātaṃ hi prakṛtau nirvāpānantaraṃ prokṣaṇādikamiti tadeva
kartavyam । <b>ataḥ praiṣāt praiṣārthakartavyatā vijñāyate</b> । tasmiṃstu kṛte tadanantarabhāvino'pi
kartavyāḥ । <b>ataḥ paraṃ tu pāṭhānniyamaḥ ।</b></p>
<note>(1) P. 1302</note>
﻿<pb n="r1102"/>
<p><b>asaṃyogāttu tadeva । dīkṣāsu yūpaṃ chinattītyapakarṣaḥ śrūyate । tatra tadantāśaṅkā-
nivṛttyarthamidamadhikaraṇam</b> । abhisaṃbandhābhāvāt <b>yāvadvacanamapakarṣa 4iti</b> pāṭhato
niyame'vagate ekasminnapakṛṣyamāṇe aparasyāpyapakarṣeṇa bhavitavyamiti yevamāśaṅkā tannivṛttyartha-

bhavataḥ । iha tu nādyāpi kramakalpaneti nāyaṃ tasya viṣayaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>prāsaṅgikaṃ ca । prāsaṅgike'pyayaṃ tulyo heturiti prāsaṅgikaṃ ca notkarṣedityuktam</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yo'yamaklṛptakramatvena kramābhisaṃbandhābhāvaḥ tadāditadantanyāyāpavāde hetuḥ sa
prāsaṅgike'pi tulyaḥ । pauroḍāśikayoḥ āparāgnikahomayoḥ sānnāyyakairanūyājaiḥ saha
kramakalpanāyā asambhavāt । kena tarhi viśeṣeṇādhikaraṇāntarārambhaḥ । <b>ucyate</b>---pūrvapakṣa-
vādī prakṛtāvanūyājānāmāparāgnikahomayośca kramakalpanādabhisaṃbandhaṃ manyate । rāddhāntastu
yadyapyanūyājasvarūpaṃ tadeva tathāpi saṃbandhināṃ rūpabhedena nāsti kramakalpaneti ।</p>

﻿<pb n="r1103"/>
<p><b>tathā'pūrvam । paurṇamāsyāṃ pāṭhāt kramasambandho nirjñāta iti tadantasyāpakarṣaṃ
manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । pāṭhakramasya paurṇamāsyāmādṛtatvāt klṛptakramāyā vedeḥ amāvāsyāyāṃ
pratikṛṣyamāṇatvāt asyā arvācīnānāmapi pratikarṣaṃ manyate । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu na paurṇa-
māsīprakṛtikaṃ1 āmāvāsyaṃ karmeti manvānaḥ apakarṣottarakālameva kramo niyamyate śeṣāṇā-
miti yāvadvacanamapakarṣa ityuktavān</b> । prakṛtivikārabhāve hi sati śāstrārthāvadhāraṇapūrvakaṃ
śāstrārthāvadhāraṇam na svātan‍tryeṇa । tena paurṇamāsyāṃ kramakalpanāmapekṣyāmāvāsyāyāṃ na
śāstrārtho varṇayitavyaḥ । tena yāvadeva vedimātramapakṛṣṭaṃ tāvadevāmāvāsyāyāṃ pratikṛṣyate ।
taduttarakālaṃ ca tatra kramaniyama iti । <b>kāryavirodhaśceha</b> haviṣāṃ bhasmībhāvalakṣaṇo-
<b>'bhyuccayaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>sāntapanīyā tūtkarṣet । parārthamuddhṛte'gnau prasaṅgādṛte nāgnihotraṃ hotavyamiti
manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī utkarṣamuktavān</b> । atrādhikaraṇe'g‍nyuddharaṇakālayordvayoraṅgayoḥ kasya
tyāgo yukta iti cintyate । sāntapanīyārthamuddhṛte'gnau daivānmānuṣādvā pratibandhabalāt
sāntapanīyāyāmutkṛṣṭāyāṃ sāyamagnihotraṃ prati puruṣasya tāvadadhikāro vidyate jīvanasyādhikāri-
viśeṣaṇasya vidyamānatvāt । nanu ca tiryagadhikaraṇe sarvāṅgosaṃhārasamarthasyaivādhikāra
<note>(1) P. 1307</note> <note>(2) R. pravṛttikramaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1104"/>
ityuktam । na ca sāntapanīyārthoddhṛtāgniḥ akṛtasāntapanīyaḥ punaragnihotrārthamag‍nyuddharaṇa-
mupasaṃhartuṃ śak‍noti । apavṛtte hi karmaṇi alaukikena svarūpeṇa gārhapatyamīhavanīyaḥ praviśati
nānyathā । apraviṣṭaśca kathamudadhriyeta । tasmādag‍nyuddharaṇopasaṃhārāsāmarthyānnādhikārasaṃbhavaḥ
<b>ucyate</b>---satyamāha bhavān samarthasyaivādhikāra iti । kintu sāmarthyamevātra cintanīyaṃ kiṃ
taditi । tatrāhitāgnitvādanyannāg‍nyuddharaṇopasaṃhārasāmarthyam । asti cātra puruṣasyāhitā-
gnitvamiti ag‍nyuddharaṇopasaṃhārasāmarthyamiti adhikārānapāyaḥ । yathā caivaṃ tathā sarvaśaktya-
dhikaraṇa eva nipuṇataramupapādayiṣyāmaḥ । tatrāpi satyadhikāre'ṅgalopenāpyanuṣṭhānamastīti
sthite cintyate---kimag‍nyuddharaṇamapahāya kālānugrahāya tasminneva kāle'gnihotraṃ hūyatāṃ, uta
dvitīye'hani sāntapanīyakaṃ kṛtvā punaragnimuddhṛtya kālamātraṃ parityajyāgnihotraṃ hūyatāmiti
cintāyāṃ prayogāṅgatvāt kālasyāṅgāṅgabhūtatvam । ato'ṅgabhūtoddharaṇamevātrānugrāhyam । na
ca parārthamuddhṛte'gnau tasminneva kāle'gnihotraṃ yuk‍taṃ kartuṃ, aprāsaṅgikatvādagnihotrasya yadi
hi kālo'trānugrāhyaḥ syāt tadā tantramadhyāvidhānāt niśīṣṭivadagnihotraṃ syāt । tataśca
parārthamuddhṛte'gnau bhaveta । na caitadasti । tasmādutkarṣa eva tasya nyāyya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ
<b>rāddhāntī tu nimittatvātkālasyānutkarṣaṃ manyate</b> । etaduktaṃ bhavati---nimittarūpaḥ kālaḥ
tadabhāve'dhikāra eva nāsti । ato na kālāntare'gnihotraṃ hotavyam । ag‍nyuddharaṇābhāve tu
adhikāsyānapāyāddhotavyamityanutkarṣo yuktaḥ । <b>kathaṃ punaḥ kālonimittam ?</b> yāvatā'ṅga
kāla uktaḥ । <b>uttaraṃ---tasmin sati prayogāt na punaradhikāriviśeṣaṇatvāt</b>, kālasya
puruṣānupasaṃhāryatvāt । yadā svayameva kālo nipatati tadā prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ ityetāvatā
nimittatā kālasyocyate na punarbhedādīnāmivādhikāriviśeṣaṇatvena । yadā svayamupanipātī
kālaḥ tadā kālāntare puruṣasya kāle karma kartuṃ sāmarthyaṃ nāstītyanadhikāraḥ । kālāntare
﻿<pb n="r1105"/>
āhitāgnitayā tu ag‍nyuddharaṇasāmarthyamastītyanapeto'dhikāraḥ । <b>ato nimitte sati
naimittikena bhavitavyamityarthāt prāsaṅgikatvasiddhiḥ । ato'nutkarṣaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>ṣoḍaśī ca । ṣoḍaśinyaṅgakālavirodhāt kādācitkatvāccotkarṣasya anutkarṣaṃ
manyate pūrvavādī</b> । <q>‘taṃ parāñcamukthyebhyo gṛhṇāti’</q> iti vacanena ṣoḍaśinaḥ ukthyottara-
kālatā vidhīyate । 1<b>utkṛṣṭe</b>pi cokthyeṣu kālasyānapāya eva, śaṅkhābhāve'pi śaṅkhavelāyā
iva । yadi paramanutkarṣe ṣoḍaśinaḥ ukthyaiḥ saha yaḥ pratītaḥ kramaḥ sa parityajyate sa
ca tyak‍tumucita eva । utkarṣe ṣoḍaśyaṅgabhūtastotrasya samayāghyuṣitakālabādhaprasakteḥ । na ca
samayādhyuṣitakālacodanā atyantāsaṃbhāvyārthā । kādācitkatvādukthyotkarṣasya । yadā hi
nokthyotkarṣaḥ tadā sarvamavikalamupapannamiti aṅgāṅgabādhācca anaṅgakramabādho nyāyya iti ।
<b>rāddhāntavādī tu avaśyaṃbhāvitvācchāstrātikramasya varamaṅgaśāstrasyātikrama ityutkarṣa-
muk‍tavān</b> । yadyapyanaṅgaṃ kramaḥ tathāpi tāvat nāśāstrārthatā kramasya । tataśca dvayoḥ
śāstrārthatve varamaṅgaśāstrasyātikrama ityutkarṣaḥ ṣoḍaśino yuktaḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti śālikanāthamiśrakṛtāyāṃ ṛjuvimalāyāṃ
pañcikāyāṃ pañcamasyādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>

<section>
<head>ṛjuvimalā</head>

<section>
<head>atha dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>sannipātte । nanu ca pravṛttyā kramo niyataḥ kimidamekaikasya kṛts‍namiti</b> ।
anenādhikaraṇāntarārambhamākṣipati । padārthānusamayamāśritya pravṛttyā kramāniyamo darśita iti
na punaḥ padārthānusamayasādhanaṃ yuktamiti । ucyate---<b>sthite etasminnadhikaraṇe taditi</b> ।
etadadhikaraṇasiddhameva padārthānusamayaṃ anāgatāvekṣaṇena tatra yuktibalenāśritya pravṛttikramaścintyata
ityarthaḥ । <b>iha punaḥ pūrvapakṣī manyate sakalapadārthānuṣṭānenāpi sahatvamupapadyata eva ।
kimiti kālavyavadhānaṃ kalpyate evamevānujñātamupapannaṃ bhavati</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi
kāṇḍānusamayo'pyāśrīyate tathāpyārādupakārakāṇāmaṅgānāṃ tantratvāt paśūnāṃ sarveṣāṃ sahaprayoga
upapadyata eva । ataḥ kimiti <b>vyavadhānaṃ kalpyate</b> । ekaiko hi paśuḥ svakīyairaṅgaiḥ saha
prayoktavyaḥ । tatra puruṣāśaktyā yāvatkālaṃ vyavadhānamāpatati tāvadeva prayogavidhinā'nu-
jñāyate । tatra yadyekaikaḥ padārthaḥ paśvantare'pi kriyate tadā'nanujñātamapi kālavyavadhānamāpadyate
<note>(1) P. 1310</note>
﻿<pb n="r1107"/>
tasmādekaikasmin kṛts‍naṃ guṇakāṇḍamapavarjayitavyamiti । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu sahatvacodanāt
ekaikasya padārthasya sahānuṣṭhānamavagamyamānaṃ na śakyate tyak‍tum । atastadanurodhena
vyavadhānānujñānaṃ na tatparityāgeneti padārthānusamayamuktavān</b> । asyārthaḥ---sarva-
paśūnāṃ sāṅgānāṃ sahānuṣṭhānasya coditatvāt ekaikamevāṅgaṃ sahakartavyamiti bhavati । tatra
sannipatyopakārakāṇyaṅgāni kāryabhedadarśanāt bhedena kartavyāni । tatraikasminnapi padārthe
sarvapaśuvartini kṛte tatpadārthānuṣṭhānaparyavasānamiti । anena prakāreṇa yāvatkālavyavadhānamāpatati
tāvadadhikāravidhiranumanyata eva nānyaditi । tena padārthānusamaya eva yuktaḥ । <b>adhi-
karaṇāntaraṃ veti kāryavirodhāt sahatvāvagamatyāgaṃ pāṭhavat</b> pradarśayitum । yaḥ
khalu yathāśās‍traṃ kāryaṃ pramāṇāyattatvāt prameyasiddheriti manvānaḥ sahatvaśravaṇabalena padārthānu-
samayaṃ manyate tatpratibodhanāyādhikaraṇāntaraṃ vetyuktam । nirjñātaṃ hi kāryaṃ yatra punarvirudhyate
tatra kāryārthatvādanuṣṭhānasya kāryānurodhena kāṇḍānusamaya eva nyāyyaḥ । yathā pāṭhakramaḥ kārya-
virodhī tyajyate tathā sahatvamapīti ।</p>
<p><b>muṣṭhikapālāvadāna । asminnadhikaraṇe'nāvṛttenāpi muṣṭyādinā kṛtaṃ śāstrārthaṃ
manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī padārthānusamayamuktavān</b> । yadyekaiko muṣṭiranusamīyate tadā <q>‘caturo
<note> P. 1311</note>
﻿<pb n="r1108"/>
muṣṭīnnirvapati’</q> iti kṛta eva śāstrārtho bhavati । sahatvacodanayā sarvaṃ sahakarta-
vyamiti prāptam । yacca sahakartavyatayā sarvaṃ prāptaṃ tasya sarvasyānusamaya
iti muṣṭyādyanusamaya eva yuktaḥ । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu codanātaḥ padārthādhyavasānaṃ
vaidikeṣu ca na lokavat pramāṇāntarāvaseyam । ekaṃ cedaṃ śās‍traṃ <q>‘caturo muṣṭhīnnirvapati’</q>
iti <q>‘dvirhaviṣo'vadyati’</q> iti ca । tasmācchāstrārthānusamayo nyāyya iti manyate</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yatkhalu śās‍tre'ṅgatayā nirūpitaṃ tatkartavyam । yacca kartavyaṃ tat sahakartavyam ।
yacca sahakartavyaṃ tadevānusametavyam । aṅgāvagamaśca vaidikeṣu śāstrataḥ na pramāṇāntarataḥ ।
śās‍treṇa ca caturmuṣṭinirvāpasya vidhānāt āvṛttasyaivāṅgatā pratipāditetyetāvata evānusamayo
nyāyya iti manyate । padārthādhyavasānaṃ aṅgādhyavasānamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>saṃyuk‍teṣu tu । yadi śāstrādanusamayo dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti ekatvācchāstrasya
etāvataivānusamaya iti pūrvapakṣaḥ</b> । śās‍treṇāvadānaṃ vidhīyata iti manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।
anyathā sarvahutataiva syāt । athāvayavenāpyavayavino vyāpāra ityucyate tathāpi niyamārthaṃ
dva‍yavadānameva vidhīyata iti tasyāṅgatvāt tasyaivānusamayena bhavitavyamiti । rāddhāntastu
nedaṃ padārthavidhānaṃ, kintu padārthasaṅkhyāvidhānametat । atrāyaṃ bhāvaḥ---nityavaccheṣapratipatti-
<note>(1) P. 1312</note>
﻿<pb n="r1109"/>
vidhānāt sarvahutaṃ tāvannāsti । tenāvadāyaiva home prāpte nāvadānaṃ vidheyaṃ, kintu tadarthā-
kṣiptāvadānāśritā tu saṅkhyā tadaṅgatvena codyata iti । ataḥ pramāṇāntaraprāptāvadānopakrama-
pradānāntenaikapadārthānusamaya eva nyāyya iti । <b>tasmātpradānāntamevānusametavyamiti
siddham</b> ।</p>
<p><b>vacanāt‍tu । arthād‍yūṣadhāraṇamiti pūrvapakṣavādī padārthānusamayaṃ manyate</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---prakṛtau yadyūpadhāraṇaṃ kṛtaṃ yajamānena tadarthādyajamānasyānyatra vyāpṛtatvāt dvitīya-
puruṣadhāritasya yūpasya añjanādīnāṃ sukaratvāt । yajamānadhāraṇavacanaṃ tu saukaryaprāptānuvāda-
mātram । yaśca prakṛtāvarthādarthaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ na sa vikṛtau codakena prāpyate । na ca
vikṛtāvapyayamevārtho'rthādeva bhaviṣyatīti śakyate vak‍tum śāstrārthānāṃ sahacodanāvagatapadārthānu-
samayavirodhāt । ataḥ padārthānusamaya eva nyāyya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>śāstrābhedāt
śāstrārthānāṃ sahatvacodanāt</b> । śāstrabhedāddhi te paśuyāgaśāstrārthā bhinnāḥ । teṣāṃ caika-
prayogacodanācoditānāṃ sahānuṣṭhānasya prāptatvāditi । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu vihitopapattyarthatvāt
kramasya kāṇḍānusamayamuktavān</b> । asyārthaḥ---yathā vihitānāṃ padārthānāmupapattirbhavati
tathābhūtakrama ādaraṇīyaḥ । tatra yadi padārthānusamaya āśrīyate tadā añjanādiparivyāṇāntaṃ
yajamānena yūpasyānavasarjanaṃ vihitaṃ sadbādhyeta । ekena yajamānena bahuyūpavartinastasyā-
śakyatvāt iti । <b>nanu dṛṣṭārthatvādanyenāpi tatkriyata ityuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yajamānena
<note>(1) P. 1313</note>
﻿<pb n="r1110"/>
yūpasyā2navasarjanaṃ dṛṣṭārtham । taccānyenāpi puruṣeṇa śakyata eva kartumiti padārthānusamayo
na hīyata iti । <b>satyaṃ yadyarthāt dṛṣṭārthatā syāt</b> । asyārthaḥ---dvividhaṃ hi dṛṣṭārthaṃ
kiñcidarthādeva prāptam, kiñcicchās‍treṇa niyamārthatayā vihitam । tatra yadarthādeva prāptaṃ
dṛṣṭārthaṃ tadyenaiva śakyate kartuṃ tenaiva kriyate । yatpunaḥ śās‍treṇaiva coditaṃ tadyathācoditameva
kartavyaṃ, yajamānaśca śās‍tracodita eva । aniyatasya puruṣasya prasak‍terniyamārthaṃ yajamāna-
vidhānamupapadyata eva । <b>tadāha---vidhau tu sati dṛṣṭe'pyarthe na śāstrārtho 3vyatikramituṃ
śakyate । darśitametat</b> ।</p>
<p><b>paśugaṇe । atrāpi śāstrabādhaṃ manvānaḥ kāṇḍānusamayaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> ।
yathā pūrvatra śāstrabādhāt kāṇḍānusamayaḥ tathā'trāpi “daivatānyavadāya na tāvatyeva hotavyaṃ
sauviṣṭakṛtānyavadyati, sauviṣṭakṛtānyavadāya na tāvatyeva hotavyaṃ aiḍānyavadyati iti vacanenāvadāna-
trayanairantaryacodanāt padārthānusamaye ca tasya bādhanāt avadānatrayānusamaya eva yukta iti ।
<b>rāddhāntavādī tu padārthānusamayepyabādhaṃ manvānaḥ sahatvānugrahāya padārthānusamaya eva nyāyya
ityuktavān</b> । asyārthaḥ---daivatāvadānānusamaye'pi kṛte punassauviṣṭakṛtānusamayaṃ kurvāṇo
naiva nairantaryaṃ bādhate । prakṛtau tvekatvāt paśoḥ ekasmin tathākṛtam । iha punaḥ saha-
coditapaśubahutvādekamevāvadānaṃ sarveṣu kartavyamiti nāsti śāstrabādhaḥ । tena sahaprayogānu-
<note>(1) P. 1314</note> <note>(2) R. napasarjanaṃ</note> <note>(3) G. śāstrārthopyati</note>
﻿<pb n="r1111"/>
grahāya padārthānusamaya eva yuktaḥ । <b>mantroccāraṇatantratā ca sahatve liṅgam</b> । manotā-
mantro hi avadānaprakāśakaḥ sa daivatānusamayapakṣe tantraṃ bhavati । itarathā sauviṣṭakṛtāvadāna-
vyavahitatvāt manotāprakāśanasya paśvantare bhedena manotāmantraḥ prayoktavyaḥ syāt ।</p>
<p><b>nānābījeṣu । kaḥ punarayaṃ viśeṣo'vadānādihomaparyantānusamaya ityanenādhikaraṇena</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---yathā <q>“saṃyuk‍te tu prakramāt”</q> ityatrādhikaraṇe avadānādihomaparyanta eka eva padārtha
iti tāvato'nusamaya uktaḥ tathehāpi kṛṣṇājināstaraṇādiphalīkaraṇānta eka eva padārtha iti
tāvataivānusamayo nyāyya iti । etenaiva gatārthametadadhikaraṇamityākṣepaḥ । samādhatte
<b>na khalukaścidviśeṣaḥ । kimarthaṃ tarhīdamadhikaraṇaṃ ? viśeṣamāha---vidhānāt padārthā-
vacchedo bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhimānaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---kṛṣṇājināstaraṇādīnāṃ pṛthak
pṛthak vihitatvāt pṛthak padārthatvaṃ pṛthagaṅgatvaṃ pṛthagevānuṣṭhānaprayuktiriti tāvanmātreṇānusamayaḥ ।
avadānaṃ tu 2na pṛthagvihitamiti mābhūta tāvanmātreṇaivānusamayaḥ । <b>rāddhāntavādī tu vadati
vidheyānyatvena vidhānopapatterna padārthāvacchedāya prabhavo'stīti pūrvokta eva nyāyyaḥ</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---vrīhīnavahantīti vākyena taṇḍulībhāvaheturvyāpāranicayaścoditaḥ । sarva eva
hi dhātavaḥ phalaviśeṣāvacchinne vyāpārakṣaṇanicaye pravartante । tadyathā paciḥ devadattaḥ
<note>(1) P. 1315</note> <note>(2) G. omits na</note>
﻿<pb n="r1112"/>
pacatītyatra cullisammārjana-edhoharaṇa-sthālyadhiśrayaṇa-udakāvasecana-agnyabhijvalana-indhanakṣepaṇa
taṇḍulāvapana-darvīghaṭṭana-viklṛttiparīkṣā-avasrāvaṇāvatāraṇātmake vyāpāravarge । ato'vadhā-
tātmaka ekaḥ kṛṣṇājināstaraṇādiphalīkaraṇāntaḥ padārtha iti tāvataivānusamayo yuktaḥ ।
avāntaravidhayastu na padārthāvacchedāya prabhavanti, vidheyamātrabhedenāpyupapatteḥ । <b>anena ca
viśeṣeṇa tadapyatrodāharaṇam</b> । juhoticodanayaivāvadānasyāpi gṛhītatvāt na pṛthak
padārthatāstīti avadānādihomāntenānusamayaḥ । pūrvādhikaraṇe bhavatu vidhānabhedādeva
padārthabhedaḥ tathāpi vidhānabheda evātra nāstīti darśitamityanavadyam ।</p>
<p><b>vikāre tvanūyājānām । kaḥ punarayaṃ kramacintāyāṃ pātrabhedopanyāsaḥ</b> । lakṣaṇe
saṅgatirnāstītyataḥ2 । <b>kramasiddha‍yurtha iti brūmaḥ bhedābhede kramānyatvadarśanāt</b> । upabhṛdbhede
hyekāmupabhṛtamupādāya prayājārthaṃ grahaṇaṃ kāryam । dvitīyāmupādāyānūyājārtham । abhede tve-
kāmevopādāya grahaṇadvayamiti kramānyatva bhavati । ataḥ kramasiddha‍yarthaiveyaṃ cinteti ।
<b>atra pūrvapakṣo dravyavikāraśaṅkayā</b> । miśrīkṛtya grahaṇe prayājādyarthasya dravyasya pṛṣattāmātra-
vikāro 3na punaranyatvameveti । <b>pātravikārāśaṅkayā ca</b> । maryādāyāṃ kriyamāṇāyāṃ
upabhṛttvaṃ na naśyati । api tu vikāramātraṃ tasyaiveti । <b>kālānyatvena copapatteḥ</b> ।
<note>(1) P. 1316</note> <note>(2) nāstītyatra</note> <note>(3) G. omits this na</note>
﻿<pb n="r1113"/>
ekasyāmevopabhṛti kālāntare pṛṣadājyamapi grahīṣyata iti । <b>rāddhāntastu dravyavikārāpatteḥ</b>
dravyaśabdena ca haviḥ pātraṃ cocyate tayorvikāra āpadyate । sa cāyuktaḥ । havirvikārābhyupagame
utpavanādyarthabādhaprasaṅgāt । pātravikāre caupabhṛtatvanāśāpattiḥ । <b>kālānyatve ca grahaṇayoḥ sahā-
vagamabādhaprasaṅgāt</b> । ataḥ tadanuguṇaḥ grahaṇasahatvānuguṇaḥ pātrabhedo nyāyya iti siddham ।</p>
<p><b>prakṛteḥ</b> । nanu kimatra cintyate ? kiṃ vaikṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ uta prākṛtamiti । yāvatā
yāvadeva2 pradhānānantaramavagamyate tadeva tadanantaraṃ kartavyamityatrāha---<b>vaikṛtānāṃ pāṭhakramaḥ
prākṛtairvyavadhīyate neticintā</b> । pradhānānantaryameva sandigdhamityarthaḥ । <b>atra pūrvapakṣamāha
---vyavadhīyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ padārthānuṣṭhānena vyavadhānāvagamāt</b> । yadi pradhānānantaraṃ
prākṛtāḥ kriyante tadā pradhānena saha yo vaikṛtānāṃ pāṭhakramo'vagataḥ sa vyavadhīyate ।
anuṣṭhānena vyavadhānāvagamāt । <b>rāddhāntastu vaikṛtaprayogavacanāt prākṛtapadārthāvagamāt
vyavadhānam</b> । vaikṛtacodanārthāvacchedāyaiva hi prākṛtāṅgayuk‍taṃ pradhānaṃ paṭhitamiti pāṭhakramata
eva vaikṛtānāṃ prākṛtebhyaḥ paścādanuṣṭhānam । <b>atassūk‍taṃ-ante tu bādarāyaṇa iti</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1316</note> <note>(2) G. tāvadeva</note>
﻿<pb n="r1114"/>
<p><b>kṛtadeśāt‍tu</b> । atrettha pūrvapakṣaracanā । sarvatra vaikṛtāni tāvatprākṛtānāṃ paścāt
kartavyānīti sthitaṃ ante tu bādarāyaṇa iti nyāyāt । tatra yāvanmātramapakṛṣyate tāvata
evāpakarṣo yuktaḥ na tadantāpakarṣanyāyena pūrveṣāmapi; vaikṛtatvenāklṛptakramaniyamatvāt yūpa-
pratikarṣavaditi । atra rāddhāntamāha---<b>rājasūyepi videvanādavo vaikṛtena pāṭhena virudhya-
mānāḥ nānte'nuṣṭhānamarhanti</b> । yatra śrutāstatraiva bhavitumarhanti । asyārthaḥ---parasparaṃ tāvat
videvanādīnāmabhiṣekasya ca vikṛtau pāṭhataḥ kramaḥ pratīyate । tatrābhiṣeke pratikṛṣṭe sati
cintyate---kiṃ videvanādayo'nte'nuṣṭheyāḥ utābhiṣekātpūrvamiti । <b>atra vaikṛtapāṭhabalena</b>
ya eva pāṭhakramaḥ pratīyate sa eva kalpyate । ante tvanuṣṭhānaṃ vaikṛtenaiva pāṭhena viruddha‍yate ।
<b>nyāyamātramitaraditi</b> । kimida nyāyamātramiti ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ---antepi yadanuṣṭhānaṃ
tadapi vaikṛtapāṭhabalenaiva pradhānacodanāgṛhītatvāt prākṛtānāṃ vaikṛtānāṃ paścādeva pāṭha iti
pūrvoktanītyā । tadeva tulye vaikṛtapāṭhe kimidamucyate nyāyamātramitaraditi pūrvapakṣite
rāddhāntamāha---<b>etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---nānte'nuṣṭhānaṃ kenacitkrameṇāvagamyate । kiṃ tarhi ?
pūrvāvagamavirodhādante'nuṣṭhānamiti nyāyamātramityucyate</b> । asyārthaḥ---vaikṛtānāṃ
yadante'nuṣṭhānaṃ tanna kenacit śrutyādipratipāditena krameṇāvagamyate । kiṃ tarhi ? pradhāna-
codanāparigṛhītatvena prākṛtānāṃ yo vaikṛtebhyaḥ pūrvamavagamaḥ tasya virodhādante'nuṣṭhānamava-
<note>(1) P. 1318</note>
﻿<pb n="r1115"/>
gamyate yathāvagamamanuṣṭhānamiti yaḥ pūrvamavagamyate sa pūrvamanuṣṭheyaḥ । anyathā'nuṣṭhānāvagamayo-
rvirodhaḥ syāt । na ca tad‍yuktam । avagamāyattatvādanuṣṭhānasyeti । yaścāsau prākṛtānāṃ
pūrvamavagamaḥ sa ānumānikaḥ tenāntenānuṣṭhānaṃ nyāyamātranibandhanam । yaśca vaikṛtānāṃ
pāṭhamātranibandhanaḥ parasparakramaḥ saḥ pratyakṣasamadhigamyaḥ । tatra pratyakṣasya śīghrapravṛttitvāta
tadvaśena yaḥ kramaḥ pūrvamaklṛptatvāt balīyāniti tadanugrahāyābhiṣekāt pūrvapaṭhitānāṃ videva
nādīnāmapi apakarṣaḥ । yūpapratikarṣe tu agnīṣomīyapraṇayanādīnāṃ yūpenaiva svaprāgbhāvibhirapi
padārthaiḥ pratyakṣa eva pāṭhakrama iti na pratikarṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><b>prākṛtācca purastādyat । atrāpi prākṛtakramāvagamāt prayogacodanāta evānte-
'nuṣṭhānaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । asyārthaḥ---prākṛtānāṃ padārthānāṃ prakṛtāveva yaḥ kramaḥ
klṛptaḥ tatra madhye vinā vacanena vaikṛtasyānupraveśo na nyāyyaḥ iti prākṛtakramavaśena prayoga-
codanātaḥ pūrvaṃ prākṛtān padārthānavagamayantyāḥ sāvitrahomādīnāmapyante'nuṣṭhānaṃ nyāyyamiti-
na ca dīkṣaṇīyādiśravaṇaṃ madhye'nupraveśamavagamayitumalam । kramasyānabhidhānāta ।
<b>punaḥ śrutistu ananyārthā kramamevāvagamayati</b> । yadyapi kramo nābhidhīyate tathāpi
pāṭhabalena kramo'vagamyate । tatra ca punaḥ śruterananyaparāyāstātparyamiti tadbalena
madhye'nupraveśaḥ ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1318</note> <note>(2) P. 1319</note>
﻿<pb n="r1116"/>
<p><b>sannipātaścet । atrāpi dīkṣaṇīyāsaṅkīrtanaṃ pūrvavat kramārthaṃ manyate pūrva-
pakṣavādī</b> । yathā dīkṣaṇīyāyāḥ punaḥ pāṭhāt sāvitrahomādibhissaha kramakalpanā tathā
rukmapratimocanādibhirapīti dīkṣaṇīyānantarameva teṣāṃ prayogo yuktaḥ । tatra dīkṣaṇīyāyāḥ
saṅkīrtanaṃ pūrvapadārthakramaparatayaivoktamiti । rāddhāntavādī <b>parastādyathok‍taṃ nyāyyaṃ manyate ।
kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ pūrvasminnevopayujyate na punaḥ parasminnapīti । atrocyate---parato'na-
nyatvāvagamāt pūrvasmiṃścānyatvāvagate yuktamuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yaḥ padārtho vaikṛte[to]
dīkṣaṇīyāyāḥ pūrvaṃ paṭhyate tasmin bādarāyaṇanyāyādantyatvamavagamyate /?/ tadanusāreṇa pāṭhasyā-
saṃbhavāt । atastatparatvaṃ 1tāvacchruteḥ । yastu parataḥ paṭhyate tasya parabhāvo bādarāyaṇa-
nyāyenāpyaviruddhaḥ । nirantarapāṭho'pi avaśyaṃ paṭhitavyatayāpyupapadyate । tena nairantaryamapi
na śakyate vak‍tumiti na tatparatvaṃ śruteḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti śrīśālikanāthakṛtāyāṃ ṛjuvimalāyāṃ
pañcikāyāṃ pañcamādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>

<head>ṛjuvimalā</head>

<section>
<head>tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>vivṛddhiḥ</b> । nanveṣā śeṣacintetyasaṅgatimāśaṅkyāha---<b>kramārtha eva pratyekasamudāya-
saṃbandhaścintyate । pratyekaṃ saṃbandhe hi vyavadhānamahatvam । samudāyasaṃbandhe tvalpatvam</b> ।
vitatiḥ kramaḥ, sā pratyekasaṃbandhe mahatī; samudāyasaṃbandhe tvalpeti । tasmādyuk‍to vicāraḥ ।
<b>kiṃ punaryuk‍taṃ ? pratyekamabhisaṃbandha iti । pratipradhānaṃ guṇā āvartanta iti nyāyāt ।
nanu ca pṛthaktvaniveśinī saṅkhyetyuk‍tam</b> । asyārthaḥ---pṛthaktvaṃ yatra samavetaṃ tatra
dvitvādikā saṅkhyā niviśata iti dvitīya evoktam । tataścaikaikatra ṣaḍādisaṅkhyā kathaṃ
niviśata iti paraṃ samudāya eva saṅkhyāvidhānamastviti । <b>satyamuktam vidhānavaśāt‍tu
yathopapadyate tathā kalpanīyam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadā tāvata[sāhityaṃ]uddeśyagataviśeṣaṇaṃ syāt
vivakṣitatvāt vivakṣāyāṃ ca vākyabhedāpatteḥ । sāhityasyāvivakṣāyāṃ pratyekameva saṃṅkhyā
vidhīyata iti niścitam । tadanurodhenābhyāsanibandhanaṃ pṛthaktvamāśritya saṅkhyopapadyata iti
kalpanīyam---yathā <q>‘triḥ prathamāmanvāha triruttamāṃ’</q> ityatra sāmidhenīnāṃ pañcadaśatvam । yata
<note>(1) P. 1320</note>
﻿<pb n="r1118"/>
eva pratyekasaṃbandho <b>nyāyyaḥ ata eva <q>‘pañcadaśānyājyāni’</q> ityevamādiṣu pratyekasambandhaḥ</b>
pañcadaśādīnāṃ, anyathā tatrāpi samudāyasambandha eva syāt । <b>atrocyate---na vidhānaṃ
padārthamanyathā kartumutsahate । padārthānurodhī hi vidhiḥ na vidhyanurodhinaḥ padārthāḥ
agninā siñcedityevamādiṣu darśitam</b> । asyārthaḥ---saṅkhyāpadārthastāvata dvitvādikaḥ
pṛthaktve sati niviśate । pṛthaktvaṃ ca yādṛśaṃ samudāye na tādṛśamabhyāse । tena vidheyabhūta-
saṅkhyāsvabhāvālocanayā samudāyasaṃbandha eva saṅkhyā vidhīyata iti padārthānusāreṇa vākyārthaḥ
pratīyate । vidhyanusāreṇa tūk‍tena nyāyena pratyekasambandhaḥ । tatra padārthasvabhāvo vihanyate ।
so'pyanyathākartuṃ na śakyata iti padārthānurodhāt samudāya eva saṅkhyāvidhirāśrayaṇīyaḥ ।
<b>tasmāt yāvatpṛthaktvaṃ tāvadabhyāsakalpanā na sambhavatīti samudāye sambandhaḥ । pṛṣadājye
tvetadviparītam</b> । tatra hi kārakatvena dravyavidhānaṃ kriyāyāśca kārakam । na ca kriyā-
samudāyaḥ kriyā । tena samudāye saṃbandhe tūpapattiriti pratyekasaṃbandha eva nyāyyaḥ ।
<b>yadapyuktaṃ pañcadaśānyājyānīti āvṛttau ḍapratyayaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ</b> tena tatra na saṅkhyā vidhīyate ।
kiṃ tarhi ? viśiṣṭasaṅkhyākā āvṛttiḥ । sā ca pratyekasaṃbandhepyaviguṇaiveti na
vidhānapadārthayoḥ kaścidvirodha iti yathāvidhānameva sambandhaḥ ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1321</note>
﻿<pb n="r1119"/>
<p><b>svasthānāt‍tu । saṅkhyāsampattyarthamabhyāse prāpte idaṃ cintyate---kiṃ daṇḍakalita-
vadabhyāsaḥ uta svasthāna iti</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatiṃ ekapādavyavasthārthamāha । nirākṛte
hi pratyekasambandhe ayaṃ vicāra āpatati । anyathā svasthānavṛddhireva syāta । <b>samudāyābhi-
sambandhāt daṇḍakalitaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । uktametat yāvatpṛthaktvamasti tāvat
nābhyasitavyamiti । paratastu saṅkhyāsiddha‍yarthamabhyāse kartavye daṇḍakalitavadevābhyāso
nyāyyaḥ । <b>pūrvapratītakramānurodhāt svasthāne yukta iti rāddhāntaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---prekṣā-
pūrvakārī yaḥ puruṣaḥ sa parvālocayati vinābhyāsena tāvat kṣemo nāsti । tenābhyāso'vaśyā-
śrayaṇīyaḥ । sa idānīṃ yadi daṇḍakalitavata syāta pūrvapratītakrama eva bādhaḥ syāt । na
cosau yuktaḥ । tasmāt svasthānavivṛddhirevāstviti । <b>samudāyasaṃbagdhasya tūbhayathā'-
virodhaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>samidhyamānavatīm । nanu vacane sati pūrvapakṣa eva na saṃbhavati</b>---<q>‘antarāle
dhāyyā’</q> iti vacane sati nāsti pūrvapakṣaḥ, vacanān‍nyāyasya durbalatvāt । <b>uttaraṃ---arthavāda-
pūrvakaṃ tadvacanamiti pūrvapakṣavādī nyāyānusāreṇāpi gacchatyeveti manyate</b> asyārthaḥ
<note>(1) P. 1322</note>
﻿<pb n="r1120"/>
---antarālatvena dhāyyānāṃ yo'yamarthavādaḥ tatpūrvakamidaṃ vacanam । na sākṣācchrūyamāṇamasti
tataśca kalpyavacana[na]nyāyaṃ bādhitumalamiti nyāyānusāreṇāyamarthavādo neya iti pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate । <b>rāddhāntastu nāyathārthagrahaṇe pramāṇamastyarthavādasyeti</b> । tena yathārthavādamī-
dṛśamevedaṃ vacanam । nanu nyāyo'tra pramāṇamarthavādasyāyathārthagrahaṇe tatrāha---<b>na śabdārthaṃ
nyāyo niruṇaddhi nyāyamātraṃ tadityuktam । ato yathārthavādamevedaṃ vidhānaṃ nyāyyam</b> ।
nārthavādasvarūpātikrameṇa । <b>dhāyyāśabdanirūpaṇaṃ tu prāsaṅgikam । darśitaṃ ca tat</b> ।</p>
<p><b>stomavivṛddhau । nyāyamātraṃ vacanaṃ bādhituṃ na kṣamata ityuktam । vacanaṃ cedaṃ
vṛṣaṇvantastṛcā bhavanti । tṛca uttamaḥ paryāsa” iti</b> । 2anena ṛrjvarthaṃmanubhāṣate
ākṣep‍tum । adhunā ākṣipati---<b>nanu dvādaśāhe etadvacanam । atadvikāreṣu keyamā-
śaṅkā</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadidamuttamasya tṛcasya paryāsatvaṃ vidhīyate tata dvādaśāha eva ।
tatprakaraṇa evāsya tṛcasya paṭhitatvāt । ataśca kratvantareṣu kathamiyamāśaṅkā---uttamāta
tṛcāta paryāsībhūtāt prāgāgantunā3 hi bhavitavyaṃ iti । pratiprakaraṇaṃ dharmāṇāṃ vyavasthitatvāt
<note>(1) P. 1323</note> <note>(2) G. ṛjutvārtha</note> <note>(3) G. āgantubhiḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1121"/>
kratvantareṣvapi dvādaśāhavikāreṣu yā[tā]vaccodakaprāptā yujyetāpyāśaṅkā । atadvikāreṣu sā
atyantamayuktā । samādhatte---<b>uttamaśabdaśravaṇāt । kimidamuttamaśabdaśravaṇāditi uttamaḥ
paryāso bhavatīti padārthāṅgatāṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</b> । uttamaśabdaśravaṇe sati uttamasya
tṛcasya paryāsatvaṃ vidhīyate na dvādaśāhikasyaiva । tenottamatṛcarūpapadārthāṅgatāṃ manyate
pūrvapakṣavādī (a)vihitaṃ ca kratvantareṣvapyuttamatvaṃ iti asya tatrāpi paryāsatā vidhīyate ।
<b>nanu ca padārthāṅgatve ānarthakyamuktam</b> । yadi padārthamātre dharmo vidhīyate tadā dharmavidhe-
rānarthakyaṃ syāt apūrvasaṃbandhābhāvāt । ato dvādaśāhasaṃbandha eva uttamatṛce paryāsatā---
vidhiriti । pariharati---<b>na tadānarthakyaṃ paryāse sambhavati sarvasya paryāsasyārthavattvāt</b> ।
vidheyaparyāsasvarūpamevedamīdṛśaṃ yena padārthamātrasambandhitayāpi vidhāne sati ānarthakyaṃ nāsti ।
<b>kratusambandhinī hi paryāsasaṃjñā</b> । kratoreva hyantasya paryāsaśabdaḥ saṃjñā, nidhanādiśabdavata
nirupapadāt paryāsaśabdāt kratvantapratipatteḥ । yat‍tu bhāṣyakāreṇa kṣetraparyāsa ityupanyastaṃ
tat sopapadasya gauṇaprayogadarśanena kratvantavacanatvapratipattaya eveti mantavyam । yatra hi
akratusaṃbandhi vidheyamavaghātādi tatra mābhūt padārthamātradharmatā, ānarthakyaprasaṅgāt । yatra
vidheyameva kratusaṃbandhi na tatrānarthakyaśaṅketi । evaṃ tāvata atadvikāreṣvasti pūrvapakṣaśaṅketi
darśitam । saṃprati dvādaśāhavikāra evodāharaṇamiti matvā <b>tadvikāreṣvapi nirākaraṇīya
evāyamartha ityupanyāsaḥ</b> । dvādaśāhavikāreṣu codakaprāp‍tyāpi śaṅkopapadyata ityarthaḥ ।
<note>(1) mā. śravaṇaprāmāṇyāt</note>
﻿<pb n="r1122"/>
<b>atrābhidhīyatte---nāyaṃ padārthadharmaḥ । kastarhi ? kratudharmaḥ । kathaṃ ? prakaraṇāt dvādaśāha-
niyogaikyamavagamyate na kratvantaraniyogaikyam</b> । avagamyate । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---yadyapi
padārthamātravarmatayā vidhāne'pi vidhyānartak‍taṃ nāsti tathāpi dvādaśāhaprakaraṇāmnānāt
dvādaśāhaniyogenaiva sahānvitābhidhānāta tatsaṃbandha eva padārthamātre vidhānaṃ
na kratvantarasambandhe । <b>nanu ca padārthānusārī niyogaḥ</b> । anyathā dvādaśopasattvamapi
jyotiṣṭomasyaiva syāditi padārthānusāreṇa kratumātrasaṃbandha eva nyāyya iti codayati ।
uttaraṃ---<b>padārthānusārepyatrāvirodhāt</b> । tatra hyahīnapadaṃ virudhyate । iha na
kasyacidvirodha iti prakaraṇāta dvādaśāhasaṃbandha eva । <b>tasmānna 1kratvantarasaṃbandhakalpanāyāṃ
pramāṇamasti</b> । tadatra vidhyānarthakyenāpūrvasaṃbandhiṣu vidhānamityevarūpaṃ rāddhāntābhāsaṃ nirākartu-
midamuk‍taṃ niyogaikyenaiva naiyogike rūpe vidhānaṃ nānarthakyaparihārāyeti । <b>yadi paraṃ dvādaśāha-
vikāra evaitatsyāt</b> tatra codakataḥ prāpteḥ <b>na ca vā tatrāpi । atha vā</b> dvādaśāhavikā-
reṣvapi nāyaṃ dharmaḥ kiṃ tarhi <b>vṛṣaṇvatāṃ dharmaḥ</b> vṛṣaṇvatāṃ tṛcānāṃ madhye ya uttamaḥ tṛcaḥ
tasyāyaṃ paryāsatvaṃ dharmaḥ । na ta te kratvantareṣu santi । tasmātteṣvapyāgantavo'nta eva ।
uttamasya hi paryāsatvavidhānāt prāk‌paryāsādāgantanaḥ syuḥ । tannāstītyuktam---<b>nanu ca
padārthadharmo na bhavatītyuktam</b> । kathaṃ vṛṣaṇvatāṃ dharma ityucyate ? <b>satyamuk‍taṃ</b> padārthadharmo na
<note>(1) G. kratvantaradhātvartha</note>
﻿<pb n="r1123"/>
bhavatīti, na punaḥ <b>kratvarthāparityāgenāpi</b> । kratvarthaparityāgena padārthadharmo na bhavatītyuktam
na punaḥ tadaparityāgenāpi । tena dvādaśāhikavṛṣaṇvat‍tṛcadharmo'yaṃ nānyadīyānyatṛcadharmaḥ ।
<b>tasmāduk‍taṃ2 tadvikāreṣvapi na bhavati</b> ।</p>
<p><b>ante tūttarayoḥ । nanu kathamatra pūrvapakṣaḥ ?</b> yāvatā vacanāt gāyatryādiṣvevāgantūnāṃ
niveśa iti yuktam । <b>vacanamadṛṣṭvetyayuktamidam । adhītavedasya hi dharmaji-
jñāsā । ayaṃ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । idamapi dvādaśāha eva vacanam</b> । na kevalaṃ pūrvādhi-
karaṇe vṛṣaṇvantastṛcā bhavanti tṛca uttamaḥ paryāsa iti dvādaśāhe vacanam । api tu <q>“trīṇi
ha vai yajñasyodarāṇi gāyatrī bṛhatyanup‍ṭup ca atra hyevāvapanti ata evodvapanti”</q> itīdamapi
dvādaśāha eva । tathāpi kimityāha---<b>atra viśeṣāgrahaṇāt tadvikāreṣu bhavatu atadvikā-
reṣu mā bhūt iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> । pūrvatra vṛṣaṇvatāmayaṃ dharma iti viśeṣagrahaṇāta
dvādaśāhavikāreṣu ca teṣāmabhāvāt paryāsatā na bhavati । iha tu viśeṣagrahaṇāta
dvādaśāhavikāreṣu gāyatryādiṣvevāvāpaḥ udvāpaśca vidheyau । ye kratavo na dvādaśāhavikārabhūtā
<note>(1) P. 1326</note> <note>(2) dviruk‍taṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1124"/>
teṣu mābhūdityatadvikāra evātrodāharaṇam । <b>atrocyate---āvāpanibandhanametadvacanaṃ yāva-
dāvāpaṃ bhavitumarhati</b> । atra vacane gāyatryādayo yajñodaratvena stūyante tadupapādanāyeda-
mucyate-<q>‘atra hyevāvapanti ata evodvapantī’</q>ti । na cānyataḥ siddhau āvāpodvāpau gāyatryā
dimātraviṣayau staḥ iti । <q>‘vacanāni tvapūrvatvāt’</q> iti vacanakalpanā । tacca vacanaṃ kalpya-
mānamāvāpamātranibandhanaṃ yāvadāvāpaṃ bhavitumarhatīti tāvanmātreṇaiva hetusamarthane yajñodara-
stutyupapattiḥ । na hyatra dvādaśāhikāvevātrāpodvāṣau hetutvenocyete api tu sāmānyata eva ।
ato vacanamapi kalpyamānaṃ sāmānyata eva yāvadāvāpaviṣayaṃ, na punaḥ dvādaśāhikāvāpaviṣayam ।
<b>kathaṃ tarhi prakṛtaniyogaikyaṃ ? na,</b> prakṛtaniyogaikyaṃ, kāryāśritatvādasya vidheḥ, kāryamāvāpa-
viṣayamāśritya gāyatryādīnāmayaṃ vidhiḥ । yo'sāvāvāpaḥ sa gāyatryādiṣu kartavyaḥ iti ।
tenānyataḥ siddhāvāpamāśritya guṇavidhirayam । tena prakṛtaniyogaikyaṃ nāsti । na ca
dvādaśāhikāvāpamātraviṣayamidaṃ vacanaṃ api tu āvāpamātraviṣayam । ataḥ kratvantaravartināmapi
gāyatryādīnāmāvāpodvāpagocaratvamiti na 2prakṛtaniyogaikyam । <b>vṛṣaṇvatsu upadeśāśraya iti</b>
viśeṣaḥ । upadiṣṭānāṃ vṛṣaṇvatāṃ tṛcānāmevottamasya paryāsatā, nānyasya; tena dvādaśāha-
niyogaikyaṃ tāsāmiti siddham ।</p>
<p><b>graheṣṭakam</b> । nanvasaṅgateyaṃ cintetyāśaṅkyāha---<b>atrāpyaṅgāṅgicintā kramārthaiva</b> ।
/?/vanacitiśeṣatve praticitīṣṭakopadhānaṃ pratisavanaṃ ca grahaṇamiti kramānyatvaṃ bhavatīti ।
<b>kathamatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> yāvatā yāgāgnisaṃbandhitvenopadeśāta graheṣṭakasya taccheṣataiva yuktā ।
<note>(1) P. 1325</note> <note>(2) G. prakṛti</note>
﻿<pb n="r1125"/>
uttaraṃ---<b>kāryānupraveśānniyogārthasya citisavananiṣpattyā cānupraveśasya</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yāvatkiñcidaṅgaṃ tatsarvaṃ niyogārthaṃ tasya sarvasya kāryānupraveśāt svayaṃ vā tat kartavyam
kiñcidvā tena kartavyam । na hyakāryānupraveśinā siddharūpeṇa niyogo niṣpadyate saṃpādyaviṣaya-
tvānniyogasya । tasmānniyogārthasya kāryānupraveśāt pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nanvetāvatāpi pūrvapakṣo na
siddha‍yati yāgāgnyanupraveśitayā niyogārthasiddheḥ atrāha-<b>citisavananiṣpattyā cānupraveśasya</b>
kāryārthatvāditi pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ । yo'pyasau yāgāgnyanupraveśaḥ so'pi citisavananiṣpattyaiva
nānyathā । tasmāt yāgāgnyanupraveśasyāpi citisavananiṣpattyā kāryānupraveśāt citisavana-
niṣpattireveṣṭakopadhānasya grahaṇasya ca kāryam । yacca yasya kāryaṃ kartavyaṃ tattasya kāryamiti savana-
citi śeṣatvameva graheṣṭakasya । upasaṃharati---<b>tasmāccitisavanaśeṣo'yamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
atrocyate---upadeśasiddhayarthaṃ hi kāryaṃ na kāryasiddha‍yartha upadeśaḥ । yāgāgnisaṃbandhaścāya-
mupadeśaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---satyaṃ kāryānupraveśitā niyogārthasya । sā tu upadeśasiddha‍yarthā
kathaṃ nāmopadiṣṭasya niyogārthatā syāditi na punaḥ kāryamapekṣyopadeśaḥ । <b>yāgāgnisaṃbandhaścāya-
mupadeśaḥ</b> । tasmāttatsiddhireva kāryaṃ na citisavananiṣpattiḥ । yacca kāryaṃ taccheṣataiva
yukteti yāgāgniśeṣataiva graheṣṭakasya । <b>nanu ca nyāyapautarukyamidaṃ aruṇayā krīṇātīti</b> ।
asyārthaḥ---aruṇādhikaraṇepyetaduk‍taṃ upadeśabalena āruṇyasya krayaniṣpattireva kāryaṃ, yadyapi
ca sākṣāt sādhanatā nāsti iti, ihāpi tadevocyate yadyapi sākṣādyāgāgnikāryatā nāsti
﻿<pb n="r1126"/>
tathāpyupadeśabalena tadeva kāryamiti । <b>tatrāsaṃbhavādapi bhavantīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।
tannirākaraṇārthamidama</b> । asmārthaḥ---atratyapūrvapakṣavādī evaṃ manyate tatrāruṇādhikaraṇe
anyena prakāreṇa kāryānupraveśābhāvāt yuktā upadeśabalenāruṇimnaḥ <b>krayakāryatā</b>2 । iha tu
citisavananiṣpattyāpi citikāryānupraveśitopapadyata iti imameva tatratyaṃ rāddhāntāmāsa
nirākartumidamadhikaraṇam । tatrāpi nāsambhavāt krayakāryatā kintu upadeśādeva । sambhavepi
kāryāntarasya upadeśabalenaiva kāryāśravaṇāt upadeśa eva kāryāśrayaṇe hetuḥ na kāryāntarasaṃbhava
<b>iti । prayojanamuktama</b> ।</p>
<p><b>ante syuravyavāyāt</b> । nanu <q>“yāṃ vai kāṃcit brāhmaṇavatīmiṣṭakāmabhijānīyāta tāṃ madhya-

padyate । sarvā brāhmaṇavatya ityanuvādaṃ manyate</b> । sarvā eveṣṭakā brāhmaṇavatyaḥ sarvāsāmeva
brāhmaṇok‍tenādhikāravidhinā gṛhītatvāt । viniyuktatvāccādhikāravidhirevāṅgānāṃ viniyojakaḥ
sahakāra[ri]mātrāṇi śrutyādīni । tataśca yadyayaṃ vidhirāśrīyate tadā sarvāsāmeva madhyamāyāṃ

aupānuvākyānāmiṣṭakānāṃ madhyamāyāṃ citāvupadhānamityanupapannaḥ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <b>evaṃ sati anyā
anyā iti darśanamupapannaṃ bhavati</b>-<q>‘āvapanaṃ vā uttamā citiḥ yadanyā anyā iṣṭakā upadadhāti’</q>

﻿<pb n="r1127"/>
iti । <b>evaṃ prāpte abhidhīyate । brāhmaṇavatyaḥ śrutiviniyuktāḥ parigṛhyante । kimiti ।
mantraviniyojyatvāccheṣāṇām । samākhyā punaḥ laukikyevetyuktama</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yadi grāhakābhiprāyeṇa brāhmaṇavatītyucyate tadā avaiśeṣikatvāta vacanamidamanarthakaṃ syāta

<p><b>prāglokaṃ pṛṇāyāḥ</b> । atredṛśo viṣayaḥ agniprakaraṇe citiprakaraṇe citiviśeṣamanārabhyaiva

iti nopapadyate lokaṃpṛṇāpi brāhmaṇavatyeva</b> । asyārthaḥ---<q>‘yāṃ vai kāñcita’</q>

<q>‘citriṇīrupadadhāti’</q> ityevamādiṣu</b> । teneṣṭakā etā brāhmaṇavatyaḥ । <b>iha punaḥ <q>‘lokaṃ
pṛṇa chidraṃ pṛṇa’</q> iti mantrapradhāno'yaṃ nirdeśaḥ iti laiṅgikyeveyam</b> । mantro hi prakaraṇe
paṭhitaḥ kañcidarthaṃ prakāśayannaṅgam । 2śak‍noti cāyaṃ cāyaṃ mantraḥ iṣṭakāmabhidhātumiti mantra-

<p><b>saṃskṛte karma । āhitāgneradikāraśravaṇāt ādhānena cāgnīnāmutpatteḥ

<p><b>pareṇāvedanāt</b> । nanvasaṅgateyaṃ cintetyata āha-<b>atrāpi 2dīkṣitapadārthakrama-

<q>“āgnāvaiṣṇavamekādaśakapālaṃ nirvapeddīkṣiṣyamāṇaḥ”</q> ityadhikāriviśeṣaṇam । <b>na cādhi-

tayā samuccayo yuktaḥ । anyathā hi vikalpaḥ syāt <b>sarveṣāmutpattyarthatvāt anapekṣaśravaṇācca ।
kathaṃ tarhi ādhānapavamāneṣṭīnāṃ samuccayaḥ</b> ādhānasya pavamāneṣṭīnāṃ cotpattyarthatvāt ana-
pekṣaśravaṇācca । uttaraṃ---<b>prayojanāntarābhāvāt na tatra tayorgrāhakaṃ kiñcidasti । iha
punaḥ jyotiṣṭomavidheḥ vikalpastulyārthānām</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadyādhānapavamāneṣṭīnāmagni-
saṃskārabhūtānāmeko vidhiḥ grāhakaḥ syāt tadā tasya sakṛtprayuk‍teḥ ekamevānuṣṭhānamiti
tulyakāryatvāt ekamevopādāpayet । tataśca vikalpaḥ syāt । na caitadasti । kāmaśrutasya-
stvāhavanīyādibhissādhyā āhavanīyameva prayuñjate ubhayasaṃskāranibandhanaṃ cāhavanīyatvamiti
tatprayuktānāṃ yuktassamuccayaḥ । daṇḍādīnāṃ tu jyotiṣṭomavidhirgrāhako'stīti ekakāryāṇāṃ
vikalpaḥ syāt । <b>tasmādasmatpakṣa eva samuccayasiddhiḥ syāt । na cābhidhānābhāvādarthā-
bhāvaśśakyate vak‍tumiti darśitam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) G. adhikārasiddhe</note> <note>(2) G. adds viṣayaḥ siddhaviṣayapratipattiradhi-
kāriviśeṣaṇānniṣpatteriti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ ।</note>
﻿<pb n="r1133"/>
<p><b>aṅgavatkratūnām । nanu cāvaśyaṃbhāvini krame pāṭhānniyama uktaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ
---yatrānekeṣāṃ padārthānāṃ ekena kartrā'nuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyaṃ tatrāvaśyaṃbhāvini krame pāṭhāt krama-
niyama uktaḥ । ekādhikāravidhiprayuktānāṃ ca ekena kartrā'nuṣṭhānaṃ prayujyate na nānādhikāra-
prayuk‍tānāṃ; atastatra kathaṃ pāṭhāt kramaniyama āśaṅkyate । kiñca kratvantaravaditi pūrvapakṣe
pravṛttyadhikaraṇe yadupanyastaṃ tatrāpi <b>vyatireko varṇitaḥ</b> vaiṣamyamuktam । <b>bhinnaprayoga-
vacanatvānnaiṣāṃ krama upapadyata iti</b> । atastenaiva vaiṣamyodbhāvanena kratvantarāṇāṃ pāramparyakrama-
niyamo nāstīti darśita eva rāddhāntaḥ । ataḥ <b>kathamatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</b> ? ucyate---<b>anekānuṣṭhāna-
nibandhano'yaṃ kramaḥ । anekāni kāmyāni karmāṇi kurvataḥ yukta eva kāminaḥ kramaniyama
iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । ekādhikāraprayuktā vā bhavantu anekādhikāraprayuktā vā padārthāḥ
sarvathā yatrānekeṣāṃ padārthānāmekenānuṣṭhānaṃ tatra kramaḥ । anekāni kāmyāni karmāṇyekena
kāminā kartavyānīti krame sati pāṭhādavagataḥ kramaniyama ādariṣyate । <b>kathaṃ tarhi sarvasvāre
pāṭhakamaḥ</b> ? uttaraṃ---<b>arthādbādho bhaviṣyati</b> । diṣṭāṃ gatiṃ gatavati yajamāne parato'nuṣṭhānā-
bhāvāt arthākhyena pramāṇena bādho bhaviṣyatīti <b>na doṣaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---vidhivitā-
cinteyaṃ na puruṣecchāvitānacintā</b> । vidhīyanta iti vidheyāḥ padārthā ucyante । teṣāṃ
vitāḥ atrādhyāye cintyate । na puruṣecchāvitānacintā । kutaḥ ? <b>acodanālakṣaṇatvāttasya</b>
<note>(1) P. 1331</note>
﻿<pb n="r1134"/>
icchāvitānasya । yadi puruṣecchāyāḥ kramaniyamo bhavet tadā kāmyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kramaniyamo
bhavet, adhikāriviśeṣaṇakrameṇādhikārasyāpi kramavattvāt । na punaḥ <b>icchāyā aniyame</b>
yathecchotpādaṃ aniyamenādhikārotpatteḥ । na cātra puruṣecchāvitānaścintyate । tasyācodanā-
lakṣaṇatayā codanālakṣaṇavedārthavicāre'saṅgatatvāt । icchāśritatvācca tasya icchāvadacodanā-
lakṣaṇatvam । evaṃ tāvat acintanīyatoktyā puruṣecchāvitānasya tannibandhanaḥ kāmyānāṃ
kramaniyamo nāstītyuktam । saṃprati sākṣāt karmaṇāmeva kramo na śābda iti darśayati
---<b>ekasya cādhikāravidheḥ aṅgavidhivitānasaṃbandho nādhikārāntaramapekṣate</b> । ekā-
dhikāravidhiprayuktānāmaṅgapradhānānāṃ yugapat 1prasaktānuṣṭhānānāṃ puruṣāśaktyā vitānasambandho bhavati
na punaradhikārāntaramapekṣate । tena bhinnādhikāraprayuktānāṃ kramāvatāro nāstītyarthaḥ । kutaḥ ?
<b>asaṃbandhāt</b> parasparamadhikārāṇāṃ saṃbandhābhāvāt । idamatrākūtam---ekādhikārānu-
praviṣṭānāṃ ekadeśasthānāmiva paṅ‌ktirūpā vitatiḥ nānyathetyarthaḥ । <b>asaṃbandhasya</b>
ca vidheyāsaṃbandhasya ca vitānasya śābdataiva <b>na śakyate vak‍tum</b> । tasmāt aśābdo'yaṃ
parasparakramaḥ kāmyānām । na ca śābdasyānuṣṭhātāro'śābdamādriyante । yadi tāvadekasmin
kāle bahavaḥ kāmā nipateyuḥ tadā yugapadadhikāre sati bahuṣu karmasu kramāpekṣā syāt । na
caitadasti । kāmānāyā yugapadutpādābhāvāt । tadāha---<b>na ca sarvakāmasyādhikāraḥ</b> । kutaḥ ?
<b>yogasiddha‍yadhikaraṇe pratyuktatvāt</b> । ataḥ kāmato'pi kāmayaugapadyādapi na vidheyeṣu karmasu
kramasaṃbandhaḥ । pāṭhamātre vā ādriyamāṇe sarvasvāre pāṭhakramaḥ kena vāryate । artheneti cet
tatrāha---<b>arthasya saṃbandhaviṣayatvāt</b> । arthākhyaṃ pramāṇaṃ vidheyasaṃbandhacodanālakṣaṇakrama-
2viṣayatvāt nācodanālakṣaṇe pramāṇaṃ bhavatīti kuto bādhakam । <b>tasmāt kāmyeṣvaniyamaḥ</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) G. prayukta</note> <note>(2) G. viṣayatvaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1135"/>
<p><b>ya etenetyagniṣṭomaḥ</b> । nanu asaṅgateyaṃ cintetyāśaṅkyāha---<b>uparitanasyādhikaraṇasya
viṣayapradarśanārthamidamadhikaraṇam</b> । uparitanaṃ hyadhikaraṇaṃ kramacintārthaṃ tasya viṣaya-
prasiddha‍yarthamityaupoddhātikatayā saṅgatirityarthaḥ । jñāte hi etenetyasyārthe tadapekṣo'nyenetyanya-
śabdārtho nirūpayituṃ śakyaḥ । <q>“eṣa vāva prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ yajjyotiṣṭomaḥ ya etenā niṣṭvā
athānyena yajate”</q> ityuk‍te jyotiṣṭoma eva pratīyate sarvasaṃsthaśca jyotiṣṭomaḥ । ataḥ sarvāsāmeva
saṃsthānāṃ 2vāda iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nityatvādagniṣṭomasaṃsthasya prakaraṇamiti rāddhāntaḥ । atra
hi agniṣṭomo jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe samāmnānāt asya vākyasya jyotiṣṭomasyaivānena yajñāntarā-
pekṣayā pūrvakālatocyate agniṣṭomasaṃsthā ca nityā । tena tatsaṃsthasyaiva prakaraṇam vikṛti-
bhūtāni saṃsthāntarāṇītyuk‍taṃ tṛtīye । anyathā nityānityasaṃyogavirodhaprasaṅgāt । tena
tatsaṃsthasyaivāyaṃ vāda iti ।</p>
<p><b>athānyeneti । etenetyagniṣṭomasaṃsthasyāvamarśāt anyeneti saṃsthānta-
rāvamarśaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । samānajātīyāpekṣo'yamanyaśabdaḥ । yathā ekapuruṣa āgataḥ
anyo netyuk‍te puruṣāntarameva pratīyate tathehāpi saṃsthāpekṣayā'nyatve saṃsthāntarameva pratīyata
iti---<b>rāddhāntī tu eṣa vāva prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ iti yajñaśruteḥ yajñāntaramevānyaśabdena</b>
<note>(1) P. 1333</note> <note>(2) G. anuvādaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1136"/>
<b>pratīyata ityuktavān</b> yajñasaṅkīrtanena yajñantaramevānyaśabdenocyate । yadyevametacchabde-
nāpi tarhi jyotiṣṭoma evocyatāṃ sarvasaṃsthaścāsāviti sarvasaṃsthasyaiva pūrvatvamapi syāta ityatrāha
---<b>agniṣṭomasaṃsthasya nityatvāt ya etenetyucyate</b> nityānityasaṃyogavirodhena nityasaṃsthasya
prakaraṇamiti pūrvatvavidhau nityatvādagniṣṭomasaṃstha evocyate । <b>tathā cāpattivihārāvupapannau
bhavataḥ</b> । bhede satyāpattivihārau nānyathā । jyotiṣṭomāpekṣayā tāvucyete na nityasaṃsthā-
pekṣayā vihāravākye <q>‘yajñāta’</q> iti śravaṇāt sarve ca jyotiṣṭomā yajña iti । ato'rthavādava-
śenāpattivihāraviṣayo yajñāntarameva anyaśabdenocyate । āpattyākṣepaparihārau bhāṣya
evoktau ।</p>
<p><b>ekastome vā</b> । ekastomānāṃ vākyaśeṣādanyeneti grahaṇam । vākyaśeṣe eka-
stomāḥ kratavaḥ kīrtyanta iti ta evānyaśabdenāpi grāhyāḥ <b>nacānyenetyanyatvamātrāvagateḥ</b>
nacaikastomā grāhyāḥ anyaśabdādanyamātrapratīteḥ । <b>nanu ca vākyaśeṣādviśeṣāvagatiri-
tyuktam</b> । anyathā hi arthavādapadānāṃ atiparokṣā vṛttiḥ syādityarthaḥ । uttaraṃ
<note>(1) P. 1334</note>
﻿<pb n="r1137"/>
<b>---sandigdheṣu vākyaśeṣānnirṇaya uktaḥ । iha tu asandigdhaiva jyotiṣṭomādanyeṣvavagati-
riti arthavādamātrametat</b> । na hyanyamātre arthavādapadānāṃ atiparokṣā vṛttiḥ anyamātra-
grahaṇe'pi ekastomasaṅkīrtanamupapadyate । saṃsthāntaraparigrahaṇe jyotiṣṭomāpekṣayā āpattivihārā-
va/?/papannāveveti yuktamāpattivihāraviṣayakratvantaragrahaṇam ।</p>

<section>
<head>caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><b>kramakopaḥ । <q>‘atra balābalacintā’</q></b> ityanena arthācca ityadhikaraṇe balābalacintā
na kṛteti darśayati । <b>pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ avidheyatvāt kramasya avagateśca
tulyatvādvikalpaḥ iti । rāddhāntastu vidheyavirodhādavagaterevātulyatvamiti śrutyarthayorbala-
vattvamuktam</b> । āśvino daśamo gṛhyate taṃ tṛtīyaṃ juhoti [iti]grahaṇe daśamatā āśvinasya
daśamaprātipadikābhihitā vākyena viniyuktā aṅgabhṛtā niyogasiddha‍yarthamupādeyeti vidheyā ।
tasyāṃ cāśrīyamāṇāyāṃ 1paurvāparyabalena viśeṣe sati yādṛśī vitatiravagamyate sā śrutipramāṇikā
akṣaramūlatvāt । tatra yadi pāṭhakrama ādriyate vihitaṃ daśamatvamaṅgabhūtameva nopapadyate ।
ato vidheyavirodhāt pāṭhakramo durbalaḥ । tathā arthakrame 3yavāgvā vidheyāyāḥ pāṭhakrameṇa
homasya parastātpāke homaṃ prati sādhanatvānupapatteḥ vidheyavirodhāt pāṭhakramasya durbalatvam ।
<b>atra śrutyarthayorvirodhe kathaṃ ? uttaraṃ---naivodāharaṇamasti</b> atha tvasti <b>artha eva tarhi</b>
<note>(1) P. 1335</note> <note>(2) G. paurvāparyaviśeṣe</note> <note>(3) G. yavāgūtpattipāṭhakrameṇa</note>
﻿<pb n="r1139"/>
<b>balīyān kārye hyatrārthaśabdenocyate । kāryārthaśca kramaḥ । ataḥ śrutimapabādhate kāryaviṣa-
tvāttasyāḥ</b> । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---śrutigamyaṃ kāryaṃ tena śrutyarthayorvirodha eva nāsti । atha
kāryaṃ kutaścit śrutinirapekṣamevāvagataṃ tadā tadvirodhinī śrutirnādaraṇīyā, kāryasya prameyatvāt
śruteśca pramāṇatvāt prameyārthatvāt pramāṇasyeti ।</p>
<p><b>avadānābhidhāraṇa</b> । atrāpi pravṛttikramamukhyakramayoḥ <b>balābalacintā । pravṛtteḥ
pūrvapravṛttatvāt pravattirbalīyasīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</b> । dadhidharmāṇāṃ yā pravṛttiḥ
anuṣṭhānaṃ sā pūrvedyuḥ pravṛttā । tannibandhanaścaiva pravṛttikramaḥ iti pravṛttirbalīyasīti manyate ।
<b>kāryārthatvātkramasya avadānasya ca pradānopakramatvāt mukhyakramo balīyaniti rāddhāntaḥ</b> ।
yathā kāryaṃ nirvarṇyate tathā kramo grāhyaḥ kāryārthattvāttasya homaścāvadānādīnāṃ kāryaṃ, tena tadvaśena
ya kramaḥ sa ādaraṇīyaḥ । pradānopakramatvāccāvadānādīnāṃ yathāpradānameva kramo grāhya iti ।
<b>darśanamuktam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1337</note>
﻿<pb n="r1140"/>
<p><b>vacanādiṣṭipūrvatvam</b> । atrāpyakṣaraparaṃ <b>kramamaṅgīkṛtya cintā</b> । akṣarebhyaḥ paraṃ1
akṣaraparaṃ akṣaravaśenāvagamyata iti yāvat । na punaḥ kramaparāṇyevākṣarāṇi kintu kāla-
parāṇi kālārthatvātsaṃyogasya । tena kālasaṃbandharūpe paurvāparye sati vitativiśeṣaḥ kramātmako-
'vasīyata ityakṣaraparatā । <b>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī <q>‘somena yakṣyamāṇa’</q> iti nākṣaraparatā kramasya
sambhavatīti manvānaḥ iṣṭipūrvatāmevāha । kathaṃ punarna saṃbhavati ? ādhānavidhānaparatvā-
dvākyasya</b> । somena yakṣyamāṇo'gnīnādadhīta iti ādhānameva somena yakṣyamāṇasya vidhīyate
2na punarādhānānantaryaṃ somayāgasya vidhīyate । tadā hyevamucyeta ādhānāntaraṃ somena
yajeteti । na caivamuktam---<b>darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvā iti tu kālavidhānāt kramasiddhiḥ</b> ।
atrābhidhīyate---<b>yeyamadyatanī vibhaktiḥ sā nādhānānantaryādṛte sambhavatīti tatrāpyarthāt
kramasiddhiḥ</b> । somena yakṣyamāṇo'gnīnādadhīta iti śrūyate । tatreyaṃ bhaviṣyadadyatane vibhaktiḥ
adyatane'syāsaṃbhavāt ādhānānantaryaṃ lakṣayati । yadyānantaryamapi na lakṣayet anupapannārthaiva
hi syāt । tena somādhānayostāvadānantaryaṃ <b>pratīyate । kva punariyaṃ na saṃbhavati ?</b> kasyāṃ
punaravasthāyāṃ kimadhikāre prayoge yeyamadyatanī vibhaktiḥ ānantaryādṛte na saṃbhavati ?
<b>adhikāre</b> । yadi jyotiṣṭomādhikāre <b>ānantaryamapi</b> na syāt tadeyaṃ na saṃbhavatītyarthaḥ ।
tasmādanantaramadhikāraḥ adhikārāyattaṃ cānuṣṭhānamiti somānuṣṭhānamanantaraṃ pratīyata iti
<note>(1) G. parama</note> <note>(2) G. na punarādhānaṃ kartavyaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="r1141"/>
<b>ādhānavidhānepyarthāt kramākṣepaḥ</b> । yadyapyādhānaṃ vidhīyate tathāpyanantarānuṣṭhānāvasitasom-
yāga ādadhīta iti śāstrārthāvagamāt । atassiddhaṃ ādhānānantaraṃ soma iti । <b>abhyuccayo
darśitaḥ</b> ।</p>
<p><b>utkarṣādbrāhmaṇasya । asminnadhikaraṇe pūrvādhikaraṇārthasya viṣayaviśeṣe'vasthā-
panam । yadanyat tat prāsaṅgikameva</b> । anenāsaṅgatidoṣaṃ pariharati । arthastu yadetat
pūrvādhikaraṇe sādhitamiṣṭipūrvatvaṃ somapūrvatvaṃ ca u/?/(na)kalpau iti tasya viśeṣe brāhmaṇaviṣaye1
'vasthāpanaṃ kriyate । ataḥ kiṃ trayāṇāmapi varṇānāmubhau kalpau uta brāhmaṇasya somapūrvatvameva
mūlavicāro'yaṃ yadanyat kimūrdhvaṃ somātkarmāntaramiti । tathā hi kiṃ kevalā paurṇamāsyutkṛṣyate
brāhmaṇasyomau kalpau iti । tatprāsaṅgikaṃ vināpyanena vicāreṇa pūrvapakṣasiddhāntayossiddhatvāt ।
atra bhāṣyakāreṇa kṛts‍nau darśapūrṇamāsāvutkṛṣyete brāhmaṇasya somapūrvatvameveti sādhayitvā'nantaraṃ
idaṃ vicāritaṃ-kimādhānakālabādhaḥ uta somakālabādha iti । tadākṣipati---<b>yaḥ punarayamantarā-
garbhiṇyupanyāsaḥ sa kimarthaḥ</b> । asyārthaḥ---pūrvasādhitameva kalpadvayaṃ gṛhītvedamadhikaraṇa-
mārabdhavyaṃ(bdhaṃ) anyathā'dhikaraṇānārambhāt । ataḥ somakālabādhanasādhanena kalpadvaya-
sādhanāt antarāgarbhiṇyupanyāso'narthakaḥ । uttaraṃ---<b>evamartho'sau । yadyanantaraṃ somādhānaṃ
tadā brāhmaṇasya kalpadvayaṃ saṃbhavati anyasya ca svakāle punariṣṭipūrvatvameva niyamyate</b>
<note>(1) P. 1337</note> <note>(2) G. viśeṣe</note>
﻿<pb n="r1142"/>
somaścādhānaṃ ca somādhānam । yadyanantaraṃ parasparamavyavahitaṃ syāta yadyādhānānantaraṃ somaḥ
syāt tadā kalpadvayasyātmalābhāt brāhmaṇasyānyasya vā kalpadvayaṃ saṃbhavati ।
svakāle punaḥ somasyeṣṭipūrvatvameveti tadidamanupapannaṃ yasmādevamucyamāne'dhikaraṇārambhaṃ prati
hetutvāt aupoddhātikī cintā syāt na punarantarāgarbhiṇī । atra vadāmaḥ । antarāga-
rbhiṇītve ayaṃ hetuḥ । pūrvaṃ hi agnīṣomīyasya pratyabhijñānena karmāntaratve niraste sati
tadvadādhānasyāpi karmāntaratvaṃ nāstīti siddhe sati vidheyāntarābhāvāt somakālabādhe sati
somāvānayorānantaryasiddhiḥ । anyathā svakālāvasthita eva some purastādanantarakālabhāvyā-
dhānānantarameva vidhīyate । tataśca kalpadvayābhāvassyāditi 1kalpadvayasiddha‍yarthamantaraiveyaṃ cintā
kriyata iti । saṃprati mūlādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣamāha---<b>kathaṃ punaridamavagamyate brāhmaṇasyaiva kalpa-
dvayamiti</b> । na hi kalpadvaye'pi brāhmaṇaśravaṇamasti । ato'viśeṣāta sarveṣāmeva kalpadvaya-
miti । <b>rāddhāntastu iṣṭipūrvatve haviṣa utkarṣāt</b> । yasmādiṣṭipūrvatve'gnīṣomīyapuroḍāśā-
tmakasya haviṣa utkarṣaḥ sa ca muk‍tasaṃśayo brāhmaṇasyaiva । tata iṣṭipūrvatvakalpe brāhmaṇasyaikapradhāna-
nyūnadarśapūrṇamāsaprayogāpatteriyamapekṣā upajāyate---kena prakāreṇa brāhmaṇaḥ prathamameva saṃpūrṇau
darśapūrṇamāsau kuryāta iti । tasyāṃ cāpekṣāyāṃ aparassomapūrvatvakalpaḥ upadiśyate ityapekṣita-
vidhiparyālocanayā brāhmaṇasyaiva somapūrvatvaṃ vijñāyata iti siddhaṃ brāhmaṇasyaiva kalpadvayam ।
tadidamupasaṃharannāha---<b>tasmāt somādhānaṃ tasyaiva anyathā hi brāhmaṇasyaivotkarṣe'napekṣi-
tārthavidhānaṃ syāt</b> । brāhmaṇasyaivaikahavirutkarṣe yadi sarveṣāmeva somapūrvatvaṃ vidhīyate
tadā'napekṣitārthavidhānaṃ syāt । <b>śeṣamuktam</b> ।</p>
<note>(1) P. 1325</note> <note>(2) G. kalpadvayasyārthasiddhimantaraiveyaṃ</note>﻿<p><b>puroḍāśastvanirdeśe । ekahaviṣa utkarṣa iti sthite tadviśeṣāvadhāraṇāyedama-
dhikaraṇam</b> । anenāvāntarasaṅgatiruktā । <b>uk‍taṃ ca</b> bhāṣyakāreṇedamadhikaraṇam ।</p>
<p><b>vikṛteḥ । pūrvaṃ nyāyato'saṃbhavamuktvā tasminnevāhani samāptyupakramau darśitavān
sasbhavārtham</b> । atredamabhimatam---ihādhikaraṇe nyāyata eva kiṃ vikṛtīnāṃ sadyaskālatā[uta]
rdva‍yahakālateti cintyate । sadyaskālatāvacanamasaditi kṛvā cintā । atra pūrvapakṣavādī
prakṛtivikṛtyoḥ dva‍yahakālatāyāṃ paurṇamāsīkālasyālpatvenāsaṃbhavaṃ manvānaḥ pratyakṣaśrutatvāt prakṛte-
rdva‍yahakālasyānugrhāya pratipadyeva vikṛtīnāmupakramasamāptī ityāha । rāddhāntī tu codakaprāpta-
dvayahakālatānugrahāya caturdaśyāṃ vikṛtīnāmupakramaḥ pañcadaśyāṃ ca samāptirityuktavān । prati---
panmātra(pra)yoge tu iha pañcadaśīsaṃbandho dva‍yahakālatā cātyantabādhitau syātām । yathok‍tena
prakāreṇa kevalapratipatsaṃbandho bādhita iti । akṣarārthastvitthaṃ---pūrvanyāyato'lpatayā
paurṇamāsīkālasyomayasaṃbandhābhāvāt pratyakṣaśrutatayā ca prakṛterdva‍yahakālatvena vikṛterdva‍yahakāla-
tāyā asaṃbhavaṃ pūrvapakṣadṛṣṭyā bhāṣyakāra uktvā asminneva pañcadaśe'hani dva‍yahakālatvāya
caturdaśyupakrāntāyā vikṛteḥ samāptiṃ pratipadi samāpayiṣyamāṇāyāśca prakṛteḥ upakramaṃ
darśitavān dvayordva‍yahakālatāsaṃbhavārthamiti na vacanapratipakṣatā saṃbhavatīti vacanāta sadyaskālatā
<note>(1) P. 1338</note> <note>(2) G. pratipanmātrayogitve</note>
﻿<pb n="r1144"/>
vikṛtīnāmityuktavān । evaṃ nyāyato vicārya saṃprati tathā'nuṣṭhānaṃ mābhūditi vacanamuddhāṭitaṃ
na vacanapratipakṣatā nyāyamātrasya saṃbhavatīti । dva‍yahakālatākārye sadyaskālatāvidhānāta
sadyaskālataiva vikṛtīnāmityuktavān bhāṣyakāraḥ ।</p>
<p><b>sānnāyya । tathā somavikārāḥ ।</b> atra sūtrakārastathāśabdaṃ prayuñjānaḥ adhikaraṇa-
dvaye'pi tulyo nyāya ityāha । sa kathaṃ tulyo nyāya ityatrāha---<b>ihādhikaraṇadva‍yepi
nādhikārādṛte kālalakṣaṇā saṃbhavatīti kṛtādhikārasyaiva kramasyādhikāra iti tadvi-
kārāṇāmapyevameveti yuktam</b> । asyārthaḥ---yadi sānnāyyāgnīṣomīyayoḥ somasyādhikāro
viśeṣe nāvasthāpyate tadā somasya darśapūrṇamāsayośca svakīyottarakālatālakṣakatvaṃ na syāt ।
tasmāt sānnāyyāgnīṣomīyayoḥ yo'dhikārī sa kṛtasomaḥ eva । tathā kṛtadarśapūrṇamāsa eva
somādhikārīti yantrite cādhikāriṇi kālo niyantuṃ śakyate nānyathetyadhikaraṇadvayepi
tulyanyāyateti । yadi tulyo nyāyaḥ kimiti tarhi adhikaraṇadvayamiti tadāha---<b>kimartha-
madhikaraṇadvayamiti</b> । uttaraṃ-<b>pūrvatra kartṛtānirdeśāt 1nāsomayājīti somayāgasya kartā
sānnāyye kartṛtayā'bhidhīyate</b> । yadi ca somayājino'dhikāraḥ syāt tadā tathāvidhaḥ
kartā bhavet, nānyathā । kṛtasome cādhikāriṇi balāt somottarakālatā bhavatīti yuk‍taṃ
<note>(1) G. somayājīti</note>
﻿<pb n="r1145"/>
tatrottarakālatvam । <b>dvitīyādhikaraṇe tu darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭveti</b> naivamiti
<b>punarāśaṅkitavān । kartṛnirdeśābhāvāt । kathaṃ tarhi rāddhānte nyāyatulyatā</b> ? uttaraṃ
---<b>nādhikārādṛte kālalakṣaṇā sambhavatīti tulyatok‍tā</b> । asyārthaḥ---atrāpi tu ktvā-
pratyayayogādibhiḥ nirvṛttadarśapūrṇamāsasamānakartṛkatā somasyāpyavagamyamānā kṛtadarśupūrṇamāsa eva
some kartetyavagamayāṃte । na cātathābhūte2'dhikāriṇi tathābhūtasya kartṛtopapadyate iti
labdhe'dhikāriṇi tadbalenaiva darśapūrṇamāsottarakālatā somasyāvagamyata iti tulyatoktā ।</p>
